A Jian - Home cooking

July 28, 2025

4_egg_dishes.txt - 4 Delicious Egg Dishes

Objectives

  • Learn four unique and flavorful egg recipes.
  • Master quick and easy cooking techniques for eggs.
  • Expand your culinary skills with diverse egg preparations.
  • Impress family and friends with creative egg dishes.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients for each recipe.
  • Learn to adjust ingredient quantities based on serving size.

Ingredients

Recipe 1: Green Pepper Sauce Egg

  • Several farm fresh eggs (adjust quantity based on servings)
  • Water starch (amount not specified)
  • Garlic cloves (multiple)
  • 1 tbsp salt
  • 1 tbsp Song Rong Xian (mushroom seasoning)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce
  • Appropriate amount of oyster sauce
  • 1 tbsp corn starch
  • ½ bowl of water
  • Several thin-skinned green peppers

Recipe 2: Mushroom and Garlic Sprout Stir-fried Egg

  • 3 farm fresh eggs
  • 1 handful of shiitake mushrooms
  • 1 handful of white button mushrooms
  • Salt
  • A few drops of white vinegar
  • Soy sauce (small amount)
  • Oyster sauce (a tiny amount)
  • Salt (a tiny amount)
  • Song Rong Xian (mushroom seasoning) (a tiny amount)
  • White sugar (a tiny amount)
  • 1 tsp potato starch
  • Small amount of water
  • Ginger
  • Garlic cloves
  • Small chili peppers (or bell peppers)

Recipe 3: Phoenix Steamed Egg

  • 6 eggs
  • Baking soda (small amount)
  • Water (substantial amount)
  • Water chestnuts (several)
  • Pork belly (amount not specified, 3 fat to 7 lean recommended)
  • Ginger
  • Green onions
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Soy sauce
  • Oyster sauce
  • 1 tbsp cornstarch
  • Sesame oil (small amount)

Recipe 4: Covered Egg Cake

  • 2 cucumbers
  • 4 eggs
  • ½ piece of ham
  • Salt (small amount)
  • Song Rong Xian (mushroom seasoning) (a tiny amount)
  • Pepper (small amount)
  • 3 small chili peppers (or omit)
  • 1 green pepper
  • Small handful of oyster mushrooms
  • Ginger
  • Garlic cloves
  • Small amount of green onions
  • Piece of lean pork
  • Soy sauce (small amount)
  • Salt (a tiny amount)
  • Five-spice powder (small amount)
  • 1 tbsp potato starch
  • Small bowl of water
  • Sesame oil (small amount)

Instructions

Recipe 1: Green Pepper Sauce Egg

  1. Crack eggs into a bowl, add water starch, and whisk until smooth.
  2. Mince garlic, combine with salt, Song Rong Xian, soy sauce, oyster sauce, cornstarch, and water; mix well.
  3. Chop green peppers.
  4. Heat oil in a pan, pour in egg mixture, and cook until set, then remove.
  5. Add more oil to the pan, stir-fry green peppers until slightly browned.
  6. Add cooked eggs and sauce, stir-fry until heated through.

Recipe 2: Mushroom and Garlic Sprout Stir-fried Egg

  1. Whisk eggs with salt and vinegar until light and frothy.
  2. Slice shiitake mushrooms thickly. Clean and separate white button mushrooms.
  3. Chop garlic sprouts into 3-4cm pieces.
  4. Mince ginger, garlic, and chili peppers.
  5. Make a sauce with soy sauce, oyster sauce, salt, Song Rong Xian, sugar, potato starch, and water.
  6. Blanch mushrooms and garlic sprouts in boiling water.
  7. Heat oil, cook eggs until tender, then remove.
  8. Stir-fry ginger, garlic, and chilies until fragrant.
  9. Add mushrooms and garlic sprouts, stir-fry until slightly dry.
  10. Add eggs and sauce, stir-fry until well combined.

Recipe 3: Phoenix Steamed Egg

  1. Soak eggs in water with baking soda, then rinse clean.
  2. Boil eggs for 8 minutes, then cool and peel.
  3. Dice water chestnuts.
  4. Mince pork belly.
  5. Mix pork, water chestnuts, ginger, green onions, salt, pepper, soy sauce, oyster sauce, cornstarch, and sesame oil.
  6. Cut eggs in half, remove yolks, and fill whites with meat mixture.
  7. Steam eggs for 10 minutes.
  8. Make a sauce with the egg liquid, soy sauce, goji berries, and cornstarch.
  9. Pour sauce over steamed eggs.

Recipe 4: Covered Egg Cake

  1. Dice cucumbers, ham, and green pepper.
  2. Whisk eggs with diced ingredients, salt, Song Rong Xian, and pepper.
  3. Mince ginger, garlic, and chop green onions.
  4. Dice lean pork.
  5. Make a sauce with soy sauce, salt, five-spice powder, potato starch, and water.
  6. Heat oil, pour in egg mixture, cook into a pancake, then flip and cook the other side.
  7. Heat more oil, stir-fry ginger and garlic until fragrant.
  8. Add pork, stir-fry until white.
  9. Add oyster mushrooms and stir-fry for 30 seconds.
  10. Add peppers, stir-fry until tender.
  11. Add sauce, stir-fry until thickened.
  12. Stir in sesame oil and green onions.
  13. Pour sauce over the egg cake.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=VWRBGsRhGKo

amaranth_with_preserved_egg.txt - 苋菜皮蛋

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare amaranth to retain nutrients and prevent bitterness.
  • Master a simple yet delicious amaranth and preserved egg recipe.
  • Understand the benefits of amaranth and its nutritional value.

Ingredients

  • 1 bunch of amaranth (红苋菜)
  • 2 preserved eggs (松花皮蛋)
  • 2 green peppers (青椒)
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜子)
  • Some ginger (生姜)
  • 1 tablespoon salt (盐)
  • 1 tablespoon alkaline (食用碱)
  • Cooking oil (菜籽油, or 猪油/橄榄油)
  • 2 bowls of pure water (纯净水)
  • A pinch of chicken essence (鸡精)

Instructions

  1. Trim the roots of the amaranth.
  2. In a large bowl, dissolve 1 tbsp salt and 1 tbsp alkaline in plenty of water.
  3. Soak the amaranth in the solution for 10 minutes to remove pesticides and bacteria.
  4. Peel and chop the preserved eggs.
  5. Mince the garlic and thinly slice the ginger.
  6. Remove the stems and slice the green peppers into small pieces (optional).
  7. Thoroughly rinse the amaranth under running water until the water runs clear.
  8. Drain the amaranth and add 1 tsp salt, mixing well. Let it sit for 10 minutes.
  9. Squeeze out excess water from the amaranth.
  10. Heat cooking oil in a wok until slightly smoking.
  11. Add the preserved eggs and stir-fry until slightly browned.
  12. Add the ginger and garlic, stir-frying until fragrant.
  13. Add the amaranth and stir-fry over high heat until the color brightens.
  14. Add the green peppers (if using) and 2 bowls of water.
  15. Cover and simmer over medium heat for 5 minutes.
  16. Season with salt and a pinch of chicken essence.
  17. Stir and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Q1M3XEWeheY

ap_bao_gu.txt - Crispy Fried King Oyster Mushrooms

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare king oyster mushrooms for optimal texture and flavor.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful sauce for the mushrooms.
  • Create a visually appealing and delicious dish.

Ingredients

  • Several fresh king oyster mushrooms
  • Water
  • Salt
  • 1 tablespoon white sugar
  • 1 tablespoon cornstarch (or potato starch)
  • 2 green chilies, thinly sliced
  • Several small red chilies, thinly sliced
  • Ginger and garlic, minced
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • 1 tablespoon sugar
  • 1 tablespoon tomato sauce (or ketchup)
  • 1 tablespoon soy sauce
  • Appropriate amount of oyster sauce
  • A little dark soy sauce
  • 1 tablespoon cornstarch
  • ½ bowl water
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Clean king oyster mushrooms thoroughly with water and salt.
  2. Blanch mushrooms in boiling water with 1 tablespoon of sugar for 8-9 seconds.
  3. Immediately transfer blanched mushrooms to ice water, then squeeze out excess water.
  4. Slice mushrooms into thick (approximately 1 cm) slices. If using larger mushrooms, cut into chunks.
  5. Toss sliced mushrooms with cornstarch until evenly coated.
  6. Slice green and red chilies. Mince ginger and garlic. Prepare chopped scallions.
  7. Prepare sauce: In a bowl, mix salt, sugar, tomato sauce, soy sauce, oyster sauce, dark soy sauce, cornstarch, and water. Stir well.
  8. Heat oil in a wok or pan until it reaches 60% heat (筷子冒密集的小泡泡).
  9. Add the coated mushrooms to the hot oil, ensuring they don't splash.
  10. Fry for 30 seconds, then stir to separate. Continue frying over medium heat for about 3 minutes, until golden brown and floating. Remove and drain.
  11. Add a little oil to the pan, sauté ginger, garlic, and chilies until fragrant.
  12. Add the prepared sauce, bring to a boil, and stir constantly to prevent sticking.
  13. Add a little hot oil to the sauce to enhance the flavor.
  14. Add the fried mushrooms, stir-fry until evenly coated with the sauce.
  15. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=5S6dUsViJ_o

apple_pie.txt - Apple Pie

Objectives

  • Learn to make crispy and chewy apple pies.
  • Master a simple and easy apple pie recipe.
  • Create a delicious treat for family and friends.

Ingredients

  • 2 apples
  • Sugar (amount to taste)
  • Glutinous rice flour (amount to adjust based on apple size)
  • 30 grams of milk
  • Breadcrumbs or white sesame seeds (for topping)
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Wash and peel two apples.
  2. Cut the apples into thin slices, then slightly thicker slices, and finally into small cubes.
  3. Place the cubed apples in a bowl.
  4. Add sugar to taste and mix well with chopsticks.
  5. Gradually add glutinous rice flour, mixing continuously until the apples are coated.
  6. Add 30 grams of milk and mix thoroughly.
  7. Knead the mixture into a smooth, firm dough. Adjust milk if needed.
  8. Pinch off small portions of dough and roll into balls.
  9. Flatten the balls into small cakes.
  10. Prepare breadcrumbs or white sesame seeds as a topping.
  11. Heat cooking oil in a pan. Use a brush to coat the pan's interior to prevent sticking.
  12. Place the apple cakes in the pan.
  13. Cover the pan and cook over low heat for 2 minutes.
  14. Flip the cakes and continue cooking for another 2 minutes, covered.
  15. Ensure even cooking by rotating the cakes.
  16. Cook until golden brown and crispy (about 6 minutes total).
  17. Serve and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=C66_4mRVlOs

apple_yam_cake.txt - 蘋果山藥小餅 (Apple Yam Cake)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious apple yam cakes.
  • Master a simple, no-steaming, no-filling recipe.
  • Create a crispy outside and soft inside texture.

Ingredients

  • Several pieces of iron stick yam (山藥 / shānyào)
  • Apples (蘋果 / píngguǒ)
  • Shelled peanuts (花生米 / huāshēngmǐ)
  • Dried cranberries (蔓越莓乾 / màn yuè méi gān)
  • 200g glutinous rice flour (糯米粉 / nuòmǐfěn) - preferably water-milled
  • Cooking oil (食用油 / shíyòngyóu)
  • Water (水 / shuǐ) - as needed

Instructions

  1. Peel the yams (wearing gloves to avoid skin irritation). Wash and cut into even small pieces. Steam for 15 minutes.
  2. Peel and thinly slice the apples. Cut the slices into thin strips, then finely dice. Set aside.
  3. Roughly crush the peanuts. Set aside.
  4. Mash the steamed yams into a smooth puree using a spatula or food processor.
  5. Add the diced apples, cranberries, and crushed peanuts to the yam puree. Mix well.
  6. Gradually add the glutinous rice flour, mixing until a dough forms. Add a little warm water if too dry, or more flour if too wet. Knead into a slightly soft dough.
  7. Wet your hands slightly. Pinch off small pieces of dough, roll into balls, and flatten into small cakes.
  8. Heat a little oil in a non-stick pan or electric griddle over low heat.
  9. Cook the cakes one by one, leaving space between them. Cover and cook for 1 minute, moving the pan to ensure even heating.
  10. Flip the cakes and continue cooking for another 1-2 minutes, flipping every minute, until golden brown and springy.
  11. Serve immediately. The cakes remain soft even when cooled.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=T28nAPDIkww

apxbg_fry.txt - Crispy Fried King Oyster Mushrooms

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare king oyster mushrooms for frying to enhance flavor and texture.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful sauce for the mushrooms.
  • Create a crispy, tender, and savory fried king oyster mushroom dish.

Ingredients

  • Several fresh king oyster mushrooms
  • Water
  • Salt
  • 1 tablespoon white sugar
  • 1 tablespoon cornstarch (or potato starch)
  • 2 green chilies
  • Several small red chilies
  • Ginger
  • Garlic
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • 1 tablespoon sugar
  • 1 tablespoon tomato sauce (or ketchup)
  • 1 tablespoon soy sauce
  • Appropriate amount of oyster sauce
  • A little dark soy sauce
  • 1 tablespoon cornstarch
  • Half bowl of water
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Wash king oyster mushrooms thoroughly with water and salt.
  2. Blanch mushrooms in boiling water with 1 tablespoon of sugar for 8-9 seconds.
  3. Immediately transfer blanched mushrooms to ice water, then squeeze out excess water.
  4. Slice mushrooms into thick (approximately 1cm) pieces.
  5. Toss mushroom slices with cornstarch until evenly coated.
  6. Finely slice green and red chilies.
  7. Mince ginger and garlic; slice and then chop green onions.
  8. Prepare sauce: In a bowl, mix salt, sugar, tomato sauce, soy sauce, oyster sauce, dark soy sauce, cornstarch, and water.
  9. Heat oil in a wok or pan until it reaches 60% heat (筷子冒密集的小泡泡).
  10. Fry coated mushrooms in batches, ensuring they don't stick together, for 30 seconds until set.
  11. Stir-fry until golden brown and floating (about 3 minutes). Remove and drain.
  12. In the remaining oil, sauté ginger, garlic, and chilies until fragrant.
  13. Add prepared sauce, bring to a simmer, and thicken.
  14. Add fried mushrooms, toss to coat, and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=5S6dUsViJ_o

bai_luobo_ji_dan.txt - 白萝卜炒鸡蛋 (Stir-fried White Radish with Egg)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and simple stir-fry of white radish and egg.
  • Understand how to prepare the radish to reduce bitterness and enhance flavor.
  • Master a quick and flavorful cooking method suitable for everyday meals.

Ingredients

  • 1 large white radish (白萝卜)
  • 4-6 eggs (鸡蛋)
  • Several cloves garlic (蒜)
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒)
  • 2 scallions/green onions (蒜苗)
  • Salt (盐)
  • MSG (味精) - Optional
  • Soy sauce (老抽)
  • Light soy sauce (生抽)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)
  • Water (清水)

Instructions

  1. Wash and peel the white radish. Cut it in half lengthwise, then into quarters, and finally into thick slices.
  2. In a bowl, whisk the eggs lightly. Set aside.
  3. Mince the garlic and finely slice the chili peppers and scallions. Set aside.
  4. Bring a pot of salted water to a boil. Add the radish slices and blanch for about 2 minutes until translucent. Drain and set aside.
  5. Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan. Add the eggs and scramble until cooked through. Remove and set aside.
  6. Add a little more oil to the pan. Add the minced garlic and chili peppers and sauté until fragrant.
  7. Add the blanched radish and stir-fry until some of the moisture is released.
  8. Add a small amount of dark soy sauce (老抽) to color the radish.
  9. Add a small bowl of water, a pinch of salt, a dash of MSG (optional), and light soy sauce (生抽). Stir-fry until the radish is well-seasoned.
  10. Add the scrambled eggs and scallions. Stir-fry until everything is heated through and well combined.
  11. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=H2nIYQi_3aY

bai_luobo_su_xian_jiaozi.txt - 白萝卜素馅饺子 (White Radish Vegetarian Dumplings)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and nutritious vegetarian dumplings using white radish.
  • Master the techniques of preparing the radish filling and wrapping the dumplings.
  • Understand the importance of blanching the radish to improve texture and taste.

Ingredients

  • 1 large white radish (白萝卜)
  • 1 carrot (胡萝卜)
  • 1 onion (洋葱)
  • 2-3 shiitake mushrooms (香菇)
  • A handful of scallions (小葱)
  • Salt (食盐)
  • Pepper (胡椒粉)
  • A little sugar (白糖)
  • Soy sauce (生抽)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • Water (清水)
  • Ready-made dumpling wrappers (饺子皮)

Instructions

  1. Wash the white radish thoroughly and peel it. Cut it into 4-5 cm long sections, then slice thinly, and finally shred into juliennes.
  2. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add the shredded radish, stir, and blanch for 90 seconds. Remove and drain, then set aside to cool.
  3. Peel and dice the carrot into small pieces.
  4. Halve the onion, then slice and dice it finely.
  5. Clean the shiitake mushrooms, slice thinly, and then dice finely.
  6. Chop the scallions into small pieces.
  7. Heat oil in a pan. Add the diced carrots, mushrooms, and onions. Stir-fry until tender. Remove and set aside.
  8. Chop the cooled white radish into small pieces.
  9. In a large bowl, combine the chopped radish, stir-fried vegetables, chopped scallions, salt, pepper, a little sugar, soy sauce, and oyster sauce. Mix well.
  10. Prepare the dumpling wrappers. Place a wrapper in your palm, and lightly wet the edges with water.
  11. Add a spoonful of filling to the center of the wrapper.
  12. Fold the wrapper in half, and pinch the edges to seal.
  13. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add the dumplings one by one.
  14. Cover and cook over high heat for 2-3 minutes, until the dumplings float to the surface.
  15. Add a second addition of cold water. Continue to cook for another 3-4 minutes, or until the dumplings are cooked through and the wrappers are translucent.
  16. Remove the dumplings with a slotted spoon and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=2v4rzrUoCLA

baked_eggplant_pie.txt - Baked Eggplant Pie

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious eggplant pie.
  • Master simple techniques for preparing and cooking eggplant.
  • Create a family-friendly dish with various ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 1 long purple eggplant
  • Salt
  • Water
  • 1/2 teaspoon white vinegar
  • 1/2 teaspoon salt
  • Garlic sprouts (or leeks)
  • Pork sausage
  • 2/3 of an onion
  • 1 large green or red pepper
  • Lettuce (optional)
  • Shrimp peel (optional)
  • 5 eggs
  • 13g of salt
  • 50g flour
  • Oil for greasing pan

Instructions

  1. Prepare the eggplant: Wash the eggplant thoroughly, rubbing with salt and water for 20-30 seconds. Rinse well. Remove the stem and cut into thin, small cubes.
  2. Marinate eggplant: In a bowl, toss the eggplant cubes with 1/2 teaspoon white vinegar and 1/2 teaspoon salt. Set aside.
  3. Prepare aromatics: Finely chop garlic sprouts (or leeks), pork sausage, onion, and green/red pepper.
  4. Combine ingredients: In a large bowl, combine the marinated eggplant, chopped aromatics, lettuce (optional), and shrimp peel (optional). Squeeze out excess water from the eggplant.
  5. Add egg mixture: Crack 5 eggs into the bowl. Use chopsticks to mix thoroughly, ensuring all ingredients are coated. Add 13g of salt.
  6. Add flour: Add 50g of flour and mix until a slightly thin batter forms.
  7. Prepare baking pan: Lightly grease an electric baking pan or skillet with oil.
  8. Bake: Pour the mixture into the prepared pan, spread evenly. Bake on medium heat for 3 minutes, uncovered.
  9. Continue baking: Cover and reduce heat to low for 1 minute. Using a spatula, scrape the edges. Cover and bake on low heat for another 3 minutes.
  10. Finish and serve: Uncover and cook until golden brown on both sides. Press gently with a spatula to check for doneness (it should not collapse). Turn off the heat and serve. Cut into small pieces for easier serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ky7u1iCCemw

baked_onion_salad.txt - Baked Onion Salad

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious baked onion salad.
  • Master the technique of steaming onions to enhance their flavor and texture.
  • Create a flavorful and visually appealing salad perfect for festive occasions.

Ingredients

  • 2 large onions
  • 2 eggs
  • 1/3 tsp thirteen incense (presumably a spice blend)
  • Pinch of pepper
  • 1 tsp potato starch
  • 1 green pepper
  • 1 red pepper
  • 1 cucumber
  • Several cloves garlic
  • Oil for frying
  • Light soy sauce
  • Vinegar
  • 1 tbsp sugar
  • Salt
  • Chili pepper (optional, to taste)
  • 1 tbsp white sesame seeds
  • 1 tbsp homemade chili oil
  • Peanuts (optional)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the onions: Trim and clean two large onions. Steam them over high heat for 2 minutes.
  2. Prepare the egg mixture: Crack two eggs into a bowl. Add thirteen incense, pepper, and potato starch. Whisk until well combined.
  3. Prepare the vegetables: Clean and chop one green and one red pepper into diamond shapes. Cut a cucumber into similar shapes. Mince the garlic.
  4. Cook the egg: Heat oil in a pan. Pour in the egg mixture and cook until set, flipping to brown both sides. Remove from pan and chop into small pieces.
  5. Prepare the sauce: In a small bowl, combine light soy sauce, vinegar, sugar, and salt. Heat over high heat for 1 minute until bubbling. Remove from heat.
  6. Prepare the onions: Once cooled, cut the steamed onions into bite-sized pieces.
  7. Assemble the salad: Combine the chopped egg, onions, peppers, cucumber, and garlic in a bowl.
  8. Add the sauce and seasonings: Pour the sauce over the salad. Add chili pepper (optional), white sesame seeds, and homemade chili oil. Toss well.
  9. Add peanuts (optional) and serve: Add peanuts if desired and mix well. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kSk_9qTvm14

baked_sweet_potato.txt - 烤红薯

Objectives

  • Learn how to select and prepare sweet potatoes for optimal baking.
  • Master a method for baking sweet potatoes that yields a sweeter, softer result.
  • Understand the benefits of pre-boiling sweet potatoes before baking.

Ingredients

  • 糖心蜜薯 (Sugar heart honey sweet potato) - quantity not specified, but enough for desired servings.
  • 清水 (Clear water) - quantity as needed for washing and boiling.
  • 食盐 (Salt) - a small spoonful for soaking and boiling.

Instructions

  1. Select Sweet Potatoes: Choose sugar heart honey sweet potatoes grown in sandy soil. These are sweeter and softer than regular sweet potatoes. Let them sit in a cool, ventilated place for a few days after harvesting for better taste.
  2. Wash Sweet Potatoes: Rinse the sweet potatoes thoroughly in clear water to remove any dirt and sand. Select slightly longer potatoes; they are easier to clean and cook. Continue washing until the water runs clear.
  3. Soak Sweet Potatoes: Drain the washed sweet potatoes and place them in a large bowl. Add plenty of water and a small spoonful of salt. Soak for 30 minutes. This prevents bloating during baking, makes them easier to cook, and increases sweetness.
  4. Boil Sweet Potatoes: Transfer the soaked sweet potatoes to a pot. Add enough water to cover them completely, along with another small spoonful of salt. Bring to a boil over high heat, stirring to dissolve the salt. Reduce heat to low, cover, and simmer for 10 minutes. Pre-boiling reduces baking time, ensures even cooking, and helps the sweet potatoes retain moisture and sweetness.
  5. Drain and Prepare for Baking: Drain the boiled sweet potatoes using a colander and let them dry. Line a baking sheet with aluminum foil. Arrange the sweet potatoes on the baking sheet. For comparison, add an unboiled sweet potato to the baking sheet.
  6. Preheat Oven and Bake: Preheat the oven to 220°C (428°F) with both top and bottom heat for 10 minutes. Bake the sweet potatoes for 25 minutes.
  7. Flip and Continue Baking: Remove the baking sheet, flip the sweet potatoes, and bake for another 25 minutes.
  8. Compare Results: Compare the texture and taste of the pre-boiled and unboiled sweet potatoes. The pre-boiled sweet potatoes will be moist, tender, and sweeter, while the unboiled ones will be hard and less sweet.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=WgJinjelV1w

banana_cake.txt - Banana Cake

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious banana cake.
  • Master a simple recipe suitable for beginners.
  • Create a fluffy and soft cake with a unique texture.

Ingredients

  • 2 ripe bananas, peeled and chopped
  • 2 eggs
  • 220g whole milk
  • 5g yeast powder
  • Sugar (to taste)
  • 150g corn flour
  • 250g all-purpose flour
  • 60g raisins
  • 60g red dates, pitted and chopped
  • Sesame seeds (black and white)
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Peel and chop the bananas into small pieces. Set aside.
  2. In a small bowl, whisk together 2 eggs until well combined.
  3. Pour the egg mixture over the chopped bananas.
  4. If using a meat grinder, process the banana and egg mixture. Alternatively, use a food processor or blender.
  5. Add 220g of whole milk to the mixture.
  6. Add 5g of yeast powder and sugar to taste. Mix well until the yeast dissolves.
  7. Add 150g of corn flour and 250g of all-purpose flour. Stir until a slightly thick batter forms without any dry lumps.
  8. Cover the batter and let it rise for 30 minutes until doubled in size.
  9. While the batter is rising, wash and clean 60g of raisins and 60g of red dates (pitted and chopped).
  10. Once the batter has risen, gently stir to remove air bubbles.
  11. Add the chopped red dates to the batter and mix well.
  12. Grease four small iron rice bowls with a thin layer of cooking oil, both inside and out.
  13. Sprinkle some black sesame seeds at the bottom of each bowl.
  14. Divide the washed raisins equally among the four bowls.
  15. Pour the batter into the bowls, filling them about 70% full.
  16. Arrange the batter evenly with chopsticks.
  17. Sprinkle some white sesame seeds on top.
  18. Steam the bowls in a steamer over high heat for 40 minutes with the lid closed.
  19. After 40 minutes, turn off the heat and let it sit for another 5 minutes before opening the lid.
  20. Carefully remove the cakes from the bowls and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=pF533DA5TgU

bbq_small_potato.txt - 烤土豆

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious, crispy roasted small potatoes.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful method using readily available ingredients.
  • Create a restaurant-quality dish at home, saving money and time.

Ingredients

  • 2 medium-large yellow potatoes (黄心土豆)
  • Plenty of small scallions (小葱), chopped into green onions
  • Plenty of garlic (蒜子), minced into garlic paste
  • 1 tbsp cumin powder (孜然粉)
  • 1 tbsp fine chili powder (细辣椒面)
  • 1/2 tbsp peppercorn powder (花椒面)
  • A pinch of salt (食用盐)
  • 2 tbsp white sesame seeds (白芝麻)
  • A pinch of black pepper (胡椒粉)
  • Vegetable oil (菜籽油)

Instructions

  1. Peel and thoroughly wash the potatoes.
  2. Cut the potatoes into small, roughly square pieces (about 1-inch cubes).
  3. Wash the cut potatoes in multiple changes of water to remove excess starch.
  4. Soak the potatoes in clean water while preparing other ingredients.
  5. Chop scallions into green onions and mince garlic. Set aside.
  6. Prepare the BBQ powder: Mix cumin powder, chili powder, peppercorn powder, salt, sesame seeds, and black pepper in a bowl. Set aside.
  7. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add the potatoes and blanch for 4 minutes until slightly translucent.
  8. Remove the potatoes and drain well.
  9. Heat vegetable oil in a flat pan until slightly smoking.
  10. Add the drained potatoes to the hot pan and stir-fry until golden brown and crispy (about 4-5 minutes), ensuring even cooking.
  11. Add minced garlic and stir-fry until fragrant.
  12. Sprinkle the BBQ powder over the potatoes and stir-fry until evenly coated.
  13. Add chopped scallions and stir-fry briefly.
  14. Serve immediately. Enjoy the crispy outside and tender inside of the roasted potatoes.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=VeLDYD17-Lw

beef_bitter_melon_stir_fry.txt - Beef Stir-fry with Bitter Melon

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious beef stir-fry with bitter melon like a star hotel chef.
  • Master the proper techniques for preparing beef and bitter melon to enhance flavor and texture.
  • Create a flavorful sauce that complements the beef and bitter melon perfectly.

Ingredients

  • 2 green bitter melons (苦瓜 kǔguā)
  • A small piece of fresh beef (牛肉 niúròu), preferably tenderloin or shank
  • Soy sauce (酱油 jiàngyóu)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油 háoyóu)
  • Wine (酒 jiǔ), for deodorizing
  • Dark soy sauce (老抽 lǎochōu), for color
  • Cornstarch (玉米淀粉 yùmǐ diànfěn)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 shíyòngyóu)
  • Garlic (大蒜 dàsuàn)
  • Ginger (生姜 shēngjiāng)
  • Edamame (毛豆 máodòu)
  • Sugar (糖 táng)
  • Water (水 shuǐ)
  • Salt (盐 yán)

Instructions

  1. Cut the beef into thin, even slices. Marinate the beef with soy sauce, oyster sauce, wine, dark soy sauce, and cornstarch. Mix well and add a little cooking oil to prevent sticking.
  2. Clean the bitter melons, remove the ends, and split them in half. Use a spoon to scoop out the seeds and scrape the white membrane to reduce bitterness.
  3. Cut the bitter melon into slightly thicker, diagonal slices.
  4. Mince garlic and ginger.
  5. Prepare the sauce: Combine soy sauce, oyster sauce, sugar, water, and cornstarch in a bowl. Stir well.
  6. Blanch the bitter melon in boiling salted water with a dash of oil for 30 seconds. Remove and set aside.
  7. Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan. Add the beef and stir-fry until browned. Remove the beef and set aside.
  8. Add more oil to the pan. Add the minced garlic and ginger and stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Add the edamame and stir-fry briefly.
  10. Return the beef to the pan. Add the blanched bitter melon. Stir-fry over medium-high heat.
  11. Pour in the prepared sauce and stir-fry until the sauce thickens and coats the ingredients.
  12. Before serving, add a little more oil to enhance the shine.
  13. Serve hot with rice.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Y253Cmipcn0

beef_eggplant_cake.txt - 牛肉茄子浇汁盖饼 (Beef Eggplant Gravy Cake)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious beef and eggplant dish.
  • Master a simple cooking technique requiring minimal cooking skills.
  • Create a flavorful dish with a crispy exterior and tender interior.

Ingredients

  • 2 Shandong black eggplants (山东黑茄子)
  • 1.5 times the normal amount of salt for stir-frying (炒菜盐)
  • Several scallions (葱), separated into white and green parts
  • A small amount of garlic (蒜)
  • A piece of ginger (姜)
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒)
  • 2 Liang (approximately 100g) of beef (牛肉), or substitute with pork or chicken
  • 4 eggs (鸡蛋)
  • A pinch of salt (盐)
  • A small amount of peanut oil (花生油)
  • 1 tablespoon of yellow bean sauce (黄豆酱)
  • 1/2 bowl of water (清水)
  • A small amount of oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • A small amount of light soy sauce (生抽)
  • A small amount of chicken bouillon (鸡精)
  • A small amount of pepper (胡椒粉)

Instructions

  1. Wash and clean two Shandong black eggplants thoroughly. Remove the stems and ends.
  2. Cut the eggplants into 1cm thick slices, then 1cm wide strips, finally into small dices.
  3. Place the diced eggplant in a bowl, add 1.5 times the normal amount of salt used for stir-frying, and mix well with your hands to draw out moisture. Let it marinate for 15 minutes.
  4. Prepare the seasonings: finely chop the white parts of the scallions, slice the garlic and ginger thinly and then mince them, and finely slice the chili peppers.
  5. Prepare the beef: Cut the beef into thin slices, then into thin strips, and finally into small dices (or mince).
  6. In a bowl, whisk 4 eggs with a pinch of salt until well combined. Set aside.
  7. Squeeze out excess water from the marinated eggplant.
  8. Heat a pan over medium-high heat. Add the eggplant and stir-fry for about 30 seconds to remove excess moisture.
  9. Add the stir-fried eggplant to the egg mixture and stir well to coat.
  10. Heat a small amount of peanut oil in a pan. Pour in the eggplant and egg mixture and spread it into a pancake shape.
  11. Cook over medium heat for about 2 minutes per side, or until golden brown and crispy. Use a lid to help cook evenly.
  12. While cooking the eggplant cake, add the minced garlic, ginger, and chili peppers to a pan with a little oil and stir-fry until fragrant.
  13. Add the beef and stir-fry until fragrant and browned.
  14. Add the yellow bean sauce and stir-fry until fragrant.
  15. Add half a bowl of water, stir well, and bring to a boil.
  16. Season with oyster sauce, light soy sauce, chicken bouillon, and pepper. Stir well.
  17. Thicken the sauce with a little cornstarch slurry.
  18. Stir in the chopped green scallions.
  19. Pour the sauce over the cooked eggplant cake.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=R1AEEbjCJwg

beef_egg.txt - 牛肉滑蛋 (Beef and Egg Stir-fry)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a tender and smooth beef and egg stir-fry.
  • Master the technique of marinating beef for optimal texture.
  • Create a nutritious and delicious dish perfect for children.

Ingredients

  • 40 RMB worth of fresh beef (approximately 800g)
  • 1 tablespoon light soy sauce (生抽)
  • 1 tablespoon water starch (水淀粉)
  • A pinch of pepper (胡椒粉)
  • 4 eggs (母鸡下的蛋)
  • 1 tablespoon salt (食盐)
  • Some green onions (小葱), chopped (葱花)
  • Ginger (姜)
  • Garlic (葱)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)

Instructions

  1. Cut the beef into small pieces, then thinly slice against the grain. Ensure slices are even in thickness for even cooking.
  2. Place the sliced beef in a bowl.
  3. Add ginger, garlic, light soy sauce, water starch, and pepper to the beef.
  4. Mix well and marinate for 10 minutes. Do not add salt at this stage to prevent tough beef.
  5. Chop green onions and set aside.
  6. Crack 4 eggs into a bowl.
  7. Add salt, chopped green onions, and water starch to the eggs.
  8. Whisk the eggs until well combined.
  9. Heat cooking oil in a pan.
  10. Add the marinated beef and stir-fry over low heat until 80% cooked.
  11. Pour the egg mixture into the pan.
  12. Gently push the eggs with a spatula to cook them evenly.
  13. Once the eggs are set, break them into smaller pieces using a spatula. Work quickly to prevent overcooking.
  14. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=VedMZx7xm-E

beef_okra.txt - 牛肉炒秋葵 (Beef Stir-fry with Okra)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a tender beef and okra stir-fry.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful recipe.
  • Prepare ingredients efficiently for quick cooking.

Ingredients

  • 秋葵 (Okra): Amount not specified, enough for the recipe.
  • 牛肉 (Beef): 里脊牛肉 (tenderloin beef), amount not specified.
  • 姜 (Ginger): A small piece, thinly sliced.
  • 葱 (Scallions): A small amount, chopped.
  • 生抽 (Light soy sauce): Small amount.
  • 蚝油 (Oyster sauce): Small amount.
  • 食盐 (Salt): To taste.
  • 蛋清 (Egg white): 1
  • 红薯淀粉 (Sweet potato starch): A handful.
  • 食用油 (Cooking oil): Small amount.
  • 蒜 (Garlic): A handful, minced.
  • 水淀粉 (Water starch): Small amount for thickening.

Instructions

  1. Wash okra thoroughly with water and salt to remove fuzz. Rinse until water runs clear.
  2. Remove the stems of the okra and slice into 2-3 cm pieces. Set aside.
  3. Slice beef along the grain into thick strips, then dice into large pieces.
  4. Marinate the beef: In a bowl, combine beef with ginger, scallions, a spoonful of water, light soy sauce, oyster sauce, and salt. Mix thoroughly for 2-3 minutes until sticky and slightly frothy.
  5. Add egg white and sweet potato starch to the marinated beef. Mix until well combined. Add a little cooking oil to prevent sticking. Marinate for 15 minutes.
  6. Mince garlic. Set aside.
  7. Heat a wok or pan and add a small amount of oil.
  8. Add beef to the hot pan and stir-fry over low heat until cooked through and slightly browned. Remove from pan and set aside. (approx. 1 minute)
  9. Add minced garlic to the pan and sauté until fragrant and lightly browned.
  10. Add okra to the pan and stir-fry until mostly cooked (70-80% done).
  11. Return the cooked beef to the pan. Stir-fry everything together.
  12. Add a small amount of water starch to thicken the sauce. Stir-fry until well combined.
  13. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=5BbkLus4d9Y

beef_soup.txt - Beef Soup

Objectives

  • Learn to cook tender and flavorful beef using a 30-year restaurant chef's method.
  • Prepare a delicious beef soup with minimal cost.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful sauce to complement the beef.

Ingredients

  • 2.5 kg Beef brisket (صدر البقر)
  • Salt (ملح)
  • Water (ماء)
  • Ginger (زنجبيل)
  • Garlic (ثوم)
  • Green onions (بصل أخضر)
  • Radish (فجل)
  • White wine (نبيذ أبيض)
  • Anise (ينسون)
  • Cinnamon (قرفة)
  • Bay leaves (أوراق الغار)
  • Sesame oil (زيت السمسم) or other cooking oil
  • Fresh Matsutake mushrooms (ماتسوتاكي طازج) (optional)
  • Balsamic soy sauce (خل الصويا البلسمي)
  • Cilantro (كزبرة)

Instructions

  1. Place beef brisket in a basin. Add salt and enough water to cover the beef. Let it sit to remove impurities and blood.
  2. Prepare the aromatics: thinly slice ginger, roughly chop garlic, and finely chop green onions.
  3. Prepare the radish: remove the top and bottom, peel half, cut in half, then into four slices. Place in a bowl, add salt, and mix to remove bitterness and add flavor.
  4. Slice the beef brisket thinly.
  5. Clean the beef and place it in a pot. Add enough water. Add white wine to remove fishy smell and enhance aroma.
  6. Bring to a high heat, boil for 2-3 minutes to remove blood foam. Remove the foam.
  7. Add spice packet (or anise, cinnamon, and bay leaves). Cover and simmer over low heat for approximately 50 minutes.
  8. Check if the beef is cooked using chopsticks. Remove and place on a cutting board. Cut into desired pieces.
  9. Prepare the sauce: In a small bowl, mix sesame oil (or other cooking oil), salt, fresh matsutake mushrooms (optional), and balsamic soy sauce. Mix well.
  10. Arrange pickled radish in a large serving bowl.
  11. Add the cooked beef brisket and soup to the bowl. Let it sit for 20 minutes.
  12. Garnish with chopped green onions and cilantro. Add a little salt and matsutake to taste.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=tjD2m-UPKl4

beef_stir_fry_okra.txt - 牛肉炒秋葵 (Niúròu chǎo qiūkuí)

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare tender beef for stir-fry.
  • Master the quick cooking technique for okra.
  • Create a flavorful and nutritious dish in minutes.

Ingredients

  • 秋葵 (Qiūkuí) Okra: A handful
  • 牛肉 (Niúròu) Beef: (amount unspecified, but enough for a serving) 里脊牛肉 (lǐjǐ niúròu) - Tenderloin beef is recommended.
  • 姜 (Jiāng) Ginger: A small piece, julienned
  • 葱 (Cōng) Scallions: A small piece, chopped
  • 生抽 (Shēngchōu) Light soy sauce: A small amount
  • 蚝油 (Háoyóu) Oyster sauce: A small amount
  • 清水 (Qīngshuǐ) Water: 1 tablespoon
  • 食盐 (Shíyán) Salt: To taste
  • 蛋清 (Dànqīng) Egg white: 1
  • 红薯淀粉 (Hóngshǔ diànfěn) Sweet potato starch: A handful
  • 食用油 (Shíyòngyóu) Cooking oil: A small amount
  • 蒜 (Suàn) Garlic: A handful, minced

Instructions

  1. Wash okra thoroughly with salt water to remove fuzz and sanitize. Rinse until water runs clear.
  2. Trim the ends of the okra and cut into 2-3 cm pieces. Set aside.
  3. Cut beef (tenderloin recommended) with the grain into thick strips, then dice into large pieces.
  4. Marinate beef: In a bowl, combine beef with ginger, scallions, water, light soy sauce, oyster sauce, and salt. Mix well, kneading the beef to tenderize and absorb the marinade (2-3 minutes).
  5. Add egg white and continue mixing until the beef is frothy.
  6. Add sweet potato starch and mix until evenly combined. Add a little cooking oil to prevent sticking. Marinate for 15 minutes.
  7. Mince garlic.
  8. Heat oil in a wok or pan. Add beef and stir-fry over low heat until cooked through and lightly browned. Remove and set aside. (approx. 1 minute)
  9. Add minced garlic to the pan and sauté until fragrant and lightly browned.
  10. Add okra and stir-fry until slightly tender-crisp. Season with salt.
  11. Add the cooked beef back to the pan. Stir-fry to combine.
  12. Add a little water starch to thicken the sauce (optional). Stir-fry until well combined and heated through.
  13. Serve immediately.

bitter_gourd_egg.txt - Steamed Bitter Gourd with Egg

Objectives

  • Learn a unique way to prepare bitter gourd, minimizing bitterness.
  • Master a simple, elegant method for steaming bitter gourd with egg.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to complement the steamed dish.

Ingredients

  • 2 medium-sized bitter gourds
  • Water
  • Salt
  • 1 tsp cooking oil
  • 3 eggs
  • 1 clove garlic, minced
  • Some dried chili peppers, thinly sliced
  • Some green onions, chopped
  • ½ tsp light soy sauce
  • ½ tsp balsamic vinegar
  • A dash of oyster sauce
  • A pinch of sugar
  • A little sesame oil

Instructions

  1. Prepare the bitter gourds: Wash two bitter gourds thoroughly with salted water. Cut off the ends and halve them lengthwise. Use a spoon to scrape out the seeds and white pith.
  2. Blanch the bitter gourds: Bring water to a boil in a pot. Add a teaspoon of salt and a teaspoon of cooking oil. Add the bitter gourd halves and blanch for 1 minute to remove bitterness. Immediately transfer to ice water to cool.
  3. Prepare the egg mixture: Crack 3 eggs into a bowl. Separate the egg whites from the yolks. Beat the egg whites until frothy. Set aside.
  4. Prepare the sauce: Mince garlic and thinly slice the dried chilies and green onions. Heat a small amount of oil in a pan. Add garlic and chilies, stirring until fragrant. Add soy sauce, balsamic vinegar, oyster sauce, sugar, and sesame oil. Mix well. Set aside.
  5. Steam the bitter gourd: Place the blanched bitter gourd halves in a steamer. Pour the egg whites over the bitter gourd, leaving some space. Steam for 3 minutes.
  6. Add the yolks: Add the egg yolks to the bitter gourd. Cover and steam for another 3 minutes. Turn off the heat and let cool slightly.
  7. Serve: Carefully remove the steamed bitter gourd from the steamer. Slice it and arrange on a plate. Drizzle with the prepared sauce. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=0i-VBzimw4I

bitter_melon_and_tofu_balls.txt - 苦瓜豆腐丸子

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and healthy bitter melon and tofu balls.
  • Master a simple technique to remove bitterness from bitter melon.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to complement the bitter melon and tofu balls.

Ingredients

  • 2 bitter melons (苦瓜)
  • 2 blocks of soft tofu (嫩豆腐)
  • 1 tablespoon salt (食盐)
  • 5 RMB worth of lean pork (瘦肉)
  • 1 tablespoon mushroom seasoning (松茸鲜)
  • A little pepper (胡椒粉)
  • Some oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • 20g cornstarch (玉米淀粉)
  • 1 carrot (胡萝卜)
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜子)
  • 1 tablespoon cornstarch (玉米淀粉)
  • 1 tablespoon soy sauce (生抽)
  • 1/2 bowl of water (清水)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)

Instructions

  1. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add 1 tablespoon of salt and blanch the tofu for 2 minutes to remove bean smell. Remove and drain, being careful not to break the tofu. Set aside to cool.
  2. Wash the bitter melons thoroughly in a large bowl with salt and water. Drain and cut off the ends. Cut the melons in half lengthwise, then remove the seeds using a spoon.
  3. Blanch the bitter melon in boiling water with a little cooking oil for 1 minute to maintain its green color. Immediately transfer to cold water to cool.
  4. Cut the cooled tofu into small square pieces and arrange in a dish.
  5. Cut the cooled bitter melon into thin strips, then dice, and finally mince. Squeeze out excess water using cheesecloth. Save the juice for drinking (optional).
  6. Mince the lean pork. Combine the minced pork and bitter melon in a bowl.
  7. Add 1 tablespoon salt, 1 tablespoon mushroom seasoning, a little pepper, and some oyster sauce to the pork and bitter melon mixture. Mix well to combine.
  8. Add 20g cornstarch and mix until the mixture can easily form into balls.
  9. Lightly oil your palms. Take a portion of the mixture and roll it into a ball, about the size of a ping pong ball. Repeat until all the mixture is used. Arrange the balls on top of the tofu in the dish.
  10. Steam the dish in a steamer over high heat for 12 minutes.
  11. While the balls are steaming, prepare the sauce: Dice a carrot and mince some garlic.
  12. Heat a pan with a little oil, add the carrot and garlic and stir-fry until fragrant.
  13. Add 1 tablespoon cornstarch, 1 tablespoon soy sauce, and 1/2 bowl of water to the pan. Stir until the sauce thickens and becomes glossy. Set aside to cool.
  14. Once the bitter melon and tofu balls are steamed, remove them from the steamer and pour the sauce over them. Serve and enjoy.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=hw8RUzw492Y

bitter_melon_egg_steam.txt - Steamed Bitter Melon with Egg

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare and cook bitter melon to reduce bitterness.
  • Master a unique method of steaming bitter melon with eggs.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to complement the steamed dish.

Ingredients

  • 2 medium-sized bitter melons
  • Salt
  • 1 teaspoon cooking oil
  • 3 eggs
  • 1 teaspoon minced garlic
  • Sliced dried chili peppers
  • Chopped green onions
  • ½ teaspoon light soy sauce
  • ½ teaspoon balsamic vinegar
  • A dash of oyster sauce
  • A pinch of sugar
  • A small amount of sesame oil

Instructions

  1. Prepare the bitter melons: Wash two bitter melons thoroughly with salted water to remove any insects. Cut off the stem and bottom, then slice lengthwise into halves. Using a spoon, scrape out the white flesh and seeds.
  2. Blanch the bitter melon: Add water to a pot and bring to a boil. Add 1 teaspoon of salt and 1 teaspoon of cooking oil. Add the bitter melon halves and blanch for 1 minute to remove bitterness. Remove and immediately rinse with cold water.
  3. Prepare the egg mixture: Crack 3 eggs into a bowl and separate the egg whites from the yolks. Beat the egg whites thoroughly. Set aside.
  4. Prepare the sauce: Mince garlic and finely chop dried chili peppers and green onions. In a small bowl, combine the minced garlic, chili peppers, green onions, light soy sauce, balsamic vinegar, oyster sauce, sugar, and sesame oil. Mix well.
  5. Steam the bitter melon: Place the blanched bitter melon halves in a steamer. Pour the egg whites over the bitter melon, filling each half about halfway. Steam for 3 minutes.
  6. Add the yolks: Add the egg yolks to the center of each bitter melon half. Cover and continue steaming for another 3 minutes.
  7. Finish and serve: Turn off the heat and let the steamed bitter melon cool slightly. Gently remove from the steamer and place on a cutting board. Press gently on both sides to help the egg separate from the bitter melon. Slice and arrange on a plate. Drizzle with the prepared sauce and serve.

bitter_melon_stir_fry.txt - Bitter Melon Stir-Fry (凉拌苦瓜)

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare a refreshing and delicious bitter melon stir-fry.
  • Master the technique of blanching bitter melon to retain its crispness.
  • Understand how to balance the bitterness of melon with sugar and other seasonings.

Ingredients

  • 2 bitter melons (choose turquoise colored ones)
  • 1 small carrot
  • 3 eggs
  • Several cloves garlic
  • 1 tablespoon white sugar
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • A dash of chicken essence
  • 1 tablespoon light soy sauce
  • Cooking oil
  • Water
  • Black fungus (optional)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Bitter Melon: Cut off the ends of the bitter melons, halve them lengthwise, and clean out the seeds and white film. Slice into coin-sized pieces.
  2. Marinate the Bitter Melon: Place the sliced bitter melon in a bowl, add a spoonful of white sugar, mix well, and let marinate for 3 minutes.
  3. Prepare the Vegetables: Peel and dice the carrot into diamond shapes. If using, prepare black fungus.
  4. Blanch the Bitter Melon: Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add the marinated bitter melon and blanch for 30 seconds. Remove immediately with a slotted spoon.
  5. Blanch Other Vegetables: Add the carrots and black fungus (if using) to the boiling water and blanch for 2 minutes. Remove with a slotted spoon.
  6. Prepare the Egg: Whisk 3 eggs in a bowl until well combined.
  7. Stir-fry the Garlic: Heat cooking oil in a wok over medium heat. Add sliced garlic and stir-fry until fragrant.
  8. Stir-fry the Carrots: Add the blanched carrots and stir-fry for 30 seconds.
  9. Add Bitter Melon: Add the blanched bitter melon and stir-fry for another 30 seconds.
  10. Season: Add salt, chicken essence, light soy sauce, and a small amount of sugar. Stir well.
  11. Add Eggs: Pour in the whisked eggs and stir quickly to combine. Cook for about 30 seconds until set.
  12. Thicken (Optional): Add a little cornstarch slurry (cornstarch mixed with water) for a thicker sauce. Stir-fry briefly.
  13. Serve: Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=2TXxhMenlV8

bitter_melon_tofu_balls.txt - 苦瓜豆腐丸子

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and healthy bitter melon and tofu balls.
  • Master techniques for removing bitterness from bitter melon.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to complement the bitter melon and tofu balls.

Ingredients

  • 2 bitter melons (苦瓜)
  • 2 blocks of soft tofu (嫩豆腐)
  • 1 tablespoon salt (食盐)
  • 5 RMB worth of lean pork (瘦肉)
  • 1 tablespoon MSG (味精) - optional
  • 1 teaspoon pepper (胡椒粉)
  • 1 tablespoon oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • 20g cornstarch (玉米淀粉)
  • 1 carrot (胡萝卜)
  • several cloves garlic (蒜)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)
  • Water (清水)
  • Soy sauce (生抽)

Instructions

  1. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add 1 tablespoon of salt and blanch the tofu for 2 minutes to remove bean smell. Remove and drain, being careful not to break the tofu. Set aside to cool.
  2. Place bitter melons in a large bowl, add 1 tablespoon of salt and plenty of water. Wash thoroughly, drain, and set aside.
  3. Cut off the ends of the bitter melons, cut them in half lengthwise, and then into halves again. Use a spoon to scoop out the seeds and white pulp.
  4. Blanch the bitter melon in boiling water with a little cooking oil for 1 minute to maintain its green color. Immediately transfer to cold water to cool.
  5. Cut the cooled tofu into small square pieces and arrange in a dish.
  6. Cut the cooled bitter melon into thin strips, then dice, and finally mince. Squeeze out excess water using cheesecloth. Reserve the bitter melon juice.
  7. Mince the lean pork.
  8. Combine the minced bitter melon, minced pork, 1 tablespoon salt, 1 tablespoon MSG (optional), 1 teaspoon pepper, and 1 tablespoon oyster sauce in a bowl. Mix well to combine.
  9. Add 20g cornstarch and mix until the mixture forms a cohesive ball.
  10. Grease your palms with oil. Take a portion of the mixture and roll into a ball, about the size of a ping pong ball. Repeat until all the mixture is used.
  11. Arrange the meatballs on top of the tofu in a dish.
  12. Steam in a steamer over high heat for 12 minutes.
  13. While the meatballs are steaming, prepare the sauce: Dice a carrot and mince several cloves of garlic.
  14. Heat some oil in a pan, add the carrot and garlic and stir-fry until fragrant.
  15. In a small bowl, whisk together 1 tablespoon cornstarch, 1 tablespoon soy sauce, and ½ bowl of water.
  16. Add the cornstarch mixture to the pan and cook until thickened and glossy. Set aside to cool.
  17. Once the meatballs are steamed, remove them from the steamer and pour the sauce over them.
  18. Serve and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=hw8RUzw492Y

boiled_shrimp.txt - Boiled Shrimp

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious, tender boiled shrimp without adding water.
  • Master a cleaning technique to ensure fresh, high-quality shrimp.
  • Prepare flavorful aromatics to enhance the shrimp's taste.

Ingredients

  • 1.5 lbs fresh shrimp (approximately 35 Yuan worth)
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • Appropriate amount of water (to cover shrimp)
  • Handful of garlic, minced
  • Small piece of ginger, minced
  • Some green onions, white and green parts separated and minced
  • A few Sichuan peppercorns, thinly sliced
  • Cooking oil
  • Red cane vinegar (optional, to remove fishy smell)
  • Soy sauce (optional, for dipping sauce)

Instructions

  1. Rinse shrimp thoroughly multiple times to remove any impurities. Soak in salted water for 5 minutes.
  2. While shrimp soaks, prepare aromatics: mince garlic and ginger; finely chop green onions (separate white and green parts); slice Sichuan peppercorns.
  3. Drain shrimp and clean again. Remove heads, veins, and tails from shrimp. Optionally, remove legs and whiskers.
  4. Prepare a pot: Place ginger slices and white parts of green onions evenly at the bottom of the pot.
  5. Add shrimp to the pot. Add a small amount of peanut oil and red cane vinegar (optional).
  6. Cover the pot, turn heat to high, and cook for 3-4 minutes. (The aromatics will release juices; no water needed).
  7. Remove the lid; the aroma of shrimp, ginger, and garlic will be released.

  8. Remove shrimp, and arrange on a plate, garnishing with the remaining green onions and the prepared sauce (soy sauce). Serve immediately.

  9. (Optional) To easily peel shrimp: Gently cut along the second joint of the shrimp, then pinch the tail to remove the shell.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=oEbHnybA3W8

braised_chicken_legs.txt - Braised Chicken Legs

Objectives

  • Learn to make tender, flavorful braised chicken legs.
  • Master a simple yet effective method for preparing chicken legs.
  • Create a dish that is appealing to both adults and children.

Ingredients

  • 3.5 jin (approximately 10) chicken legs
  • 1 handful of salt
  • 3 eggs
  • 50g corn starch
  • Chopped scallions and ginger
  • 1 tbsp cooking wine
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce
  • A small amount of dark soy sauce (for color)
  • Appropriate amount of oyster sauce
  • A pinch of pepper
  • A pinch of five-spice powder
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Wash chicken legs thoroughly: Rinse chicken legs in a large bowl with a handful of salt to remove dirt and sanitize. Rinse again with clean water to remove excess salt and blood.
  2. Score chicken legs: Make small cuts on the surface of the chicken legs to help them absorb flavor.
  3. Prepare egg mixture: Crack 3 eggs into a bowl, whisk until yolks and whites are fully combined.
  4. Coat chicken legs: Add the egg mixture to the chicken legs and toss to coat evenly.
  5. Add cornstarch: Add 50g of cornstarch to the chicken legs and mix well to coat.
  6. Fry chicken legs: Heat a generous amount of oil in a wok until it reaches 40% heat (筷子测试). Fry chicken legs for 30 seconds per side to set the egg and starch coating, then continue frying for approximately 5 minutes until lightly browned. Remove and drain excess oil.
  7. Marinate chicken legs: Add chopped scallions and ginger, 1 tbsp cooking wine, 1 tbsp soy sauce, a small amount of dark soy sauce, oyster sauce, pepper, and five-spice powder to the fried chicken legs. Mix well, ensuring the chicken legs are evenly coated with the marinade. Marinate for at least 1 hour, flipping halfway through.
  8. Steam chicken legs: Arrange marinated chicken legs in a dish, brush with remaining marinade. Steam in a steamer over medium heat for 40 minutes.
  9. Garnish and serve: Garnish with chopped scallions and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=G9Ks4D4VbGo

braised_chicken_with_noodles.txt - 香菇燉雞麵 (Xiānggū dūn jī miàn)

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare tender, flavorful braised chicken without a gamey smell.
  • Master a simple yet delicious braised chicken noodle soup recipe.
  • Understand techniques for cleaning and preparing chicken and mushrooms.

Ingredients

  • 半只本地鸡 (bàn zhǐ běndì jī) - Half a local chicken
  • 适量盐 (shìliàng yán) - Appropriate amount of salt
  • 开水 (kāishuǐ) - Boiling water
  • 香菇 (xiānggū) - Shiitake mushrooms
  • 土豆 (tǔdòu) - Potato (1 large)
  • 香叶 (xiāng yè) - Bay leaf (1)
  • 八角 (bā jiǎo) - Star anise (2)
  • 花椒 (huājiāo) - Sichuan peppercorns (a small handful)
  • 生抽 (shēng chōu) - Light soy sauce
  • 老抽 (lǎo chōu) - Dark soy sauce
  • 豆瓣酱 (dòubàn jiàng) - Doubanjiang (fermented bean paste) (1 tbsp)
  • 胡椒粉 (hújiāo fěn) - Pepper powder
  • 食用油 (shíyòng yóu) - Cooking oil
  • 姜片 (jiāng piàn) - Ginger slices
  • 葱花 (cōng huā) - Chopped green onions
  • 泡好的面条 (pào hǎo de miàntiáo) - Pre-soaked noodles

Instructions

  1. Rinse the half chicken thoroughly. Rub salt all over the skin for 2 minutes to clean and remove impurities. Rinse with boiling water.
  2. Clean shiitake mushrooms, soak in clean water. Cut a small portion into small pieces.
  3. Cut the peeled potato into small, bite-sized pieces.
  4. Prepare the sauce: Mix light soy sauce, dark soy sauce, 1 tbsp of doubanjiang, and pepper powder in a bowl.
  5. Heat cooking oil in a pot. Add the chicken and braise over medium heat until browned, stirring to release any water.
  6. Add ginger slices and green onions, followed by the bay leaf, star anise, and Sichuan peppercorns. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  7. Pour in the prepared sauce and stir until the color changes.
  8. Add the soaking water from the mushrooms. Bring to a boil, then add the soaked mushrooms and potatoes.
  9. Cover and simmer for 10 minutes.
  10. In a separate bowl, add pre-soaked noodles.
  11. Once the 10 minutes are up, transfer the braised chicken and vegetables to the bowl with the noodles.
  12. Cover and simmer over low heat for 6-8 minutes.
  13. Garnish with chopped green onions and serve hot.

braised_chinese_cabbage_with_tofu.txt - 白菜豆腐煲

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious braised Chinese cabbage with tofu dish.
  • Master the simple steps to prepare and cook this affordable and flavorful recipe.
  • Understand the health benefits of Chinese cabbage and tofu.

Ingredients

  • 1 head of napa cabbage
  • 1 block of firm tofu
  • 1 green onion (chopped)
  • 1 piece of ginger (minced)
  • 2 cloves of garlic (minced)
  • Shrimp peel (amount not specified)
  • Cooking oil (amount not specified)
  • Water (amount not specified)
  • Salt (amount not specified)
  • Sugar (amount not specified)
  • Pepper (amount not specified)
  • Light soy sauce (amount not specified)

Instructions

  1. Cut the napa cabbage in half, then separate it into pieces. Use a knife to separate the root and leaves.
  2. Cut the cabbage into slanted pieces.
  3. Soak the cabbage pieces in water, wash twice, and drain.
  4. Make small slits in the tofu block. Cut larger tofu blocks in half, then into smaller pieces.
  5. Chop the green onion, mince the ginger, and mince the garlic.
  6. Heat cooking oil in a pan or wok. If no oil is available, use pork belly.
  7. Add shrimp peel and sauté until fragrant.
  8. Add the green onion, ginger, and garlic; stir until wilted.
  9. Add the cabbage and stir-fry for one minute.
  10. Add the tofu and stir-fry for about one minute.
  11. Season with salt, sugar, pepper, and light soy sauce. Stir until seasoning dissolves.
  12. Cover and simmer over low heat for 3-5 minutes, or until cabbage is tender.
  13. Garnish with pepper and chopped green onion.

braised_pork_belly_tofu.txt - Braised Pork Belly with Tofu

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious, tender braised pork belly that's rich but not greasy.
  • Master the technique of caramelizing the pork belly for enhanced flavor and color.
  • Prepare a flavorful braising liquid to infuse the pork belly and tofu with deliciousness.

Ingredients

  • 3.5 lbs pork belly
  • Water
  • Star anise
  • Bay leaves
  • Cinnamon
  • Ginger slices
  • Green onion knot
  • Dried sea pepper
  • Sugar
  • Cooking oil
  • Cooking wine
  • Soy sauce
  • 101°C boiling water
  • Salt
  • Garlic
  • Fried tofu

Instructions

  1. Cut the pork belly into large pieces.
  2. Score the pork belly skin and rinse to remove mucus.
  3. Cut the pork belly into bite-sized pieces.
  4. Prepare aromatics: star anise, bay leaves, cinnamon, ginger, green onion, and dried sea pepper.
  5. Heat a wok, add oil, and stir-fry the pork belly until the fat renders and it caramelizes. Remove and set aside, reserving the oil.
  6. In the same wok, add a little oil and sugar, and stir-fry until the sugar caramelizes to a reddish-brown color.
  7. Add the pork belly back to the wok and coat it evenly with the caramelized sugar.
  8. Add the aromatics and stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Deglaze the wok with cooking wine.
  10. Add soy sauce and stir-fry until well combined.
  11. Add 101°C boiling water, ensuring enough liquid to cover the pork belly. Skim off any foam.
  12. Bring to a boil, then reduce heat, cover, and simmer for 40 minutes.
  13. After 40 minutes, uncover, add salt, garlic, and stir.
  14. Simmer for another 10 minutes.
  15. Add fried tofu, stir to coat, and simmer for 2 more minutes, allowing the tofu to absorb the braising liquid.
  16. Garnish with chopped green onions before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Br4ia3Wm56c

braised_pork_belly.txt - Braised Pork Belly (红烧猪肚)

Objectives

  • Learn to make tender, flavorful braised pork belly.
  • Master the technique of caramelizing sugar for rich color and flavor.
  • Achieve a balance of fat and lean in the final dish.

Ingredients

  • 2 kg pork belly (猪肚, zhūdù)
  • 18 grams rock sugar (冰糖, bīngtáng)
  • 2 bay leaves (香叶, xiāngyè)
  • 2 star anise (八角, bājiǎo)
  • 1 cinnamon stick (桂皮, guìpí)
  • 1 onion (洋葱, yángcōng), sliced
  • Ginger (生姜, shēngjiāng), sliced
  • Green onions (葱, cōng), sliced (optional)
  • Light soy sauce (生抽, shēngchōu)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油, háoyóu)
  • Huadiao wine (花雕酒, huādiāo jiǔ)
  • Table salt (食盐, shíyán)
  • Cooking oil (食用油, shíyòngyóu)
  • Water (水, shuǐ)

Instructions

  1. Blanch the pork belly: Boil the pork belly briefly to remove impurities and excess fat. Scrape off any remaining residue with a knife.
  2. Cut the pork belly: Cut the blanched pork belly into evenly sized, large pieces.
  3. Prepare aromatics: Slice the onion and ginger. If using, slice green onions.
  4. Fry the pork belly: Heat oil in a wok or pot over medium heat. Fry the pork belly until lightly browned on all sides, rendering out some of the fat. This takes about 5 minutes. Avoid over-frying, which will make the meat tough.
  5. Caramelize the sugar: Add rock sugar to a pan with a little water and oil. Stir constantly until it melts and turns a deep reddish-brown color.
  6. Combine ingredients: Add the fried pork belly to the caramelized sugar, followed by the bay leaves, star anise, and cinnamon stick. Stir-fry to blend the flavors.
  7. Add liquid and seasonings: Add boiling water to cover the pork belly. Add light soy sauce, oyster sauce, Huadiao wine, and a pinch of salt. Stir well.
  8. Simmer: Cover the pot and simmer over low heat for 30 minutes, or pressure cook for 12 minutes.
  9. Finish: After simmering, increase the heat to reduce the sauce. Add sliced onion, ginger, and garlic. Continue to reduce the sauce until it thickens.
  10. Garnish and serve: Garnish with sliced green onions. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=8cMuUCndRjk

braised_pork_belly_with_tofu.txt - Braised Pork Belly with Fried Tofu

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious, melt-in-your-mouth braised pork belly.
  • Master the technique of perfectly caramelizing the pork belly.
  • Create a flavorful braising sauce that complements the pork and tofu.
  • Prepare a visually appealing dish suitable for family gatherings or special occasions.
  • Learn to balance richness with lightness in a braised dish.
  • Understand the importance of slow cooking and low heat for tender results.

Ingredients

  • 3.5 lbs pork belly
  • Water
  • Star anise
  • Bay leaves
  • Cinnamon stick
  • Ginger slices
  • Green onion knot
  • Dried sea pepper
  • Sugar
  • Cooking oil
  • Cooking wine
  • Soy sauce
  • 1 tsp salt
  • A handful of garlic
  • Fried tofu

Instructions

  1. Cut the pork belly into large pieces.
  2. Score the skin of the pork belly and rinse thoroughly.
  3. Blanch the pork belly in hot water for 10 minutes to remove impurities.
  4. Cut the pork belly into bite-sized pieces.
  5. Prepare the aromatics: star anise, bay leaves, cinnamon, ginger slices, green onion, and dried sea pepper.
  6. Heat cooking oil in a wok or large pan.
  7. Add the pork belly and stir-fry until the excess fat renders and the pork is caramelized. Reserve the rendered fat.
  8. Clean the wok and add a small amount of oil, then add sugar and stir-fry until caramelized.
  9. Add the pork belly back to the wok and coat it with the caramelized sugar. Cook over low heat to avoid burning.
  10. Add the aromatics (star anise, bay leaves, etc.) and stir-fry until fragrant.
  11. Add cooking wine to deglaze the pan.
  12. Add soy sauce and stir-fry until evenly colored.
  13. Add enough boiling water to cover the pork belly.
  14. Bring to a boil, skimming off any foam.
  15. Cover and simmer over low heat for 40 minutes.
  16. Add 1 teaspoon of salt and a handful of garlic.
  17. Simmer for another 10 minutes.
  18. Add the fried tofu and stir to coat.
  19. Simmer for another 2 minutes until the tofu has absorbed the sauce.
  20. Garnish with chopped green onions before serving.

braised_pork_feet.txt - Braised Pork Feet (红烧猪蹄)

Objectives

  • Learn how to properly clean and prepare pig feet for braising.
  • Master a flavorful braising technique for tender, delicious pork feet.
  • Achieve a rich, savory sauce to complement the braised pork feet.

Ingredients

  • 1.5 catties (approximately 750g) of pig feet, chopped
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • Flour (amount unspecified)
  • Spring onions (amount unspecified)
  • Ginger (amount unspecified)
  • Cooking wine (amount unspecified)
  • Cooking oil (amount unspecified)
  • Ginger (amount unspecified)
  • Scallions (amount unspecified)
  • Star anise (amount unspecified)
  • Cinnamon (amount unspecified)
  • Dried chili peppers (amount unspecified)
  • Rock sugar (optional, amount unspecified)
  • 1 tablespoon light soy sauce
  • Dark soy sauce (amount unspecified)
  • Oyster sauce (amount unspecified)
  • 1 can (~330ml) of beer
  • 1 bowl of water
  • Green and red peppers (optional, amount unspecified)
  • Garlic shoots (optional, amount unspecified)

Instructions

  1. Clean the Pig Feet: Place chopped pig feet in a casserole dish. Add salt and flour, mix well to absorb blood and impurities. Rinse thoroughly under running water until the water runs clear.
  2. Blanch the Pig Feet: Blanch pig feet in boiling water with spring onions, ginger, and cooking wine for 2 minutes. Skim off foam. Immediately rinse under cold water.
  3. Sauté Pig Skin: Heat cooking oil in a pan. Add pig feet skin-side down and sauté until fat renders and skin is slightly crispy.
  4. Add Aromatics and Seasonings: Add ginger, scallions, star anise, cinnamon, dried chili peppers, and optional rock sugar to the pan. Stir-fry briefly.
  5. Braising Liquid: Add light soy sauce, dark soy sauce, oyster sauce, beer, and water to the pan.
  6. Braise the Pig Feet: Bring to a boil, then reduce heat and simmer for 38 minutes with the lid on.
  7. Adjust and Thicken: Stir the braised pig feet. Remove spices. Add optional green and red peppers and garlic shoots. Increase heat to slightly thicken the sauce.
  8. Serve: Remove from heat and serve.

broccoli_stir_fry.txt - مقلي البروكلي باللحم المفروم

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious broccoli stir-fry.
  • Preserve the nutrients in broccoli through steaming instead of boiling.
  • Create a flavorful sauce that complements the broccoli and minced meat.
  • Prepare a quick and easy side dish perfect for entertaining guests.

Ingredients

  • 2 heads of broccoli
  • 2 tsp salt
  • 1 firm tomato
  • 100g lean minced meat
  • A few dried chilies
  • Small piece of ginger
  • A few cloves of garlic
  • Cooking oil
  • Sugar
  • Chicken bouillon
  • Light soy sauce
  • Water

Instructions

  1. Prepare a bowl of water with 2 tsp of salt.
  2. Wash and cut broccoli into small florets. Soak in salted water for 5 minutes.
  3. Dice the tomato.
  4. Mince the meat.
  5. Slice the dried chilies thinly (optional).
  6. Mince the ginger and garlic.
  7. Steam the broccoli for 1 minute until bright green.
  8. Heat oil in a pan or wok.
  9. Add minced meat and stir-fry until browned.
  10. Add minced garlic and ginger, then stir-fry.
  11. Add dried chilies (if using) and stir-fry.
  12. Add diced tomatoes and stir-fry until softened.
  13. Add the steamed broccoli, salt, sugar, chicken bouillon, and light soy sauce.
  14. Add enough water to create a sauce.
  15. Stir-fry over high heat for 1 minute, or until sauce thickens.
  16. Drizzle with oil before serving.

cabbage_casserole.txt - Cabbage Casserole

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and heartwarming Cabbage Casserole.
  • Master the technique of frying tofu to golden perfection.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients for a budget-friendly meal.

Ingredients

  • 1 head of Chinese cabbage (approximately 2 yuan)
  • 1 dollar worth of pork belly, thinly sliced
  • Ample garlic, minced
  • Dried sea peppers, finely chopped
  • Some old tofu, cut into rectangular pieces
  • Cooking oil
  • Salt
  • Chicken essence
  • Light soy sauce
  • Oyster sauce
  • Dark soy sauce
  • Minced garlic sprouts (for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Cut the Chinese cabbage stalks, then split the cabbage in half lengthwise.
  2. Use a diagonal knife to cut the cabbage into small pieces (about 5 cm long).
  3. Wash the cabbage thoroughly. Separate the cabbage leaves and clappers.
  4. Prepare the pork belly by thinly slicing it and setting aside.
  5. Mince the garlic and set aside.
  6. Finely chop the dried sea peppers and set aside.
  7. Cut the garlic sprouts into slices and set aside.
  8. Cut the old tofu into rectangular pieces.
  9. Heat a wok or pan with cooking oil until slightly smoking.
  10. Fry the tofu pieces until golden brown on both sides, ensuring they are set before flipping.
  11. Spread the fried tofu evenly in a casserole dish. You can optionally add some onions to the bottom.
  12. In the same wok, stir-fry the pork belly until slightly yellow.
  13. Add the minced garlic and stir-fry for 30 seconds.
  14. Add the dried sea peppers and stir-fry briefly.
  15. Add the cabbage clappers and stir-fry over high heat for about a minute.
  16. Reduce heat to low, season with salt, chicken essence, light soy sauce, and oyster sauce.
  17. Increase heat to high, stir in dark soy sauce for color.
  18. Add the cabbage leaves and stir-fry until well combined.
  19. Pour the cabbage mixture over the tofu in the casserole dish.
  20. Reduce heat to low and simmer for 1-2 minutes, allowing the sauce to be absorbed.
  21. Add the minced garlic sprouts.
  22. Serve hot.

cabbage_egg.txt - Cabbage Stir-fry with Egg

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy cabbage stir-fry with egg.
  • Master the technique of keeping cabbage crisp and preventing excess water.
  • Create a flavorful dish that's perfect for families.

Ingredients

  • 2 Chicken Heart Cabbages (小白菜)
  • 1 teaspoon Salt (盐)
  • Water (清水)
  • 1 Carrot (胡萝卜), julienned
  • 3 Eggs (鸡蛋)
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒), finely sliced (optional)
  • Several cloves garlic (蒜), minced
  • 2 scallions (小葱), chopped
  • Cooking oil (食用油)
  • 1 tbsp Salt (盐)
  • 1 tbsp Chicken bouillon (鸡精)
  • Appropriate amount Oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • Small amount Soy sauce (生抽)

Instructions

  1. Wash the cabbages thoroughly with salted water to remove pesticides and maintain freshness. Drain well.
  2. Cut the cabbages in half, remove the hard core, and slice into thin strips.
  3. Add 1 tbsp salt to the cabbage, mix well, and let it marinate for 10 minutes to soften and release moisture.
  4. Wash the marinated cabbage again to remove excess salt, then squeeze out excess water. Set aside.
  5. Peel and julienne the carrot. Set aside.
  6. Whisk 3 eggs in a bowl until well combined. Set aside.
  7. Finely slice the chili peppers (optional) and mince the garlic. Chop the scallions. Set aside.
  8. Heat oil in a wok or frying pan. Add the whisked eggs and quickly stir-fry until cooked. Remove and set aside.
  9. Add the cabbage to the wok and stir-fry over high heat for 1 minute to remove excess moisture. Remove and set aside.
  10. Add more oil to the wok, add garlic and chili peppers (if using), and stir-fry until fragrant.
  11. Add the carrots and stir-fry until softened.
  12. Add the cabbage and eggs back to the wok.
  13. Season with 1 tbsp salt, 1 tbsp chicken bouillon, an appropriate amount of oyster sauce, and a small amount of soy sauce.
  14. Stir-fry everything together over high heat for 1 minute until well combined and heated through.
  15. Garnish with chopped scallions and serve immediately.

cabbage_onion_cake.txt - Cabbage and Onion Cake 包菜洋葱饼

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious cabbage and onion cake.
  • Master a simple and easy-to-follow recipe.
  • Create a flavorful dish suitable for the whole family.

Ingredients

  • 1 whole cabbage
  • 1/2 onion
  • 瘦肉 (lean pork, amount unspecified)
  • 10 RMB worth of fresh shrimp (虾仁, amount unspecified)
  • 1 egg (土鸡蛋)
  • 小勺毛毛盐 (a small spoonful of salt)
  • 少许鸡精 (a pinch of chicken bouillon)
  • 少许胡椒粉 (a pinch of pepper)
  • 50g 面粉 (50g all-purpose flour)
  • 黑芝麻 (black sesame seeds, amount unspecified)
  • 食用油 (cooking oil, amount unspecified)

Instructions

  1. Cut the cabbage in half, remove the core, and separate the leaves.
  2. Soak the cabbage leaves in salted water for 5 minutes, then rinse thoroughly.
  3. Cut the cabbage into small pieces.
  4. Cut half an onion into small pieces.
  5. Cut the lean pork into small pieces.
  6. Thaw the shrimp, peel and devein them, and score the backs for better flavor absorption.
  7. Combine the cabbage, onion, pork, shrimp, egg, salt, chicken bouillon, and pepper in a bowl. Mix well.
  8. Add 50g of flour and mix until a slightly sticky batter forms.
  9. Heat some oil in an electric griddle.
  10. Make small patties from the batter and place them on the griddle.
  11. Sprinkle black sesame seeds on top.
  12. Cook for 3 minutes per side, or until golden brown and crispy.
  13. Serve and enjoy!
