cabbage_rolls.txt - Cabbage Rolls ( الملفوف المحشي)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and nutritious cabbage rolls.
  • Master the technique of preparing and stuffing cabbage leaves.
  • Create a flavorful and visually appealing dish suitable for entertaining guests.

Ingredients

  • 1 whole Chinese cabbage (also called Maobai cai) - 白菜 (báicài)
  • 1 teaspoon salt - 盐 (yán)
  • 10-20 fresh shrimp, peeled and deveined - 虾 (xiā)
  • 3 fatty pork, 7 lean pork - 肥肉 (féiròu), 瘦肉 (shòuròu)
  • Lotus root (optional) - 莲藕 (lián ǒu)
  • Water chestnuts (optional) - 荸荠 (bíqí)
  • Ginger - 姜 (jiāng)
  • 1 teaspoon salt - 盐 (yán)
  • Pepper - 胡椒 (hújiāo)
  • Light soy sauce - 生抽 (shēng chōu)
  • 1 teaspoon soy sauce for coloring - 老抽 (lǎo chōu)
  • 1 egg - 鸡蛋 (jīdàn)
  • Green onions - 葱 (cōng)
  • Sesame oil - 芝麻油 (zhīma yóu)
  • 10 grams of water - 水 (shuǐ)

Instructions

  1. Separate and blanch the cabbage leaves: Boil water with a teaspoon of salt. Blanch the cabbage leaves for 20 seconds, then immediately plunge them into ice water.
  2. Prepare the shrimp: Peel and devein the shrimp. Cut them along the back and remove the black veins. Season with salt and sugar, and set aside.
  3. Prepare the meat filling: Finely chop or mince the pork. Combine with chopped lotus root or water chestnuts (optional), ginger, salt, pepper, light soy sauce, dark soy sauce, egg, green onions, sesame oil, and water. Mix thoroughly until sticky.
  4. Prepare the filling: Add chopped green onions and ginger to the meat filling.
  5. Prepare the cabbage leaves: Remove the core from the cabbage leaves.
  6. Assemble the rolls: Place a spoonful of the meat filling onto a cabbage leaf. Roll the leaf tightly, tucking in the sides.
  7. Steam the rolls: Arrange the rolls in a steamer basket. Steam over high heat for 8 minutes.
  8. Make the sauce: Add the excess liquid from steaming to a pan, bring to a boil, and thicken into a sauce.
  9. Finish the dish: Pour the sauce over the cabbage rolls. Garnish with chopped green onions and ginger. Drizzle with hot oil to enhance the aroma.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=fGhMGnDRXhY

cabbage_roll.txt - Cabbage Roll ( الملفوف المحشي)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and nutritious cabbage rolls.
  • Master the technique of preparing and stuffing cabbage leaves.
  • Create a flavorful broth to complement the cabbage rolls.

Ingredients

  • 1 whole Chinese cabbage ( الملفوف الصيني ) (also called Mao Bai Cai (ماو بايكاي))
  • 1 teaspoon table salt (ملعقة صغيرة من ملح الطعام)
  • Several dozen fresh shrimp (عشرات من الروبيان الطازج)
  • 3 fatty and 7 lean meat pieces (ثلاث لحوم دهنية وسبعة لحوم خالية من الدهون)
  • Chopped lotus root (جذر اللوتس المفروم) or water chestnuts (كستناء الماء المفروم) (optional)
  • 1 teaspoon salt (ملعقة صغيرة من ملح الطعام)
  • Pepper (فلفل)
  • Light soy sauce (صلصة الصويا الخفيفة)
  • 1 teaspoon soy sauce for coloring (ملعقة صغيرة من صلصة الصويا للتلوين)
  • 1 egg (بيضة دجاجة)
  • Green onions (بصل أخضر)
  • Sesame oil (زيت السمسم المطحون)
  • 10 grams of water (10 جرامًا من الماء)
  • Thin broth (مرق رقيق)

Instructions

  1. Blanch cabbage leaves: Boil water with 1 teaspoon of salt. Blanch the cabbage leaves (root side down) for 10 seconds, then blanch the leaves for 20 seconds until tender. Immediately transfer to cold water.
  2. Prepare shrimp: Peel and devein fresh shrimp. Season with salt and sugar.
  3. Prepare meat filling: Mince 3 fatty and 7 lean meat pieces (or use a meat grinder). Add chopped lotus root or water chestnuts, ginger, 1 teaspoon salt, pepper, light soy sauce, 1 teaspoon soy sauce for coloring, 1 egg, green onions, sesame oil, and 10 grams of water. Mix well in one direction until the meat is sticky.
  4. Prepare garnish: Slice green onions and ginger, and soak in water.
  5. Assemble cabbage rolls: Remove the core from the blanched cabbage leaves. Place a layer of meat filling on each leaf, top with shrimp, and roll tightly.
  6. Steam cabbage rolls: Steam the rolls in boiling water for 8 minutes over high heat. Turn off the heat and remove the rolls.
  7. Make the broth: Pour the excess liquid from steaming into a pot. Add thin broth and simmer until thickened.
  8. Serve: Pour the thickened broth over the cabbage rolls. Garnish with sliced green onions and ginger. Drizzle with hot oil to enhance aroma.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=fGhMGnDRXhY

cabbage_salad.txt - 爽口白菜丝

Objectives

  • Learn to make a quick and delicious cabbage salad.
  • Master the technique of cutting cabbage for optimal texture.
  • Understand the role of marinating and seasoning in enhancing flavor.

Ingredients

  • 2 small cabbages
  • Salt (less than usual for cooking)
  • A pinch of white sugar
  • 1 bunch of scallions, chopped
  • 1 piece of ginger, minced
  • Several cloves of garlic, minced
  • 1 green chili pepper, sliced
  • 1 red chili pepper, sliced
  • A little chili powder
  • A little white sesame seeds
  • Several peppercorns
  • White sugar
  • Rice vinegar (preferably)
  • A little light soy sauce
  • Oyster sauce
  • A little chicken bouillon
  • Hot oil

Instructions

  1. Remove the outer leaves and root end of the cabbages. Wash thoroughly, paying attention to the slimy layer on the cabbage stalks.
  2. Cut the cabbages into thin, even strips lengthwise, following the grain of the leaves.
  3. Place the cut cabbage in a bowl, add a little less salt than usual for cooking, and a pinch of white sugar. Mix well and let marinate for about 10 minutes.
  4. While the cabbage marinates, prepare the other ingredients: mince the scallions, ginger, and garlic; slice the chili peppers.
  5. After 10 minutes, rinse the marinated cabbage to remove excess salt. Drain well.
  6. Add the sliced chili peppers, minced scallions, ginger, and garlic to the cabbage.
  7. Sprinkle with chili powder, white sesame seeds, and peppercorns.
  8. Add white sugar, rice vinegar, a little light soy sauce, oyster sauce, and chicken bouillon. Mix well.
  9. Pour hot oil over the salad and toss to combine.

cabbage_soup.txt - Cabbage Soup

Objectives

  • Learn a simple, healthy way to prepare cabbage.
  • Understand the health benefits of consuming cabbage.
  • Master a quick and easy cabbage cooking method.

Ingredients

  • Cabbage (amount not specified, but enough for a large pot)
  • Salt (to taste)
  • Water (enough to cover cabbage leaves)
  • Ginger (one piece, thinly sliced)
  • Sichuan peppercorns (a few, for aroma)

Instructions

  1. Wash and prepare the cabbage: Cut half a cabbage into large pieces. Rinse thoroughly in salted water to remove any impurities. Drain well.
  2. Prepare aromatics: Thinly slice a piece of ginger and set aside. Prepare a few Sichuan peppercorns.
  3. Boil the cabbage: Add the prepared cabbage leaves to a large pot of boiling water. Cover and cook over high heat for 15 minutes.
  4. Season and serve: After 15 minutes, the cabbage will be tender. Season with salt to taste. Serve hot.

cabbage_tofu_stew.txt - 白菜豆腐煲

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy cabbage and tofu stew.
  • Master the technique of pan-frying tofu to achieve a golden-brown crust.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to enhance the taste of the stew.

Ingredients

  • 3 blocks of tofu (approximately 2 RMB)
  • 3 eggs
  • A few cloves of garlic, sliced
  • 1 small piece of ginger, thinly sliced
  • A small handful of scallions, whites and greens separated
  • 2-3 chili peppers (线椒), sliced (optional; can substitute with小米椒 for spicier dish)
  • 1 small spoonful of salt
  • 1 small spoonful of sugar
  • 2 small spoonfuls of yellow bean sauce (黄豆酱)
  • Appropriate amount of soy sauce (生抽)
  • ½ bowl of water
  • A small amount of sesame oil (香油)
  • Cabbage leaves (amount not specified)

Instructions

  1. Cut the tofu into triangular slices and place in a bowl.
  2. Crack the eggs into a bowl and whisk until smooth and frothy.
  3. Pour the egg mixture over the tofu, ensuring each piece is coated.
  4. Heat a small amount of oil in a pan.
  5. Add the tofu to the hot pan and gently shake the pan to prevent sticking.
  6. Fry the tofu for about a minute per side, until golden brown and crispy.
  7. Set aside the fried tofu.
  8. Prepare the aromatics: slice the garlic, ginger, and chili peppers; chop the scallions (separate whites and greens).
  9. Prepare the sauce: in a bowl, mix salt, sugar, yellow bean sauce, soy sauce, and water until well combined.
  10. Heat a small amount of sesame oil in a sand pot (砂锅).
  11. Add the garlic, ginger, and chili peppers, and sauté until fragrant.
  12. Add the cabbage leaves and arrange them in the pot.
  13. Place the fried tofu on top of the cabbage.
  14. Pour the prepared sauce over the tofu and cabbage.
  15. Cover the pot and simmer for 5 minutes.
  16. After 5 minutes, remove the lid, sprinkle with chopped scallions, and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=0cFAJMYZcg0

cabbage_tofu_vermicelli_stew.txt - Cabbage and Tofu Vermicelli Stew

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and warming Cabbage and Tofu Vermicelli Stew.
  • Master the technique of preparing the ingredients and cooking the stew.
  • Understand how to balance flavors and achieve a satisfying taste.

Ingredients

  • Sweet potato powder (amount not specified)
  • Hot water (amount not specified)
  • Pork belly or fatty meat (amount not specified)
  • 1 large head of cabbage
  • Soft tofu (amount not specified)
  • Ginger (1 piece)
  • Garlic (a handful)
  • Green onions (amount not specified)
  • Star anise (amount not specified)
  • Dried chili peppers (optional, a handful)
  • Vermicelli noodles (amount not specified)
  • Dark soy sauce (amount not specified)
  • Soy sauce (amount not specified)
  • Rapeseed oil (small amount)
  • Salt (small amount)
  • Cooking wine (amount not specified)
  • Oyster sauce (amount not specified)

Instructions

  1. Prepare sweet potato powder by mixing it with hot water. Let it soak if time permits.
  2. Cut pork belly into pieces. Set aside.
  3. Clean and chop the cabbage, separating the stalks and leaves. Chop the stalks and roughly tear the leaves. Set aside.
  4. Cut the tofu into small squares. Set aside.
  5. Thinly slice the ginger, mince the garlic, and chop the green onions. Set aside.
  6. Prepare the star anise and dried chilies (optional). Set aside.
  7. Cook vermicelli noodles in boiling water until tender, then drain. Toss with dark soy sauce and soy sauce to color and season. Set aside.
  8. Heat rapeseed oil in a wok or pan. Add tofu and fry until golden brown on all sides, season with salt. Set aside.
  9. Add pork belly to the wok and stir-fry until slightly browned, releasing excess fat.
  10. Add ginger, garlic, and chili (if using) and stir-fry until fragrant.
  11. Add cooking wine to deglaze the pan, followed by dark soy sauce and oyster sauce. Stir-fry until the sauce thickens.
  12. Add cabbage stalks and stir-fry until softened.
  13. Add cabbage leaves and stir-fry until wilted.
  14. Add boiling water, salt, and light soy sauce to the wok.
  15. Add the fried tofu and vermicelli. Stir to combine.
  16. Cover the wok and simmer over medium heat for 6-8 minutes.
  17. Garnish with green onions before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=e99E4q89rG4

cabbage_vegetarian_dumplings.txt - Cabbage Vegetarian Dumplings

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and soft cabbage vegetarian dumplings.
  • Master the dumpling dough and filling preparation techniques.
  • Cook perfect dumplings with thin wrappers and juicy fillings.

Ingredients

  • 300 grams all-purpose flour
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • Hot water (amount as needed)
  • 500 grams Chinese cabbage
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • Green onions (amount as needed)
  • Ginger (amount as needed)
  • Carrots (amount as needed)
  • Cilantro (amount as needed)
  • 1 star anise
  • A small piece of cinnamon
  • 1 bay leaf
  • Cooking oil
  • 2 tablespoons sesame paste
  • 1 tablespoon thirteen-spice powder (or five-spice powder)
  • 1 teaspoon pepper
  • Salt (to taste)
  • Oyster sauce (amount as needed)
  • Sesame oil (amount as needed)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Dough: Add 300 grams of flour and 1 teaspoon of salt to a bowl. Gradually add hot water while mixing with chopsticks until a soft, firm dough forms. Knead until smooth and elastic. Cover with a damp cloth.
  2. Prepare the Cabbage: Chop 500 grams of Chinese cabbage into small pieces. Add 1 tablespoon of salt, mix well, and set aside to release moisture. Squeeze out excess water using a cheesecloth.
  3. Prepare the Aromatics: Thinly slice green onions, ginger, and carrots. Chop cilantro.
  4. Prepare the Flavor Base: Heat oil in a pan. Add star anise, cinnamon, and bay leaf; sauté until fragrant. Add ginger, carrots, and green onions; stir-fry until moisture evaporates. Add cilantro and continue stir-frying until slightly browned. Remove from heat.
  5. Prepare the Sesame Paste: Add 2 tablespoons of sesame paste to the stir-fried mixture and mix well. Set aside.
  6. Prepare the Filling: Combine the squeezed cabbage, green onions, thirteen-spice powder (or five-spice powder), pepper, salt, oyster sauce, and sesame oil with the sesame paste mixture. Mix thoroughly. Set aside.
  7. Prepare the Dumpling Wrappers: Roll out the dough into small balls, then roll each ball into thin circles using a rolling pin (thicker in the middle, thinner at the edges).
  8. Assemble the Dumplings: Place a spoonful of filling in the center of each wrapper. Fold over and pinch the edges to seal tightly.
  9. Cook the Dumplings: Bring water to a boil in a pot. Add the dumplings one by one. Gently shake the pot to prevent sticking. Cook for about 30 seconds, then add a little more water. Repeat this process twice. Cook until the dumplings float to the surface and the wrappers are cooked through.
  10. Serve: Remove the dumplings with a slotted spoon. Serve on a plate, garnished with chopped green onions.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=xr6qmWXTi4g

carrot_egg_custard.txt - Carrot and Egg Custard

Objectives

  • Learn a new way to cook carrots.
  • Make a delicious and visually appealing carrot and egg custard.
  • Master a simple steaming technique for a perfect custard texture.

Ingredients

  • 2 carrots, peeled and julienned
  • 5 eggs
  • 1 small bunch of scallions, chopped
  • 1 tbsp cornstarch
  • A little water
  • Salt
  • 1 tsp Song Rong Xian (松茸鲜 - a type of mushroom seasoning)
  • Pepper
  • Vegetable oil
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce
  • More than 1 tbsp rice vinegar
  • Optional: Chili oil
  • Sesame seeds
  • Dried chilies, chopped
  • Garlic, minced

Instructions

  1. Peel and julienne the carrots.
  2. Boil water in a pot, add salt, and blanch the carrots for 45 seconds.
  3. Drain the carrots and rinse with cold water to cool.
  4. Squeeze out excess water from the carrots.
  5. Whisk 5 eggs in a large bowl.
  6. In a small bowl, mix cornstarch and a little water until smooth.
  7. Add the cornstarch mixture to the eggs and whisk until well combined.
  8. Add the carrots, scallions, salt, Song Rong Xian, and pepper to the egg mixture. Whisk thoroughly for about 1 minute.
  9. Lightly oil a small square baking dish or line it with parchment paper.
  10. Pour the egg mixture into the prepared dish.
  11. Use chopsticks to remove air bubbles.
  12. Cover the dish with heat-resistant plastic wrap and pierce a few holes with a toothpick.
  13. Steam over high heat for 10 minutes.
  14. While the custard steams, prepare the sauce: chop dried chilies, mince garlic, and chop scallions.
  15. Heat oil in a pan until slightly smoking.
  16. Pour the hot oil over the chilies, garlic, and scallions.
  17. Add soy sauce, rice vinegar, and optional chili oil. Stir well.
  18. After 10 minutes, turn off the heat and let the custard cool slightly.
  19. Remove the plastic wrap.
  20. Loosen the custard from the edges with a spatula.
  21. Invert the custard onto a cutting board.
  22. Remove the parchment paper (if used).
  23. Cut the custard into small squares.
  24. Serve the custard with the prepared sauce and sesame seeds.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=84Fu6Mj_2Ec

carrot_egg.txt - 凉拌胡萝卜鸡蛋

Objectives

  • Learn a new way to prepare carrots and eggs.
  • Create a refreshing and flavorful cold dish.
  • Make a simple yet delicious side dish perfect for hot weather.

Ingredients

  • 1 large carrot, peeled and cut into thin diamond shapes
  • 2 eggs
  • ½ head of Napa cabbage, thinly sliced
  • Several cloves garlic, minced
  • Several dried chilies, finely chopped (or to taste, can substitute with小米辣)
  • Sesame seeds
  • 1 tablespoon soy sauce (生抽)
  • Homemade chili oil (油泼辣子)
  • Pinch of salt (毛毛盐)
  • Chicken bouillon (鸡精)
  • A dash of rice vinegar (陈醋)
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Prepare the carrots: Peel, wash, and cut a large carrot into thin diamond-shaped slices. Set aside.
  2. Prepare the eggs: Crack two eggs into a bowl, whisk until well combined and frothy. Heat a pan with oil, pour in the egg mixture and cook until set on both sides. Slice into diamond shapes. Set aside.
  3. Prepare the cabbage: Thinly slice half a head of Napa cabbage. Rinse thoroughly with water and drain well.
  4. Prepare the sauce: Mince several cloves of garlic and finely chop several dried chilies (or小米辣). Combine garlic, chilies, sesame seeds, soy sauce, chili oil, a pinch of salt, chicken bouillon, and rice vinegar in a small bowl. Mix well.
  5. Blanch vegetables: Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add a spoonful of salt, then add the carrots and blanch for 1 minute. Add the cabbage and blanch for 49 seconds. Immediately remove and plunge into ice water to cool. Drain well and squeeze out excess water.
  6. Combine ingredients: In a large bowl, combine the blanched carrots and cabbage, the sliced cooked eggs, and the prepared sauce. Mix thoroughly.
  7. Serve: Transfer to a serving dish and enjoy.

cauliflower_recipe.txt - Cauliflower Recipe

Objectives

  • Learn a simple, quick cauliflower cooking method.
  • Prepare flavorful cauliflower without deep frying.
  • Create a nutritious and delicious cauliflower dish suitable for all ages.

Ingredients

  • 1 medium cauliflower (approx. 3.50 yuan)
  • 1 small teaspoon salt
  • Water (for soaking and blanching)
  • Several cloves garlic, minced
  • Small section green onions (or scallions), finely diced
  • 1 small teaspoon salt (for sauce)
  • A pinch of sugar
  • 1 small teaspoon fresh matsutake mushroom (or substitute)
  • Soy oyster sauce (amount unspecified)
  • Water (for sauce)
  • 1 tablespoon cornstarch
  • Cooking oil (amount unspecified)
  • 3 tablespoons shrimp shells (optional)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Cauliflower: Remove leaves from cauliflower. Cut into small, even-sized florets using scissors.
  2. Soak the Cauliflower: Place cauliflower florets in a bowl. Add a small teaspoon of salt and enough water to cover. Soak for 10 minutes to remove insects and dirt. Stir well.
  3. Prepare Aromatics: Mince garlic and finely dice green onions (or scallions). Set aside.
  4. Rinse Cauliflower: Rinse the soaked cauliflower twice with clean water. Drain well.
  5. Prepare Sauce: In a bowl, combine a small teaspoon of salt, a pinch of sugar, a small teaspoon of fresh matsutake mushroom (or substitute), soy oyster sauce, and water. Mix until dissolved. Add cornstarch and stir until smooth. No lumps should remain.
  6. Blanch Cauliflower: Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add a tablespoon of salt and some oil. Add the cauliflower and blanch for 2 minutes (or 3 minutes for softer texture). Remove with a slotted spoon and drain well.
  7. Sauté Aromatics: Heat oil in a pan or wok over medium-low heat. Add minced garlic and sauté until fragrant.
  8. Add Shrimp Shells (Optional): Add 3 tablespoons of shrimp shells and stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Add Sauce and Cauliflower: Add a little water to the pan, bring to a boil, then add the prepared sauce. Stir until thickened. Add the blanched cauliflower and stir to coat.
  10. Serve: Turn off heat. Garnish with diced green onions. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=mv-MXNs-EYY

cauliflower_restaurant_style.txt - Restaurant-Style Cauliflower

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare fresh, tender cauliflower with a restaurant-like taste.
  • Master a simple method to remove impurities and enhance cauliflower's color.
  • Create a flavorful cauliflower dish using readily available ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 1 head of fresh cauliflower
  • 1 tsp salt
  • 2 g baking soda
  • Plenty of spring water
  • Several shiitake mushrooms
  • Plenty of garlic cloves
  • 1 piece of peeled ginger
  • Several scallions
  • Several dried chilies
  • 2 slices of pork belly
  • Cooking oil
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce
  • Oyster sauce
  • A pinch of salt
  • A pinch of sugar
  • A little bit of mushroom seasoning

Instructions

  1. Select a fresh cauliflower with vibrant green stalks.
  2. Break the cauliflower into florets, discarding the tough stem.
  3. Place florets in a large bowl.
  4. Add 1 tsp salt, 2 g baking soda, and enough spring water to submerge the cauliflower.
  5. Soak for 5 minutes, then rinse thoroughly until the water runs clear.
  6. Drain well.
  7. Prepare the ingredients: slice shiitake mushrooms, mince garlic and ginger, chop scallions and dried chilies, and thinly slice pork belly.
  8. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add 1 tbsp salt and some cooking oil.
  9. Blanch the cauliflower for 60 seconds, then add the shiitake mushrooms and blanch for another 30 seconds.
  10. Immediately remove and rinse with cold water to maintain crispness. Drain well.
  11. Heat oil in a wok or pan. Add the pork belly and stir-fry until lightly browned.
  12. Add minced ginger and garlic and stir-fry until fragrant.
  13. Add soy sauce for color and dried chilies for flavor. Stir-fry briefly.
  14. Add the blanched cauliflower and shiitake mushrooms. Stir-fry until well combined.
  15. Season with 1 tbsp soy sauce, oyster sauce, a pinch of salt, a pinch of sugar, and a little mushroom seasoning. Stir-fry to combine.
  16. Continue stir-frying until the cauliflower is tender-crisp and well coated with the sauce.
  17. Add chopped scallions and stir-fry briefly.
  18. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=PvhqUT4NxQI

cauliflower_stir_fry.txt - مقلي القرنبيط

Objectives

  • Learn a method for stir-frying cauliflower that preserves nutrients.
  • Create a crispy, flavorful cauliflower dish suitable for families.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients for an economical and delicious meal.

Ingredients

  • 2 heads of cauliflower (approximately 4 yuan)
  • 1 carrot, peeled and diced into diamond shapes
  • 1/2 cup of soaked black fungus
  • 1 piece of fatty pork belly, sliced
  • Optional: Lean meat, cut into pieces
  • 1/2 large red chili pepper, thinly sliced into diamond shapes
  • 1 small onion, finely chopped
  • Ginger and garlic, minced
  • Salt
  • Baking soda
  • White sugar
  • Oyster sauce
  • Light soy sauce
  • Vegetable oil (if not using pork belly fat)

Instructions

  1. Cut the cauliflower into small florets using scissors (to prevent flowerets from falling off).
  2. Place cauliflower in a large bowl. Add salt and baking soda. Mix well and let it soak for 5 minutes.
  3. Rinse the cauliflower thoroughly twice with clean water.
  4. Prepare the carrot, black fungus, pork belly (and optional lean meat), red chili pepper, and onion. Dice or slice ingredients as specified above.
  5. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add the cauliflower, carrot, and black fungus. Cover and steam for 3 minutes.
  6. In a separate wok or pan, add the pork belly and cook until the fat renders and the pork is browned. Remove from pan.
  7. Add onion, ginger, and garlic to the pan and stir-fry briefly.
  8. Add the lean meat (if using) and stir-fry until the color changes.
  9. Add the steamed cauliflower to the pan. Stir to combine.
  10. Season with salt, a small amount of sugar, oyster sauce, and light soy sauce. Stir well to combine.
  11. Add the red chili pepper and stir-fry for 1 minute.
  12. Continue stirring until all ingredients are well coated and heated through.
  13. Remove from heat and serve.

celery_tofu_egg_drop_soup.txt - Celery Leaf Tofu Egg Drop Soup 芹菜豆腐鸡蛋汤

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious, low-calorie, and low-fat soup.
  • Utilize celery leaves effectively in cooking.
  • Prepare a simple yet nutritious meal for weight loss.
  • Learn how to properly clean celery leaves to remove pesticides.
  • Make a soup that's both tasty and healthy.
  • Understand the benefits of tofu and tomatoes in a weight loss diet.

Ingredients

  • A small handful of celery leaves (芹菜叶 qín cài yè)
  • 2 teaspoons baking soda (小苏打 xiǎo sū dǎ)
  • 50-cent block of firm tofu (半块豆腐 bàn kuài dòufu)
  • 1 tomato (一个番茄 yīgè fánqié)
  • 2 eggs (两个鸡蛋 liǎng gè jīdàn)
  • 10 grams of oil (10克油 10 kè yóu)
  • Salt (盐 yán)
  • Pepper (胡椒粉 hú jiāo fěn)
  • Boiling water (开水 kāishuǐ)

Instructions

  1. Pick celery leaves and wash thoroughly. Soak in water with baking soda for 10 minutes to remove pesticides, then rinse again until the water runs clear. Dry and chop.
  2. Cut the tofu into small cubes. Soak in salted boiling water to remove excess soy flavor and firm the texture. Drain well.
  3. Dice the tomato into small cubes.
  4. Crack two eggs into a bowl and whisk lightly.
  5. Heat 10 grams of oil in a pan. Sauté diced tomatoes with a pinch of salt until softened.
  6. Add boiling water to the pan to create a tomato broth. Bring to a boil.
  7. Add the blanched tofu to the boiling broth and stir. Cover and simmer for 2-3 minutes.
  8. Turn off the heat. Pour the egg mixture slowly along the side of the pan, gently swirling the pan to create egg ribbons.
  9. Add the chopped celery leaves and stir. Cook for 15 seconds.
  10. Season with pepper to taste.
  11. Serve the soup hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=zDh6QLBtk5k

chestnut_roasted_chicken.txt - Chestnut Roasted Chicken

Objectives

  • Prepare a delicious and seasonal chestnut roasted chicken dish.
  • Learn to perfectly roast chicken, achieving a tender and flavorful result.
  • Master the preparation of chestnuts, including peeling and cooking techniques.

Ingredients

  • Chestnuts (amount unspecified, but enough to fill the dish)
  • 1/2 a chicken (cut into pieces)
  • Salt (amount unspecified)
  • Flour (amount unspecified)
  • Water (amount unspecified)
  • Mushrooms (amount unspecified, cleaned and cut into small pieces)
  • 2 cloves garlic (cut into fourths)
  • Ginger (amount unspecified, finely chopped)
  • Rapeseed oil (amount unspecified)
  • Light soy sauce (amount unspecified)
  • Pepper (amount unspecified)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the chestnuts: Boil in water (101°C) for 2 minutes. Peel after boiling; they will be easier to peel.
  2. Prepare the chicken: Cut the chicken into small pieces. Place in a bowl, add salt and flour. Mix until the chicken is sticky. Add water, and rinse until the water runs clear.
  3. Prepare the aromatics: Clean and cut the mushrooms into small, triangular pieces. Chop the garlic and ginger finely.
  4. Heat rapeseed oil in an iron wok until it smokes. Add the chicken and stir-fry over high heat for about 5 minutes until browned.
  5. Add ginger and garlic, stir-fry for 15 seconds.
  6. Season with salt, light soy sauce, and pepper. Stir-fry evenly.
  7. Add another bowl of water, cover, and simmer over medium-low heat for 30 minutes.
  8. Uncover, add the peeled chestnuts and chopped mushrooms. Stir-fry evenly.
  9. Cover again, reduce heat, and simmer for 8 minutes.
  10. Increase heat to thicken the sauce.
  11. Serve hot, ideally with rice.

chicken_legs_recipe.txt - مقرمشة دجاج بالصلصة

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare crispy chicken legs with a flavorful sauce.
  • Understand the importance of blanching chicken legs for improved texture and appearance.
  • Master a simple yet aromatic sauce recipe.

Ingredients

  • عدد قليل من أرجل الدجاج الطازجة الكبيرة (A few large fresh chicken legs)
  • قطعة كبيرة من الزنجبيل (A large piece of ginger)
  • بصل أحمر (Red onion)
  • ثوم (Garlic)
  • بصل أخضر (Green onion)
  • كزبرة (Cilantro)
  • ملعقة من صلصة الصويا الداكنة (1 tablespoon dark soy sauce)
  • خل (Vinegar)
  • صلصة المحار (Oyster sauce)
  • ملح (Salt)

Instructions

  1. Blanch chicken legs in boiling water for a few minutes to tighten the skin and enhance flavor.
  2. Prepare the sauce ingredients: thinly slice ginger, finely chop red onion, garlic, green onion, and cilantro.
  3. Combine chopped ingredients with dark soy sauce, vinegar, and oyster sauce in a bowl; set aside.
  4. Lightly fry the sauce ingredients until slightly browned. Add chopped green onions and cilantro; continue frying until fragrant.
  5. Remove the fried ingredients using a slotted spoon, reserving the fragrant oil. Add the reserved oil to the sauce mixture.
  6. Bring the sauce to a boil over high heat, stirring until thickened.
  7. Season the chicken legs with a handful of salt to clean and disinfect the skin.
  8. Place the chicken legs in a dish, top with ginger slices to remove fishy odor and enhance aroma.
  9. Steam the chicken legs until cooked through.
  10. Cut the cooked chicken legs into equal pieces.
  11. Arrange the chicken pieces on a plate and pour the prepared sauce over them.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=drxEt2O7iqU

chicken_nuggets.txt - 鸡米花 (Jī mǐ huā)

Objectives

  • Learn to make crispy, tender chicken nuggets at home.
  • Master a simple, easy-to-follow recipe.
  • Create a healthier alternative to store-bought nuggets.

Ingredients

  • Several pieces of fresh chicken breast (鲜艳粉嫩, 光泽度好)
  • 1 tbsp salt (食盐)
  • 2 packs of chicken nugget breading (炸鸡裹粉)
  • Chopped green onions (葱丝)
  • Chopped ginger (姜丝)
  • 1 tbsp cooking wine (料酒)
  • Some light soy sauce (生抽)
  • Some chicken juice (鸡汁)
  • Some salt (食盐)
  • Some black pepper (胡椒粉)
  • 1 tsp five-spice powder (五香粉)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)
  • Tomato ketchup (番茄酱) (optional)

Instructions

  1. Select fresh, pink chicken breasts with a good sheen.
  2. Dissolve 1 tbsp of salt in clean water.
  3. Soak chicken breasts in the saltwater for 5 minutes.
  4. Rinse the chicken and pat dry.
  5. Slice the chicken breasts in half lengthwise, then into strips, and finally into larger-sized chicken nuggets.
  6. Place the chicken nuggets in a large bowl.
  7. Add chopped green onions, ginger, 1 tbsp cooking wine, light soy sauce, chicken juice, salt, pepper, and 1 tsp five-spice powder.
  8. Mix thoroughly until the chicken is sticky.
  9. Marinate for 10 minutes.
  10. Prepare two packs of chicken nugget breading in a separate bowl.
  11. Add the marinated chicken to the breading and mix until fully coated.
  12. Remove the chicken nuggets with a slotted spoon, shaking off excess breading.
  13. Lightly coat the chicken with water.
  14. Dredge the chicken in breading again, shaking off excess. The chicken should have a scaly appearance.
  15. Heat a generous amount of cooking oil in a pan over medium-low heat (4-5成热).
  16. Add the chicken nuggets and fry for 30 seconds until lightly browned.
  17. Stir the chicken nuggets to prevent sticking and ensure even cooking.
  18. Continue frying until the chicken is golden brown.
  19. Remove the chicken nuggets and drain on a slotted spoon.
  20. Remove any residue from the oil with a fine-mesh strainer.
  21. Increase the oil temperature to 8成热.
  22. Return the chicken nuggets to the hot oil and fry for another 30 seconds.
  23. Remove the chicken nuggets, drain, and serve. Serve with tomato ketchup, if desired.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=k1OLlllXsk4

chicken_steam.txt - Steamed Chicken with Mushrooms and Potatoes

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare tender and flavorful steamed chicken.
  • Master a simple yet delicious recipe suitable for families.
  • Understand the importance of proper chicken preparation for optimal taste and texture.

Ingredients

  • 1 whole chicken (about 1.5 lbs), cut into small pieces
  • 1 tbsp salt
  • 1 tbsp flour
  • Water (enough to cover chicken)
  • A pinch of baking soda
  • A little cooking wine
  • Several pieces of ginger, smashed and minced
  • Several cloves of garlic, smashed and minced
  • Cooking oil
  • Pepper
  • 1 tbsp oyster sauce
  • 1 tbsp soybean paste (Huangdoujiang)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (light)
  • A dash of dark soy sauce (for color)
  • 1 potato, peeled and diced
  • Several fresh shiitake mushrooms, stems removed and scored
  • Green onions (for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Cut the chicken into small pieces.
  2. In a large bowl, toss the chicken with salt and flour, rubbing thoroughly to remove blood and impurities (about 2-3 minutes).
  3. Rinse the chicken thoroughly with water until the water runs clear. Repeat twice.
  4. Add baking soda and cooking wine to the chicken, mix well, and let stand for 2 minutes. Rinse again. Drain well.
  5. Prepare the ginger-garlic mixture: mince smashed ginger and garlic.
  6. Heat cooking oil until slightly smoking. Pour hot oil over the ginger-garlic mixture to release its aroma.
  7. Add pepper, oyster sauce, soybean paste, light soy sauce, dark soy sauce, and cooking wine to the ginger-garlic oil. Mix well. (No additional salt needed).
  8. Add the drained chicken to the bowl with the sauce and mix until evenly coated. Marinate for 20 minutes.
  9. Blanch the diced potatoes and scored shiitake mushrooms in boiling water with salt for about 1 minute. Rinse with cold water.
  10. Arrange the blanched mushrooms in the bottom of a large bowl.
  11. Place the marinated chicken evenly over the mushrooms.
  12. Pour the remaining marinade over the chicken.
  13. Steam in a covered steamer over high heat for 30 minutes.
  14. Garnish with green onions before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vl3LK2lCTV8

chicken_stew_noodles.txt - Chicken Stew with Noodles دجاج مطهو مع نودلز

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare tender, flavorful chicken without a gamey smell.
  • Master a simple yet delicious chicken stew recipe.
  • Create a comforting and hearty meal perfect for cold weather.

Ingredients

  • Half a local chicken
  • Salt (a handful)
  • Water (boiling)
  • Shiitake mushrooms (small amount, roughly chopped)
  • 1 large potato (peeled and cut into small pieces)
  • 1 fragrant leaf
  • 2 star anise
  • Small handful of peppercorns
  • Light soy sauce
  • Dark soy sauce
  • 1 tablespoon soybean paste
  • Pepper (to taste)
  • Cooking oil
  • Ginger slices
  • Chopped green onions
  • Pre-soaked noodles

Instructions

  1. Place the chicken in a large basin. Sprinkle a handful of salt on the surface and rub it into the chicken skin for 2 minutes. This washes away impurities and sweat glands.
  2. Rinse the chicken and pour boiling water over it to blanch. This makes the skin firmer and crispier.
  3. Clean the shiitake mushrooms, chop them into small pieces, and soak them in clean water.
  4. Cut the peeled potato into small, diagonally sliced pieces.
  5. Prepare the sauce: Mix light soy sauce, dark soy sauce, 1 tbsp soybean paste, and pepper in a bowl. Set aside.
  6. Heat cooking oil in a pot. Add the chicken and stir-fry over medium heat until browned.
  7. Add ginger slices and chopped green onions, then add the fragrant leaf, star anise, and peppercorns. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  8. Pour in the prepared sauce and stir until the color changes.
  9. Add the water used to soak the mushrooms. Bring to a boil, then add the soaked mushrooms and potatoes.
  10. Cover and simmer for 10 minutes.
  11. Add pre-soaked noodles to a large bowl.
  12. Pour the chicken stew over the noodles.
  13. Cover and simmer over low heat for 6-8 minutes.
  14. Garnish with chopped green onions and serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OmKOiK0Hf8M

chinese_braised_cabbage_with_tofu.txt - Chinese Braised Cabbage with Tofu

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious Chinese braised cabbage with tofu dish.
  • Understand the benefits of cabbage and tofu for health and digestion.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful recipe perfect for cold weather.

Ingredients

  • 1 head of Napa Cabbage
  • 1 block firm tofu
  • 1 green onion
  • 1 piece ginger
  • 2 cloves garlic
  • Shrimp peels (amount unspecified)
  • Oil (amount unspecified, lard suggested)
  • Water (amount unspecified)
  • Salt (amount unspecified)
  • Sugar (amount unspecified)
  • Pepper (amount unspecified)
  • Light soy sauce (amount unspecified)

Instructions

  1. Cut the Napa cabbage in half, then separate it into pieces. Use a knife to separate the roots and leaves. Wash thoroughly, soak in water, drain. Cut into slanted pieces.
  2. Cut the tofu into small pieces. Make small slits in the tofu to enhance flavor and tenderness during frying.
  3. Finely chop the green onion, ginger, and garlic. Mince the garlic for better aroma.
  4. Heat oil (or lard) in a pan. Add shrimp peels and fry until fragrant.
  5. Add chopped green onion, ginger, and garlic to the pan; stir-fry until softened.
  6. Add the cabbage pieces and stir-fry for about a minute.
  7. Add the tofu and stir-fry for about a minute until evenly heated.
  8. Season with salt, sugar, pepper, and light soy sauce. Stir to combine.
  9. Add water, cover, and simmer over low heat for 3-5 minutes until cabbage is tender.
  10. Garnish with a sprinkle of pepper and chopped green onion. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=xQP_HLvROSc

claypot_beef_stew_with_fermented_tofu.txt - Claypot Beef Stew with Fermented Tofu

Objectives

  • Learn to make a flavorful and tender claypot beef stew.
  • Master the technique of preparing the beef for maximum tenderness.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients to create a comforting and nutritious dish.

Ingredients

  • Dried yuba (tofu skin), cut into small pieces
  • 2 pink tomatoes, cross-cut, blanched
  • 7 taels (approximately 210g) beef sirloin, thinly sliced against the grain
  • 1 tsp grated ginger
  • 1 tsp salt
  • Appropriate amount of pepper
  • 1 tsp light soy sauce
  • Pinch of oyster sauce
  • 5g sweet potato starch
  • Water
  • Cooking oil
  • 1 white onion, chopped
  • Green onions, chopped
  • 2 small heads of ginger, minced
  • Several cloves of garlic, minced
  • 1 large red chili pepper, deseeded and sliced
  • 1 purple onion, thinly sliced
  • Fermented tofu (optional), blanched
  • ½ tbsp light soy sauce
  • Small bowl of water
  • 100g beer

Instructions

  1. Soak dried yuba in water for 30 minutes.
  2. Blanch tomatoes in boiling water for 3 minutes to easily remove skins. Peel and chop into chunks.
  3. Thinly slice beef against the grain.
  4. Marinate beef with ginger, salt, pepper, light soy sauce, oyster sauce, sweet potato starch, and water. Mix well until sticky.
  5. Chop white onion, green onions, ginger, garlic, and red chili pepper.
  6. Blanch fermented tofu for 1 minute, drain well.
  7. Heat cooking oil in a clay pot. Add tomatoes and salt, stir-fry until slightly caramelized (about 30 seconds).
  8. Add onion, ginger, garlic, and chopped green onions to the pot; stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Add blanched yuba, spreading evenly.
  10. Add marinated beef, spreading evenly.
  11. Add ½ tbsp light soy sauce and a small bowl of water.
  12. Bring to a boil, cover, and simmer for 3 minutes.
  13. Pour 100g of beer around the edges of the pot.
  14. Continue simmering until beef is tender.
  15. Garnish with sliced red chili pepper and chopped green onions.
  16. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QqYt0rb_Mbw

clear_soup_noodles.txt - Malinaw na Sopas na Pansit

Objectives

  • Prepare a nutritious and delicious noodle soup breakfast in 5 minutes.
  • Learn a simple, quick method for cooking noodles.
  • Master a flavorful soup base using readily available ingredients.

Ingredients

  • Green onions (tinadtad na berdeng sibuyas)
  • Cilantro (kulantro)
  • 1 tbsp Salt (asin)
  • ½ tbsp Matsutake mushrooms (sariwang matsutake mushroom)
  • 1 dash Pepper (paminta)
  • ½ tbsp Light soy sauce (light soy sauce)
  • 2 tbsp Lettuce and shrimp skin (litsugas at balat ng hipon)
  • Cooking oil (mantika)
  • Noodles (pansit)
  • Boiled eggs (nilagang itlog)

Instructions

  1. Finely chop green onions and cilantro. Set aside.
  2. Prepare the soup base: In a bowl, combine salt, matsutake mushrooms, pepper, light soy sauce, lettuce, shrimp skin, and cooking oil. Mix well.
  3. Heat a pot. Add a small amount of oil and heat until slightly smoking.
  4. Fry the boiled eggs until golden brown on both sides. Set aside.
  5. Add water to the pot and bring to a boil.
  6. Add noodles to the boiling water and stir quickly with chopsticks.
  7. Add another bowl of water to the pot, repeat twice for smoother noodles.
  8. Cook until noodles are tender but not mushy. Turn off heat.
  9. Pour the soup base into a bowl.
  10. Add the cooked noodles to the bowl and stir to combine.
  11. Top with fried eggs, green onions, and cilantro.
  12. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=amp03PE-USg

cold_cucumber.txt - Cold Cucumber

Objectives

  • Learn to make a refreshing cold cucumber dish.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful preparation method.
  • Achieve a crisp texture and vibrant green color in the cucumbers.

Ingredients

  • 2 long cucumbers (unpeeled)
  • 1/2 onion, finely chopped
  • Several cloves garlic, minced
  • A small handful of sea peppers (optional)
  • A few drops of sesame oil (optional)
  • 1/2 spoonful salt
  • 1/2 spoonful sugar
  • A dash of chicken essence
  • 1/2 spoonful soy sauce
  • 1/2 spoonful aged vinegar
  • Peanuts (optional)
  • Hot oil

Instructions

  1. Prepare the cucumbers: Wash cucumbers thoroughly. Rub with salt to remove surface residue. Rinse and pat dry. Trim the ends.
  2. Chop the aromatics: Finely chop half an onion and mince several garlic cloves. Set aside.
  3. Blanch the cucumbers: Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add the cucumbers and blanch for 30 seconds.
  4. Cool the cucumbers: Immediately transfer the blanched cucumbers to a bowl of ice water to stop the cooking process and maintain their vibrant green color. Soak completely until cool.
  5. Prepare the cucumbers for plating: Remove cucumbers from the ice bath, drain well and place on a plate. Score the cucumber skins with a knife to improve appearance.
  6. Season and toss: Add the chopped onion and minced garlic to the cucumbers. Add sea peppers and sesame oil (if using).
  7. Add the dressing: Heat some oil and pour it over the cucumbers. Add salt, sugar, chicken essence, soy sauce, and aged vinegar. Stir in peanuts (if using).
  8. Mix and serve: Using disposable gloves, gently toss the cucumbers and seasoning until well combined. Let sit briefly to allow flavors to meld. Serve chilled.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZjlPO9O22-k

cold_salad.txt - Cold Cabbage Salad

Objectives

  • Learn to make a refreshing and inexpensive cold cabbage salad.
  • Master simple techniques for preparing and blanching vegetables.
  • Create a flavorful and aromatic sauce for the salad.

Ingredients

  • 1 small Chinese cabbage (approx. 6-7 lbs), 白菜 (báicài)
  • 1 carrot, 胡萝卜 (húluóbo)
  • 1 yellow potato, 黄土豆 (huáng tǔdòu)
  • 3 millet peppers (optional), 小米椒 (xiǎomǐjiāo)
  • Several cloves garlic, 大蒜 (dàsuàn)
  • 1 tbsp sesame oil, 芝麻油 (zhīmayóu)
  • 1 tbsp chili powder, 辣椒粉 (làjiāofěn)
  • 1 tbsp light soy sauce, 生抽 (shēng chōu)
  • 1/2 tbsp vinegar, 醋 (cù)
  • Salt, 盐 (yán)
  • Mushroom powder, 蘑菇粉 (mógufěn)
  • Pepper oil, 花椒油 (huājiāoyóu)
  • White sesame seeds, 白芝麻 (bái zhīma)
  • Water, 水 (shuǐ)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the cabbage: Remove outer leaves, wash thoroughly to remove mucus, and cut into thin strips.
  2. Prepare the carrot: Peel, remove ends, slice thinly, then julienne.
  3. Prepare the potato: Peel, cut into thick slices, then julienne. Wash to remove excess starch.
  4. Prepare the aromatics: Mince garlic and thinly slice millet peppers (omit if you dislike spice).
  5. Make the sauce: In a bowl, combine sesame oil, chili powder, light soy sauce, vinegar, salt, mushroom powder, pepper oil, and white sesame seeds. Mix well.
  6. Blanch the vegetables: Boil water with a pinch of salt. Blanch carrots for 1 minute, potatoes for 30 seconds, and cabbage for 30 seconds. Immediately transfer blanched vegetables to a bowl of ice water to retain color and crispness.
  7. Drain and cool: After vegetables are completely cool, drain thoroughly, gently squeezing out excess water.
  8. Combine and mix: Add the sauce to the blanched vegetables. Wearing disposable gloves, gently toss to coat evenly.
  9. Marinate: Let the salad marinate for at least 1 minute to allow flavors to meld.
  10. Serve: Arrange the salad on a plate and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=df6dpIx5mmQ

cong_shao_doufu.txt - 葱烧豆腐 (Cōng Shāo Dòufu)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and flavorful Cōng Shāo Dòufu (葱烧豆腐).
  • Master the technique of frying tofu to achieve a golden-brown, crispy exterior.
  • Understand how to create a flavorful sauce that perfectly complements the tofu.

Ingredients

  • 老豆腐 (Lǎo Dòufu) - Firm Tofu: Amount not specified, but enough to be broken into irregular pieces.
  • 小葱 (Xiǎo Cōng) - Scallions: A few stalks.
  • 生抽 (Shēng Chōu) - Light Soy Sauce: 1 large spoonful
  • 老抽 (Lǎo Chōu) - Dark Soy Sauce: A tiny bit
  • 白糖 (Bái Táng) - White Sugar: Amount not specified
  • 食盐 (Shí Yán) - Salt: Amount not specified
  • 胡椒粉 (Hú Jiāo Fěn) - Pepper Powder: Amount not specified
  • 玉米淀粉 (Yù Mǐ Diàn Fěn) - Corn Starch: Amount not specified
  • 蚝油 (Háo Yóu) - Oyster Sauce: 1 small spoonful
  • 清水 (Qīng Shuǐ) - Water: 1 small spoonful
  • 食用油 (Shí Yòng Yóu) - Cooking Oil: Amount not specified

Instructions

  1. Break the firm tofu into irregular pieces. This helps the sauce adhere better.
  2. Cut the scallions into small segments, separating the white and green parts.
  3. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, mix light soy sauce, a tiny bit of dark soy sauce, white sugar, salt, pepper powder, corn starch, oyster sauce, and water. Stir well.
  4. Heat cooking oil in a pan over low heat. Add half of the green scallions and slowly sauté until fragrant and slightly browned. Remove the scallions, leaving the infused oil.
  5. Add the tofu pieces to the pan and fry until golden brown on all sides. Season with a pinch of salt.
  6. Add the remaining scallions to the pan.
  7. Pour the prepared sauce over the tofu and scallions. Bring to a boil, then cover and simmer over medium-low heat for 2 minutes.
  8. Remove the lid, increase heat to high, and reduce the sauce until thickened.
  9. Serve hot with rice.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=gAzWZcEhzac

crispy_banana.txt - 脆皮香蕉

Objectives

  • Learn to make a crispy banana dish that's popular online.
  • Understand the simple steps involved in preparing this economical and delicious treat.
  • Master the technique of frying bananas to achieve a crispy exterior and soft interior.

Ingredients

  • 5 香蕉 xiāng jiāo (bananas)
  • 100克 gè (grams) 土豆淀粉 tǔ dòu diàn fěn (potato starch)
  • 1勺 sháo (spoon) 白糖 bái táng (white sugar)
  • 1勺 sháo (spoon) 自制番茄酱 zì zhì fān qié jiàng / 番茄沙司 fān qié shā sī (homemade tomato sauce/ tomato ketchup)
  • 1勺 sháo (spoon) 米醋 mǐ cù (rice vinegar)
  • 少许 shǎo xǔ (a little) 清水 qīng shuǐ (water)
  • 足量 zú liàng (sufficient amount) 食用油 shí yòng yóu (cooking oil)
  • 少许 shǎo xǔ (a little) 白芝麻 bái zhī ma (white sesame seeds)

Instructions

  1. Peel and cut 5 bananas into small, evenly sized pieces.
  2. Place the banana pieces in a large bowl.
  3. Lightly spray the bananas with water.
  4. Add 100 grams of potato starch to the bananas.
  5. Wear disposable gloves and mix thoroughly to coat the bananas evenly with starch.
  6. Gently shake off excess starch from a few banana pieces and set aside in a plate.
  7. Prepare the sugar-vinegar sauce: In a bowl, mix one spoonful of white sugar, one spoonful of homemade or store-bought tomato sauce/ketchup, and one spoonful of rice vinegar. Set aside.
  8. Heat a wok or pan with a generous amount of cooking oil until it reaches six parts hot (筷子放入冒密集的小泡泡 kuài zi fàng rù mào mì jí de xiǎo pào pào - insert chopsticks and small bubbles appear densely).
  9. Add the banana pieces to the hot oil; do not stir immediately. Let them set for about 20-30 seconds.
  10. Gently shake the pan to submerge the bananas in the oil.
  11. Stir the bananas with a spatula. Fry for approximately 2-3 minutes until golden brown, crispy on the outside, and soft on the inside.
  12. Remove the fried bananas and drain excess oil.
  13. Set aside.
  14. In the same pan, leave a little oil and add the sugar-vinegar sauce.
  15. Cook the sauce until it thickens.
  16. Add a little white sesame seeds to the sauce.
  17. Add the fried bananas to the sauce and stir to coat evenly.
  18. Turn off the heat.
  19. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=07McrnenSUA

crispy_caramelized_banana.txt - Crispy Caramelized Banana

Objectives

  • Learn to make crispy caramelized bananas at home.
  • Master a simple, easy-to-follow cooking method.
  • Create a delicious and affordable treat for the whole family.

Ingredients

  • 2 bananas
  • 3 eggs
  • 250 grams bread crumbs (yellow preferred)
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Prepare the bananas: Cut off the banana stems. Remove half the peel from each banana using a knife or scissors.
  2. Slice the bananas: Cut the peeled bananas lengthwise into 5cm sections. Remove the remaining peel.
  3. Prepare the egg wash: Crack 3 eggs into a bowl and whisk in one direction until well combined.
  4. Prepare the bread crumbs: Place 250 grams of yellow bread crumbs in a separate bowl.
  5. Coat the bananas: Dip each banana slice in the egg wash, ensuring even coverage.
  6. Bread the bananas: Coat the egg-washed banana slices in the bread crumbs, pressing gently to adhere.
  7. Fry the bananas: Heat cooking oil in a pan until it reaches about 50% heat (small bubbles appear when a chopstick is inserted).
  8. Fry in batches: Carefully place the breaded bananas in the hot oil, one at a time. Avoid overcrowding the pan.
  9. Cook the bananas: Fry over low heat until the bananas are set, then gently push them with chopsticks to ensure even cooking.
  10. Finish frying: Fry over medium heat for approximately 2 minutes, until golden brown and crispy. Avoid overcooking to prevent cracking.
  11. Drain the bananas: Remove the fried bananas from the oil using a slotted spoon to drain excess oil.
  12. Serve: Place the crispy caramelized bananas on a plate and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=FjnGyRUxYVQ

crispy_chicken_breast.txt - مقرمش صدر دجاج

Objectives

  • Prepare juicy and crispy chicken breast.
  • Create a simple, flavorful sauce to complement the chicken.
  • Learn a quick and easy cooking method for delicious chicken.

Ingredients

  • Chicken breasts (amount not specified, adjust to your needs)
  • 1 tbsp salt
  • 1 tbsp pepper
  • 1 tbsp cooking wine
  • Water (amount not specified)
  • Cornstarch (amount not specified)
  • Cooking oil (amount not specified)
  • Thinly sliced green onions (amount not specified)
  • Finely chopped coriander (amount not specified)
  • 1 tbsp light soy sauce
  • Pinch of salt
  • 2 tbsp white sugar
  • 1 tbsp cooking wine

Instructions

  1. Marinate chicken: Add 1 tbsp salt to fresh water, mix well. Add prepared chicken breasts and marinate for 5 minutes.
  2. Clean and re-marinate: Remove chicken, clean, and briefly soak in lightly salted water to keep it fresh and tender.
  3. Slice chicken: Remove chicken from water and slice thinly and evenly.
  4. Season chicken: Place sliced chicken in a bowl. Add 1 tbsp salt, pepper, and cooking wine. Mix well and let it absorb the juices.
  5. Create batter: Add water and cornstarch, mix until chicken is coated with a thin layer of batter. This keeps it moist and crispy.
  6. Coat with oil: Coat the chicken with cooking oil and set aside.
  7. Prepare garnish: Thinly slice green onions and finely chop coriander. Add to a bowl.
  8. Make the sauce: In a separate bowl, mix light soy sauce, a pinch of salt, white sugar, and cooking wine. Stir well and set aside.
  9. First fry: Heat cooking oil to 40-50% heat. Fry chicken pieces slowly over medium-low heat until the cornstarch batter is cooked through. Stir frequently with chopsticks to prevent sticking.
  10. Second fry: Once chicken floats and skin is slightly charred, remove and drain oil. Increase oil temperature to 70-80%. Re-fry chicken for about 30 seconds until crispy and golden brown.
  11. Make sauce: Add a little cooking oil to the sauce and bring to a boil over high heat, stirring constantly.
  12. Combine: Add the fried chicken to the boiling sauce. Add grated radish (if using), green onions, and coriander. Stir quickly over high heat until chicken absorbs the sauce (about 7-9 seconds).

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6tGgvhKM7po

crispy_chicken_wings.txt - 家庭版脆皮鸡翅

Objectives

  • Learn to make crispy, flavorful chicken wings at home.
  • Master a simple, yet effective method for cleaning and marinating chicken wings.
  • Achieve perfectly crispy skin and tender meat using a double-frying technique.

Ingredients

  • 1.5斤 fresh chicken wings (about 750g)
  • 1 tablespoon flour (for cleaning)
  • 1 piece ginger (拍扁, then minced)
  • 1 small section of green onion (sliced)
  • 1 tablespoon Shaoxing wine (黄酒)
  • 1 tablespoon salt (食盐)
  • A pinch of pepper (胡椒粉)
  • 1 tablespoon five-spice powder (五香粉)
  • 1 tablespoon soy sauce (生抽酱油)
  • Appropriate amount of oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • 2 eggs (from a hen)
  • 1 tablespoon cornstarch (玉米淀粉)
  • 1 teaspoon all-purpose flour (普通面粉)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)

Instructions

  1. Rinse chicken wings under running water.
  2. Place chicken wings in a bowl, add 1 tbsp flour, and mix thoroughly to remove impurities.
  3. Rinse chicken wings with water multiple times until the water runs clear.
  4. Drain chicken wings and pat dry.
  5. Score both sides of each chicken wing.
  6. Place chicken wings in a bowl.
  7. Add minced ginger, sliced green onion, Shaoxing wine, salt, pepper, five-spice powder, soy sauce, and oyster sauce.
  8. Mix well with hands until thoroughly coated.
  9. Marinate for 20 minutes.
  10. In a bowl, combine marinated chicken wings, 2 eggs, 1 tbsp cornstarch, and 1 tsp all-purpose flour. Mix well until evenly coated.
  11. Heat cooking oil in a wok to medium heat (筷子放入冒密集小泡泡).
  12. Fry chicken wings in batches until lightly browned and set (about 5 minutes).
  13. Remove chicken wings and drain oil.
  14. Increase oil temperature.
  15. Return chicken wings to the wok and fry again for 49-64 seconds (or longer for extra crispiness).
  16. Remove chicken wings, drain oil, and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=KV4Orbc8ToY

crispy_glutinous_rice_balls.txt - 脆皮汤圆

Objectives

  • Learn to make crispy glutinous rice balls.
  • Master the technique of creating a crispy exterior while maintaining a soft, chewy interior.
  • Elevate a simple dessert into a visually appealing and delicious treat.

Ingredients

  • 1 package of glutinous rice balls (sesame or peanut filling)
  • Water
  • Salt
  • 2-3 eggs
  • 2 scallions, chopped
  • Breadcrumbs (golden color preferred)
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Bring plenty of water to a boil in a pot over high heat. Add a pinch of salt.
  2. Add the glutinous rice balls to the boiling water. Do not stir for the first 30 seconds to allow the skin to set.
  3. After 30 seconds, stir gently to prevent sticking. Cover and continue boiling until the rice balls float freely.
  4. Add a little more water, bring back to a boil, and cook until all rice balls float.
  5. Remove rice balls with a slotted spoon and immediately transfer to a bowl of cold water to cool.
  6. Drain the cooled rice balls and place them in a bowl.
  7. Add the chopped scallions to the bowl with the rice balls.
  8. In a separate bowl, whisk 2-3 eggs until the whites and yolks are fully combined.
  9. Pour the egg mixture over the rice balls and gently stir to coat evenly.
  10. Add the breadcrumbs to the rice balls, coating them completely.
  11. Heat plenty of cooking oil in a pan to medium heat (4-5 out of 10).
  12. Add the breaded rice balls to the hot oil and fry for about 15 seconds, or until the breadcrumbs are golden brown and crispy. Do not overcook.
  13. Remove the rice balls with a slotted spoon and place them on a plate to drain excess oil.
  14. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=9zMbrVgvvOY

crispy_tangyuan.txt - 脆皮汤圆

Objectives

  • Learn to make crispy tangyuan (glutinous rice balls) with a crunchy exterior and a soft, gooey interior.
  • Master the technique of coating tangyuan with egg and breadcrumbs for optimal texture.
  • Create a visually appealing and delicious dessert or snack perfect for holidays or gatherings.

Ingredients

  • 1 package of tangyuan (sesame or peanut filling)
  • Water
  • Salt
  • 2-3 scallions (green onions), finely chopped
  • 2-3 eggs
  • Breadcrumbs (preferably golden yellow)
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Bring plenty of water to a boil in a pot over high heat. Add a little salt and stir.
  2. Add the tangyuan to the boiling water. Do not stir for the first 30 seconds to allow the skin to set.
  3. After 30 seconds, gently stir to prevent sticking. Cover and cook until the tangyuan floats freely.
  4. Add a little more water, bring back to a boil, and cook until all tangyuan float.
  5. Remove the tangyuan with a slotted spoon and immediately rinse in cold water to cool. Drain well.
  6. Place the cooled tangyuan in a bowl and add the chopped scallions.
  7. In a separate bowl, whisk 2-3 eggs until the whites and yolks are fully combined.
  8. Pour the egg mixture over the tangyuan and gently stir to coat evenly.
  9. Add the tangyuan to the breadcrumbs, ensuring they are fully coated.
  10. Heat plenty of cooking oil in a pan to about 40-50% heat.
  11. Add the breaded tangyuan and fry for about 15 seconds, or until the breadcrumbs are golden and crispy. Do not overcook.
  12. Remove the tangyuan with a slotted spoon and place them on a plate to drain excess oil.
  13. Serve immediately and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=9zMbrVgvvOY

crispy_tender_loofah.txt - مقرمشة ولذيذة اللوف

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare crispy and tender fried loofah.
  • Master a technique to prevent loofah from turning black or watery during frying.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to complement the fried loofah.

Ingredients

  • 1 large loofah
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • A few drops white vinegar
  • Water (to cover loofah)
  • Green pepper (amount to taste)
  • Garlic (amount to taste)
  • Ginger (amount to taste)
  • 4 eggs
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • 1 drop chicken essence
  • A little sugar
  • 1 tablespoon cornstarch
  • Soy sauce (amount to taste)
  • Water (amount to taste)
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Peel and wash the loofah. Cut off both ends and slice into smaller pieces. Break each piece in half. Cut the loofah into long strips.
  2. Place the loofah strips in a large bowl. Add 1 teaspoon salt and a few drops of white vinegar. Add enough water to cover the loofah. Mix well and let it soak for 10 minutes. This prevents oxidation and browning.
  3. Drain the loofah.
  4. Prepare the green pepper: Cut, halve, and remove seeds. Slice into strips.
  5. Prepare the garlic and ginger: Slice and mince.
  6. Whisk 4 eggs in a bowl until yolks and whites are fully combined.
  7. Prepare the sauce: In a small bowl, mix 1 teaspoon salt, 1 drop of chicken essence, a little sugar, 1 tablespoon cornstarch, soy sauce, and water. Mix well.
  8. Heat cooking oil in a pan. Pour in the egg mixture and gently push it to cook quickly. Don't stir too much. Remove and set aside.
  9. Add sliced garlic and minced ginger to the pan and sauté until fragrant.
  10. Add the loofah strips and stir-fry over high heat for a short time to reduce water content.
  11. Add green pepper and continue to stir-fry until the loofah is tender.
  12. Add the fried egg, stir-fry briefly, and then pour in the prepared sauce. Stir until the sauce is absorbed.
  13. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=jOEc7MrKRZI

cucumber_egg_salad.txt - 黄瓜鸡蛋凉拌菜

Objectives

  • Learn to make a refreshing cucumber and egg salad.
  • Master the techniques for preparing the ingredients.
  • Create a flavorful and easy-to-make summer dish.

Ingredients

  • 2 eggs
  • 2 cucumbers (黄瓜)
  • 1 carrot (胡萝卜)
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜)
  • A few small chili peppers (小米椒)
  • 2 scallions (小葱)
  • 1 tbsp salt (食盐)
  • 1 tbsp sugar (白糖)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽)
  • 1 tbsp vinegar (陈醋)
  • A little sesame oil (小磨香油)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)

Instructions

  1. Wash and drain the cucumbers, carrots, and eggs.
  2. Cut the cucumbers into small pieces, then into diamond-shaped slices.
  3. Cut the carrots into small pieces, then into diamond-shaped slices.
  4. Separate the egg whites and yolks. Whisk each separately.
  5. Mince the garlic and chili peppers.
  6. Chop the scallions.
  7. Mix salt, sugar, soy sauce, vinegar, and sesame oil in a bowl to make a sauce. Set aside.
  8. Heat a pan with a little oil. Pour in the egg whites and cook over low heat for 2 minutes until set. Remove from pan.
  9. Add more oil to the pan and cook the egg yolks until golden brown. Remove from pan and let cool.
  10. Blanch the carrot slices in boiling water for 49 seconds. Drain.
  11. Cut the cooled egg whites and yolks into diamond shapes.
  12. Combine the cucumbers, carrots, egg slices, and sauce in a bowl. Mix well.
  13. Serve and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LopLCG763o8

cucumber_egg_soup.txt - Cucumber Egg Soup 黄瓜鸡蛋汤

Objectives

  • Learn a unique way to prepare cucumber and egg without frying or cold dressing.
  • Create a flavorful and nutritious soup with a simple recipe.
  • Master the technique of enhancing the taste and texture of cucumbers using sugar.

Ingredients

  • 2 cucumbers (黄瓜)
  • 4 eggs (鸡蛋)
  • 1 tablespoon white sugar (白糖)
  • 1 block firm tofu (老豆腐)
  • 1 cup shiitake mushrooms (海鲜菇)
  • Several scallions (小葱), separated into white and green parts
  • 1 piece ginger (生姜)
  • Several cloves garlic (蒜子)
  • 2-3 small chili peppers (小米椒)
  • Several shrimp (虾仁), deveined and cleaned
  • Salt (食盐)
  • Pepper (胡椒粉)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)

Instructions

  1. Wash and slice the cucumbers into 1cm thick slices. Place in a bowl, add white sugar, mix well, and let marinate for 10 minutes.
  2. Cut the tofu into small cubes. Set aside.
  3. Clean the shiitake mushrooms and set aside.
  4. Crack the eggs into a bowl (do not whisk). Set aside.
  5. Mince the scallion whites, julienne the ginger, mince the garlic, and slice the chili peppers. Chop the scallion greens. Set aside.
  6. Devein the shrimp, score the backs, and marinate with some scallion, ginger, and salt for 10 minutes.
  7. Squeeze out excess water from the marinated cucumbers.
  8. Heat oil in a pan. Add the eggs and cook over medium-low heat for 1 minute per side, until golden brown. Cut into small pieces. Set aside.
  9. Add more oil to the pan. Add the tofu and cook over medium-low heat for 2 minutes per side, until golden brown. Set aside.
  10. Add more oil to the pan. Add the shrimp and stir-fry until pink. Add the shiitake mushrooms and stir-fry until cooked.
  11. Add the minced scallion whites, ginger, and garlic to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant.
  12. Add the fried tofu and eggs to the pan.
  13. Pour in boiling water to the pan. Season with salt and pepper. Stir well.
  14. Transfer everything to a clay pot. Cover and bring to a boil. Reduce heat and simmer for 5 minutes.
  15. Garnish with sliced chili peppers and chopped scallions. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=NGM6MKvLvMI

cucumber_egg.txt - 黄瓜炒鸡蛋 (Huángguā chǎo jǐdàn)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple and delicious cucumber and egg stir-fry.
  • Master the techniques for stir-frying cucumbers and eggs to maintain texture and flavor.
  • Create a quick and easy weeknight meal that's appealing to both adults and children.

Ingredients

  • 2 cucumbers (黄瓜 - huángguā)
  • 3 eggs (鸡蛋 - jǐdàn)
  • 1 hot dog (火腿肠 - huǒtuǐ cháng) - or substitute with another sausage
  • A small amount of salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • A small amount of cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòng yóu)
  • Some spring onions (小葱 - xiǎocōng), chopped
  • A piece of ginger (生姜 - shēngjiāng), minced
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜 - suàn), minced
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒 - xiǎomǐ jiāo) - or substitute with bell peppers if you don't like spicy food
  • Light soy sauce (生抽 - shēngchōu)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油 - háoyóu)

Instructions

  1. Wash two cucumbers and three eggs thoroughly with salt and water. Do not peel the cucumbers.
  2. Cut the cucumbers into 3-4 cm long diagonal slices, then cut them into diamond shapes. Set aside.
  3. Slice the hot dog diagonally into thin slices. Set aside.
  4. Crack the eggs into a bowl, add a dash of salt, and whisk until the egg whites and yolks are fully combined. Set aside.
  5. Mince the spring onions, ginger, garlic, and chili peppers. Set aside.
  6. Heat a wok or frying pan with a small amount of cooking oil until it slightly smokes.
  7. Pour in the whisked eggs and quickly stir until they are set but still tender and golden yellow. Remove from the pan.
  8. Add a little more oil to the pan. Add the cucumbers and stir-fry for about 1 minute until slightly softened. Remove from the pan.
  9. Add the minced spring onions, ginger, and garlic to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Add the hot dog slices and stir-fry until heated through.
  11. Add the chili peppers and stir-fry briefly.
  12. Add the cooked cucumbers and eggs to the pan.
  13. Season with light soy sauce and oyster sauce (no additional salt needed).
  14. Stir-fry everything together for about 49 seconds until well combined and heated through.
  15. Turn off the heat and serve hot with rice.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=1YgJZ537uUc

cu_liu_bai_cai.txt - 醋溜白菜 (Cu Liu Bai Cai)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple and delicious stir-fried Napa cabbage dish.
  • Master the technique of preparing and cooking Napa cabbage for optimal texture.
  • Understand the importance of the sauce in achieving the desired flavor profile.

Ingredients

  • 1/2 large Napa cabbage (大白菜)
  • 1 tablespoon salt (盐)
  • 1 tablespoon cooking oil (食用油) +猪油 (optional)
  • 1 tablespoon soy sauce (生抽)
  • 1 tablespoon rice vinegar (陈醋)
  • 1 teaspoon sesame oil (松茸鲜 - this seems to be a brand name, could also be substituted with regular sesame oil)
  • 1/2 teaspoon sugar (白糖)
  • 1/2 teaspoon cornstarch (玉米淀粉)
  • 1 tablespoon water (清水)
  • 1 small piece of ginger (生姜), minced
  • several cloves of garlic (蒜), minced
  • a few dried chilies (干海椒), cut into small pieces
  • some scallions (小葱), minced

Instructions

  1. Remove the leaves from half a large Napa cabbage. Wash thoroughly, paying attention to the stem, removing any sticky residue. Drain well.
  2. Separate the leaves and stems. Tear the leaves into small pieces. Slice the stems into uniform strips.
  3. Place the cabbage in a bowl, add salt, and mix well. Let it sit for 10 minutes to soften and release moisture.
  4. While the cabbage marinates, prepare the other ingredients: mince the ginger, garlic, and scallions; cut the dried chilies into small pieces.
  5. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, whisk together soy sauce, rice vinegar, sesame oil, sugar, cornstarch, and water until smooth. Set aside.
  6. Gently squeeze out excess water from the marinated cabbage.
  7. Heat oil (and optional pig oil) in a wok or pan. Add ginger, garlic, and dried chilies; stir-fry until fragrant.
  8. Add the cabbage stems and stir-fry for about 1 minute.
  9. Add the cabbage leaves and stir-fry until wilted.
  10. Pour the prepared sauce into the pan and stir-fry for about 1 minute until the sauce thickens and coats the cabbage evenly.
  11. Serve hot with rice.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=4lyrXuEX7cM

daikon_radish_balls.txt - Daikon Radish Balls

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and healthy steamed daikon radish balls.
  • Master the technique of preparing and mixing the daikon radish.
  • Create a flavorful filling with pork, mushrooms, and shrimp skin.

Ingredients

  • 1 large daikon radish
  • 1 tsp salt
  • 100g pork, minced
  • 100g fresh mushrooms, cleaned and sliced
  • 1 piece ginger, minced
  • Several cloves garlic, minced
  • Some green onions, chopped (separate white and green parts)
  • Light soy sauce
  • Oyster sauce
  • Pepper
  • 3 tbsp sweet potato starch
  • 20g water
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Prepare the daikon radish: Peel, remove the top and bottom, and cut into 3-4cm lengths. Slice thinly, then julienne. Place in a bowl, add salt, mix well, and let sit to draw out moisture. Squeeze out excess water.
  2. Prepare the filling: Clean and slice mushrooms. Mince ginger and garlic. Chop green onions (separate white and green parts).
  3. Stir-fry the filling: Heat oil in a pan. Add minced pork and stir-fry until white. Add white parts of green onions, ginger, and garlic; stir-fry until fragrant. Add mushrooms and stir-fry. If using, add shrimp skin. Season with light soy sauce, oyster sauce, and pepper.
  4. Combine filling and radish: Add the squeezed daikon radish to the stir-fried filling. Add sweet potato starch and water. Mix thoroughly until slightly sticky.
  5. Shape the balls: Take small portions of the mixture and roll into balls, about the size of ping pong balls.
  6. Steam the balls: Place the balls in a steamer basket, leaving space between them. Steam over high heat for 15 minutes.
  7. Serve: Remove from steamer and serve. Garnish with chopped green onions if desired.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Xnuea6Oyqas

doufu_doujiao_bing.txt - Tofu and Green Bean Pancake

Objectives

  • Learn a simple, nutritious recipe using tofu and green beans.
  • Master a quick cooking method without frying or stewing.
  • Create a delicious and visually appealing breakfast pancake.

Ingredients

  • 1 block firm tofu
  • 1 handful of fresh green beans
  • 1 tbsp salt
  • 3 eggs (for the pancake batter)
  • 1 egg (for brushing)
  • 1 tsp baking soda
  • 1 tbsp MSG (or to taste)
  • A pinch of black pepper
  • 2 tbsp all-purpose flour (approximately 100g)
  • 1 carrot, diced
  • 1-2 hot dogs, thinly sliced
  • Cooking oil
  • Sesame seeds (optional)

Instructions

  1. Wash green beans and soak in salted water (1 tbsp salt in water) for 5 minutes to remove pesticides and preserve freshness. Drain.
  2. Boil water in a pot, add 1 tbsp salt. Add tofu and blanch for 1 minute to remove bean curd smell. Drain and set aside.
  3. In a large bowl, crumble the blanched tofu and mix in 3 beaten eggs. Set aside.
  4. Add baking soda to the remaining water from blanching the tofu. Blanch the green beans for 2 minutes until bright green. Immediately transfer to ice water to cool and maintain crispness. Drain.
  5. Finely dice the blanched green beans (approx. 0.5cm).
  6. Dice the carrot.
  7. Combine the diced green beans, diced carrots, crumbled tofu mixture, salt (1 tbsp), MSG (1 tbsp), pepper in a bowl. Mix well.
  8. Add 2 tbsp of flour (approx. 100g) to the mixture and stir until well combined. Set aside.
  9. Whisk 1 egg in a small bowl. Set aside.
  10. Slice hot dogs thinly.
  11. Heat a little oil in a pan. Brush the oil evenly.
  12. Pour the tofu and green bean batter into the pan and spread it evenly to form a pancake.
  13. Cover and cook over low heat for 3 minutes until set.
  14. Brush the pancake with the whisked egg.
  15. Arrange hot dog slices evenly on top.
  16. Sprinkle with sesame seeds (optional).
  17. Cover and cook for another 3 minutes.
  18. Flip the pancake and cook the other side until golden brown (another 3 minutes).
  19. Cut into desired shapes and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=EuM08htbIog

doufu_egg_cake.txt - Tofu and Egg Cake 豆腐鸡蛋饼

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious tofu and egg cake without steaming or boiling.
  • Master a simple, easy-to-learn recipe.
  • Achieve tender, flavorful tofu and egg cake.

Ingredients

  • 2 blocks of tender tofu (cut into 1cm cubes)
  • 2 slices of lean pork (minced)
  • Several cloves of garlic (minced)
  • Several small chili peppers (thinly sliced)
  • 4 eggs
  • Salt
  • Cooking oil
  • 2 tablespoons of Puning doubanjiang (fermented soybean paste)
  • Water
  • Small amount of water starch (cornstarch slurry)
  • Optional: Chopped green onions

Instructions

  1. Cut the tofu into 1cm cubes. Place in a bowl and set aside.
  2. Mince the lean pork. Place in a bowl.
  3. Mince the garlic. Place in a bowl.
  4. Thinly slice the chili peppers. Place in a bowl.
  5. Whisk 4 eggs until light and fluffy. Set aside.
  6. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add a spoonful of salt.
  7. Add the tofu to the boiling water and blanch for 2 minutes.
  8. Remove the tofu with a slotted spoon and drain well.
  9. Heat a pan and add the blanched tofu. Stir-fry until the surface is dry.
  10. Add an appropriate amount of cooking oil and stir-fry until the tofu is evenly coated.
  11. Add a little salt to season.
  12. Stir-fry the tofu until lightly browned on all sides.
  13. Pour in the whisked eggs and gently shake the pan to mix evenly.
  14. Cover the pan and cook over low heat for 2 minutes until the bottom is golden brown.
  15. Flip the tofu and egg mixture and cook the other side until golden brown and crispy.
  16. Remove the tofu and egg cake from the pan and set aside.
  17. Add the minced pork to the pan and stir-fry until it changes color.
  18. Add the minced garlic and chili peppers and stir-fry until fragrant.
  19. Add 2 tablespoons of Puning doubanjiang and stir-fry until fragrant.
  20. Add half a bowl of water and bring to a boil.
  21. Add a small amount of water starch to thicken the sauce.
  22. Pour the sauce over the tofu and egg cake.
  23. Garnish with chopped green onions (optional).

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=n7CMEonF-_w

doufu_shao_suntai.txt - Tofu with Garlic Scapes

Objectives

  • Learn to make a flavorful and economical Tofu with Garlic Scapes dish.
  • Master the technique of pan-frying tofu to achieve a golden-brown crust.
  • Understand how to balance the textures and flavors of tofu, garlic scapes, and meat.

Ingredients

  • 1 block firm tofu (approximately 400g), cut into small cubes
  • 50g pork, minced
  • 1 bunch garlic scapes, chopped
  • 2 cloves garlic, minced
  • 1 piece ginger, minced
  • 2-3 small green chilies, finely chopped
  • 1 small bunch scallions, chopped
  • Salt
  • Light soy sauce (生抽)
  • Dark soy sauce (老抽)
  • Five-spice powder (五香粉)
  • Chicken essence (鸡精)
  • Water starch (水淀粉)
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Tofu: Rinse the tofu and place it in a bowl of water with a pinch of salt for at least 30 minutes to remove excess water and reduce beany smell.
  2. Cut the Tofu: Cut the soaked tofu into small cubes.
  3. Prepare the Meat: Mince the pork. (Optional: Use a food processor for convenience.)
  4. Prepare the Garlic Scapes: Chop the garlic scapes.
  5. Prepare the Aromatics: Mince the garlic, ginger, and chilies. Chop the scallions.
  6. Pan-fry the Tofu: Heat oil in a pan over medium heat. Add the tofu cubes and sprinkle with salt. Pan-fry until golden brown on all sides. Remove and set aside.
  7. Stir-fry Garlic Scapes: Add more oil to the pan. Add the garlic scapes and stir-fry for 30 seconds until slightly softened. Remove and set aside.
  8. Stir-fry the Pork: Add the minced pork to the pan and stir-fry until browned.
  9. Add Aromatics: Add the minced garlic, ginger, and chilies. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Add Tofu and Seasoning: Add the pan-fried tofu, salt, light soy sauce, dark soy sauce, and five-spice powder. Stir-fry until well combined.
  11. Simmer: Add a bowl of water, ensuring the tofu is submerged in the liquid. Cover and simmer for a few minutes to allow the flavors to meld.
  12. Thicken the Sauce: Add water starch to thicken the sauce.
  13. Add Garlic Scapes: Add the stir-fried garlic scapes and chicken essence. Stir-fry until well combined.
  14. Serve: Turn off the heat. Transfer the Tofu with Garlic Scapes to a serving dish and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=qd2787heh4U

doujia_egg.txt - 外婆菜炒豆角 (Wàipó cài chǎo dòujiǎo)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple and delicious side dish of stir-fried green beans with preserved vegetables.
  • Master the technique of stir-frying to achieve a crispy and tender texture.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients for a quick and easy weeknight meal.

Ingredients

  • 1 cup long green beans (长豆角 - cháng dòujiǎo), cut into 1cm pieces
  • 3 eggs (土鸡蛋 - tǔ jī dàn)
  • Salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • A few drops of white vinegar (白醋 - bái cù)
  • 1 package of preserved vegetables (外婆菜 - wàipó cài)
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒 - xiǎo mǐ jiāo), finely sliced
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜 - suàn), minced
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòng yóu)
  • 1/2 tablespoon soy sauce (生抽 - shēng chōu)

Instructions

  1. Wash and cut long green beans into 1cm pieces.
  2. Whisk 3 eggs with salt and a few drops of white vinegar until light and fluffy.
  3. Pour egg mixture over the green beans, and mix well. Set aside.
  4. Finely slice chili peppers and mince garlic.
  5. Heat oil in a wok or frying pan over medium heat.
  6. Add the green bean and egg mixture to the pan and cook until golden brown on both sides, about 2 minutes per side. Break into smaller pieces with a spatula.
  7. Remove the cooked green beans and eggs from the pan and set aside.
  8. Add minced garlic and chili peppers to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Add the preserved vegetables and stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Return the green bean and egg mixture to the pan.
  11. Stir-fry over high heat for 1 minute.
  12. Add 1/2 tablespoon of soy sauce and stir-fry until well combined.
  13. Serve hot.
