dou_jiao_chao_rou_mo.txt - 豆角炒肉末 (Dou Jiao Chao Rou Mo)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy home-style green bean stir-fry with minced meat.
  • Master the techniques for preparing and cooking the ingredients to achieve optimal flavor and texture.
  • Understand the importance of ingredient selection and proper cooking methods for a flavorful dish.

Ingredients

  • Fresh long green beans (choose crisp and tender ones)
  • Garlic (several cloves, minced)
  • Scallions (separate white and green parts, white part minced)
  • Small chili peppers (several, finely sliced)
  • Pork front leg meat (with both lean and fatty parts, minced)
  • Salt
  • Cooking oil
  • Cooking wine (料酒, liàojiǔ)
  • Dark soy sauce (老抽, lǎochōu)
  • Light soy sauce (生抽, shēngchōu)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油, háoyóu)
  • MSG (optional,味精, wèijīng)
  • Song Rong Xian (松茸鲜, a type of mushroom seasoning, optional)

Instructions

  1. Wash the green beans thoroughly and remove both ends.
  2. Cut the green beans into 0.5cm pieces.
  3. Mince the garlic.
  4. Mince the scallion whites.
  5. Slice the small chili peppers into thin rings.
  6. Cut the pork into slices, then mince it, leaving slightly larger pieces.
  7. Heat oil in a wok or pan. Add the green beans and stir-fry until slightly softened and slightly browned (about 70-80% cooked). Add salt to season during this step.
  8. Remove the green beans and set aside.
  9. Add the minced pork to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Add cooking wine to remove any fishy smell.
  11. Add the minced garlic, scallions, and chili peppers; stir-fry until fragrant.
  12. Add dark soy sauce for color.
  13. Add the cooked green beans back to the pan.
  14. Season with salt, Song Rong Xian (if using), light soy sauce, and oyster sauce.
  15. Stir-fry over high heat for about 1 minute until well combined and flavors are infused.
  16. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Zz2tnhCQytM

dou_jiao.txt - Stir-fried Green Beans with Pork

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare crisp and flavorful stir-fried green beans.
  • Master the technique of blanching green beans to maintain color and texture.
  • Learn how to create a delicious stir-fry with simple ingredients and techniques.

Ingredients

  • Fresh green beans (amount not specified)
  • 2 green bell peppers
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒)
  • Several cloves of garlic
  • 3 RMB worth of lean pork
  • Water
  • Salt
  • Cooking oil
  • Peanut oil
  • Pork lard (猪油)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • Light soy sauce (生抽)
  • Mushroom seasoning (松茸鲜)

Instructions

  1. Wash and clean the green beans. Trim the ends and cut into 1-2 cm segments. Set aside in a bowl.
  2. Cut green peppers and small chili peppers into thin rings. Mince the garlic finely. Set aside.
  3. Cut the pork into thin slices, then mince into slightly coarse pieces. Set aside.
  4. Boil water in a pot. Add a small spoonful of salt and half a spoonful of cooking oil.
  5. Add the green beans and blanch for 2 minutes until tender. Drain immediately and set aside.
  6. Heat a wok or pan with a little peanut oil and half a spoonful of pork lard. Melt the lard.
  7. Add the minced pork and stir-fry until fragrant and crumbly.
  8. Add the minced garlic and chopped peppers. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Add the blanched green beans.
  10. Season with a pinch of salt, a small spoonful of mushroom seasoning, oyster sauce, and light soy sauce.
  11. Stir-fry over high heat for 1 minute until well combined and heated through.
  12. Remove from heat and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=SGqouO0jaIs

dou_jiao_wai_po_cai.txt - 外婆菜炒豆角 (Wàipó cài chǎo dòujiǎo)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy summer side dish.
  • Master the technique of stir-frying for optimal flavor and texture.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients for a quick and satisfying meal.

Ingredients

  • 1 handful of long green beans (长豆角 - cháng dòujiǎo)
  • 3 eggs (土鸡蛋 - tǔ jīdàn)
  • Salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • A few drops of white vinegar (白醋 - báicù)
  • 1 package of "Wai Po Cai" (外婆菜 - wàipó cài) (Pickled vegetables, usually radish, mustard greens, and cabbage)
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒 - xiǎomǐjiāo)
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜 - suàn)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòngyóu)
  • Half a spoonful of light soy sauce (生抽 - shēngchōu)

Instructions

  1. Trim the ends of the green beans and wash them thoroughly.
  2. Cut the green beans into 1cm segments.
  3. Crack 3 eggs into a bowl.
  4. Add salt and a few drops of white vinegar to the eggs.
  5. Whisk the eggs until the whites and yolks are fully combined and smooth.
  6. Pour the egg mixture over the green beans.
  7. Toss gently to coat the beans evenly with the egg mixture.
  8. Set aside.
  9. Chop the chili peppers into small rings.
  10. Mince the garlic.
  11. Heat a small amount of oil in a pan or wok.
  12. Add the green bean and egg mixture to the hot pan.
  13. Spread the mixture evenly in the pan.
  14. Cook over medium-low heat for about 2 minutes per side, or until golden brown and cooked through.
  15. Break the cooked mixture into smaller pieces using a spatula.
  16. Stir-fry for another 30 seconds.
  17. Remove from the pan and set aside.
  18. Add a little more oil to the pan.
  19. Add the minced garlic and chili peppers and stir-fry until fragrant.
  20. Add the "Wai Po Cai" and stir-fry until fragrant.
  21. Add the cooked green bean and egg mixture back into the pan.
  22. Stir-fry over high heat for 1 minute.
  23. Add half a spoonful of light soy sauce.
  24. Stir-fry until evenly coated.
  25. Serve hot. Enjoy with rice.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZF1EbZP5H0w

dry_steamed_noodles_with_egg.txt - 干蒸面条拌鸡蛋

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple, refreshing summer noodle dish.
  • Master a quick and easy method for cooking noodles and eggs.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to complement the noodles and vegetables.

Ingredients

  • 3 土鸡蛋 (tǔ jī dàn) - earth eggs (free range eggs)
  • 1 块5毛钱超市买来的面饼 (kuài wǔ máo qián chāoshì mǎi lái de miàn bǐng) - 50 cent supermarket noodle cake (a type of flatbread)
  • 1 节去皮的胡萝卜 (jié qù pí de hú luó bo) - 1 section peeled carrot
  • 半黄瓜 (bàn huáng guā) - half a cucumber
  • 蒜 (suàn) - garlic
  • 小葱 (xiǎo cōng) - scallions
  • 油泼辣子 (yóu pō là zi) - chili oil
  • 半勺生抽 (bàn sháo shēng chōu) - half a spoonful of light soy sauce
  • 半勺香醋 (bàn sháo xiāng cù) - half a spoonful of rice vinegar
  • 1勺白糖 (1 sháo bái táng) - 1 spoonful of white sugar
  • 小勺松茸鲜 (xiǎo sháo sōng róng xiān) - a small spoonful of matsutake mushroom seasoning (or substitute)
  • 少许胡椒粉 (shǎo xǔ hú jiāo fěn) - a little pepper powder
  • 小磨香油 (xiǎo mó xiāng yóu) - sesame oil
  • 香菜 (xiāng cài) - coriander (cilantro)
  • 16克花生米 (16 kè huā shēng mǐ) - 16g peanuts
  • 食用油 (shí yòng yóu) - cooking oil (for noodles)
  • 芝麻花生酱 (zhī ma huā shēng jiàng) - sesame peanut butter (optional)

Instructions

  1. Soak the noodle cake in a bowl of water for 1 minute.
  2. Bring plenty of water to a boil in a pot.
  3. Add the soaked noodle cake and washed eggs to the boiling water.
  4. Cover and steam for 15 minutes, adding a little cooking oil to the noodles halfway through.
  5. While steaming, prepare the vegetables and sauce:
    • Cut the carrot into thin strips.
    • Cut the cucumber into thin strips.
    • Mince the garlic finely.
    • Chop the scallions finely.
    • Mix the chili oil, light soy sauce, rice vinegar, sugar, matsutake seasoning (or substitute), pepper, and sesame oil in a bowl.
    • Chop the coriander.
  6. Remove the eggs and noodles from the steamer. Let the eggs cool in cold water, then peel and cut in half.
  7. Fluff the noodles.
  8. Combine the noodles, eggs, carrot, cucumber, peanuts, and sauce in a bowl. Add sesame peanut butter if desired.
  9. Toss everything together until well combined.
  10. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=YG--SjxbnsY

egg_cucumber_salad.txt - 凉拌鸡蛋黄瓜

Objectives

  • Learn to make a refreshing and flavorful egg and cucumber salad.
  • Master simple knife skills for cutting vegetables.
  • Create a delicious and easy-to-make summer dish.

Ingredients

  • 2-3 eggs
  • 2 cucumbers (黄瓜)
  • 1 carrot (胡萝卜)
  • Several cloves garlic (蒜)
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒)
  • 2 scallions (小葱)
  • 1 tbsp salt (食盐)
  • 1 tbsp sugar (白糖)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽)
  • 1 tbsp rice vinegar (陈醋)
  • A dash of sesame oil (小磨香油)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)

Instructions

  1. Wash and dry the cucumbers, carrots, and eggs.
  2. Cut the cucumbers into small sections, then into diamond-shaped slices. Aim for even thickness.
  3. Cut the peeled carrot into small sections, then into diamond-shaped slices.
  4. Separate the egg whites and yolks. Whisk each separately.
  5. Mince the garlic and finely slice the chili peppers.
  6. Chop the scallions.
  7. In a bowl, combine salt, sugar, soy sauce, rice vinegar, and sesame oil. Mix well.
  8. Heat a pan with a little oil. Spread the oil evenly.
  9. Pour in the egg whites, cook over low heat for 2 minutes until set and able to slide freely in the pan. Remove.
  10. Add more oil to the pan. Pour in the egg yolks and cook over low heat until golden brown and able to slide freely in the pan. Remove and let cool.
  11. Boil water in a pot. Blanch the carrot slices for 49 seconds. Drain.
  12. Add the blanched carrots to the bowl with the cucumber slices.
  13. Cut the cooled egg whites and yolks into diamond shapes. Add to the bowl.
  14. Add the prepared sauce to the bowl.
  15. Mix everything together gently using disposable gloves.
  16. Serve and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LopLCG763o8

eggplant_braised_meat.txt - 家常茄夹

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy eggplant dish.
  • Master the technique of preparing the eggplant and meat filling.
  • Create a flavorful braising sauce to enhance the dish.

Ingredients

  • 1 long purple eggplant (approximately 1.5 yuan)
  • 100g fatty and lean pork, skin removed
  • 1 small spoon of salt
  • 1 spoon of Songrong Xian (mushroom seasoning)
  • Pepper powder
  • A small amount of light soy sauce
  • A little white sugar
  • 2 drops of small-ground sesame oil
  • 1 large spoon of starch
  • Ginger and garlic juice
  • ½ egg white
  • Starch for coating eggplant
  • Garlic cloves, minced
  • Several scallions, chopped into green onions
  • Several small chili peppers, sliced
  • 1 spoon of soy sauce
  • Oyster sauce
  • A small amount of salt
  • White sugar
  • 1 spoon of Songrong Xian (mushroom seasoning)
  • Pepper powder
  • 1 spoon of corn starch
  • ½ bowl of water
  • Dark soy sauce (for color)
  • Cooking oil
  • Onion (for bottom of the pot)
  • Baby bok choy

Instructions

  1. Wash the eggplant thoroughly without peeling. Cut into slices, almost but not completely through (use chopsticks to help if needed).
  2. Mince the pork, removing the skin.
  3. Season the pork: Add salt, Songrong Xian, pepper powder, light soy sauce, white sugar, sesame oil, starch, ginger-garlic juice, and egg white. Mix well and knead thoroughly.
  4. Coat each eggplant slice with starch.
  5. Fill each eggplant slice with the seasoned pork mixture, and pinch to close.
  6. Mince garlic, chop scallions and chili peppers.
  7. Prepare the sauce: Mix soy sauce, oyster sauce, salt, sugar, Songrong Xian, pepper powder, corn starch, and water. Add dark soy sauce for color.
  8. Heat oil in a pan. Pan-fry the eggplant slices until golden brown on both sides.
  9. Layer the bottom of a sand pot with onions. Add the fried eggplant.
  10. In the same pan, sauté minced garlic, scallions, and chili peppers until fragrant.
  11. Add the garlic-scallion-pepper mixture, and baby bok choy to the sand pot with the eggplant.
  12. Pour the prepared sauce over the ingredients in the sand pot.
  13. Cover and simmer for 6 minutes.
  14. Garnish with chopped scallions and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=u3PuuN8KWro

eggplant_cake.txt - Simple and Delicious Eggplant Cake

Objectives

  • Learn to make a flavorful and nutritious eggplant cake.
  • Master a simple yet effective method for preparing eggplant.
  • Create a dish appealing to children and families.

Ingredients

  • 1 long purple eggplant
  • Salt (for washing eggplant)
  • 1/2 teaspoon white vinegar
  • Salt (for eggplant seasoning)
  • 2-3 cloves garlic, thinly sliced
  • OR substitute with leeks
  • Pork sausage (amount unspecified), diced
  • 2/3 of an onion, diced
  • 1 large green or red pepper, diced
  • Lettuce (optional)
  • Shrimp skin (optional)
  • 5 eggs
  • 13+ dashes of salt (amount unspecified)
  • 50 grams of flour
  • Oil (for greasing pan)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the eggplant: Wash the eggplant thoroughly with salted water, scrubbing for 20-30 seconds. Remove the stem and cut into thin slices, then dice into small cubes.
  2. Marinate the eggplant: In a large bowl, toss the diced eggplant with 1/2 teaspoon of white vinegar and salt. Mix well and set aside.
  3. Prepare aromatics: Thinly slice the garlic (or leeks), dice the onion and pepper. Dice the pork sausage.
  4. Combine ingredients: In a large bowl, combine the marinated eggplant, garlic (or leeks), diced pork sausage, onion, and pepper. Add optional lettuce and shrimp skin.
  5. Add egg and flour: Crack 5 eggs into the mixture. Using chopsticks, thoroughly mix the ingredients, coating everything evenly. Add salt and 50 grams of flour, mixing until a slightly thin batter forms.
  6. Cook the cake: Lightly grease an electric baking pan or skillet with oil. Pour the batter into the pan and spread it evenly.
  7. Bake: Cook on medium heat for 3 minutes, then open the lid and continue cooking until the bottom is browned. Reduce heat to low, cover and cook for another minute.
  8. Flip and finish: Using a spatula, carefully flip the cake. Cover and cook on low heat for another 3 minutes, or until golden brown on both sides.
  9. Serve: Once cooked, let the cake cool slightly. Cut into small pieces and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ky7u1iCCemw

eggplant_casserole.txt - Eggplant Casserole (茄子煲)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy eggplant casserole.
  • Master the technique of preparing and stuffing eggplant slices.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to enhance the eggplant casserole.

Ingredients

  • 1 long purple eggplant (茄子, qiézi)
  • 150g pork with visible fat and lean (肥瘦相间的肉, féishòuxiāngjiān de ròu)
  • 1 small spoonful of salt (一小勺食盐, yī xiǎo sháo shíyán)
  • 1 spoonful of Song Rong Xian (一勺松茸鲜, yī sháo sōngróng xiān) - a type of seasoning
  • Pepper powder (胡椒粉, hújiāofěn)
  • A small amount of light soy sauce (少许的生抽, shǎoxǔ de shēngchōu)
  • A little white sugar (点白糖, diǎn báitáng)
  • 2 drops of small grind sesame oil (两粒小磨香油, liǎng lì xiǎo mó xiāngyóu)
  • 1 large spoonful of starch (一大勺淀粉, yī dà sháo diànfěn)
  • Ginger and green onion juice (葱姜汁, cōngjiāng zhī)
  • ½ egg white (半个蛋清, bàn ge dànqīng)
  • Starch (淀粉, diànfěn)
  • Garlic (蒜, suàn)
  • Several green onions (几根小葱, jǐ gēn xiǎocōng)
  • Several small chili peppers (几个小米椒, jǐ ge xiǎomǐjiāo)
  • 1 spoonful of soy sauce (一勺生抽, yī sháo shēngchōu)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油, háoyóu)
  • White sugar (白糖, báitáng)
  • 1 spoonful of Song Rong Xian (一勺松茸鲜, yī sháo sōngróng xiān)
  • Pepper powder (胡椒粉, hújiāofěn)
  • 1 spoonful of cornstarch (一勺玉米淀粉, yī sháo yùmǐ diànfěn)
  • ½ bowl of water (小半碗的水, xiǎo bàn wǎn de shuǐ)
  • Dark soy sauce (老抽, lǎochōu)
  • Cooking oil (食用油, shíyòngyóu)
  • Onion (洋葱, yángcōng)
  • Chinese cabbage (小白菜, xiǎobáicài)

Instructions

  1. Wash the eggplant thoroughly, but do not peel it.
  2. Cut the eggplant into thick slices, almost but not completely through. Use chopsticks as a guide if needed for even slices.
  3. Prepare the pork: remove the skin from the fatty parts and finely chop into a slightly coarse mince.
  4. Season the pork: Add salt, Song Rong Xian, pepper powder, a little light soy sauce, white sugar, sesame oil, starch, ginger and green onion juice, and half an egg white. Mix thoroughly with gloves until well combined and slightly sticky.
  5. Coat each eggplant slice with starch.
  6. Stuff the pork mixture generously into each eggplant slice.
  7. Pan-fry the stuffed eggplant slices until golden brown on both sides. May need to do this in batches.
  8. While the eggplant is frying, prepare the sauce: Mix soy sauce, oyster sauce, salt, sugar, Song Rong Xian, pepper, cornstarch, and water. Add dark soy sauce for color.
  9. Prepare the casserole: Layer thinly sliced onions at the bottom of a casserole dish.
  10. Add the pan-fried eggplant slices to the casserole dish.
  11. Sauté minced garlic, sliced green onions, and chili peppers (optional) in the remaining oil from the pan.
  12. Add the sautéed mixture and chopped Chinese cabbage to the casserole.
  13. Pour the prepared sauce over the eggplant.
  14. Cover and simmer for 6 minutes.
  15. Garnish with chopped green onions before serving.

eggplant_cowpeas.txt - Eggplant and Cowpeas Stir-fry

Objectives

  • Learn a quick and less oily method for cooking eggplant and cowpeas.
  • Master a flavorful stir-fry sauce for enhanced taste.
  • Prepare a delicious side dish suitable for rice or wine.

Ingredients

  • 2 long eggplants
  • A handful of cowpeas
  • Several cloves garlic, flattened
  • A couple of small peppers, thinly sliced
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce
  • 1 tsp oyster sauce
  • A pinch of salt
  • A pinch of sugar
  • 1 tbsp Cantonese black bean sauce
  • A small amount of canola oil

Instructions

  1. Trim both ends of the cowpeas and cut them into thumb-sized pieces.
  2. Cut the eggplants into long strips.
  3. Steam the cowpeas and eggplants for 5-7 minutes until cooked.
  4. Prepare the sauce by combining soy sauce, oyster sauce, salt, sugar, and Cantonese black bean sauce.
  5. Heat a small amount of canola oil in a pan until it lightly smokes.
  6. Add the flattened garlic and sliced peppers to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant.
  7. Add the steamed eggplant and cowpeas to the pan.
  8. Pour the sauce over the vegetables.
  9. Stir-fry everything together over medium-high heat for about 1 minute, until well combined and heated through.

eggplant_longbeans.txt - Eggplant and Long Beans

Objectives

  • Learn a quick and less oily method for cooking eggplant and long beans.
  • Prepare a flavorful sauce to enhance the dish.
  • Master a simple stir-fry technique for perfectly cooked vegetables.

Ingredients

  • 2 long eggplants
  • A handful of long beans (cowpeas)
  • Several cloves garlic, flattened
  • A couple of small chili peppers, thinly sliced
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce
  • 1 tsp oyster sauce
  • A pinch of salt
  • A pinch of sugar
  • 1 tbsp Cantonese black bean sauce
  • A small amount of canola oil

Instructions

  1. Trim the ends of the long beans and cut them into thumb-sized pieces.
  2. Trim the ends of the eggplants and cut them into long strips.
  3. Steam both the long beans and eggplants for 5-7 minutes until cooked.
  4. While steaming, prepare the sauce by combining soy sauce, oyster sauce, salt, sugar, and Cantonese black bean sauce in a bowl. Stir well.
  5. Heat a small amount of canola oil in a wok or pan until it lightly smokes.
  6. Add the flattened garlic and sliced chilies to the hot oil and stir-fry briefly to release their aroma.
  7. Add the steamed eggplant and long beans to the pan.
  8. Pour the prepared sauce over the vegetables.
  9. Stir-fry everything together over medium-high heat for about 1 minute, until well combined and heated through. The sauce should coat the vegetables nicely.
  10. Serve immediately.

eggplant_meat_omelet.txt - Eggplant and Meat Omelet 茄子肉饼 - Qiézi ròu bǐng

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious eggplant and meat omelet.
  • Master the technique of preparing eggplant to enhance its texture.
  • Understand the importance of controlling heat during cooking.

Ingredients

  • 2 Eggplants (茄子 - qiézi)
  • 2-3 Eggs (鸡蛋 - jīdàn)
  • 1 piece of pork front leg meat (前腿肉 - qiántuǐ ròu), thinly sliced and minced
  • 1 small bunch of scallions (小葱 - xiǎocōng), chopped
  • 1 piece of ginger (生姜 - shēngjiāng), minced
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜 - suàn), minced
  • Salt (盐 - yán)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòngyóu)

Instructions

  1. Wash eggplants thoroughly, then soak in salted water to remove bitterness.
  2. Cut eggplants into 0.5 mm thin slices, then into thin strips.
  3. Mix eggplant strips with salt and let it sit for 5 minutes to draw out moisture.
  4. Mince the pork front leg meat.
  5. Chop scallions, mince ginger and garlic.
  6. Crack eggs into a bowl and whisk well.
  7. Heat cooking oil in a pan.
  8. Add minced scallions, ginger, and garlic to the hot oil and stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Add minced pork and stir-fry until cooked and fragrant.
  10. Add the eggplant strips and stir-fry for about 2 minutes until slightly softened.
  11. Pour in the whisked eggs and stir gently to allow for quick coagulation.
  12. Cover the pan and cook on low heat for about 2 minutes per side, or until golden brown.
  13. Serve hot.

eggplant_pancakes.txt - 香酥茄子饼 (Xiāng sū qiézi bǐng)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and affordable eggplant pancakes at home.
  • Master the technique of preparing eggplant for optimal texture and flavor.
  • Create a flavorful meat filling that complements the eggplant perfectly.

Ingredients

  • 2 medium-sized eggplants (same size, green skin preferred)
  • ½ medium onion (切丝, qiēsī - shredded, then diced)
  • 1 medium carrot (切丝, qiēsī - shredded, then diced)
  • 200g minced pork
  • A handful of scallions (切段, qiēduàn - cut into segments)
  • Salt (适量, shìliàng - to taste)
  • Pepper (少许, shǎoxǔ - a little)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce
  • 1 tbsp oyster sauce
  • 1 egg
  • Flour (适量, shìliàng - to taste)
  • Cooking oil
  • Sesame seeds (for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Clean the eggplants, cut off the tips, and slice into 2cm thick rounds.
  2. Using a tool, carefully remove the eggplant flesh, leaving the skin intact. Chop the eggplant flesh into small pieces quickly to prevent discoloration.
  3. Shred and dice the onion, thinly slice, shred, and dice the carrot. Mince the pork. Cut scallions into segments.
  4. In a bowl, combine the minced eggplant, onion, carrot, pork, scallions, salt, pepper, soy sauce, oyster sauce, and egg. Mix well.
  5. Add flour and mix until no dry particles remain. The mixture should be slightly sticky.
  6. Soak the eggplant skins in water to prevent oxidation.
  7. Heat cooking oil in an electric pancake maker (or frying pan).
  8. Place the eggplant skins in the electric pancake maker.
  9. Spoon the meat mixture into the eggplant skins, filling them about 80% full.
  10. Sprinkle sesame seeds on top.
  11. Cover and cook over low heat for 3 minutes.
  12. Flip and cook for another 4-5 minutes, or until golden brown and crispy.
  13. Serve hot. Press gently to check doneness; a springy texture indicates they are cooked.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=714IfDpQRSM

eggplant_stir_fry.txt - مقلي الباذنجان مع صلصة

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare delicious and nutritious eggplant stir-fry.
  • Master the technique of stir-frying eggplant to achieve a tender and flavorful result.
  • Understand how to create a flavorful sauce to complement the eggplant.

Ingredients

  • 2 long eggplants
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • A little white vinegar
  • 1 green chili pepper
  • 1 red chili pepper
  • Some green onions
  • 1 piece ginger
  • A few cloves of garlic
  • 3 eggs
  • 1 tbsp soybean paste
  • 1 tbsp fermented soybean paste
  • 1 tbsp light soy sauce
  • 1 tbsp sugar
  • 1 tbsp chicken extract (optional)
  • Appropriate amount of water
  • Cooking oil
  • Water starch (for thickening the sauce)

Instructions

  1. Wash and cut the eggplants into small cubes (about 1cm thick). Do not cut them too large.
  2. In a bowl, soak the eggplant cubes in water with 1 teaspoon salt and a little white vinegar for 10 minutes to prevent oxidation.
  3. Prepare the chili peppers, green onions, ginger, and garlic by finely chopping them.
  4. In a separate bowl, whisk 3 eggs in one direction until light and frothy.
  5. Prepare the sauce: In a small bowl, combine soybean paste, fermented soybean paste, light soy sauce, sugar, chicken extract (optional), and water. Mix well.
  6. Drain the eggplant cubes and pat them dry.
  7. In a large bowl, combine the drained eggplant cubes with the whisked eggs, ensuring each cube is coated.
  8. Heat cooking oil in a wok or large pan.
  9. Add the eggplant and egg mixture to the hot oil. Do not stir immediately. Let it set, then flatten with a spatula.
  10. Cook over low heat, gently shaking the pan occasionally, until the bottom is golden brown.
  11. Flip and continue cooking until golden brown on both sides.
  12. Increase the heat to high and stir-fry for about 3 minutes until the eggplant is cooked and the moisture is reduced.
  13. In the same wok, add more cooking oil and sauté the chopped green onions, ginger, and garlic over low heat until fragrant.
  14. Add the stir-fried eggplant to the wok.
  15. Pour in the prepared sauce and stir well to coat the eggplant.
  16. Bring the sauce to a simmer.
  17. Add the chopped chili peppers.
  18. Increase the heat and stir-fry until the chili peppers are tender.
  19. Mix in water starch to thicken the sauce.
  20. Serve hot, optionally over rice.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=lDok0DWV5jY

egg_tofu_cake.txt - Egg Tofu Cake 鸡蛋豆腐饼

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious egg tofu cake without steaming or boiling.
  • Master a simple and easy-to-learn recipe.
  • Create a flavorful dish that's both delicious and satisfying.

Ingredients

  • 2 blocks of soft tofu (cut into 1cm cubes)
  • 200g lean pork (minced)
  • Several cloves garlic (minced)
  • Several small chili peppers (finely sliced)
  • 4 eggs
  • Salt
  • Cooking oil
  • 2 tablespoons of Puning Doujiang (fermented soybean paste)
  • Water
  • Water starch (for thickening)
  • Spring onions (optional, for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Cut the tofu into 1cm cubes. Place in a bowl and set aside.
  2. Mince the pork. Place in a bowl.
  3. Mince the garlic and finely slice the chili peppers. Place in separate bowls.
  4. Crack 4 eggs into a bowl and whisk until smooth. Set aside.
  5. Boil water in a pot. Add salt and stir until dissolved.
  6. Add the tofu to the boiling water and blanch for 2 minutes.
  7. Remove the tofu with a slotted spoon, drain, and set aside.
  8. Heat a pan and add the blanched tofu. Stir-fry to dry the surface.
  9. Add cooking oil to the pan, stir-fry the tofu until lightly browned. Add a pinch of salt.
  10. Pour the egg mixture into the pan. Gently shake the pan to mix the eggs and tofu.
  11. Cover and simmer over low heat for 2 minutes until the bottom is golden brown.
  12. Flip the tofu and egg mixture and cook the other side until golden brown and crispy.
  13. Remove the cooked tofu and egg cake from the pan and set aside.
  14. Add the minced pork to the pan and stir-fry until browned.
  15. Add the minced garlic and chili peppers, stir-fry until fragrant.
  16. Add the Puning Doujiang and stir-fry to combine.
  17. Add half a bowl of water and bring to a boil.
  18. Add a small amount of water starch to thicken the sauce.
  19. Pour the sauce over the tofu and egg cake.
  20. Garnish with spring onions (optional).
  21. Serve immediately.

enoki_mushroom_egg_dish.txt - Enoki Mushroom and Egg Dish

Objectives

  • Learn to make a flavorful Enoki mushroom and egg dish.
  • Master a unique cooking method without boiling or frying.
  • Prepare a nutritious and delicious meal suitable for families.

Ingredients

  • 1 bunch Enoki mushrooms
  • 1/2 cucumber
  • 1 carrot
  • 1/2 green bell pepper
  • 1 small piece of ginger
  • 2 cloves garlic
  • 1 small white onion
  • Some green onions
  • 3 yuan worth of lean ground meat
  • 3 eggs
  • Salt
  • Sugar
  • Soy sauce
  • Oyster sauce
  • Cornstarch
  • Water
  • Cooking oil
  • Sesame oil (optional)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Enoki Mushrooms: Remove the roots, cut in half lengthwise, then tear into smaller pieces by hand. Wash thoroughly, soak in water with salt for 10 minutes, drain, and set aside.
  2. Prepare the Cucumber: Cut the cucumber in half, then into quarters. Thinly slice, then dice into small cubes.
  3. Prepare the Carrot: Slice the carrot thinly, then dice into small pieces.
  4. Prepare the Green Bell Pepper: Remove the stem and seeds. Dice into small cubes.
  5. Prepare the Aromatics: Finely mince the ginger, garlic, and white onion. Chop the green onions.
  6. Prepare the Sauce: In a bowl, mix soy sauce, oyster sauce, a pinch of salt and sugar, half a teaspoon of cornstarch, and a little water. Stir well.
  7. Prepare the Eggs: Whisk 3 eggs with a pinch of salt.
  8. Cook the Enoki Mushroom and Egg: Heat cooking oil in a pan. Add the Enoki mushrooms and egg mixture. Spread evenly. Cook until set, pressing gently with a spatula to ensure even cooking. Cook until golden brown on both sides.
  9. Cook the Ground Meat: Add cooking oil to the pan. Add the ground meat and cook until browned. Add the onion, ginger, and garlic; stir-fry.
  10. Combine Vegetables and Meat: Add the diced carrots, cucumber, and green bell pepper to the ground meat. Stir-fry for about a minute until slightly softened. Add the red pepper.
  11. Add Sauce and Finish: Pour in the prepared sauce and stir until thickened. Add sesame oil before serving (optional).
  12. Serve: Garnish with chopped green onions. Serve the Enoki mushroom and egg dish over the ground meat and vegetable mixture.

enoki_mushroom_egg_omelet.txt - Enoki Mushroom and Egg Omelet

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious Enoki mushroom and egg omelet.
  • Master a unique cooking method that avoids boiling or frying.
  • Prepare a family-friendly dish with simple, accessible ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 1 pack Enoki mushrooms
  • 1/2 cucumber
  • 1/2 carrot
  • 1/2 green bell pepper
  • 1 small piece of ginger
  • 2 cloves garlic
  • 1 small white onion
  • Some green onion
  • 3 eggs
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • 13 sesame oil
  • Ground meat (amount unspecified)
  • Soy sauce (amount unspecified)
  • Oyster sauce (amount unspecified)
  • Sugar (amount unspecified)
  • 1/2 teaspoon cornstarch
  • Water (amount unspecified)
  • Sesame oil (amount unspecified for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Clean the Enoki mushrooms: Remove roots, cut in half, tear into small pieces, soak in water with salt for 10 minutes.
  2. Prepare the vegetables: Cut cucumber into small cubes, thinly slice carrot and dice, dice green bell pepper, mince ginger and garlic, finely chop white onion and green onions.
  3. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, combine soy sauce, oyster sauce, salt, sugar, cornstarch, and water. Mix well.
  4. Prepare the meat: Finely chop ground meat.
  5. Prepare the eggs: Whisk 3 eggs with salt and sesame oil.
  6. Cook the omelet: Heat oil in a pan, add Enoki mushrooms and egg mixture. Spread evenly, cook until set, flipping halfway through to ensure even cooking and a crispy exterior.
  7. Stir-fry the meat and vegetables: Stir-fry ground meat until browned, add onion, ginger, and garlic. Add carrot and cucumber, stir-fry for 1 minute. Add bell pepper and stir-fry for another minute.
  8. Combine and finish: Add the prepared sauce to the meat and vegetables, stir until thickened.
  9. Serve: Top the omelet with the meat and vegetable stir-fry. Garnish with sesame oil and green onions.

fansi_qiezi_bao.txt - 粉丝茄子煲 (Fěnsi Qiézi Bāo)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy 粉丝茄子煲 (Fěnsi Qiézi Bāo).
  • Master the technique of preparing eggplant to prevent oxidation and maximize flavor.
  • Understand how to create a flavorful sauce to enhance the dish.

Ingredients

  • 2 servings of粉絲 (fěnsi) -粉絲 (bean thread noodles)
  • 2 eggplants (茄子 - qiézi)
  • 2 slices of lean pork (瘦肉 - shòuròu)
  • 1 green pepper (青椒 - qīngjiāo)
  • 1 red pepper (红椒 - hóngjiāo)
  • Several scallions (葱 - cōng)
  • White vinegar (白醋 - báicù)
  • Salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • Soy sauce (生抽 - shēngchōu)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油 - háoyóu)
  • Black vinegar (陈醋 - chéncù)
  • Dark soy sauce (老抽 - lǎochōu)
  • Cornstarch (淀粉 - diànfěn)
  • Water (清水 - qīngshuǐ)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòngyóu)

Instructions

  1. Soak two servings of粉絲 (bean thread noodles) in 60°C warm water until soft.
  2. Cut off the stem of the eggplants, peel them, wash them, and cut them into thin strips.
  3. Place the eggplant strips in a bowl, add a little white vinegar to prevent oxidation, and add two small spoons of salt. Mix well and let it marinate for 10 minutes.
  4. Cut the lean pork into thin slices, then mince it coarsely. Set aside.
  5. Cut the green and red peppers into small squares, removing the seeds. Set aside.
  6. Separate the scallions into white and green parts. Mince the white parts and chop the green parts into small pieces. Set aside.
  7. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, mix one spoonful of soy sauce, oyster sauce, half a spoonful of black vinegar, a little dark soy sauce for color, one spoonful of cornstarch, and a small amount of water. Mix well. Set aside.
  8. Place the soaked粉絲 (bean thread noodles) at the bottom of a sand pot.
  9. Rinse the marinated eggplant to remove excess salt, and squeeze out excess water.
  10. Heat a small amount of cooking oil in a wok or pan. Add the eggplant and stir-fry for about 88 seconds until softened. Set aside.
  11. Add the minced pork to the wok and stir-fry until white and fragrant.
  12. Add the stir-fried eggplant and stir-fry until fragrant.
  13. Add the green and red peppers and white parts of the scallions. Stir-fry for 15 seconds.
  14. Pour the prepared sauce into the wok and stir until the sauce coats the eggplant.
  15. Drizzle with a little cooking oil and sprinkle with chopped green scallions.
  16. Pour the eggplant mixture into the sand pot with the粉絲 (bean thread noodles). Cover and simmer over low heat for 3 minutes.
  17. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=xlpekOreu68

fermented_cabbage.txt - مخلل الملفوف

Objectives

  • Prepare a refreshing fermented cabbage dish.
  • Learn a unique cooking method for cabbage.
  • Create a crunchy and flavorful side dish.

Ingredients

  • 1 large head of cabbage
  • Several cloves of garlic
  • Dried chili peppers (amount not specified)
  • Rice water (amount not specified)
  • Salt (amount not specified)
  • White vinegar (amount not specified)
  • 2 kg weight (for pressing cabbage)
  • Lean minced meat (optional)
  • Cooking oil
  • Lard (optional, for flavor)
  • Chicken broth (amount not specified)
  • Light soy sauce (amount not specified)

Instructions

  1. Clean the cabbage thoroughly; no need to remove the outer leaves.
  2. Place the cabbage in a large bowl. Add minced garlic and dried chilies for flavor. Set aside.
  3. Rinse rice in a bowl; use the rice water to wash vegetables or water plants.
  4. Pour the rice water into a pot and bring to a boil over high heat.
  5. Once boiling, turn off the heat and pour the water over the cabbage.
  6. Use chopsticks to ensure the cabbage is submerged.
  7. Add a handful of salt and some white vinegar to promote fermentation.
  8. Place a 2 kg weight on top of the cabbage and cover.
  9. Let it ferment for a day and a half.
  10. After fermentation, rinse the cabbage thoroughly under clean water.
  11. Drain and chop the cabbage; avoid chopping too finely to maintain crunchiness.
  12. Finely chop the soaked dried chilies and garlic.
  13. Optionally, add lean minced meat for extra flavor. Mince the meat.
  14. Heat oil in a pan; add lard for extra aroma (optional).
  15. Add the minced meat and cook until browned.
  16. Increase heat and stir-fry all ingredients for about 80 seconds until fragrant.
  17. Add chicken broth, light soy sauce, and stir well.
  18. Continue stir-frying until flavors blend.
  19. Serve the fermented cabbage with steamed rice.

fish_fragrant_eggs.txt - 鱼香鸡蛋 (Yúxiāng jǐdàn)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a flavorful and easy Fish Fragrant Egg dish.
  • Master the technique of preparing the eggs for a tender texture.
  • Understand how to balance the sweet, sour, and spicy flavors in the sauce.

Ingredients

  • 3-4 fresh eggs (鸡蛋 - jǐdàn)
  • 1/2 teaspoon salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • 1 tablespoon water (清水 - qīngshuǐ)
  • 1 teaspoon white vinegar (白醋 - báicù)
  • 1 medium carrot, julienned (胡萝卜 - húluóbo)
  • 2-3 scallions, chopped (小葱 - xiǎocōng)
  • 1 piece ginger, minced (生姜 - shēngjiāng)
  • 3-4 cloves garlic, minced (大蒜 - dàsuàn)
  • 1 tablespoon rice vinegar (陈醋 - chéncù)
  • 1 tablespoon soy sauce (生抽 - shēngchōu)
  • 1/2 teaspoon pepper (胡椒粉 - hújiāofěn)
  • 1 teaspoon sugar (白糖 - báitáng)
  • 1 teaspoon cornstarch (玉米淀粉 - yùmǐ diànfěn)
  • 1 teaspoon oyster sauce (蚝油 - háoyóu)
  • 1 tablespoon chili powder (细辣椒面 - xì làjiāomiàn)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòngyóu)

Instructions

  1. Wash eggs with salt water for 5 minutes to remove surface bacteria. Crack eggs into a bowl, add white vinegar, and whisk until well combined. Set aside.
  2. Julienne the carrot and chop the scallions, ginger, and garlic. Set aside.
  3. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, combine rice vinegar, soy sauce, pepper, sugar, cornstarch, oyster sauce, chili powder, and a little water. Mix well and set aside.
  4. Heat oil in a pan until slightly smoking. Add the egg mixture and quickly scramble until set but still tender. Remove from pan.
  5. Add the ginger and garlic to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant.
  6. Add the carrots and stir-fry until softened.
  7. Add the sauce to the pan and stir-fry for about 50 seconds until thickened.
  8. Add the scrambled eggs back to the pan and stir-fry to coat with the sauce.
  9. Garnish with chopped scallions.
  10. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=nu2ltDvXgk8

five_spice_pork_belly_mushroom.txt - 五花肉烧蘑菇 (Wǔhuāròu shāo mógū)

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare delicious and tender five-spice pork belly with mushrooms.
  • Master the technique of creating a rich and flavorful sauce.
  • Learn to properly clean and prepare both pork belly and mushrooms.

Ingredients

  • 500g Pork belly (五花肉 - wǔhuāròu), pre-cleaned
  • 250g Fresh shiitake mushrooms (香菇 - xiānggū)
  • 1/2 Purple onion (紫皮洋葱 - zǐpí yángcōng)
  • Several cloves garlic (蒜 - suàn)
  • 2-3 Dried chilies (干辣椒 - gān làjiāo)
  • 2 Scallions (蒜苗 - suànmiáo)
  • 1 tbsp Salt (盐 - yán)
  • 1 tbsp Sugar (白糖 - báitáng) (Ideally rock sugar/冰糖 - bīngtáng)
  • 1 tbsp Soy sauce (生抽 - shēng chōu)
  • 1 tsp Dark soy sauce (老抽 - lǎo chōu)
  • 1 tsp Cooking wine (料酒 - liàojiǔ)
  • 1 tbsp Chicken bouillon (鸡汁 - jī zhī)
  • Star anise (八角 - bājiǎo)
  • Cinnamon stick (桂皮 - guìpí)
  • Bay leaves (香叶 - xiāngyè)
  • Ginger (生姜 - shēngjiāng)
  • 1 piece Scallion (葱 - cōng)
  • Flour (面粉 - miànfěn)

Instructions

  1. Clean the pork belly: Rinse the pork belly, remove any impurities, and soak it in salted water for 10 minutes to remove impurities and blood.
  2. Boil the pork belly: Place the pork belly in a pot with water, add cooking wine, salt, star anise, cinnamon, and dried chilies. Boil for 10 minutes. Remove and let cool.
  3. Cut the pork belly: Slice the pork belly into large thick slices, then cut into smaller square pieces.
  4. Prepare the mushrooms: Remove the stems from the shiitake mushrooms. Wash thoroughly with salt and flour, paying attention to the inner surface. Slice into smaller pieces.
  5. Prepare the aromatics: Finely slice the purple onion, roughly chop the garlic, slice the dried chilies, and chop the scallions.
  6. Caramelize the sugar: Heat oil in a wok or pan. Add sugar and cook over low heat until caramelized to an amber color.
  7. Stir-fry the pork belly: Add the pork belly to the caramelized sugar and stir-fry until evenly browned.
  8. Add aromatics and braising liquid: Add star anise, cinnamon, bay leaves, ginger, and scallions to the pork belly. Stir-fry until fragrant, then add a large bowl of water, enough to cover the pork belly. Bring to a boil, then reduce heat and simmer for 30 minutes.
  9. Add soy sauce and color: Add dark soy sauce (for color) and light soy sauce (for flavor). Stir well, cover, and continue simmering.
  10. Add mushrooms: Remove the aromatics. Add the mushrooms, salt, and chicken bouillon. Stir, cover, and simmer for 3-5 minutes until mushrooms are tender.
  11. Add garlic and chilies: Add the chopped garlic and dried chilies. Stir-fry briefly.
  12. Add scallions: Add the chopped scallions and stir-fry until wilted.
  13. Serve: Place sliced onions in the bottom of a serving pot (e.g., a clay pot). Add the finished five-spice pork belly and mushrooms. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=eZMFNQ_ag-k

five_spice_pork_belly.txt - 五花肉电饭煲焖制

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious five-spice pork belly using a rice cooker.
  • Master a simple, beginner-friendly cooking method.
  • Achieve tender, flavorful pork belly without adding water.

Ingredients

  • 1 jin 3 liang (approximately 750g) of five-spice pork belly (五花肉)
  • 1 block of red fermented tofu (紅油豆腐乳)
  • 1 tbsp light soy sauce (生抽)
  • A dash of dark soy sauce (老抽)
  • 1 tbsp oyster sauce (蠔油)
  • 1 tsp sweet bean sauce (甜麵醬)
  • 1 tbsp yellow soybean paste (黃豆醬)
  • 1 stalk of scallion (蔥), white and green parts separated
  • A piece of ginger (薑), julienned
  • 1/2 onion (洋蔥), diced
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜), roughly chopped
  • 100g beer (啤酒)
  • Minced garlic (蒜末)
  • Garlic chives or scallion (大蒜葉或蔥花)
  • 1 tsp chili powder (細辣椒麵)
  • A dash of light soy sauce (生抽)
  • A dash of aged vinegar (陳醋)
  • A pinch of sugar (白糖)
  • A dash of sesame oil (小磨香油)

Instructions

  1. Clean the pork belly: Use a lighter to singe off any remaining hairs. Rinse with warm water and scrape off any remaining dirt.
  2. Prepare the marinade: In a bowl, mash the red fermented tofu. Add light soy sauce, dark soy sauce, oyster sauce, sweet bean sauce, and yellow soybean paste. Mix well.
  3. Prepare aromatics: Chop the scallion (separate white and green parts), ginger, and garlic.
  4. Marinate the pork: Add the chopped scallion greens, ginger, and the prepared marinade to the pork belly. Mix thoroughly, ensuring the pork is coated evenly. Marinate for 40 minutes.
  5. Prepare the rice cooker: Place the diced onion, chopped scallion whites, ginger, and garlic in the rice cooker inner pot. Arrange evenly.
  6. Add the pork: After 40 minutes, place the marinated pork belly on top of the aromatics in the rice cooker. Pour the remaining marinade over the pork.
  7. Cook the pork: Pour 100g of beer along the sides of the pot. Close the lid and cook on the "cook rice" setting for 40 minutes.
  8. Prepare the dipping sauce: While the pork is cooking, prepare a dipping sauce with minced garlic, garlic chives or scallion, chili powder, light soy sauce, aged vinegar, sugar, and sesame oil. Mix well.
  9. Serve: After 40 minutes, open the rice cooker. Spoon out some of the cooking liquid and add it to the dipping sauce. Remove the pork, slice into bite-sized pieces, and arrange on a plate. Serve with the dipping sauce.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=X-cbbXBKhf0

five_spice_pork_belly_with_mushrooms.txt - 五花肉烧蘑菇

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and tender five-spice pork belly dish with mushrooms.
  • Master the technique of preparing and cooking the pork belly for optimal flavor and texture.
  • Understand how to enhance the overall taste with various seasonings and cooking methods.

Ingredients

  • 500g pork belly (五花肉), skin removed and cleaned
  • 200g fresh shiitake mushrooms (香菇)
  • 1/2 purple onion (紫皮洋葱), thinly sliced
  • Several cloves garlic (蒜子), halved
  • 2-3 dried chilies (干辣椒), sliced
  • 2 scallions (蒜苗), chopped
  • 1 tbsp salt (食盐)
  • 1 tbsp sugar (白糖) or rock sugar (冰糖)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽)
  • 1 tsp dark soy sauce (老抽)
  • 1 tsp chicken essence (鸡汁)
  • 1 tbsp cooking oil (食用油)
  • 1 star anise (八角)
  • 1 cinnamon stick (桂皮)
  • 2 bay leaves (香叶)
  • 1 piece ginger (生姜)
  • 1 scallion section (葱节)
  • Water (清水)

Instructions

  1. Clean the pork belly thoroughly, removing any impurities. Cut into large thick slices, then into smaller square pieces.
  2. Soak the pork belly in salted water for 10 minutes to remove impurities and reduce odor.
  3. Boil the pork belly with star anise, cinnamon, dried chilies, bay leaves, and a splash of cooking wine for 10 minutes. Remove and let cool.
  4. Clean the shiitake mushrooms, remove stems, and slice. Wash thoroughly with salt and flour to remove dirt. Slice into smaller pieces.
  5. Prepare the other ingredients: slice purple onion, halve garlic cloves, slice dried chilies, and chop scallions.
  6. Heat oil in a wok or pan. Add sugar and stir over low heat until caramelized (amber color).
  7. Add pork belly and stir-fry until browned.
  8. Add star anise, cinnamon, bay leaves, ginger, and scallion section. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Add water to cover the pork belly. Bring to a boil, then reduce heat and simmer for 30 minutes.
  10. Remove the aromatics (spices and ginger/scallion). Add shiitake mushrooms, salt, and chicken essence. Stir-fry and simmer for 3-5 minutes until mushrooms are cooked through.
  11. Add garlic and dried chilies, stir-fry briefly. Add scallions and stir-fry until wilted.
  12. Serve the braised pork belly and mushrooms over sliced onions in a heat-retaining pot, if desired.

five_spice_pork.txt - 五花肉

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare delicious five-spice pork using simple ingredients.
  • Master the technique of steaming and stir-frying for optimal flavor and texture.
  • Understand how to balance flavors without using additional salt.

Ingredients

  • 1 jin 2 liang (approximately 750g) fresh five-layer pork belly (五花肉)
  • Water (清水)
  • Garlic sprouts (蒜苗), sliced diagonally
  • Garlic leaves (蒜叶), sliced straight
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒), sliced diagonally
  • Several green bell peppers (青椒), sliced diagonally
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜), minced
  • A piece of ginger (生姜), minced
  • Several scallions (小葱), white parts only, minced
  • 豆豉 (Douchi, fermented black soybeans)
  • Red oil Doubanjiang (红油豆瓣酱)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • Dark soy sauce (老抽)
  • Light soy sauce (生抽)
  • A pinch of sugar (白糖)
  • A pinch of MSG (optional,味精)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the pork: Burn the pork skin with a hot pan (猪皮朝下烫) to remove impurities and hair. Immerse in water for 2 minutes, then scrape and thoroughly wash the skin.
  2. Steam the pork: Steam the cleaned pork belly in a steamer over high heat for 15 minutes. Remove and let cool slightly.
  3. Prepare the aromatics: Slice garlic sprouts and leaves, chili peppers, and green peppers. Mince garlic, ginger, and scallions (white parts only).
  4. Slice the pork: Cut the cooled pork belly into thin, even slices.
  5. Stir-fry the pork: Heat a pan and stir-fry the pork slices over low heat until the skin is golden brown and some fat renders. Reserve the rendered fat.
  6. Sauté aromatics and seasonings: Add minced garlic, ginger, and scallions to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant. Add douchi and red oil doubanjiang, stir-frying until fragrant and the oil turns red.
  7. Add vegetables and seasonings: Add the sliced green and chili peppers and garlic stems. Season with oyster sauce, dark soy sauce, light soy sauce, a pinch of sugar, and a pinch of MSG (optional). Stir-fry until everything is cooked through and flavors are combined.
  8. Finish and serve: Add the garlic leaves, stir-fry briefly, and remove from heat. Serve immediately. Note: No salt is needed due to the salt content in the sauces.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=L_wRF3OKY70

five_spice_pork_with_glutinous_rice.txt - 五花肉糯米饭

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious, tender five-spice pork with glutinous rice.
  • Master the technique of preparing and cooking the pork for optimal texture.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to enhance the overall taste of the dish.

Ingredients

  • 200g glutinous rice (糯米, nù mǐ)
  • 8 RMB/jin five-layer pork belly (五花肉, wǔ huā ròu)
  • 2 eggs (鸡蛋, jī dàn)
  • 50g cornstarch (玉米淀粉, yù mǐ diàn fěn)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油, háo yóu)
  • 1 tbsp salt (食盐, shí yán)
  • 1 tbsp sugar (白糖, bái táng)
  • 1 tbsp yellow soybean paste (黄豆酱, huáng dòu jiàng)
  • Some light soy sauce (生抽, shēng chōu)
  • A little dark soy sauce (老抽, lǎo chōu)
  • Water (清水, qīng shuǐ)
  • Cooking oil (食用油, shí yòng yóu)
  • Spring onions (葱花, cōng huā)

Instructions

  1. Rinse the glutinous rice gently several times without rubbing to avoid damaging the nutrients. Drain the water; reserve for other uses. Soak the rice in water for 40 minutes.
  2. Prepare the pork belly: Scorch the skin of the pork belly over a high heat until tiger stripes appear. Soak in warm water for 2 minutes, then scrape off any impurities. Rinse and cut into small, square pieces (similar to mahjong tiles).
  3. Whisk two eggs until light and fluffy, then add to the pork and mix well. Add cornstarch and mix until each piece of pork is evenly coated.
  4. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, combine oyster sauce, salt, sugar, yellow soybean paste, light soy sauce, dark soy sauce, and water. Stir until well combined.
  5. Heat oil in a pan over medium-low heat. Fry the pork pieces until golden brown on all sides, turning frequently to prevent burning. Remove and drain excess oil.
  6. Add the fried pork to a large bowl. Pour the sauce over the pork and mix well, ensuring each piece is coated. Let it marinate for 10 minutes.
  7. Drain the soaked glutinous rice. Spread it evenly in a larger bowl. Arrange the marinated pork pieces on top of the rice. Pour any remaining sauce over the pork and rice.
  8. Steam in a covered steamer over high heat for 30 minutes.
  9. Garnish with chopped spring onions before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=NRenUyUBkiA

five_star_spicy_peppers.txt - Five-Star Spicy Peppers

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious five-star spicy peppers.
  • Master the technique of deep-frying peanuts for added texture.
  • Understand the importance of properly preparing ingredients and controlling oil temperature.

Ingredients

  • 400g red chili peppers (红辣椒)
  • 20g salt (盐)
  • 2 tablespoons sugar (糖)
  • 30g water (水)
  • 100g peanuts (花生)
  • ½ large onion (洋葱)
  • 2 scallions (葱)
  • Coriander (芫荽)
  • Ginger (姜)
  • Garlic (蒜)
  • 800g sesame oil (芝麻油)
  • 1 tablespoon white sesame seeds (白芝麻)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the chili peppers: Add 400g chili peppers, 20g salt, 2 tablespoons sugar, and 30g water to a bowl. Mix well using chopsticks, ensuring all ingredients are combined. Set aside.

  2. Prepare the peanuts: Add 100g peanuts to a pan and dry-fry over medium heat for 6-7 minutes, stirring constantly, until fragrant and lightly browned. Remove from heat and let cool.

  3. Prepare the aromatics: Finely chop ½ large onion, 2 scallions, coriander, ginger, and garlic. Set aside.

  4. Deep-fry aromatics: Heat 800g sesame oil in a wok to 45-50°C. Add the chopped onion, garlic, and ginger. Fry until fragrant and slightly browned, stirring constantly.

  5. Add spices and fry: After 2 minutes of frying the aromatics, add the spices and continue frying for another 3-5 minutes until slightly dry. Remove from oil and set aside. The fried spices are not consumed.

  6. Prepare the peanuts: Use a hair dryer (or gently toss) to remove excess oil from the fried peanuts. Place the peanuts in a plastic bag and gently crush them.

  7. Combine ingredients: Add the crushed peanuts and 1 tablespoon of white sesame seeds to the prepared chili peppers. Mix well.

  8. Add oil to chili peppers: Pour the hot oil from step 4 over the chili pepper mixture. Repeat the process. The oil will evaporate some of the water.

  9. Add optional flavorings: Add a small amount of white wine to enhance the flavor and preservation time. Mix well.

  10. Serve: Let the chili peppers sit for a while, allowing the oil to rise to the surface. Serve immediately or store in the refrigerator.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=i9C-c_bdMjc

four_nourishing_soups.txt - Four Nourishing Soups

Objectives

  • Learn to make four delicious and nutritious soups.
  • Master techniques for preparing various ingredients.
  • Understand the importance of proper cooking methods for optimal flavor and texture.

Ingredients

Soup 1: Tofu and Three Delights Soup

  • 1 block of tofu
  • Shiitake mushrooms
  • 2 eggs
  • 1 small carrot
  • Ginger
  • Scallions
  • 2 stalks of cilantro
  • Salt
  • Sugar
  • White pepper
  • Light soy sauce
  • Water
  • Cornstarch

Soup 2: Radish and Pork Rib Soup

  • Pork ribs (tiger head bone preferred)
  • 2 white radishes
  • Salt
  • Flour
  • Ginger
  • Scallions
  • Vegetable oil

Soup 3: Spinach and Egg Soup

  • 1 small bunch of spinach
  • 2 eggs
  • 1 small carrot
  • Scallions
  • Ginger
  • Cornstarch
  • Salt
  • Vegetable oil
  • Mushroom seasoning
  • White pepper
  • Light soy sauce

Soup 4: Winter Melon and Pork Rib Soup

  • 1 lb pork ribs
  • 1 piece winter melon
  • Ginger
  • Scallions
  • Salt
  • Flour
  • Vegetable oil

Instructions

Soup 1: Tofu and Three Delights Soup

  1. Blanch tofu in boiling water to remove beany smell.
  2. Tear shiitake mushrooms into small pieces and rinse.
  3. Whisk 2 eggs until smooth.
  4. Dice carrot and mince ginger and scallions.
  5. Mince cilantro, reserving stems for tea.
  6. Dice tofu into 0.5cm cubes.
  7. Prepare sauce: mix salt, sugar, pepper, soy sauce, and water.
  8. Prepare cornstarch slurry: mix cornstarch and water.
  9. Boil water, add ginger for 15 seconds.
  10. Add carrots for 15 seconds, then tofu for 30 seconds.
  11. Add mushrooms and simmer for 1 minute.
  12. Add cornstarch slurry in three additions until desired thickness.
  13. Turn off heat, add egg in two additions, stirring gently.
  14. Return to high heat, stir.
  15. Add sauce, stir to combine.
  16. Garnish with cilantro and scallions.

Soup 2: Radish and Pork Rib Soup

  1. Season pork ribs with salt and flour, massage well, and soak in warm water for 5 minutes.
  2. Peel and cut radishes into chunks.
  3. Mince ginger and make a scallion knot.
  4. Rinse pork ribs thoroughly.
  5. Heat oil, stir-fry ginger until fragrant.
  6. Add ribs and stir-fry until slightly browned.
  7. Add boiling water, bring to a boil, skim off foam.
  8. Add scallion knot, cover, and simmer for 38 minutes.
  9. Remove scallion knot.
  10. Add radishes, cover, and simmer for 15 minutes.
  11. Add salt, stir, and simmer for 2 minutes.

Soup 3: Spinach and Egg Soup

  1. Trim spinach, wash thoroughly.
  2. Cut spinach into segments.
  3. Dice carrot and mince scallions and ginger.
  4. Whisk eggs until smooth.
  5. Prepare cornstarch slurry.
  6. Boil water, add salt and oil.
  7. Blanch spinach for 30 seconds, then plunge into cold water.
  8. Squeeze out excess water.
  9. Heat oil, stir-fry ginger and scallions.
  10. Add water, salt, mushroom seasoning, pepper, and soy sauce.
  11. Add carrots, simmer for 2 minutes.
  12. Add cornstarch slurry.
  13. Turn off heat, add eggs, stir gently.
  14. Add spinach, stir, and simmer for 30 seconds.
  15. Garnish with scallions.

Soup 4: Winter Melon and Pork Rib Soup

  1. Season pork ribs with salt and flour, soak in water for 20 minutes.
  2. Cut winter melon into chunks.
  3. Chop scallions and slice ginger.
  4. Rinse pork ribs thoroughly, remove excess fat.
  5. Heat oil, stir-fry scallions and ginger.
  6. Add ribs and stir-fry until moisture evaporates.
  7. Add boiling water, bring to a boil, cover, and simmer for 40 minutes.
  8. Remove scallions and ginger.
  9. Add winter melon, corn, and carrots.
  10. Cover and simmer for 18 minutes.
  11. Add salt, stir, and turn off heat.
  12. Garnish with scallions.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=U8mjykzF8N8

fragrant_dried_tofu.txt - Fragrant Dried Tofu (香干)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and fragrant dried tofu.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful cooking method.
  • Understand the importance of preparing the sauce in advance.

Ingredients

  • Dried smoked tofu (香干) (amount not specified)
  • Warm water (amount not specified)
  • Red chili peppers (amount not specified), thinly sliced
  • Green chili peppers (amount not specified), thinly sliced
  • Garlic (amount not specified), sliced
  • Garlic sprouts (2 stalks), diagonally sliced
  • 1 tbsp light soy sauce (生抽)
  • A little dark soy sauce (老抽)
  • Some oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • Salt (amount not specified)
  • Sugar (amount not specified)
  • 1 tsp cornstarch (生粉)
  • Water (amount not specified)
  • Cooking oil (amount not specified)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the dried tofu: Soak the dried smoked tofu in warm water, then clean and cut into pieces.
  2. Prepare the chili peppers: Thinly slice red and green chili peppers and set aside.
  3. Prepare the garlic: Slice garlic and garlic sprouts and set aside.
  4. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, combine light soy sauce, dark soy sauce, oyster sauce, salt, sugar, cornstarch, and water. Mix well and set aside.
  5. Cook the tofu: Add a little water to a wok or pan. Add the dried tofu, a pinch of salt, and a little dark soy sauce for color. Cook over high heat for 2 minutes. Remove with a slotted spoon to drain excess water.
  6. Stir-fry aromatics: Heat oil in the wok. Add sliced garlic and garlic sprouts; stir-fry until fragrant.
  7. Stir-fry tofu: Add the drained dried tofu to the wok. Stir-fry over high heat until evenly coated.
  8. Add chili peppers: Add the sliced red and green chili peppers; stir-fry until slightly softened.
  9. Add sauce: Pour in the prepared sauce and stir-fry until the sauce coats the tofu evenly.
  10. Add garlic sprouts: Add the garlic sprouts and stir-fry until cooked through.
  11. Serve: The fragrant dried tofu is ready to serve.

fried_bean_curd_with_egg.txt - Fried Bean Curd with Egg

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple, nutritious, and delicious fried bean curd with egg dish.
  • Master the techniques for preparing and cooking the ingredients to achieve optimal taste and texture.
  • Understand the importance of marinating beans and preparing a flavorful sauce in advance.

Ingredients

  • 1.5 lbs green beans (about a dollar's worth)
  • Several eggs (number unspecified)
  • 1 spoonful of salt
  • Water for washing beans
  • Handful of garlic seeds
  • Chili (optional)
  • Several green peppers
  • Pinch of salt (for seasoning)
  • Sugar (small amount for freshness)
  • Small spoonful of starch
  • Moderate amount of soy sauce
  • Small amount of soy sauce (for color)
  • Dash of oyster sauce
  • ½ spoonful of Yangtze water (likely rice wine)
  • Cooking oil (double the usual amount for frying)
  • White vinegar (small amount to remove fishy smell)

Instructions

  1. Clean and cut green beans into 5mm dice.
  2. Add a spoonful of salt, mix well, and marinate for 10 minutes to remove green taste.
  3. Wash off excess salt with water to keep beans crisp.
  4. Prepare garlic, chili (optional), and green peppers; slice and set aside.
  5. Make the sauce: Combine salt, sugar, starch, soy sauce, oyster sauce, and Yangtze water in a bowl. Stir well.
  6. Crack eggs into a bowl with the marinated beans. Add a little white vinegar to remove fishy smell. Mix well.
  7. Heat double the usual amount of cooking oil in a pan.
  8. Pour the bean and egg mixture into the hot oil and stir constantly until the eggs are set.
  9. Reduce heat to medium-low and fry until the bottom is set, then flip and fry the other side until golden brown.
  10. Remove the fried bean curd and eggs from the pan.
  11. Add garlic, chili (optional), and green peppers to the pan. Stir-fry on low heat until fragrant.
  12. Add the fried bean curd and eggs to the pan.
  13. Pour in the prepared sauce and stir-fry until well combined and heated through.
  14. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=MKv_Bu2Pu5Q

fried_beans_eggs.txt - Fried Beans with Eggs

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple, nutritious, and delicious fried bean and egg dish.
  • Master the technique of preparing beans for optimal flavor and texture.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to complement the fried beans and eggs.

Ingredients

  • 1.5 lbs green beans (about a dollar's worth)
  • Several eggs (quantity unspecified)
  • 1 spoonful of salt
  • 1 handful of garlic cloves
  • 1-2 chili peppers (optional)
  • Several green peppers
  • Pinch of salt
  • Pinch of sugar
  • 1 small spoonful of starch
  • Moderate amount of soy sauce
  • A little soy sauce (for color)
  • Dash of oyster sauce
  • 1/2 spoonful of Yangtze River water (likely rice wine)
  • White vinegar
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Trim the ends of the green beans and cut them into 5mm dice.
  2. Add a spoonful of salt to the beans and massage them for 10 minutes to remove the green taste and add flavor.
  3. Wash the beans to remove excess salt, ensuring they remain crisp.
  4. Prepare the sauce: Combine a pinch of salt, sugar, starch, soy sauce, a little soy sauce for color, oyster sauce, and Yangtze River water in a bowl. Stir well.
  5. Crack eggs into a bowl, add a little white vinegar to remove fishy smell, and mix with the beans.
  6. Heat a wok or pan with double the usual amount of cooking oil.
  7. Add the bean and egg mixture, stirring constantly until the eggs set.
  8. Reduce heat to medium-low, and continue frying until the bottom is set.
  9. Flip the mixture and fry until golden brown on both sides.
  10. Remove the fried beans and eggs from the pan.
  11. Add sliced garlic, green and red peppers to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant.
  12. Add the fried beans and eggs and the prepared sauce to the pan.
  13. Stir-fry over high heat until well combined and heated through.
  14. Serve immediately.

fried_cabbage_vermicelli.txt - Fried Cabbage Vermicelli

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy fried cabbage vermicelli dish.
  • Master the technique of preparing chewy vermicelli and crispy cabbage.
  • Understand the importance of seasoning and stir-frying techniques.

Ingredients

  • Vermicelli (amount not specified, needs to be soaked for 5 hours)
  • 1/2 Cabbage, cored and cut into thicker pieces
  • Salt (for washing cabbage)
  • 101°C boiling water (amount not specified)
  • Dark soy sauce (amount not specified)
  • Cooking oil (amount not specified)
  • 2 Eggs
  • White vinegar (a dash)
  • Scallions (amount not specified)
  • Ginger (amount not specified)
  • Garlic (amount not specified)
  • Dried sea pepper (amount not specified)
  • Light soy sauce (amount not specified)
  • Oyster sauce (amount not specified)
  • Sugar (a pinch)
  • Allspice (a pinch)
  • Sesame oil (a dash)

Instructions

  1. Soak vermicelli in water for 5 hours (or overnight).
  2. Prepare the cabbage: Cut the cabbage in half, remove the core, and cut into thicker pieces. Wash with salted water to sterilize and remove impurities. Drain well.
  3. Prepare the vermicelli: Drain the soaked vermicelli and cut into smaller pieces with scissors. Blanch in 101°C boiling water for 30 seconds.
  4. Season the vermicelli: Add dark soy sauce and cooking oil to the blanched vermicelli. Mix well to coat evenly.
  5. Prepare the egg mixture: Whisk 2 eggs with a dash of white vinegar in a bowl.
  6. Prepare the aromatics: Finely chop scallions, ginger, garlic, and dried sea pepper. Set aside.
  7. Heat the wok: Add cooking oil to a hot wok until it slightly smokes.
  8. Fry the eggs: Add the egg mixture to the hot oil and fry until lightly set. Remove from wok.
  9. Stir-fry aromatics and cabbage: Add dried sea pepper, scallions, ginger, and garlic to the wok and stir-fry until fragrant. Add the prepared cabbage and stir-fry for about 1 minute until slightly softened.
  10. Season the cabbage: Add salt, sugar, allspice, light soy sauce, and oyster sauce to the cabbage. Stir-fry until well combined and flavors meld.
  11. Add vermicelli: Add the seasoned vermicelli to the wok and stir-fry until heated through and well combined with the cabbage.
  12. Finish and serve: Add a dash of sesame oil. Stir-fry briefly. Remove from heat and serve immediately.

fried_cauliflower_with_pork.txt - مقلي القرنبيط مع لحم الخنزير المفروم

Objectives

  • Learn to make crispy and delicious fried cauliflower at home.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful recipe suitable for everyday meals.
  • Prepare and cook cauliflower to enhance its nutritional value and taste.

Ingredients

  • 1 head of fresh cauliflower
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • Flour (for cleaning cauliflower)
  • 2-3 cloves garlic, thinly sliced
  • Small piece of ginger, thinly sliced
  • Dried chili peppers, thinly sliced (or red chili peppers)
  • Several garlic sprouts, chopped
  • Optional: Garlic leaves, chopped
  • Lean pork, diced
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • 1 teaspoon cornstarch
  • Cooking wine
  • Vegetable oil (peanut oil recommended)
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • Sugar (to taste)
  • Oyster sauce (to taste)
  • 1 teaspoon light soy sauce

Instructions

  1. Prepare the cauliflower: Cut the cauliflower into florets. Wash thoroughly, adding salt and flour to the water to remove impurities. Rinse several times until the water runs clear.
  2. Steam the cauliflower: Steam the cauliflower for 2 minutes to enhance its nutritional value and texture.
  3. Prepare the aromatics: Thinly slice garlic and ginger. Slice dried chili peppers (or red chili peppers) and chop garlic sprouts and leaves (if using).
  4. Prepare the pork: Dice lean pork. Marinate with salt, cornstarch, and cooking wine. Mix well and set aside.
  5. Stir-fry the pork: Heat oil in a wok or pan. Add the marinated pork and stir-fry until white.
  6. Add aromatics and chili peppers: Add the garlic, ginger, and chili peppers to the pork. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  7. Add the cauliflower: Add the steamed cauliflower to the wok and stir-fry until evenly coated.
  8. Season the cauliflower: Add salt, sugar, oyster sauce, and light soy sauce. Stir-fry over high heat.
  9. Add garlic leaves: Add the garlic leaves (if using) and stir-fry for 5-8 seconds.
  10. Serve: Drizzle with extra oil before serving. The fried cauliflower is ready to serve. It should be crispy, refreshing, nutritious, and delicious.

fried_chicken_leg.txt - 炸鸡腿

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious, tender, and flavorful fried chicken legs.
  • Master a simple yet effective method for preparing and marinating chicken legs.
  • Create a dish that is appealing to both adults and children.

Ingredients

  • 10 chicken legs (approximately 3.5 jin/2.1 lbs)
  • 1 handful of salt
  • 3 eggs
  • 50g cornstarch
  • Chopped scallions
  • Chopped ginger
  • 1 tbsp cooking wine
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce
  • A dash of dark soy sauce
  • Appropriate amount of oyster sauce
  • A dash of pepper
  • A dash of five-spice powder
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Wash the chicken legs thoroughly with salt to remove dirt and sanitize. Rinse with clean water.
  2. Pat the chicken legs dry and score the surface to allow better flavor penetration.
  3. Crack 3 eggs into a bowl and whisk until well combined.
  4. Pour the egg mixture over the chicken legs and toss to coat evenly.
  5. Add 50g of cornstarch and mix well to coat the chicken legs with a thin layer of starch.
  6. Heat a wok or large pan with plenty of cooking oil until it reaches medium heat (a chopstick inserted will bubble rapidly).
  7. Fry the chicken legs for 30 seconds per side to set the egg and starch coating.
  8. Continue frying for approximately 5 minutes until the chicken legs are three-quarters cooked and golden brown.
  9. Remove the chicken legs with a slotted spoon and drain the excess oil.
  10. In a large bowl, add the fried chicken legs, chopped scallions, ginger, cooking wine, soy sauce, dark soy sauce, oyster sauce, pepper, and five-spice powder.
  11. Mix well to ensure the chicken legs are evenly coated with the marinade. (Best to do while the chicken is still slightly warm).
  12. Marinate the chicken legs for 1 hour, flipping them halfway through to ensure even flavoring.
  13. Arrange the marinated chicken legs in a large dish. Brush the remaining marinade evenly over the chicken legs.
  14. Steam the chicken legs in a steamer for 40 minutes over medium heat.
  15. Garnish with chopped scallions.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=G9Ks4D4VbGo

fried_eggplant.txt - Fried Eggplant

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and savory fried eggplant dish.
  • Master the technique of frying eggplant to achieve a crispy texture.
  • Understand the importance of simple seasoning for enhancing the eggplant's natural flavor.

Ingredients

  • 2 long, black-skinned eggplants (or purple-skinned/Shandong eggplant)
  • Garlic, several cloves, smashed
  • A handful of inky black tempeh
  • 2-3 turns of green pepper, finely chopped
  • Salt
  • Rapeseed oil
  • Oyster sauce
  • Light soy sauce

Instructions

  1. Prepare the eggplants: Remove stems and cut into thick (approximately 1 cm) diagonal slices.
  2. Prepare the aromatics: Smash garlic cloves and chop green pepper finely.
  3. Fry the eggplants: Heat a pan over low heat (no oil needed). Add eggplant slices and fry slowly, pressing down to release moisture. Fry for about 2 minutes per side until slightly caramelized. Repeat in batches if necessary. Set aside.
  4. Prepare the sauce: Heat a pan with rapeseed oil until lightly smoking. Add green pepper and stir-fry until slightly wrinkled (about 30 seconds).
  5. Add aromatics and sauce: Add smashed garlic and black tempeh to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant. Add the fried eggplants, oyster sauce, and light soy sauce.
  6. Finish the dish: Stir-fry everything together over high heat for about 49 seconds until well combined. Do not overcook.
  7. Serve: Serve immediately.

fried_eggplant_with_green_pepper.txt - مقلي الباذنجان مع الفلفل الأخضر

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious, non-oily, and affordable fried eggplant dish.
  • Master a simple, beginner-friendly cooking method.
  • Prepare a flavorful sauce to enhance the eggplant's taste.

Ingredients

  • 3 purple eggplants (باذنجان بنفسجي)
  • 2 green bell peppers (فلفل لولبي)
  • Several cloves of garlic (ثوم)
  • Small piece of green onion (بصل أخضر)
  • 1 tbsp light soy sauce (صلصة الصويا الخفيفة)
  • A little oyster sauce (صلصة المحار)
  • Salt (ملح)
  • Sugar (سكر)
  • Chicken extract (خلاصة الدجاج)
  • 1/2 tbsp potato starch (نشا البطاطس)
  • Water (ماء)
  • Cooking oil (زيت الطهي)

Instructions

  1. Remove the stems from the eggplants. Wash them with salted water, rinse, and pat dry. Cut them in half.
  2. Steam the eggplant halves for 8 minutes over high heat.
  3. While the eggplant steams, prepare the green peppers: remove stems and seeds, pat dry, and cut into pieces. If desired, add some chili peppers, chopped.
  4. Mince the garlic and finely chop the green onion.
  5. Prepare the sauce: Combine light soy sauce, oyster sauce, salt, sugar, chicken extract, potato starch, and water. Mix well until the starch dissolves. Set aside.
  6. Once steamed, let the eggplant cool slightly, then slice into shorter pieces.
  7. Heat cooking oil in a pan or wok. Add the green peppers and a pinch of salt, stir-fry for about a minute until slightly softened.
  8. Add the garlic and green onion, stir-fry briefly.
  9. Add the steamed eggplant to the pan and stir-fry until heated through.
  10. Pour the sauce over the eggplant and continue stir-frying until the sauce thickens and the eggplant is coated.
  11. Remove from heat and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=EZnN5XtaBFA

fried_eggplant_with_tempeh.txt - Fried Eggplant with Tempeh and Black Beans

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and savory fried eggplant dish.
  • Master the technique of frying eggplant to achieve a crispy texture.
  • Utilize simple ingredients to create a flavorful and satisfying meal.

Ingredients

  • 2 long black-skinned eggplants (or purple-skinned/Shandong eggplant)
  • Several cloves garlic, minced
  • A handful of inky black tempeh
  • 2-3 green chilies
  • Salt
  • Rapeseed oil
  • Oyster sauce
  • Light soy sauce

Instructions

  1. Prepare the eggplants: Remove the stems and cut the eggplants into thick (approximately 1cm) diagonal slices.
  2. Prepare the aromatics: Mince the garlic and roughly chop the green chilies.
  3. Fry the eggplants: Heat a pan over low heat. Add the eggplant slices without oil, frying slowly to remove moisture. Press down on the eggplants to encourage faster moisture evaporation. Fry for about 2 minutes per side, until caramelized. Repeat until all eggplant slices are fried. Set aside.
  4. Stir-fry aromatics: Heat a wok or pan with a small amount of rapeseed oil until slightly smoking. Add the green chilies and stir-fry until slightly wrinkled (about 30 seconds). Add the minced garlic and tempeh, stir-frying until fragrant.
  5. Combine and season: Add the fried eggplants to the wok. Season with oyster sauce and light soy sauce.
  6. Finish: Stir-fry everything over high heat for approximately 49 seconds, ensuring even cooking. Do not overcook.
  7. Serve: Serve immediately and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=3k-M56s0MVw

fried_egg_vegetable_pancake.txt - Pritong Itlog at Gulay na Pancake

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and affordable fried egg and vegetable pancake.
  • Master the technique of preparing and cooking the pancake for optimal texture.
  • Understand the importance of properly mixing ingredients for a balanced flavor.

Ingredients

  • A handful of green vegetables (specific type not specified)
  • 3 eggs
  • A few drops of white vinegar
  • 1/2 onion, thinly sliced and diced
  • 1 carrot, peeled, thinly sliced and diced
  • Salt
  • 1 tbsp five-spice powder
  • A little pepper
  • 2 tbsp all-purpose flour
  • Cooking oil
  • White sesame seeds

Instructions

  1. Clean and chop the green vegetables into small pieces. Wash thoroughly.
  2. Crack 3 eggs into a bowl. Add a few drops of white vinegar and whisk until yolks and whites are fully combined.
  3. Chop 1/2 onion into small cubes.
  4. Peel and chop 1 carrot into small cubes.
  5. Combine the chopped vegetables, eggs, salt, 1 tbsp five-spice powder, a little pepper, and 2 tbsp flour in a large bowl. Mix well until there are no dry flour particles.
  6. Heat cooking oil in a pan.
  7. Pour the batter into the heated pan and press it into a cake shape with a spatula.
  8. Sprinkle with white sesame seeds.
  9. Cover and cook over low heat for 5 minutes.
  10. Flip the pancake and cook for another 5 minutes, covered.
  11. Turn the heat to medium, and cook until both sides are golden brown.
  12. Remove from pan, let cool slightly, and cut into desired pieces before serving.

fried_noodles.txt - 炒面 (Chǎomiàn)

Objectives

  • Learn to make flavorful, non-clumpy fried noodles.
  • Master the techniques for perfectly cooked noodles and vegetables.
  • Create a restaurant-quality dish at home economically.

Ingredients

  • 1-2 packages dried noodles (5 RMB)
  • 1 small head of baby bok choy, thinly sliced
  • 1 carrot, julienned
  • 1 small onion, chopped
  • 1 egg
  • 100g lean pork, thinly sliced
  • Salt
  • White vinegar
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽, shēngzhōu)
  • 1 tsp dark soy sauce (老抽, lǎochōu)
  • 1 tsp sugar
  • 1 tsp chicken bouillon
  • 1 tsp thirteen spice (十三香, shísānxīang)
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Boil water in a pot. Add dried noodles and cook for 2 minutes over low heat, then 1 minute over high heat. Drain and rinse with cold water. Set aside.
  2. Thinly slice baby bok choy and julienne carrots. Chop onion.
  3. Whisk together egg, salt, and a few drops of white vinegar.
  4. Stir-fry carrots in a little oil until softened. Remove and set aside.
  5. Stir-fry pork until browned and cooked through. Remove and set aside.
  6. Stir-fry bok choy until wilted. Remove and set aside.
  7. In a separate bowl, whisk together soy sauce, dark soy sauce, sugar, salt, chicken bouillon, and thirteen spice.
  8. Heat oil in a wok or large pan. Add noodles and stir-fry over high heat until heated through.
  9. Add the prepared vegetables, pork, and egg. Stir-fry until everything is well combined.
  10. Pour in the sauce and stir-fry until the noodles are evenly coated and the sauce has thickened.
  11. Add chopped onion and stir-fry briefly.
  12. Serve immediately.
