fried_peanut.txt - 香酥花生米 (Xiāng sū huāshēngmǐ)

Objectives

  • Learn to make crispy fried peanuts without burning them.
  • Understand the importance of pre-processing peanuts for optimal results.
  • Master a simple yet delicious recipe perfect for snacking or as a side dish.
  • Learn how to prevent peanuts from becoming soggy or going bad quickly.
  • Discover a method to enhance the flavor and aroma of fried peanuts.

Ingredients

500克 (500 grams) 花生米 (huāshēngmǐ) - Peanuts 1 汤匙 (1 tablespoon) 面粉 (miànfěn) - Flour 清水 (qīngshuǐ) - Water 少量 (a little) 白醋 (bái cù) - White vinegar 少许 (a little) 食用油 (shíyòng yóu) - Cooking oil 高度白酒 (gāodù báijiǔ) - High-proof liquor (optional) 食盐 (shíyán) or 白糖 (báitáng) - Salt or sugar (to taste)

Instructions

  1. Select 500 grams of peanuts, discarding any damaged, moldy, or sprouted ones.
  2. Add a tablespoon of flour to the peanuts and mix thoroughly to absorb dust and impurities.
  3. Rinse the peanuts well under running water to remove the flour and any remaining debris.
  4. Add a little white vinegar to the water for a second rinse to help prevent the peanuts from peeling during frying.
  5. Drain the peanuts completely using a colander or absorbent towel/paper towels; optionally, use a hair dryer or sun to dry them.
  6. Heat a wok or pan over low heat. Add the peanuts and stir-fry until the surface moisture evaporates completely.
  7. Add a small amount of cooking oil (just enough to lightly coat the peanuts). Continue to stir-fry over low heat.
  8. Stir-fry until you hear a crackling sound, indicating the peanuts are almost done.
  9. Add a little high-proof liquor (optional) for enhanced aroma and preservation. Stir to combine.
  10. Once the peanuts are golden brown and crispy, remove from heat.
  11. Transfer the peanuts to a plate or bowl, and toss with chopsticks to cool quickly.
  12. Season with salt or sugar to taste. Garnish and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=fRjwguYyBbo

fried_pork_black_fungus.txt - Fried Pork with Black Fungus

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare black fungus to prevent popping during frying.
  • Master a technique for frying black fungus that results in a crispy texture.
  • Create a flavorful and tender fried pork dish with black fungus.

Ingredients

  • 50 grams black fungus (木耳, mù'ěr)
  • 1 tsp sugar (糖, táng)
  • 1 tsp flour (面粉, miànfěn)
  • Hot water (热水, rèshuǐ)
  • 2 green peppers (青椒, qīngjiāo)
  • Garlic (蒜, suàn)
  • Ginger (姜, jiāng)
  • Lean pork (瘦肉, shòuròu)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油, háoyóu)
  • Light soy sauce (生抽, shēngchōu)
  • Salt (盐, yán)
  • Chicken essence (鸡精, jījīng)
  • 1 tsp potato starch (土豆淀粉, tǔdòu diànfěn)
  • Cooking wine (料酒, liàojiǔ)
  • Oil (油, yóu)
  • Rock sugar (冰糖, bīngtáng)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the black fungus: Add sugar and flour to the black fungus. Add hot water, mix, and wash to remove impurities. Soak for 5 minutes.
  2. Prepare the green peppers: Remove the stems and seeds. Slice thinly.
  3. Prepare the garlic and ginger: Mince garlic and ginger.
  4. Prepare the pork: Cut the pork into slightly thick pieces for easier frying.
  5. Marinate the pork: Add oyster sauce, light soy sauce, salt, chicken essence, potato starch, and cooking wine to the pork. Mix well and add a little oil to retain moisture. Marinate for later use.
  6. Clean the black fungus: After soaking for 15 minutes, rinse the expanded fungus thoroughly with water twice to remove all impurities and flour. Drain well. If large, cut into smaller pieces.
  7. Blanch the black fungus: Blanch the black fungus in boiling water for 3 minutes until cooked. Drain and keep warm; do not rinse.
  8. Fry the pork: Heat a wok with a little peanut oil. Turn off heat, let cool slightly until the oil is 60% hot. Add the marinated pork and cook until tender.
  9. Stir-fry aromatics: Add minced ginger and garlic to the wok and stir-fry until fragrant. Add dark soy sauce for color. Set aside.
  10. Fry the black fungus and green pepper: Add more oil to the wok. Add the blanched black fungus and stir-fry. Add rock sugar to the green pepper and mix well. Stir-fry green pepper until slightly raw. Increase heat to high, stir-fry until the water evaporates from the vegetables.
  11. Combine and finish: Add cooking wine and stir-fry for about 1 minute. Add the fried pork. Stir-fry everything together over high heat. Season with salt, mixing until seasoning dissolves.
  12. Serve: The fried pork with black fungus is ready to serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=u7_O6ugDgBE

fried_rice_with_egg.txt - Fried Rice with Egg

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and nutritious fried rice with egg.
  • Master the technique of frying rice to achieve distinct, non-sticky grains.
  • Incorporate various ingredients like pork sausage, corn, and vegetables for enhanced flavor and visual appeal.

Ingredients

  • Leftover rice (amount not specified)
  • 3 eggs
  • Pork sausage (amount not specified)
  • 1 small cucumber
  • Carrot (amount not specified)
  • ½ piece of corn on the cob
  • Sweet peas (amount not specified)
  • Green onions (amount not specified)
  • Salt
  • Cooking oil
  • Pepper

Instructions

  1. Fluff leftover rice with a spoon or disposable gloves to prevent sticking during frying. Use non-sticky rice or cook rice with slightly less water for firmer texture.
  2. Separate egg yolks and whites. Lightly whisk egg yolks. Whisk egg whites separately until stiff peaks form.
  3. Combine whisked egg yolks with the rice and mix thoroughly. Set aside.
  4. Prepare pork sausage: Score the casing, remove it, and dice the sausage into small cubes.
  5. Prepare cucumber: Remove the seeds and dice into small cubes.
  6. Prepare carrot: Peel, shred, and dice into small pieces.
  7. Prepare corn: Remove kernels from half a corn cob.
  8. Blanch sweet peas and corn kernels in boiling salted water for 2 minutes. Remove with a slotted spoon.
  9. Stir-fry pork sausage and corn kernels in a pan over medium heat until fragrant. Remove from pan.
  10. Add cooking oil to the pan and pour in the egg whites. Stir-fry until set, then chop into small pieces.
  11. Add the rice mixture to the pan. Stir-fry, pressing down with a spatula to prevent sticking. Stir-fry for 2 minutes until grains are distinct.
  12. Add diced carrots and stir-fry for 10 seconds.
  13. Add diced cucumber and pork sausage mixture. Stir-fry briefly.
  14. Add blanched sweet peas and corn. Stir-fry to combine.
  15. Season with salt and pepper to taste.
  16. Stir in chopped green onions.
  17. Serve immediately.

fried_tofu.txt - Fried Tofu

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and affordable fried tofu dish.
  • Master a simple, easy-to-follow recipe suitable for beginners.
  • Create a visually appealing and flavorful dish using readily available ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 2 Yuan worth of fried tofu (choose smaller pieces for better results)
  • A handful of green onions (white parts only), chopped
  • 1 piece of peeled ginger, thinly sliced then julienned
  • 3-4 cloves of garlic, thinly sliced
  • 2-3 red chilies (optional, for spiciness), deseeded and thinly sliced, or red pepper flakes as a substitute
  • A few leeks, chopped (optional, for added aroma)
  • 1 tsp salt
  • A dash of chicken essence (optional)
  • A pinch of sugar
  • 2 tbsp light soy sauce
  • 1 tbsp dark soy sauce
  • A dash of oyster sauce
  • 1 tbsp cornstarch
  • Water
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Prepare the fried tofu: Cut each piece from one corner to the middle, without cutting it in half. Set aside.
  2. Prepare the aromatics: Chop the green onions (white parts only), julienne the ginger, and thinly slice the garlic and chilies (if using). Chop leeks if using. Set aside separately.
  3. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, combine salt, chicken essence (optional), sugar, light soy sauce, dark soy sauce, oyster sauce, cornstarch, and water. Mix thoroughly until the cornstarch is dissolved. Set aside.
  4. Heat a wok or pan: Add a small amount of cooking oil. Heat until the oil is shimmering.
  5. Sauté aromatics: Add the garlic, ginger, and green onions to the hot oil. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  6. Add the tofu: Add the prepared fried tofu to the wok. Stir-fry over medium heat for about 2 minutes until fragrant.
  7. Add the sauce: Pour the prepared sauce evenly over the fried tofu. Stir to coat the tofu completely.
  8. Simmer: Bring to a simmer and cook for 3 minutes, adding more water if the sauce becomes too thick.
  9. Add chilies (optional): Add the chopped chilies (or red pepper flakes) and stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Add leeks (optional): Add the chopped leeks and stir-fry briefly until wilted.
  11. Serve: Remove from heat, transfer to a plate, and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LYW02x_F1qY

fried_tofu_with_vegetables.txt - Fried Tofu with Vegetables (家常炒豆腐)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and simple fried tofu dish.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients for a quick and easy meal.
  • Create a flavorful stir-fry combining tofu, pork belly (optional), and greens.

Ingredients

  • 1 plate of fried tofu (3 yuan)
  • Small green vegetables (quantity unspecified)
  • Small rapeseed (quantity unspecified)
  • Pork belly (optional, quantity unspecified)
  • Garlic (quantity unspecified)
  • Ginger (quantity unspecified)
  • Green onions (white part only, quantity unspecified)
  • Cooking oil (quantity unspecified)
  • Soy sauce (quantity unspecified)
  • Oyster sauce (quantity unspecified)
  • Light soy sauce (quantity unspecified)
  • Salt (a small spoonful)
  • Sugar (a small amount)
  • Water (one bowl)

Instructions

  1. Cut the fried tofu in half, then into smaller pieces. Set aside in a bowl.
  2. Clean the small green vegetables, removing stems and leaves. Separate and set aside.
  3. Clean and chop the small rapeseed. Separate stems and leaves. Set aside.
  4. If using, thinly slice the pork belly. Set aside.
  5. Mince the garlic and ginger. Set aside.
  6. Chop the white parts of the green onions. Set aside.
  7. Heat cooking oil in a pan over medium heat.
  8. Add the pork belly (if using) and fry until lightly browned, releasing some fat.
  9. Add the garlic, ginger, and green onions. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Add soy sauce, oyster sauce, and light soy sauce. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  11. Add the fried tofu and stir-fry until fragrant.
  12. Pour in one bowl of water, stir to combine, and let the tofu absorb the broth.
  13. Bring to a boil and simmer for 3 minutes.
  14. Add the rapeseed stems and stir-fry over high heat until tender.
  15. Season with a small spoonful of salt and a small amount of sugar. Stir well.
  16. Add the rapeseed leaves and stir-fry until wilted.
  17. Add the small green vegetables and stir-fry until tender.
  18. Add a little gravy, stir to thicken slightly.
  19. Serve hot with rice.

fried_yuba.txt - Fried Yuba (Piniritong Yuba)

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare delicious fried yuba for a celebratory New Year's Eve meal.
  • Master the technique of blanching yuba to maintain its texture and flavor.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to complement the yuba's taste.

Ingredients

  • A small handful of yuba (dried bean curd sheets)
  • Water
  • Salt (optional, for faster soaking)
  • Chives, chopped
  • Garlic, minced
  • Dried chili peppers (optional, for added fragrance)
  • Green and red chili peppers, sliced (for color and spice)
  • Black fungus (soaked and washed)
  • Cooking oil
  • 1 tablespoon bean paste
  • Light soy sauce
  • Oyster sauce
  • Chicken essence
  • Sugar
  • Salt
  • Water starch (to thicken the sauce)

Instructions

  1. Soak the yuba in water (with optional salt for faster soaking).
  2. Cut the soaked yuba into small pieces.
  3. Drain the yuba and chop it into smaller pieces. Set aside.
  4. Chop chives, garlic, and dried chili peppers (if using). Set aside.
  5. Chop green and red chili peppers. Set aside.
  6. Blanch the black fungus in boiling water for 2 minutes.
  7. Blanch the yuba for 15 seconds, then immediately plunge into cold water to stop cooking. Drain.
  8. Heat oil in a wok or pan.
  9. Sauté garlic, dried chili (if using), and onion until fragrant.
  10. Add bean paste and stir-fry until fragrant.
  11. Add a half bowl of water, bring to a boil.
  12. Add light soy sauce and oyster sauce. Stir to dissolve.
  13. Add blanched yuba and black fungus.
  14. Stir-fry for about a minute.
  15. Add green and red chili peppers. Stir-fry until cooked.
  16. Season with salt, chicken essence, and sugar.
  17. Thicken the sauce with water starch.
  18. Serve hot.

frozen_shrimp.txt - Frozen Shrimp

Objectives

  • Learn how to properly thaw frozen shrimp to maintain freshness and tenderness.
  • Understand the importance of removing the shrimp's fishy odor.
  • Master a quick and easy cooking method for perfectly cooked frozen shrimp.

Ingredients

  • Frozen shrimp (quantity not specified)
  • Ginger slices
  • Green onions (scallions)
  • Cooking wine (料酒 liàojiǔ)
  • Salt
  • High-grade white wine (高度白酒 gāodù bái jiǔ)

Instructions

  1. Remove frozen shrimp from freezer 10 minutes before thawing.
  2. Sprinkle salt on the shrimp to help thaw and kill bacteria.
  3. Let the shrimp sit for 8 minutes.
  4. Clean the shrimp by removing the pointy parts and whiskers.
  5. Place the thawed shrimp in a bowl.
  6. Add ginger slices, green onions, and cooking wine to the bowl.
  7. Marinate the shrimp for a few minutes to remove fishy odor.
  8. Bring a pot of water to a boil.
  9. Add a few slices of ginger and green onions to the boiling water.
  10. Add a spoonful of salt and a small amount of high-grade white wine to the boiling water.
  11. Once the water boils again, add the marinated shrimp.
  12. Cook over high heat until the shrimp turn red and curl.
  13. Remove the shrimp and immediately place them in ice water to maintain firmness and texture.
  14. Serve with a light soy sauce or vinegar dip.

fu_jian_hun_tun.txt - 福建馄饨 (Fujian Wonton)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious Fujian-style wontons.
  • Master the techniques for preparing the flavorful meat filling.
  • Create a flavorful and aromatic wonton broth.

Ingredients

  • 瘦肉 (Shòu ròu) - Lean pork (amount unspecified, but suggested "二肥八瘦" - 20% fat, 80% lean)
  • 肥肉 (Féi ròu) - Fatty pork (small amount)
  • 小葱 (Xiǎo cōng) - Scallions (several)
  • 生姜 (Shēng jiāng) - Ginger (a piece)
  • 食盐 (Shí yán) - Salt (a small spoon)
  • 松茸鲜 (Sōngróng xiān) - Mushroom seasoning (a spoon)
  • 胡椒粉 (Hújiāo fěn) - Pepper powder (a small amount)
  • 蚝油 (Háoyóu) - Oyster sauce (a spoon)
  • 生抽 (Shēng chōu) - Light soy sauce (a spoon)
  • 鸡蛋 (Jī dàn) - Egg (1)
  • 香菜 (Xiāng cài) - Coriander/Cilantro (several)
  • 馄饨皮 (Húntún pí) - Wonton wrappers (amount unspecified)
  • 生菜 (Shēng cài) - Lettuce (optional, for broth)
  • 虾皮 (Xiā pí) - Dried shrimp (optional, for broth)
  • 紫菜 (Zǐ cài) - Seaweed (a small amount, for broth)
  • 陈醋 (Chén cù) - Black vinegar (a spoon, for broth)
  • 猪油 (Zhū yóu) - Lard (a spoon, for broth)
  • 开水 (Kāi shuǐ) - Boiling water (for broth)

Instructions

  1. Dice lean and fatty pork into thick slices, then mince finely (using a knife or food processor).
  2. Mince scallions and ginger, then mix with warm water to extract their juices. Set aside.
  3. In a bowl, combine minced pork, salt, mushroom seasoning, pepper, oyster sauce, and light soy sauce. Mix thoroughly with gloves until slightly sticky.
  4. Add the scallion-ginger mixture and continue mixing until the meat absorbs the juices.
  5. Add a whole egg and mix for about a minute until well combined.
  6. Add chopped scallions and coriander, and mix again. Set aside.
  7. Choose thin, square wonton wrappers. Place a spoonful of filling in the center of each wrapper.
  8. Using either the pinching or chopstick method, seal the wontons.
  9. Prepare the broth: In a bowl, combine salt, mushroom seasoning, pepper, optional lettuce and shrimp, chopped scallions and coriander, seaweed, light soy sauce, black vinegar, and lard. Add boiling water and stir.
  10. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add wontons and cook for about 10-15 seconds before gently stirring to prevent sticking.
  11. Continue cooking for about 3 minutes, or until the wontons float to the surface.
  12. Remove wontons and serve in bowls with the prepared broth.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=wcinRGWYvTk

fu_zhu_rou_mo_xi_hong_shi.txt - 泡腐竹肉沫西红柿

Objectives

  • Learn to quickly and effectively soak dried bean curd sheets (腐竹).
  • Master a flavorful recipe combining bean curd sheets, minced meat, and tomatoes.
  • Create a visually appealing and delicious dish suitable for special occasions or gatherings.

Ingredients

  • 高安腐竹 (Gāo'ān fǔzhú) - Dried bean curd sheets from Gao'an (amount not specified, adjust to your needs)
  • 食盐 (Shíyán) - Salt (a pinch)
  • 白醋 (Bái cù) - White vinegar (a splash)
  • 清水 (Qīngshuǐ) - Clean water (a generous amount for soaking)
  • 西红柿 (Xīhóngshì) - Tomatoes (1, about 200g)
  • 瘦肉 (Shòuròu) - Lean pork (approx. 200g)
  • 小葱 (Xiǎocōng) - Scallions (a few stalks)
  • 生姜 (Shēngjiāng) - Ginger (1 piece)
  • 大蒜 (Dàsuàn) - Garlic (several cloves)
  • 黄豆酱 (Huángdòujiàng) - Yellow soybean paste (1 large spoonful)
  • 胡椒粉 (Hújiāofěn) - Black pepper powder (a small amount)
  • 生抽 (Shēngchōu) - Light soy sauce (a small amount)
  • 蚝油 (Háoyóu) - Oyster sauce (a small amount)
  • 玻璃芡 (Bōlí qiàn) - Glass glaze (optional, for thickening)
  • 食用油 (Shíyòngyóu) - Cooking oil (a small amount)

Instructions

  1. Cut the dried bean curd sheets into small pieces.
  2. Add salt and white vinegar to a bowl of water. Soak the bean curd sheets until fully expanded (approx. 1 hour).
  3. Dice the tomatoes, removing the core. Mince the pork, scallions, ginger, and garlic.
  4. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add salt and blanch the soaked bean curd sheets for about 1 minute to remove the beany smell. Remove and set aside.
  5. Heat oil in a wok or pan. Add the minced pork and stir-fry until browned and fragrant.
  6. Add the minced scallions, ginger, and garlic; stir-fry until fragrant.
  7. Add the diced tomatoes and stir-fry briefly. Add salt to help release the juices. Use a spatula to press the tomatoes to release their juices.
  8. Add yellow soybean paste, pepper, light soy sauce, and oyster sauce. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Add water, bring to a boil, then add the blanched bean curd sheets. Stir gently, cover, and simmer for 2-3 minutes.
  10. Remove the lid, increase heat, and reduce the sauce to desired consistency. Optionally, add a glass glaze to thicken the sauce.
  11. Transfer to a serving dish (a casserole is recommended). Garnish with chopped scallions. Serve hot.

gan_guo_tudou_pian.txt - 干锅土豆片 (Gan Guo Tu Dou Pian)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and flavorful Gan Guo Tu Dou Pian (Dry Pot Potato Slices).
  • Master a simple and easy-to-learn recipe.
  • Achieve a crispy texture and rich flavor in the potatoes.

Ingredients

  • 2 large potatoes (黄心土豆 - huáng xīn tǔdòu - yellow-fleshed potatoes are preferred)
  • 1-2 green bell peppers (青椒 - qīngjiāo)
  • 1-2 red bell peppers (红椒 - hóngjiāo)
  • 2 stalks of garlic chives (蒜苗 - suànmiáo)
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜子 - suànzi)
  • 1 tablespoon soy sauce (生抽 - shēngchōu)
  • A dash of dark soy sauce (老抽 - lǎochōu)
  • 1 teaspoon oyster sauce (蚝油 - háoyóu)
  • 1 teaspoon salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • A dash of mushroom seasoning (松茸鲜 - sōngrōng xiān)
  • A dash of five-spice powder (五香粉 - wǔxiāngfěn)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòngyóu)

Instructions

  1. Peel and wash two large potatoes. Cut them in half and then slice into 0.5cm thick pieces. Wash the potato slices in water to remove excess starch.
  2. Cut green and red bell peppers into diagonal slices. Slice garlic into thin pieces. Cut garlic chives into small segments.
  3. In a bowl, mix soy sauce, dark soy sauce, oyster sauce, salt, mushroom seasoning, and five-spice powder.
  4. Heat cooking oil in a pan or wok over medium heat. Add the potato slices and stir-fry until golden brown and crispy.
  5. Add the green and red peppers and garlic, stir-frying until fragrant.
  6. Pour in the prepared sauce and stir-fry until the potatoes are well coated and flavorful.
  7. Add the garlic chives and stir-fry for a few seconds until wilted.
  8. Serve immediately and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ooxiEsF6E4I

gan_guo_tudoupian.txt - 干锅土豆片 (Gan Guo Tu Dou Pian)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy Gan Guo Tu Dou Pian (Dry Pot Potato Slices).
  • Master the technique of frying potatoes until golden and crispy.
  • Understand how to balance flavors with various sauces and spices.

Ingredients

  • Several small potatoes (马铃薯 - màlíngshǔ)
  • A small piece of fatty pork or five-spice pork (肥肉/五花肉 - féiròu/wǔhuāròu)
  • Plenty of garlic cloves (蒜 - suàn)
  • Half a small onion (洋葱 - yángcōng)
  • Several stalks of chives (韭菜苔 - jiǔcài tái)
  • Several grams of dried chili peppers (干海椒 - gānhǎijiāo)
  • Vegetable oil (菜籽油 - cài zǐyóu)
  • 28 Liuyang Douchi (浏阳豆豉 - liúyáng dòuchǐ)
  • One tablespoon of Doubanjiang (豆瓣酱 - dòubànjiàng)
  • Salt (盐 - yán)
  • One spoonful of Songrong Xian (松茸鲜 - sōngrōng xiān)
  • One spoonful of soy sauce (生抽 - shēng chōu)
  • Appropriate amount of oyster sauce (蚝油 - háoyóu)
  • White sesame seeds (白芝麻 - bái zhīma)

Instructions

  1. Clean several small potatoes thoroughly and peel them. Cut into 0.5cm thick slices.
  2. Wash the potato slices gently to remove excess starch for a crispier texture. Drain and set aside.
  3. Cut a small piece of fatty pork or five-spice pork into thin slices. Set aside.
  4. Mince garlic cloves and set aside.
  5. Cut half a small onion into thin strips. Set aside.
  6. Cut several chives into slightly longer segments. Set aside.
  7. Cut several grams of dried chili peppers into small pieces. Set aside.
  8. Heat a pan with a little vegetable oil over low heat.
  9. Fry the potato slices until golden brown and crispy. Remove and set aside.
  10. Add the sliced pork to the pan and cook until excess oil is rendered. Remove excess oil, reserving for later use.
  11. Add the minced garlic to the pan and stir-fry.
  12. Add the 28 Liuyang Douchi and one tablespoon of Doubanjiang. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  13. Add the fried potatoes, onions, and dried chilies to the pan. Stir-fry until well combined.
  14. Season with a little salt, one spoonful of Songrong Xian, one spoonful of soy sauce, and an appropriate amount of oyster sauce.
  15. Add the chives. Stir-fry over high heat for about 1 minute.
  16. Sprinkle with white sesame seeds.
  17. Turn off the heat and transfer to a dry pot. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=tDh4NpnjitI

garlic_broccoli.txt - Garlic Broccoli

Objectives

  • Learn to select the freshest broccoli.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful garlic broccoli recipe.
  • Achieve vibrant color and optimal texture in the final dish.

Ingredients

  • Fresh broccoli (approximately 1 head)
  • 2 tablespoons table salt
  • 1 carrot
  • Several cloves garlic
  • 1 bowl of water
  • 1 tablespoon cooking wine
  • 1 tablespoon fresh Matsutake mushrooms (or MSG)
  • Chicken essence (to taste)
  • Oyster sauce (to taste)
  • A dash of light soy sauce
  • 1 tablespoon cornstarch
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Select Fresh Broccoli: Choose broccoli that is deep green, with small, tightly closed buds that feel firm to the touch. The spaces between the flower buds should be small, and the green color around the rhizome should be vibrant (avoid white).

  2. Prepare Broccoli: Cut the broccoli into small florets. Do not discard the rhizome; peel it thinly, cut into diamond-shaped segments, and set aside.

  3. Prepare Carrot: Peel and cut the carrot into small, diamond-shaped pieces.

  4. Prepare Garlic: Mince several cloves of garlic finely, almost to a paste consistency. This will enhance the garlic flavor.

  5. Make the Sauce: In a bowl, combine water, cooking wine, Matsutake mushrooms (or MSG), chicken essence, oyster sauce, light soy sauce, and cornstarch. Mix thoroughly until well combined.

  6. Clean Broccoli: Soak the broccoli florets in salted water for 10 minutes, then rinse thoroughly with clean water.

  7. Blanch Vegetables: Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add the broccoli florets and blanch for 40 seconds. Add the carrots and broccoli stems, and blanch for another 20 seconds. Remove with a slotted spoon and drain well.

  8. Sauté Garlic: Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan over medium-low heat (40% heat). Add the minced garlic and sauté gently until fragrant, stirring frequently to prevent burning.

  9. Combine and Simmer: Add the prepared sauce to the pan with the sautéed garlic. Bring to a simmer.

  10. Add Broccoli and Carrots: Add the blanched broccoli and carrots to the pan. Stir well to coat everything in the sauce. Increase heat to high, and stir-fry until the sauce thickens slightly.

  11. Finish and Serve: Stir in a little more oil before serving to enhance the color and shine. Stir for about 10 seconds. Turn off the heat and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=sQpejhb0Nh0

garlic_chrysanthemum.txt - Garlic Chrysanthemum

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare delicious garlic chrysanthemum.
  • Master the blanching and stir-fry techniques for optimal texture and flavor.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to complement the chrysanthemum.

Ingredients

  • Chrysanthemum: 1 pound (approximately 3 yuan 80 cents in the video)
  • Salt: 1 tablespoon (for soaking and blanching)
  • Sugar: A pinch
  • Light Soy Sauce: 1 tablespoon
  • Oyster Sauce: A dash
  • Potato Starch: 1 tablespoon
  • Water: Half a bowl (for sauce)
  • Garlic: Several cloves
  • Vegetable Oil: A small amount (for stir-frying)
  • Lettuce & Shrimp Peel: 1 tablespoon (optional)
  • Bean Paste: ½ tablespoon (optional)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Chrysanthemum: Place chrysanthemum in a large bowl of salted water (2 minutes). Clean the stems, rinse twice until water runs clear, and drain well. Trim old parts, cut stems into 2-3cm pieces, chop leaves finely, and set aside.
  2. Prepare the Garlic: Lightly flatten garlic cloves with a knife, then finely chop and set aside.
  3. Make the Sauce: In a bowl, whisk together salt, sugar, light soy sauce, oyster sauce, potato starch, and water until smooth. Set aside.
  4. Blanch the Chrysanthemum: Bring water to a boil in a pot with a pinch of salt. Blanch the stems for 25 seconds, then add the leaves and blanch for 8 seconds. Immediately transfer to ice water to cool, then squeeze out excess water.
  5. Stir-fry the Garlic: Heat a wok or pan until slightly smoking. Add oil, swirl to coat. Add chopped garlic and stir-fry until fragrant and golden brown.
  6. Add Aromatics and Paste (Optional): Add lettuce and shrimp peel (if using), stir-fry until fragrant. Add bean paste (if using) and stir-fry until fragrant.
  7. Add Sauce and Chrysanthemum: Pour in the prepared sauce, increase heat, and bring to a simmer until thickened. Add the blanched chrysanthemum, stir-fry until evenly coated and heated through (approximately 30 seconds).
  8. Serve: Remove from heat, transfer to a plate, and serve. The remaining sauce can be poured over the dish.

garlic_onion_omelet.txt - Garlic Onion Omelet with Spicy Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious garlic onion omelet.
  • Master a flavorful spicy sauce to complement the omelet.
  • Prepare the ingredients efficiently for quick cooking.

Ingredients

2 large onions 2 eggs 1/3 tsp thirteen spice (Chinese five spice?) Pinch of pepper 1 tsp potato starch 1 green chili pepper 1 red chili pepper 1 cucumber Several cloves garlic Cooking oil Light soy sauce Vinegar 1 tbsp sugar Salt 1 tbsp white sesame seeds 1 tbsp homemade chili oil Optional: Chili pepper flakes, peanuts

Instructions

  1. Steam two whole onions for 2 minutes.
  2. In a bowl, whisk 2 eggs with thirteen spice, pepper, and potato starch.
  3. Slice green and red chili peppers into diamond shapes.
  4. Slice cucumber into diamond shapes.
  5. Mince garlic finely.
  6. Heat a pan with a thin layer of oil.
  7. Pour in the egg mixture and cook into a thin omelet, flipping to cook both sides until golden brown.
  8. Remove from pan, cool, and chop into small pieces.
  9. In a small bowl, mix light soy sauce, vinegar, sugar, and salt. Simmer for 1 minute until bubbly.
  10. Cut the steamed onions into small pieces.
  11. In a bowl, combine the chopped omelet, onions, cucumber, chili peppers, and minced garlic.
  12. For added spice, include chili pepper flakes.
  13. Drizzle with white sesame seeds and homemade chili oil. Toss to combine.
  14. Add the simmered sauce to the mixture and toss well.
  15. Add peanuts (optional) and toss again.
  16. Serve immediately.

garlic_spinach.txt - Garlic Spinach

Objectives

  • Learn to cook delicious and nutritious garlic spinach.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful spinach cooking method.
  • Preserve the vibrant green color of the spinach.

Ingredients

  • 1 bunch spinach (approx. 1 lb, 3 yuan)
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • A pinch of sugar
  • Matsutake mushrooms (amount unspecified)
  • 1 teaspoon cooking wine
  • 1 tablespoon light soy sauce
  • 1 tablespoon potato starch
  • Appropriate amount of water
  • Several cloves garlic
  • Cooking oil
  • Sesame oil (optional)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Spinach: Wash the spinach thoroughly, removing roots and stems. Rinse twice with water until the water runs clear. Cut the spinach into 4-5 cm pieces, separating stems and leaves.
  2. Prepare the Garlic: Mince several cloves of garlic finely.
  3. Make the Sauce: In a bowl, combine salt, sugar, matsutake mushrooms, cooking wine, light soy sauce, potato starch, and water. Mix well until the starch dissolves. Set aside.
  4. Blanch the Spinach: Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add a small spoonful of salt and some oil. Add the spinach stems and blanch for 28 seconds. Add the leaves and blanch for another 15 seconds on high heat until bright green. Remove with a slotted spoon and set aside.
  5. Sauté Garlic: Heat oil in a pan. Add the minced garlic and sauté until fragrant (about 30 seconds).
  6. Combine and Simmer: Add the prepared sauce to the pan and stir until thickened.
  7. Finish and Serve: Add the blanched spinach to the pan and toss to coat. Drizzle with sesame oil (optional). Turn off the heat and serve immediately.

garlic_sprout_egg.txt - Garlic Sprout Egg

Objectives

  • Prepare a delicious and crispy garlic sprout egg dish.
  • Learn a simple technique for making flavorful and tender eggs.
  • Master the cooking process, including steaming, blanching, and stir-frying.

Ingredients

  • A handful of fresh garlic sprouts (choose thicker, emerald green ones)
  • 3 eggs
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • A little water
  • Fresh mushrooms
  • 1 handful green onions (white parts only)
  • Ginger (sliced thinly, then into small cubes)
  • Garlic (minced)
  • A few slices of dried chili pepper
  • Oyster sauce
  • Light soy sauce
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Prepare Garlic Sprouts: Gently squeeze water from garlic sprouts, wash, chop into 3-4cm pieces. Mix with salt and a little water, let soak for 5 minutes.
  2. Prepare Mushrooms: Trim mushroom stems, wash, and slice thickly. Set aside.
  3. Prepare Eggs: Crack 3 eggs into a bowl, add salt, and whisk thoroughly until light and frothy. Set aside.
  4. Prepare Aromatics: Finely chop green onions, ginger, garlic, and dried chilies. Set aside.
  5. Steam Garlic Sprouts: Steam garlic sprouts for 2 minutes.
  6. Blanch Mushrooms: Blanch mushrooms for 2 minutes, then drain.
  7. Cook Eggs: Heat oil in a pan. Add egg mixture and cook until soft and set. Remove from pan.
  8. Sauté Aromatics: Add more oil to the pan. Sauté green onions, ginger, garlic, and chilies until fragrant.
  9. Add Sauces: Stir in oyster sauce and light soy sauce until fragrant.
  10. Add Mushrooms: Add blanched mushrooms and stir-fry evenly.
  11. Combine: Add steamed garlic sprouts to the pan.
  12. Finish Eggs: Add the cooked eggs to the pan. Season with salt and pepper. Stir-fry over high heat for 49 seconds until well combined and heated through.
  13. Serve: Drizzle with more oil before serving. Serve hot with rice.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=11JFTDo_hsU

golden_egg.txt - Golden Eggs and Braised Eggs

Objectives

  • Learn two simple and delicious ways to cook eggs.
  • Master a quick and efficient method for cutting eggs into slices.
  • Prepare flavorful braised eggs with aromatic spices.
  • Learn how to select fresh eggs and clean them properly.

Ingredients

  • Fresh eggs (quantity depends on household size)
  • Salt
  • Water
  • Cooking oil
  • Ginger
  • Garlic
  • Chili peppers (小米椒)
  • Dried chili flakes (optional)
  • Scallions (蒜苗)
  • Soy sauce (生抽)
  • Star anise (八角)
  • Cassia bark (桂皮)
  • Bay leaves (香叶)
  • Sichuan peppercorns (花椒)
  • Dried chilies (干海椒)
  • Sugar (白糖)
  • Dark soy sauce (老抽)

Instructions

Part 1: Golden Eggs (金钱蛋)

  1. Select fresh eggs by shaking them; no sound indicates freshness.
  2. Prepare eggs according to household size, place in a bowl, add salt and water, and let soak for 10 minutes.
  3. Rinse eggs thoroughly to remove impurities.
  4. Use a thread to cut the eggs into 1cm thick slices (avoiding the yolk).
  5. Heat oil in a pan until slightly smoking.
  6. Fry egg slices over high heat until golden brown on both sides (about 1 minute per side).
  7. In the same pan, stir-fry ginger, garlic, and chili peppers until fragrant.
  8. Add the fried eggs, salt, soy sauce, and optional dried chili flakes.
  9. Stir-fry until the sauce is combined and scallions are wilted.
  10. Serve immediately.

Part 2: Braised Eggs (卤蛋)

  1. Score the eggs vertically with a knife, being careful not to cut too deep.
  2. Place the eggs in a bowl.
  3. Add star anise, cassia bark, bay leaves, Sichuan peppercorns, dried chilies, ginger, garlic, salt, sugar, and dark soy sauce.
  4. Add enough water to cover the eggs.
  5. Bring to a boil, then reduce heat and simmer for 30 minutes.
  6. Serve after the eggs are fully colored and flavored. You can let them soak longer for a stronger flavor.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=rzGVjIiZKk0

gongbao_jidin.txt - 宫保鸡丁 (Gōngbǎo Jīdīng)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and authentic Gongbao Chicken at home.
  • Master the technique of marinating chicken for a tender texture.
  • Create a flavorful sauce that balances sweet, sour, spicy, and savory notes.

Ingredients

  • Chicken breast: 鸡胸肉 (Jīxiōngròu) - amount not specified, but adjust to your needs.
  • Salt: 盐 (Yán) - 1 tbsp for marinating, a dash for sauce.
  • Baking soda: 小苏打 (Xiǎo sū dǎ) - 1 tsp
  • Ginger: 姜 (Jiāng) - a small amount, sliced.
  • Pepper: 胡椒粉 (Hújiāofěn) - a small amount.
  • Cooking wine: 料酒 (Liàojiǔ) - a small amount.
  • Potato starch: 土豆淀粉 (Tǔdòu diànfěn) - 1 tbsp for marinating, 1 tbsp for sauce.
  • Cooking oil: 食用油 (Shíyòngyóu) - a small amount for marinating, amount for cooking not specified.
  • Carrot: 胡萝卜 (Húluóbo) - 1/2, diced.
  • Cucumber: 黄瓜 (Huángguā) - 1, diced.
  • Scallion: 大葱 (Dàcōng) - 1/2, sliced.
  • Dried chili peppers: 干辣椒 (Gānlàjiāo) - a handful.
  • Sichuan peppercorns: 花椒 (Huājiāo) - a small handful.
  • Sugar: 白糖 (Báitáng) - 1 tbsp
  • Soy sauce: 生抽 (Shēngchōu) - 1 tbsp
  • Dark soy sauce: 老抽 (Lǎochōu) - a dash
  • Rice vinegar: 米醋 (Mǐcù) or 香醋 (Xiāngcù) - 1/2 tbsp
  • Water: 清水 (Qīngshuǐ) - amount not specified.
  • Peanuts: 花生米 (Huāshēngmǐ) - a handful, for garnish.
  • Sesame seeds: 白芝麻 (Báizhīma) - a pinch, for garnish.
  • Sesame oil: 香油 (Xiāngyóu) - a dash, for garnish.

Instructions

  1. Marinate chicken: Rinse chicken breast and soak in salt water for 5 minutes. Rinse again, cut into small pieces, and marinate with salt, baking soda, ginger, pepper, cooking wine, potato starch, and oil for 20 minutes.
  2. Prepare vegetables: Dice carrot and cucumber. Slice scallion, and prepare dried chilies and Sichuan peppercorns.
  3. Make the sauce: Combine sugar, soy sauce, dark soy sauce, rice vinegar, salt, pepper, potato starch, and water in a bowl. Mix well.
  4. Stir-fry chicken: Stir-fry marinated chicken over high heat until golden brown. Remove and set aside.
  5. Stir-fry vegetables and spices: Stir-fry carrots for 1 minute. Add scallions, chilies, and peppercorns; stir-fry until fragrant. Add cucumber and stir-fry briefly.
  6. Combine and finish: Add the cooked chicken back to the pan. Stir-fry until heated through. Pour in the sauce and stir-fry until thickened.
  7. Garnish and serve: Stir in peanuts, sesame seeds, and sesame oil. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Et82TJoKE1A

gongbao_jitding.txt - 宫保鸡丁 (Gong Bao Ji Ding)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and affordable Gong Bao Ji Ding at home.
  • Master the technique of marinating chicken for a tender and flavorful result.
  • Understand the importance of balancing flavors in this classic Sichuan dish.

Ingredients

  • 1 lb boneless, skinless chicken breast (or chicken thighs)
  • 1 tbsp salt
  • 1/2 tsp baking soda (小苏打 - xiǎo sū dǎ)
  • 1 tbsp ginger, julienned (姜丝 - jiāng sī)
  • 1 tsp black pepper (胡椒粉 - hú jiāo fěn)
  • 1 tbsp cooking wine (料酒 - liào jiǔ)
  • 2 tbsp potato starch (土豆淀粉 - tǔdòu diànfěn)
  • 1 tsp cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòng yóu)
  • 1/2 carrot, diced (胡萝卜 - hú luó bo)
  • 1 cucumber, diced (黄瓜 - huáng guā)
  • 1/2 green onion, chopped (大葱 - dà cōng)
  • 1 handful dried chilies (干辣椒 - gān là jiāo)
  • 1 handful Sichuan peppercorns (花椒 - huā jiāo)
  • 1 tbsp sugar (白糖 - bái táng)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽 - shēng chōu)
  • A dash of dark soy sauce (老抽 - lǎo chōu)
  • 1/2 tbsp rice vinegar or other white vinegar (米醋/香醋 - mǐ cù/xiāng cù)
  • A dash of salt (盐 - yán)
  • A dash of black pepper (胡椒粉 - hú jiāo fěn)
  • 1 tbsp potato starch (土豆淀粉 - tǔdòu diànfěn)
  • Water (清水 - qīng shuǐ)
  • Peanuts (花生米 - huā shēng mǐ)
  • Sesame seeds (白芝麻 - bái zhī ma)
  • Sesame oil (香油 - xiāng yóu)

Instructions

  1. Marinate chicken: In a bowl, mix salt and water. Add chicken breast, soak for 5 minutes, rinse, and pat dry. Cut chicken into small pieces.
  2. Prepare marinade: In a bowl, mix chicken with salt, baking soda, ginger, pepper, cooking wine, and potato starch. Mix well until sticky (about 1-2 minutes). Add a little cooking oil and mix gently. Marinate for 20 minutes.
  3. Prepare vegetables: Dice carrot and cucumber. Chop green onion.
  4. Prepare sauce: In a bowl, mix sugar, soy sauce, dark soy sauce, vinegar, salt, pepper, potato starch, and water. Mix well.
  5. Stir-fry chicken: Heat oil in a wok or large pan over high heat. Stir-fry chicken until golden brown (about 1-2 minutes). Remove and set aside.
  6. Stir-fry vegetables: Add carrot to the pan and stir-fry for 1 minute until slightly softened. Add green onion, chilies, and peppercorns. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  7. Add cucumber and chicken: Add cucumber and stir-fry briefly. Add the cooked chicken, stir-fry until heated through.
  8. Add sauce: Add sauce and stir-fry until thickened.
  9. Garnish and serve: Stir in peanuts, sesame seeds, and sesame oil. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Et82TJoKE1A

guangdong_steamed_rice_noodles.txt - Guangdong Steamed Rice Noodles

Objectives

  • Make a delicious and easy Guangdong-style steamed rice noodle breakfast.
  • Use simple ingredients and a quick cooking method.
  • Create a flavorful and nutritious meal suitable for weekday mornings.

Ingredients

3 servings of fresh rice noodles (新竹米粉 - Xīnzhú mǐfěn) 1/2 small onion, thinly sliced 1 carrot, peeled and julienned 2 handfuls bean sprouts, rinsed and drained 2-4 eggs A small piece of lean pork, thinly sliced and shredded 1 tsp salt A pinch of black pepper A pinch of corn starch A little water A small amount of chopped scallions A small piece of ginger, minced Several cloves of garlic, minced A dash of soy sauce A pinch of salt A pinch of five-spice powder A little peanut oil

Instructions

  1. Soak the rice noodles in warm water until softened.
  2. While the noodles soak, prepare the vegetables: slice the onion, julienne the carrot, and rinse the bean sprouts.
  3. Whisk the eggs together thoroughly until no lumps remain. Set aside.
  4. Prepare the pork: slice and shred the pork, then add salt, pepper, cornstarch, and water. Mix well to marinate.
  5. Mince the ginger and garlic. Chop the scallions.
  6. Once the noodles are soft, drain them and place them in a bowl. Add a dash of soy sauce, salt, five-spice powder, and peanut oil. Mix well.
  7. Heat oil in a pan and cook the eggs until fluffy. Set aside.
  8. In the same pan, sauté the ginger, garlic, and scallions until fragrant.
  9. Add the marinated pork and stir-fry until the color changes.
  10. Add the carrots, onions, and bean sprouts. Stir-fry until tender-crisp. Season with a pinch of salt.
  11. Add the rice noodles to the pan and stir-fry until well combined. Add a little soy sauce to taste.
  12. Transfer the mixture to a larger dish. Top with the cooked eggs.
  13. Steam for 3-5 minutes, or until heated through.
  14. Garnish with chopped scallions.
  15. Serve immediately.

guangdong_style_steamed_rice_noodles.txt - 广东式蒸米粉

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy Guangdong-style steamed rice noodle breakfast.

  • 3 servings of fresh rice noodles (新竹米粉, Xīnzhú mǐfěn)
  • 1/2 small onion, thinly sliced
  • 1 carrot, peeled and julienned
  • 20 cents worth of bean sprouts, rinsed and drained
  • 2-4 eggs, whisked
  • A small piece of lean pork, thinly sliced and shredded
  • 1 small spoonful of salt
  • A pinch of black pepper
  • A little cornstarch
  • A little water
  • A small amount of chopped scallions
  • A small piece of ginger, minced
  • Several cloves of garlic, minced
  • A dash of soy sauce
  • A pinch of salt
  • A pinch of five-spice powder
  • A little peanut oil

Instructions

guoba_tofu.txt - Crispy Tofu with Egg and Minced Meat

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious crispy tofu dish.
  • Master a unique cooking method for achieving a crispy exterior and soft interior.
  • Create a flavorful tofu dish with simple ingredients and easy-to-follow steps.

Ingredients

  • 1 block Laodoufu (old tofu)
  • 1 tbsp dried shrimp peel
  • 4 eggs
  • A handful of green onions, chopped
  • A small amount of lean meat, finely minced
  • 1 tsp table salt
  • A pinch of fresh matsutake (optional)
  • Five-spice powder (to taste)
  • A pinch of sugar
  • 1 tbsp cornmeal
  • 1 tbsp potato starch
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Crumble the Laodoufu in a bowl using clean hands, squeezing out excess water. Knead it like tofu residue.
  2. Add the dried shrimp peel, eggs, and chopped green onions to the crumbled tofu. Mix well with chopsticks until thoroughly combined. Set aside.
  3. Finely mince the lean meat.
  4. In a separate bowl, combine the minced meat, salt, matsutake (if using), five-spice powder, sugar, cornmeal, and potato starch. Mix well with chopsticks until the seasoning is evenly distributed.
  5. Heat a wok or pan with a small amount of oil. Swirl the oil to coat the pan evenly to prevent sticking.
  6. Add the tofu mixture to the hot pan, spreading it into a pancake shape. Smooth the surface.
  7. Cook over medium-low heat until the bottom is set. This takes approximately 3-4 minutes.
  8. Use a spatula to gently break the tofu pancake into smaller pieces.
  9. Flip the tofu pieces and continue cooking, pressing gently with the spatula to ensure even cooking and to incorporate the minced meat filling.
  10. Fry until both sides are golden brown and crispy. If you prefer a crispier texture, continue frying for a longer time.
  11. Remove from heat, transfer to a plate, and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=H7YqSWmlLWU

herb_carp_slow_cooked.txt - Slow-Cooked Herb Carp

Objectives

  • Prepare and cook herb carp using a simple yet flavorful method.
  • Ensure the fish is tender, juicy, and not fishy or spicy.
  • Present a step-by-step guide for cooking delicious and easy-to-eat herb carp.

Ingredients

  • Fresh herb carp (cleaned and scaled)
  • 1/2 teaspoon salt
  • Pinch of pepper
  • 1 tablespoon rice wine
  • 1 tablespoon cornstarch
  • 1 tablespoon all-purpose flour
  • Onion (amount unspecified)
  • Ginger (amount unspecified)
  • Garlic (amount unspecified)
  • Green and red chili peppers (amount unspecified, optional)
  • Green onions (amount unspecified)
  • 1 egg
  • Cooking oil (amount unspecified)
  • 1 tablespoon red bean paste
  • Light soy sauce (amount unspecified)
  • Dark soy sauce (amount unspecified)
  • Sugar (amount unspecified)
  • Vinegar (amount unspecified)
  • Water (amount unspecified)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the fish: Clean, scale, and fillet the herb carp. Remove the bones and cut the fish into bite-sized pieces.
  2. Marinate the fish: In a large bowl, combine the fish pieces with chopped onion, ginger, salt, pepper, and rice wine. Mix well and set aside for 20 minutes.
  3. Prepare the batter: In a separate bowl, whisk together the egg, cornstarch, all-purpose flour. Add the marinated fish and gently toss until evenly coated.
  4. Prepare aromatics: Mince garlic, ginger, and green onions. Slice green and red chili peppers thinly (optional).
  5. Fry the fish: Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan over medium-low heat. Add the fish pieces one by one and fry slowly until golden brown on all sides.
  6. Make the sauce: In the same pan, add oil and sauté minced garlic, ginger, and green onions until fragrant.
  7. Add the paste and seasonings: Stir in red bean paste, then add light and dark soy sauce, sugar, vinegar, and a little more salt and pepper.
  8. Simmer the fish: Add water to the pan, cover, and simmer over medium-low heat for 3-5 minutes.
  9. Finish the dish: Uncover the pan, add sliced chili peppers (if using), and increase the heat to thicken the sauce.
  10. Serve: Turn off the heat, transfer the slow-cooked herb carp to a serving dish, and serve immediately.

homemade_spice_powder.txt - Homemade Spice Powder

Objectives

  • Learn to make homemade spice powder (onion, cilantro, and green onion) cheaply.
  • Minimize waste by using the entire plant.
  • Preserve the spice powder for future use.

Ingredients

  • A handful of green onions
  • A bunch of cilantro
  • Celery (amount not specified)

Instructions

  1. Trim the roots from a handful of green onions. Reserve the roots for other uses.
  2. Wash the green onions thoroughly and place them in a bamboo basket to air dry.
  3. Wash and clean the cilantro, then place it in a bamboo basket to air dry.
  4. Cut the celery into smaller pieces to speed up drying.
  5. Cut the green onions in half, remove the hard core, and chop into small pieces.
  6. Place the chopped green onions in an air fryer and bake at 120°C for 20 minutes.
  7. Remove the baked green onions, place them in a bowl, and crush them into a fine powder using your hands.
  8. Transfer the green onion powder to a clean, dry jar and refrigerate for up to a month.
  9. Dry the cilantro and celery in the air fryer at 120°C for approximately 30 minutes, stirring halfway through for even drying.
  10. Crush the dried cilantro and celery into a powder using your hands.
  11. Store the cilantro and celery powder in a labeled jar. (Optional: Use a grinder for finer powder).

home_style_cauliflower.txt - Home-Style Cauliflower

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare fresh cauliflower for optimal texture and flavor.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful stir-fry technique for cauliflower.
  • Create a restaurant-quality cauliflower dish at home.

Ingredients

  • 1 head of fresh cauliflower
  • 1 tsp salt
  • 2 g baking soda
  • Water to cover cauliflower
  • Several shiitake mushrooms
  • Several cloves garlic
  • 1 piece ginger
  • Several scallions
  • Several dried chilies
  • 2 slices five-spice pork belly
  • Cooking oil
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce
  • Oyster sauce
  • A pinch of salt
  • A pinch of sugar
  • A pinch of mushroom seasoning

Instructions

  1. Select a fresh cauliflower with green stalks. Cut the cauliflower into florets, leaving the older stem behind. Do not chop, but break apart the florets to maintain shape.
  2. Place the cauliflower florets in a large bowl. Add salt, baking soda, and enough water to submerge the cauliflower. Soak for 5 minutes.
  3. Rinse the cauliflower thoroughly under running water until the water runs clear to remove any insects or dirt. Drain well.
  4. Prepare the accompanying ingredients: Slice shiitake mushrooms thickly, mince garlic and ginger, chop scallions and dried chilies, and thinly slice the pork belly.
  5. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add the cauliflower and blanch for 60 seconds with 1 tbsp salt and a little oil to preserve color. Add the mushrooms and blanch for 30 seconds.
  6. Immediately remove the vegetables and plunge them into ice water to maintain crispness. Drain well.
  7. Heat oil in a wok or frying pan. Add the pork belly and stir-fry until golden brown, rendering the fat.
  8. Add the ginger and garlic and stir-fry until fragrant. Add the dried chilies.
  9. Add the soy sauce to color, then add the blanched cauliflower and mushrooms. Stir-fry until well combined.
  10. Season with soy sauce, oyster sauce, a pinch of salt, sugar, and mushroom seasoning. Stir-fry until flavors are well incorporated.
  11. Stir-fry until the cauliflower is tender-crisp and has absorbed the flavors.
  12. Add the chopped scallions and stir-fry briefly.
  13. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=PvhqUT4NxQI

hongshao_qiezi.txt - 红烧茄子 (Hóngshāo Qiézi) - Braised Eggplant

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and flavorful braised eggplant.
  • Master the technique of preparing eggplant to achieve a crispy texture.
  • Create a simple yet restaurant-quality dish at home.

Ingredients

  • 2 fresh eggplants (茄子 - qiézi)
  • Salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • White vinegar (白醋 - báicù)
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒 - xiǎomǐjiāo), finely sliced
  • Several cloves garlic (蒜 - suàn), smashed and minced
  • 2 green onions (小葱 - xiǎocōng), chopped
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽 - shēngchōu)
  • A dash of dark soy sauce (老抽 - lǎochōu)
  • Appropriate amount of oyster sauce (蚝油 - háoyóu)
  • 1 tbsp sugar (白糖 - báitáng)
  • 1 tbsp mushroom seasoning (松茸鲜 - sōngróng xiān)
  • 1 tsp cornstarch (玉米淀粉 - yùmǐ diànfěn)
  • Water (清水 - qīngshuǐ)
  • 30g cornstarch (玉米淀粉 - yùmǐ diànfěn)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòngyóu)

Instructions

  1. Wash eggplants, rub with salt, rinse, and drain.
  2. Cut eggplants into chunks, place in a bowl, add salt and white vinegar, mix well, and marinate for 10 minutes.
  3. Prepare chili peppers, minced garlic, and chopped green onions.
  4. In a small bowl, mix soy sauce, dark soy sauce, oyster sauce, sugar, mushroom seasoning, cornstarch, and water.
  5. Rinse the marinated eggplants, squeeze out excess water, and add 30g cornstarch, mixing well.
  6. Heat oil in a wok or pan, add eggplants, and stir-fry until softened. Remove and set aside.
  7. Add a little oil to the pan, add garlic and chili peppers, and stir-fry until fragrant.
  8. Add the eggplant and the prepared sauce. Stir-fry over high heat for about 2 minutes until flavors combine.
  9. Garnish with green onions and chili peppers.
  10. Serve and enjoy!

hot_sour_soup.txt - حساء حار وحامض

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious hot and sour soup.
  • Master the simple steps to prepare this flavorful dish.
  • Understand the techniques for achieving the perfect texture and taste.

Ingredients

  • 2 tomatoes
  • Handful of enoki mushrooms
  • 2 shiitake mushrooms
  • 1 piece of soft tofu
  • Chicken breast (amount unspecified)
  • 1 small piece of ginger
  • Handful of coriander leaves
  • 2 eggs
  • 30g light soy sauce
  • 30g balsamic vinegar
  • Salt (to taste)
  • Pepper (to taste)
  • 10g chili oil (or red oil)
  • Water (amount unspecified)
  • 10g camellia oil
  • Water starch (amount unspecified)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the tomatoes: Score the tomatoes, blanch in boiling water for 2 minutes, then peel. Remove the core and chop into small pieces.
  2. Prepare the enoki mushrooms: Trim the roots and separate into florets. Rinse with clean water.
  3. Prepare the shiitake mushrooms: Wash and slice thinly.
  4. Prepare the tofu: Cut into thin slices and blanch in boiling water to remove any beany smell.
  5. Prepare the chicken: Peel and slice thinly.
  6. Prepare the ginger: Slice thinly.
  7. Prepare the coriander: Chop roughly.
  8. Prepare the egg mixture: Crack 2 eggs into a bowl, whisk with light soy sauce, balsamic vinegar, salt, pepper, and chili oil until well combined.
  9. Blanch the chicken, mushrooms, and tofu: Blanch all ingredients except tomatoes and eggs in boiling water for 30 seconds. Remove and drain.
  10. Sauté the aromatics and tomatoes: Heat camellia oil in a pot, sauté ginger and chopped tomatoes.
  11. Add broth and simmer: Add water to the pot and bring to a boil. Skim off any foam.
  12. Add blanched ingredients and tofu: Add the blanched ingredients and tofu to the pot. Simmer for 2 minutes.
  13. Add the hot and sour sauce: Add the egg mixture to the soup.
  14. Thicken the soup: Add water starch in small amounts until the desired thickness is achieved.
  15. Gently stir in the egg mixture: Pour the egg mixture into the soup in a straight line, without stirring vigorously. Let it simmer on low heat for a few seconds.
  16. Garnish and serve: Sprinkle with chopped coriander. Serve hot.

huacai_chao_roumo.txt - Stir-fried Cauliflower with Minced Meat

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare and cook cauliflower for optimal texture.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful stir-fry recipe.
  • Understand the importance of pre-treatment for vegetables.

Ingredients

  • 1 head of cauliflower (choose one with tightly packed florets and green stems)
  • 200g lean pork, thinly sliced and minced
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • 1 small onion, thinly sliced
  • 1 green chili pepper, diagonally sliced
  • 1 red chili pepper, diagonally sliced
  • 2 cloves garlic, smashed and minced
  • 1 tablespoon cooking oil
  • 1 tablespoon soy sauce (or to taste)
  • 1 tablespoon chicken bouillon (or to taste)
  • 1 teaspoon homemade garlic sauce (optional)
  • 1/2 small bowl of water
  • 1 small piece of ginger, minced
  • 1 small bunch of scallions, minced
  • 1 teaspoon cumin seeds (optional)

Instructions

  1. Trim the cauliflower into individual florets. Discard the core.
  2. In a large bowl, submerge the cauliflower florets in salted water for 10 minutes to disinfect and clean.
  3. Rinse the cauliflower thoroughly with clean water twice and drain well.
  4. Mince the lean pork.
  5. Mince the ginger and garlic.
  6. Slice the onion, green and red chili peppers and scallions.
  7. Heat cooking oil in a wok or large pan over medium-low heat.
  8. Add the cauliflower florets and stir-fry until slightly browned. Remove from pan and set aside.
  9. Add minced ginger and garlic to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Add the minced pork and stir-fry until browned and cooked through.
  11. Add 1 tablespoon of soy sauce and stir-fry until fragrant.
  12. Add the cauliflower back into the pan along with the sliced green and red peppers. Stir to combine.
  13. Add 1/2 small bowl of water.
  14. Add 1 teaspoon salt, 1 tablespoon chicken bouillon, and 1 teaspoon homemade garlic sauce (if using). Stir to combine.
  15. Cover the pan and simmer for approximately 1 minute.
  16. Add the sliced onions and cumin seeds (if using).
  17. Cover and simmer for another 10-15 seconds.
  18. Stir in the chopped scallions.
  19. Serve immediately.

huacai_chao.txt - Stir-fried Cauliflower

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious stir-fried cauliflower at home.
  • Master the technique of stir-frying cauliflower to achieve a crisp texture.
  • Utilize simple ingredients and easy-to-follow steps for a restaurant-quality dish.

Ingredients

  • 1 head of organic cauliflower (approximately 1 lb)
  • 100g five-spice pork belly (五花肉)
  • 2-3 scallions (小葱), chopped
  • 1 piece of ginger (生姜), minced
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜), minced
  • 2 stalks of garlic chives (蒜苗), chopped
  • 1 tbsp salt (食盐)
  • 1 tsp sugar (白糖)
  • 1 tbsp yellow bean sauce (黄豆酱)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽)
  • 1 tbsp oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • A handful of dried chili peppers (干辣椒段)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)
  • Optional: cumin seeds (孜然粒)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the cauliflower: Trim the cauliflower into florets. Place florets in a large bowl, add salt and enough water to submerge. Soak for 10 minutes to sanitize and remove any pesticides. Rinse thoroughly with clean water and drain well.
  2. Prepare the meat and aromatics: Cut the pork belly into thin slices. Mince the ginger and garlic. Chop the scallions and garlic chives.
  3. Stir-fry the cauliflower: Heat a small amount of oil in a wok or large pan over medium-low heat. Add the cauliflower and stir-fry until slightly browned and slightly tender-crisp. Remove and set aside.
  4. Stir-fry the pork belly: Add the pork belly slices to the same pan and cook over low heat until the fat renders and the pork is slightly browned.
  5. Add aromatics and seasoning: Add the minced ginger, garlic, and scallions to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant. Add salt, sugar, yellow bean sauce, soy sauce, oyster sauce, and dried chilies. Stir well to combine.
  6. Combine and stir-fry: Add the pre-cooked cauliflower to the pan and stir-fry until well coated with the sauce.
  7. Add garlic chives and cumin (optional): Add the chopped garlic chives and optional cumin seeds. Stir-fry until the garlic chives are wilted.
  8. Serve: Remove from heat and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=rWU32RMyzHg

huangdoujiang.txt - Homemade Yellow Soybean Paste

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and healthy homemade yellow soybean paste.
  • Master the technique of steaming soybeans to achieve perfect texture.
  • Understand the importance of using quality ingredients and proper cooking methods.
  • Learn how to make flavorful and aromatic cooking oil using spices.

Ingredients

  • 400g dried soybeans (黃豆 huángdòu)
  • Water (清水 qīngshuǐ)
  • Ginger (薑 jiāng)
  • Green onions (蔥 cōng)
  • Bay leaves (香葉 xiāngyè)
  • Cinnamon sticks (桂皮 guìpí)
  • Star anise (八角 bājiǎo)
  • Dried red peppercorns (紅花椒 hóng huājiāo)
  • Dried chili peppers (乾海椒 gānhǎijiāo)
  • Peanuts (花生米 huāshēngmǐ - optional)
  • Peanut oil (花生油 huāshēngyóu)
  • Sweet bean sauce (甜麵醬 tián miànjiàng) - 1 tbsp
  • Garlic paste (蒜蓉醬 sùróngjiàng) - 2 tbsp or minced garlic
  • Salt (食鹽 shíyán) - 2 tbsp
  • Songrong fresh (松茸鮮 sōngróngxiān) - 2 tbsp (presumably a type of seasoning)
  • Oyster sauce (蠔油 háoyóu)
  • Rock sugar (冰糖 bīngtáng) - 18g
  • Dark soy sauce (老抽 lǎochōu)
  • Sesame seeds (熟芝麻 shú zhīma) - for garnish

Instructions

  1. Rinse 400g of dried soybeans thoroughly to remove dust and impurities.
  2. Soak the soybeans in water for at least one hour until fully hydrated.
  3. Mince ginger and green onions.
  4. Prepare spices: bay leaves, cinnamon sticks, star anise, dried red peppercorns, and dried chili peppers.
  5. Steam the soaked soybeans for 50 minutes until easily mashed. Add peanuts for enhanced texture if desired.
  6. Heat peanut oil in a pan over medium heat.
  7. Add spices to the hot oil and sauté for 1-2 minutes until fragrant and slightly browned.
  8. Remove the spices using a sieve, reserving the fragrant oil.
  9. Add minced ginger and green onions to the fragrant oil and stir until fragrant.
  10. Add 1 tbsp sweet bean sauce and stir well.
  11. Add the steamed soybeans to the pan.
  12. Add 2 tbsp garlic paste (or minced garlic), 2 tbsp salt, 2 tbsp Songrong fresh, oyster sauce, 18g rock sugar, and dark soy sauce.
  13. Stir well and simmer over medium-low heat for 15 minutes, stirring constantly to prevent sticking.
  14. Continue simmering until the soybeans are golden brown and most of the moisture has evaporated.
  15. Remove from heat and let cool completely.
  16. Transfer the finished soybean paste to an airtight container and refrigerate.
  17. Garnish with sesame seeds before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6x2ltq0Sa7w

huanggua_chaorou.txt - Cucumber Stir-fry with Pork

Objectives

  • Learn a technique to make crispy cucumbers for stir-fry.
  • Prepare flavorful pork and aromatic sauce for the dish.
  • Master a quick and easy stir-fry method for a delicious summer meal.

Ingredients

  • 3 fresh cucumbers (黄瓜 huángguā)
  • Salt (食盐 shíyán) - double the usual amount for stir-frying
  • Pork (五花肉/瘦肉 wǔhuāròu/shòuròu) - amount to your preference
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒 xiǎomǐjiāo)
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜 suàn)
  • Some scallions (葱 cōng) - only the white parts
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽 shēngchōu)
  • 1/2 tbsp mushroom seasoning (松茸鲜 sōngrōngxiān)
  • 1/2 tsp sugar (白糖 báitáng)
  • A pinch of pepper (胡椒粉 hújiāofěn)
  • 1 tbsp potato starch (土豆淀粉 tǔdòudiànfěn)
  • A small amount of water (清水 qīngshuǐ)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 shíyòngyóu)

Instructions

  1. Wash and trim 3 cucumbers. Slice them into 0.5cm thick rounds.
  2. Place cucumber slices in a bowl. Add double the usual amount of salt used for stir-frying. Mix well by hand and let it sit for 10 minutes to draw out moisture.
  3. While cucumbers are marinating, prepare the pork (five-spice pork or lean pork) and cut into pieces.
  4. Cut chili peppers into small rings, garlic into slices, and only the white parts of the scallions into small pieces.
  5. After 10 minutes, rinse the cucumbers thoroughly under running water to remove excess salt. Squeeze out excess water and set aside.
  6. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, combine soy sauce, mushroom seasoning, sugar, pepper, potato starch, and a little water. Mix until well combined.
  7. Heat a wok or pan over medium-high heat. Add a small amount of oil. Once hot, swirl the oil to coat the pan.
  8. Add the pork to the pan and stir-fry until lightly browned and the excess fat is rendered.
  9. Add the garlic and chili peppers to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Add a small amount of dark soy sauce (老抽 lǎochōu) for color.
  11. Add the marinated cucumbers to the wok. Stir-fry over high heat for about 2 minutes to remove excess moisture. (No additional salt is needed).
  12. Add the prepared sauce to the wok and stir-fry until the cucumbers are coated and heated through.
  13. Finally, add the chopped scallions and stir-fry for another 5-8 seconds.
  14. Remove from heat and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=I-Il-r2NYuI

huaruoshuarou.txt - 滑肉 (Huá ròu) - Slippery Meat

Objectives

  • Learn a new way to cook pork, beyond soup.
  • Achieve a tender and flavorful pork dish.
  • Impress family and friends with a delicious homemade meal.

Ingredients

  • 1 piece of fresh pork (pork leg or snowflake pork recommended), cut into thin, even slices
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽 - shēng chōu)
  • Pepper powder (胡椒粉 - hú jiāo fěn)
  • A pinch of salt (食盐 - shí yán)
  • 1 tbsp cooking wine (料酒 - liào jiǔ)
  • 2 green bell peppers (青椒 - qīng jiāo), deseeded and sliced into rings
  • 2 red bell peppers (红椒 - hóng jiāo), deseeded and sliced into rings
  • 1 piece of ginger (生姜 - shēng jiāng), peeled, thinly sliced, then finely minced
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜 - suàn), smashed and minced
  • 2 scallions (小葱 - xiǎo cōng), finely chopped
  • Some dried chili segments (干辣椒段 - gān là jiāo duàn)
  • A handful of sesame seeds (芝麻 - zhī ma)
  • A little salt (食盐 - shí yán)
  • White sugar (白糖 - bái táng)
  • Soy sauce (生抽 - shēng chōu)
  • Rice vinegar (香醋 - xiāng cù)
  • 1 bowl of sweet potato starch (红薯粉 - hóng shǔ fěn)
  • Hot water (开水 - kāi shuǐ)

Instructions

  1. Cut the pork into thin, even slices.
  2. Marinate the pork slices in soy sauce, pepper powder, salt, and cooking wine. Mix well and let it sit for 10 minutes.
  3. While the pork marinates, prepare the ingredients: slice the bell peppers, mince the ginger and garlic, chop the scallions, and prepare the dried chilies.
  4. Prepare the sauce: Combine the minced ginger, garlic, scallions, dried chilies, sesame seeds, salt, sugar, soy sauce, and rice vinegar in a bowl. Add hot oil. Mix well.
  5. Sift the sweet potato starch to remove lumps.
  6. Add the sifted sweet potato starch to the marinated pork, mixing until the pork is evenly coated.
  7. Add a little hot water to the pork and starch mixture, mixing until it reaches a slightly thick consistency. Add more sweet potato starch if needed.
  8. Bring a pot of water to a boil, then reduce heat to low.
  9. Gently add the pork mixture to the boiling water, ensuring the pieces don't stick together.
  10. Cook until the starch on the surface of the pork is set and the pork floats to the surface (about 5-6 minutes).
  11. Remove the cooked pork with a slotted spoon and drain.
  12. Pour the prepared sauce over the cooked pork.
  13. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Sj1gzt-kcA8

hu_pi_qing_jiao.txt - 虎皮青椒 (Tiger Skin Green Peppers)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious Tiger Skin Green Peppers.
  • Master the technique for achieving the signature "tiger skin" texture.
  • Understand the importance of ingredient selection and preparation.

Ingredients

  • 湖南樟树港辣椒 (Hunan Changshu Gang Peppers): Amount not specified, but enough to fill a wok.
  • 食盐 (Shiyan - Salt): A moderate amount for soaking peppers.
  • 清水 (Qing shui - Clean Water): A moderate amount for soaking peppers.
  • 大蒜 (Da suan - Garlic): Several cloves, minced.
  • 小米椒 (Xiao mi jiao - Small chili peppers): 2, sliced into rings.
  • 五香粉 (Wu xiang fen - Five-spice powder): 1 small spoon.
  • 生抽 (Sheng chou - Light soy sauce): 1 large spoon.
  • 香醋 (Xiang cu - Rice vinegar): 1/3 of a large spoon.
  • 酱油 (Jiang you - Soy sauce): A small amount.
  • 蚝油 (Hao you - Oyster sauce): A small amount.
  • 土豆淀粉 (Tu dou dian fen - Potato starch): 1 small spoon.
  • 清水 (Qing shui - Clean Water): A moderate amount for the sauce.
  • 食用油 (Shi yong you - Cooking oil): A generous amount for stir-frying.

Instructions

  1. Wash and soak the Hunan Changshu Gang peppers in salt water to remove impurities. Rinse thoroughly and drain. Avoid using large green peppers or green line peppers.
  2. Mince the garlic and slice the small chili peppers into rings.
  3. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, combine five-spice powder, light soy sauce, rice vinegar, soy sauce, oyster sauce, potato starch, and water. Mix well.
  4. Heat a wok with a generous amount of oil over high heat until very hot.
  5. Add the drained peppers to the hot oil. Stir-fry continuously, pressing down on the peppers to help them cook evenly and develop the "tiger skin" texture. Stir-fry for approximately 90 seconds until the peppers are slightly wilted and the skin is wrinkled.
  6. Remove the peppers from the wok using a strainer. Do not clean the wok; leave the remaining oil in the wok.
  7. Add the minced garlic and sliced small chili peppers to the wok and stir-fry until fragrant.
  8. Pour the prepared sauce into the wok and bring to a boil over high heat. Stir until the sauce thickens slightly.
  9. Add the stir-fried peppers back to the wok and toss quickly to coat them evenly with the sauce.
  10. Remove from heat and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=fCKCfe2rRwY

hu_tou_gu_luo_bo_tang.txt - 虎头骨萝卜汤 (Hu Tou Gu Luo Bo Tang)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious Hu Tou Gu Luo Bo Tang (Tiger Head Bone Radish Soup).
  • Master the techniques for preparing and cooking the ingredients to achieve optimal flavor and texture.
  • Understand the importance of using fresh, high-quality ingredients for the best results.

Ingredients

  • 虎头骨排骨 (Hu Tou Gu Pai Gu) - Tiger Head Bone Pork Ribs (quantity not specified, adjust to your needs)
  • 白萝卜 (Bai Luo Bo) - White Radish (2 medium)
  • 食用盐 (Shi Yong Yan) - Edible Salt (1 small spoon)
  • 普通面粉 (Pu Tong Mian Fen) - Plain Flour (1 spoon)
  • 生姜 (Sheng Jiang) - Ginger (a generous amount)
  • 葱 (Cong) - Scallions (1)
  • 山茶油 (Shan Cha You) - Camellia Oil (a small amount, or substitute with olive oil or peanut oil)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the ribs: Add a small spoonful of salt and a spoonful of plain flour to the ribs. Mix well with your hands to coat the ribs evenly. This helps to remove impurities and blood.
  2. Soak the ribs: Add lukewarm water to the bowl with the ribs and let them soak for 5 minutes.
  3. Prepare the radish: Peel and wash the white radish. Cut into large chunks.
  4. Prepare the aromatics: Cut the ginger into thick slices and chop the scallions into sections.
  5. Rinse the ribs: After soaking, remove the ribs and rinse thoroughly under running water (warm water is recommended in winter) to remove any remaining impurities and blood. Drain well.
  6. Stir-fry the ribs: Heat a small amount of oil in a pot. Add the ginger slices and stir-fry until fragrant. Remove the ginger and reduce the heat. Add the ribs and stir-fry until slightly browned and the moisture is removed. This step is crucial for a rich and flavorful soup.
  7. Add boiling water: Add boiling water to the pot, ensuring the ribs are fully submerged. Bring to a boil, then skim off any foam or impurities.
  8. Simmer the ribs: Add the scallion sections, cover the pot, and simmer over low heat for 38 minutes.
  9. Add the radish: Remove the scallions. Add the radish chunks to the pot, ensuring they are submerged in the broth. Cover and simmer for another 15 minutes.
  10. Season and finish: Add a small spoonful of salt. Stir gently. Cover and simmer for another 2 minutes to allow the flavors to meld. No other seasonings are needed.
  11. Serve: Turn off the heat. Ladle the soup into bowls and serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=R5d5zzpV4hY

ice_sugar_ginger.txt - 冰糖醋姜 (Bīngtáng cù jiāng)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and crunchy pickled ginger.
  • Understand the proper techniques for preparing and preserving ginger.
  • Avoid common mistakes in pickling ginger, such as using too much salt.

Ingredients

  • Ginger (仔姜 or 小黄姜 - Zǎijiāng or Xiǎo huáng jiāng, preferred for better texture)
  • White sugar (白糖 - Báitáng)
  • Ice sugar (冰糖 - Bīngtáng)
  • Salt (食盐 - Shíyán)
  • Honey (蜂蜜 - Fēngmì)
  • White vinegar (白醋 - Báicù)
  • High-proof liquor (高度白酒 - Gāodù bái jiǔ) - for sealing

Instructions

  1. Prepare the ginger: Wash and peel a suitable amount of young ginger (仔姜 or 小黄姜). Cut into small pieces for easier cleaning.
  2. Clean thoroughly: Submerge ginger in plenty of water to remove dirt and impurities, paying attention to crevices. Choose firm, fresh ginger for optimal results.
  3. Initial Marinating: Place cleaned ginger in a bowl. Add an adequate amount of white sugar to remove bitterness and maintain crispness. Avoid adding salt at this stage. Mix well and let it marinate for at least 30 minutes.
  4. Drain and slice: After marinating, drain excess water. Slice the ginger into pieces of even thickness using a non-stick knife and cutting board for better preservation.
  5. Final Marinating: Place sliced ginger in a large bowl. Add ice sugar, a small amount of salt, honey, and white vinegar. Mix thoroughly to ensure even flavor distribution.
  6. Sterilize and store: Sterilize a glass jar or airtight container with boiling water and let it dry completely. Pack the marinated ginger slices into the container, including the marinade.
  7. Seal and preserve: Add a small amount of high-proof liquor to seal. Close the container tightly and store in a cool, dry place away from direct sunlight. Refrigeration is recommended in hot weather.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=GBWA1QKp1d8

ice_sugar_vinegar_ginger.txt - 冰糖醋姜

Objectives

  • Learn to make crispy, sweet and sour pickled ginger.
  • Understand the importance of selecting fresh ginger and proper cleaning techniques.
  • Master the correct method of pickling ginger to avoid common mistakes.

Ingredients

  • Ginger (仔姜 or 小黄姜 preferred)
  • White sugar (白糖)
  • Ice sugar (冰糖)
  • Salt (食盐)
  • Honey (蜂蜜)
  • White vinegar (白醋)
  • High-proof liquor (高度白酒)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the ginger: Choose fresh, firm ginger (仔姜 or 小黄姜). Break into smaller pieces for easy cleaning.
  2. Clean the ginger: Rinse thoroughly under running water. Use a knife to scrape off the outer layer, paying attention to crevices. Ensure all dirt is removed.
  3. Initial Marinating: Place cleaned ginger in a large bowl. Add enough white sugar to coat the ginger completely. Mix well and let it marinate for at least 30 minutes. This removes bitterness and maintains crispness. Do not add salt at this stage.
  4. Drain and Slice: After 30 minutes, drain the excess water from the ginger. Slice the ginger into evenly sized, moderately thin pieces. Use a non-stick knife and cutting board.
  5. Final Marinating: Place sliced ginger in a large bowl. Add ice sugar, a small amount of salt, honey, and white vinegar. Mix thoroughly to coat all ginger pieces evenly.
  6. Store: Transfer the marinated ginger into a sterilized glass jar or airtight container. Pour in the marinade, ensuring the ginger is fully submerged. Add a small amount of high-proof liquor to seal.
  7. Seal and Store: Seal the container tightly. Store in a cool, dry place away from direct sunlight. For hot weather, refrigerate.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=GBWA1QKp1d8

jiachang_shaocaizi.txt - Home-Style Braised Eggplant

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy home-style braised eggplant dish.
  • Master the technique of preparing eggplant to prevent oil absorption and discoloration.
  • Understand how to create a flavorful sauce to enhance the eggplant's taste.

Ingredients

  • 2 purple eggplants
  • Salt
  • White vinegar
  • Water
  • 1 green bell pepper
  • 1/2 small onion
  • Fatty pork, cut into minced meat
  • Several small chili peppers
  • 1 piece ginger
  • Several garlic cloves
  • Scallions (separate white and green parts)
  • Soy sauce (light)
  • Oyster sauce
  • 1 tbsp.葱蓉鲜 (Congrong Xian, a type of seasoning sauce)
  • A pinch of white sugar
  • 1 tbsp. yellow soybean paste
  • 1 tbsp. potato starch
  • Water
  • Peanut oil

Instructions

  1. Wash eggplants thoroughly with salt water to clean the skin. Do not peel.
  2. Cut eggplants into small square pieces and soak in salt water, white vinegar, and water for 10 minutes to prevent oil absorption and oxidation.
  3. Cut green pepper, onion, small chili peppers, ginger, and garlic into small pieces.
  4. Mince fatty pork.
  5. Mix soy sauce, oyster sauce, 葱蓉鲜, sugar, yellow soybean paste, potato starch, and water to make a sauce.
  6. Drain the eggplant and set aside.
  7. Heat peanut oil in a pan, add minced pork and stir-fry until slightly browned.
  8. Add eggplant and stir-fry until soft. (Medium heat, about 2 minutes)
  9. Add ginger, garlic, and chili peppers; stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Add green pepper and onion; stir-fry until tender (about 20 seconds).
  11. Pour in the sauce and stir well to coat.
  12. Add sesame oil and chopped scallions.
  13. Serve immediately. Optionally, reheat in a clay pot for a richer flavor.

jiangxi_chaomifan.txt - Authentic Jiangxi Fried Rice Noodles

Objectives

  • Learn to make authentic Jiangxi-style fried rice noodles.
  • Master the techniques for achieving a dry, flavorful, and non-greasy dish.
  • Understand the importance of ingredient selection and preparation.

Ingredients

  • Fresh rice noodles (amount depends on serving size, pre-soaked in boiling water)
  • 80¢ worth of green bean sprouts
  • A handful of small Chinese cabbage (小白菜), chopped
  • 2¥ worth of lean pork, thinly sliced
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒), finely chopped (adjust to spice preference)
  • Plenty of chopped scallions (葱花)
  • Cooking oil
  • 2 eggs
  • Dried chili flakes (干辣椒面)
  • Soy sauce (老抽)
  • Salt
  • Pepper

Instructions

  1. Prepare ingredients: Soak rice noodles in boiling water. Wash and drain green bean sprouts. Chop cabbage into small pieces. Thinly slice pork. Finely chop chili peppers and scallions.

  2. Heat a wok or large pan over high heat. Add a small amount of cooking oil.

  3. Add eggs, scramble and cook until fragrant.

  4. Add chili peppers and pork, stir-fry until fragrant.

  5. Add dried chili flakes and stir-fry until fragrant and dispersed.

  6. Add green bean sprouts and cabbage, stir-fry until slightly wilted and dry.

  7. Add soaked rice noodles to the wok.

  8. Add soy sauce (老抽) for color, salt, and pepper to taste. (No light soy sauce (生抽) needed).

  9. Stir-fry constantly over high heat until noodles are soft, cooked through, and slightly crispy. The wok should sizzle. This should take about 80 seconds.

  10. Add chopped scallions and stir-fry for a few seconds.

  11. Serve immediately. The finished dish should be dry and not oily.
