jiang_yan_doufu.txt - 酱腌豆腐 (Jiang Yan Doufu)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a flavorful and tender braised tofu dish.
  • Master a simple yet effective method for removing bean curd smell.
  • Create a delicious and visually appealing side dish perfect for any meal.

Ingredients

  • 2 blocks of firm tofu (老豆腐 - lǎo dòufu)
  • Salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • Warm water (温水 - wēnshuǐ)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòng yóu)
  • Soy sauce (酱油 - jiàngyóu)
  • Chicken bouillon (鸡汁 - jī zhī)
  • Green chilies (青椒 - qīngjiāo)
  • Red chilies (红椒 - hóngjiāo)
  • Scallions (小葱 - xiǎocōng)
  • Ginger (生姜 - shēngjiāng)
  • Garlic (蒜 - suàn)

Instructions

  1. Add salt to the surface of the tofu blocks and submerge them in warm water to remove the bean curd smell and maintain freshness. Soak for at least 20 minutes, or even a whole day in summer.
  2. Cut the soaked tofu into small square pieces.
  3. In a large bowl, marinate the tofu with sufficient salt, an appropriate amount of soy sauce (for color), a spoonful of chicken bouillon, and cooking oil. Gently mix to avoid breaking the tofu. Marinate for 20 minutes.
  4. Prepare the garnishes: finely chop scallions, ginger, and garlic. Slice green and red chilies into rings, then roughly chop them.
  5. Heat a small amount of cooking oil in a wok. Add the chilies and a spoonful of salt, stir-fry until half-cooked, then set aside.
  6. In a clean wok, sauté the chopped scallions, ginger, and garlic until fragrant over low heat.
  7. Add the marinated tofu to the wok, spreading it evenly. Increase heat and pan-fry until fragrant.
  8. Pour the remaining marinade from the bowl into the wok. Cover and simmer for 3-5 minutes.
  9. Open the lid, and if the sauce is still abundant, increase the heat to reduce the sauce.
  10. Add the stir-fried chilies and remaining garlic. Cover and simmer for about 1 minute.
  11. Serve the fragrant braised tofu hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=zRLEujDTo54

jiang_yan_luobo.txt - 酱腌萝卜 (Pickled Radish)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a quick and easy pickled radish dish.
  • Understand the process of preparing and marinating the radish.
  • Create a flavorful and refreshing side dish perfect for any meal.

Ingredients

  • 1 large white radish (白萝卜)
  • Salt (盐)
  • White sugar (白糖)
  • 1 piece ginger (生姜), peeled and thinly sliced
  • Several cloves garlic (蒜), peeled and thinly sliced
  • Optional: Chopped chili peppers (剁辣椒)
  • White sugar (白糖)
  • White vinegar (白醋)
  • Soy sauce (酱油)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油)

Instructions

  1. Wash the radish thoroughly and peel it.
  2. Cut the radish in half lengthwise, then into quarters, and finally into thin slices.
  3. Place the radish slices in a bowl. Add a small amount of salt and white sugar. Mix well to coat.
  4. Marinate for about 30 minutes, allowing the radish to release its moisture.
  5. While the radish marinates, prepare the ginger and garlic by thinly slicing them. Prepare any optional chili peppers.
  6. After 30 minutes, drain the excess water from the marinated radish. Do not rinse.
  7. Add the ginger, garlic, and optional chili peppers to the bowl with the radish.
  8. Add a small amount of white sugar, white vinegar, soy sauce, and oyster sauce.
  9. Using disposable gloves, mix thoroughly to combine all ingredients.
  10. Refrigerate for at least 30 minutes, or up to 2 hours for a stronger flavor.
  11. Serve chilled.

jian_yu.txt - Pan-fried Fish

Objectives

  • Learn to pan-fry fish without sticking or breaking.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful fish recipe.
  • Acquire techniques for preparing and marinating fish for optimal results.

Ingredients

  • 1 fresh perch (or similar fish)
  • 2 tbsp cooking wine (料酒 liàojiǔ)
  • 1 piece ginger (生姜 shēngjiāng), sliced
  • Several scallions (小葱 xiǎocōng), chopped
  • Salt (食盐 shíyán)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽 shēngchōu)
  • 1/2 tbsp cooking wine (料酒 liàojiǔ)
  • Sugar (白糖 báitáng)
  • 1/2 tbsp rice vinegar (香醋 xiāngcù)
  • Pepper (胡椒粉 hújiāofěn)
  • 1 piece ginger (生姜 shēngjiāng), sliced
  • 1 clove garlic (蒜瓣 sùnbàn), sliced
  • 1 scallion (大葱 dàcōng), chopped
  • 1 red bell pepper (大红椒 dà hóngjiāo), diced
  • Flour (面粉 miànfěn)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 shíyòngyóu)
  • Flower pepper (花椒 huājiāo)
  • 1 tbsp Doubanjiang (红油豆瓣酱 hóngyóu dòubànjiàng)
  • Water (清水 qīngshuǐ)

Instructions

  1. Clean the fish thoroughly, removing scales, gills, and the black membrane in the belly cavity.
  2. Trim the fins and tail for a cleaner look.
  3. Pat the fish dry with paper towels.
  4. Make shallow diagonal cuts on both sides of the fish.
  5. Marinate the fish with cooking wine, ginger, and scallions for 20 minutes.
  6. Prepare the sauce: Mix soy sauce, cooking wine, salt, sugar, rice vinegar, and pepper in a bowl.
  7. Prepare the garnish: Slice ginger and garlic, chop scallions and dice red bell pepper.
  8. Coat the fish with a thin layer of flour.
  9. Heat oil in a pan, coating it with ginger to prevent sticking.
  10. Add the fish to the hot pan and fry over medium heat for about 5 minutes per side, or until golden brown and easily movable.
  11. Remove the fish and set aside.
  12. Add flower pepper to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant.
  13. Add ginger, garlic, and scallions, then stir-fry until fragrant.
  14. Add Doubanjiang and stir-fry until the oil turns red.
  15. Add water and bring to a boil.
  16. Return the fish to the pan, add the prepared sauce, cover, and simmer for 2 minutes.
  17. Open the lid, baste the fish with the sauce, and simmer for another 3-5 minutes.
  18. Add the diced red bell pepper and cook for 2 minutes.
  19. Thicken the sauce with a cornstarch slurry (optional).
  20. Transfer the fish to a serving plate and pour the sauce over it.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=DH-IFAVe6Vw

kimchi_noodles.txt - Kimchi Noodles (شعيرية الكرنب)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy kimchi noodle dish at home.
  • Master the technique of stir-frying noodles and vegetables for optimal flavor and texture.
  • Understand the importance of properly preparing ingredients (e.g., soaking noodles, seasoning cabbage).

Ingredients

  • Half a head of cabbage (قطع الملفوف إلى نصفين)
  • Salt (الملح)
  • Noodles (الشعيرية)
  • Garlic (الثوم)
  • Ginger (الزنجبيل)
  • Green onions (البصل الأخضر)
  • White onions (البصل الأبيض)
  • Dried chili flakes (شرائح الفلفل الحار المجففة)
  • Thinly sliced pork belly (بطن لحم الخنزير المقشر)
  • Dark soy sauce (صلصة الصويا الداكنة)
  • Cooking oil (زيت الطهي)
  • Light soy sauce (صلصة الصويا الخفيفة)
  • Sugar (السكر)
  • Fresh matsutake mushrooms (الماتسوتاكي الطازج) (Optional)

Instructions

  1. Cut the cabbage in half, then into thin strips. If too long, cut into slightly thicker strips.
  2. Place cabbage in a bowl and add salt, then soak.
  3. Soak the noodles.
  4. Mince garlic and ginger. Chop green onions, white onions.
  5. Prepare dried chili flakes (wash and dry).
  6. Thinly slice pork belly and set aside.
  7. Once cabbage is softened and has released water, drain excess water and rinse to remove salt. Squeeze out excess water.
  8. Boil water, add noodles and cook for 1 minute until tender. Remove with a slotted spoon.
  9. Add cooked noodles to a larger bowl, add dark soy sauce and cooking oil to prevent sticking. Stir-fry until evenly colored. Set aside.
  10. Stir-fry pork belly until slightly curled and golden brown.
  11. Add minced ginger and garlic, white onions, and stir-fry until fragrant.
  12. Add dried chili flakes and stir-fry until fragrant.
  13. Increase heat, add cabbage and stir-fry until cooked.
  14. Add noodles, season with a pinch of salt, a little sugar, and optional fresh matsutake mushrooms.
  15. Stir-fry until well combined and fragrant.
  16. Add a teaspoon of light soy sauce.
  17. Sprinkle chopped green onions and stir-fry until fragrant.

lazy_breakfast_wontons.txt - Lazy Breakfast Wontons

Objectives

  • Create a nutritious and delicious breakfast wonton recipe.
  • Minimize cooking time and effort.
  • Showcase a visually appealing and easy-to-follow cooking method.

Ingredients

  • 1 fresh cucumber (去皮的黄瓜 - qù pí de huángguā)
  • ½ peeled carrot (半个去皮的胡萝卜 - bàn ge qù pí de húluóbo)
  • 3 grams table salt (3克食盐 - 3 kè shíyán)
  • Black fungus (木耳 - mù'ěr), blanched and shredded
  • Blanched bamboo shoots (焯水的竹笋 - chāo shuǐ de zhúsǔn), shredded
  • 3 eggs (3个鸡蛋 - 3 gè jīdàn)
  • Pinch of salt (少许盐 - shǎoxǔ yán)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòng yóu)
  • Spring onions (葱花 - cōnghuā), chopped
  • 1 teaspoon fluffy salt (一茶匙蓬松盐 - yī chá chí péng sōng yán)
  • Pepper (胡椒粉 - hújiāofěn)
  • Sesame oil (麻油 - máyóu)
  • Wonton wrappers (馄饨皮 - húntún pí)
  • Water (水 - shuǐ)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the cucumber: Cut off the ends, slice, then shred. Avoid cutting into the melon sac.
  2. Prepare the carrot: Peel and slice thinly.
  3. Combine cucumber and carrot shreds: Add 3 grams of salt, mix well, and set aside for 5 minutes to marinate and release water.
  4. Prepare the black fungus: Blanch, shred, and chop finely.
  5. Prepare the bamboo shoots: Blanch and chop finely.
  6. Prepare the spring onions: Chop finely.
  7. Prepare the egg filling: Whisk 3 eggs with a pinch of salt until well combined.
  8. Cook the eggs: Heat oil in a pan over low heat, add the egg mixture, and cook until set. Mash the cooked eggs and set aside to cool.
  9. Squeeze excess water: Squeeze out excess water from the marinated cucumber and carrot shreds.
  10. Chop the cucumber and carrot mixture: Chop the squeezed cucumber and carrot mixture into smaller pieces.
  11. Combine filling ingredients: Combine the chopped cucumber and carrot mixture, cooked eggs, black fungus, bamboo shoots, and spring onions in a bowl.
  12. Season the filling: Add 1 teaspoon of salt, pepper, and sesame oil. Mix well.
  13. Assemble the wontons: Place a wonton wrapper on a flat surface, brush with water, add filling, fold in half, and press gently to seal.
  14. Steam the wontons: Bring water to a boil, place wontons in a steamer basket, ensuring space between them, and steam for 5 minutes.
  15. Serve: Remove wontons from the steamer and serve immediately. Enjoy with milk or soy milk.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=DQmYlGEb8Go

lazy_steamed_rice.txt - 懒人焖饭

Objectives

  • Learn to make a one-pot rice dish with meat and vegetables.
  • Minimize cooking time and effort.
  • Create a nutritious and delicious meal.

Ingredients

  • Rice (amount depends on serving size)
  • Water (for washing and cooking rice)
  • Mushrooms (香菇 xiānggū), diced
  • Carrots (胡萝卜 húluóbo), diced
  • Corn (玉米 yùmǐ), kernels
  • String beans (甜豆 tiándòu), peeled
  • Pork belly (五花肉 wǔhuāròu), diced (about 10 RMB worth)
  • Rock sugar (冰糖 bīngtáng), a small amount
  • Ginger (姜 jiāng), 2 slices
  • Star anise (八角 bājiǎo), 1
  • Cinnamon (桂皮 guìpí), a small piece
  • Salt (食盐 shíyán), a small spoon
  • Pepper (胡椒粉 hújiāofěn), a pinch
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油 háoyóu), an appropriate amount
  • Soy sauce (生抽 shēngchōu), 1 spoon
  • Dark soy sauce (老抽 lǎochōu), a pinch
  • Eggs (鸡蛋 jīdàn), 3
  • Sesame seeds (芝麻 zhīma), for garnish

Instructions

  1. Wash rice thoroughly and soak in plenty of water for 30 minutes. Save the rice water for other uses.
  2. Prepare vegetables: dice mushrooms, carrots, and corn. Cut string beans into pieces.
  3. Dice pork belly and set aside.
  4. Heat oil in a pan, add pork belly and stir-fry until the skin is slightly crispy.
  5. Add rock sugar and stir-fry until melted and the pork is browned.
  6. Add ginger, star anise, and cinnamon; stir-fry until fragrant.
  7. Add all prepared vegetables and stir-fry evenly.
  8. Pour in enough water to cover the ingredients.
  9. Season with salt, pepper, oyster sauce, soy sauce, and dark soy sauce. Stir well.
  10. Bring to a boil, then transfer everything to a rice cooker.
  11. Add soaked rice and level it.
  12. Crack 3 eggs on top.
  13. Cook rice according to the rice cooker instructions.
  14. After cooking, let it sit for 10 minutes before opening the lid.
  15. Stir the rice, then serve in bowls. Press down firmly and invert onto plates for presentation.
  16. Garnish with sesame seeds.

lemon_hand_torn_chicken_legs.txt - Lemon Hand-Torn Chicken Legs with Three Flavors

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare flavorful and healthy steamed chicken legs.
  • Master three delicious ways to enjoy the cooked chicken: lemon-hand-torn, ginger-flavored, and in broth.
  • Utilize simple ingredients to create a nutritious and appealing meal.

Ingredients

  • 4-5 fresh chicken legs
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • Several red dates
  • A small piece of Astragalus root
  • 28 goji berries
  • 1/2 lemon, thinly sliced (seeds removed)
  • A small handful of cilantro, chopped
  • Several cloves garlic, minced
  • A small chili pepper, finely chopped
  • 2 tablespoons white sesame seeds
  • Hot oil
  • 1 tablespoon soy sauce
  • 1 tablespoon rice vinegar
  • 1 teaspoon sugar
  • A small piece of sand ginger, minced
  • A few slices of ginger
  • Peanuts (optional)

Instructions

  1. Wash chicken legs thoroughly with salt to remove impurities and sanitize. Rinse well with clean water.
  2. Trim excess fat from chicken legs.
  3. Pierce chicken legs with toothpicks to promote even cooking and nutrient release.
  4. Place red dates, astragalus, and goji berries in a bowl in the center of a larger serving dish.
  5. Arrange cleaned chicken legs around the bowl in the larger dish.
  6. Place a few slices of ginger on top of each chicken leg.
  7. Steam chicken legs in a steamer over high heat for 30 minutes.
  8. While steaming, prepare the sauces: 8.1 For the lemon sauce: Combine sliced lemon (seeds removed), chopped cilantro, minced garlic, chili, sesame seeds, and hot oil in a bowl. Add soy sauce, rice vinegar, and sugar; mix well. 8.2 For the sand ginger sauce: Mince sand ginger, add salt, and drizzle with hot oil.
  9. After steaming, remove chicken legs and let cool slightly.
  10. Remove the bowl from the center of the dish, revealing the flavorful broth. Season broth with salt.
  11. Remove chicken meat from bones and shred into bite-sized pieces.
  12. Divide shredded chicken into two portions.
  13. For the lemon hand-torn chicken: Mix one portion of shredded chicken with the lemon sauce, cilantro, and peanuts (if using).
  14. For the sand ginger chicken: Mix the other portion of shredded chicken with the sand ginger sauce.
  15. Serve the lemon hand-torn chicken and the sand ginger chicken separately, alongside the flavorful broth.

liangban_fuzhu.txt - 凉拌腐竹 (Liángbàn fǔzhú)

Objectives

  • Learn to quickly soak dried bean curd sheets.
  • Prepare a flavorful and versatile dressing.
  • Make a refreshing and healthy cold dish perfect for any occasion.
  • Understand the nutritional benefits of bean curd sheets.
  • Learn a simple yet impressive recipe suitable for beginners.

Ingredients

  • Dried bean curd sheets (腐竹 - fǔzhú)
  • Water (水 - shuǐ)
  • Salt (盐 - yán)
  • White vinegar (白醋 - bái cù)
  • Onion (洋葱 - yángcōng), small piece
  • Coriander (香菜 - xiāngcài), small bunch
  • Chili peppers (小米椒 - xiǎomǐ jiāo), several
  • Garlic (蒜 - suàn), several cloves
  • Hot oil (热油 - rè yóu)
  • Sugar (白糖 - bái táng)
  • Soy sauce (生抽 - shēng chōu)
  • Rice vinegar (陈醋 - chén cù)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油 - háo yóu)
  • Roasted peanuts (花生米 - huāshēng mǐ), optional

Instructions

  1. Rinse dried bean curd sheets under running water to remove dust and impurities.
  2. In a bowl, combine bean curd sheets with a spoonful of salt, a little white vinegar, and enough 40°C warm water to cover them completely.
  3. Cover the bowl and let the bean curd sheets soak for about 30 minutes.
  4. After 30 minutes, rinse the softened bean curd sheets under running water twice.
  5. Drain the bean curd sheets and set aside.
  6. Finely slice the onion and chop the coriander into segments. Set aside.
  7. Finely slice and then mince the chili peppers and garlic. Set aside.
  8. In a small bowl, combine minced chili peppers and garlic. Add a spoonful of hot oil to enhance the aroma.
  9. Add a spoonful of salt, sugar, soy sauce, rice vinegar, and oyster sauce to the chili-garlic mixture. Stir well to combine. This is the dressing.
  10. Bring a pot of water to a simmer (70% heat).
  11. Blanch the soaked bean curd sheets in the simmering water for 2 minutes to remove any beany smell.
  12. Remove the bean curd sheets, drain well, and place them in a large bowl.
  13. Add the sliced onion and chopped coriander to the bowl.
  14. Pour the prepared dressing over the bean curd sheets.
  15. Add the roasted peanuts (if using).
  16. Gently toss everything together until well combined. Make sure the bean curd sheets are evenly coated with the dressing.
  17. Serve and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=azs4VFY6pZ8

liangban_huanggua.txt - 凉拌黄瓜 (Liangban Huanggua)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple and refreshing cold cucumber salad.
  • Master the technique of preparing cucumbers for optimal texture and flavor.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients to create a flavorful side dish.

Ingredients

  • Several cucumbers (黄瓜 - huángguā)
  • 1 tablespoon salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • 2 tablespoons white sugar (白糖 - báitáng)
  • Several cloves garlic (蒜子 - suànzi)
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒 - xiǎomǐjiāo) or large red peppers (大红椒 - dà hóngjiāo)
  • 1/4 cup leftover peanuts (花生米 - huāshēngmǐ)
  • 1 tablespoon soy sauce (生抽 - shēngchōu)
  • 1 tablespoon rice vinegar (陈醋 - chéncù)

Instructions

  1. Wash cucumbers thoroughly with salt water to remove pesticide residue. Rinse twice with clean water.
  2. Remove the ends of the cucumbers and cut them in half lengthwise if long.
  3. Make shallow cuts along the sides of the cucumbers, then gently pat them to create even slices.
  4. Cut the cucumbers into small pieces.
  5. Place the cucumbers in a bowl, add salt and white sugar, and mix well. Let it marinate for 30 minutes.
  6. While marinating, prepare the garlic and chili peppers. Mince the garlic and finely slice the chili peppers.
  7. After 30 minutes, drain the excess water from the cucumbers.
  8. Add the peanuts, garlic, chili peppers, white sugar, soy sauce, and rice vinegar to the cucumbers.
  9. Mix thoroughly with gloves until well combined.
  10. Serve immediately or marinate for another 30 minutes for enhanced flavor.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=mPB27kXOE8Y

liangban_jiucai.txt - 凉拌韭菜

Objectives

  • Learn a new way to prepare chives beyond stir-frying or dumplings.
  • Create a delicious and visually appealing chive dish for guests.
  • Make a flavorful cold chive dish that is easy to prepare.

Ingredients

  • 2 eggs
  • 20g water
  • 2 tbsp potato starch or cornstarch
  • A dash of pepper
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒)
  • Several cloves of garlic
  • 1 tsp salt
  • 1 tsp 松茸鲜 (matsutake mushroom seasoning)
  • 1/2 tsp light soy sauce (生抽)
  • 1/2 tsp rice vinegar (香醋)
  • A little sesame oil (小磨香油)
  • A bunch of tender chives (韭菜)

Instructions

  1. Wash chives thoroughly until water runs clear. Drain and set aside.
  2. Cut off the root ends of the chives and chop into 5cm segments. Place in a large bowl.
  3. In a separate bowl, mix potato or cornstarch with water until smooth.
  4. Add eggs and pepper to the starch mixture. Stir until well combined.
  5. Finely chop chili peppers and garlic. Crush the chili peppers slightly.
  6. Prepare the sauce: Combine salt, 松茸鲜, light soy sauce, rice vinegar, and sesame oil in a small bowl. Mix well.
  7. Heat a small amount of oil in a pan. Pour in the egg mixture and cook until set, then flip and cook the other side.
  8. Cut the cooked egg into thin strips and set aside.
  9. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add chives and blanch for 18 seconds.
  10. Immediately remove chives and plunge into ice water. Drain well, squeezing out excess water.
  11. Combine blanched chives, egg strips, and prepared sauce in a large bowl. Toss gently to coat.
  12. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=xPs8ydUTk-U

liangban_pidan_huanggua.txt - 凉拌皮蛋黄瓜 (Liangban Pidan Huanggua)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a refreshing and visually appealing Liangban Pidan Huanggua (涼拌皮蛋黃瓜).
  • Master a simple yet flavorful dressing for this dish.
  • Understand the preparation steps for both the crystal eggs and cucumbers.

Ingredients

  • 8 无铅水晶皮蛋 (Wú qiān shuǐjīng pí dàn) - Lead-free crystal preserved eggs
  • 1 条黄瓜 (Tiáo huánggua) - Cucumber
  • 姜 (Jiāng) - Ginger (amount unspecified)
  • 蒜 (Suàn) - Garlic (amount unspecified)
  • Several 小米椒 (Xiǎo mǐjiāo) - Small chili peppers
  • 2 根小葱 (Gēn xiǎocōng) - Scallions
  • 1 spoonful 白芝麻 (Bái zhīma) - White sesame seeds
  • 1 spoonful 生抽 (Shēngchōu) - Light soy sauce
  • 少许陈醋 (Shǎoxǔ Chéncù) - A little bit of black vinegar
  • 少许食盐 (Shǎoxǔ shíyán) - A little bit of salt
  • 少许松茸鲜 (Shǎoxǔ sōngrōng xiān) - A little bit of Matsutake mushroom seasoning (or similar)
  • 油泼辣子 (Yóu pō làzi) - Chili oil

Instructions

  1. Peel the crystal preserved eggs and cut them into small pieces.
  2. Arrange the cut preserved egg pieces around the edge of a bowl.
  3. Peel the cucumber, leaving some skin on for aesthetics. Lightly score the cucumber lengthwise to prevent splattering when slicing.
  4. Cut the cucumber into slices and place them in the center of the bowl, on top of the preserved eggs.
  5. Mince the ginger and garlic.
  6. Finely slice the chili peppers.
  7. Chop the scallions into small pieces.
  8. Combine the minced ginger, garlic, chili peppers, and chopped scallions in a bowl.
  9. Add a spoonful of white sesame seeds to the bowl.
  10. Heat oil and pour it over the ginger, garlic, chili, and scallion mixture to enhance the aroma.
  11. In a separate bowl, prepare the dressing by combining a spoonful of light soy sauce, a little black vinegar, a little salt, a little Matsutake mushroom seasoning (or similar), and some chili oil.
  12. Mix the dressing well.
  13. Pour the dressing over the cucumbers and preserved eggs in the bowl.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=0hU781C7sVw

liangban_xingbaogu.txt - 凉拌杏鲍菇 (Liangban Xingbaogu)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and healthy cold dish suitable for summer.
  • Understand the nutritional benefits of king oyster mushrooms.
  • Master a simple and quick cooking method for a flavorful side dish.

Ingredients

  • Several king oyster mushrooms (杏鲍菇 - xìngbàogū)
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒 - xiǎomǐjiāo)
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜 - suàn)
  • Some scallions (大葱 - dàcōng)
  • Several sprigs of cilantro (香菜 - xiāngcài)
  • 1 small spoonful of white sugar (白糖 - báitáng)
  • 1 large spoonful of white sesame seeds (白芝麻 - báizhīma)
  • 1 spoonful of finely ground chili powder (细辣椒面 - xì làjiāomiàn)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòngyóu)
  • 1 small spoonful of salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • A pinch of white sugar (白糖 - báitáng)
  • A little bit of Songrong fresh (松茸鲜 - sōngróngxiān)
  • Some oyster sauce (蚝油 - háoyóu)
  • 1 spoonful of soy sauce (生抽 - shēngchōu)
  • Some rice vinegar (陈醋 - chéncù)
  • 2 spoonfuls of roasted peanuts (炒好的花生米 - chǎo hǎo de huāshēngmǐ)

Instructions

  1. Clean the king oyster mushrooms thoroughly with water to remove dust and impurities.
  2. Cut off both ends of the mushrooms and slice them into 0.5mm thick pieces. Set aside.
  3. Finely chop the chili peppers, garlic, and scallions. Chop the cilantro into small segments. Combine these in a small bowl.
  4. Bring plenty of water to a boil in a pot. Add two crushed garlic cloves and the sliced king oyster mushrooms. Boil for 5 minutes.
  5. Add a small spoonful of sugar to remove any off-flavors from the mushrooms.
  6. Remove the mushrooms with a strainer and rinse them under cold water to cool them down.
  7. Squeeze out excess water from the mushrooms and tear them into small strips.
  8. Add the chopped chili peppers, garlic, scallions, and cilantro to the bowl with the mushrooms.
  9. Add the white sesame seeds and chili powder to the bowl.
  10. Heat cooking oil in a pan until it slightly smokes. Pour the hot oil over the ingredients to enhance their aroma.
  11. Season with salt, a pinch of sugar, a little Songrong fresh, oyster sauce, soy sauce, and rice vinegar.
  12. Add the roasted peanuts and mix thoroughly with chopsticks until the mushrooms and seasonings are well combined.
  13. Serve and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=MY-VoTt1yTI

loofah_egg_soup.txt - Loofah and Egg Soup

Objectives

  • Learn to make a flavorful and healthy loofah soup.
  • Master the technique of preparing loofah to maintain its color.
  • Create a delicious soup with a balanced combination of ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 1 loofah
  • 1 package seafood mushrooms
  • 1 ham sausage
  • 1 tomato
  • 1/2 onion
  • Ginger
  • Garlic
  • Green onions
  • 3 eggs
  • 2 drops white vinegar
  • Oil
  • Salt
  • Goji berries (optional)
  • Boiling water

Instructions

  1. Prepare the loofah: Peel, rinse, and cut into bite-sized pieces. Place in water with a pinch of salt to maintain color.
  2. Prepare the seafood mushrooms: Clean and cut into small pieces.
  3. Prepare the ham sausage: Remove the wrapping and slice thinly.
  4. Prepare the tomato: Scrape the skin off with a spoon.
  5. Prepare aromatics: Finely chop onion, ginger, garlic, and separate green onion whites and greens.
  6. Prepare the eggs: Whisk 3 eggs with 2 drops of white vinegar until light and frothy.
  7. Fry the eggs: Heat oil in a pan, add egg mixture, and fry until golden brown on both sides. Set aside and chop into diamond shapes.
  8. Sauté aromatics: Add onion, ginger, and garlic to the pan and sauté until fragrant.
  9. Add tomato and salt: Add the tomato and salt, cooking until softened.
  10. Add loofah and stir-fry: Add the loofah and stir-fry until slightly softened.
  11. Add seafood mushrooms: Add the seafood mushrooms and stir-fry for 15 seconds.
  12. Add boiling water: Pour in boiling water to create the soup base.
  13. Add remaining ingredients: Add the fried egg, ham sausage, and stir to combine.
  14. Simmer: Bring to a boil, then simmer for 30 seconds, seasoning with salt to taste.
  15. Garnish and serve: Garnish with goji berries (optional) and serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=M5qH8rMW5rU

loofah_egg_stir_fry.txt - لوبيا بيض مقلي

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare loofah to prevent discoloration.
  • Master a quick and flavorful loofah and egg stir-fry.
  • Understand the importance of proper cooking techniques for maintaining the vibrant green color of the loofah.

Ingredients

  • 2 fresh loofahs
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • 2-3 eggs
  • Pinch of salt
  • 2 drops white vinegar
  • 1/2 large red pepper, deseeded and cut into diamond shapes
  • 1 green pepper, cut into diamond shapes
  • A few stalks of scallions (white parts only), chopped
  • Several cloves garlic, minced
  • 1 package of white jade mushroom
  • Chicken bouillon
  • A little sugar
  • 2 teaspoons cornstarch
  • Water
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Loofah: Use the back of a knife to peel the loofah thinly, maintaining its vibrant green color. Clean and trim the ends. Cut into bite-sized pieces (slightly larger than desired, as it shrinks during cooking). Soak in water with 1 teaspoon of salt for 10 minutes to prevent oxidation and browning.
  2. Prepare the Vegetables and Mushrooms: Cut the red and green peppers into diamond shapes. Chop the scallions (white parts only) and mince the garlic. Cut the white jade mushroom in half and then slice. Rinse and set aside.
  3. Prepare the Egg Mixture: Crack 2-3 eggs into a bowl. Add a pinch of salt and 2 drops of white vinegar. Whisk thoroughly until light and frothy with no lumps.
  4. Prepare the Sauce: In a separate bowl, combine chicken bouillon, a little sugar, 2 teaspoons cornstarch, and water. Mix well.
  5. Blanch the Loofah: Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add the loofah and blanch for 30 seconds. Remove with a strainer to drain excess water.
  6. Blanch the Mushrooms: Blanch the white jade mushrooms for 15 seconds, then remove with a slotted spoon to drain.
  7. Stir-fry the Aromatics: Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan. Add the chopped scallions and minced garlic and stir-fry until fragrant over low heat.
  8. Stir-fry the Loofah: Add the blanched loofah to the wok and stir-fry for 1 minute until tender.
  9. Add the Remaining Ingredients: Add the blanched mushrooms, then the egg mixture, followed by the red and green peppers. Stir-fry for 15 seconds.
  10. Thicken the Sauce: Pour the prepared sauce into the wok and stir constantly until thickened.
  11. Finish and Serve: Add a drizzle of oil before serving to enhance the appearance. Stir well. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ROEPTSveP3w

lotus_egg_cake.txt - 莲藕鸡蛋饼

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious lotus root and egg cake.
  • Master the techniques for preparing lotus root, meat, and vegetables.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to enhance the cake's taste.

Ingredients

  • 1 lotus root (choose one with closed ends)
  • 1 carrot
  • 3 RMB worth of lean pork
  • 1 tomato
  • 1 piece of ginger
  • Several scallions (separate white and green parts)
  • Several cloves of garlic
  • Appropriate amount of tomato sauce
  • Salt
  • Sugar
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce
  • Rice vinegar
  • Corn starch
  • Water
  • 4 eggs
  • 50g all-purpose flour
  • 50g corn starch
  • Cooking oil
  • Pepper

Instructions

  1. Prepare the lotus root: Remove both ends, peel, and cut into thin slices, then into shreds, and finally into small dices. Soak in water with a little white vinegar to prevent browning.
  2. Prepare the carrot: Peel, cut into thin slices, then shreds, and finally into small dices. Set aside.
  3. Prepare the pork: Cut into slices, then mince. Set aside.
  4. Prepare the tomato: Cut in half, remove the core, cut into large pieces, then small dices. Set aside.
  5. Prepare the ginger and garlic: Mince ginger and garlic. Set aside.
  6. Prepare the scallions: Separate white and green parts. Mince the white parts and chop the green parts into small pieces. Set aside.
  7. Make the sauce: In a bowl, mix tomato sauce, salt, sugar, soy sauce, rice vinegar, cornstarch, and a little water until smooth. Set aside.
  8. Drain the lotus root and mix with carrot dices.
  9. In a bowl, whisk 4 eggs with salt and pepper.
  10. Add the lotus root and carrot mixture to the eggs.
  11. Add 50g of all-purpose flour and 50g of cornstarch to the egg mixture. Stir until a thick batter forms.
  12. Heat a pan with oil. Pour the batter into the pan and spread evenly. Cover and cook over low heat for 3 minutes.
  13. Flip the cake and cook for another 3 minutes, until golden brown on both sides. Remove from pan.
  14. Add oil to the pan. Add the minced pork and stir-fry until browned.
  15. Add the minced ginger and garlic, and diced tomatoes. Stir-fry until the tomatoes release their juices.
  16. Pour in the prepared sauce and bring to a boil, cooking until thickened.
  17. Pour the sauce over the lotus root and egg cake.
  18. Garnish with chopped scallions.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=zqVGxn_pwbo

lotus_root_balls.txt - كرات جذر اللوتس

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare lotus root for cooking.
  • Master the art of making flavorful lotus root balls.
  • Create a delicious and nutritious sauce to complement the lotus root balls.

Ingredients

  • Lotus Root: 1 large lotus root
  • Pork: 2 parts lean pork, 8 parts fatty pork
  • Carrots: 1 large carrot
  • Shiitake Mushrooms: 2
  • Ginger: 1 piece
  • Green Onions: 1 bunch
  • Salt: 1 tsp + to taste
  • Pepper: to taste
  • Mushroom Powder: to taste
  • Light Soy Sauce: to taste
  • Flour: 1 tbsp (15g)
  • Cornstarch: 1 tbsp (15g)
  • Sugar: to taste
  • Oyster Sauce: to taste
  • Cooking Oil: a little
  • White Vinegar: a little
  • Water: enough to cover lotus root

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Lotus Root: Peel and cut the lotus root into thin slices, then into smaller pieces. Soak in water with white vinegar to prevent oxidation.
  2. Prepare the Pork: Cut lean and fatty pork into thin slices, then mince finely with a knife (or use a meat grinder).
  3. Prepare the Vegetables: Peel and slice carrots thickly. Cut remaining carrots into small pieces. Wash and chop shiitake mushrooms into small cubes. Peel and mince ginger finely. Chop white and green parts of green onions separately.
  4. Prepare the Pork Filling: Combine minced pork, minced green onions (white part), salt, pepper, mushroom powder, light soy sauce, and minced ginger. Mix well.
  5. Combine Lotus Root and Pork: Mix the prepared lotus root and pork filling thoroughly. Add flour and cornstarch, mixing until well combined.
  6. Shape the Balls: Form the mixture into small balls, about the size of ping pong balls.
  7. Steam the Balls: Steam the lotus root balls for 12 minutes over high heat.
  8. Prepare the Sauce: Heat oil in a pan. Sauté minced ginger and green onions (white part). Add sliced carrots, shiitake mushrooms, and stir-fry until tender.
  9. Finish the Sauce: Add water, salt, sugar, pepper, soy sauce, oyster sauce, and a light broth. Simmer until the sauce thickens.
  10. Combine and Serve: Once the lotus root balls are steamed, pour the prepared sauce over them. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=k_b5VPdyS88

lotus_root_meat_roll.txt - Lotus Root Meat Rolls

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious lotus root meat rolls without using yeast or rolling dough.
  • Master a simple recipe suitable for beginners.
  • Learn how to prepare the lotus root and meat filling.
  • Achieve a crispy exterior and tender interior texture.
  • Learn efficient time-saving techniques.

Ingredients

  • Dried shiitake mushrooms (soaked and chopped)
  • 1 carrot (peeled and diced)
  • Ground pork (or minced pork)
  • Ginger (minced)
  • Garlic (minced)
  • 1 small bunch of scallions (chopped)
  • 1 tbsp salt
  • 1 tbsp Song Rong Xian (mushroom seasoning - substitute with your preferred seasoning)
  • A pinch of pepper
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce
  • Appropriate amount of oyster sauce
  • 1 tbsp cornstarch
  • 1 tbsp water
  • 1 lotus root (peeled and diced)
  • Wonton wrappers
  • 3 eggs
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Soak dried shiitake mushrooms, squeeze out excess water, chop finely, and set aside.
  2. Peel and dice the carrot into small pieces.
  3. Mince the pork (or use a food processor).
  4. Mince the ginger and garlic.
  5. Chop the scallions.
  6. In a bowl, combine the minced pork, minced ginger, minced garlic, chopped scallions, salt, Song Rong Xian, pepper, soy sauce, oyster sauce, cornstarch, and water. Mix well until the meat is sticky.
  7. Peel and dice the lotus root. Squeeze out excess water.
  8. Combine the diced lotus root, minced meat mixture, and diced carrots in a bowl. Mix well.
  9. Prepare wonton wrappers.
  10. Take a wonton wrapper, brush the edges with water, add a spoonful of the filling, wrap it into a roll, and seal. Repeat with remaining filling.
  11. Beat 3 eggs until light and fluffy.
  12. Dip each lotus root roll into the egg mixture.
  13. Heat cooking oil in a pan over medium heat.
  14. Carefully place the egg-coated lotus root rolls into the hot oil.
  15. Fry over low heat until golden brown and crispy, flipping frequently to ensure even cooking.
  16. Increase heat to high for the last 30 seconds to crisp the exterior and reduce oil absorption.
  17. Remove the lotus root rolls from the oil using a slotted spoon, allowing excess oil to drain.
  18. Serve immediately and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=-oyViwOEcEs

lotus_root_stir_fry.txt - مقلية جذور اللوتس النباتية

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare crispy fried lotus root.
  • Master the technique of cutting lotus root into thin strips.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to complement the lotus root.

Ingredients

  • 4 sections of fresh lotus root
  • 1 piece of ginger
  • Green and red chili peppers
  • 1 handful of scallions (white parts only)
  • Salt
  • Soy sauce
  • Sugar
  • Oyster sauce
  • Balsamic vinegar
  • Cooked soy sauce
  • Oil for frying

Instructions

  1. Peel the lotus root, removing a thin layer of skin. Wash thoroughly.
  2. Cut the lotus root into thin slices, then into fine strands. Alternatively, use a grater to shred the lotus root.
  3. Wash the shredded lotus root again and drain well.
  4. Prepare the seasonings: Peel and thinly slice the ginger. Remove seeds from the chili peppers and slice thinly. Cut the scallion whites into 3cm pieces.
  5. Make the sauce: Combine salt, soy sauce, sugar, oyster sauce, balsamic vinegar, and cooked soy sauce in a bowl. Mix well.
  6. Heat oil in a wok or pan. Add the ginger and dried chili peppers and stir-fry briefly until fragrant. Remove from pan.
  7. Add the shredded lotus root to the hot oil and stir-fry over high heat for 1 minute until tender.
  8. Add the sliced green and red chili peppers and the prepared sauce. Continue stir-frying until the lotus root is coated and colored.
  9. Add the sliced scallions and stir-fry a few more times to combine.
  10. Serve immediately.

lvy_potatoes.txt - Pan-Fried Perch with Potatoes

Objectives

  • Learn to make a flavorful pan-fried perch with potatoes.
  • Master a simple yet delicious recipe suitable for family dinners.
  • Acquire skills in preparing and cooking perch to maintain its tenderness.

Ingredients

  • 1 fresh perch (cleaned and scaled)
  • 1 potato
  • Salt
  • Cornstarch
  • Cooking oil
  • 1 small bunch of scallions (chopped)
  • 1 piece of ginger (minced)
  • Several cloves of garlic (minced)
  • Several small chili peppers (finely sliced)
  • 1 tbsp yellow bean sauce
  • 1 bowl of purified water
  • 松茸鲜 (Songrong Xian - Matsutake flavoring)
  • Pepper
  • Soy sauce (生抽 - shēng zhōu)
  • A little dark soy sauce (老抽 - lǎo zhōu) for coloring
  • Water starch (for thickening)
  • Sesame oil (小磨香油 - xiǎo mó xiāng yóu)

Instructions

  1. Clean the perch, remove fins, and score both sides.
  2. Apply salt evenly to the perch (inside and out), and marinate for 10 minutes.
  3. Peel and dice the potato. Soak in water to prevent oxidation.
  4. Prepare the scallions, ginger, garlic, and chili peppers.
  5. Coat the marinated perch with cornstarch.
  6. Pan-fry the perch over medium-low heat until golden brown on both sides. Set aside.
  7. Pan-fry the potato cubes until golden brown. Set aside.
  8. In the same pan, stir-fry the scallions, ginger, and garlic until fragrant.
  9. Add yellow bean sauce and stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Add purified water, bring to a boil.
  11. Season with Songrong Xian, pepper, soy sauce, and a little dark soy sauce.
  12. Add the pan-fried perch, cover, and simmer for 2 minutes.
  13. Continuously spoon the sauce over the perch to ensure even flavor.
  14. Transfer the perch to a bowl.
  15. Thicken the remaining sauce with water starch.
  16. Add sesame oil to the sauce.
  17. Add the pan-fried potatoes to the bowl with the perch.
  18. Pour the thickened sauce over the perch and potatoes.
  19. Garnish with chopped scallions.

meat_and_beans.txt - 肉末豆角

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy meat and green bean dish.
  • Understand the importance of blanching green beans to maintain color and prevent poisoning.
  • Master a simple technique for flavorful stir-fried meat and vegetables.

Ingredients

  • 1 handful of fresh green beans (豇豆)
  • 2 teaspoons of salt (食盐)
  • Water (山泉水)
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜籽)
  • 1 piece of ginger (生姜)
  • Several red chilies (红椒)
  • 1 piece of five-spice pork belly (五花肉)
  • 1 teaspoon of edible salt (食用盐)
  • A little edible oil (食用油)
  • 1 tablespoon of soybean paste (黄豆酱)
  • 1 teaspoon of salt (毛毛盐)
  • A little sugar (白糖)
  • A little oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • A little light soy sauce (生抽)

Instructions

  1. Trim the ends of the green beans and cut them into 2cm segments.
  2. Place the green beans in a bowl, add 2 teaspoons of salt and water, and soak for 5 minutes.
  3. Mince the garlic and ginger finely. Slice the red chilies into thin rings.
  4. Cut the pork belly into slices, then mince it finely.
  5. Rinse the soaked green beans and drain.
  6. Bring a pot of water to a boil, add a teaspoon of salt and a little oil. Add the green beans and blanch for 3 minutes.
  7. Remove the green beans and rinse with cold water to maintain their color and crispness. Drain.
  8. Heat a wok or pan over medium-high heat. Add the minced pork and stir-fry until browned and the fat is rendered.
  9. Add the soybean paste and stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Add the minced garlic, ginger, and chili rings; stir-fry until fragrant.
  11. Add the blanched green beans and stir-fry until the moisture evaporates.
  12. Season with salt, sugar, oyster sauce, and light soy sauce. Stir-fry until well combined and heated through.
  13. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=fBKsAHooPJY

meat_and_string_beans.txt - 肉末豆角

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy home-style meat and string bean dish.
  • Master the technique of stir-frying string beans to maintain their crispness and color.
  • Understand the importance of properly preparing ingredients for optimal flavor.

Ingredients

  • 1 handful fresh string beans (豇豆)
  • 2 tsp salt (盐)
  • Water (山泉水)
  • Several cloves garlic (蒜籽)
  • 1 piece ginger (生姜)
  • Several red chilies (红椒)
  • 1 piece five-spice pork belly (五花肉)
  • 1 tsp edible salt (食用盐)
  • A little edible oil (食用油)
  • 1 tbsp yellow soybean paste (黄豆酱)
  • 1 tsp prickly ash (花椒)
  • A little sugar (白糖)
  • A little oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • A little light soy sauce (生抽)

Instructions

  1. Trim the ends off the string beans and cut them into 2cm segments.
  2. Place the string beans in a bowl, add 2 tsp salt and water, and soak for 5 minutes.
  3. Mince the garlic cloves finely.
  4. Mince the ginger and red chilies.
  5. Cut the pork belly into slices and then mince it.
  6. Rinse the soaked string beans and drain well.
  7. Bring a pot of water to a boil, add 1 tsp salt and a little oil.
  8. Add the string beans and blanch for 3 minutes.
  9. Remove the string beans and immediately rinse with cold water to maintain color and crispness. Drain well.
  10. Heat a wok or pan over medium-high heat. No oil needed.
  11. Add the minced pork and stir-fry until browned and fragrant, rendering out excess fat.
  12. Add 1 tbsp yellow soybean paste and stir-fry until fragrant.
  13. Add the minced garlic, ginger, and chilies; stir-fry until fragrant.
  14. Add the blanched string beans and stir-fry until slightly softened.
  15. Season with 1 tsp salt, a pinch of sugar, a little oyster sauce, and a little light soy sauce.
  16. Stir-fry until the flavors are well combined and the dish is fragrant.
  17. Serve hot.

meat_eggplant.txt - 肉末茄子 (Ròumò Qiézi)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and tender braised eggplant dish with minced meat.
  • Master the technique of frying eggplant to achieve a non-oily texture.
  • Utilize simple seasonings to highlight the natural flavors of the ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 1 large eggplant (approximately 500g)
  • 50g 瘦肉 (shòuròu) - lean pork
  • 2 cloves garlic (大蒜, dàsuàn)
  • 7-8g小米椒 (xiǎomǐjiāo) - small chili peppers
  • 1 small bunch of scallions (小葱, xiǎocōng), separated into white and green parts
  • Salt (食盐, shíyán)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油, háoyóu)
  • Cooking oil (食用油, shíyòngyóu)
  • Water (开水, kāishuǐ)

Instructions

  1. Wash the eggplant thoroughly, scrubbing its skin with salt to remove any dirt. Do not peel the eggplant.
  2. Cut off the stem and bottom of the eggplant. Cut into 5-6cm sections, then into thick slices, and finally into strips. Set aside in a bowl.
  3. Mince the garlic and finely chop the chili peppers and scallions. Separate the white and green parts of the scallions. Set aside.
  4. Mince the pork into fine pieces.
  5. Heat a wok or pan with a generous amount of cooking oil over medium-high heat until slightly smoking.
  6. Add the eggplant strips and fry until golden brown and slightly softened. Remove with a slotted spoon and drain excess oil thoroughly.
  7. Add the minced pork to the wok and stir-fry until browned.
  8. Add the minced garlic, scallion whites, and chili peppers to the wok and stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Add oyster sauce and stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Add about half a bowl of boiling water, 1.5 teaspoons of salt, and the fried eggplant.
  11. Stir well to combine and simmer until the eggplant is tender and the sauce has thickened slightly.
  12. Garnish with chopped scallion greens before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=pPsCeQdfEO4

meat_tofu_egg_steam.txt - 肉末豆腐蒸鸡蛋 (Meat and Tofu Steamed Egg)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious steamed egg dish with meat and tofu.
  • Master simple yet effective techniques for preparing the ingredients.
  • Create a flavorful and visually appealing dish suitable for children and adults.

Ingredients

  • 1 block of silken tofu (内酯豆腐 - nèizhǐ dòufu)
  • 1 tomato (西红柿 - xīhóngshì)
  • Some scallions (小葱 - xiǎocōng)
  • 3 eggs (鸡蛋 - jīdàn)
  • Pepper (胡椒粉 - hújiāofěn)
  • Salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • Small piece of beef (牛肉 - niúròu)
  • 1 tbsp soybean paste (黄豆酱 - huángdòujiàng)
  • Water starch (水淀粉 - shuǐdiànfěn)
  • Ginger (生姜 - shēngjiāng)
  • Garlic (蒜 - suàn)

Instructions

  1. Cut the silken tofu into small cubes.
  2. Cut the tomato in half, remove the core, and dice it.
  3. Chop the scallions into small pieces.
  4. Mix half of the chopped scallions with the tofu and tomato in a bowl.
  5. Whisk 3 eggs in a separate bowl until the yolks and whites are well combined.
  6. Add the whisked eggs to the bowl with the tofu and tomato.
  7. Season with pepper and salt, then gently mix everything together.
  8. Steam the mixture in a steamer over high heat for 10 minutes.
  9. While steaming, prepare the beef filling: dice and mince the beef.
  10. Chop the remaining scallions, ginger, and garlic.
  11. Heat oil in a pan, sauté the ginger, garlic, and scallions until fragrant.
  12. Add the minced beef and stir-fry until it changes color.
  13. Add soybean paste and stir-fry until fragrant.
  14. Thicken the sauce with water starch.
  15. Once the steamed egg mixture is cooked, remove it from the steamer.
  16. Top the steamed egg with the beef sauce and sprinkle with the remaining scallions.

minced_pork_wonton.txt - Minced Pork Wonton

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and tender minced pork wonton filling.
  • Master two simple wonton wrapping techniques.
  • Prepare a flavorful and aromatic wonton soup base.

Ingredients

  • 200g lean pork (shoulder or tenderloin)
  • 50g fatty pork
  • Several scallions
  • Ginger
  • Several scallions and cilantro (for garnish)
  • 1 tsp salt
  • 1 tbsp MSG (松茸鲜)
  • A pinch of pepper
  • 1 tbsp oyster sauce
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽)
  • 1 egg
  • Wonton wrappers (square, thin)
  • For the soup: salt, MSG (松茸鲜), pepper, lettuce (optional), shrimp skin (optional), scallions, cilantro, seaweed (紫菜), soy sauce (生抽), rice vinegar (陈醋), lard (猪油), boiling water

Instructions

  1. Dice lean and fatty pork into thick slices, then mince finely (or use a meat grinder).
  2. Mince scallions and ginger. Mix with warm water to extract their juices. Set aside.
  3. Mince scallions and cilantro for garnish. Set aside.
  4. In a large bowl, combine minced pork, salt, MSG, pepper, oyster sauce, and soy sauce.
  5. Wear disposable gloves and mix thoroughly until slightly sticky.
  6. Add the scallion-ginger water and mix well.
  7. Continue mixing until the meat is well combined and slightly elastic.
  8. Add a whole egg and mix for about 1 minute until fully incorporated.
  9. Add minced scallions and cilantro for garnish and mix gently. Set aside.
  10. Prepare wonton wrappers.
  11. Method 1 (Simple): Place a spoonful of filling in the center of a wrapper. Brush the corners with water, fold into a half-moon shape, and pinch to seal.
  12. Method 2 (Quick): Place a spoonful of filling in the center of a wrapper. Use chopsticks to lift the wrapper, gently pinching the edges with your left hand to form a wonton.
  13. Arrange finished wontons on a plate.
  14. Prepare the soup base: In a large bowl, combine salt, MSG, pepper, lettuce (optional), shrimp skin (optional), minced scallions and cilantro, seaweed, soy sauce, rice vinegar, and lard. Add boiling water and stir well.
  15. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add wontons and cook for 10-15 seconds without stirring. Gently stir to prevent sticking.
  16. Continue cooking for about 3 minutes, or until wontons float to the surface.
  17. Remove wontons and place them in soup bowls. Pour the prepared soup base over the wontons.
  18. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=wcinRGWYvTk

money_egg.txt - Money Egg and Braised Egg

Objectives

  • Learn two simple and delicious egg recipes.
  • Master the technique for cutting eggs into perfect circles.
  • Learn how to braise eggs for maximum flavor and visual appeal.
  • Understand how to prepare eggs for easy peeling.
  • Learn how to make a flavorful sauce for the money eggs.

Ingredients

  • Fresh eggs (quantity depends on household size)
  • Salt
  • Water
  • Cooking oil
  • Ginger
  • Garlic
  • Chili peppers (小米椒)
  • Dried chili flakes (optional)
  • Garlic chives (蒜苗)
  • Soy sauce (生抽)
  • Star anise (八角)
  • Cassia bark (桂皮)
  • Bay leaves (香叶)
  • Sichuan peppercorns (花椒)
  • Dried chilies (干海椒)

Instructions

Money Egg (金钱蛋)

  1. Prepare fresh eggs: Gently shake the eggs to ensure freshness (no rattling sound).
  2. Add salt and water to a bowl with eggs, let it sit for 10 minutes. This helps remove impurities.
  3. Rinse the eggs thoroughly under running water.
  4. Boil the eggs in a pot of water until cooked (6-8 minutes after boiling).
  5. Immediately transfer the boiled eggs to cold water for easy peeling.
  6. Peel the eggs carefully.
  7. Use a thread to slice the eggs into 1cm thick circles. This prevents the yolk from breaking and makes slicing faster.
  8. Heat cooking oil in a pan until it slightly smokes.
  9. Fry the egg slices in the hot oil over high heat until golden brown on both sides (about 1 minute per side).
  10. Remove the fried eggs and set aside; reserve the fragrant oil.
  11. Sauté ginger, garlic, and chili peppers in the reserved oil until fragrant.
  12. Add the fried egg slices, salt, soy sauce, and optional dried chili flakes. Stir-fry until well combined.
  13. Add garlic chives and stir-fry until wilted.
  14. Serve immediately.

Braised Eggs (卤蛋)

  1. Score the peeled, boiled eggs with shallow vertical cuts.
  2. Place the eggs in a bowl.
  3. Add star anise, cassia bark, bay leaves, Sichuan peppercorns, dried chilies, ginger slices, garlic slices, salt, sugar, and soy sauce to the bowl.
  4. Add enough water to cover the eggs.
  5. Bring the mixture to a boil, then reduce heat and simmer for 30 minutes, allowing the eggs to fully absorb the flavors.
  6. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=rzGVjIiZKk0

mushroom_egg_stir_fry.txt - Mushroom and Egg Stir-Fry

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious mushroom and egg stir-fry.
  • Master the techniques for preparing and cooking the ingredients.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to enhance the dish.

Ingredients

  • 3 yuan worth of fresh mushrooms
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • 1 tablespoon flour
  • 6 chicken eggs
  • 1 tablespoon light soy sauce
  • 1 tablespoon oyster sauce
  • 1 tablespoon cornstarch
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • 1 tablespoon pepper
  • Water
  • Several cloves of garlic
  • Several millet peppers
  • 1 green pepper
  • Some green onions
  • Cooking oil
  • Sugar

Instructions

  1. Clean the mushrooms thoroughly: Rinse multiple times, scrubbing to remove dirt and insects. Add salt and flour to the water to aid in cleaning.
  2. Trim and slice the mushrooms: Cut off the tough stems and slice the mushroom caps thinly, about the thickness of a coin.
  3. Prepare the eggs: Crack 6 eggs into a bowl, whisk until yolks and whites are fully combined. Set aside.
  4. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, combine light soy sauce, oyster sauce, cornstarch, salt, pepper, and a little water. Mix well until smooth. Set aside.
  5. Prepare the aromatics: Mince garlic, thinly slice millet peppers, halve and slice the green pepper, finely chop the white parts of the green onions, and slice the green parts lengthwise. Set aside.
  6. Blanch the mushrooms: Bring water to a boil in a pot. Add a spoonful of sugar, then add the mushrooms. Blanch for about 2 minutes to remove oxalic acid and some odor. Drain and rinse under cold water.
  7. Combine eggs and mushrooms: Add the whisked eggs to the blanched mushrooms and gently mix until the mushrooms are evenly coated. Set aside.
  8. Stir-fry the mushrooms and eggs: Heat oil in a wok or pan over medium heat. Add the mushroom and egg mixture, stirring gently to cook evenly until lightly golden and slightly soft. Remove and set aside.
  9. Stir-fry aromatics and sauce: In a clean wok or pan, heat oil. Add garlic and millet peppers and stir-fry until fragrant. Add the mushroom and egg mixture, stir-frying until heated through. Add green pepper and the prepared sauce, stirring until thickened.
  10. Finish and serve: Stir in the chopped green onions, stir-fry briefly, and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=cZbDRC4zvcs

mushroom_egg.txt - Scrambled Eggs with Mushrooms

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious scrambled egg and mushroom dish.
  • Master the techniques of cleaning, preparing, and cooking the ingredients.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to enhance the taste of the dish.

Ingredients

  • 3 yuan worth of fresh mushrooms
  • 6 chicken eggs
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • 1 tablespoon flour
  • 1 tablespoon light soy sauce
  • 1 tablespoon oyster sauce
  • 1 tablespoon cornstarch
  • 1 tablespoon pepper
  • Water (amount to cover mushrooms and for sauce)
  • Several cloves of garlic
  • Several millet peppers
  • 1 green pepper
  • Some green onions (white and green parts separated)
  • 1 tablespoon sugar
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Clean the Mushrooms: Clean the mushrooms thoroughly. Add salt and flour to the water to help remove dirt and insects. Rinse several times until the water runs clear.
  2. Prepare the Mushrooms: Cut off the tough stems of the mushrooms. Slice the mushroom caps thinly, about the thickness of a coin. Set aside.
  3. Prepare the Eggs: Crack 6 eggs into a bowl. Beat well with chopsticks until the whites and yolks are fully combined. Set aside.
  4. Prepare the Sauce: In a bowl, combine light soy sauce, oyster sauce, cornstarch, salt, pepper, and a little water. Mix well until the sauce is smooth and set aside.
  5. Prepare the Aromatics: Mince the garlic and finely chop the millet peppers. Cut the green pepper into small pieces. Finely chop the white parts of the green onions and cut the green parts into long sections. Set aside.
  6. Blanch the Mushrooms: Bring water to a boil in a pot. Add sugar and the sliced mushrooms. Blanch for about 2 minutes to remove oxalic acid and some of the mushroom's odor. Drain and rinse with cold water.
  7. Combine Eggs and Mushrooms: In a large bowl, combine the blanched mushrooms and the beaten eggs. Mix well with chopsticks until the mushrooms are evenly coated.
  8. Stir-fry the Eggs and Mushrooms: Heat oil in a pan over medium heat. Add the egg and mushroom mixture. Stir-fry gently until lightly golden and slightly soft. Set aside.
  9. Stir-fry Aromatics and Sauce: In a clean pan, heat oil. Add the minced garlic and millet peppers. Stir-fry briefly. Add the stir-fried egg and mushroom mixture, green pepper, and prepared sauce. Stir-fry until the sauce thickens and coats everything.
  10. Finish and Serve: Add the chopped white and green parts of the green onions. Stir-fry for a few seconds until the onions are wilted. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=cZbDRC4zvcs

mushroom_stir_fry.txt - Mushroom Stir-fry with Egg

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare and clean shiitake and oyster mushrooms.
  • Master a flavorful mushroom stir-fry recipe.
  • Create a delicious side dish suitable for wine or rice.

Ingredients

  • 6 Yuan worth of shiitake and oyster mushrooms
  • Salt
  • 1 Carrot, peeled and thinly sliced
  • 1 large green bell pepper, deseeded and diamond-shaped sliced
  • Some chili peppers (or red peppers), thinly sliced
  • Several cloves garlic, minced
  • A small piece of ginger, minced
  • 1 small green onion, chopped
  • 1/2 tbsp light soy sauce
  • A little oyster sauce
  • 1 tsp table salt
  • Pepper
  • 1 tbsp cornstarch
  • 1/2 bowl of water
  • 3 eggs
  • Cooking oil
  • Sugar

Instructions

  1. Prepare a bowl of salted water. Soak the mushrooms for 5 minutes to clean and sterilize them.
  2. Rinse the mushrooms twice with clean water, drain.
  3. Slice the mushrooms into slightly thicker slices (about 1 cm) to prevent excessive shrinkage during cooking.
  4. Prepare the vegetables: thinly slice the carrot, dice the green pepper into diamond shapes, thinly slice the chili peppers, mince the garlic and ginger, and chop the green onion.
  5. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, combine light soy sauce, oyster sauce, salt, pepper, cornstarch, and water. Mix well until the cornstarch dissolves. Set aside.
  6. Prepare the egg: Crack 3 eggs into a bowl (no need to whisk). Heat oil in a pan and fry the eggs until cooked through on both sides. Remove and chop into pieces. Set aside.
  7. Blanch the mushrooms: Boil water in a pot. Add mushrooms and a pinch of sugar (to remove odor). Boil for 1 minute. Remove with a slotted spoon and immediately rinse with cold water to remove oxalic acid. Drain and set aside.
  8. Stir-fry the vegetables: Add oil to a wok or pan. Add the carrots and stir-fry for 30 seconds. Add the onion, ginger, and garlic; stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Add the mushrooms, chili peppers, and fried eggs to the pan. Stir-fry until well combined.
  10. Add the prepared sauce, increase heat, and stir-fry until the sauce thickens.
  11. Add the green pepper and stir-fry for about 1 minute until tender-crisp.
  12. Drizzle some oil over the dish before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=rJr_NarhcR0

mushroom_three_fresh_soup.txt - 菌菇三鲜汤

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious mushroom three-fresh soup.
  • Master simple techniques for preparing ingredients like tomatoes and mushrooms.
  • Create a flavorful broth using readily available ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 1 tomato
  • 1 pack of oyster mushrooms (白玉菇)
  • 1 pack of crab flavor mushrooms (蟹味菇)
  • 1 pack of golden needle mushrooms (金针菇)
  • 1 block of inner pot tofu (内酯豆腐)
  • A small handful of cilantro (香菜)
  • 2 eggs (母鸡下的蛋)
  • Shanxi aged vinegar (山西陈醋)
  • Soy sauce (生抽)
  • Salt (食盐)
  • Song Rong Xian (松茸鲜) - a type of mushroom seasoning
  • Pepper (胡椒粉)
  • Cornstarch or potato starch (玉米淀粉 or 土豆淀粉)
  • Water (清水)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)

Instructions

  1. Score a cross on the tomato and blanch it in 101°C water. Peel and cut into small pieces, discarding the core.
  2. Clean oyster mushrooms, crab flavor mushrooms, and golden needle mushrooms. Cut the golden needle mushrooms into 2cm segments.
  3. Cut the inner pot tofu into small squares.
  4. Chop cilantro.
  5. Whisk two eggs with Shanxi aged vinegar, soy sauce, salt, Song Rong Xian, and pepper in a bowl.
  6. Mix cornstarch/potato starch with water to make a slurry. Set aside.
  7. Heat oil in a pot. Sauté the tomato until softened. Add water and bring to a boil.
  8. Add oyster mushrooms, crab flavor mushrooms, and golden needle mushrooms. Boil for 2 minutes. Skim off any foam.
  9. Add the tofu and the egg mixture. Stir to combine.
  10. Add the slurry and simmer until the soup thickens.
  11. Stir in cilantro.
  12. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=T554ekyCWP8

mutton_soup.txt - Mutton Soup

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare flavorful and tender mutton soup.
  • Understand the importance of removing impurities and odor from mutton.
  • Master a simple yet effective recipe for a delicious mutton soup.

Ingredients

  • Fresh mutton (amount unspecified, adjust to your needs)
  • 1 tsp salt
  • Strong liquor (amount unspecified)
  • Lukewarm water (amount unspecified, enough to cover the mutton)
  • Green onions (amount unspecified, for garnish and dipping sauce)
  • Millet peppers (amount unspecified, for dipping sauce)
  • Garlic (amount unspecified, for dipping sauce)
  • 1 tbsp white sesame seeds
  • 1 tbsp chili powder (optional, for dipping sauce)
  • Cooking oil (amount unspecified, for dipping sauce)
  • 1 tbsp light soy sauce
  • 1 tbsp balsamic vinegar
  • Ginger (amount unspecified)
  • 1/2 white radish
  • Salt and pepper (to taste)
  • Kaempferia angelica (amount unspecified, per kg of mutton)
  • Angelica (amount unspecified, per kg of mutton)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the mutton: Trim excess fat and cut into long pieces.
  2. Marinate the mutton: In a bowl, combine the mutton with salt, liquor, and lukewarm water. Mix well and let it marinate for at least one hour to remove impurities and odor.
  3. Prepare the dipping sauce: Finely chop green onions, millet peppers, and garlic. In a bowl, combine these ingredients with white sesame seeds, chili powder (if using), cooking oil, light soy sauce, and balsamic vinegar. Mix well.
  4. Blanch the mutton: Rinse the marinated mutton thoroughly under running water until the water runs clear. Bring a pot of water to a boil, add the mutton, and let it boil for 2 minutes. Remove the mutton and rinse again with warm water (avoid cold water to prevent toughness).
  5. Simmer the soup: In a large pot, add a piece of ginger to the bottom. Add the blanched mutton and cover with boiling water. Add Kaempferia angelica and Angelica (adjust amount based on mutton quantity). Bring to a boil, then reduce heat to low and simmer for 50 minutes. Do not add peppercorns, star anise, or cinnamon as they can darken the soup and affect the freshness of the mutton.
  6. Prepare the radish: Peel and chop a half white radish into smaller pieces.
  7. Add radish and finish: After 50 minutes, add the chopped radish to the pot. Simmer for another 20 minutes, stirring occasionally.
  8. Season and serve: Season the soup with salt and pepper to taste. The mutton should be tender and easily fall off the bone. Serve hot with the dipping sauce.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=-rrLHWRjHTs

neizhi_doufu_zheng_jidan.txt - Steamed Egg with Inner Pot Tofu and Minced Meat

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious steamed egg dish with inner pot tofu and minced meat.
  • Master the simple steps involved in preparing this dish.
  • Understand how to enhance the flavor and texture of the dish through proper cooking techniques.

Ingredients

  • 1 box inner pot tofu (盒内酯豆腐)
  • 4 eggs (个鸡蛋)
  • 100g pork tenderloin or shoulder (梅花肉或前腿肉 100克)
  • Appropriate amount of scallions (适量小葱)
  • 1 piece ginger (一块生姜)
  • Several cloves garlic (几瓣蒜)
  • Salt (食盐)
  • White pepper (胡椒粉)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • Light soy sauce (生抽)
  • Dark soy sauce (老抽)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)

Instructions

  1. Invert a box of inner pot tofu into a suitable bowl.
  2. Crack 4 eggs into the bowl with the tofu.
  3. Use a knife to gently cut the tofu into small pieces. Avoid breaking the tofu.
  4. Add an appropriate amount of water to a pot. Place the bowl of tofu and eggs in the pot. Cover and steam over high heat for 10 minutes.
  5. While the tofu and eggs are steaming, prepare the minced meat. Cut the pork into thin slices, then mince. Alternatively, use a food processor.
  6. Mince scallions, ginger, and garlic.
  7. Once the tofu and eggs are steamed, remove from the pot.
  8. Heat a small amount of cooking oil in a pan. Add minced scallions, ginger, and garlic and stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Add the minced meat and stir-fry until the color changes.
  10. Season with salt, white pepper, oyster sauce, light soy sauce, and a small amount of dark soy sauce for color. Stir-fry until the sauce is fragrant and the meat is well-seasoned.
  11. Thicken the sauce with a little cornstarch slurry.
  12. Pour the sauce evenly over the steamed egg and tofu.
  13. Garnish with chopped scallions.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Z4Z5gaMob_0

nilagang_repolyo_at_tofu.txt - Nilagang Repolyo at Tofu

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare a delicious and warming Nilagang Repolyo at Tofu.
  • Master simple techniques for cooking tofu and cabbage.
  • Create a nutritious and flavorful dish using readily available ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 1 block soft tofu (cut into 4, then thinly sliced)
  • 1 Chinese cabbage (cut into pieces, leaves separated from stalks)
  • 5 yuan worth of pork belly (thinly sliced)
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • Several red chilies (thinly sliced)
  • A handful of garlic (thinly sliced)
  • A small piece of ginger (peeled and thinly sliced)
  • 2 scallions (white and green parts separated, thinly sliced)
  • 4 eggs
  • 1 small spoonful salt
  • 1 small spoonful five-spice powder
  • Moderate amount light soy sauce
  • A dash of oyster sauce
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Prepare the tofu: Cut a block of soft tofu into four pieces, then slice thinly. Set aside.
  2. Prepare the cabbage: Cut off the roots of the Chinese cabbage. Separate the leaves and stalks. Wash thoroughly with salted water to sterilize. Drain well. Cut the stalks diagonally into slices; tear the leaves into bite-sized pieces.
  3. Prepare the pork belly: Thinly slice 5 yuan worth of pork belly and set aside.
  4. Prepare the aromatics: Thinly slice red chilies, garlic, and ginger. Separate the white and green parts of the scallions.
  5. Prepare the eggs: Crack 4 eggs into a bowl and set aside.
  6. Fry the tofu: Heat oil in a pan. Fry tofu slices over low heat until golden brown on all sides. Season with a little salt to prevent sticking. Set aside.
  7. Fry the eggs: In the same pan, fry the eggs until golden brown on both sides. Cut into pieces and set aside.
  8. Stir-fry pork belly and aromatics: In a separate pan, stir-fry the pork belly over low heat until excess fat renders. Add ginger, garlic, and chilies; stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Stir-fry the cabbage: Add the cabbage stalks to the pan and stir-fry until slightly softened.
  10. Season the stir-fry: Add salt, five-spice powder, light soy sauce, and oyster sauce. Stir well to combine.
  11. Assemble the soup: In a pot, add a little oil. Add the cabbage leaves, fried eggs, fried tofu, stir-fried pork belly mixture, and enough water to cover.
  12. Simmer: Bring to a boil, then reduce heat and simmer for 2 minutes with the lid on.
  13. Finish: Add the scallions and simmer for another minute.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=o4iwYhjZ8mw

nongjia_qiezi.txt - Farmer's Style Eggplant

Objectives

  • Learn a quick and easy method for cooking eggplant without deep-frying.
  • Master a flavorful sauce that complements the eggplant's texture.
  • Achieve tender, flavorful eggplant that pairs perfectly with rice.

Ingredients

  • 2 eggplants (long, approximately 1 pound each)
  • Salt (double the amount usually used for stir-fry)
  • 1-2 green bell peppers (thick, meaty)
  • 2-3 small chili peppers (小米椒 - xiǎo mǐ jiāo)
  • Several cloves of garlic
  • Several scallions (葱白 - cōng bái - white parts only)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽 - shēng chōu)
  • Appropriate amount of oyster sauce (蚝油 - háo yóu)
  • A little dark soy sauce (老抽 - lǎo chōu)
  • A pinch of sugar
  • 1 tsp mushroom seasoning (松茸鲜 - sōng róng xiān)
  • 1 tsp cornstarch (玉米淀粉 - yùmǐ diànfěn)
  • Water
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Cut off the top and bottom of the eggplants. Cut into long segments, then slice into thick pieces, and finally julienne into long strips.
  2. Place eggplant strips in a large bowl, add double the usual amount of salt for stir-fry, mix well to coat, and marinate for 10 minutes.
  3. While eggplant marinates, prepare the green peppers: clean, remove stems and seeds, slice into thick strips.
  4. Prepare the chili peppers: finely chop.
  5. Prepare the garlic: mince finely.
  6. Prepare the scallions: finely mince the white parts only.
  7. Prepare the sauce: In a small bowl, mix soy sauce, oyster sauce, dark soy sauce, sugar, mushroom seasoning, cornstarch, and water until smooth. Set aside.
  8. After 10 minutes, rinse the eggplant to remove excess salt, then squeeze out as much water as possible. Set aside.
  9. Heat a wok or pan, add a small amount of oil. Add the eggplant and stir-fry until the moisture is removed (about 3 minutes). Remove eggplant and set aside.
  10. Add more oil to the pan, then add garlic, chili peppers, and stir-fry until fragrant.
  11. Add green peppers and stir-fry until tender-crisp.
  12. Add the stir-fried eggplant and the prepared sauce. Stir-fry over high heat until everything is well combined and heated through. Stir-fry until the eggplant is soft and the sauce has thickened.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=BJlLmypiW8Y

oil_choy_sum_with_pork.txt - 油麥菜炒肉末 (Yóumài cài chǎo ròumò)

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare oil choy sum for optimal texture and flavor.
  • Master a quick and flavorful stir-fry technique.
  • Create a delicious and healthy side dish perfect for rice.

Ingredients

  • 2 bunches 油麥菜 (yóumài cài) - Oil Choy Sum
  • 1 tsp 食鹽 (shíyán) - Salt
  • Water (山泉水 - shān quán shuǐ - mountain spring water, tap water is fine)
  • 1/2 large red pepper 大紅椒 (dà hóng jiāo)
  • 1 green pepper 青椒 (qīng jiāo)
  • Garlic 蒜 (suàn)
  • Ginger 洋薑 (yáng jiāng) - Note: The transcript mentions 洋薑豆豉 (yáng jiāng dòuchǐ), which translates to ginger and fermented black beans. It's unclear if this is a specific ingredient or if the two are separate. Clarification needed.
  • Fermented black beans 豆豉 (dòuchǐ)
  • 5 Flower Pork 五花肉 (wǔ huā ròu) - optional
  • Lean pork 瘦肉 (shòu ròu) - optional
  • Cooking oil 食用油 (shíyòng yóu)
  • 松茸鮮 (sōngróng xiān) - Matsutake mushroom seasoning (a type of umami enhancer, optional)

Instructions

  1. Remove oil choy sum leaves and rinse thoroughly.
  2. Soak oil choy sum in a bowl of lightly salted water for 2-5 minutes.
  3. Rinse oil choy sum again to remove any remaining dirt.
  4. Blanch oil choy sum in boiling water for 5 seconds to remove bitterness.
  5. Immediately transfer to a bowl of cold water to maintain crispness.
  6. Drain oil choy sum well and set aside.
  7. Cut off the tough ends of the oil choy sum.
  8. Chop the oil choy sum into small pieces (approximately 0.5 mm). Discard the very tips.
  9. Chop the oil choy sum stems into small pieces.
  10. Chop the red and green peppers into small pieces.
  11. Mince the garlic.
  12. Dice the 5-flower pork (optional), removing the skin.
  13. Mince the lean pork (optional).
  14. Heat a wok or pan with a small amount of oil.
  15. Remove excess oil, leaving a small amount for cooking.
  16. Add the diced 5-flower pork and stir-fry until lightly browned.
  17. Add the minced lean pork (if using) and stir-fry until browned.
  18. Add the garlic, ginger, and fermented black beans (if using), and stir-fry until fragrant.
  19. Add the chopped peppers and stir-fry briefly.
  20. Add the prepared oil choy sum.
  21. Season with salt and Matsutake mushroom seasoning (optional).
  22. Stir-fry everything until well combined and heated through (approximately 77 seconds).
  23. Serve immediately.

oil_爆_蒜蓉虾.txt - Oil-爆 Garlic Shrimp

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious, flavorful garlic shrimp.
  • Master a simple yet effective cooking technique for shrimp.
  • Achieve tender, juicy shrimp with a fragrant garlic sauce.

Ingredients

  • Frozen shrimp (quantity not specified)
  • Ginger slices (a small amount)
  • Cooking wine (a small amount)
  • Garlic cloves (a generous amount)
  • Scallions (a few)
  • Cooking oil (a small amount)
  • Soy sauce (a small amount)
  • Oyster sauce (a small amount)

Instructions

  1. Thaw frozen shrimp (method shown in a previous video).
  2. Place shrimp in a bowl. Add ginger slices and a little cooking wine. Marinate for a few minutes to remove fishy smell and make shrimp more tender.
  3. While shrimp marinates, prepare the garlic. Mince garlic cloves. Chop scallions. Set aside.
  4. Rinse marinated shrimp, drain, and pat dry. Cut a slit along the back of each shrimp for better flavor absorption and faster cooking.
  5. Heat a wok or pan over medium heat. Add a small amount of cooking oil.
  6. Add shrimp to the hot pan and stir-fry until golden brown (about 2-3 minutes). Remove and set aside.
  7. Add a little more oil to the pan. Add 2/3 of the minced garlic and sauté over low heat until fragrant and cooked.
  8. Add the cooked shrimp to the pan. Season with a small amount of soy sauce and oyster sauce. Stir-fry until well combined and flavors are incorporated.
  9. Add the remaining 1/3 of the minced garlic and chopped scallions. Stir-fry over high heat for 5-8 seconds.
  10. Serve immediately.
