okra_egg.txt - Okra and Egg Stir-fry

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare okra for cooking, removing impurities and preserving its color.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful sauce for the okra and egg stir-fry.
  • Create a delicious and nutritious okra and egg dish, suitable for home cooking.

Ingredients

  • 4 eggs
  • Okra (amount not specified)
  • Red bell pepper (small amount, sliced)
  • Garlic (small handful, minced)
  • Salt (pinch)
  • Sugar (dash)
  • Soy sauce (1/2 spoonful)
  • Oyster sauce (dash)
  • Potato starch (small spoonful)
  • Water (small amount)
  • White vinegar (dash)
  • Peanut or corn oil (for frying)

Instructions

  1. Clean the Okra: Wash okra thoroughly with water, salt, and gentle scrubbing to remove surface fluff and impurities. Rinse twice more. Drain on a bamboo mat.
  2. Prepare the Sauce: In a bowl, combine salt, sugar, soy sauce, oyster sauce, potato starch, and water. Stir until well mixed and set aside.
  3. Prepare the Eggs: Crack 4 eggs into a bowl. Add salt and white vinegar. Whisk vigorously until yolks and whites are fully combined and no lumps remain. Set aside.
  4. Blanch the Okra: Bring water to a boil in a pan. Add the okra and blanch for about 1 minute until slightly softened and a turquoise color. Immediately transfer to a bowl of ice water to cool and maintain color. Drain well.
  5. Cut the Okra: Cut the blanched okra into horseshoe slices (approximately 0.5 cm thick).
  6. Coat Okra with Egg: Add the cut okra to the bowl with the egg mixture. Stir gently to coat each piece evenly.
  7. Fry the Okra and Eggs: Heat peanut or corn oil in a pan until it lightly smokes. Add the okra and egg mixture. Cook over medium-low heat, gently shaking the pan to ensure even cooking, until the bottom is set (about 2 minutes). Flip and continue frying until golden brown on both sides. Break into smaller pieces with a spatula. Remove and set aside.
  8. Stir-fry Aromatics: In the same pan (no need to clean or add more oil), add minced garlic and sliced red pepper. Stir-fry for about 15 seconds over medium-low heat.
  9. Combine and Add Sauce: Add the fried okra and eggs to the pan with the garlic and pepper. Stir-fry over high heat. Pour in the prepared sauce and stir-fry until well combined.
  10. Serve: Transfer the finished okra and egg stir-fry to a plate and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=lpZHD1TsQ1Q

okrasteam.txt - Steamed Okra with Garlic, Chili, and Soy Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn to clean okra effectively to remove fuzz.
  • Master a simple steaming method to preserve okra's nutrients and vibrant color.
  • Prepare a flavorful sauce to enhance the taste of the steamed okra.

Ingredients

  • 500g Okra (approximately 1 jin)
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • 1 tablespoon baking soda
  • Plenty of pure water
  • Several cloves garlic, sliced
  • Several small chili peppers, finely chopped (or substitute with large red peppers)
  • Some scallions (white parts only), chopped
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • A pinch of sugar
  • Some mushroom seasoning (松茸鲜)
  • Some oyster sauce
  • A little light soy sauce
  • 1 teaspoon potato starch
  • Appropriate amount of water
  • Some peanut oil

Instructions

  1. Wash okra: Place okra in a large bowl. Add salt and baking soda. Add plenty of water to thoroughly clean the okra, removing fuzz. Rinse twice with clean water to remove baking soda residue. Drain and set aside.
  2. Prepare garlic and chili: Slice garlic. Finely chop chili peppers (or red peppers), then roughly crush them for a stronger flavor. Chop scallion whites.
  3. Make the sauce: In a bowl, combine salt, sugar, mushroom seasoning, oyster sauce, light soy sauce, potato starch, and water. Mix well until the starch dissolves. Set aside.
  4. Prepare the okra for steaming: Place drained okra in a bowl. Add peanut oil and toss to coat each piece evenly. This helps prevent discoloration and retains nutrients during steaming.
  5. Steam the okra: Add water to a steamer. Arrange okra in the steamer basket, leaving some space between pieces for even steaming. Steam over high heat for 3 minutes and 30 seconds. Do not blanch the okra.
  6. Prepare the sauce for finishing: Heat oil in a pan. Add garlic, chili, and scallions. Sauté until fragrant over medium-low heat. Add the prepared sauce and cook until thickened.
  7. Finish and serve: Remove the steamed okra from the steamer. Gently tear each okra piece lengthwise into smaller pieces. Arrange the okra on a plate. Pour the sauce over the okra and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=d16bU_IuW4g

onion_egg_cake.txt - 洋葱鸡蛋饼 (Yángcōng jīdàn bǐng)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious onion egg cake.
  • Master the technique of preparing and cooking the onion to prevent eye irritation.
  • Create a visually appealing and flavorful dish suitable for breakfast or snacks.

Ingredients

  • 1 medium purple onion (紫皮洋葱 - zǐpí yángcōng)
  • 1 medium carrot (胡萝卜 - húluóbo)
  • 1 medium apple (苹果 - píngguǒ)
  • 2-3 eggs (鸡蛋 - jīdàn)
  • 1 tbsp salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • 1 tsp pepper (胡椒粉 - hújiāofěn)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽 - shēngchōu)
  • 1 tbsp oyster sauce (蚝油 - háoyóu)
  • 1 tbsp all-purpose flour (普通面粉 - pǔtōng miànfěn)
  • 1 tbsp potato starch or cornstarch (土豆淀粉/玉米淀粉 - tǔdòu diànfěn/yùmǐ diànfěn)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòng yóu)
  • Optional: Black sesame seeds (黑芝麻 - hēizhīma)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the onion: Wash, cut in half, then into fourths. Soak in water with 1 tbsp salt for 5 minutes to reduce eye irritation. Drain and finely chop. Set aside a few thicker onion rings.
  2. Prepare the carrot: Peel, cut into long strips, then thin slices, then julienne, and finally dice.
  3. Prepare the apple: Peel, thinly slice, remove core, julienne, and finally dice.
  4. Prepare the green pepper (if using): Remove stem and seeds, julienne, and then dice.
  5. Combine the vegetables: Mix the diced carrot, apple, and green pepper (if using) in a bowl.
  6. Prepare the eggs: Crack eggs into a bowl, whisk until yolks and whites are fully combined.
  7. Mix the batter: Add the whisked eggs to the bowl with the vegetables. Add salt, pepper, soy sauce, oyster sauce, flour, and starch. Mix until smooth and slightly viscous.
  8. Prepare the electric griddle: Add cooking oil and spread evenly. Arrange the onion rings on the griddle.
  9. Pour the batter: Pour the batter into the onion rings, spreading evenly.
  10. Cook the cake: Cover the griddle and cook over low heat for 3 minutes per side, or until golden brown and crispy. Optionally sprinkle black sesame seeds on top.
  11. Remove and serve: Remove the onion egg cake from the griddle, and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=pRBvnVzup0s

pan_fried_fish.txt - Pan-Fried Fish

Objectives

  • Learn to pan-fry fish without breaking the skin.
  • Prepare and marinate fish for optimal flavor and texture.
  • Make a delicious and visually appealing pan-fried fish dish.

Ingredients

  • 1 whole bream (approx. 15 yuan)
  • Salt
  • Ginger (several slices, thinly sliced, and julienned)
  • Green onions (small bunch, finely chopped and julienned)
  • Cooking wine
  • 1/2 tbsp light soy sauce
  • 1/2 tbsp vinegar
  • 1 tbsp sugar
  • 1 tbsp dark soy sauce
  • 1 star anise
  • Pepper oil (or Sichuan peppercorns)
  • 1 bowl of water
  • Flour (thin layer for coating)
  • Cooking oil
  • Garlic (several cloves, minced)

Instructions

  1. Clean the fish: Remove the black membrane and blood clots from the fish's belly. Rinse thoroughly.
  2. Prepare the fish: Trim fins and tail. Use a knife at a 45-degree angle to score the fish, creating a pattern on both sides.
  3. Marinate the fish: Sprinkle salt evenly on both sides of the fish. Prepare a ginger and green onion mixture by boiling the chopped ingredients in water, then using a rolling pin to extract the juice. Pour the juice over the fish, ensuring both sides are coated. Place julienned ginger and green onions inside the fish's belly. Marinate for 20 minutes.
  4. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, combine cooking wine, light soy sauce, vinegar, sugar, dark soy sauce, star anise, pepper oil (or Sichuan peppercorns), and water. Mix until well dissolved. Set aside.
  5. Prepare for frying: Lightly dust the marinated fish with flour.
  6. Heat the pan: Heat a wok or large pan until it slightly smokes. Add cooking oil.
  7. Fry the fish: Once the oil is hot, carefully place the fish tail-first into the pan. Fry for 30 seconds to set the shape. Gently slide the fish into the pan. Fry for 2-3 minutes per side over medium-low heat, until the fish slides easily in the pan, indicating it's cooked.
  8. Add sauce and simmer: Remove excess oil from the pan. Pour the prepared sauce into the pan. Add minced garlic under the fish to prevent sticking. Bring to a simmer, then cover and cook for 2 minutes.
  9. Finish the dish: Open the lid, spoon the sauce over the fish, repeat 3-4 times. Increase heat to high to reduce the sauce and thicken it. Add water starch to further thicken the sauce. Garnish with chopped green onions.

pan_fried_xiaolongbao.txt - Pan-Fried Xiaolongbao (煎小笼包)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious pan-fried Xiaolongbao.
  • Prepare flavorful tofu and leek filling.
  • Master the technique of pan-frying for a crispy crust.

Ingredients

  • For the Filling:
    • 1 block firm tofu (豆腐, dòufu)
    • 1 tablespoon salt (盐, yán)
    • 1 handful leeks (韭菜, jiǔcài), chopped
    • 1 tablespoon sesame oil (芝麻油, zhīma yóu)
    • 1 carrot (胡萝卜, húluóbo), shredded
    • 3 eggs (鸡蛋, jīdàn)
    • 1 teaspoon white vinegar (白醋, bái cù)
    • 1/2 teaspoon light soy sauce (生抽, shēng chōu)
    • Generous amount oyster sauce (蚝油, háoyóu)
    • 1 teaspoon salt (盐, yán)
    • A little pepper (胡椒粉, hújiāo fěn)
    • A little ground sesame oil (芝麻油, zhīma yóu)
  • For the Xiaolongbao:
    • Dumpling wrappers (饺子皮, jiǎozi pí)
    • Cooking oil (食用油, shíyòng yóu)
    • Water (水, shuǐ)
    • Black sesame seeds (黑芝麻, hēi zhīma)
    • White sesame seeds (白芝麻, bái zhīma)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Tofu: Place tofu in a bowl, add salt and boiling water. Let it sit for 3 minutes to remove the beany smell. Drain and cut into small pieces.
  2. Prepare the Leeks: Chop leeks finely. Toss with sesame oil.
  3. Prepare the Carrot: Peel, clean, and shred the carrot.
  4. Prepare the Egg Filling: Whisk 3 eggs with a little white vinegar until light and fluffy.
  5. Combine Filling Ingredients: Stir-fry the shredded carrots until softened. Add the egg mixture to the tofu, and stir to coat. In a separate pan, stir-fry the egg-tofu mixture until set. Add the carrots, soy sauce, oyster sauce, salt, pepper, and sesame oil. Stir-fry until well combined. Add the leeks and stir-fry briefly. Set aside to cool.
  6. Assemble the Xiaolongbao: Roll out dumpling wrappers slightly larger. Fill each wrapper with 2 spoonfuls of filling. Pinch to seal, forming a bun shape.
  7. Pan-Fry the Xiaolongbao: Heat cooking oil in a non-stick pan. Arrange Xiaolongbao in the pan. Cover and cook over low heat for 3 minutes.
  8. Add Water & Finish Cooking: Add a little water to the pan, cover, and cook for another 3 minutes.
  9. Add Sesame Seeds: Remove the lid, and sprinkle black and white sesame seeds on top.
  10. Serve: Carefully remove the Xiaolongbao from the pan. Serve immediately, optionally inverting onto a plate for a crispier bottom.

perfect_hard_boiled_eggs.txt - Perfect Hard-Boiled Eggs

Objectives

  • Learn a foolproof method for perfectly peeling hard-boiled eggs.
  • Understand the importance of pre-soaking eggs in a baking soda and salt solution.
  • Master the optimal cooking time for hard-boiled eggs that are both safe and delicious.

Ingredients

  • Eggs (number depends on your needs)
  • Baking soda (a pinch)
  • Salt (a pinch)
  • Water
  • White vinegar (a little)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the eggs: Wash the eggs thoroughly.
  2. Pre-soak the eggs: In a bowl, dissolve a pinch of baking soda and salt in water. Add the eggs and let them soak for 5 minutes.
  3. Scrub the eggs: Scrub the eggs one by one with a kitchen towel to remove dirt and bacteria.
  4. Rinse the eggs: Rinse the eggs in clean water with a little white vinegar.
  5. Boil the water: Add water to a pot and bring it to a boil (dense bubbles at the bottom).
  6. Add salt to boiling water: Add a tablespoon of salt to the boiling water.
  7. Add eggs to boiling water: Gently place the eggs in the boiling water.
  8. Cook the eggs: Cook for at least 8 minutes to ensure safety and optimal texture.
  9. Cool the eggs: Immediately transfer the cooked eggs to a bowl of cold water to stop the cooking process and make peeling easier.
  10. Peel the eggs: Once cool, peel the eggs. They should peel easily.

phoenix_egg.txt - Phoenix Steamed Egg

Objectives

  • Learn to make a visually appealing and delicious Phoenix Steamed Egg dish.
  • Master the technique of perfectly cooking and preparing eggs for optimal texture.
  • Utilize simple ingredients to create a nutritious and flavorful meal.

Ingredients

6 eggs A pinch of baking soda Plenty of cold water Several water chestnuts A piece of five-spice pork belly (30% fat, 70% lean) Ginger (sliced) Green onions (sliced) Salt Pepper Soy sauce Oyster sauce Corn starch Sesame oil

Instructions

  1. Prepare the eggs: Crack 6 eggs into a bowl. Add a pinch of baking soda and plenty of cold water. Let it soak for 2 minutes.
  2. Clean the eggs: Use a paper towel to clean the egg shells thoroughly.
  3. Boil the eggs: Place eggs in a pot of cold water. Bring to a boil over high heat, then reduce heat to low and simmer for 8 minutes.
  4. Prepare the water chestnuts: Wash, peel, and finely dice the water chestnuts.
  5. Prepare the pork: Mince the five-spice pork belly. It should have a slightly coarse texture.
  6. Combine fillings: Mix the minced pork, diced water chestnuts, sliced ginger, and sliced green onions in a bowl. Season with salt, pepper, soy sauce, oyster sauce, corn starch, and sesame oil. Mix well.
  7. Cool and peel the eggs: Remove the boiled eggs from the pot and place them in cold water to cool. Peel the eggs.
  8. Halve the eggs: Cut each egg in half lengthwise. Remove the yolks and set aside.
  9. Fill the egg whites: Stuff the pork mixture into the egg white halves.
  10. Steam the eggs: Arrange the filled egg whites in a steamer basket. Steam over medium heat for 10 minutes.
  11. Prepare the sauce: In a small saucepan, combine the reserved egg yolks with some soy sauce, goji berries and a little bit of water. Bring to a simmer. Add corn starch to thicken.
  12. Finish and serve: Pour the sauce over the steamed eggs. Serve immediately.

phoenix_steamed_egg.txt - 凤凰蒸蛋 (Fènghuáng zhēng dàn)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and visually appealing Phoenix Steamed Eggs.
  • Master the technique of perfectly cooking and peeling hard-boiled eggs.
  • Create a flavorful and nutritious meat filling for the eggs.
  • Prepare a flavorful sauce to enhance the dish.

Ingredients

  • 6 eggs
  • A pinch of baking soda
  • Plenty of water
  • Several water chestnuts
  • A piece of five-layer pork (three parts fat, seven parts lean)
  • Ginger (sliced)
  • Green onions (sliced)
  • A small spoonful of salt
  • A little pepper
  • Soy sauce
  • Oyster sauce
  • One spoonful of cornstarch
  • Sesame oil
  • A little water for boiling eggs
  • Soy sauce for the sauce
  • Goji berries
  • Cornstarch for thickening sauce

Instructions

  1. Prepare the eggs: Add baking soda and plenty of water to 6 eggs. Soak for 2 minutes. Clean the egg shells with a paper towel to remove dirt and bacteria. Rinse thoroughly and drain.
  2. Boil the eggs: Add plenty of cold water to a pot, add the eggs, bring to a boil over high heat, then reduce heat and simmer for 8 minutes.
  3. Prepare the water chestnuts: Wash, peel, and finely dice the water chestnuts into small particles. Place in a bowl.
  4. Prepare the pork: Chop the five-layer pork into small, slightly coarse pieces.
  5. Combine the filling ingredients: Combine the pork and water chestnuts in a bowl. Add sliced ginger and green onions. Season with salt, pepper, soy sauce, oyster sauce, cornstarch, and sesame oil. Mix well with disposable gloves until evenly combined. Set aside.
  6. Cool and peel the eggs: Remove the boiled eggs from the pot and place them in cold water to cool. Once cool, peel the eggs.
  7. Prepare the eggs for steaming: Cut each egg in half lengthwise. Remove the yolks and set aside (save for other uses).
  8. Fill the egg whites: Fill each egg white with the meat mixture, packing it firmly.
  9. Steam the eggs: Arrange the filled egg whites in a steamer basket. Steam over medium-high heat for 10 minutes.
  10. Make the sauce: Pour the liquid from the steamer into a saucepan. Add soy sauce, goji berries, and bring to a boil. Thicken with cornstarch.
  11. Finish and serve: Remove the steamed eggs. Pour the sauce over the eggs. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=WBTyxRSuLW0

pickle_cucumber.txt - Pickled Cucumber

Objectives

  • Learn to make a restaurant-style pickled cucumber recipe.
  • Master a flavorful brine for crispy, sweet, and sour pickled cucumbers.
  • Understand how to properly prepare cucumbers for pickling.

Ingredients

  • 6 jin (approx. 3.6kg) tender yellow cucumbers with thorns
  • 10 yuan worth of cucumbers
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒)
  • Plenty of garlic cloves (蒜子)
  • 1 lemon
  • 200g light soy sauce (生抽)
  • 80g Shanxi aged vinegar (山西老陈醋)
  • 50g dark soy sauce (老抽)
  • 100g cold dressing (凉拌汁)
  • 200g white sugar (白糖)
  • Salt (食盐)

Instructions

  1. Wash the cucumbers thoroughly with water and salt to remove any thorns.
  2. Cut off both ends of the cucumbers and slice them into approximately 2cm segments.
  3. Finely slice the small chili peppers (adjust quantity to taste).
  4. Thinly slice the garlic cloves.
  5. Thinly slice the lemon.
  6. In a large bowl, combine the sliced cucumbers, chili peppers, garlic, and lemon slices.
  7. In a separate bowl, whisk together the light soy sauce, aged vinegar, dark soy sauce, cold dressing, and white sugar.
  8. Pour the prepared brine over the cucumbers and mix well to coat evenly. Ensure all cucumbers are submerged in the brine.
  9. Cover the bowl with plastic wrap to prevent bacterial contamination.
  10. Let it sit at room temperature overnight (approximately 10 hours).
  11. After 10 hours, the cucumbers will be pickled and ready to serve.
  12. Serve and enjoy! The brine can be reused by reheating it and adding more light soy sauce.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=iy6iwqPvtvE

pickled_cabbage.txt - مخلل الملفوف

Objectives

  • Prepare a refreshing pickled cabbage dish.
  • Learn a unique cooking method for cabbage to avoid bitterness.
  • Create a flavorful and crunchy pickled cabbage side dish.

Ingredients

  • 1 head of cabbage
  • Several cloves of garlic
  • Some dried chili peppers
  • Salt
  • White vinegar
  • 2 kg weight (for pressing cabbage)
  • Rice washing water
  • Optional: Lean ground meat, chicken broth, light soy sauce

Instructions

  1. Clean the cabbage thoroughly; no need to remove the outer leaves.
  2. Place the cabbage in a large bowl. Add garlic and dried chilies for flavor. Set aside.
  3. Rinse rice in a bowl, reserving the water. Use this water to wash vegetables or water plants.
  4. Pour the rice water into a metal pot. Bring to a boil over high heat.
  5. Once boiling, turn off the heat. Pour the hot rice water over the cabbage.
  6. Gently stir the cabbage with chopsticks to ensure it's submerged.
  7. Add a handful of salt and some white vinegar to promote fermentation and enhance flavor.
  8. Place a 2 kg weight on top of the cabbage and cover. Let it ferment for a day and a half.
  9. After fermentation, rinse the cabbage thoroughly in clean water. This is because it was not washed before fermentation.
  10. Drain the cabbage and cut it into bite-sized pieces. Avoid cutting it too small to maintain crunchiness.
  11. Chop the soaked dried chilies and garlic into a mince.
  12. Optional: Add lean ground meat. Mince it finely.
  13. Heat oil in a pan. Add some pork lard for extra aroma.
  14. Add the minced meat (and chilies and garlic) over low heat, cooking until the color changes.
  15. Increase the heat and stir-fry all ingredients for about 80 seconds until the aroma of the salt is released.
  16. Add chicken broth and light soy sauce. Stir well.
  17. Stir-fry over high heat until the flavors combine. Cook for about one minute.
  18. Serve the pickled cabbage as a side dish with steamed rice.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=mSbWyG8Skl8

pickled_radish.txt - Pickled Radishes

Objectives

  • Learn to make crispy and delicious pickled radishes.
  • Master a simple pickling technique suitable for beginners.
  • Understand how to balance flavors and achieve the perfect crunch.

Ingredients

  • 500g White Radishes (approx. cost 5 cents/lb)
  • 1 tbsp Salt (for washing and initial pickling)
  • 2 tbsp Sugar
  • Several cloves Garlic (thinly sliced)
  • 1 piece Ginger (thinly sliced)
  • Several pieces Dried Chili Peppers (thinly sliced)
  • 2 Green Chilies (thinly sliced)
  • 1 tbsp Salt (for the sauce)
  • Appropriate amount Sugar (for the sauce)
  • Small amount Chicken Bouillon (for the sauce)
  • 1 tbsp Light Soy Sauce (for the sauce)
  • 1/2 tbsp Balsamic Vinegar (for the sauce)
  • 1/2 tbsp Fish Sauce (for the sauce)
  • 10g White Vinegar (for the sauce)
  • 1/2 bowl Water (for the sauce)
  • 2 Star Anise (for the sauce)
  • 20g Sichuan Peppercorns (for the sauce)

Instructions

  1. Wash the radishes thoroughly with salt to clean and sterilize.
  2. Remove the root and stem ends of the radishes.
  3. Cut the radishes in half, then into quarters, then into smaller pieces. Aim for a size that will allow for even pickling and a crispy texture.
  4. Place the cut radishes in a large bowl.
  5. Add 2 tablespoons of sugar to the radishes.
  6. Mix well and let the radishes sit for 20 minutes to draw out moisture.
  7. While the radishes are sitting, prepare the other ingredients: thinly slice garlic, ginger, dried chili peppers, and green chilies.
  8. In a separate bowl, prepare the sauce: combine salt, sugar, chicken bouillon, light soy sauce, balsamic vinegar, fish sauce, white vinegar, and water. Mix well.
  9. Add star anise and Sichuan peppercorns to the sauce.
  10. Bring the sauce to a boil over high heat, stirring constantly to release the flavors of the spices.
  11. Continue boiling for 2 minutes.
  12. Strain the spices from the sauce using a slotted spoon.
  13. Let the sauce cool.
  14. While the sauce cools, drain excess water from the marinated radishes using a cheesecloth or clean kitchen towel, pressing firmly to remove as much liquid as possible.
  15. Add the sliced garlic, ginger, chilies to the drained radishes.
  16. Pour the cooled sauce over the radishes.
  17. Wearing disposable gloves, mix thoroughly to ensure the radishes are evenly coated in the sauce.
  18. Cover the bowl with plastic wrap and refrigerate for at least 2 hours to allow the flavors to meld.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=gUfzN97kpJg

pidan_shourouzhou.txt - 皮蛋瘦肉粥 (Pidan Shourou Zhou)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious pidan shourou zhou (皮蛋瘦肉粥).
  • Master the techniques for preparing the rice and ingredients.
  • Achieve a smooth, flavorful, and non-fishy texture.

Ingredients

  • Rice (amount depends on serving size)
  • 2-3 松花皮蛋 (songhua pidan) - preserved duck eggs
  • Pork (lean meat), about 200g
  • Spring water (amount depends on serving size)
  • 1 tbsp Salt (食盐)
  • 1 tbsp Cornstarch (玉米淀粉)
  • Ginger (生姜), a small piece
  • Green onions (小葱), a few stalks
  • Pepper (胡椒粉), a pinch

Instructions

  1. Rinse rice thoroughly and soak in water for 10 minutes.
  2. Prepare 2-3 preserved duck eggs (松花皮蛋), remove shells, and rinse.
  3. Drain soaked rice and place in a sand pot.
  4. Add the preserved duck eggs to the rice.
  5. Wearing disposable gloves, roughly crush the preserved duck eggs and mix with the rice.
  6. Add spring water to the sand pot, cover, and simmer over low heat for 40 minutes.
  7. While the rice is simmering, prepare the pork: slice thinly, then into fine strips.
  8. Marinate the pork strips with salt and cornstarch until well combined and no cornstarch is visible. Set aside for 10 minutes.
  9. Prepare the ginger and green onions: finely slice ginger and chop green onions. Set aside.
  10. After 40 minutes, open the sand pot and check the rice.
  11. Add the marinated pork and ginger to the pot. Stir well.
  12. Bring to a boil over high heat and cook for 2-3 minutes.
  13. Season with a pinch of salt and pepper.
  14. Stir in the chopped green onions.
  15. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Y9ts7qo8TkQ

pi_dan_xian_cai_tang.txt - 皮蛋苋菜汤 (Pidan Xiancai Tang)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious Pidan Xiancai Tang (皮蛋苋菜汤).
  • Master the simple and quick cooking method.
  • Understand the benefits of amaranth and preserved egg.

Ingredients

  • Fresh amaranth (苋菜): Amount not specified, enough for a serving.
  • Salt (食盐): A pinch.
  • Water (清水): Enough for soaking and cooking.
  • Preserved eggs (皮蛋): Several, choose those with a QQ texture and yolk.
  • Ginger (生姜): 1 piece, thinly sliced and finely shredded.
  • Garlic (蒜): Several cloves, minced.
  • Pork lard (猪油): 1 scoop.
  • Pepper (胡椒粉): To taste.

Instructions

  1. Remove the old roots from the amaranth, leaving only the tender parts.
  2. Place the amaranth in a large bowl, add a pinch of salt and plenty of water, soak for 10 minutes to remove insects and impurities.
  3. Rinse the amaranth thoroughly with clean water, drain, and set aside.
  4. Peel and crush the preserved eggs, set aside.
  5. Slice the ginger thinly, then shred finely. Mince the garlic.
  6. Bring plenty of water to a boil in a pot. Add the amaranth and blanch for 1 minute to remove oxalic acid. Remove with a colander.
  7. Transfer the blanched amaranth to a clay pot.
  8. Heat a wok, add pork lard. Add the preserved eggs and stir-fry until they become tiger-striped (虎皮状).
  9. Add the ginger and garlic to the wok and stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Pour in a bowl of boiling water, add salt and pepper to taste. Stir.
  11. Pour the mixture into the clay pot with the amaranth.
  12. Cover and simmer for 2-3 minutes.
  13. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=iQaqntDcb64

pig_liver.txt - Preparing Delicious Pig Liver

Objectives

  • Learn to select fresh, high-quality pig liver.
  • Master a technique to remove the pig liver's gaminess and odor.
  • Prepare tender and flavorful pig liver for a delicious meal.
  • Learn a simple recipe to make pig liver palatable for everyone.
  • Understand the importance of slow cooking and soaking for optimal texture.

Ingredients

  • Pig Liver (quantity not specified)
  • Salt (quantity not specified)
  • Water (quantity not specified)
  • White wine or rice wine (quantity not specified)
  • Minced garlic (optional, quantity not specified)
  • Sichuan peppercorns (optional, quantity not specified)
  • Light soy sauce (optional, quantity not specified)
  • Balsamic vinegar (optional, quantity not specified)

Instructions

  1. Select Fresh Pig Liver: Choose liver that is purplish-red or light red, shiny, and with a smooth, even texture. Avoid liver that is dark, black, or has lumps, nodules, or bruises.

  2. Pre-treat the Liver: Use toothpicks to make small holes across the liver's surface on both sides to help drain blood and reduce odor.

  3. Salt and Rinse: Rub salt thoroughly onto the liver, pressing firmly to draw out blood. Rinse the liver well and soak for at least 30 minutes. Rinse two more times with clean water.

  4. Boil to Remove Impurities: Place the liver in a pot, cover with water, and bring to a simmer over low heat. This slow cooking helps remove blood and impurities. Gently scrape the liver to encourage bleeding. Simmer for about 10 minutes.

  5. Second Soak: After simmering, rinse the liver and place it back in a pot with fresh cold water, adding more salt, white wine or rice wine.

  6. Simmer and Soak Again: Bring to a boil, skimming off any foam. Simmer for 10 minutes, then turn off the heat and let the liver cool naturally in the water. This longer soak helps tenderize the liver.

  7. Cool and Slice: Once cool, remove the liver, place it on a cutting board, and slice into bite-sized pieces.

  8. Optional Seasoning: For enhanced flavor, you can add minced garlic, Sichuan peppercorns, light soy sauce, and balsamic vinegar to the sliced liver.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=-Izxc4mAUQk

pinggu_chao.txt - Stir-fried Oyster Mushrooms

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare oyster mushrooms for cooking.
  • Master a simple and flavorful stir-fry recipe.
  • Expand your cooking repertoire with a new, easy dish.

Ingredients

  • 1 bunch fresh oyster mushrooms
  • 2 RMB worth of lean pork (minced)
  • Salt
  • Water
  • Small onion (chopped)
  • Ginger (minced)
  • Garlic (minced)
  • 2 green bell peppers (sliced)
  • 2 red bell peppers (sliced)
  • 2 garlic chives (chopped)
  • 1 tbsp yellow bean sauce
  • 1 tsp chicken bouillon
  • Soy sauce (light)
  • Dark soy sauce (for color)
  • Sesame oil
  • Sugar
  • Cooking oil
  • Peppercorns

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Mushrooms: Trim the roots of the oyster mushrooms and separate them into smaller pieces. Tear larger pieces in half. Wash thoroughly with salted water to remove any impurities. Drain well.
  2. Prepare the Pork: Cut lean pork into thin slices, then mince. Do not mince too finely; some texture is desirable.
  3. Prepare Aromatics: Finely chop the small onion, mince the ginger, and mince the garlic. Slice the green and red bell peppers thinly. Chop the garlic chives.
  4. Blanch Mushrooms: Bring water to a boil. Add the oyster mushrooms and a tablespoon of sugar. Blanch for about 1 minute. Remove and drain.
  5. Stir-fry Aromatics and Pork: Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan. Add the onion, ginger, garlic, and peppercorns. Stir-fry until fragrant. Add the minced pork and stir-fry until the color changes.
  6. Add Seasoning: Add the yellow bean sauce, a pinch of salt, chicken bouillon, and light soy sauce. Stir well to combine and dissolve the seasonings.
  7. Add Mushrooms: Add the blanched oyster mushrooms and stir-fry until well coated with the sauce.
  8. Add Peppers: Add the sliced green and red bell peppers. Add dark soy sauce for color and a drizzle of sesame oil. Stir-fry until the peppers are tender-crisp.
  9. Add Garlic Chives: Add the chopped garlic chives. Add a little water starch to make the sauce more glossy. Stir-fry for about 20 seconds until the garlic chives are wilted.
  10. Serve: Remove from heat and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=5Mcc6h64tdc

pork_belly_umeboshi_vegetables_stew.txt - Pork Belly with Umeboshi and Vegetables Stew Nilagang Baboy na may Umeboshi at Gulay

Objectives

  • Learn to make a flavorful and easy pork belly stew with umeboshi plums and vegetables.
  • Master the technique of preparing pork belly for optimal taste and texture.
  • Understand the importance of balancing flavors and cooking times for a delicious stew.

Ingredients

  • 1 kg pork belly (choose one with skin)
  • 150g dried plum (umeboshi), clean and sand-free
  • Several scallions (green onions)
  • Several pieces of ginger
  • 1 bunch garlic sprouts
  • 1 piece star anise (八角 - bā jiǎo)
  • 2 bay leaves (香葉 - xiāng yè)
  • 1 small piece of cinnamon (肉桂 - ròu guì)
  • A handful of dried Sichuan peppercorns (花椒 - huā jiāo)
  • A handful of rock sugar (冰糖 - bīng táng)
  • Cooking oil
  • Salt
  • Light soy sauce (生抽 - shēng chōu)
  • Dark soy sauce (老抽 - lǎo chōu)
  • Water

Instructions

  1. Soak the dried plums in water for 30 minutes.
  2. Clean the pork belly skin by scrubbing with a knife after briefly boiling and rinsing it.
  3. Cut the pork belly into large pieces.
  4. Prepare the aromatics: thinly slice the scallions and ginger, and cut the garlic sprouts at a 45-degree angle.
  5. Rinse the soaked plums twice and drain.
  6. Heat oil in a pot and fry the pork belly over medium heat for about 3 minutes until the skin is slightly browned.
  7. Remove excess oil from the pot.
  8. Add the ginger and scallions to the pot and stir-fry briefly until fragrant.
  9. Add the peppercorns, star anise, bay leaves, cinnamon, and rock sugar. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Season with salt, light soy sauce, and dark soy sauce. Stir well.
  11. Add enough boiling water to cover the pork belly. Bring to a boil, then skim off any scum.
  12. Reduce heat, cover, and simmer for 40 minutes.
  13. Add the plums and stir to combine. Cover and simmer for another 15 minutes, stirring occasionally to prevent sticking.
  14. Turn the heat to high and reduce the sauce.
  15. Add the garlic sprouts, stir-fry briefly, and turn off the heat.
  16. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QXtP49yWAwM

pork_belly_with_umeboshi_and_vegetables.txt - Pork Belly with Umeboshi and Vegetables

Objectives

  • Learn to make a flavorful and easy pork belly stew with dried plums and vegetables.
  • Master a simple method for preparing tender and delicious pork belly.
  • Understand how to enhance the dish's aroma and taste through proper cooking techniques.

Ingredients

  • 1 kg pork belly (choose one with skin)
  • 150g dried plums (umeboshi), clean and sand-free, soaked in water for 30 minutes
  • Several scallions (green onions)
  • Several pieces of ginger, bruised
  • Several garlic sprouts, sliced at a 45-degree angle
  • 1 star anise
  • 2 bay leaves
  • A small piece of cinnamon
  • A handful of dried Sichuan peppercorns
  • A handful of rock sugar
  • Salt
  • Light soy sauce
  • Dark soy sauce
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Prepare the pork belly: Blanch the pork belly skin to remove any hair or strong smell. Scrub the skin clean with a knife, then cut into large pieces.
  2. Prepare aromatics: Prepare the scallions, ginger (bruise it), and garlic sprouts (slice at a 45-degree angle).
  3. Prepare the plums: Soak the dried plums in water for 30 minutes, then drain and rinse twice.
  4. Fry the pork belly: Heat oil in a pot, add the pork belly pieces and fry over medium heat for about 3 minutes until the skin is slightly browned. Remove excess oil.
  5. Sauté aromatics: Add the bruised ginger and scallions to the pot and stir-fry briefly until fragrant.
  6. Add spices: Add the peppercorns, star anise, bay leaves, cinnamon, and rock sugar. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  7. Season: Add salt, light soy sauce, and dark soy sauce. Stir to combine.
  8. Add water and simmer: Add enough boiling water to cover the pork belly. Bring to a boil, then skim off any scum. Reduce heat, cover, and simmer for 40 minutes.
  9. Add plums: Add the soaked and rinsed plums. Stir gently and let them absorb the flavors of the pork belly. Cover and simmer for another 15 minutes on low heat, stirring occasionally to prevent sticking.
  10. Finish: Turn the heat to high and let the sauce thicken slightly. Add the garlic sprouts, stir-fry briefly, and turn off the heat.
  11. Serve: Remove the pork belly and serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QXtP49yWAwM

pork_liver_stir_fry.txt - Stir-fried Willow Leaf Pork Liver

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare and clean willow leaf pork liver for stir-frying.
  • Master a flavorful stir-fry recipe using readily available ingredients.
  • Achieve tender and fragrant pork liver with a simple, step-by-step method.

Ingredients

  • Willow leaf pork liver (choose pink, not dark or mottled)
  • Water
  • 1 tbsp table salt
  • Pepper
  • 1 tbsp Hunan Long brand soy sauce
  • Garlic cloves, minced
  • Garlic leaves, minced
  • Millet peppers, minced (or red peppers if you prefer less spice)
  • Ginger, minced
  • Rapeseed oil (or peanut oil)
  • Dried chili peppers
  • Matsutake mushrooms (optional)
  • Light soy sauce

Instructions

  1. Clean the Pork Liver: Cut the pork liver in half, then into willow leaf-shaped slices (or smaller pieces if your knife skills are not sharp). Place in a large bowl, add water, and use your hands to mix and rinse, removing blood clots. Rinse repeatedly until the water runs clear. Drain well.

  2. Prepare Aromatics: Mince garlic cloves and leaves, millet peppers (or other peppers), and ginger. Set aside.

  3. Marinate the Liver: In a large bowl, add the drained pork liver, salt, pepper, and soy sauce. Mix thoroughly, ensuring the liver is evenly coated. Marinate for 15 minutes.

  4. Stir-fry Aromatics: Heat rapeseed oil in a wok or large pan until slightly smoking. Add dried chili peppers and stir-fry until fragrant. Remove the chilies.

  5. Stir-fry the Liver: Add the marinated pork liver to the hot oil and stir-fry for 15 seconds over high heat (or 30 seconds if using a smaller burner).

  6. Add Aromatics and Mushrooms: Add the minced ginger, garlic, and millet peppers to the wok. Stir-fry until fragrant. Add the stir-fried pork liver and matsutake mushrooms (if using).

  7. Finish the Dish: Add light soy sauce and stir-fry until the sauce is evenly distributed and the liver is cooked through and tender. Add garlic sprouts and stir-fry until wilted.

  8. Serve: Serve immediately. The dish should be fragrant and the liver tender.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=RDgctDNFll8

pork_liver.txt - Delicious Pork Liver

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare fresh pork liver to remove impurities and reduce odor.
  • Master a cooking method to achieve tender and flavorful pork liver.
  • Learn to make a delicious dipping sauce to enhance the taste.

Ingredients

  • Pork liver (quantity not specified)
  • Salt (quantity not specified)
  • Water (quantity not specified)
  • White wine or rice wine (quantity not specified)
  • Chopped garlic (optional, quantity not specified)
  • Millet pepper (optional, quantity not specified)
  • Light soy sauce (optional, quantity not specified)
  • Balsamic vinegar (optional, quantity not specified)

Instructions

  1. Select Fresh Liver: Choose pork liver that is purplish-red or light red, shiny, and with a uniform, smooth texture, free of lumps or bruises.

  2. Pre-treat the Liver: Use 4-5 toothpicks to create small holes in the liver on both sides to drain blood and reduce odor.

  3. Salt and Massage: Rub salt evenly onto the liver, pressing firmly to help drain blood. Let it sit for at least 30 minutes.

  4. Rinse and Boil: Rinse the liver thoroughly. Place it in a pot, cover with water, and bring to a low simmer. Use your hands to gently scrape the liver to help release blood. Simmer for about 10 minutes.

  5. Second Boil: Rinse the liver again. Place it in a fresh pot of cold water, adding more salt and white wine or rice wine. Bring to a boil, skimming off any foam. Simmer for 10 minutes. Turn off the heat and let it cool naturally.

  6. Cool and Slice: Once cooled, remove the liver, place it on a cutting board, and slice it into bite-sized pieces.

  7. Prepare Dipping Sauce (Optional): Mix chopped garlic, millet pepper, light soy sauce, and balsamic vinegar for a dipping sauce.

  8. Serve: Serve the sliced liver with the optional dipping sauce.

pork_meatball.txt - 猪肉丸

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious, homemade pork meatballs.
  • Understand the importance of meat selection and preparation for optimal texture.
  • Master the technique of making bouncy and flavorful pork meatballs.
  • Learn how to store the meatballs for future use.

Ingredients

  • 3.5斤猪后腿肉 (Approximately 2100g pork leg meat)
  • 15克食用小苏打 (15g baking soda)
  • 15克盐 (15g salt)
  • 3克白糖 (3g sugar)
  • 50克木薯淀粉 (50g tapioca starch)
  • 适量蒜酥 (Appropriate amount of garlic crisp)
  • 200克左右肥肉 (Approximately 200g pork fat)
  • 冰块 (Ice cubes)

Instructions

  1. Separate lean and fatty pork. Remove the skin from the fatty pork.
  2. Cut the lean pork into thick slices, then into strips. Remove all the sinew.
  3. Cut the fatty pork into thin slices.
  4. Spread the cut pork (lean and fat) on a plate and freeze for 2 hours.
  5. Grind the frozen pork with ice cubes in batches in a meat grinder, adding baking soda, salt, sugar, tapioca starch, and garlic crisp. Add ice cubes in three batches to maintain a low temperature. The ratio of lean to fat is approximately 800g:200g.
  6. After grinding, continuously stir the meat mixture in one direction for several minutes until it becomes sticky and doesn't fall off the spatula.
  7. Squeeze the meat mixture into meatballs and place them in cold water. The meatballs should float if properly made.
  8. Cook the meatballs in a pot of water over low heat for about 20 minutes, or until they turn white.
  9. Transfer the cooked meatballs to a bowl of ice water for 10 minutes to make them more bouncy.
  10. Store the meatballs in a sealed bag in the refrigerator for up to a month.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=CGLQwxlw-Rc

pork_mushroom_stir_fry.txt - 猪肉口蘑炒

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy pork and mushroom stir-fry.
  • Master the technique of tenderizing pork and enhancing the flavor of mushrooms.
  • Create a flavorful dish with minimal oil and seasonings.

Ingredients

  • 猪后腿肉 (Zhū hòutuǐ ròu) - Pork hind leg meat: amount as needed, cut into thumb-sized pieces
  • 葱 (Cōng) - Scallions: a small amount, thinly sliced
  • 姜 (Jiāng) - Ginger: a small amount, thinly sliced
  • 生抽 (Shēng chōu) - Light soy sauce: a small amount
  • 蚝油 (Háoyóu) - Oyster sauce: a small amount
  • 胡椒粉 (Hújiāofěn) - Pepper powder: a small amount
  • 蛋清 (Dàn qīng) - Egg white: 1
  • 红薯淀粉 (Hóngshǔ diànfěn) - Sweet potato starch: amount as needed
  • 口蘑 (Kǒumó) - Mushrooms: amount as needed, stems removed and cut into small squares
  • 蒜 (Suàn) - Garlic: a large amount, minced
  • 食用油 (Shíyòng yóu) - Cooking oil: amount as needed
  • 花生油 (Huāshēng yóu) - Peanut oil: a small amount
  • 水淀粉 (Shuǐ diànfěn) - Water starch: a small amount

Instructions

  1. Cut pork hind leg meat into thumb-sized pieces.
  2. In a bowl, mix the pork with sliced scallions, ginger, light soy sauce, oyster sauce, and pepper powder. Mix thoroughly.
  3. Add salt and water to the pork mixture, and mix well to absorb the water.
  4. Add egg white and mix well.
  5. Add sweet potato starch and mix until each piece of pork is coated.
  6. Marinate for 20 minutes.
  7. Clean and trim the stems of the mushrooms. Cut into small squares.
  8. Mince garlic.
  9. Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan. Add the marinated pork and cook over low heat until browned and fragrant (2-3 minutes). Remove and set aside.
  10. Add mushrooms to the pan and stir-fry until slightly softened and moisture is released. You can cover the pan to steam for 1-2 minutes. Remove and set aside.
  11. Wash the pan and add a small amount of peanut oil. Add minced garlic and sauté until golden brown (1-2 minutes).
  12. Return the pork and mushrooms to the pan. Stir-fry to combine.
  13. Season with pepper, light soy sauce, and water starch. Stir-fry until the sauce thickens and coats the ingredients.
  14. Stir-fry for another 30 seconds and serve immediately.

pork_rib_radish_soup.txt - Pork Rib and Radish Soup

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and warming pork rib and radish soup.
  • Master the technique of preparing pork ribs for tender and flavorful soup.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients to create a hearty and healthy meal.

Ingredients

  • Pork ribs (approx. 1 lb)
  • 30 grams flour
  • 1 piece ginger (sliced)
  • Green onions (chopped, amount to taste)
  • Cooking wine (amount to taste)
  • Rice vinegar (small amount)
  • Water (enough to cover ribs)
  • White radish (1-2, amount to taste)
  • Salt (to taste)

Instructions

  1. Rinse pork ribs and soak in water for 1 hour to remove blood and impurities.
  2. Drain water, add flour to the ribs and rub thoroughly. Rinse twice more until water runs clear. Pat dry.
  3. Mince ginger and chop green onions.
  4. Heat oil in a pot and add pork ribs. Stir-fry until lightly browned.
  5. Add cooking wine to remove any odor. Stir-fry for a few more minutes.
  6. Add enough boiling water to cover the ribs. Bring to a boil, then skim off any foam or grease.
  7. Add rice vinegar. Add ginger and green onions.
  8. Cover and simmer over low heat for 30 minutes.
  9. While the ribs simmer, prepare the radish: Wash and cut into chunks. Chop more green onions.
  10. After 30 minutes, add the radish chunks to the soup. Stir gently.
  11. Cover and simmer over medium-low heat for another 20 minutes.
  12. Season with salt to taste.
  13. Check tenderness of ribs and radish with chopsticks.
  14. Garnish with chopped green onions.
  15. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=UEgbSLvg0Wo

pork_rib_soup.txt - لحم ضلع الخنزير الحساء

Objectives

  • Prepare flavorful pork rib soup.
  • Clean and prepare pork ribs properly.
  • Incorporate various vegetables for a nutritious soup.
  • Achieve a rich, aromatic, and tender soup.
  • Cook a balanced and healthy meal for the family.

Ingredients

  • Pork ribs (quantity not specified)
  • Corn (quantity not specified)
  • Yam (quantity not specified)
  • Radish (quantity not specified)
  • Ginger (one piece)
  • Green onions (one bunch)
  • Salt (small amount)
  • Cornstarch (small amount)
  • Water (sufficient amount)
  • Pepper (to taste)

Instructions

  1. Rinse pork ribs thoroughly under running water.
  2. Add a small amount of salt and cornstarch to the ribs, and gently rub to remove blood and impurities.
  3. Rinse the ribs again with warm water until the water runs clear.
  4. Drain the ribs well. Do not boil them to preserve nutrients and flavor.
  5. While waiting, prepare the vegetables: chop corn, yam, and radish into bite-sized pieces.
  6. Peel and slice ginger into thicker pieces.
  7. Tie a knot with the green onions.
  8. Add the ribs to a pot and stir-fry until lightly browned. This enhances the flavor and aroma.
  9. Add sliced ginger and green onions; continue stir-frying until fragrant.
  10. Pour in enough boiling water to cover the ribs.
  11. Bring to a boil, then skim off any foam or impurities.
  12. Cover the pot and simmer over low heat for 35 minutes.
  13. Add corn and carrots to the pot. Simmer for 10 minutes.
  14. Add yam and radish; continue simmering for another 10 minutes.
  15. Add pepper and salt to taste.
  16. Add green onions and serve.

pork_ribs_radish_soup.txt - Pork Ribs and Radish Soup

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and warming pork rib soup.
  • Master a technique for tenderizing pork ribs.
  • Prepare flavorful and nutritious side dishes to complement the soup.

Ingredients

  • Pork ribs (approximately 12 yuan/pound)
  • 30 grams of flour
  • Green onions
  • Ginger
  • Cooking oil
  • Cooking wine
  • Rice vinegar
  • Homegrown white radish
  • Carrots (optional)

Instructions

  1. Rinse the pork ribs under running water.
  2. Soak the ribs in water for an hour to remove blood and impurities.
  3. Drain the water, add 30 grams of flour to the ribs, and mix thoroughly to absorb remaining impurities.
  4. Rinse the ribs twice more with clean water until the water runs clear.
  5. Pat the ribs dry.
  6. Mince ginger and chop green onions.
  7. Heat oil in a pot.
  8. Add the ribs and stir-fry until lightly browned.
  9. Add cooking wine to remove any gamey smell.
  10. Add enough boiling water to cover the ribs.
  11. Skim off any foam or grease from the surface.
  12. Add a small amount of rice vinegar to help release nutrients from the bones.
  13. Add minced ginger and green onions.
  14. Cover the pot, reduce heat, and simmer for 30 minutes.
  15. While the ribs simmer, prepare the side dishes: wash and roughly chop the white radish and carrots (if using).
  16. After 30 minutes, add the chopped radish to the soup.
  17. Stir and cover the pot again.
  18. Increase heat to medium and simmer for another 20 minutes.
  19. Season with salt to taste.
  20. Add chopped green onions for garnish.
  21. Serve hot.

pork_ribs_soup.txt - لحم ضلع الخنزير الحساء

Objectives

  • Prepare delicious and nutritious pork rib soup.
  • Learn to properly clean and prepare pork ribs.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful recipe suitable for families.
  • Utilize readily available vegetables for a balanced meal.
  • Create a visually appealing and aromatic soup.

Ingredients

  • Pork ribs (quantity not specified)
  • Salt (a small teaspoon)
  • Cornstarch (a small amount)
  • Water (enough to cover ribs)
  • Carrots (quantity not specified)
  • Corn (quantity not specified)
  • Yam (quantity not specified)
  • Radish (quantity not specified)
  • Ginger (one piece)
  • Green onions (a bunch)
  • Pepper (to taste)

Instructions

  1. Wash pork ribs thoroughly: Place ribs in a basin, add a small teaspoon of salt and some cornstarch. Gently rub to remove blood, water, and impurities. Rinse with warm water for about two minutes until the water runs clear. Drain well. Do not boil the ribs.
  2. Prepare vegetables: Chop carrots, corn, yam, and radish into bite-sized pieces. Peel and slice ginger into thicker pieces. Tie a knot in a bunch of green onions.
  3. Sauté ribs: Add ribs to a pot and sauté until lightly browned. This enhances flavor and removes excess water.
  4. Add aromatics: Add sliced ginger and green onions to the pot and continue sautéing until fragrant.
  5. Add water and simmer: Pour in enough boiling water to cover the ribs. Bring to a boil, then reduce heat, cover, and simmer for 35 minutes. Remove excess fat from the surface.
  6. Add vegetables (first batch): Add carrots and corn to the pot. Cover and simmer over low heat for 20 minutes.
  7. Add remaining vegetables: Add yam and radish. Cover and simmer for another 20 minutes.
  8. Season and garnish: Add pepper and salt to taste. Stir in some berries (type unspecified) and sprinkle with chopped green onions.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=br5jRi1oh9o

pork_ribs_with_sour_cabbage.txt - 排骨炖酸菜

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and nutritious pork ribs with sour cabbage stew.
  • Master the technique of preparing and cleaning pork ribs for optimal flavor.
  • Create a flavorful and aromatic stew perfect for cold weather.

Ingredients

  • 1 large piece of pork ribs (about 100 yuan worth)
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • Water for soaking and cooking
  • Homemade sour cabbage (or store-bought, rinsed well)
  • 1-2芋头 (Taro)
  • 1 tablespoon cooking oil
  • Several pieces of ginger
  • Several dried chilies
  • A little soy sauce (老抽)
  • Half a spoonful of yellow soybean paste (黄豆酱)
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Garlic (蒜末)
  • Green onion (葱花)
  • Flour (面粉)

Instructions

  1. Chop the pork ribs into small pieces.
  2. Place the ribs in a bowl, add salt and plenty of water, mix well, and soak for 15 minutes.
  3. Clean the sour cabbage thoroughly and cut into small pieces.
  4. Peel and cut the taro into large chunks.
  5. Drain the soaked pork ribs.
  6. Add flour to the ribs and mix thoroughly until sticky.
  7. Wash the ribs with water to remove impurities.
  8. Rinse the ribs thoroughly until the water runs clear.
  9. Drain the ribs again.
  10. Add the ribs to a pot with ginger slices and water.
  11. Bring to a boil, skimming off any foam.
  12. Remove the blanched ribs and set aside.
  13. Heat oil in a pan, add taro and fry for 2-3 minutes until golden brown. Set aside.
  14. Add ginger and chilies to the same pan, stir-fry.
  15. Add sour cabbage and stir-fry until moisture evaporates. Set aside.
  16. Add oil to a clean pot, add the ribs and pan-fry until golden brown on both sides.
  17. Add boiling water to the pot, cover, and simmer for 20 minutes.
  18. Add salt, pepper, soy sauce, and yellow soybean paste. Stir well.
  19. Add the fried sour cabbage and taro. Stir to combine.
  20. Cover and simmer for another 10 minutes.
  21. Open the lid, and if necessary, simmer uncovered to reduce the sauce.
  22. Check if the taro is cooked through.
  23. Garnish with garlic and green onions.
  24. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=3YuHIxsd2K4

pork_rind_jelly.txt - Pork Rind Jelly (Halaya ng Balat ng Baboy)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and crystal-clear pork rind jelly.
  • Master the cleaning and preparation techniques for pork skin.
  • Create a flavorful and versatile dipping sauce to complement the jelly.

Ingredients

  • Pork skin (amount not specified)
  • Ginger (amount not specified)
  • Cooking wine (small amount)
  • Spring water (enough to cover ingredients)
  • Salt (1 tablespoon + small amount)
  • Onion (amount not specified)
  • Garlic (amount not specified)
  • Pepper (amount not specified)
  • Scallions (amount not specified)
  • Light soy sauce (amount not specified)
  • Vinegar (1 tablespoon)
  • Sesame oil (optional, amount not specified)
  • Chili oil (optional, amount not specified)

Instructions

  1. Wash the pork skin thoroughly with lukewarm water to remove dirt and blood. Clean the hair off completely.
  2. In a pot, add the cleaned pork skin, sliced ginger, cooking wine, and enough spring water to cover. Bring to a boil over high heat.
  3. Once boiling, reduce heat and simmer for 7-8 minutes, skimming off any foam that forms. The skin should be slightly softened.
  4. Remove the pork skin from the pot, let it cool, and then place it on a chopping board.
  5. Using a knife, carefully shave off any excess fat from the pork skin.
  6. Cut the pork skin into pieces of any size.
  7. Place the cut pork skin in a large bowl, add 1 tablespoon of salt, and rub it thoroughly with clean hands to remove any lingering odor.
  8. Rinse the pork skin with lukewarm water several times, then rinse with running water until the water runs clear.
  9. Prepare a large pot. Add the cleaned pork skin, onion, and ginger.
  10. Add boiling water (3.5 times the volume of the pork skin). Bring to a boil, then reduce heat and simmer for 5 minutes, skimming off any foam.
  11. After 5 minutes, remove the ginger and green onions (optional). Add a small amount of salt, stir well, and reduce heat to low.
  12. Simmer for 20 minutes, or until the broth is cloudy and the pork skin is cooked through.
  13. Pour the hot mixture into a prepared mold and let it cool naturally. Remove any bubbles.
  14. To make the dipping sauce: In a small bowl, combine minced garlic, pepper, scallions, light soy sauce, vinegar, sesame oil (optional), and chili oil (optional). Mix well.
  15. Once the pork rind jelly has cooled and set, unmold it, slice, and serve with the dipping sauce.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=5QZ0YlsnFhU

pork_stir_fry_with_garlic_sprouts.txt - لحم الخنزير المقلي مع براعم الثوم

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare delicious pork stir-fry with garlic sprouts.
  • Master the technique of blanching garlic sprouts to maintain their green color.
  • Create a flavorful dish using readily available ingredients.

Ingredients

  • Garlic sprouts (amount not specified, but enough for a serving)
  • Pork tenderloin (amount not specified)
  • Mushrooms (amount not specified)
  • Green onions (amount not specified)
  • Pickled chili peppers (amount not specified, can substitute with red pepper)
  • 1 tbsp salt
  • 1/2 egg white
  • 1 tsp cornstarch
  • Light soy sauce (amount not specified)
  • Cooking oil (amount not specified)

Instructions

  1. Prepare Garlic Sprouts: Remove old parts of garlic sprouts. Wash thoroughly, drain, and chop into 3cm pieces. Place in a bowl, add 1 tbsp salt, and mix well. Let it sit for 10 minutes.
  2. Prepare Vegetables: Wash and trim mushrooms, then slice thickly. Chop green onions finely. Slice pickled chili peppers thinly (or use red pepper).
  3. Prepare Pork: Slice pork tenderloin thinly, then cut into small pieces. Place in a bowl.
  4. Marinate Pork: Add 1/2 egg white, 1 tsp cornstarch, and light soy sauce to the pork. Mix well with clean hands until the pork absorbs the marinade. Let it sit for 5 minutes.
  5. Blanch Garlic Sprouts: Drain the salted garlic sprouts. Add some cooking oil and toss with chopsticks. Steam for 2 minutes until bright green. Set aside.
  6. Blanch Mushrooms: Blanch mushrooms for 1 minute to remove oxalic acid. Drain well.
  7. Stir-fry Pork: Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan. Add pork and stir-fry over medium-low heat until cooked through.
  8. Add Vegetables: Add blanched mushrooms, green onions, and chili peppers to the pork. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Combine and Season: Add the blanched garlic sprouts to the pork and vegetables. Season with salt and light soy sauce. Stir-fry over high heat for 1 minute, until fragrant.
  10. Serve: Drizzle with a little light sauce before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=zwbOF0w7zZA

potato_balls.txt - Crispy Potato and Carrot Balls

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and healthy potato and carrot balls.
  • Master the technique of double-frying for extra crispy exterior.
  • Create a fun and appealing vegetable dish for children.

Ingredients

  • 1 large potato (about the size of the palm)
  • ½ medium carrot
  • Salt (to taste)
  • Five-spice powder (to taste)
  • 2-3 green onions, chopped
  • 1 egg
  • Starch (適量, to taste)
  • Flour (適量, to taste)
  • Cooking oil (for frying)

Instructions

  1. Peel and grate the potato and carrot into thin strips using a grater.
  2. In a bowl, combine the shredded potato and carrot, add salt, mix well, and marinate for 10 minutes.
  3. Add five-spice powder and chopped green onions to the marinated vegetables.
  4. Crack an egg into the mixture.
  5. Add starch and flour to bind the mixture (adjust amount as needed).
  6. Mix everything thoroughly with chopsticks.
  7. Take small handfuls of the mixture and roll them into balls (don't worry about making them perfectly round).
  8. Heat a generous amount of cooking oil in a pan until it's about 50% hot (chopsticks inserted should produce small bubbles).
  9. Carefully add the potato balls to the hot oil and fry until they are set.
  10. Stir the balls occasionally with chopsticks to ensure even cooking.
  11. Once the balls are lightly golden, remove them from the pan using a slotted spoon and set aside.
  12. Increase the oil temperature to about 80% hot.
  13. Return the potato balls to the hot oil and fry for 40-49 seconds until golden brown and crispy.
  14. Remove the potato balls from the oil, drain on a paper towel to remove excess oil.
  15. Serve the crispy potato and carrot balls immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Uhr3jkNfq1A

potato_egg_cake.txt - 土豆鸡蛋饼 (Tǔdòu jīdàn bǐng)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a crispy and flavorful potato and egg cake.
  • Master a simple and quick recipe suitable for both adults and children.
  • Understand the importance of properly preparing and mixing ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 1 large potato (土豆 - tǔdòu), peeled and shredded
  • 1/2 carrot (胡萝卜 - húluóbo), peeled and shredded
  • 4 eggs (鸡蛋 - jīdàn)
  • 1 tablespoon salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • 1 tablespoon pepper salt (椒盐粉 - jiāo yán fěn)
  • Black sesame seeds (黑芝麻 - hēi zhīma) for garnish
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòng yóu)

Instructions

  1. Peel and shred one large potato and half a carrot.
  2. Mix the shredded potato and carrot with 1 tablespoon of salt and let it sit for 10 minutes.
  3. In a separate bowl, whisk 4 eggs with 1 tablespoon of salt and 1 tablespoon of pepper salt.
  4. After 10 minutes, squeeze out excess water from the potato and carrot mixture.
  5. Add the potato and carrot mixture to the egg mixture and stir until well combined and slightly stringy.
  6. Preheat an electric griddle and brush it with cooking oil.
  7. Pour the batter onto the preheated griddle and spread evenly.
  8. Sprinkle black sesame seeds on top for garnish.
  9. Close the lid and cook for 3 minutes per side, or until golden brown and crispy.
  10. Remove from the griddle, let it cool slightly, then cut into smaller pieces for serving.

potato_nest.txt - Potato Nest

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and visually appealing potato nests.
  • Master the technique of making potato dough and shaping it into nests.
  • Create a flavorful and savory filling for the potato nests.

Ingredients

  • 2 medium potatoes
  • Ginger (amount unspecified)
  • Garlic (amount unspecified)
  • 3 millet peppers
  • Spring onions (amount unspecified)
  • Lean meat (amount unspecified)
  • Potato starch or cornstarch or tapioca starch (amount unspecified)
  • Cooking wine (amount unspecified)
  • Bean paste (1 tablespoon)
  • Salt (a pinch)
  • Oyster sauce (a small amount)
  • Light soy sauce (a small amount)
  • Sesame oil (a small amount)
  • Cooking oil (amount unspecified)

Instructions

  1. Peel and thinly slice two potatoes.
  2. Boil the sliced potatoes in water for 20 minutes.
  3. While the potatoes are boiling, prepare the other ingredients:
    • Mince ginger and garlic.
    • Thinly slice millet peppers.
    • Chop spring onions (separate white and green parts).
    • Dice lean meat.
  4. Once the potatoes are cooked, mash them until smooth.
  5. Gradually add potato starch (or cornstarch/tapioca starch) to the mashed potatoes and mix until a dough forms.
  6. Knead the dough until smooth.
  7. Roll small portions of the dough into balls, then press a small dimple into the center of each ball to create a nest shape.
  8. Set aside the potato nests.
  9. Heat cooking oil in a pan. Add diced meat and stir-fry until browned.
  10. Add cooking wine to remove any fishy smell.
  11. Add minced ginger, garlic, and sliced millet peppers to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant.
  12. Add bean paste, a pinch of salt, oyster sauce, and a small amount of light soy sauce. Stir well.
  13. Add a tablespoon of boiling water and bring to a simmer.
  14. Add the potato nests to the pan and stir gently to coat them in the sauce.
  15. Simmer for 3-5 minutes, stirring occasionally to prevent sticking.
  16. Before serving, drizzle with sesame oil and garnish with chopped green onions.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=q8yuYNLmA6g

potato_onion_pancakes.txt - Potato and Onion Pancakes (فطائر البطاطس المصنوعة من البصل)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and nutritious potato and onion pancakes.
  • Master a quick and easy recipe perfect for a busy day.
  • Understand the benefits of using purple onions.

Ingredients

  • 2 potatoes (yellow hearts, قلوب صفراء)
  • 3 small onions (smaller, أصغر)
  • Salt (ملح)
  • Water (ماء)
  • 3 eggs (بيض)
  • Green and red pepper (فلفل أخضر وأحمر)
  • Flour (طحين) - approximately 150 grams (150 جرام)
  • Cooking oil (زيت الطهي)
  • Black sesame seeds (سمسم أسود)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the potatoes: Peel and slice the potatoes into even pieces. Soak sliced potatoes in clean water to remove starch and prevent browning. Drain well.
  2. Prepare the onions: Finely slice the purple onions. (Note: Purple onions are recommended for their health benefits.)
  3. Prepare the peppers: Halve the green and red peppers, remove seeds, and thinly slice.
  4. Prepare the egg batter: Whisk 3 eggs in a bowl until well combined and frothy.
  5. Combine ingredients: Add the drained potatoes, sliced onions, and peppers to the egg batter. Season with salt.
  6. Add flour: Gradually add approximately 150 grams of flour, mixing well to avoid lumps. The batter should be thick.
  7. Cook the pancakes: Heat a lightly oiled electric pan on medium heat. Pour a thin layer of batter onto the hot pan.
  8. Sprinkle with sesame seeds: Sprinkle black sesame seeds over the pancake.
  9. Cook the first side: Cover and cook for 3 minutes.
  10. Flip and cook the second side: Open the lid, brush with a little oil, reduce heat to low, and cook for another 2 minutes. Flip and cook for an additional 5 minutes until golden brown on both sides.
  11. Serve: Once cooked, cut into desired pieces and serve immediately. Enjoy with porridge or soy milk.

potato_onion_pancake.txt - Potato and Onion Pancakes

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and nutritious potato and onion pancakes.
  • Master a quick and easy recipe perfect for a busy day.
  • Understand the benefits of using purple onion and the preparation techniques for optimal flavor and texture.

Ingredients

  • 2 potatoes (yellow hearts preferred)
  • 3 small purple onions
  • 3 eggs
  • 1 green chili pepper
  • 1 red chili pepper
  • 150g all-purpose flour
  • Salt
  • Water
  • Cooking oil
  • Black sesame seeds

Instructions

  1. Prepare the potatoes: Peel and slice the potatoes evenly. Place in clean water to remove starch and prevent browning. Drain well and set aside.
  2. Prepare the onions: Cut the purple onions into thin slices. (Note: The video highlights the health benefits of purple onions).
  3. Prepare the chilies: Halve the green and red chilies, remove seeds, and slice thinly.
  4. Prepare the egg batter: Whisk 3 eggs with a little salt until fully combined and smooth.
  5. Combine ingredients: Gently squeeze excess water from the potatoes. Add the potatoes, sliced onions, egg batter, and chilies to a bowl.
  6. Add flour: Gradually add 150g of flour, mixing well to avoid lumps. The batter should be thick.
  7. Cook the pancakes: Heat a little oil in an electric pan over medium heat. Pour a thin layer of batter onto the hot pan.
  8. Sprinkle with sesame seeds: Sprinkle black sesame seeds on top of the pancake.
  9. Cook and flip: Cover and cook for 3 minutes. Open the lid, brush with a little oil, reduce heat, and cook for another 2 minutes. Flip and cook for another 5 minutes until golden brown on both sides.
  10. Serve: Once cooked, cut into desired pieces and serve immediately. Enjoy with porridge or soy milk (optional).

potato_orchid_noodles.txt - Potato Orchid Noodles

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and healthy potato orchid noodles.
  • Master the steaming technique for potatoes and broccoli.
  • Prepare a flavorful sauce to complement the noodles.

Ingredients

  • 3 small potatoes
  • 1 head of broccoli
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • A few drops white vinegar
  • Water (for steaming and soaking)
  • A handful of garlic
  • 2 scallions
  • 2 fresh red chilies
  • White sesame seeds
  • Hot oil (for aroma)
  • 1 tablespoon light soy sauce
  • Vinegar (for sauce)
  • Pepper oil (for sauce)
  • Tapioca starch (or cornstarch/potato starch)
  • Mushroom powder or shrimp shell powder (optional)
  • 0.1g edible alkali (optional)

Instructions

  1. Peel and thinly slice the potatoes. Arrange on a plate and gently flatten with your hands. Steam for 15 minutes.
  2. Soak broccoli in salted water with a few drops of white vinegar for 5 minutes to remove insects and impurities.
  3. While steaming, prepare the sauce ingredients: mince garlic and scallions, dice red chilies, and add white sesame seeds. Heat oil and pour over the mixture for aroma. Add soy sauce, vinegar, and pepper oil; mix well.
  4. Cut the broccoli into florets and rinse twice.
  5. After steaming, mash the potatoes with chopsticks until smooth.
  6. Season the mashed potatoes: add salt, mushroom powder (or shrimp shell powder), minced broccoli, and edible alkali (optional). Mix well.
  7. Gradually add tapioca starch, mixing continuously with chopsticks, until a smooth, medium-firm dough forms.
  8. Knead the dough until smooth and elastic.
  9. Sprinkle tapioca starch on a cutting board. Roll out the dough into long strips, then cut into thin slices. Sprinkle with more tapioca starch to prevent sticking.
  10. Boil water. Add the potato noodles and cook for 2 minutes. Add more water and cook until tender. Remove with a slotted spoon. Cool and rinse with cold water (add ice cubes in summer).
  11. Place the cooked noodles in a bowl. Pour the prepared sauce over the noodles and toss to coat. Serve immediately. Optional: fry with mushrooms or shredded pork.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kbAndYSktOg

potato_pancake.txt - 土豆丝煎饼 (Tǔdòusī Jiānbǐng)

Objectives

  • Learn a simple method to make delicious potato pancakes.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients for a quick and easy recipe.
  • Achieve a crispy exterior and soft interior texture in the potato pancake.

Ingredients

  • 2 small potatoes (中等大小的土豆, zhōngděng dàxiǎo de tǔdòu)
  • Flour (面粉, miànfěn) - Amount not specified, just enough to bind the potato shreds.
  • Cooking oil (食用油, shíyòng yóu) - Small amount for greasing the pan.
  • Salt (盐, yán) - A pinch.
  • Chili powder (辣椒面, làjiāomiàn) - Optional, a pinch.
  • Chopped green onions (葱花, cōnghuā) - Optional, for garnish.

Instructions

  1. Wash and peel two small potatoes.
  2. Use a grater to shred the potatoes into fine, even strands. (Alternatively, finely slice with a knife if skilled).
  3. Gradually add flour to the potato shreds, mixing until they are just sticky enough to hold together. Do not add too much flour.
  4. Heat a non-stick pan or flat pan over medium-low heat.
  5. Lightly brush the pan with cooking oil.
  6. Pour the potato mixture into the pan and spread it into a thin, even pancake.
  7. Cook over medium-low heat until the bottom is golden brown and crispy.
  8. Carefully flip the pancake and cook the other side until golden brown and crispy. (Use a plate to help flip if needed). This will take approximately 5-6 minutes total.
  9. Remove from heat and transfer to a serving plate.
  10. Sprinkle with a little salt, chili powder (optional), and chopped green onions (optional).
  11. Serve immediately and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kg8N2butTqQ

potatos_stir_fry.txt - 粉蒸土豆丝 (Fen Zheng Tu Dou Si)

Objectives

  • Learn a new way to prepare potatoes beyond frying or boiling.
  • Master the technique of making delicious and visually appealing steamed potato shreds.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to enhance the taste of the potato shreds.

Ingredients

  • 2 potatoes (土豆 - tǔdòu)
  • Red pepper shreds (红椒丝 - hóngjiāosī)
  • A small handful of chopped cilantro (香菜段 - xiāngcài duàn)
  • Several dried chilies, chopped (干海椒 - gānhǎijiāo)
  • Several cloves of garlic, minced (蒜末 - suànmò)
  • 1 tbsp sesame seeds (熟芝麻 - shú zhīma)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòngyóu)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽 - shēng chōu)
  • 1/2 tbsp rice vinegar (米醋 - mǐcù)
  • A little sesame oil (小磨香油 - xiǎo mó xiāngyóu)
  • Chopped green onions (葱花 - cōnghuā)
  • 1/2 tsp salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • 1 tsp thirteen-spice (十三香 - shísānxīang)
  • 50g cornstarch (玉米淀粉 - yùmǐ diànfěn)

Instructions

  1. Peel and wash two potatoes.
  2. Slice the potatoes thinly (0.3-0.5mm) and then shred them into coarse strips. Alternatively, use a grater.
  3. Rinse the potato shreds in water to remove starch and prevent oxidation.
  4. Prepare red pepper shreds, chopped cilantro, and minced garlic. Chop dried chilies.
  5. Make the sauce: In a bowl, combine chopped dried chilies, minced garlic, sesame seeds, soy sauce, rice vinegar, sesame oil, and chopped green onions. Mix well.
  6. Season the potato shreds: Add salt, thirteen-spice, and oil to the potato shreds. Toss to coat evenly.
  7. Add cornstarch to the seasoned potato shreds and mix well.
  8. Steam the potato shreds: Spread the potato shreds evenly in a steamer basket over boiling water. Steam for 3 minutes.
  9. Cool and loosen: Remove from steamer and let cool slightly. Loosen the shreds with chopsticks to prevent sticking.
  10. Combine ingredients: Add red pepper shreds, cilantro, and the prepared sauce to the cooled potato shreds. Mix thoroughly.
  11. Serve: Transfer the mixed potato shreds to a serving dish and enjoy.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=719EZwJ_4NA

potato_stir_fry.txt - 粉蒸土豆丝 (Fen Zheng Tu Dou Si)

Objectives

  • Learn a new way to prepare potatoes beyond frying or boiling.
  • Create a flavorful and visually appealing potato dish.
  • Master the technique of steaming potato shreds for optimal texture.

Ingredients

  • 2 large potatoes (土豆 - tǔdòu)
  • 1 red bell pepper (红椒 - hóng jiāo), julienned
  • A small handful of cilantro (香菜 - xiāngcài), chopped
  • Several dried chilies (干海椒 - gānhǎijiāo), finely chopped
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜 - suàn), minced
  • 1 tbsp sesame seeds (熟芝麻 - shú zhīma), toasted
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽 - shēng chōu)
  • ½ tbsp rice vinegar (米醋 - mǐcù)
  • A dash of sesame oil (小磨香油 - xiǎo mó xiāngyóu)
  • A few scallions (葱花 - cōnghuā), chopped
  • ½ tsp salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • 1 tsp thirteen-spice (十三香 - shísānxīang)
  • 1 tsp cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòngyóu)
  • 50g cornstarch (玉米淀粉 - yùmǐ diànfěn)

Instructions

  1. Peel and wash two potatoes. Slice into thin (0.3-0.5mm) pieces, then julienne into thick shreds. Alternatively, use a grater. Rinse in water to remove starch.
  2. Julienne a red bell pepper and chop cilantro. Finely chop dried chilies and mince garlic.
  3. In a small bowl, combine minced garlic, chopped dried chilies, sesame seeds, soy sauce, rice vinegar, sesame oil, and chopped scallions. Mix well.
  4. Rinse and drain the potato shreds thoroughly. In a large bowl, toss the potato shreds with salt, thirteen-spice, cooking oil, and cornstarch until evenly coated.
  5. Spread the potato mixture evenly in a steamer basket. Steam over high heat for 3 minutes.
  6. Remove from steamer and let cool slightly. Transfer to a large bowl and gently loosen with chopsticks to prevent sticking.
  7. Add the julienned red pepper, prepared sauce, and chopped cilantro. Mix thoroughly with disposable gloves until all ingredients are well combined.
  8. Serve immediately. Note: Ensure the potato shreds are relatively dry when mixing the cornstarch to avoid clumping.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=719EZwJ_4NA

pumpkin_dumplings.txt - 南瓜丸子 (Nánguā Wánzi)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and easy pumpkin dumplings.
  • Utilize leftover pumpkin creatively.
  • Master a simple yet elegant dessert recipe.

Ingredients

  • 750g Old Pumpkin (老南瓜) (lǎo nánguā)
  • 2 small spoons White Sugar (白糖) (bái táng)
  • 2 large spoons Glutinous Rice Flour (糯米粉) (nuòmǐ fěn)
  • A little water (水) (shuǐ) as needed
  • Multiple spoons of water for boiling (水) (shuǐ)
  • 2 spoons Sesame Seeds (熟芝麻) (shú zhīma)
  • 1 spoon Homemade 桂花蜜 (Guìhuā mì) (or orange juice)
  • 2 small spoons White Sugar (白糖) (bái táng)
  • A small handful of Goji Berries (枸杞) (gǒuqǐ)
  • Cooking oil (食用油) (shíyòng yóu)

Instructions

  1. Peel and cut a 750g old pumpkin into thin slices.
  2. Steam the pumpkin slices for 15 minutes until translucent and easily pierced with chopsticks.
  3. Remove the pumpkin and mash it into a smooth puree, discarding the steaming liquid (save for drinking later).
  4. Add 2 small spoons of white sugar and 2 large spoons of glutinous rice flour to the pumpkin puree.
  5. Mix until a crumbly dough forms, adding more flour or water as needed to achieve a soft, non-sticky consistency.
  6. Knead the dough into a smooth ball, let it rest for 2 minutes.
  7. Pinch off small pieces of dough and roll them into balls.
  8. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add the pumpkin balls and cook for 1 minute over high heat.
  9. Reduce heat to low, and continue cooking until the balls float to the surface and are cooked through, stirring occasionally to prevent sticking.
  10. Remove the cooked pumpkin balls with a slotted spoon and rinse them in cold water to maintain a chewy texture.
  11. Heat oil in a pan, add sesame seeds and stir-fry until fragrant.
  12. Add homemade桂花蜜 (or orange juice), white sugar, and goji berries. Stir-fry until thickened.
  13. Add the pumpkin balls to the sauce, stir-fry until evenly coated.
  14. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LR9lJKLZzFc

pumpkin_pancake.txt - Pumpkin Pancake

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and healthy pumpkin pancakes.
  • Master a simple method for preparing pumpkin and other vegetables.
  • Create a visually appealing and tasty pancake.

Ingredients

  • Leftover pumpkin (amount not specified)
  • Cucumber (amount not specified)
  • Carrot (amount not specified)
  • Green onions (amount not specified)
  • Glutinous rice flour (amount not specified)
  • Cooking oil (amount not specified)
  • Salt (1 tablespoon)
  • Sugar (1 tablespoon)
  • Pepper (amount not specified)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the pumpkin: Cut leftover pumpkin into small pieces, remove seeds, wash, and steam for 20 minutes.
  2. Prepare the vegetables:
    • Cut cucumber into small pieces.
    • Peel and slice carrots thinly, then chop into small pieces.
    • Chop green onions finely.
  3. Mash the steamed pumpkin with a fork.
  4. Gradually add glutinous rice flour to the mashed pumpkin, mixing well to form a smooth dough.
  5. Heat cooking oil in a pan.
  6. Sauté carrots for about 30 seconds.
  7. Add cucumber and continue to sauté.
  8. Add salt, sugar, and pepper. Stir well.
  9. Add chopped green onions and mix thoroughly.
  10. Take small portions of the pumpkin dough, roll into balls, and flatten into pancakes.
  11. Lightly oil an electric baking pan.
  12. Cook the pancakes for 3 minutes per side, flipping halfway through, until golden brown and puffed up.
  13. Serve and enjoy!
