pumpkin_red_date_steamed_cakes.txt - Pumpkin and Red Date Steamed Cakes

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and nutritious pumpkin and red date steamed cakes.
  • Master the steaming technique for perfectly fluffy cakes.
  • Prepare and process the pumpkin and red dates effectively.

Ingredients

  • 1 medium pumpkin (approx. 6-7 kg)
  • 50g sugar (adjust to taste)
  • 2 eggs
  • 50g pure milk
  • 5g yeast powder
  • All-purpose flour (amount not specified, added gradually)
  • Xinjiang red dates (amount not specified)
  • Water for washing and steaming

Instructions

  1. Cut the pumpkin in half using the back of a knife.
  2. Peel and cut the pumpkin into small slices.
  3. Steam the pumpkin slices in a steamer over high heat for 15 minutes.
  4. Once cooked, mash the hot pumpkin.
  5. Let the mashed pumpkin cool slightly.
  6. Add 2 eggs, 50g of milk, and 5g of yeast powder to the cooled pumpkin.
  7. Mix well until the yeast dissolves (ensure pumpkin is cool to prevent yeast from dying).
  8. Gradually add flour while mixing until a dough forms.
  9. Knead the dough until smooth and elastic.
  10. Cover and let the dough rise until doubled in size.
  11. Wash the red dates twice with water to remove dust and impurities.
  12. Remove the pits from the red dates and chop them into small pieces.
  13. Once the dough has risen, add the chopped red dates and mix well.
  14. Dust a clean surface with flour.
  15. Place the dough on the floured surface and gently knead to remove excess air.
  16. Shape the dough into long strips and divide into equal-sized pieces.
  17. Shape each piece into a flower-like shape.
  18. Place the shaped dough pieces in a steamer.
  19. Steam over high heat for 15-16 minutes, then let it sit for an additional 5 minutes before opening the lid.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=yly9kX6dxL8

pumpkin_sesame_cake.txt - Pumpkin Sesame Cakes

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious, crispy, soft, chewy, and sweet pumpkin sesame cakes.
  • Master a simple recipe perfect for breakfast or afternoon tea.
  • Learn how to prepare the pumpkin, sesame filling, and assemble the cakes.

Ingredients

  • 1 pound pumpkin
  • Sesame seeds (amount not specified, adjust to taste)
  • White sugar (amount not specified, adjust to taste)
  • Brown sugar (amount not specified, adjust to taste)
  • Lard or cooking oil (small amount)
  • Glutinous rice flour (amount not specified, adjust to taste)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Pumpkin: Peel and cut the pumpkin into thin, even slices. Steam for 15 minutes until tender.
  2. Make the Sesame Filling: Dry-roast sesame seeds in a pan over medium-low heat until fragrant and all moisture is gone. Grind the roasted sesame seeds using a food processor or blender. Mix with white sugar to desired sweetness.
  3. Prepare the Lard (Optional): If using lard, heat it in a pan over low heat until the fat renders and turns oily. Add this to the sesame filling and mix well.
  4. Prepare the Pumpkin Mixture: Mash the steamed pumpkin in a bowl. Add white sugar and glutinous rice flour, mixing until well combined. Add flour gradually as needed to achieve a smooth, workable dough.
  5. Shape the Cakes: Take a portion of the pumpkin dough (slightly larger than a ping-pong ball), flatten it in your hand, and make a small well in the center. Add brown sugar and sesame filling.
  6. Assemble and Coat: Gently shape the dough into a small cake. Dip the sides in water to help with shaping and coat thoroughly in sesame seeds. Gently press to secure the sesame seeds.
  7. Cook the Cakes: Heat a lightly oiled pan. Cook the cakes over low heat for approximately 1 minute per side, flipping carefully, until golden brown and slightly puffed. Ensure frequent flipping to prevent burning. The entire cooking process takes about 5.5 minutes.
  8. Serve: Remove the cakes from the pan and serve immediately. They are best enjoyed fresh but can be stored in the refrigerator or freezer.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=gxrzegslJpA

qing_chao_ou_pian.txt - 清炒藕片 (Stir-fried Lotus Root Slices)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and refreshing stir-fried lotus root dish.
  • Master the technique of preparing lotus root to prevent discoloration.
  • Understand the importance of proper seasoning and cooking time.

Ingredients

  • Appropriate amount of lotus root (adjust based on serving size)
  • 1 small carrot, cut into diamond shapes
  • 1 large green pepper, cut into diamond shapes
  • Several cloves of garlic, sliced
  • A small piece of ginger, thinly sliced
  • 1 tsp salt
  • 1 tsp sugar
  • 1 tsp mushroom seasoning (松茸鲜)
  • A dash of white vinegar
  • 1 tsp potato starch
  • Appropriate amount of water
  • Cooking oil
  • White vinegar for soaking lotus root slices

Instructions

  1. Select fresh, bright yellow lotus root. Discard any dark or waterlogged pieces. Cut off the lotus root nodes (save for boiling water).
  2. Peel the lotus root and rinse thoroughly. Cut into thin, even slices.
  3. Soak the lotus root slices in water with a little white vinegar to prevent discoloration.
  4. Prepare the carrot and green pepper by cutting them into diamond-shaped pieces.
  5. Prepare the garlic and ginger by slicing them thinly.
  6. Make the seasoning sauce: In a bowl, mix salt, sugar, mushroom seasoning, a dash of white vinegar, potato starch, and water until smooth.
  7. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Blanch the lotus root slices for 77-49 seconds (approx 70 seconds). Immediately remove and drain well.
  8. Heat a small amount of oil in a wok or pan over medium heat. Add the ginger and garlic, sauté until fragrant.
  9. Add the lotus root and carrot slices to the wok. Stir-fry over high heat until slightly softened.
  10. Add the green pepper slices and the prepared seasoning sauce. Stir-fry until the sauce thickens and coats the vegetables.
  11. Drizzle with a little sesame oil before serving.
  12. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=AAMWW9xaIcw

qingjiao_chao_jidan.txt - 青椒炒鸡蛋 (Qīngjiāo chǎo jǐdàn) - Stir-fried Green Peppers with Eggs

Objectives

  • Learn a quick and easy recipe for stir-fried green peppers with eggs.
  • Achieve a flavorful and tender egg and pepper dish.
  • Master a simple technique for perfectly cooked eggs and peppers.

Ingredients

  • 土鸡蛋 (tǔ jǐdàn) - Farm eggs (number depends on servings)
  • 水淀粉 (shuǐ diànfěn) - Water starch (a small amount)
  • 蒜 (suàn) - Garlic (multiple cloves)
  • 食盐 (shíyán) - Salt (1 scoop)
  • 松茸鲜 (sōngrōng xiān) - (Assume this is a type of seasoning, adjust based on actual product) (1 scoop)
  • 生抽 (shēng chōu) - Light soy sauce (1 scoop)
  • 蚝油 (háoyóu) - Oyster sauce (appropriate amount)
  • 玉米淀粉 (yùmǐ diànfěn) - Corn starch (1 scoop)
  • 清水 (qīngshuǐ) - Water (half a bowl)
  • 薄皮青椒 (báo pí qīngjiāo) - Thin-skinned green peppers (several)
  • 食用油 (shíyòng yóu) - Cooking oil (ample amount)

Instructions

  1. Crack eggs into a bowl. Add water starch and whisk until smooth and even. Set aside.
  2. Mince garlic and combine with salt, 松茸鲜, light soy sauce, oyster sauce, cornstarch, and water in a bowl. Mix well. Set aside.
  3. Roughly chop green peppers into bite-sized pieces. Set aside.
  4. Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan over medium heat. Add egg mixture and cook until set, then break into larger pieces. Remove and set aside.
  5. Add a little more oil to the pan. Add green peppers and stir-fry until slightly softened and slightly blistered.
  6. Return the cooked eggs to the pan.
  7. Pour in the prepared sauce. Stir-fry over high heat for about 30 seconds until the sauce thickens and coats the eggs and peppers.
  8. Serve immediately.

qingjiao_dan.txt - 青椒酱汁鸡蛋; 菌菇蒜苔炒鸡蛋; 凤凰蒸鸡蛋; 盖浇鸡蛋饼

Objectives

  • Learn four different ways to cook eggs.
  • Master techniques for frying, steaming, and making egg pancakes.
  • Create flavorful and visually appealing egg dishes.
  • Learn to use common ingredients in creative ways.
  • Improve cooking skills and expand culinary repertoire.

Ingredients

青椒酱汁鸡蛋 (Green Pepper Sauce Eggs):

  • Several 土鸡蛋 (earth eggs)
  • Water starch (淀粉水)
  • Garlic (蒜)
  • Salt (食盐)
  • Songrong Xian (松茸鲜) - a type of seasoning
  • Soy sauce (生抽)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • Corn starch (玉米淀粉)
  • Water (清水)
  • Thin-skinned green peppers (薄皮青椒)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)

菌菇蒜苔炒鸡蛋 (Mushroom Garlic Stem Stir-fried Eggs):

  • 3 笨鸡蛋 (rustic eggs)
  • Shiitake mushrooms (香菇)
  • White jade mushrooms (白玉菇)
  • Salt (食盐)
  • White vinegar (白醋)
  • Soy sauce (生抽)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • Salt (食盐)
  • Songrong Xian (松茸鲜)
  • Sugar (白糖)
  • Potato starch (土豆淀粉)
  • Water (清水)
  • Garlic chives (蒜苔)
  • Ginger (生姜)
  • Chili peppers (小米椒) or red pepper (大红椒)

凤凰蒸鸡蛋 (Phoenix Steamed Eggs):

  • 6 eggs (鸡蛋)
  • Baking soda (小苏打)
  • Water (清水)
  • Water chestnuts (马蹄)
  • Pork belly (五花肉)
  • Ginger (姜)
  • Green onions (葱)
  • Salt (食盐)
  • Pepper (胡椒粉)
  • Soy sauce (生抽)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • Corn starch (玉米淀粉)
  • Sesame oil (小磨香油)
  • Goji berries (枸杞)

盖浇鸡蛋饼 (Covered Egg Pancake):

  • 2 cucumbers (黄瓜)
  • 4 eggs (鸡蛋)
  • ½ piece of ham (火腿)
  • Salt (食盐)
  • Songrong Xian (松茸鲜)
  • Pepper (胡椒粉)
  • 3 chili peppers (小米椒)
  • 1 green pepper (青椒)
  • Seafood mushrooms (海鲜菇)
  • Ginger (生姜)
  • Garlic (蒜)
  • Green onions (葱)
  • Lean meat (瘦肉)
  • Soy sauce (生抽)
  • Five-spice powder (五香粉)
  • Potato starch (土豆淀粉)
  • Water (清水)
  • Sesame oil (小磨香油)

Instructions

青椒酱汁鸡蛋 (Green Pepper Sauce Eggs):

  1. Crack eggs into a bowl, add water starch, and whisk until smooth.
  2. Prepare garlic, chop and mix with salt, Songrong Xian, soy sauce, oyster sauce, cornstarch, and water.
  3. Prepare green peppers, pat, and chop into small pieces.
  4. Heat oil, pour in egg mixture, and fry until set.
  5. Add more oil, stir-fry green peppers until slightly charred.
  6. Add fried eggs and sauce, stir-fry until combined.
  7. Serve.

菌菇蒜苔炒鸡蛋 (Mushroom Garlic Stem Stir-fried Eggs):

  1. Whisk eggs with salt and white vinegar.
  2. Slice shiitake mushrooms thickly.
  3. Clean and break apart white jade mushrooms.
  4. Chop garlic chives into 3-4 cm segments.
  5. Mince ginger and garlic, chop chili peppers.
  6. Mix soy sauce, oyster sauce, salt, Songrong Xian, sugar, potato starch, and water for sauce.
  7. Blanch mushrooms and garlic chives in boiling water.
  8. Heat oil, fry eggs until tender.
  9. Stir-fry minced garlic, ginger, and chili peppers until fragrant.
  10. Add mushrooms and garlic chives, stir-fry for 1 minute.
  11. Add fried eggs and sauce, stir-fry until combined.
  12. Serve.

凤凰蒸鸡蛋 (Phoenix Steamed Eggs):

  1. Add baking soda to eggs, soak in water for 2 minutes, clean, and boil for 8 minutes.
  2. Prepare water chestnuts, dice.
  3. Mince pork belly.
  4. Mix water chestnuts, pork, ginger, green onions, salt, pepper, soy sauce, oyster sauce, cornstarch, and sesame oil.
  5. Cool boiled eggs, peel, and cut in half.
  6. Remove yolks, fill whites with meat mixture.
  7. Steam in a steamer for 10 minutes.
  8. Make a sauce with the egg liquid, soy sauce, goji berries, and cornstarch.
  9. Pour sauce over steamed eggs and serve.

盖浇鸡蛋饼 (Covered Egg Pancake):

  1. Dice cucumbers, ham, and chili peppers.
  2. Chop green pepper, seafood mushrooms, ginger, garlic, and green onions.
  3. Dice lean meat.
  4. Mix eggs with diced vegetables, ham, salt, Songrong Xian, and pepper.
  5. Mix soy sauce, salt, five-spice powder, potato starch, and water for sauce.
  6. Heat oil, pour in egg mixture, and cook into a pancake.
  7. Flip and cook the other side.
  8. Heat oil, stir-fry ginger and garlic until fragrant.
  9. Add meat, stir-fry until white.
  10. Add seafood mushrooms and stir-fry for 30 seconds.
  11. Add green and red peppers, stir-fry until combined.
  12. Add sauce, stir-fry until thickened.
  13. Stir in sesame oil and green onions.
  14. Pour sauce over the egg pancake and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=VWRBGsRhGKo

qingjiao_muer_chaoroupian.txt - 青椒木耳炒肉片 (Qīngjiāo mù'ěr chǎo ròupiàn) - Stir-fried Pork with Green Pepper and Wood Ear Mushrooms

Objectives

  • Learn a restaurant-style method for marinating pork to prevent dryness and off-flavors.
  • Master a quick and easy stir-fry technique for tender and flavorful pork.
  • Prepare a delicious and balanced side dish using readily available ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 1 piece of pork tenderloin (里脊肉 - lǐjǐròu)
  • 100g dried wood ear mushrooms (黑木耳 - hēimù'ěr), soaked and chopped
  • 2 green bell peppers (青椒 - qīngjiāo), seeded and diced
  • Some scallions (葱 - cōng), chopped (separate portions for marinade and stir-fry)
  • 1 piece ginger (姜 - jiāng), sliced and julienned (separate portions for marinade and stir-fry)
  • Several cloves garlic (蒜 - suàn), sliced (separate portions for marinade and stir-fry)
  • Optional: Dried chili peppers (干海椒 - gānhǎijiāo) for spice
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽 - shēngchōu)
  • A dash of dark soy sauce (老抽 - lǎochōu)
  • 1 tsp salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • A pinch of pepper (胡椒粉 - hújiāofěn)
  • 1/2 egg white (蛋清 - dànqīng)
  • 1 tbsp cornstarch (玉米淀粉 - yùmǐ diànfěn)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòngyóu)
  • Water (水 - shuǐ)
  • Flower pepper (花椒 - huājiāo)

Instructions

  1. Freeze the pork tenderloin briefly for easier slicing.
  2. Prepare the vegetables: chop the wood ear mushrooms, seed and dice the green peppers, and prepare the scallions, ginger, and garlic.
  3. Make the ginger-scallion marinade: combine chopped scallions, julienned ginger, salt, and flower pepper in a bowl. Crush to release juices, then add warm water.
  4. Prepare the sauce: Mix soy sauce, dark soy sauce, and salt in a separate bowl.
  5. Slice the pork thinly against the grain.
  6. Marinate the pork: Add soy sauce, pepper, a little dark soy sauce, and the ginger-scallion marinade to the pork in small batches, mixing well to ensure absorption. Do not add salt or cooking wine.
  7. Add egg white and cornstarch to the marinated pork, mixing until evenly coated.
  8. Set aside to marinate for 10 minutes.
  9. Blanch the wood ear mushrooms in boiling water for 90 seconds. Drain.
  10. Heat oil in a wok or pan over high heat. Stir-fry the pork until it turns white and the cornstarch is set. Remove and set aside.
  11. Add more oil to the pan, then add scallions, ginger, and garlic; stir-fry until fragrant.
  12. Add the wood ear mushrooms and green peppers; stir-fry until tender-crisp.
  13. Add the cooked pork and prepared sauce; stir-fry until heated through and the sauce is evenly distributed (about 1 minute).
  14. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=byfmJ5yUQ2c

qiu_gui_ji_dan_bing.txt - 秋葵鸡蛋饼 (Qiūkuí jǐdàn bǐng) - Okra Egg Cake

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and healthy okra egg cake.
  • Master the technique of preparing and cooking okra.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to complement the okra egg cake.

Ingredients

  • Fresh okra (amount not specified)
  • 4 chicken eggs
  • 1 tablespoon salt (divided use)
  • 1 tablespoon pepper
  • Cooking oil (amount not specified)
  • 2 RMB worth of lean pork (amount not specified)
  • Several cloves garlic
  • Several small chili peppers
  • 2 tablespoons Puning doubanjiang (普宁豆酱)
  • Water (amount not specified)
  • Small amount of water starch (水淀粉)
  • Optional: Green onions for garnish

Instructions

  1. Wash the okra thoroughly, scrubbing with salt to remove the fuzzy layer. Rinse twice with clean water until the water runs clear.
  2. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add 1 tablespoon of salt and a little cooking oil. Blanch the okra for 2 minutes. Do not remove the stems and ends during blanching.
  3. Immediately transfer the blanched okra to an ice bath to cool. Drain and set aside.
  4. Trim the ends of the okra slightly and slice into thin rounds.
  5. In a large bowl, combine the sliced okra, 4 eggs, 1 tablespoon of salt, and 1 tablespoon pepper. Mix well to coat the okra with the egg mixture. Set aside.
  6. Chop the lean pork into small pieces, then mince into a slightly coarse texture.
  7. Mince the garlic and thinly slice the chili peppers.
  8. Heat cooking oil in a pan or wok. Pour in the okra and egg mixture. Stir quickly until the egg is set.
  9. Reduce heat to low and slowly pan-fry the okra and egg mixture until golden brown on both sides. Use a lid to help flip the cake.
  10. Remove the cooked okra egg cake and set aside.
  11. Add more oil to the pan and add the minced pork, stir-frying until the color changes.
  12. Add the minced garlic and chili peppers and stir-fry until fragrant.
  13. Add the Puning doubanjiang and stir-fry to release the aroma.
  14. Add a small bowl of water and bring to a boil.
  15. Thicken the sauce with a small amount of water starch.
  16. Pour the sauce over the okra egg cake. Garnish with green onions, if desired.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ujZ6j9JKQWk

radish_glutinous_rice_cake.txt - Radish Glutinous Rice Cake

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and nutritious radish-filled glutinous rice cakes.
  • Master the techniques of preparing the radish filling and glutinous rice dough.
  • Create visually appealing and perfectly steamed radish glutinous rice cakes.

Ingredients

  • 1 bowl glutinous rice flour (approx. 400g)
  • 200g rice flour
  • 200ml boiling water
  • 1 white radish, peeled and finely shredded (or grated)
  • Dried mushrooms, soaked and chopped
  • 200g pork, finely minced
  • Ginger, peeled and minced
  • Scallions (both white and green parts), finely chopped
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Light soy sauce
  • Oyster sauce
  • Dried lettuce (optional)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Radish: Peel and finely shred (or grate) one white radish. Blanch in boiling water for 2 minutes to remove bitterness, then immediately plunge into cold water to cool. Squeeze out excess water using cheesecloth. Chop into small pieces.
  2. Prepare the Mushrooms: Soak dried mushrooms in warm water until soft. Wash thoroughly, squeeze dry, and chop into small pieces.
  3. Prepare the Pork: Finely mince 200g of pork. (Alternatively, use a meat grinder).
  4. Prepare the Aromatics: Mince ginger and chop scallions (separate white and green parts).
  5. Stir-fry the Filling: Heat oil in a pan. Stir-fry minced pork until browned. Add ginger and scallions, then stir-fry until fragrant. Add mushrooms and stir-fry until dry. Season with salt, pepper, light soy sauce, oyster sauce, and dried lettuce (optional). Stir well.
  6. Combine Radish and Filling: Add the prepared radish to the stir-fried filling. Mix well and set aside.
  7. Make the Glutinous Rice Dough: In a bowl, combine glutinous rice flour and rice flour. Gradually add boiling water while stirring with chopsticks until a smooth, slightly soft dough forms. Knead until smooth.
  8. Assemble the Rice Cakes: Divide the dough into equal portions. Roll each portion into a ball, make a dimple in the center, and fill with the radish mixture. Pinch the edges to seal tightly. Roll into a smooth ball.
  9. Steam the Rice Cakes: Arrange the filled rice cakes in a steamer, leaving some space between each. Steam over high heat for 15 minutes, then simmer for another 2 minutes.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Hh1WhMv-GP4

radish_pork_ribs_soup.txt - Radish Pork Ribs Soup 萝卜排骨汤

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious radish pork ribs soup.
  • Master techniques for preparing and cooking the ingredients to maximize flavor.
  • Understand the importance of simmering for optimal tenderness and taste.

Ingredients

  • Pork ribs (虎头骨, hǔtóugǔ): amount unspecified, but enough for a family meal.
  • White radish (白萝卜, bái luóbo): 2 medium-sized.
  • Salt (食用盐, shíyòng yán): 1 small spoon.
  • Flour (普通面粉, pǔtōng miànfěn): 1 spoon.
  • Ginger (生姜, shēng jiāng): a generous amount, sliced thickly.
  • Scallions (葱, cōng): 1, chopped into sections.
  • Vegetable oil (山茶油, shā chá yóu or other oil like olive or peanut oil): a small amount.

Instructions

  1. Prepare the pork ribs: Add a small spoon of salt and one spoon of flour to the ribs. Mix well with your hands to remove blood and impurities.
  2. Soak the ribs: Add lukewarm water and let the ribs soak for 5 minutes.
  3. Prepare the radish: Peel and wash the radishes. Cut into large chunks.
  4. Prepare aromatics: Slice the ginger thickly and chop the scallions.
  5. Rinse the ribs: After soaking, rinse the ribs thoroughly with water (warm water is recommended in winter) to remove impurities and excess oil. Drain.
  6. Stir-fry the ribs: Heat oil in a pot. Add ginger and stir-fry until fragrant. Reduce heat, add ribs and stir-fry for 2 minutes until slightly browned.
  7. Simmer the ribs: Add boiling water to the pot. Bring to a boil, then skim off any foam or impurities. Add scallions, cover, and simmer over low heat for 38 minutes.
  8. Add the radish: Remove the scallions. Add the radish, cover, and simmer for another 15 minutes until tender.
  9. Season and finish: Add a small spoon of salt. Stir and simmer for another 2 minutes. Turn off heat.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=R5d5zzpV4hY

radish_shrimp_stir_fry.txt - Radish and Shrimp Stir-fry

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple, healthy, and delicious radish and shrimp stir-fry.
  • Understand the importance of preparing the radish properly to remove bitterness.
  • Master the technique of stir-frying to achieve the perfect texture and flavor.

Ingredients

  • 1 large white radish
  • Salt (for soaking radish)
  • Water (for soaking radish)
  • 1 bunch scallions (green onions), chopped
  • 1 piece ginger, minced
  • Several cloves garlic, minced
  • A handful of sun-dried shrimp
  • Cooking oil
  • Salt (for seasoning)
  • A pinch of sugar
  • A pinch of black pepper
  • Oyster sauce

Instructions

  1. Wash the radish thoroughly and peel it.
  2. Cut the radish into 4-5 cm long sections, then slice into thin pieces, and finally julienne into thin strips.
  3. Place the radish strips in a large bowl, add salt and plenty of water, and soak for 10 minutes to remove bitterness.
  4. Chop the scallions, mince the ginger, and mince the garlic. Set aside.
  5. Drain the radish strips and set aside.
  6. Heat oil in a wok or large pan over high heat.
  7. Add the radish strips and stir-fry until slightly translucent and some moisture is released (about 60-70% cooked).
  8. Remove the radish and set aside.
  9. Add the scallions, ginger, and garlic to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Add the sun-dried shrimp and stir-fry until fragrant.
  11. Return the radish strips to the pan and stir-fry to combine.
  12. Season with salt, a pinch of sugar, black pepper, and oyster sauce.
  13. Stir-fry for about 1 minute until flavors are well combined.
  14. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=HC0rJChxGeo

red_amaranth_and_preserved_egg.txt - 红苋菜皮蛋

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare red amaranth to retain nutrients and prevent bitterness.
  • Master a simple and delicious red amaranth and preserved egg recipe.
  • Understand the importance of thorough vegetable cleaning for health and hygiene.

Ingredients

  • Red amaranth (one bunch)
  • 2 preserved eggs (松花皮蛋)
  • Garlic (适量)
  • Ginger (适量)
  • 2 green peppers (青椒)
  • Salt (适量)
  • Cooking soda (食用碱, 适量)
  • Vegetable oil (preferably rapeseed oil, 菜籽油)
  • 2 bowls of pure water (纯净水)
  • Chicken bouillon (鸡精, 少许)

Instructions

  1. Trim the roots off the red amaranth.
  2. In a large bowl, dissolve a spoonful of salt and a spoonful of cooking soda in plenty of water.
  3. Soak the red amaranth in the solution for 10 minutes to remove pesticides and sanitize.
  4. Peel and chop the preserved eggs.
  5. Mince the garlic and thinly slice the ginger.
  6. Remove the stems and slice the green peppers into small pieces (optional).
  7. Rinse the red amaranth thoroughly under running water until the water runs clear.
  8. Drain the amaranth and place it in a large bowl.
  9. Add a small spoonful of salt to the amaranth and mix well to remove oxalic acid and enhance tenderness.
  10. Let the amaranth sit for 10 minutes, then squeeze out excess water.
  11. Heat vegetable oil in a wok until slightly smoking.
  12. Add the preserved eggs and stir-fry until slightly browned.
  13. Add the ginger and garlic and stir-fry until fragrant.
  14. Add the red amaranth and stir-fry over high heat until the color brightens.
  15. Add the green peppers (if using) and two bowls of water.
  16. Cover and simmer over medium heat for 5 minutes.
  17. Season with salt and a little chicken bouillon.
  18. Stir and serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Q1M3XEWeheY

red_braised_chicken_legs.txt - 红烧鸡腿

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and tender red-braised chicken legs.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful recipe perfect for family meals.
  • Understand the importance of proper cleaning and preparation for optimal taste and texture.

Ingredients

  • Several chicken legs (adjust to the number of people)
  • Salt
  • Flour
  • Ginger slices
  • Scallions (葱结)
  • Cooking wine (料酒)
  • Water
  • Garlic
  • Bay leaves (香叶)
  • Cinnamon (桂皮)
  • Sichuan peppercorns (花椒)
  • Dried chilies (干辣椒段)
  • Rock sugar (老冰糖) or granulated sugar (冰糖粒)
  • Light soy sauce (生抽)
  • Dark soy sauce (老抽)
  • Beer (啤酒)
  • Rice wine (米酒, optional)
  • Water (approximately equal to the volume of chicken legs)
  • Chopped scallions (葱花, for garnish)
  • Sesame seeds (熟芝麻, for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Choose fresh chicken legs. Sprinkle salt and flour on the chicken legs and rub thoroughly to remove impurities and sanitize. Rinse well with water.
  2. Score the chicken legs to help them cook faster and absorb flavors more effectively.
  3. In a pot, boil the chicken legs in water with ginger slices, scallions, and cooking wine until the blood is removed (about 2-3 minutes after boiling).
  4. Remove the chicken legs and rinse them in warm water to remove any impurities or blood residue.
  5. Place the cleaned chicken legs in a larger pot (砂锅). Add ginger, garlic, bay leaves, cinnamon, Sichuan peppercorns, dried chilies, rock sugar (or granulated sugar), light soy sauce, dark soy sauce, beer, and rice wine (if using).
  6. Add enough water to almost cover the chicken legs.
  7. Bring to a simmer over medium-low heat, cover, and braise for 20 minutes, turning the chicken legs halfway through.
  8. Increase the heat to high and reduce the sauce until it thickens.
  9. Turn off the heat, garnish with chopped scallions and sesame seeds.
  10. Serve hot. Enjoy with rice.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=hxvo3KGC0TY

red_braised_eggplant.txt - 红烧茄子 (Hóngshāo qiézi)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and flavorful red-braised eggplant.
  • Master a simple yet effective method for preparing eggplant to maintain its crispness.
  • Understand how to create a balanced sauce that enhances the eggplant's flavor.

Ingredients

  • 2 fresh eggplants (茄子, qiézi)
  • Salt (盐, yán)
  • White vinegar (白醋, báicù)
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒, xiǎomǐjiāo)
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜, suàn)
  • 2 green onions (葱, cōng)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽, shēngchōu)
  • A little dark soy sauce (老抽, lǎochōu)
  • Appropriate amount of oyster sauce (蚝油, háoyóu)
  • 1 tbsp sugar (白糖, báitáng)
  • 1 tbsp mushroom seasoning (松茸鲜, sōngróng xiān)
  • 1 tsp corn starch (玉米淀粉, yùmǐ diànfěn)
  • Water (水, shuǐ)
  • 30g corn starch (玉米淀粉, yùmǐ diànfěn)
  • Cooking oil (食用油, shíyòngyóu)

Instructions

  1. Wash the eggplants, rubbing them with salt to remove impurities. Rinse thoroughly with water to remove excess salt.
  2. Cut off both ends of the eggplants and slice them into large chunks.
  3. Place the eggplant pieces in a large bowl, add salt and white vinegar, mix well, and let it sit for 10 minutes to draw out moisture.
  4. While the eggplant is marinating, prepare the ingredients: finely slice the chili peppers, mince the garlic, and chop the green onions.
  5. In a small bowl, combine soy sauce, dark soy sauce, oyster sauce, sugar, mushroom seasoning, corn starch, and water. Mix well.
  6. Rinse the marinated eggplant under running water to remove excess salt and squeeze out as much water as possible.
  7. Add 30g of corn starch to the eggplant and toss to coat evenly.
  8. Heat cooking oil in a wok or large pan over high heat. Add the eggplant and stir-fry until softened. Remove and set aside.
  9. Add a small amount of oil to the pan. Add the minced garlic and chili peppers and stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Add the stir-fried eggplant and the prepared sauce to the pan. Stir-fry over high heat for about 2 minutes, until the flavors are well combined.
  11. Garnish with chopped green onions and chili peppers. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=3rDoT7K5BOc

red_braised_pork.txt - 红烧肉 (Hóngshāo ròu)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious, tender red-braised pork.
  • Master the technique of creating a rich, flavorful sauce.
  • Achieve a visually appealing, glossy finish on the pork.

Ingredients

  • 500g Three-layer pork belly (三层五花肉 - Sāncéng wǔhuā ròu)
  • 1 large onion, chopped into small segments (一根大葱切成小段 - Yī gēn dàcōng qiē chéng xiǎoduàn)
  • 1 piece ginger, thinly sliced (一块生姜切成薄片 - Yī kuài shēngjiāng qiē chéng báo piàn)
  • 2 star anise (两个八角 - Liǎng gè bājiǎo)
  • 1 small piece cassia bark (一小块桂皮 - Yī xiǎo kuài guìpí)
  • Several dried chilies (几个干海椒 - Jǐ gè gānhǎijiāo)
  • 18g rock sugar (冰糖 - Bīngtáng) (optional)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - Shíyòng yóu)
  • 1 can of beer (一罐啤酒 - Yī guàn píjiǔ)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (一勺生抽 - Yī sháo shēngchōu)
  • 1 tbsp salt (一勺食盐 - Yī sháo shíyán)

Instructions

  1. Heat a wok until slightly smoking. Rub the pork belly skin-side down to remove any remaining hairs. Blanch the skin for about 20 seconds until it blisters slightly ("tiger skin").
  2. Rinse the pork belly under warm water and scrape off any impurities from the skin using a knife until clean. Rinse twice more.
  3. Cut the pork belly into large, square pieces (about the size of mahjong tiles).
  4. Prepare the aromatics: chop the onion into segments, slice the ginger thinly, and gather the star anise, cassia bark, and dried chilies.
  5. Prepare the caramel: Add a small amount of oil to a wok. Add the rock sugar and cook over low heat, stirring constantly, until it melts and turns a reddish-brown color with small bubbles. Quickly add a small amount of boiling water and stir until the color is bright and glossy.
  6. Heat a wok. Add the pork belly and cook over low heat, rendering out excess fat until the surface is lightly browned. Remove excess rendered fat.
  7. Add the prepared aromatics to the wok and stir-fry until fragrant.
  8. Pour in the caramel sauce, add the beer, soy sauce, and salt. Mix well.
  9. Cover and simmer over low heat for one hour (or pressure cook for 10 minutes).
  10. Remove the aromatics. Increase the heat and reduce the sauce, leaving a small amount of sauce.
  11. Serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=b0qNo-F6jOE

red_sweet_potato_sprouts.txt - 红薯苗

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare fresh red sweet potato sprouts.
  • Master a cooking method that prevents discoloration and excessive water release.
  • Create a delicious and nutritious side dish.

Ingredients

  • 1 large bunch of fresh red sweet potato sprouts (about 1 Chinese Yuan)
  • 2 teaspoons salt
  • Several cloves garlic, minced
  • A small amount of dried chili peppers, chopped (rinsed)
  • Vegetable oil (and optionally, lard for added flavor)
  • A pinch of sugar
  • A pinch of MSG (optional)

Instructions

  1. Trim the roots from the red sweet potato sprouts (2-3cm).
  2. Cut the sprouts into smaller, more manageable pieces.
  3. Soak the cut sprouts in a large bowl of salted water to disinfect and clean. Rinse thoroughly until the water runs clear.
  4. Drain the sprouts in a colander.
  5. Transfer the drained sprouts to a bowl, add 2 teaspoons of salt, and toss to coat evenly. Let it marinate for 10 minutes.
  6. While the sprouts marinate, mince the garlic and chop the dried chili peppers. Rinse the chili peppers to remove dust and prevent burning.
  7. After 10 minutes, rinse the marinated sprouts again with clean water to remove excess salt. Drain thoroughly.
  8. Heat a wok or pan over high heat. Add a small amount of oil (and lard, if using).
  9. Add the minced garlic and chopped chili peppers and sauté until fragrant over low heat.
  10. Add the drained sweet potato sprouts to the wok. Stir-fry quickly over high heat to prevent excess water release.
  11. Season with a pinch of salt, sugar, and MSG (if using). Stir-fry for another 5-8 seconds.
  12. Remove from heat and serve immediately.

ribs_with_sour_cabbage.txt - 排骨炖酸菜

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and nutritious ribs with sour cabbage stew.
  • Master the techniques for preparing and cooking the ribs and vegetables.
  • Create a flavorful and aromatic dish perfect for a cold winter day.

Ingredients

  • 1 large piece of pork ribs (about 100 yuan worth)
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • Water for soaking ribs
  • Homemade sour cabbage (or store-bought, needs extra rinsing)
  • 1 medium-sized芋头 (taro)
  • Flour
  • Ginger slices
  • Dry chili peppers
  • Cooking oil
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Dark soy sauce (老抽)
  • Soybean paste (黄豆酱)
  • Garlic
  • Green onions

Instructions

  1. Cut the ribs into small pieces.
  2. Soak the ribs in salt water for 15 minutes.
  3. Clean the sour cabbage and cut into small pieces.
  4. Peel and cut the taro into large chunks.
  5. Drain the soaked ribs and toss with flour until sticky.
  6. Rinse the ribs thoroughly with water to remove blood and impurities.
  7. Blanch the ribs in boiling water with ginger slices to remove impurities.
  8. Remove the scum from the blanching water.
  9. Set aside the blanched ribs.
  10. Heat oil in a pan and lightly fry the taro until golden brown.
  11. Set aside the fried taro.
  12. Stir-fry the ginger, chilies, and sour cabbage until fragrant and dry.
  13. Set aside the stir-fried sour cabbage.
  14. Heat oil in a pan and lightly fry the ribs until golden brown on both sides.
  15. Add boiling water to the ribs, cover, and simmer for 20 minutes.
  16. Season with salt, pepper, dark soy sauce, and soybean paste.
  17. Add the fried taro and stir-fried sour cabbage.
  18. Cover and simmer for another 10 minutes.
  19. Open the lid and cook to reduce the sauce.
  20. Check if the taro is cooked through.
  21. Garnish with garlic and green onions.
  22. Serve hot.

roast_radish_egg.txt - Roasted Radish and Egg

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple yet delicious radish and egg dish.
  • Understand the importance of blanching radish to reduce bitterness.
  • Master a quick and easy stir-fry technique.

Ingredients

  • 1 large white radish, peeled and cut into thick pieces
  • 4-6 eggs
  • Several cloves garlic, minced
  • Several small chili peppers, finely sliced
  • 2 scallions, chopped
  • Salt
  • MSG (optional)
  • Soy sauce (老抽)
  • Light soy sauce (生抽)
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Wash and peel a large white radish. Cut it into thick pieces.
  2. Blanch the radish pieces in boiling salted water for about 2 minutes to reduce bitterness and make it tender. Drain and set aside.
  3. Beat 4-6 eggs in a bowl; lightly whisk.
  4. Heat oil in a pan and cook the eggs until set. Break into smaller pieces and set aside.
  5. In the same pan, add more oil and sauté minced garlic and chili peppers until fragrant.
  6. Add the blanched radish and stir-fry until some of the moisture evaporates.
  7. Add dark soy sauce (老抽) to color the radish.
  8. Add a small bowl of water to help the radish absorb the flavors.
  9. Season with salt, MSG (optional), and light soy sauce (生抽). Stir-fry until the sauce thickens.
  10. Add the cooked eggs and scallions. Stir-fry until everything is well combined.
  11. Serve hot.

salt_baked_quail_eggs.txt - 盐焗鹌鹑蛋

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious salt-baked quail eggs using a rice cooker.
  • Understand the importance of using coarse salt and various spices.
  • Learn a simple method for preserving leftover salt for future use.

Ingredients

  • Quail eggs (quantity not specified)
  • Coarse salt (approximately 600g, 粗盐 (cū yán))
  • Flower pepper (花椒 (huājiāo), quantity not specified)
  • Star anise (八角 (bājiǎo), 2)
  • Ginger slices (姜片 (jiāngpiàn), quantity not specified)
  • Bay leaves (香叶 (xiāngyè), quantity not specified)
  • Edible salt (食用盐 (shíyòng yán), small amount for washing eggs)

Instructions

  1. Gently wash the quail eggs with edible salt to clean them. Drain the water.
  2. Place coarse salt in the rice cooker inner pot and spread it evenly. (Fine salt can be substituted, using less and spreading thinly).
  3. Add flower pepper, two star anise, ginger slices, and bay leaves to the salt.
  4. Add the quail eggs to the rice cooker, arranging them in a single layer.
  5. Pour 300g of coarse salt over the eggs. Do not stir.
  6. Add another layer of spices (star anise, bay leaves, flower pepper, ginger slices) on top of the salt and spread evenly.
  7. Place the rice cooker inner pot into the appliance and press the "cook" button.
  8. After the rice cooker switches off, let the eggs steam for another two hours.
  9. Carefully remove the eggs, gently breaking the hardened salt shell. The eggs should float to the surface.
  10. Crack the shells and enjoy the salt-baked quail eggs. The leftover salt can be reused after cooling and storing it in a sealed bag.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=hNqkGU8-ONM

sandginger_chicken.txt - 沙姜鸡 (Shājiāng jī)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and tender Sand Ginger Chicken.
  • Master the technique of cleaning and preparing a whole chicken.
  • Understand how to create a flavorful sauce to complement the chicken.

Ingredients

  • 1 whole three-yellow chicken (三黄鸡 - Sānhuáng jī)
  • 1 tablespoon salt (盐 - Yán)
  • 101°C boiling water (101度开水 - 101 dù kāishuǐ)
  • 1 packet salt-baked chicken powder (盐焗鸡粉 - Yánjú jīfěn)
  • Red onion (红葱头 - Hóng cōngtóu)
  • Ginger (生姜 - Shēngjiāng)
  • Sand ginger (沙姜 - Shājiāng)
  • 2 scallions (葱叶 - Cōngyè)
  • Cooking wine (料酒 - Liàojiǔ)
  • Vegetable oil (热油 - Rèyóu)
  • Soy sauce (生抽 - Shēng chōu)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油 - Háoyóu)
  • Sugar (白糖 - Báitáng)
  • Mushroom seasoning (松茸鲜 - Sōngróng xiān)

Instructions

  1. Sprinkle salt on the chicken and rub thoroughly to clean and disinfect. Rinse with water. Remove innards and excess fat. Rinse again.
  2. Blanch the chicken in 101°C boiling water to tighten the skin and enhance color. Cool slightly.
  3. Prepare the ingredients: thinly slice ginger, finely chop sand ginger and red onion. Finely chop scallions.
  4. Add salt-baked chicken powder, chopped scallions, half of the red onion, sand ginger, and cooking wine to the chicken. Rub evenly inside and out.
  5. Stuff the chicken cavity with remaining ginger, scallions, and sand ginger. Marinate for 30 minutes.
  6. While the chicken marinates, prepare the sauce: heat oil, add remaining red onion and sand ginger to release their aroma. Stir in soy sauce, oyster sauce, sugar, and mushroom seasoning. Mix well.
  7. Place ginger slices in a steamer. Steam the marinated chicken for 25 minutes on high heat. Let it rest for 5 minutes after turning off the heat.
  8. Remove the chicken and let it cool slightly. Dissect the chicken into smaller pieces. Remove the innards.
  9. Arrange the chicken pieces on a plate. Pour the prepared sand ginger sauce over the chicken.
  10. Serve and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=CXl655fqZUQ

sausage_potato.txt - 香肠炒土豆片 (Xiāngcháng chǎo tǔdòupiàn)

Objectives

  • Learn to cook delicious and easy sausage and potato dish.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful cooking technique.
  • Understand how to prepare ingredients for optimal results.

Ingredients

  • 自制香肠 (zìzhì xiāngchāng) - Homemade Sausage (amount not specified)
  • 土豆 (tǔdòu) - Potatoes (2)
  • 面粉 (miànfěn) - Flour (small amount for cleaning sausage)
  • 蒜 (suàn) - Garlic (amount not specified)
  • 红线椒 (hóng xiàn jiāo) - Red Chili Peppers (amount not specified)
  • 干海椒 (gān hǎijiāo) - Dried Chili Peppers (a handful)
  • 大蒜苗 (dàsuàn miáo) - Garlic Sprouts (amount not specified)
  • 武安酸辣 (Wǔ'ān suānlà) - Wu'an Spicy and Sour Sauce (1 small spoon)
  • 松茸鲜 (sōngróng xiān) - Matsutake Fresh Seasoning (1 small spoon)
  • 白糖 (báitáng) - White Sugar (a pinch)
  • 生抽 (shēng chōu) - Light Soy Sauce (small amount)
  • 清水 (qīngshuǐ) - Water (small amount)
  • 食用油 (shíyòng yóu) - Cooking Oil (small amount)

Instructions

  1. Clean the homemade sausage with warm water, add a little flour, and wipe it with paper towels for a thorough clean.
  2. Rinse the pot with water twice to remove any residual flour.
  3. Boil the sausage in rice water for 15 minutes on low heat after the water boils.
  4. Peel and clean the potatoes, cut them into thick slices, and soak them in water for 10 minutes to prevent oxidation.
  5. Prepare the garlic, red chili peppers, and garlic sprouts by chopping them.
  6. After 15 minutes, remove the sausage and let it cool.
  7. Blanch the potato slices in boiling water for about 80 seconds until translucent.
  8. Drain the potatoes and cut the cooled sausage into thick slices.
  9. Heat the oil in a pan, stir-fry the sausage for about 30 seconds.
  10. Add the potato slices and stir-fry until they are combined with the sausage.
  11. Add dried chilies, stir-fry until fragrant.
  12. Add the chopped chili peppers and garlic, stir-fry until well combined.
  13. Season with Wu'an spicy and sour sauce, Matsutake fresh seasoning, a pinch of sugar, and a small amount of light soy sauce and water.
  14. Stir-fry until the seasoning is melted and the potatoes are cooked through.
  15. Add the garlic sprouts and stir-fry until wilted.
  16. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=7stKwziazbU

scrambled_eggs_with_mushrooms.txt - Scrambled Eggs with Mushrooms

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious scrambled egg dish with mushrooms.
  • Master a simple cooking method suitable for beginners.
  • Learn to prepare and cook various ingredients effectively.

Ingredients

  • 3 eggs
  • A handful of shiitake mushrooms
  • A handful of white jade mushrooms
  • A dash of salt
  • A few drops of white vinegar
  • A handful of washed garlic moss (approximately 3-4 cm long, chopped)
  • A piece of ginger (thinly sliced, then minced)
  • Some garlic (minced)
  • Some millet peppers (thinly sliced; red pepper can be substituted)
  • A small amount of light soy sauce
  • A dash of oyster sauce
  • A small amount of table salt
  • A few fresh matsutake mushrooms (optional)
  • A little sugar
  • A small teaspoon of potato starch
  • A little water
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Crack 3 eggs into a bowl.
  2. Add salt and a few drops of white vinegar to the eggs.
  3. Whisk the eggs until the whites and yolks are fully combined and no lumps remain.
  4. Wash and slice the shiitake and white jade mushrooms into slightly thicker pieces. Trim off the root ends of the white jade mushrooms.
  5. Clean the mushrooms thoroughly and set aside.
  6. Chop the garlic moss into 3-4 cm pieces.
  7. Mince the ginger and garlic.
  8. Thinly slice the millet peppers.
  9. Prepare the sauce: Combine light soy sauce, oyster sauce, salt, matsutake mushrooms (optional), sugar, potato starch, and water. Mix well until dissolved.
  10. Bring water to a boil in a pot.
  11. Blanch the seafood mushrooms for 30 seconds, then add a bit of sugar to remove any unpleasant odor. Immediately transfer to cold water to cool. Drain.
  12. Blanch the garlic moss for 40 seconds to remove oxalic acid. Transfer to cold water to cool, then drain.
  13. Heat oil in a wok or pan.
  14. Pour in the whisked eggs and scramble until cooked through. Remove from pan and set aside.
  15. Add the minced garlic, ginger, and millet peppers to the pan and sauté until fragrant.
  16. Add the mushrooms and stir-fry over high heat until moisture evaporates (about 1 minute).
  17. Add the scrambled eggs back to the pan.
  18. Pour in the prepared sauce and stir until everything is well combined and the sauce is absorbed.
  19. Serve hot with rice.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=lZmC1cDlI1Y

shanghai_green_stir_fry.txt - Shanghai Green Stir-Fry 上海青炒法

Objectives

  • Learn to stir-fry Shanghai greens to maintain their bright green color.
  • Master a cleaning method to remove pesticides and impurities.
  • Achieve a flavorful and crunchy stir-fry with properly cooked stems and leaves.

Ingredients

  • Shanghai Greens (approximately 1 bunch)
  • 1 tablespoon white salt
  • 1 tablespoon baking soda
  • Handful of garlic (minced)
  • Small bowl of dried chili peppers (finely chopped)
  • 20 grams lard
  • 1 tablespoon white table salt
  • A pinch of white sugar
  • A dash of chicken powder (optional)
  • A dash of white sesame seeds

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Shanghai Greens: Remove any bad or yellowed leaves. Thoroughly wash the greens.
  2. Soak and Clean: In a bowl, add 1 tablespoon of salt and 1 tablespoon of baking soda to the greens. Mix well and let soak for 2 minutes. Rinse thoroughly until the water runs clear. Drain and set aside.
  3. Prepare Aromatics: Mince the garlic and finely chop the dried chilies.
  4. Separate Stems and Leaves: Separate the stems from the leaves of the Shanghai greens. Cut larger stems in half.
  5. Heat the Lard: Heat 20 grams of lard in an 82-year-old iron pot (or any wok) over medium heat until melted.
  6. Sauté Aromatics: Add the minced garlic and chopped chilies to the hot lard. Sauté until fragrant.
  7. Stir-fry Stems: Add the Shanghai green stems to the pot. Stir-fry for about 1 minute until slightly softened.
  8. Stir-fry Leaves: Add the Shanghai green leaves to the pot. Stir-fry for 5-8 times until tender.
  9. Season: Add 1 tablespoon of salt, a pinch of sugar, a dash of chicken powder (optional), and a dash of white sesame seeds. Stir-fry for about 10 seconds to combine flavors.
  10. Serve: Remove from heat and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=9PZoJEAQWN8

shan_yao_ge_da_tang.txt - 山药疙瘩汤 (Shān yào gé da tāng)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple, delicious, and nutritious yam soup.
  • Master a quick and easy yam preparation method to prevent skin irritation.
  • Create a flavorful and visually appealing soup suitable for all ages.

Ingredients

  • 2 铁棍山药 (tiě gùn shān yào) - Iron stick yams
  • 2 scoops plain flour (普通面粉 - pǔ tōng miàn fěn)
  • 1 tomato (西红柿 - xī hóng shì), diced
  • Several small pieces of Chinese flowering cabbage (小白菜 - xiǎo bái cài), diced
  • 2 eggs (土鸡蛋 - tǔ jī dàn)
  • Salt (食用盐 - shí yòng yán)
  • A few drops of white vinegar (白醋 - bái cù)
  • Several scallions (小葱 - xiǎo cōng), chopped
  • Some ginger (老姜 - lǎo jiāng), minced
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shí yòng yóu)
  • Water (山泉水 - shān quán shuǐ)
  • Sesame oil (小磨香油 - xiǎo mó xiāng yóu)
  • Light soy sauce (生抽 - shēng chōu)
  • Rice vinegar (陈醋 - chén cù)

Instructions

  1. Peel two iron stick yams using a peeler, wearing disposable gloves to avoid skin irritation. Wash and chop into small pieces.
  2. Place the yam pieces in a bowl, add two scoops of flour, and mix thoroughly until each piece is coated.
  3. Dice one tomato and several pieces of Chinese flowering cabbage. Set aside.
  4. In a bowl, whisk two eggs with a dash of salt and a few drops of white vinegar until well combined.
  5. Chop several scallions and some ginger into fine pieces. Set aside.
  6. Heat oil in a pan. Add the egg mixture and scramble, then remove and set aside.
  7. Add more oil to the pan, then add the minced ginger and white parts of the scallions. Sauté until fragrant.
  8. Add the diced tomatoes and sauté until softened and releasing their juices. Season with a small spoonful of salt.
  9. Add a generous amount of water, cover, and bring to a boil.
  10. Add the yam pieces, stirring to prevent sticking. Cook until they float. Skim off any foam.
  11. After about two minutes, add the diced Chinese flowering cabbage and the scrambled eggs. Stir well.
  12. Season with a pinch of salt, a little light soy sauce, and a small amount of rice vinegar. Stir.
  13. Before serving, drizzle with sesame oil and sprinkle with chopped scallions.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=w4a5jELpuD8

shan_yao_ji_dan_tang.txt - 山药鸡蛋汤 (Shān yào jī dàn tāng)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious yam and egg soup.
  • Understand how to prepare yam to prevent skin irritation.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful broth using readily available ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 铁棍山药 (Tiě gùn shān yào) - Iron stick yam (amount not specified, adjust to your needs)
  • 鸡蛋 (Jī dàn) - Eggs (3)
  • 胡萝卜 (Hú luó bo) - Carrot (1)
  • 香菇 (Xiāng gū) - Shiitake mushrooms (a few)
  • 小葱 (Xiǎo cōng) - Scallions (a few)
  • 香菜 (Xiāng cài) - Cilantro (a few)
  • 猪油 (Zhū yóu) - Lard (a small amount)
  • 姜 (Jiāng) - Ginger (a small piece)
  • 食盐 (Shí yán) - Salt (a small half spoon)
  • 胡椒粉 (Hú jiāo fěn) - Pepper powder (a small half spoon)
  • 鸡精 (Jī jīng) - Chicken bouillon (a small half spoon)
  • 生抽 (Shēng chōu) - Light soy sauce (a small amount)
  • 清水 (Qīng shuǐ) - Water (a small amount for the seasoning)
  • 淀粉 (Diàn fěn) - Starch (an appropriate amount for thickening)
  • 纯净水 (Chún jìng shuǐ) - Purified water (amount not specified, adjust to your needs)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the yam: Wear disposable gloves to avoid skin irritation from the yam's sap. Gently pat the yam to remove excess moisture. Cut into small pieces. Set aside.
  2. Prepare the eggs: Crack 3 eggs into a bowl. Whisk thoroughly until the egg whites and yolks are well combined and smooth. Set aside.
  3. Prepare the vegetables: Dice the carrot and finely chop the shiitake mushrooms. Chop the scallions and cilantro into small pieces. Set aside.
  4. Prepare the seasoning: In a small bowl, combine salt, pepper, chicken bouillon, a small amount of light soy sauce, and a little water. Mix well until dissolved. Prepare a cornstarch slurry in a separate bowl.
  5. Sauté aromatics: Heat a pot, add a small amount of lard, and sauté the minced ginger until fragrant.
  6. Cook vegetables: Add the diced carrots and shiitake mushrooms to the pot and stir-fry for about 1 minute.
  7. Add water and yam: Add an appropriate amount of purified water, cover, and simmer for 1-2 minutes. Add the yam, stir gently to distribute, and cook over high heat for 3-5 minutes until tender.
  8. Add seasoning and thicken: Add the prepared seasoning, stir, and cook for 1 minute to allow the flavors to meld. Gradually add the cornstarch slurry while stirring continuously until the desired consistency is reached.
  9. Add eggs: Turn off the heat. Slowly pour the egg mixture into the pot. Cover and let it sit for a few seconds to set. The residual heat will cook the eggs.
  10. Garnish and serve: Sprinkle with chopped scallions and cilantro. Stir gently and serve immediately in bowls.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=lPGidwAnTGc

shan_yao_xiao_mantou.txt - 山药小馒头 (Shān yào xiǎo mántou)

Objectives

  • Learn to make fluffy and soft yam buns without adding water.
  • Understand the benefits of yam for digestion and health.
  • Create a nutritious and delicious breakfast or snack for family.

Ingredients

  • 几个铁棍山药 (Jǐ ge tiě gùn shān yào) - Several iron rod yams
  • 一个去皮的胡萝卜 (Yīgè qù pí de hú luó bo) - One peeled carrot
  • 一点白糖 (Yī diǎn bái táng) - A little white sugar
  • 两个大鸡蛋 (Liǎng ge dà jī dàn) - Two large eggs
  • 5克酵母 (5 kè jiàomǔ) - 5 grams of yeast
  • 400克面粉 (400 kè miàn fěn) - 400 grams of flour

Instructions

  1. Prepare several iron rod yams. Wear disposable gloves to prevent skin irritation from yam sap. Peel, wash, and cut the yams into uniform small sections. Steam for 15 minutes until easily pierced with chopsticks.
  2. While the yams are steaming, prepare the carrot. Peel, thinly slice, julienne, and finely dice the carrot. Set aside.
  3. Once the yams are steamed, transfer them to a large bowl. Add a little white sugar and mash into a smooth puree.
  4. Add two large eggs to the yam puree and mix well. The temperature of the yam will decrease.
  5. Add 5 grams of yeast and 400 grams of flour gradually, mixing until a large, crumbly mixture forms.
  6. Knead the mixture into a soft dough. Add the diced carrots and continue mixing.
  7. Cover the dough and let it rise in a warm place until doubled in size.
  8. Once doubled, punch down the dough to release air. Knead for 2-3 minutes to develop gluten.
  9. Roll the dough into a long rope, divide it into equal-sized portions, and roll each portion into a small rope.
  10. Use a scraper to cut the small ropes into small bun shapes. Place them in a tray lined with oiled paper.
  11. Let the shaped buns rise in a steamer for 10 minutes.
  12. Steam over medium heat for 12 minutes, then let them sit for another 3 minutes to prevent shrinkage.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=o4MFc1jblEg

shuizhengdan.txt - 水蒸蛋 (Shuǐ zhēng dàn) - Steamed Egg

Objectives

  • Learn to make smooth, tender steamed eggs without air bubbles.
  • Understand how to prepare eggs for optimal texture.
  • Master the steaming time based on bowl depth.

Ingredients

  • Several fresh eggs (number not specified)
  • Salt (amount not specified)
  • Water (1.2 times the volume of the beaten eggs, or 1:1.5 ratio for experienced cooks)
  • Light soy sauce (for garnish)
  • Sesame oil (for garnish)
  • Chopped scallions (for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Prepare fresh eggs: Check for freshness by gently shaking; fresh eggs will have no noticeable movement inside. Wash eggs with salt water for 5 minutes to remove residue. Discard eggs with cracked shells.
  2. Crack eggs into a large bowl. Add a pinch of salt and whisk thoroughly until the egg whites and yolks are fully combined and no lumps remain.
  3. Add 1.2 times the volume of boiling water to the beaten eggs (or 1:1.5 ratio for experienced cooks), whisking continuously.
  4. Filter the mixture through a fine-mesh sieve to remove air bubbles. Use a small spoon to remove any remaining bubbles on the surface.
  5. Transfer the filtered egg mixture to a heatproof bowl.
  6. Place the bowl in a steamer, cover, and steam over high heat for 7.5 minutes (or 10 minutes for deeper bowls, 8 minutes for shallower bowls like the one shown).
  7. Remove from steamer and let cool slightly.
  8. Drizzle light soy sauce and sesame oil over the steamed eggs.
  9. Cut the steamed egg into smaller pieces using a small knife for easier serving.
  10. Garnish with chopped scallions.
  11. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=B3Y9SeSrzU0

silguachaochengzi.txt - 丝瓜炒蛏子 (Silgua Chao Chengzi)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple, delicious, and affordable Silgua Chao Chengzi (丝瓜炒蛏子).
  • Master the technique of stir-frying to achieve a vibrant green color and tender texture.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients to create a refreshing summer dish.

Ingredients

  • 2 丝瓜 (Silgua) - loofah squash
  • 一些蛏子 (yīxiē chèngzi) - some razor clams
  • 海鲜菇 (hǎixiān gū) - shiitake mushrooms
  • 一块生姜 (yī kuài shēngjiāng) - a piece of ginger
  • 少量山泉水 (shǎoliàng shānquán shuǐ) - a small amount of spring water
  • 少许食用油 (shǎoxǔ shíyòng yóu) - a little cooking oil
  • 一小勺食盐 (yī xiǎo sháo shíyán) - a small spoon of salt

Instructions

  1. Peel and chop the loofah squash into bite-sized pieces. Wash and set aside.
  2. Clean the shiitake mushrooms, remove the roots, and set aside.
  3. Thinly slice the ginger.
  4. Steam the razor clams with a little spring water for 2 minutes until cooked. Remove and set aside, reserving the cooking liquid.
  5. Separate the clam meat from the shells.
  6. Blanch the loofah squash in boiling water for 49 seconds until bright green. Drain well.
  7. Blanch the shiitake mushrooms for 20 seconds. Drain well.
  8. Heat oil in a wok or pan over medium heat. Add ginger and stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Add the loofah squash, shiitake mushrooms, and razor clams to the wok. Stir-fry over high heat until the moisture evaporates.
  10. Add a small spoonful of salt and stir-fry for about 80 seconds.
  11. Pour in the reserved clam cooking liquid and simmer for 1 minute.
  12. Thicken the sauce with a cornstarch slurry (if desired).
  13. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6l_kjWtDosE

silgua_chaozhengzi.txt - 丝瓜炒蛏子 (Silgua Chao Zhengzi)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple, delicious, and affordable Silgua Chao Zhengzi (丝瓜炒蛏子).
  • Master the technique of cooking fresh clams and preserving their flavor.
  • Understand the importance of blanching vegetables for optimal color and texture.

Ingredients

  • 2 条丝瓜 (tiáo sīguā) - 2 pieces of loofah
  • Some 蛏子 (chèngzi) - clams (amount not specified)
  • Some 海鲜菇 (hǎixiān gū) - seafood mushrooms (amount not specified)
  • 1 块生姜 (kuài shēngjiāng) - 1 piece of ginger
  • 少量山泉水 (shǎoliàng shānquán shuǐ) - a small amount of spring water
  • 少许食用油 (shǎoxǔ shíyòng yóu) - a little cooking oil
  • 一小勺食盐 (yī xiǎo sháo shíyán) - a small spoon of salt

Instructions

  1. Peel and clean the loofah, remove the ends, and cut into chunks. Set aside.
  2. Clean the seafood mushrooms, remove the roots, and set aside.
  3. Peel and thinly slice the ginger. Set aside.
  4. Steam the clams with a small amount of spring water for 2 minutes until cooked. Remove and separate the clam meat from the shells. Reserve the clam broth.
  5. Blanch the loofah in boiling water for 49 seconds until bright green. Drain well.
  6. Blanch the seafood mushrooms for about 20 seconds. Drain well.
  7. Heat a little oil in a wok or pan. Add the ginger and stir-fry until fragrant.
  8. Add the loofah and seafood mushrooms, stir-fry until slightly softened.
  9. Add the clams and stir-fry over high heat until the moisture evaporates.
  10. Add a small spoonful of salt. Stir well.
  11. Pour in the reserved clam broth and simmer for 1 minute.
  12. Thicken the sauce with a light cornstarch slurry (if desired, not explicitly mentioned).
  13. Serve immediately.

silgua_hebao_dan.txt - 丝瓜荷包蛋 (Silgua Hebao Dan)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and juicy Silgua Hebao Dan (丝瓜荷包蛋).
  • Master the technique of preventing silk squash from oxidizing.
  • Understand the importance of high-heat oil for frying eggs.

Ingredients

  • Several fresh, tender silk squashes (丝瓜 - sīguā)
  • Several eggs (鸡蛋 - jīdàn)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòngyóu)
  • Salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • White vinegar (白醋 - báicù)
  • Scallions (小葱 - xiǎocōng), chopped
  • Ginger (生姜 - shēngjiāng), minced
  • Garlic (蒜 - suàn), minced
  • Chili peppers (小米椒 - xiǎomǐjiāo), finely sliced (optional; can substitute with large red pepper)
  • Soy sauce (生抽 - shēngchōu)
  • Sugar (白糖 - báitáng)

Instructions

  1. Peel and cut the silk squash into bite-sized pieces.
  2. Place the silk squash in a bowl of water with white vinegar and salt to prevent oxidation. Let it soak.
  3. Chop scallions, mince ginger and garlic, and slice chili peppers.
  4. Crack eggs into a bowl (do not whisk).
  5. Heat oil in a pan until slightly smoking.
  6. Fry the eggs until golden brown on both sides.
  7. Cut the fried eggs into small pieces.
  8. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add oil and salt.
  9. Blanch the silk squash for 90 seconds.
  10. Drain the silk squash.
  11. Heat the remaining oil from frying the eggs in a pan.
  12. Sauté the scallions, ginger, garlic, and chili peppers until fragrant.
  13. Add the blanched silk squash and fried eggs to the pan.
  14. Season with soy sauce and sugar.
  15. Stir-fry for about 50 seconds.
  16. Turn off the heat and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=0TZcTc1XP6c

silgua_hebaodan.txt - 丝瓜荷包蛋 (Sīguā Hébāodàn) - 丝瓜荷包蛋

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and juicy Silgua Hebaodan dish.
  • Master a simple cooking method for this flavorful recipe.
  • Understand how to prevent silk squash from oxidizing.

Ingredients

  • Several fresh, tender silk squashes (丝瓜 - sīguā)
  • Several eggs (鸡蛋 - jīdàn)
  • Some scallions (小葱 - xiǎocōng), ginger (生姜 - shēngjiāng), and garlic (蒜 - suàn)
  • A few millet peppers (小米椒 - xiǎomǐjiāo) or red peppers (大红椒 - dà hóngjiāo)
  • Appropriate amount of cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòngyóu)
  • Salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • White vinegar (白醋 - báicù)
  • Light soy sauce (生抽 - shēngchōu)
  • Sugar (白糖 - báitáng)

Instructions

  1. Peel and cut the silk squash into bite-sized pieces.
  2. Place the cut silk squash in water with a little white vinegar and salt to prevent oxidation. Let it soak.
  3. Crack eggs into a bowl (do not whisk).
  4. Chop scallions, ginger, and garlic into fine pieces. Mince the millet peppers (or red peppers).
  5. Drain the silk squash.
  6. Heat oil in a pan until slightly smoking.
  7. Fry the eggs until golden brown on both sides, then cut into small pieces.
  8. In a separate pot, bring water to a boil. Add a little oil and salt.
  9. Blanch the silk squash for 90 seconds. Drain.
  10. Use the remaining oil from frying the eggs to sauté the scallions, ginger, garlic, and peppers.
  11. Add the blanched silk squash and fried eggs to the pan.
  12. Season with light soy sauce and sugar. Stir-fry for about 50 seconds.
  13. Serve immediately.

simple_minced_pork_tofu.txt - Simple Minced Pork Tofu

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare tender tofu for cooking.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful minced pork and tofu recipe.
  • Understand how to create a smooth and thickened sauce.

Ingredients

  • 2 pieces fresh soft tofu
  • Minced pork (amount not specified, adjust to preference)
  • 1 onion, finely chopped
  • 1 piece ginger, thinly sliced then minced
  • A small handful of garlic, minced
  • Salt (to taste)
  • Chicken broth (amount not specified)
  • Pepper (to taste)
  • 1 tablespoon soybean paste
  • Dark soy sauce (amount not specified, for coloring)
  • Water (for sauce and boiling tofu)
  • Water starch (to thicken the sauce)
  • Sesame oil (optional, for garnish)
  • Chopped green onions (optional, for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Tofu: Cut the tofu in half horizontally and then vertically into smaller pieces. Boil in salted water for 1 minute to remove any beany smell and firm the tofu. Remove and drain well.
  2. Prepare the Meat: Finely mince the pork. (Alternatively, use a meat grinder).
  3. Prepare Aromatics: Finely chop the onion, mince the ginger, and mince the garlic.
  4. Stir-fry the Meat: Heat oil in a pan or wok. Add the minced pork and stir-fry until fragrant and the color changes.
  5. Add Aromatics: Add the chopped onion, ginger, and garlic to the pan. Continue stir-frying until softened.
  6. Season and Simmer: Season with salt, chicken broth, pepper, and soybean paste. Stir-fry until fragrant. Add a small amount of water, stir well.
  7. Add Color and Thicken: Add dark soy sauce for color. Stir in water starch to thicken the sauce. Simmer for 1-2 minutes until the sauce thickens and coats the ingredients.
  8. Combine and Serve: Add the boiled tofu to the pan. Gently stir to combine and heat through (about 1-2 minutes). Garnish with sesame oil and chopped green onions, if desired. Serve hot with rice.
