slow_cooked_pork_ribs_with_potatoes.txt - Slow Cooked Pork Ribs with Potatoes

Objectives

  • Learn to cook tender and juicy pork ribs without boiling.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful recipe perfect for family gatherings.
  • Prepare a dish that showcases culinary skills during festivals.

Ingredients

  • 2 kg fresh pork ribs (approximately 50 yuan)
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • Water (for soaking and cooking)
  • 1 yellow heart potato
  • 1 onion
  • Ginger
  • Garlic
  • Green onions
  • 1 star anise
  • 1 fragrant leaf
  • A small piece of cinnamon
  • A handful of peppercorns
  • Flour (for cleaning ribs)
  • Dark soy sauce (for coloring)
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Cut pork ribs into smaller pieces.
  2. Place ribs in a bowl, add salt, and enough water to cover. Mix well and soak for 20 minutes to draw out blood.
  3. Prepare the potatoes: peel, wash, cut in half, then into smaller pieces. Soak in water to prevent oxidation.
  4. Prepare aromatics: chop onion, ginger, and garlic. Cut green onions into larger pieces.
  5. Prepare spices: gather star anise, fragrant leaf, cinnamon, and peppercorns.
  6. Grate some ginger and finely chop some green onions for later use.
  7. Drain the soaked ribs. Sprinkle with flour, and use your hands to mix thoroughly to absorb blood and impurities. Let it sit for about 2 minutes until sticky.
  8. Rinse the ribs several times with water until the water runs clear.
  9. Add sliced ginger and green onions to the rinsed ribs, and rub them gently to infuse the flavor. Let it sit for about 10 minutes.
  10. Heat a wok with some cooking oil. Add potatoes and stir-fry until golden brown on all sides. Set aside.
  11. Heat the wok again with oil. Add the ribs and stir-fry over high heat until slightly dry to remove odor.
  12. Stir-fry the ribs for about 3 minutes until lightly browned.
  13. Add star anise, onion, ginger, and garlic to the wok and stir-fry until fragrant.
  14. Add dark soy sauce for color.
  15. Add boiling water to the wok, cover, and simmer over low heat for 40 minutes.
  16. After 40 minutes, add the fried potatoes, some salt, and stir well. Cover and simmer for another 5 minutes.
  17. Stir a few times during the last 5 minutes to ensure even cooking.
  18. Finally, add the reserved chopped green onions and stir-fry briefly to release their aroma.
  19. Turn off the heat. Serve the slow-cooked pork ribs with potatoes hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=MPXCVjYOVK4

snowflake_meatball.txt - 雪花丸子 (Xuěhuā Wánzi)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and visually appealing Snowflake Meatballs.
  • Master the technique of combining tofu, eggs, and glutinous rice for a unique texture.
  • Create a flavorful filling using readily available ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 200g glutinous rice (糯米, nuòmǐ)
  • 1 bowl of water
  • 1 block of soft tofu (嫩豆腐, nèn dòufu)
  • 2 free-range eggs (土雞蛋, tǔ jīdàn)
  • A handful of scallions, chopped (蔥花, cōnghuā)
  • 1 piece of ginger, minced (薑末, jiāngmò)
  • Leftover lotus root, diced (蓮藕丁, lián'ǒu dīng) (or water chestnuts as substitute)
  • Fatty and lean pork, minced (肉末, ròumò)
  • 1 tsp salt (鹽, yán)
  • 1 tbsp Song Rong Xian seasoning (松茸鮮, sōngrōng xiān)
  • Generous amount of pepper powder (胡椒粉, hújiāofěn)
  • 2 tbsp potato starch or cornstarch (馬鈴薯澱粉/玉米澱粉, mǎlíngshǔ diànfěn/yùmǐ diànfěn)

Instructions

  1. Soak 200g of glutinous rice in a bowl of water for 1 hour until fully expanded.
  2. Prepare a block of soft tofu, crack in 2 eggs, and mix thoroughly with disposable gloves until completely combined and the tofu is shredded. Set aside.
  3. Finely chop scallions and set aside.
  4. Mince ginger and set aside.
  5. Dice leftover lotus root (or water chestnuts) into small pieces and set aside.
  6. Mince fatty and lean pork into fine pieces.
  7. Combine minced pork, diced lotus root, minced ginger, and half of the chopped scallions into the tofu and egg mixture.
  8. Add salt, Song Rong Xian seasoning, a generous amount of pepper powder, and mix well until all ingredients are evenly distributed and the mixture is smooth.
  9. Stir in 2 tablespoons of potato starch or cornstarch and mix well.
  10. Rinse the soaked glutinous rice and drain thoroughly.
  11. Mix the glutinous rice until it reaches a slightly thick consistency.
  12. Using your hands, shape the tofu and meat mixture into small balls.
  13. Roll each meatball in the glutinous rice to coat evenly.
  14. Place the coated meatballs in a steamer basket.
  15. Steam over high heat for 20 minutes with the lid on.
  16. After steaming, remove from steamer and garnish with remaining chopped scallions.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=4_EWv5L3tw0

spinach_egg_roll.txt - 菠菜鸡蛋卷

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and nutritious spinach egg rolls.
  • Master a simple and quick cooking method for spinach.
  • Create a versatile dipping sauce to enhance the flavor.

Ingredients

  • 1 bunch spinach (菠菜)
  • 3 eggs (鸡蛋)
  • 1 carrot (胡萝卜)
  • 60g all-purpose flour (普通面粉)
  • 1 sheet beancurd sheet (千张/豆皮)
  • A few drops of white vinegar (白醋)
  • Salt (盐)
  • Cooking oil (油)
  • Spring onions (葱白)
  • Pickled chili peppers (小米椒)
  • Garlic (蒜)
  • White sesame seeds (白芝麻)
  • Sugar (白糖)
  • Soy sauce (生抽)
  • Rice vinegar (陈醋)

Instructions

  1. Trim and wash the spinach thoroughly, removing any dirt.
  2. Cut the spinach into 3-4cm segments.
  3. Peel and thinly slice a carrot, then julienne it into thicker strands.
  4. Crack 3 eggs into a bowl, add a few drops of white vinegar, and whisk until smooth.
  5. Bring water to a boil in a pot, add a pinch of salt.
  6. Blanch the carrot for 15 seconds, then remove and drain.
  7. Blanch the spinach for 10 seconds, immediately transfer to cold water to cool and drain thoroughly.
  8. Combine the blanched spinach and carrots in a large bowl.
  9. Add the whisked eggs and mix well to combine all ingredients.
  10. Stir in 60g of all-purpose flour until a thick batter forms.
  11. Take one sheet of beancurd sheet and spread a thin layer of the spinach mixture evenly.
  12. Tightly roll the beancurd sheet.
  13. Repeat steps 11 and 12 with the remaining beancurd sheet and batter.
  14. Place the rolls in a steamer and steam for 15 minutes.
  15. Let cool, then slice into 2cm thick pieces.
  16. Prepare the dipping sauce: finely chop spring onions, pickled chili peppers, and garlic. Add white sesame seeds.
  17. Pour hot oil over the chopped ingredients to enhance the aroma.
  18. Season with a pinch of salt, a tiny bit of sugar, 1 tablespoon of soy sauce, and ½ tablespoon of rice vinegar. Mix well.
  19. Arrange the spinach egg rolls on a plate, drizzle with the dipping sauce, and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_nwQH_nRFvE

spinach_egg_soup.txt - 菠菜鸡蛋汤

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious spinach and egg soup.
  • Master the techniques for preparing spinach and achieving a smooth, flavorful broth.
  • Understand the importance of using fresh ingredients and proper cooking methods.

Ingredients

  • 1 small bunch of spinach (about 3 RMB worth)
  • 1 small carrot
  • 1 small piece of ginger
  • 1 small bunch of scallions
  • 2 eggs
  • 1 tablespoon cornstarch
  • Water
  • Salt
  • Cooking oil -松茸鲜 (Matsutake mushroom seasoning) -Pepper -Light soy sauce

Instructions

  1. Trim the roots off the spinach, wash thoroughly, and cut into small pieces. Set aside.
  2. Peel and finely slice the carrot. Set aside.
  3. Mince the white parts of the scallions and finely chop the green parts separately. Set aside.
  4. Peel and julienne the ginger. Set aside.
  5. Whisk two eggs in a bowl until light and frothy. Set aside.
  6. Mix cornstarch with water to create a slurry. Set aside.
  7. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add a small amount of salt and oil.
  8. Blanch the spinach in the boiling water for 30 seconds.
  9. Immediately remove the spinach, rinse with cold water, and squeeze out excess water. Set aside. (Blanching prevents the spinach from losing nutrients and keeps it vibrant green).
  10. Heat a small amount of oil in a clean pot or pan. Add the ginger and white parts of the scallions, sauté until fragrant.
  11. Add a bowl of water (preferably spring water), salt, 松茸鲜 (Matsutake mushroom seasoning), pepper, and light soy sauce to the pot. Bring to a boil.
  12. Add the carrot slices and simmer for 2 minutes.
  13. Stir in the cornstarch slurry until the soup thickens slightly.
  14. Turn off the heat and quickly pour in the whisked eggs, stirring gently to create egg ribbons.
  15. Add the blanched spinach, stir gently, and heat for 30 seconds.
  16. Garnish with chopped scallions and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Y_vPCQsuNKg

spinach_egg_stir_fry.txt - Spinach and Egg Stir-fry

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare spinach for cooking, maximizing nutrient retention.
  • Create a flavorful and easy spinach and egg dish.
  • Master a simple yet delicious sauce for the stir-fry.

Ingredients

  • 1 bunch fresh spinach (approx. 2.50 yuan)
  • 3 free-range eggs
  • 1 tablespoon soybean paste
  • 1/2 tablespoon light soy sauce
  • 1 tablespoon oyster sauce
  • Several fresh matsutake mushrooms (optional, amount not specified)
  • 1 teaspoon cornstarch
  • Water (amount not specified)
  • Rice vinegar (amount not specified)
  • Several cloves garlic, minced
  • Cooking oil (amount not specified)
  • Table salt (amount not specified)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Spinach: Carefully trim the spinach roots, scrubbing to remove dirt. Rinse thoroughly under running water until the water runs clear. This removes sediment often found on the roots.
  2. Cut the Spinach: Make a lengthwise cut through the root of the spinach to make it easier to cook. Cut the spinach into small pieces, separating the stems from the leaves. Set aside.
  3. Mince Garlic: Finely mince the garlic cloves.
  4. Prepare the Egg Mixture: Crack 3 eggs into a bowl. Add rice vinegar. Whisk until light and frothy. Set aside.
  5. Make the Sauce: In a bowl, combine soybean paste, light soy sauce, oyster sauce, matsutake mushrooms (if using), water, and cornstarch. Stir until well blended.
  6. Stir-fry the Eggs: Heat oil in a wok or pan. Add the egg mixture and cook, lightly scrambling the eggs into small pieces. Remove from pan and set aside.
  7. Stir-fry Garlic: Add more oil to the pan. Add the minced garlic and stir-fry until fragrant.
  8. Add Sauce and Eggs: Add the prepared sauce to the pan. Stir until slightly thickened. Add the previously cooked scrambled eggs and mix well. Set aside.
  9. Blanch Spinach: Bring water to a boil in a pot. Add a small amount of salt and oil. Add the spinach stems first and blanch for 10 seconds. Add the spinach leaves and blanch for another 15 seconds until bright green. Remove with a slotted spoon and drain well.
  10. Combine and Serve: Place the blanched spinach on a plate. Pour the egg and soy sauce mixture over the spinach. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=3BYpKZjJ91E

steamed_chicken_legs.txt - Steamed Chicken Legs with 3 Ways to Eat

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare and steam chicken legs for maximum flavor and tenderness.
  • Master three different flavor profiles for the chicken: lemon, sesame-ginger, and a simple savory broth.
  • Utilize simple ingredients to create a nutritious and delicious meal.

Ingredients

  • 4-5 fresh chicken legs
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • Several red dates
  • A small piece of Astragalus root (黄芪 huángqí)
  • 28 goji berries (枸杞 gōuqǐ)
  • 1-2 slices ginger per chicken leg
  • ½ lemon, thinly sliced (remove seeds)
  • A small handful of cilantro, chopped
  • Several cloves garlic, minced
  • A small handful of chili peppers, finely chopped
  • 2 tablespoons white sesame seeds
  • 1 tablespoon soy sauce (生抽 shēng chōu)
  • 1 tablespoon rice vinegar (陈醋 chéncù)
  • 1 teaspoon sugar (白糖 báitáng)
  • A small piece of sand ginger (沙姜 shā jiāng), minced
  • Hot oil (for aromatics)
  • Peanuts (optional)
  • Salt (for seasoning broth)

Instructions

  1. Wash chicken legs thoroughly with salt to remove impurities. Rinse well.
  2. Trim excess fat from chicken legs.
  3. Prick chicken legs with toothpicks to allow for faster cooking and better flavor penetration.
  4. Place red dates, Astragalus, and goji berries in a bowl in the center of a larger plate.
  5. Arrange chicken legs around the bowl on the plate, top each with 1-2 ginger slices.
  6. Steam chicken legs in a steamer over high heat for 30 minutes.
  7. While steaming, prepare the sauces: 7.1 Lemon Sauce: Thinly slice and deseed ½ lemon. Chop cilantro and mince garlic. 7.2 Sesame Ginger Sauce: Mince sand ginger and chili peppers. 7.3 Broth: Prepare a simple broth from the steaming liquid with salt.
  8. After steaming, remove chicken legs and let them cool slightly.
  9. Remove chicken meat from bones and shred into bite-sized pieces.
  10. Lemon Chicken: Mix shredded chicken with lemon slices, cilantro, garlic, peanuts (optional), soy sauce, rice vinegar, sugar, and sesame seeds. Toss well.
  11. Ginger Chicken: Mix a portion of shredded chicken with minced sand ginger, chili peppers, and salt. Drizzle with hot oil.
  12. Serve the remaining chicken broth seasoned with salt.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=lnphAWYDl8o

steamed_chicken.txt - Steamed Chicken (Cantonese Style)

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare a classic Cantonese steamed chicken dish.
  • Master the technique of cleaning and marinating chicken for optimal flavor and texture.
  • Understand the importance of steaming time and temperature for perfectly cooked chicken.

Ingredients

  • 1 whole chicken
  • 1 tablespoon flour
  • 2-3 green onions, chopped
  • 1 piece ginger, sliced
  • 8 grams salt
  • 20 grams cooking oil
  • 1 piece ginger, minced (for sauce)
  • 2 scallions, minced (for sauce)
  • Pinch of salt (for sauce)
  • Hot oil (for sauce)
  • Niulanshan liquor (optional, for steaming)

Instructions

  1. Prepare a basin of warm water. Add a spoonful of flour.
  2. Place the chicken in the warm water and massage thoroughly, inside and out, for 2-3 minutes to remove impurities and blood.
  3. Rinse the chicken twice more with water until the water runs clear.
  4. Drain the chicken and place it on a chopping board. Remove claws and toenails.
  5. Chop green onions and ginger. Place in a bowl with 8 grams of salt.
  6. Mix the chopped green onions and ginger with the chicken, massaging the mixture into the chicken's skin and flesh for several minutes.
  7. Marinate the chicken for 15 minutes.
  8. Add 20 grams of cooking oil to the marinated chicken and coat evenly.
  9. Prepare the sauce: mince ginger and scallions, mix with a pinch of salt and hot oil.
  10. Prepare a steamer with boiling water. Add Niulanshan liquor (optional).
  11. Place the marinated chicken on a plate in the steamer.
  12. Steam for 30 minutes.
  13. Turn off the heat. Let the chicken cool slightly before removing.
  14. Serve the chicken with its juices and the prepared ginger-scallion sauce.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=dktLvuGRiw4

steamed_radish.txt - Steamed Radish with Garlic, Ginger, and Chili

Objectives

  • Learn a simple, flavorful recipe for steamed radish.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients to create a delicious dish.
  • Master a quick and easy cooking method suitable for beginners.

Ingredients

  • 1 large white radish
  • Salt (for washing)
  • 1 large handful of flour
  • Several scallions, chopped
  • 1 piece ginger, thinly sliced then minced
  • Several cloves garlic, smashed then minced
  • Several dried chilies
  • 1 tablespoon white sesame seeds
  • Chili powder (to taste)
  • A pinch of Sichuan peppercorns or 13-spice blend
  • Salt (to taste)
  • Hot oil (for pouring)
  • A little soy sauce
  • A little rice vinegar

Instructions

  1. Wash the radish thoroughly in salted water.
  2. Peel the radish and use a grater to shred it into thin, even strips. Alternatively, finely slice the radish.
  3. Add a large handful of flour to the shredded radish and mix gently to absorb excess moisture.
  4. Gradually add more flour, mixing until each radish strip is evenly coated.
  5. Shake off excess flour.
  6. Spread the radish evenly in a plate.
  7. Steam over high heat for 6 minutes.
  8. While steaming, prepare the aromatics: mince scallions, ginger, and garlic.
  9. Once steamed, gently fluff the radish with your hands and transfer it to a bowl.
  10. Add the minced scallions, ginger, garlic, dried chilies, sesame seeds, chili powder, Sichuan peppercorns/13-spice blend, and salt.
  11. Pour hot oil over the mixture to enhance the aroma.
  12. Add a small amount of soy sauce and rice vinegar.
  13. Gently mix everything together using a scooping motion to avoid breaking the radish.
  14. Serve immediately while hot.

steamed_sea_bass.txt - Steamed Sea Bass

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare fresh sea bass for steaming.
  • Master a technique to eliminate fishy odor.
  • Create a flavorful and aromatic steamed sea bass dish.

Ingredients

  • 1 whole sea bass (about 1 pound)
  • 1 piece ginger, peeled and thinly sliced
  • Several green onions, thinly sliced
  • Cooking wine
  • Cooking oil
  • Salt (optional, added to sauce only)
  • Soy sauce
  • Oyster sauce (optional)
  • Fish sauce (optional)
  • 1 small carrot, thinly sliced
  • 1 small onion, thinly sliced
  • Shrimp peels (optional, for added umami)
  • Sugar (optional, small amount)
  • Ground pepper (optional, small amount)
  • Chili pepper (optional, for added color and spice)

Instructions

  1. Clean the Sea Bass: Ask your fishmonger to clean the fish, removing scales, fins, and internal organs. Thoroughly clean the belly cavity, removing any blood clots to prevent fishy odor. Trim fins with scissors for a cleaner appearance and to remove a layer of mucus that can impart a fishy smell.

  2. Prepare the Fish: Using a knife, score the fish along the backbone from the belly, being careful not to cut all the way through. This helps reduce steaming time and improves presentation.

  3. Marinate the Fish: In a bowl, combine sliced ginger and green onions. Add cooking wine and mix well. Gently massage this mixture all over the fish for about 2 minutes to remove mucus and fishy smell. Do not add salt at this stage. Set aside to marinate for 10 minutes.

  4. Prepare for Steaming: Pat the fish dry with a kitchen towel. Place the fish in a steamer basket, using chopsticks or a fork to keep it elevated. This ensures even steaming. Brush the fish with a thin layer of cooking oil to prevent moisture loss and enhance shine. Top with more green onions and ginger slices.

  5. Steam the Fish: Bring a pot of water to a rolling boil. Place the steamer basket over the boiling water. Steam the fish over high heat for 8 minutes (adjust time based on fish size). Use a bamboo skewer to check for doneness; it should easily pierce the thickest part of the fish.

  6. Prepare the Sauce: While the fish steams, prepare the sauce. In a small saucepan, combine water, soy sauce, oyster sauce (optional), fish sauce (optional), and a pinch of sugar and pepper. Add sliced ginger, green onions, carrots, and onion. Simmer over low heat for 2-3 minutes. Strain the sauce through a fine-mesh sieve.

  7. Finish the Dish: Once the fish is cooked, carefully remove it from the steamer. Pour the prepared sauce over the fish. Garnish with additional green onions, ginger, and chili (optional). Drizzle with hot oil to enhance the aroma. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=2BCaBAbiWDg

steamed_tof_radish_pork.txt - Steamed Tofu, Radish, and Pork

Objectives

  • Prepare tender and flavorful pork slices.
  • Blanch radishes to reduce bitterness and enhance flavor.
  • Create a savory sauce to complement the tofu, radish, and pork.
  • Steam the ingredients together for a delicious and healthy meal.
  • Learn a simple yet delicious family recipe.

Ingredients

  • 200g firm tofu (old tofu preferred)
  • 1 medium white radish
  • 2 eggs
  • 1 tbsp cooking oil
  • 1 tsp salt
  • Few cloves garlic, minced
  • 1 piece ginger, minced
  • Few dried chilies, thinly sliced
  • Handful of parsley, roughly chopped (4-5cm length)
  • 100g pork tenderloin, thinly sliced
  • 1/2 egg white
  • Pinch of baking soda
  • Pinch of cornstarch (sweet potato starch preferred)
  • Cooking wine
  • 1 tbsp red bean paste
  • 1 tbsp oyster sauce
  • 1 tbsp light soy sauce
  • Mushroom powder
  • Pepper

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Tofu: Cut the tofu in half, then into slices, then into small cubes. Place in a bowl, add 1 tsp salt and boiling water. Let it sit to remove bean smell.
  2. Prepare the Radish: Peel the radish thinly. Cut off ends, halve it, then cut into thicker slices (about the thickness of two coins).
  3. Prepare the Pork: Thinly slice pork tenderloin. Do not slice too thinly to prevent breaking. Marinate with salt, pepper, cooking wine, baking soda (to tenderize), and 1/2 egg white. Mix until sticky, then add sweet potato starch to retain moisture.
  4. Prepare the Aromatics: Mince garlic and ginger. Thinly slice dried chilies. Chop parsley.
  5. Prepare the Tofu Mixture: Drain the tofu. Crack 2 eggs into the tofu and mix well with chopsticks until fully combined.
  6. Blanch the Radish: Boil water in a pot. Add the radish slices and blanch for 2 minutes. Remove and set aside.
  7. Stir-fry the Tofu and Egg: Heat oil in a pan. Add the tofu and egg mixture and stir-fry until golden brown on all sides. Remove and set aside.
  8. Stir-fry the Pork: Heat more oil in the pan. Stir-fry the marinated pork until cooked through. Remove and set aside.
  9. Prepare the Sauce: Add more oil to the pan. Add garlic, ginger, chilies, and stir-fry briefly to release aroma. Add red bean paste and stir-fry. Add a bowl of water and bring to a boil. Season with oyster sauce, light soy sauce, salt, mushroom powder, and pepper.
  10. Combine and Steam: Add the cooked pork to the sauce and simmer for 30 seconds. Add the parsley stems and stir-fry. Add the stir-fried tofu and radish to the sauce. Transfer everything to a heatproof dish. Cover and steam over medium heat for 3-5 minutes.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=oLn0DLyv82U

steamed_tofu_radish_pork.txt - Steamed Tofu, Radish, and Pork

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare tender and flavorful pork.
  • Master the technique of steaming tofu and radish for optimal texture.
  • Create a balanced and delicious family-friendly dish.

Ingredients

  • 1 block firm tofu (about 400g)
  • 1 large white radish
  • 2 eggs
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • 100g pork tenderloin
  • 2 cloves garlic, minced
  • 1 piece ginger, minced
  • Several dried chilies, thinly sliced
  • A handful of parsley, roughly chopped (4-5cm pieces)
  • Cooking wine
  • Baking soda
  • 1/2 egg white
  • Sweet potato starch
  • Cooking oil
  • 1 tbsp red bean paste
  • 1 tbsp oyster sauce
  • 1 tbsp light soy sauce
  • Mushroom powder
  • Pepper

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Tofu: Cut the tofu in half, then into slices, then into small cubes. Place in a bowl, add 1 tsp salt and boiling water. Let it sit to remove any bean smell.
  2. Prepare the Radish: Peel the radish thinly. Cut off the ends, halve it, then slice into thick pieces (about the thickness of two coins).
  3. Prepare the Pork: Slice the pork tenderloin into thicker strips, then into thicker strands (avoid cutting too finely). Marinate with salt, pepper, cooking wine, a little baking soda, and 1/2 egg white until sticky. Add sweet potato starch.
  4. Prepare the Sauce Ingredients: Mince garlic and ginger. Thinly slice dried chilies. Roughly chop parsley (4-5cm pieces).
  5. Prepare the Egg and Tofu: Drain the tofu. Crack 2 eggs into the tofu and mix well with chopsticks until fully combined.
  6. Blanch the Radish: Boil water in a pot. Blanch the radish for 2 minutes to reduce bitterness. Remove and set aside.
  7. Fry Tofu and Egg: Heat oil in a pan. Fry the tofu and egg mixture until golden brown on all sides. Set aside.
  8. Stir-fry Pork: Heat oil in the same pan. Stir-fry the marinated pork until cooked through. Remove and set aside.
  9. Prepare the Sauce: Add more oil to the pan. Add ginger, garlic, and chilies; stir-fry until fragrant. Add red bean paste and stir-fry. Add water, bring to a boil, then add oyster sauce, light soy sauce, salt, mushroom powder, and pepper.
  10. Combine and Simmer: Add the cooked pork, then celery stalks. Stir-fry evenly. Add the fried tofu and radish to the sauce. Cover and simmer over medium-low heat for 3-5 minutes. Serve hot.

steamed_tofu.txt - Steamed Tofu with Spicy Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple, delicious steamed tofu dish.
  • Understand the importance of proper steaming time for optimal texture.
  • Master a flavorful sauce using readily available ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 10 pieces of small tofu (approximately 100g)
  • 2 scallions, white and green parts separated
  • Several cloves of garlic, minced
  • 2 pickled peppers, minced (optional)
  • 15g light soy sauce (生抽)
  • 5g oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • 2g dark soy sauce (老抽)
  • 3g white vinegar (白醋)
  • A pinch of black pepper (黑胡椒粉)
  • 20g homemade chili oil (自制红油)

Instructions

  1. Cut the tofu into even slices and arrange them neatly in a plate, layering them flat. Set aside.
  2. Finely mince the scallions, separating the white and green parts. Mince the garlic and pickled peppers (if using).
  3. In a bowl, combine the minced scallions (white parts), garlic, and pickled peppers.
  4. Add the light soy sauce, oyster sauce, dark soy sauce, white vinegar, black pepper, and chili oil to the bowl.
  5. Mix the sauce thoroughly until all ingredients are well combined. Set aside.
  6. Place the prepared tofu and sauce into a steamer.
  7. Steam over high heat for 8 minutes. Do not over-steam.
  8. Carefully remove the tofu from the steamer and drain any excess liquid. (Save the liquid, it has beneficial properties).
  9. Pour the sauce over the steamed tofu.
  10. Garnish with the minced scallion greens.
  11. Serve immediately and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=et2Bh1elWVM

steam_egg.txt - Steamed Egg

Objectives

  • Learn to make tender, flavorful steamed eggs.
  • Master the techniques for achieving a smooth, pore-free texture.
  • Understand the importance of ingredient ratios and cooking temperature.

Ingredients

  • 3 eggs (approx. 150g)
  • A small spoonful of salt
  • 225g of warm water (30-40°C)
  • Chopped scallions (for garnish)
  • A dash of soy sauce (for seasoning)
  • A dash of sesame oil (for seasoning)

Instructions

  1. Wash 3 fresh eggs with light salt water to remove surface contaminants.
  2. Crack eggs into a large bowl.
  3. Add a small spoonful of salt and whisk thoroughly until egg whites and yolks are fully combined.
  4. Strain the egg mixture through a sieve to remove any foam. Repeat several times for a smoother texture.
  5. Add warm water (225g, 30-40°C) to the egg mixture at a 1:1.5 ratio. Whisk well.
  6. Strain the mixture again to remove any remaining bubbles.
  7. Cover the bowl with plastic wrap, piercing several small holes with a toothpick for ventilation.
  8. Bring water to a boil in a steamer.
  9. Place the covered bowl into the steamer.
  10. Steam over low heat for 10 minutes with the lid on.
  11. Remove from steamer and let cool slightly.
  12. Score the steamed egg into small squares using a knife.
  13. Drizzle with soy sauce and sesame oil, then gently mix to coat.
  14. Garnish with chopped scallions.
  15. Serve immediately while hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=66NMh5hesME

stir_fried_bean_sprouts.txt - 炝炒豆芽

Objectives

  • Learn to stir-fry bean sprouts to maintain crispness.
  • Master a quick and easy recipe for delicious bean sprouts.
  • Understand the importance of blanching and quick cooking for optimal texture.

Ingredients

  • Green bean sprouts (脆嫩的绿豆芽)
  • Small葱 (葱末, 小葱段) - scallions (chopped and segments)
  • Ginger (生姜, 姜末) - ginger (sliced and minced)
  • Garlic (蒜子, 蒜末) - garlic (minced)
  • Dried chili peppers (干海椒)
  • Sichuan peppercorns (花椒)
  • Cooking oil (猪油 preferred)
  • Soy sauce (生抽)
  • Salt (食盐)
  • Chicken bouillon (鸡汁)
  • Rice vinegar (锅边醋)

Instructions

  1. Wash green bean sprouts thoroughly and drain.
  2. Mince scallions, ginger, and garlic. Chop some scallions into longer segments.
  3. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Blanch bean sprouts for 30 seconds, then immediately remove and drain.
  4. Heat oil in a wok or large pan over high heat. Add minced scallions, ginger, and garlic; stir-fry until fragrant.
  5. Add dried chili peppers and Sichuan peppercorns; stir-fry until fragrant.
  6. Add blanched bean sprouts and stir-fry quickly until heated through.
  7. Season with soy sauce, salt, and chicken bouillon. Stir-fry until well combined.
  8. Add the longer scallion segments and rice vinegar. Stir-fry for 30 seconds.
  9. Serve immediately.

stir_fried_beef_with_bitter_melon.txt - 星級酒店苦瓜炒牛肉

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare tender and flavorful beef for stir-fry.
  • Master the technique of blanching bitter melon to reduce bitterness.
  • Create a delicious and visually appealing stir-fry of beef and bitter melon.

Ingredients

  • 2 green bitter melons (苦瓜)
  • A small piece of fresh beef (牛肉), tenderloin or shank recommended
  • Soy sauce (醬油)
  • Oyster sauce (蠔油)
  • Wine (酒), for deodorizing
  • Dark soy sauce (老抽), for color
  • Cornstarch (生粉)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)
  • Garlic (蒜頭)
  • Ginger (薑)
  • Edamame (毛豆)
  • Sugar (糖)
  • Water (水)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Beef: Cut the beef into thin, even slices. Marinate with soy sauce, oyster sauce, wine, dark soy sauce, and cornstarch. Mix well and add a little cooking oil to prevent sticking.

  2. Prepare the Bitter Melon: Clean the bitter melons, remove the ends, and halve them. Use a spoon to scrape out the white membrane and seeds to reduce bitterness. Cut into slightly thicker, 45-degree diagonal slices.

  3. Prepare the Aromatics and Sauce: Mince garlic and ginger. Prepare the sauce by combining soy sauce, oyster sauce, sugar, water, and cornstarch.

  4. Blanch the Bitter Melon: Boil water with salt and a little oil. Add the bitter melon slices and blanch for 30 seconds. Remove and set aside.

  5. Stir-fry the Beef: Add oil to a wok or pan. Add the beef and stir-fry until browned. Remove and set aside.

  6. Stir-fry Aromatics: Add a little more oil to the pan. Add the minced garlic and ginger and edamame. Stir-fry until fragrant.

  7. Combine and Stir-fry: Return the beef to the pan. Add the blanched bitter melon. Stir-fry over medium-high heat.

  8. Add Sauce and Finish: Pour in the prepared sauce and stir-fry until the sauce thickens and coats the ingredients. Add a little extra oil just before serving for shine.

stir_fried_bitter_melon_with_egg.txt - Stir-fried Bitter Melon with Egg

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare crisp and delicious stir-fried bitter melon.
  • Master the technique of blanching vegetables to retain their color and texture.
  • Understand how to balance the bitterness of bitter melon with sugar and other seasonings.

Ingredients

  • 2 bitter melons
  • 1 small carrot
  • 3 eggs
  • Several garlic cloves
  • 1 tablespoon white sugar
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • A dash of chicken essence
  • 1 tablespoon light soy sauce
  • Cooking oil
  • Water
  • Black fungus (optional)

Instructions

  1. Clean and prepare the bitter melons: Cut off the ends, halve them lengthwise, scoop out the seeds and white film, and slice into coin-thick pieces.
  2. Marinate the bitter melon: Place the sliced bitter melon in a bowl, add a spoonful of white sugar, mix well, and let it marinate for 3 minutes.
  3. Prepare the carrot: Peel and cut the carrot into diamond-shaped pieces. If large, cut into smaller pieces.
  4. Prepare the eggs: Crack 3 eggs into a bowl and whisk until well combined.
  5. Prepare the garlic: Mince several garlic cloves.
  6. Blanch the bitter melon: Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add the marinated bitter melon and blanch for 30 seconds. Remove with a slotted spoon and drain well.
  7. Blanch the carrot and black fungus (optional): Add the carrot and black fungus (if using) to the boiling water and blanch for 2 minutes. Remove with a slotted spoon and drain well.
  8. Stir-fry the garlic: Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan over medium heat. Add the minced garlic and stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Stir-fry the carrot: Add the blanched carrots and stir-fry for 30 seconds.
  10. Add the bitter melon: Add the blanched bitter melon and stir-fry for another 30 seconds.
  11. Season: Add salt, chicken essence, light soy sauce, and a small spoonful of sugar. Stir well.
  12. Stir-fry the eggs: Pour the whisked eggs into the pan and stir-fry until cooked through and tender.
  13. Finish and serve: Add a little cornstarch slurry (cornstarch mixed with water) and a touch of oil to the pan, stir to combine, and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=2TXxhMenlV8

stir_fried_broccoli_with_mushrooms.txt - Stir-fried Broccoli with Mushrooms

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare and clean broccoli for optimal flavor and texture.
  • Master a quick and easy stir-fry technique for vibrant green broccoli.
  • Create a delicious and nutritious side dish using simple ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 1 head of broccoli
  • 1 package small white mushrooms (白玉菇 - báiyù gū)
  • 1 small piece of ginger (姜 - jiāng)
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜 - suàn)
  • 1 small bunch of scallions (葱 - cōng)
  • Salt (盐 - yán)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòng yóu)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油 - háoyóu)
  • Chicken bouillon (鸡精 - jī jīng)
  • Water (水 - shuǐ)
  • Water starch (水淀粉 - shuǐ diànfěn)

Instructions

  1. Select a firm, dark green broccoli head. Cut the florets from the stalk, reserving the stalk for another use. Cut large florets into smaller pieces.
  2. Soak the broccoli florets in salted water for 10 minutes to remove insects and impurities. Rinse thoroughly with clean water.
  3. Clean and trim the white mushrooms.
  4. Mince the scallions, ginger, and garlic.
  5. Blanch the broccoli and mushrooms in boiling salted water with a little oil for 6-7 seconds until slightly tender-crisp. Drain well.
  6. Heat a wok or pan with a small amount of oil. Add minced scallions, ginger, and garlic, and sauté until fragrant.
  7. Add a small amount of water to the wok. Add oyster sauce, a pinch of salt, and a tiny bit of chicken bouillon. Bring to a boil.
  8. Mix a little water starch to thicken the sauce.
  9. Add the blanched broccoli and mushrooms. Stir-fry quickly until heated through and coated in the sauce.
  10. Drizzle with a little cooking oil to add shine and flavor.
  11. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=MTws_P0QHTo

stir_fried_broccoli_with_tomato.txt - 素炒西兰花

Objectives

  • Learn a restaurant-style recipe for stir-fried broccoli.
  • Make a delicious and nutritious broccoli dish.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients for an easy-to-make side.

Ingredients

  • 1 large head of broccoli (approx. 5 RMB)
  • 1 large tomato
  • 1 handful of oyster mushrooms
  • 1 small piece of ginger
  • Several cloves of garlic
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽)
  • Appropriate amount of oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • A little salt (食盐)
  • A pinch of sugar (白糖)
  • 1 tsp Matsutake mushroom seasoning (松茸鲜)
  • Pepper (胡椒粉)
  • 1 tsp cornstarch (玉米淀粉)
  • Appropriate amount of water
  • Cooking oil (食用油)

Instructions

  1. Remove broccoli leaves and separate florets. Cut large florets into smaller, uniform pieces.
  2. Soak broccoli in light salt water for 15 minutes to remove insects and impurities.
  3. Cut tomato into small dice, making decorative cuts but not cutting all the way through.
  4. Cut oyster mushrooms into small pieces.
  5. Mince ginger and garlic finely. Finely slice chili peppers.
  6. Prepare sauce: Combine soy sauce, oyster sauce, salt, sugar, Matsutake mushroom seasoning, pepper, cornstarch, and water in a bowl. Mix well.
  7. Rinse broccoli thoroughly after salt water soak.
  8. Boil water in a pot, add salt, and blanch broccoli for 1 minute.
  9. Add oyster mushrooms and blanch for 20 seconds.
  10. Remove broccoli and mushrooms with a colander and set aside.
  11. Heat oil in a wok or pan. Add diced tomatoes and stir-fry for 2 minutes until softened and releasing juices. Press tomatoes with a spatula to expedite juice release.
  12. Add minced ginger, garlic, and chili peppers. Stir-fry for 20 seconds until fragrant.
  13. Add blanched broccoli and mushrooms. Stir-fry for 1 minute to combine.
  14. Pour in prepared sauce and stir-fry until sauce thickens and coats the vegetables.
  15. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=4Ls82CHIWC4

stir_fried_cabbage.txt - Stir-fried Cabbage with Vinegar

Objectives

  • Learn to make crispy and refreshing stir-fried cabbage.
  • Master a quick and easy recipe for a delicious side dish.
  • Understand the importance of properly cleaning and preparing cabbage.

Ingredients

  • 1 Chinese cabbage
  • 1 tsp salt
  • A pinch of sugar
  • A pinch of mushroom powder (instead of chicken broth)
  • Appropriate amount of light soy sauce
  • 1/2 tbsp balsamic vinegar
  • 1 tbsp cornstarch
  • Several cloves garlic, sliced
  • A handful of scallions (white parts only), chopped
  • Some dried chili peppers, deseeded and chopped
  • Cooking oil (vegetable or lard)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Cabbage: Remove the root of the cabbage, peel it, and cut it into pieces. Wash thoroughly in a large basin of water to remove dirt and insect eggs. Drain well in a colander.

  2. Make the Sauce: In a bowl, combine salt, sugar, mushroom powder, light soy sauce, balsamic vinegar, and cornstarch. Mix well until all ingredients are dissolved. Set aside.

  3. Prepare Aromatics: Slice garlic and chop the white parts of scallions. Deseed and chop the dried chili peppers.

  4. Prepare the Cabbage: Separate the cabbage leaves from the stalks. Cut the stalks in half lengthwise, then slice at a 45-degree angle. Set aside.

  5. Season Cabbage: Add 0.5 times the usual amount of salt to the chopped cabbage. Mix well with clean hands for a minute or two to remove moisture. Let it sit for 2 minutes.

  6. Rinse and Drain: Rinse the salt from the cabbage and drain well.

  7. Stir-fry Aromatics: Heat cooking oil (lard preferred) in a wok or pan. Add garlic and scallions, stir-frying until fragrant. Add dried chili peppers and stir-fry until fragrant.

  8. Stir-fry Cabbage Stalks: Add the cabbage stalks to the wok. Increase heat to high and stir-fry for about 30 seconds to remove moisture.

  9. Stir-fry Cabbage Leaves: Add the cabbage leaves and continue to stir-fry over high heat until tender.

  10. Add Sauce: Add the prepared sauce to the wok and stir-fry over high heat until the sauce thickens and coats the cabbage.

  11. Finish and Serve: Drizzle with a little extra cooking oil for shine. Stir and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=XKmoeidADxI

stir_fried_chinese_morning_glory.txt - Stir-fried Chinese Morning Glory (空心菜)

Objectives

  • Learn the proper way to prepare and cook Chinese morning glory to prevent discoloration and maintain a crisp texture.
  • Understand the importance of separating stems and leaves for even cooking.
  • Master a quick and flavorful stir-fry technique for Chinese morning glory.

Ingredients

  • 2 jin (approximately 1 kg) Chinese morning glory (空心菜 kōngxīncài)
  • 1 gram baking soda (小苏打 xiǎosūdǎ)
  • 1 small spoon of salt (食盐 shíyán)
  • Spring water (山泉水 shānquánshuǐ)
  • Several cloves garlic (蒜子 suànzi)
  • Dried chili peppers (干海椒 gānhǎijiāo)
  • Small amount of cooking oil (食用油 shíyòngyóu)
  • 2 small spoons of salt (食盐 shíyán)
  • A pinch of white sugar (白糖 báitáng)
  • Pork lard (猪油 zhūyóu) (optional, for enhanced flavor)

Instructions

  1. Separate the stems from the leaves of the Chinese morning glory. Reserve the stems for other uses (e.g., stir-frying with peppers or bean curd).
  2. Remove any wilted or yellow leaves from the morning glory.
  3. In a large bowl, dissolve 1 gram of baking soda and a small spoon of salt in spring water.
  4. Soak the morning glory in the baking soda solution for 5 minutes. This helps remove pesticide residue.
  5. Mince the garlic and cut the dried chilies into small pieces. Remove chili seeds.
  6. Rinse the morning glory thoroughly under running water until the water runs clear. This removes any remaining baking soda and pesticide residue.
  7. Drain the morning glory well. Do not chop; instead, pinch the leaves and stems into smaller pieces, separating leaves and stems.
  8. In a pot, bring a small amount of water to a boil over high heat.
  9. Add 2 small spoons of salt and a little cooking oil to the boiling water. Stir to dissolve the salt.
  10. Add the morning glory stems to the boiling water and blanch for 15 seconds.
  11. Add the morning glory leaves and blanch for an additional 10 seconds.
  12. Immediately remove the blanched morning glory with a strainer and drain well.
  13. In a separate wok or pan, heat pork lard (or cooking oil) over medium heat.
  14. Add the minced garlic and dried chilies and sauté until fragrant.
  15. Add the drained morning glory, a pinch of salt, and a tiny bit of white sugar.
  16. Increase the heat to high and stir-fry for about 10-15 seconds.
  17. Remove from heat and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=b-YL9d6N7Gg

stir_fried_lettuce_with_egg.txt - Stir-fried Lettuce with Egg

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare and stir-fry lettuce for a crispy texture.
  • Master a simple and delicious stir-fry recipe using readily available ingredients.
  • Understand the techniques for stir-frying to preserve nutrients and enhance flavor.

Ingredients

  • 4 heads of lettuce (3 yuan)
  • 1/2 large red pepper
  • Several cloves of garlic
  • 5 eggs
  • Salt to taste
  • 2 drops white vinegar
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Peel the lettuce leaves one by one, being careful not to waste any. Discard any old, tough outer layers.
  2. Using a paring knife, carefully remove the tough outer layer of the lettuce. This ensures a crispier texture when stir-fried.
  3. Cut the lettuce into bite-sized pieces, not too thinly.
  4. Wash the lettuce thoroughly and set aside.
  5. Remove the seeds from half a large red pepper. Cut the pepper into long strips, then into diamond shapes. Set aside.
  6. Mince the garlic cloves finely. Set aside.
  7. Crack 5 eggs into a bowl. Add a small amount of salt and two drops of white vinegar (to remove odor). Whisk well until the whites and yolks are fully combined.
  8. Heat a wok or pan over medium-high heat. Add a generous amount of oil (1.2 times the usual amount). Swirl to coat.
  9. Once the oil is hot (slightly smoking), add the minced garlic and stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Add the lettuce to the wok. Stir-fry over high heat for about one minute, or until the lettuce is slightly softened but still crisp. Remove from wok and set aside.
  11. In the same wok, add more oil if needed. Stir-fry the red pepper until tender.
  12. Return the lettuce to the wok. Add the eggs, and stir-fry everything together until the eggs are cooked through and the lettuce and eggs are well combined. Season with salt to taste. No other seasonings are needed.
  13. Before serving, drizzle with a bit more oil to enhance the color and shine.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Da_TTEVGkfg

stir_fried_lettuce_with_pork_belly.txt - Stir-fried Lettuce with Pork Belly

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare fresh lettuce for stir-frying.
  • Master the technique of stir-frying pork belly to remove excess fat.
  • Create a flavorful and balanced stir-fry with a simple sauce.

Ingredients

  • 3 heads of green lettuce
  • 5 yuan worth of pork belly
  • Green onions (amount unspecified)
  • Ginger (amount unspecified)
  • Garlic (amount unspecified)
  • Dried chili peppers (amount unspecified)
  • 2 tablespoons soy bean paste
  • Salt (amount unspecified)
  • Pepper (amount unspecified)
  • Peanut oil (amount unspecified)
  • Water (amount unspecified)

Instructions

  1. Trim the ends of the lettuce. Check for freshness by breaking off a piece to ensure it's crisp and tender inside.
  2. Peel off the outer layer of the lettuce and scrape away the white film to clean it thoroughly.
  3. Cut the lettuce in half lengthwise, then slice it into strips. Do not slice too thickly.
  4. Clean and slice the pork belly into small pieces.
  5. Finely chop the green onions, ginger, and garlic.
  6. Bring water to a boil in a pot. Add lettuce, a pinch of salt, and blanch for 90 seconds. Drain immediately.
  7. Heat peanut oil in a wok or pan over low heat.
  8. Add pork belly and stir-fry slowly until the fat is rendered and the pork is flavorful. Remove excess fat.
  9. Add chopped green onions, ginger, and garlic to the wok and stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Add dried chili peppers and stir-fry until fragrant.
  11. Add soy bean paste, salt, and pepper. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  12. Add half a bowl of water, stir well, and bring to a boil.
  13. Add the blanched lettuce to the wok and stir-fry until heated through and the flavors are combined (about 1-2 minutes). Cover the wok to speed up cooking if desired.
  14. Stir in remaining green onions and serve immediately.

stir_fried_mung_bean_sprouts.txt - 小炒豆芽

Objectives

  • Learn to make crispy and refreshing stir-fried mung bean sprouts.
  • Master techniques to prevent the sprouts from becoming soggy.
  • Understand the importance of pre-soaking and blanching vegetables.

Ingredients

  • 1 jin (approx. 500g) mung bean sprouts
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • 1 small bottle cap of rice vinegar
  • 1/2 carrot, julienned
  • 1 small handful of chives, chopped
  • Pre-soaked black fungus (木耳), washed and drained
  • 3 eggs
  • 1 small spoonful of salt
  • Several cloves garlic, minced
  • Several small chili peppers, finely sliced
  • Cooking oil
  • 1 small spoonful of salt
  • 1 small spoonful of chicken bouillon (鸡精)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • A little light soy sauce (生抽)

Instructions

  1. Soak mung bean sprouts in a bowl with 1 tablespoon of salt, a small bottle cap of rice vinegar, and plenty of water for 5 minutes.
  2. Julienne the carrot.
  3. Chop the chives, removing the root ends.
  4. Wash and drain the pre-soaked black fungus.
  5. Whisk 3 eggs with a small spoonful of salt until light and fluffy.
  6. Mince the garlic and slice the chili peppers.
  7. Blanch the black fungus in boiling water for 2 minutes. Drain.
  8. Heat oil in a wok or pan. Add the egg mixture and scramble until cooked to your preference. Remove from pan.
  9. Add a little more oil to the pan. Add the minced garlic and chili peppers, stir-frying until fragrant.
  10. Add the julienned carrots and blanched black fungus. Stir-fry until combined.
  11. Add the soaked mung bean sprouts and stir-fry over high heat until well combined.
  12. Season with 1 small spoonful of salt, 1 small spoonful of chicken bouillon, oyster sauce, and a little light soy sauce. Stir-fry until flavors are well incorporated.
  13. Add the chopped chives and the scrambled eggs. Stir-fry until everything is cooked through.
  14. Serve immediately.

stir_fried_mushroom.txt - 素炒香菇

Objectives

  • Learn to clean and prepare fresh mushrooms for optimal flavor.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful stir-fry technique for mushrooms.
  • Enhance the taste and texture of mushrooms through specific cooking steps.

Ingredients

  • 1 jin (approximately 500g) fresh mushrooms
  • Salt
  • Flour
  • Water
  • White sugar
  • Garlic cloves (a generous amount)
  • Cooking oil
  • Light soy sauce (生抽)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油)

Instructions

  1. Remove the stems from the mushrooms and clean the caps thoroughly. Use scissors to remove the stems; choose mushrooms with thick flesh.
  2. Wash the mushroom caps: Add salt and flour to a bowl of water. Soak the mushrooms for 1-2 minutes. This helps remove dirt and impurities. Rinse thoroughly with clean water.
  3. Blanch the mushrooms: Add a handful of white sugar to a bowl of boiling water (101°C). Blanch the mushrooms for 1-2 minutes to remove any unpleasant odor. Drain and squeeze out excess water.
  4. Cut the mushrooms: Cut the blanched mushrooms into small pieces.
  5. Prepare the garlic: Mince a generous amount of garlic cloves.
  6. Stir-fry the garlic: Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan. Add the minced garlic and stir-fry over low heat until fragrant.
  7. Season the garlic: Add a pinch of salt, a pinch of white sugar, a little light soy sauce, and a little oyster sauce. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  8. Stir-fry the mushrooms: Add the prepared mushrooms to the pan and stir-fry until they release their moisture. Press down on the mushrooms to help them cook evenly. You can also cover the pan and steam for 1-2 minutes.
  9. Thicken the sauce: Once the mushrooms have released their moisture, add a bit of thickening agent (the transcript mentions "玻璃芡," which may refer to a cornstarch slurry or similar). Stir-fry for about 30 seconds.
  10. Serve: Turn off the heat and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Y3dKI5ZEH7k

stir_fried_pork_with_oyster_mushrooms.txt - Stir-fried Pork with Oyster Mushrooms

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and tender stir-fried pork with oyster mushrooms dish.
  • Master the technique of blanching oyster mushrooms to enhance texture and flavor.
  • Understand the importance of using high heat for stir-frying to achieve a crispy texture.

Ingredients

  • 1 lb oyster mushrooms (approx. 3 yuan)
  • 4.08 yuan lean pork (tenderloin recommended)
  • Several cloves garlic
  • Ginger (amount unspecified)
  • Green onions (amount unspecified)
  • 4-5 green chilies
  • 4-5 red chilies
  • Oyster sauce (amount unspecified)
  • Dark soy sauce (amount unspecified)
  • Light soy sauce (amount unspecified)
  • Salt (1/2 tsp)
  • Pepper (amount unspecified)
  • Vegetable oil (e.g., rapeseed oil)
  • Sugar (small amount)

Instructions

  1. Clean and trim the oyster mushrooms, tearing them into small pieces. Slice thicker root parts thinly. Rinse and drain well.
  2. Slice the lean pork thinly and set aside. (No need to marinate.)
  3. Mince garlic and ginger. Chop green onions. Slice green and red chilies thinly.
  4. Bring water to a boil in a pot. Add oyster mushrooms, a pinch of sugar (to remove odor), and blanch for 1 minute.
  5. Immediately transfer blanched mushrooms to ice water to maintain a smooth texture. Drain well.
  6. Heat rapeseed oil in a wok or pan until it slightly smokes.
  7. Add minced garlic and ginger; stir-fry until fragrant.
  8. Add the sliced pork and stir-fry over high heat until the color changes. Add oyster sauce and dark soy sauce for flavor and color. Stir-fry for about 20 seconds.
  9. Remove the pork from the wok and set aside, leaving the oil in the wok.
  10. Add the green and red chilies to the wok and stir-fry until softened.
  11. Add the blanched oyster mushrooms and stir-fry over high heat for about a minute to remove moisture.
  12. Season with salt, pepper, and light soy sauce.
  13. Return the pork to the wok. Stir-fry everything together over high heat for 5-8 seconds until well combined.

stir_fried_red_cabbage_stems.txt - Stir-Fried Red Cabbage Stems (Pinakbet ng pulang repolyo)

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare fresh red cabbage stems for stir-frying.
  • Master a simple and flavorful stir-fry recipe.
  • Understand the importance of minimal seasoning to highlight the cabbage's natural sweetness.

Ingredients

  • 3.50 yuan worth of fresh red cabbage stems (approx. 1 bunch)
  • Salt (to taste)
  • 2-3 cloves garlic, thinly sliced
  • Small piece of ginger, thinly sliced
  • 1-2 dried chilies, finely chopped
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Red Cabbage Stems: Do not wash the red cabbage stems immediately after purchase. Add a pinch of salt, mix with your hands until it dissolves, then soak in water for 5 minutes. This helps remove dirt. Rinse twice more, drain thoroughly.
  2. Cut the Red Cabbage Stems: Trim off any old parts of the stems. Lightly tap with a knife to help release flavor. Cut into long strips. Set aside the smaller, younger leaves separately.
  3. Prepare Aromatics: Thinly slice garlic and ginger. Finely mince them. Finely chop dried chilies.
  4. Stir-fry Aromatics: Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan. Add minced garlic, ginger, and dried chilies. Stir-fry over low heat until fragrant.
  5. Stir-fry Cabbage: Add the red cabbage stems to the wok. Increase heat to medium-high and stir-fry for 1 minute.
  6. Season and Finish: Add a small teaspoon of salt. Stir-fry for another minute. Add more salt to taste, as beetroot is naturally salty. Continue to stir-fry until the cabbage is tender-crisp and slightly changes color (about 9 minutes total).
  7. Serve: Remove from heat and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QC0XIM1CDqU

stir_fried_red_cabbage_tender_stems.txt - Stir-fried Red Cabbage Tender Stems (凉拌紫甘蓝嫩茎)

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare and stir-fry fresh red cabbage tender stems.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful recipe highlighting the cabbage's natural sweetness.
  • Understand the importance of proper cleaning and preparation techniques for optimal taste and texture.

Ingredients

  • 3.50 yuan worth of fresh red cabbage tender stems (紫甘蓝嫩茎)
  • Salt (盐)
  • Garlic (蒜)
  • Ginger (姜)
  • Dried chili peppers (干辣椒)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)

Instructions

  1. Purchase fresh red cabbage tender stems from a vegetable market.
  2. Do not wash the stems immediately. Add a small amount of salt, mix with hands until dissolved, then soak in water for 5 minutes.
  3. After soaking, rinse the stems thoroughly two more times to remove dirt and dust. Drain well.
  4. Place the stems on a cutting board. Trim off any old parts of the stem. Lightly tap with a knife to help release flavor during stir-frying.
  5. Cut the stems into long strips. Separate smaller, younger leaves.
  6. Prepare garlic and ginger: Flatten with a knife, then finely mince.
  7. Prepare dried chilies: Cut into small pieces.
  8. Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan.
  9. Once oil is hot, add minced garlic, ginger, and dried chilies. Stir-fry until fragrant over low heat.
  10. Add the red cabbage stems. Increase heat and stir-fry for 1 minute.
  11. Add a small spoonful of salt. Add more salt if needed, as beetroot is saltier.
  12. Continue stir-frying over high heat for another minute, until the cabbage is tender-crisp and the garlic is fragrant and slightly browned.
  13. Remove from heat and serve.

stir_fried_tofu_skin.txt - Stir-Fried Tofu Skin

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare a delicious and easy stir-fried tofu skin dish.
  • Master simple knife skills for cutting tofu skin and vegetables.
  • Understand the technique of blanching tofu skin to improve texture and remove beany smell.

Ingredients

  • 2 yuan and 30 cents worth of tofu skin (amount unspecified)
  • Dried mushrooms (amount unspecified)
  • Garlic (amount unspecified)
  • A small piece of ginger (amount unspecified)
  • 4 millet peppers (amount unspecified)
  • Screw pepper (amount unspecified)
  • 3 yuan worth of pork belly (amount unspecified)
  • Approximately 1 gram of baking soda
  • Water (amount unspecified)
  • Cooking oil (amount unspecified)
  • 1 small spoonful of salt
  • Chicken essence (amount unspecified)
  • 18 grams of white sugar
  • Light soy sauce (amount unspecified)

Instructions

  1. Cut the tofu skin into wider pieces, then into diamond-shaped pieces.
  2. Soak dried mushrooms in warm water.
  3. Mince garlic and ginger, slice millet peppers and screw pepper into thin rounds, and cut pork belly into pieces. If the pork belly is difficult to cut, freeze it first.
  4. Add water to a pan, bring to a boil, add baking soda, then add the tofu skin. Blanch for about 1 minute.
  5. Remove the tofu skin, rinse under cold water to remove baking soda.
  6. Heat oil in a wok. Add pork belly and fry until lightly browned, releasing some fat.
  7. Add ginger, garlic, millet peppers, and screw pepper to the wok; stir-fry until fragrant.
  8. Add water to the wok, then add the blanched tofu skin. Stir to combine.
  9. Season with salt, chicken essence, and white sugar. Stir well.
  10. Bring to a boil, then simmer for 1 minute.
  11. Add light soy sauce to enhance color.
  12. Simmer until the sauce thickens.
  13. Add green pepper and stir-fry until tender.
  14. Turn off the heat, serve and enjoy.

su_chao_luobo.txt - 素炒萝卜 (Su Chao Luobo)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and simple stir-fried radish dish.
  • Master the technique of blanching radish to remove bitterness and enhance flavor.
  • Understand how to create a flavorful sauce that perfectly complements the radish.

Ingredients

  • 2 large white radishes (白萝卜, bái luóbo)
  • A small handful of garlic cloves (蒜子, suàn zi)
  • 1 piece of ginger (生姜, shēng jiāng)
  • Salt (食盐, shíyán)
  • Soy sauce (酱油, jiàngyóu)
  • Light soy sauce (生抽, shēng chōu)
  • Chicken bouillon (鸡汁, jī zhī) - optional
  • Water (清水, qīngshuǐ)
  • Water starch (水淀粉, shuǐ diànfěn)
  • Sesame oil (香油, xiāngyóu)
  • Leftover chopped celery (芹菜碎, qíncài suì) - optional

Instructions

  1. Wash and peel two large white radishes.
  2. Cut the radishes into 3cm thick rounds, then cut into smaller pieces.
  3. Mince the garlic cloves and julienne the ginger.
  4. Bring a pot of water to a boil, add a pinch of salt, and add the radish pieces.
  5. Blanch the radishes for 3-5 minutes until translucent. Remove and drain.
  6. Heat oil in a wok or iron pan. Add minced garlic and ginger, sauté until fragrant and slightly browned. Remove and set aside.
  7. Add the blanched radishes to the pan and stir-fry for about 1 minute until slightly softened and any excess moisture is removed.
  8. Add a large bowl of water (or chicken broth for enhanced flavor).
  9. Season with salt, soy sauce (to add color, use sparingly), and light soy sauce (for flavor). Add chicken bouillon if desired.
  10. Stir well, cover, and simmer over high heat for about 8 minutes.
  11. Remove the lid, and add water starch and sesame oil. Stir-fry until the sauce thickens and coats the radish pieces.
  12. Add any leftover chopped celery and stir-fry for a few seconds.
  13. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=AXTN-_hbFiA

sugar_coated_peanuts.txt - Sugar Coated Peanuts (Matamis at Malutong na Mani)

Objectives

  • Learn to make crispy, sweet, and non-greasy sugar-coated peanuts.
  • Master a simple method for preparing this traditional New Year's Eve snack.
  • Understand the steps involved in perfectly coating peanuts with a sugar glaze.

Ingredients

  • 500 grams of peanuts
  • 2 eggs
  • Plain flour (small amount, added gradually)
  • Cooking oil (for frying)
  • 5 tablespoons of sugar
  • 1 bowl of cold boiled water
  • 1 tablespoon white sesame seeds
  • 1 tablespoon black sesame seeds

Instructions

  1. Prepare peanuts: Dry the peanuts thoroughly. Remove any moldy or damaged peanuts. Rinse and drain well. If weather permits, sun-dry for 30 minutes; otherwise, use a hairdryer.

  2. Prepare the peanut coating: In a large bowl, add the peanuts and two eggs. Mix well with chopsticks until the peanuts are evenly coated with egg wash. Gradually add plain flour, mixing continuously until each peanut is coated in a thin layer of flour. Sift the peanuts to remove excess flour.

  3. Fry the peanuts: Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan until it reaches 50% heat (small bubbles appear around chopsticks when inserted). Add the peanuts, shaking the pan to ensure even heating. Fry for 3-5 minutes, stirring frequently, until golden and crispy. Remove and drain on paper towels.

  4. Prepare the sugar glaze: Clean the wok/pan. Add 5 tablespoons of sugar and 1 bowl of cold boiled water. Cook over high heat, stirring constantly, until the sugar dissolves completely (approximately 3-5 minutes). The mixture will go from large bubbles to small bubbles.

  5. Combine and coat: Turn off the heat. Add white and black sesame seeds, stir. Add the fried peanuts and stir-fry until the peanuts are evenly coated with the sugar glaze.

  6. Cool and serve: Allow the sugar-coated peanuts to cool completely. The peanuts will have a layer of white frost. Serve and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=pY4dXBFs0e0

sugar_vinegar_egg.txt - 糖醋荷包蛋 (Tangcu Heobao Dan)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and easy sugar vinegar eggs.
  • Master the technique of frying eggs to achieve a crispy texture.
  • Create a flavorful sauce that perfectly complements the eggs.

Ingredients

  • 8 eggs (雞蛋 - jīdàn)
  • Salt (鹽 - yán)
  • Water (水 - shuǐ)
  • Scallions, chopped (蔥末 - cōngmò)
  • Ginger, minced (薑末 - jiāngmò)
  • Garlic, minced (蒜末 - suànmò)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽 - shēng chōu)
  • A dash of dark soy sauce (老抽 - lǎo chōu)
  • Oyster sauce (蠔油 - háoyóu)
  • Sugar (白糖 - báitáng)
  • Cornstarch (玉米淀粉 - yùmǐ diànfěn)
  • 1/2 tbsp vinegar (陳醋 - Chéncù)
  • Water (水 - shuǐ)
  • Tomato sauce (番茄醬 - fānqié jiàng) (optional, amount to taste)
  • Cooking oil (油 - yóu)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the eggs: Wash eggs with salt water for 5 minutes to remove residue. Discard any cracked eggs. Dry the eggs.
  2. Prepare the garnish: Finely chop scallions, mince ginger and garlic. Set aside.
  3. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, combine soy sauce, dark soy sauce, oyster sauce, sugar, cornstarch, vinegar, water, and tomato sauce (optional). Mix well. Set aside.
  4. Fry the eggs: Heat oil in a pan over medium-high heat. Crack eggs into the pan one at a time. Fry until the bottoms are set, then flip and fry the other side until golden brown. Repeat with remaining eggs.
  5. Sauté aromatics: Using the remaining oil in the pan, sauté the minced scallions, ginger, and garlic until fragrant.
  6. Combine and simmer: Add the fried eggs to the pan with the sautéed aromatics. Pour the prepared sauce over the eggs. Cover and simmer for 2-3 minutes.
  7. Garnish and serve: Sprinkle with chopped scallions. Turn off the heat and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=d-Z2qETjUHo

sugar_vinegar_poached_egg.txt - 糖醋荷包蛋 (Tángcù Hébāodàn)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and easy sugar vinegar poached eggs.
  • Master the technique of frying eggs to achieve a golden-brown crust.
  • Prepare a flavorful sauce to perfectly complement the eggs.

Ingredients

  • 8 eggs (雞蛋 - jīdàn)
  • Salt (鹽 - yán)
  • Water (水 - shuǐ)
  • Spring onions, chopped (蔥末 - cōngmò)
  • Ginger, minced (姜末 - jiāngmò)
  • Garlic, minced (蒜末 - suànmò)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽 - shēngchōu)
  • A dash of dark soy sauce (老抽 - lǎochōu)
  • Oyster sauce (蠔油 - háoyóu)
  • Sugar (白糖 - báitáng)
  • Cornstarch (玉米淀粉 - yùmǐ diànfěn)
  • 1/2 tbsp rice vinegar (陳醋 - Chéncù)
  • Water (水 - shuǐ)
  • Ketchup (番茄醬 - fānqié jiàng) (optional, amount to taste)
  • Cooking oil (油 - yóu)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the eggs: Wash eggs with salt water for 5 minutes to remove bacteria. Discard any cracked eggs. Dry the eggs.
  2. Prepare the garnish: Chop spring onions, mince ginger and garlic. Set aside.
  3. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, mix soy sauce, dark soy sauce, oyster sauce, sugar, cornstarch, rice vinegar, water, and ketchup (optional). Stir well. Set aside.
  4. Fry the eggs: Heat oil in a pan over medium-high heat. Crack eggs into the pan one at a time. Fry until the bottom is set, then flip and fry the other side until golden brown. Repeat for all eggs.
  5. Stir-fry aromatics: Use the remaining oil in the pan to stir-fry the minced spring onions, ginger, and garlic until fragrant.
  6. Combine and simmer: Add the fried eggs to the pan. Pour in the prepared sauce. Gently stir to coat the eggs in the sauce. Cover and simmer for 2-3 minutes.
  7. Garnish and serve: Sprinkle with chopped spring onions. Turn off the heat. Serve immediately.

sweet_and_sour_chicken_breast.txt - Sweet and Sour Chicken Breast

Objectives

  • Prepare succulent sweet and sour chicken breast.
  • Learn a simple, flavorful marinade for chicken.
  • Master a quick and easy sweet and sour sauce.

Ingredients

  • Fresh chicken breast (amount not specified)
  • 1 tbsp salt
  • Water (for brining)
  • Salt (for seasoning)
  • Pepper (amount not specified)
  • Cooking wine (amount not specified)
  • Light soy sauce (amount not specified)
  • 1 tbsp light soy sauce (for sauce)
  • Balsamic vinegar (amount not specified)
  • 1 tsp pepper (for sauce)
  • White sugar (amount not specified)
  • 1 tsp salt (for sauce)
  • 1 tsp cornstarch (for sauce)
  • Bottled tomato sauce (small amount, for color)
  • 1 tbsp water (for sauce)
  • Potato starch (amount not specified, for coating chicken)
  • Cooking oil (amount not specified)
  • White sesame seeds (amount not specified, for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the chicken: Choose fresh, pinkish, tender, and glossy chicken breasts. Brine the chicken breast in salted water for 1 hour. Rinse and pat dry.
  2. Slice and Marinate: Cut the chicken breast into long strips, then into 2cm pieces. Place in a bowl. Add salt, pepper, cooking wine, and light soy sauce. Mix well with clean hands until chicken is coated. Let marinate for 20 minutes.
  3. Make the sauce: In a bowl, combine light soy sauce, balsamic vinegar, pepper, white sugar, salt, cornstarch, a small amount of tomato sauce, and 1 tbsp of water. Mix thoroughly. Set aside.
  4. Coat the chicken: Add potato starch to the marinated chicken, tossing gently to coat evenly.
  5. Fry the chicken: Heat oil in a wok or pan over medium heat. Fry the chicken pieces in batches until lightly golden brown. Remove with a slotted spoon and set aside.
  6. Thicken the sauce: Pour the sweet and sour sauce into the pan and cook over medium-low heat, stirring until it thickens and bubbles.
  7. Combine and finish: Add the fried chicken to the sauce. Increase heat and stir-fry until the chicken is coated and the sauce is thick. Garnish with white sesame seeds.
  8. Serve: Serve immediately. Enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=2xjJdjiH2R4

sweet_and_sour_chicken.txt - Sweet and Sour Chicken

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy sweet and sour chicken dish.
  • Understand the importance of marinating chicken for flavor and tenderness.
  • Master the technique of double-frying chicken for a crispy texture.

Ingredients

  • Fresh chicken breast (amount not specified)
  • 1 tbsp salt
  • Water (for brine)
  • Salt (for seasoning)
  • Pepper (amount not specified)
  • Cooking wine (amount not specified)
  • Light soy sauce (amount not specified)
  • 1 tbsp light soy sauce (for sauce)
  • Balsamic vinegar (amount not specified)
  • 1 tsp pepper (for sauce)
  • White sugar (amount not specified)
  • 1 tsp salt (for sauce)
  • 1 tsp cornstarch (for sauce)
  • Tomato sauce (amount not specified)
  • 1 tbsp water (for sauce)
  • Potato starch (amount not specified)
  • Oil (for frying)
  • White sesame seeds (for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Marinate chicken breast in a light saltwater brine for at least one hour. This helps keep the meat fresh and tender.
  2. Clean and rinse the chicken breast.
  3. Cut the chicken breast into long strips, then into 2cm pieces.
  4. In a bowl, marinate the chicken pieces with salt, pepper, cooking wine, and light soy sauce. Mix well and let it sit for 20 minutes.
  5. Prepare the sweet and sour sauce: Combine light soy sauce, balsamic vinegar, pepper, white sugar, salt, cornstarch, and tomato sauce. Mix well with 1 tbsp of water and set aside.
  6. Add potato starch to the marinated chicken and toss to coat evenly.
  7. Heat oil in a wok or pan to 50% heat, then reduce to low heat.
  8. Deep fry the chicken pieces in batches until lightly golden brown. Remove and set aside.
  9. In a separate pan, heat the prepared sweet and sour sauce over medium-low heat. Stir until it thickens and bubbles.
  10. Add the fried chicken pieces to the sauce. Increase the heat and stir-fry quickly until the sauce coats the chicken evenly.
  11. Garnish with white sesame seeds before serving.
