sweet_and_sour_tofu.txt - Sweet and Sour Tofu

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare crispy tofu cubes.
  • Make a delicious sweet and sour sauce.
  • Create a balanced sweet and sour flavor profile.
  • Cook tofu that is crispy on the outside and tender on the inside.
  • Prepare a dish suitable for children.
  • Learn a technique to prevent tofu from sticking together.
  • Remove the beany smell from tofu.
  • Efficiently fry tofu without splattering oil.

Ingredients

  • Old tofu (quantity unspecified)
  • Water
  • Salt
  • 150g Cornstarch or potato starch
  • Tomato paste (quantity unspecified)
  • Sugar (quantity unspecified)
  • Salt (quantity unspecified)
  • White vinegar (quantity unspecified)
  • Cooking oil (quantity unspecified)
  • Sesame seeds (quantity unspecified)

Instructions

  1. Cut the old tofu into thick slices, then into strips, and finally into bite-sized cubes.
  2. Soak the tofu cubes in warm, salted water for 5 minutes to remove the beany smell.
  3. Blanch the tofu in boiling water for 2 minutes to further remove the beany smell and prevent breakage during frying. Immediately transfer to cold water to stop the cooking process and prevent sticking. Drain well.
  4. Prepare the sweet and sour sauce: Mix tomato paste, sugar, salt, and white vinegar in a bowl until dissolved. Set aside.
  5. Toss the drained tofu cubes in cornstarch until evenly coated. Shake off excess starch.
  6. Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan to 60% heat (oil shimmers, small bubbles appear when a chopstick is inserted).
  7. Carefully add the tofu cubes to the hot oil using a slotted spoon, avoiding overcrowding. Do not stir immediately.
  8. Fry for 30 seconds, then gently stir to ensure even cooking. Continue frying for about 1 minute until lightly set.
  9. Reduce heat to medium-low and continue frying for 3-5 minutes, until golden brown.
  10. Remove the tofu and set aside. Increase the oil temperature to 80% heat.
  11. Return the tofu to the hot oil and fry for another 15 seconds to achieve extra crispiness. Remove with a slotted spoon, draining excess oil.
  12. Add the sweet and sour sauce to the wok or pan. Simmer over medium heat for 1 minute until slightly thickened.
  13. Add the fried tofu to the sauce, tossing to coat evenly. Cook until the tofu absorbs the sauce.
  14. Before serving, sprinkle with toasted sesame seeds and toss gently.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=UdnMXpyPelo

sweet_potato_crispy.txt - Crispy Sweet Potato

Objectives

  • Learn a new way to prepare sweet potatoes beyond steaming or boiling.
  • Create a crispy, sweet, and flavorful sweet potato snack.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients for an easy-to-make recipe.

Ingredients

  • 1 large sweet potato (about 250g)
  • 2 eggs (母鸡的蛋 - mother hen's eggs)
  • 1 small spoon of salt (一小勺食盐)
  • 1 large spoon of all-purpose flour (一大勺普通面粉)
  • 1/2 spoon of corn starch or potato starch (半勺玉米淀粉或土豆淀粉)
  • Appropriate amount of water (适量的清水)
  • 1 spoon of corn oil (一勺玉米油)
  • A large handful of white sesame seeds (一大把白芝麻)
  • Cooking oil (食用油) for frying

Instructions

  1. Wash and peel the sweet potato.
  2. Cut the sweet potato into thick slices (about 1cm thick).
  3. Boil the sweet potato slices in water for about 1 minute.
  4. Drain the sweet potato slices and place them in a bowl.
  5. In a separate bowl, whisk together the eggs, salt, flour, cornstarch (or potato starch), and water until a thick batter forms.
  6. Add the corn oil and sesame seeds to the batter and mix well.
  7. Pour the batter over the sweet potato slices and toss to coat evenly.
  8. Heat cooking oil in a pan over medium heat until it reaches 60% heat (筷子放进去冒密集的小泡泡).
  9. Fry the sweet potato slices in batches, ensuring to flip them frequently for even cooking.
  10. Once the sweet potato slices are golden brown and crispy, remove them from the pan and drain on a wire rack.
  11. Increase the oil temperature and deep fry the sweet potato slices again for about 30 seconds to make them extra crispy.
  12. Remove from the pan and drain excess oil.
  13. Serve immediately. Optional: Add salad dressing, tomato sauce, barbecue powder, or cumin powder to taste.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=NgA3QNfGeO4

sweet_potato_egg_pancakes.txt - Sweet Potato Egg Pancakes

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and soft sweet potato egg pancakes.
  • Master the technique of preparing the sweet potato batter.
  • Understand the importance of low-heat frying for optimal texture.

Ingredients

  • 3 small sweet potatoes
  • 4 grams yeast powder
  • 60 grams warm water
  • 2 tablespoons flour
  • Scallions (amount not specified)
  • 88 grams sugar
  • Cooking oil (amount not specified)
  • White sesame seeds (amount not specified)

Instructions

  1. Prepare 3 small sweet potatoes: peel, clean, and thinly slice them.
  2. Grind the sliced sweet potatoes using a food processor until finely ground.
  3. In a large bowl, combine the ground sweet potatoes, 4 grams of yeast powder, and mix well using chopsticks.
  4. Add 60 grams of lukewarm water and mix until the yeast is dissolved.
  5. Gradually add 2 tablespoons of flour, mixing until a smooth batter forms without dry flour particles. Adjust flour or water as needed to achieve the right consistency.
  6. Cover the bowl and let the batter rise in a warm place until doubled in size (approximately 40 minutes).
  7. While the batter rises, prepare the scallions: chop finely.
  8. In a separate bowl, combine the chopped scallions and 88 grams of sugar; mix well. Add warm water if the mixture is too dry.
  9. Heat a frying pan and lightly brush with cooking oil to prevent sticking.
  10. Once the oil is hot, turn off the heat.
  11. Pour a portion of the batter into the pan, spreading it into a pancake shape.
  12. Smooth the surface of the pancake with a silicone spatula and sprinkle with white sesame seeds.
  13. Cover the pan and cook over low heat for 4 minutes.
  14. Flip the pancake and cook the other side for another 4 minutes, ensuring even cooking by gently moving the pan.
  15. Repeat steps 10-14 until all the batter is used.
  16. Once cooked, let the pancakes cool slightly before slicing and serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=U3RC9J8vakk

sweet_potato_egg_pancake.txt - Sweet Potato Egg Pancake

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious sweet potato egg pancakes.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful recipe perfect for all ages.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients for easy preparation.

Ingredients

  • 3 small sweet potatoes
  • 4 grams yeast powder
  • 60 grams lukewarm water
  • 2 tablespoons flour (adjust as needed for consistency)
  • Scallions (amount to taste)
  • 88 grams sugar
  • Cooking oil
  • White sesame seeds

Instructions

  1. Prepare 3 small sweet potatoes: peel, clean, and thinly slice them.
  2. Grind the sliced sweet potatoes using a food processor until finely ground.
  3. In a large bowl, combine the ground sweet potato, 4 grams of yeast powder, and mix well using chopsticks.
  4. Add 60 grams of lukewarm water and continue mixing until well combined.
  5. Gradually add 2 tablespoons of flour, mixing thoroughly to eliminate dry particles. Adjust flour or water as needed to achieve a smooth batter consistency.
  6. Cover the batter and let it rise in a warm place for about 40 minutes, or until doubled in size.
  7. Prepare the scallions by finely chopping them.
  8. In a separate bowl, combine the chopped scallions and 88 grams of sugar. Mix well; add lukewarm water if the mixture is too dry.
  9. Heat a pan and brush it evenly with cooking oil to prevent sticking. You may use an electric pan if preferred.
  10. Once the oil is hot, turn off the heat. Pour a portion of the batter onto the pan, spreading it into a cake shape.
  11. Use a silicone spatula to smooth the surface and sprinkle with white sesame seeds.
  12. Cover the pan and cook over low heat for 4 minutes.
  13. Carefully flip the pancake and cook the other side for another 4 minutes, ensuring even browning. Continuously adjust the position of the pan during cooking to prevent burning.
  14. Repeat steps 10-13 until all the batter is used.
  15. Once cooked, let the pancakes cool slightly before slicing and serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=U3RC9J8vakk

sweet_potato_leaves.txt - Sweet Potato Leaves Stir-fry

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare sweet potato leaves to prevent yellowing and maintain vibrant green color.
  • Master a simple yet restaurant-quality stir-fry technique for sweet potato leaves.
  • Understand the importance of proper cleaning and pre-treatment of sweet potato leaves.

Ingredients

  • 500g sweet potato leaves
  • Pinch of salt
  • Pinch of baking soda
  • 2-3 cloves garlic, minced
  • 2-3 red chilies, thinly sliced
  • 1 tbsp cooking oil (for coating leaves)
  • Lard (for stir-frying)
  • Sauce:
    • 1 tbsp salt
    • Dash of white sugar
    • Dash of chicken essence
    • 1 tsp cornstarch
    • Water

Instructions

  1. Clean Sweet Potato Leaves: Remove old leaves, insect eyes, and bugs. Wash thoroughly.
  2. Pre-treat Leaves: In a large bowl, add sweet potato leaves, a pinch of salt, and a pinch of baking soda. Add enough water to submerge the leaves. Soak for 10 minutes.
  3. Rinse and Drain: Rinse sweet potato leaves thoroughly under running water, cleaning each leaf individually to remove any remaining impurities. Drain well.
  4. Prepare Aromatics: Mince garlic and thinly slice red chilies.
  5. Make Sauce: In a small bowl, whisk together salt, sugar, chicken essence, cornstarch, and water until smooth. Set aside.
  6. Oil the Leaves: Add cooking oil to the drained sweet potato leaves. Toss gently to coat each leaf. This prevents blackening during stir-frying.
  7. Separate Stems and Leaves: Separate the stems from the leaves for easier cooking.
  8. Stir-fry Aromatics: Heat lard in a wok or iron pan over medium-high heat. Add minced garlic and red chilies. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Stir-fry Sweet Potato Stems: Add sweet potato stems to the pan and stir-fry for about 5 minutes until slightly softened.
  10. Stir-fry Leaves: Add sweet potato leaves to the pan. Increase heat to high and stir-fry for about 50 seconds, ensuring even cooking and preventing water from accumulating.
  11. Add Sauce: Pour the prepared sauce into the pan and stir-fry until the sauce coats the leaves evenly.
  12. Serve: Turn off the heat and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=jCXltVkG_eU

taro_balls.txt - Crispy Taro Balls

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and crispy taro balls.
  • Master the technique of preparing and frying taro for optimal texture.
  • Understand the importance of oil temperature control in deep frying.

Ingredients

  • 1 Taro (5 yuan)
  • 1 Carrot
  • Some scallions
  • Salt
  • 1 tsp Pepper
  • 1 tbsp Flour
  • 1 tbsp Potato starch
  • 1 tbsp Water
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Cut the taro in half, then peel and thinly slice it. Alternatively, use a slicer for easier preparation.
  2. Peel and thinly slice a carrot.
  3. Finely chop some scallions.
  4. Combine the sliced taro and carrot in a bowl.
  5. Add salt, pepper, flour, potato starch, and water to the bowl. Mix well.
  6. Form small balls from the mixture.
  7. Heat cooking oil in a pan to 50% heat (oil should bubble when a chopstick is inserted).
  8. Gently place the taro balls in the hot oil, avoiding overcrowding. Fry on medium-low heat for approximately 1 minute per side, until lightly browned.
  9. Increase the heat slightly and continue frying, frequently turning the balls to ensure even cooking and a crispy exterior. Fry until golden brown and crispy (about 6 minutes).
  10. Remove the taro balls and let excess oil drain.
  11. For extra crispiness, briefly return the balls to the hot oil for 20 seconds before removing.
  12. Serve immediately and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=33uZwBy8HrM

taro_meatballs.txt - Taro Meatballs

Objectives

  • Learn to make soft and chewy taro meatballs.
  • Master a simple method for preparing taro.
  • Create a flavorful and nutritious dish using readily available ingredients.

Ingredients

  • Taro (amount not specified)
  • 500g Sweet potato starch (or sweet potato flour)
  • Water (for boiling and cooling)
  • Vegetable oil (for frying)
  • Lard (optional, for added flavor)
  • Onion (amount not specified)
  • Dried chili peppers (amount not specified)
  • Light soy sauce (amount not specified)
  • Dark soy sauce (amount not specified)
  • Salt (amount not specified)
  • Pepper (amount not specified)
  • Green onions (amount not specified)
  • Cilantro (amount not specified)

Instructions

  1. Clean the taro thoroughly using a brush, scrubbing off any dirt. Rinse multiple times with clean water until the water runs clear.
  2. Place the cleaned taro in a pressure cooker. Cook under pressure for 20 minutes.
  3. After pressure cooking, allow the steam to dissipate before carefully opening the pressure cooker.
  4. Remove the taro and peel it while still hot. Mash the taro using a food masher until smooth.
  5. Add 500g of sweet potato starch to the mashed taro. Wear disposable gloves and knead thoroughly until a smooth, medium-firm dough is formed. No dry starch particles should remain.
  6. Transfer the dough to a cutting board and continue kneading. Divide the dough into small portions and roll into long strips. Cut the strips into smaller pieces.
  7. Shape the small pieces into small balls.
  8. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Gently add the taro balls, being careful not to burn your hands.
  9. Cook over high heat for 30 seconds, then stir gently. Cover and cook for 3 minutes.
  10. When the taro balls float and expand, immediately remove them and transfer to a bowl of cold water to cool. This process makes them chewier.
  11. While preparing the sauce, finely chop dried chili peppers, white parts of green onions, and green onion leaves separately. Finely chop cilantro.
  12. Heat a pan with a little lard (or vegetable oil). Add chopped onions and chili peppers and stir-fry until fragrant.
  13. Add light and dark soy sauce, salt, and pepper to taste. (No other seasonings are added in this recipe).
  14. Add the cooled taro balls to the pan and stir-fry until heated through.
  15. Simmer for another 5 minutes, covered.
  16. Add your preferred green vegetables and cook for 1 minute.
  17. Stir in chopped cilantro and green onions. Remove from heat.
  18. Serve and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=08IyY8pTRLw

taro_meatball.txt - Taro Meatballs

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and healthy taro meatballs.
  • Master the art of preparing taro for optimal texture and flavor.
  • Combine taro with various ingredients for a nutritious and flavorful dish.

Ingredients

  • 1 large taro
  • Salt
  • Dried mushrooms (soaked in warm water)
  • 1 small carrot (shredded)
  • Sausage (finely chopped)
  • Dried plum meat (finely chopped)
  • Several cloves of garlic (minced)
  • A small piece of ginger (minced)
  • Green onions (white and green parts, chopped separately)
  • Cooking oil
  • Light soy sauce
  • Pepper
  • Oyster sauce
  • 60g tapioca starch

Instructions

  1. Cut the taro in half. Peel and cut into thin slices, then shred (or use a grater).
  2. Place shredded taro in a bowl, add salt, mix well, and set aside for 10 minutes.
  3. Prepare the soaked mushrooms, shredding them by hand and rinsing thoroughly. Set aside.
  4. Prepare the carrot: peel, slice thinly, then shred. Set aside.
  5. Prepare the sausage: chop finely. Set aside.
  6. Prepare the dried plum meat: remove skin, slice thinly, then mince. Set aside.
  7. Mince garlic and ginger. Set aside.
  8. Chop green onion whites and greens separately. Set aside.
  9. Heat cooking oil in a pan. Add sausage and cook until browned, releasing fat.
  10. Add minced garlic, ginger, and green onion whites. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  11. Add mushrooms and carrots. Stir-fry over medium heat until cooked.
  12. Season with light soy sauce, pepper, and oyster sauce.
  13. Add the shredded taro to the pan and mix well.
  14. Add tapioca starch and mix thoroughly until no dry starch remains.
  15. Wear disposable gloves. Take a small amount of the mixture and shape it into a ball (about the size of a ping pong ball).
  16. Place the formed meatballs in a steamer basket.
  17. Steam over high heat for 18 minutes and 8 seconds.
  18. Garnish with chopped green onions before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=eUAYkMB2s-c

tender_chicken_legs.txt - Tender and Delicious Hand-cut Chicken Legs

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare tender and flavorful chicken legs.
  • Master a simple yet delicious recipe for home-cooked chicken.
  • Understand techniques for cleaning and tenderizing chicken legs.

Ingredients

  • Fresh chicken legs (quantity not specified)
  • Salt (amount to taste)
  • Flour (amount to taste)
  • Green onions (amount to taste)
  • Ginger (amount to taste)
  • 1 tbsp cooking wine
  • Water (enough to cover chicken legs)
  • Garlic (amount to taste)
  • 1 tbsp salt
  • Sugar (amount to taste)
  • Soy sauce (amount to taste)
  • A handful of white sesame seeds
  • Cooking oil (amount to taste)

Instructions

  1. Sprinkle salt and flour on the chicken legs. Rub thoroughly to remove impurities.
  2. Rinse the chicken legs with clean water.
  3. Use a cleaver to lightly pound the chicken legs to tenderize and speed up cooking.
  4. Place chicken legs in a pot. Add green onions, ginger, and cooking wine.
  5. Add enough water to cover the chicken legs. Cover and simmer over low heat for 15 minutes.
  6. While chicken cooks, prepare the sauce: finely chop green onions, ginger, and garlic.
  7. In a small bowl, combine chopped green onions, ginger, garlic, 1 tbsp salt, sugar, soy sauce, and white sesame seeds.
  8. Pour hot oil over the sauce to enhance the aroma. Set aside.
  9. After 15 minutes, remove chicken legs from the pot and rinse with clean water. Let cool.
  10. Once cool, cut chicken legs into bite-sized pieces.
  11. Pour the prepared sauce over the chicken pieces.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=KXHaPxlDzm4

tender_chicken_stew.txt - Tender Chicken Stew (لذيذ جداً دجاج مطهو مع فطر)

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare tender, flavorful chicken without a gamey smell.
  • Master a simple yet effective chicken marinade technique.
  • Create a delicious chicken stew with mushrooms and noodles.

Ingredients

  • Young chicken (about 1 year old), cut into pieces
  • 1 tsp flour
  • 1/2 tbsp light soy sauce
  • Cooking wine (to remove gamey smell)
  • Some oyster sauce
  • A little pepper
  • A handful of mushrooms
  • A handful of sweet potato noodles
  • 1 onion, chopped
  • Ginger, sliced
  • Garlic, chopped
  • 1 green pepper, deseeded and sliced
  • 1 red pepper, deseeded and sliced
  • A handful of cilantro, chopped (including roots, for soaking in water to alleviate cold)
  • Vegetable oil (canola or peanut oil)
  • 1 tbsp soybean paste
  • 1 tsp table salt
  • A little dark soy sauce (for coloring)
  • Boiling water

Instructions

  1. Cut the young chicken into bite-sized pieces.
  2. Add 1 tsp of flour to the chicken, mix well, and rinse thoroughly with water until the water runs clear. This removes blood and impurities.
  3. Marinate the chicken with 1/2 tbsp light soy sauce, cooking wine, oyster sauce, and a little pepper. Do not add salt yet. Mix well and let it marinate for 20 minutes.
  4. Soak mushrooms and sweet potato noodles in warm water.
  5. Chop onion, ginger, garlic, green and red peppers, and cilantro.
  6. Heat vegetable oil in a wok or pan until it slightly smokes.
  7. Sauté onion, ginger, and garlic until fragrant.
  8. Add green and red peppers and continue sautéing until fragrant.
  9. Add the marinated chicken and stir-fry over high heat for about 2 minutes to release moisture and prevent a gamey smell.
  10. Add 1 tbsp soybean paste, 1 tsp salt, and a little dark soy sauce. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  11. Add boiling water to just cover the chicken. Do not use cold water.
  12. Bring to a simmer, then reduce heat and cover. Let it simmer for 10 minutes.
  13. Add the soaked mushrooms and noodles. Cover and simmer for another 10 minutes.
  14. Add the green and red peppers and cook for 30 seconds.
  15. Garnish with cilantro.
  16. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=3Ri95qtnYoA

three_color_chicken_cubes.txt - 三色鸡丁

Objectives

  • Learn to make tender and juicy chicken cubes.
  • Create a delicious and easy-to-make chicken and vegetable stir-fry.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful cooking technique.

Ingredients

  • Fresh chicken breast (amount not specified)
  • 1 tbsp salt (for chicken marinade)
  • Ginger slices (a few)
  • Salt (amount not specified, for chicken marinade)
  • Pepper (amount not specified, for chicken marinade)
  • Soy sauce (amount not specified, for chicken marinade)
  • Cornstarch (amount not specified, for chicken marinade)
  • Peanut oil (amount not specified, for chicken marinade)
  • 1 large potato
  • 1 carrot
  • 1 large green pepper
  • Scallions (amount not specified)
  • 1 piece ginger
  • Garlic cloves (a few)
  • Cooking oil (amount not specified)
  • 1 tbsp yellow soybean paste

Instructions

  1. Select fresh, vibrant pink chicken breast with a good sheen.
  2. Marinate chicken breast in salt water for 5 minutes to disinfect, improve texture, and enhance nutrition.
  3. Rinse and drain the chicken, then slice it into long strips and finally dice it into even cubes.
  4. In a bowl, mix the chicken with ginger slices, salt, pepper, soy sauce, and cornstarch. Add peanut oil to seal in moisture.
  5. Peel and dice the potato into small cubes. Soak in water to prevent oxidation and remove excess starch.
  6. Peel, slice, and dice the carrot into larger cubes.
  7. Remove the stem and seeds from the green pepper, then dice into small pieces.
  8. Mince the scallions, ginger, and garlic.
  9. Heat oil in a wok or pan. Stir-fry potato cubes until translucent and slightly browned. Remove and set aside.
  10. Stir-fry carrot cubes until slightly browned. Remove and set aside.
  11. Stir-fry the marinated chicken cubes until cooked through and slightly browned. Remove and set aside.
  12. Add more oil to the pan, stir-fry minced scallions, ginger, and garlic until fragrant.
  13. Add yellow soybean paste and stir-fry until fragrant.
  14. Add the chicken, potato, carrot, and green pepper to the pan. Stir-fry until well combined and heated through.
  15. Add a bit of oil and thicken the sauce by stir-frying for about 30 seconds.
  16. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=icl-izH70Kw

tofu_broccoli.txt - Tofu and Broccoli Stir-fry

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple, healthy, and delicious tofu and broccoli stir-fry.
  • Understand how to prepare tofu and broccoli for optimal texture and flavor.
  • Master a quick and easy cooking method suitable for busy individuals.

Ingredients

  • 2 blocks firm tofu (老豆腐)
  • 1 small head of broccoli (西兰花)
  • 1 egg (鸡蛋)
  • Salt (食盐)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)
  • Soy sauce (生抽)
  • Garlic (蒜末)
  • Scallions (葱花)
  • Mushroom seasoning (松茸鲜)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the broccoli: Remove the florets from the stem using a knife. Set aside the florets; save the stems for another meal.
  2. Prepare the tofu: Crumble the tofu into a large bowl using your hands. Set aside.
  3. Blanch the broccoli: Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add a pinch of salt and a little cooking oil. Add the broccoli florets and blanch for 30 seconds. Remove immediately with a slotted spoon.
  4. Combine ingredients: Add the blanched broccoli to the bowl with the crumbled tofu. Add one egg, salt, mushroom seasoning, minced garlic, chopped scallions, and soy sauce. Mix well with chopsticks until all ingredients are thoroughly combined.
  5. Stir-fry: Heat cooking oil (preferably lard) in a wok or frying pan over medium-low heat. Add the tofu and broccoli mixture to the pan. Stir-fry continuously, allowing the tofu to brown slightly and the moisture to evaporate.
  6. Finish and serve: Continue stir-frying until the tofu is slightly crispy and fragrant. Turn off the heat, transfer to a serving dish, and serve immediately. Enjoy with rice.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=K_8Q23wZTGM

tofu_chrysanthemum_stirfry.txt - 香煎豆腐茼蒿

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and healthy tofu and chrysanthemum stir-fry.
  • Master a simple cooking technique requiring minimal culinary skills.
  • Create a low-fat, nutritious dish perfect for weight management.

Ingredients

  • 1 bunch of chrysanthemum greens (茼蒿菜)
  • 1 block of firm tofu (老豆腐)
  • 2 fresh eggs (土鸡蛋)
  • Salt (食盐)
  • Chicken bouillon (鸡精)
  • Thirteen spice blend (十三香)
  • Pepper (胡椒粉)
  • Light soy sauce (生抽)
  • Garlic (蒜子)
  • Peanut oil (花生油)

Instructions

  1. Clean the chrysanthemum greens: Remove wilted leaves and roots. Wash thoroughly, separating each leaf to remove dirt. Drain well.
  2. Prepare the tofu: Add salt to the tofu surface, then submerge it in warm water to remove beany smell and maintain freshness. Once soaked, drain and crumble into a bowl.
  3. Mix tofu and eggs: Add crumbled tofu to a bowl. Add 2 eggs, chicken bouillon, thirteen spice, pepper, and a small amount of light soy sauce. Mix well.
  4. Prepare the chrysanthemum: Chop the chrysanthemum greens finely and add to the tofu mixture. Mix well.
  5. Prepare the garlic: Mince the garlic cloves.
  6. Stir-fry the garlic: Heat peanut oil in a wok or pan. Add minced garlic and stir-fry until fragrant over low heat.
  7. Stir-fry tofu and chrysanthemum: Add the tofu and chrysanthemum mixture to the pan. Stir-fry over high heat for 3-5 minutes, ensuring even cooking and to evaporate moisture.
  8. Adjust cooking time: Continue stir-frying until the tofu is slightly browned and the greens are cooked through (approximately 6 minutes total). The tofu and greens should be separate and not mushy.
  9. Serve: Serve immediately. Enjoy the delicious and healthy stir-fry while it's hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=YIEmNF93L0Y

tofu_egg_drop_soup.txt - 豆腐蛋花湯 (Dòufu dàn huā tāng)

Objectives

  • Prepare a flavorful and nutritious tofu and egg drop soup.
  • Learn a simple method for preserving tofu freshness.
  • Master the technique of creating a smooth, thickened soup.

Ingredients

  • 1 block of tofu (amount not specified)
  • 3 eggs
  • 1/2 cup of chopped tomatoes (amount approximate)
  • 1 small can of seafood mushrooms (amount not specified)
  • Peanut oil (amount not specified)
  • Salt (amount to taste)
  • Light soy sauce (amount to taste)
  • Pepper (amount to taste)
  • Oyster sauce (amount to taste)
  • Water (amount not specified)
  • Water for starch thickening (amount not specified)
  • Chopped green onions (amount to taste)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Tofu: Soak the tofu in clean water with a pinch of salt to preserve freshness.
  2. Prepare the Eggs: Crack 3 eggs into a bowl, whisk the whites and yolks together thoroughly. Set aside.
  3. Prepare the Tomatoes: Dice the tomatoes into small cubes.
  4. Prepare the Mushrooms: Clean and chop the seafood mushrooms into approximately 1cm cubes. Remove roots and wash thoroughly.
  5. Marinate the Tofu: Cut the tofu into small cubes. Add the whisked eggs to the tofu cubes and mix until the tofu is evenly coated. Set aside.
  6. Fry the Egg and Tofu Mixture: Heat peanut oil in a pan. Fry the tofu and egg mixture until golden brown. Remove and set aside.
  7. Prepare the Soup Base: Add a little oil to the pan, add a pinch of salt. Add a small amount of water, stir. Season with salt, light soy sauce, pepper, and oyster sauce. Stir, increase heat, and bring to a boil. Simmer for about 1 minute to cook out the tomato flavor.
  8. Combine and Simmer: Add the fried tofu and egg mixture to the soup. Add the prepared seafood mushrooms, stir gently to distribute. Cover and simmer over low heat for 3-5 minutes.
  9. Thicken and Garnish: Uncover, stir to evenly distribute ingredients. Increase heat and bring to a simmer. Add a little cornstarch slurry to thicken the broth. Sprinkle with chopped green onions.
  10. Serve: Serve hot in a bowl.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=4aCejcWVFF4

tofu_egg_meat_steam.txt - Steamed Tofu with Egg and Minced Meat

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious steamed tofu dish with eggs and minced meat.
  • Master the simple steps involved in preparing this family-friendly recipe.
  • Understand the benefits of using silken tofu for a smoother texture.

Ingredients

  • 1 box silken tofu (内酯豆腐)
  • 4 eggs (鸡蛋)
  • 100g pork shoulder or plum meat (梅花肉 or 前腿肉), minced (剁成肉末)
  • 1-2 stalks scallions (小葱), chopped (切成葱末)
  • 1 piece ginger (生姜), minced (切成姜末)
  • Several cloves garlic (蒜子), minced (切成蒜末)
  • Salt (食盐)
  • White pepper (胡椒粉)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • Light soy sauce (生抽)
  • Dark soy sauce (老抽)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)

Instructions

  1. Invert a box of silken tofu into a suitable bowl.
  2. Crack 4 eggs into the bowl on top of the tofu.
  3. Use a knife to gently cut the tofu into smaller pieces within the bowl.
  4. Add enough water to a pot, place the bowl inside, cover, and steam over high heat for 10 minutes.
  5. While steaming, mince the pork. Alternatively, use a food processor.
  6. Chop the scallions, mince the ginger, and mince the garlic.
  7. Heat oil in a pan, add minced garlic, ginger, and scallions; stir-fry until fragrant.
  8. Add the minced pork and stir-fry until the color changes.
  9. Season with salt, white pepper, oyster sauce, light soy sauce, and a little dark soy sauce.
  10. Stir-fry until the sauce thickens slightly.
  11. Once the tofu and eggs are steamed, remove and pour the meat sauce evenly over the top.
  12. Garnish with chopped scallions.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Z4Z5gaMob_0

tofu_green_vegetable_stew.txt - توفو مطهو ببطء مع خضار خضراء

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple, delicious tofu and green vegetable stew.
  • Master the technique of frying tofu until golden and crispy.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to enhance the taste of the stew.

Ingredients

  • Shanghai green root pieces (quantity unspecified)
  • Salt (to taste)
  • Water (for washing and cooking)
  • Firm tofu (quantity unspecified)
  • Garlic (quantity unspecified)
  • Green onions (quantity unspecified)
  • Red pepper (quantity unspecified)
  • Dried sea pepper (small amount)
  • Fresh shiitake mushrooms (2)
  • 1 tsp salt
  • A little sugar
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce
  • 1 tbsp oyster sauce
  • 1 tbsp cornstarch
  • White vinegar (amount unspecified)
  • Water (for sauce)
  • Cooking oil (for frying)
  • Sesame oil (for finishing)

Instructions

  1. Prepare Shanghai green root pieces: Remove the roots, trim the corners, wash thoroughly with salted water, then rinse with clean water twice.
  2. Prepare the tofu: Cut firm tofu into small pieces.
  3. Prepare the aromatics: Crush and chop garlic. Finely chop green onions and red pepper. Set aside.
  4. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, combine salt, sugar, soy sauce, oyster sauce, cornstarch, vinegar, and water. Mix well.
  5. Fry the tofu: Heat cooking oil in a pan. Add tofu and fry slowly until golden brown on both sides. Remove and set aside.
  6. Fry the shiitake mushrooms: Add shiitake mushrooms to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant. Remove and set aside.
  7. Sauté aromatics: Add cooking oil to the pan, add green onions, dried sea pepper, and garlic. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  8. Add greens: Increase heat, add Shanghai greens and stir-fry for 1 minute until tender.
  9. Combine ingredients: Add fried tofu and mushrooms to the pan. Stir-fry.
  10. Add water and simmer: Add water, simmer for 1 minute. Add red pepper.
  11. Add sauce and thicken: Pour in the prepared sauce, allowing the stew to absorb the sauce completely.
  12. Finish: Drizzle with sesame oil and stir-fry quickly a few times. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=U5cWr2dSPIg

tofu_green_veg.txt - Slow-Cooked Tofu with Green Vegetables

Objectives

  • Prepare a simple, delicious, and nutritious tofu dish suitable for all ages.
  • Learn to properly clean and prepare green vegetables.
  • Master a flavorful sauce for the tofu and vegetables.
  • Understand the importance of using firm tofu for frying.
  • Learn a quick and easy cooking method.

Ingredients

  • Shanghai green root pieces (quantity not specified)
  • Salt (to taste)
  • Water (for washing)
  • Firm tofu (quantity not specified)
  • Garlic (several cloves)
  • Green onions (quantity not specified)
  • Red chili pepper (1, or to taste)
  • Dried sea pepper (a pinch)
  • Fresh shiitake mushrooms (2)
  • 1 tsp salt
  • A little sugar
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce
  • 1 tbsp oyster sauce
  • 1 tbsp cornstarch
  • White vinegar (amount not specified)
  • Water (amount not specified)
  • Cooking oil (amount not specified)
  • Sesame oil (amount not specified)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Shanghai green root pieces: Wash thoroughly with salted water, then rinse twice with clean water.
  2. Prepare the tofu: Cut firm tofu into small pieces.
  3. Prepare the aromatics: Crush and chop garlic. Finely chop green onions and red chili pepper.
  4. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, mix salt, sugar, soy sauce, oyster sauce, cornstarch, vinegar, and water.
  5. Fry the tofu: Heat cooking oil in a pan. Add tofu and fry until golden brown on both sides. Remove and set aside.
  6. Fry the mushrooms: In the same pan, fry shiitake mushrooms until fragrant. Remove and set aside.
  7. Sauté aromatics: Add cooking oil to the pan, add green onions, dried sea pepper, and garlic. Sauté until fragrant.
  8. Add mustard seeds: Increase heat, add mustard seeds, and stir-fry for 1 minute until fragrant.
  9. Combine ingredients: Add the fried tofu and mushrooms to the pan. Stir-fry evenly.
  10. Add water and simmer: Add water and simmer for 1 minute.
  11. Add chili and sauce: Add red chili pepper and the prepared sauce. Stir well.
  12. Simmer until sauce thickens: Allow the dish to simmer until the sauce has thickened and the vegetables are tender.
  13. Finish: Drizzle with sesame oil and stir-fry quickly a few times. Serve hot.

tofu_lactone_egg_stir_fry.txt - 豆腐乳炒蛋 (Dòufu rǔ chǎo dàn)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and simple tofu lactone and egg stir-fry.
  • Master the technique of stir-frying aromatics for maximum flavor.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to complement the tofu and eggs.

Ingredients

  • 2 cans of tofu lactone (豆腐乳 - Dòufu rǔ)
  • 3-4 eggs (雞蛋 - Jīdàn) from free-range chickens
  • 適量 scallions (蔥 - Cōng) , finely chopped
  • 適量 cilantro (香菜 - Xiāngcài) ,finely chopped
  • 適量 ginger (薑 - Jiāng), thinly sliced
  • 適量 garlic (蒜 - Suàn), minced
  • 適量 dried chilies (乾辣椒 - Gān làjiāo), sliced into rings
  • 適量 cooking oil (食用油 - Shíyòng yóu)
  • Salt (鹽 - Yán) to taste

Instructions

  1. Turn the cans of tofu lactone upside down and remove the packaging. Cut into small cubes.
  2. Crack the eggs into a bowl and whisk until the whites and yolks are fully combined. Set aside.
  3. Finely chop the scallions, cilantro, and dried chilies. Thinly slice the ginger and mince the garlic.
  4. Heat a wok or pan over medium-high heat. Add cooking oil.
  5. Add the ginger, garlic, and dried chilies to the hot oil. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  6. Add the chopped scallions and cilantro. Stir-fry until slightly browned.
  7. Remove the aromatics from the wok using a slotted spoon, leaving the infused oil behind.
  8. Add the cubed tofu lactone to the wok. Stir-fry until lightly browned.
  9. Add the minced ginger and garlic. Stir-fry briefly.
  10. Add the whisked eggs to the wok. Stir-fry until mostly cooked.
  11. Pour the infused oil and aromatics from step 7 over the tofu and eggs. Stir to combine.
  12. Add salt to taste.
  13. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=GuvEYMaJuGY

tofu_leek_cake.txt - Tofu and Leek Cake

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious Tofu and Leek Cake.
  • Master a simple and quick cooking method.
  • Impress your family with this easy yet flavorful dish.

Ingredients

  • 1 block firm tofu
  • 1 bunch leeks
  • 4 eggs
  • Salt
  • Water
  • Plum blossom pork or front leg pork (optional, thinly sliced and minced)
  • Garlic (minced)
  • Oyster sauce
  • Chicken bouillon
  • Light soy sauce
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Press tofu to remove excess water. Sprinkle with salt and soak to remove odor and enhance flavor.
  2. Wash and chop leeks into slices.
  3. Mince plum blossom pork or front leg pork (optional). Mince garlic.
  4. In a bowl, whisk together eggs, salt, pepper, oyster sauce, chicken bouillon, light soy sauce, and minced garlic.
  5. Cut the soaked tofu into small pieces.
  6. Add the tofu to the egg mixture and gently mix with chopsticks until evenly combined.
  7. Heat a non-stick pan over medium-low heat. Add a small amount of oil.
  8. Add the leeks and tofu mixture to the pan. Stir quickly to combine and form a cake shape.
  9. Cover the pan and cook slowly, stirring occasionally to ensure even cooking.
  10. Flip the cake carefully when one side is browned. Continue cooking until both sides are lightly browned and the inside is cooked through (approximately 6 minutes total).
  11. Press the cake gently with a spatula to release any remaining moisture.
  12. Serve hot. Pairs well with rice porridge.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=TF0VbHb42g8

tofu_minced_meat.txt - Simple Homemade Minced Meat Tofu

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare tender and flavorful tofu.
  • Master a simple yet nutritious minced meat tofu recipe.
  • Understand techniques for enhancing tofu texture and taste.

Ingredients

  • 2 pieces fresh soft tofu
  • Minced pork (amount not specified, adjust to preference)
  • 1 onion, finely chopped
  • 1 piece ginger, finely chopped
  • A handful of garlic, minced
  • Salt (to taste)
  • Chicken broth (amount not specified)
  • Pepper (to taste)
  • 1 tbsp soybean paste
  • Dark soy sauce (amount not specified, for color)
  • Water (for cooking and starch slurry)
  • Water starch (to thicken the sauce)
  • Sesame oil (optional, for garnish)
  • Chopped green onions (optional, for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Tofu: Cut the tofu in half horizontally and then vertically into smaller pieces. Boil in salted water for 1 minute to remove beany smell and firm the tofu. Drain well.
  2. Prepare the Meat: Mince pork (or use a meat grinder).
  3. Prepare Aromatics: Finely chop onion, ginger, and garlic.
  4. Stir-fry the Meat: Heat oil in a pan, add minced pork and stir-fry until fragrant and browned.
  5. Add Aromatics: Add chopped onion, ginger, and garlic to the pan and continue stir-frying until softened.
  6. Season: Add salt, chicken broth, pepper, and soybean paste. Stir-fry to blend flavors.
  7. Add Water and Dark Soy Sauce: Add a small amount of water to the pan, stir well. Add dark soy sauce for color. Bring to a boil.
  8. Thicken the Sauce: Mix water starch and add to the pan, stirring constantly until the sauce thickens.
  9. Combine and Simmer: Add the boiled tofu to the pan. Gently stir to coat and simmer for 1-2 minutes.
  10. Garnish and Serve: Garnish with sesame oil and chopped green onions (optional). Serve hot with rice.

tofu_minced_pork.txt - توفو لحم الخنزير المفروم

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy tofu and minced pork dish.
  • Master the technique of frying tofu to achieve a crispy exterior and soft interior.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to complement the tofu and minced pork.

Ingredients

  • 4 blocks of tofu (approximately 2 yuan)
  • 2 yuan worth of lean minced pork
  • A handful of garlic, minced
  • ½ large green and red pepper, diced
  • White part of 1 scallion, finely chopped
  • Some ginger, minced
  • Cooking oil
  • Salt
  • Light soy sauce or barbecue sauce (for dipping)
  • ½ teaspoon soy sauce
  • 1 tbsp oyster sauce
  • 50g cooking salt
  • Sugar
  • Chicken essence
  • Water

Instructions

  1. Cut the 4 blocks of tofu into small cubes.
  2. Mince the lean pork.
  3. Mince the garlic, dice the peppers, finely chop the scallion white, and mince the ginger.
  4. Heat cooking oil in a pot. Add a pinch of salt to the oil.
  5. Add the tofu cubes to the hot oil and fry slowly over medium heat until golden brown and crispy on both sides. Gently shake the pan to ensure even cooking.
  6. Once the tofu is fried, set it aside.
  7. Add more oil to the pot and stir-fry the minced pork until it changes color.
  8. Add the minced garlic, ginger, and scallion to the pork and stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Add water to the pot, along with soy sauce, oyster sauce, salt, sugar, and chicken essence. Stir well to combine.
  10. Add the fried tofu to the sauce and simmer for 2 minutes, covered.
  11. After 2 minutes, uncover the pot, add the diced peppers, and stir-fry for 15 seconds.
  12. Add a thickener (likely cornstarch slurry) and stir-fry quickly.
  13. Serve the tofu and minced pork hot. Enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=qXBEMcImuew

tofu_omelet.txt - توفو اومليت مع بيض الدجاج

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy tofu omelet.
  • Utilize simple, readily available ingredients.
  • Create a flavorful dish suitable for all ages.

Ingredients

  • 2 cans of lactone tofu
  • Eggs (from your own chickens, if possible)
  • Chopped green onions
  • Chopped dried chilies
  • Ginger (peeled and thinly sliced)
  • Garlic (minced)
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Invert and open the cans of lactone tofu. Cut into small cubes.
  2. Crack fresh eggs into a bowl and whisk until yolks and whites are fully combined. Set aside.
  3. Finely chop dried chilies, ginger, and garlic. Set aside.
  4. Chop green onions and set aside.
  5. Heat a wok or pan with cooking oil. Add the chopped chilies, ginger, garlic, and green onions. Stir-fry until fragrant and slightly browned.
  6. Remove the stir-fried mixture with a slotted spoon, reserving the infused oil in the pan.
  7. Add more cooking oil to the pan. Add the cubed lactone tofu and stir-fry until lightly browned.
  8. Add the reserved stir-fried mixture back into the pan with the tofu.
  9. Add the whisked eggs to the pan. Stir gently.
  10. Cover the pan and cook over low heat for approximately 1 minute.
  11. Remove the lid and continue cooking until the bottom of the omelet is golden brown and the top is set. The aroma of tofu and eggs will be strong.
  12. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=GuvEYMaJuGY

tofu_recipe.txt - Simple Homemade Tofu

Objectives

  • Learn a simple, delicious tofu recipe perfect for picky eaters.
  • Master a technique to keep tofu fresh and flavorful.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to complement the tofu.

Ingredients

  • 2 pieces of firm tofu
  • Salt
  • Water
  • 1 piece of scallion (green onion)
  • Ginger (amount unspecified)
  • Garlic cloves (amount unspecified)
  • Dried chilies (amount unspecified)
  • 2 scallions (green onions)
  • Coriander (cilantro) (amount unspecified)
  • Cooking oil (amount unspecified)
  • 2 tsp soy bean paste
  • Salt (amount unspecified)
  • Dark soy sauce (amount unspecified)
  • Water (amount unspecified)
  • Water starch (amount unspecified)

Instructions

  1. Add salt to the surface of the tofu and soak in warm water to keep it fresh and flavorful.
  2. Finely chop scallion, ginger, garlic, dried chilies, and coriander.
  3. Cut the soaked tofu into small pieces using a spoon or your hands.
  4. Heat cooking oil in a pan over medium-low heat.
  5. Add the tofu to the pan and fry slowly until golden brown on both sides, stirring frequently.
  6. Remove the fried tofu and set aside; leave the oil in the pan.
  7. Add the chopped scallions, ginger, garlic, and chilies to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant.
  8. Add soy bean paste, salt, and dark soy sauce; stir until fragrant.
  9. Add a small amount of water, bring to a boil, and simmer for 1-2 minutes.
  10. Add water starch to thicken the sauce.
  11. Return the fried tofu to the pan, stir, and simmer for 2 minutes.
  12. Garnish with coriander and scallions before serving.

tofu_sanxian_tang.txt - Tofu Sanxian Soup (豆腐三鲜汤)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy Tofu Sanxian Soup.
  • Master the techniques for preparing the tofu and vegetables.
  • Create a flavorful and refreshing soup perfect for any meal.

Ingredients

  • 1 block of tofu (cut into 1cm cubes)
  • 1 medium tomato (diced)
  • 1 small bowl of enoki mushrooms (cut into small segments)
  • A small bunch of cilantro (chopped)
  • 2 scallions (chopped)
  • 3 eggs
  • 1 tbsp cornstarch
  • 1/2 bowl of water (for cornstarch slurry)
  • Cooking oil
  • 1 tsp salt
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽 - shēngzhōu)
  • 1 tbsp mushroom seasoning (松茸鲜 - sōngróng xiān)
  • A pinch of pepper

Instructions

  1. Cut the tofu into 1cm cubes and soak in 80°C water for 10 minutes.
  2. Dice the tomato into small pieces.
  3. Cut the enoki mushrooms into small segments.
  4. Chop the cilantro and scallions.
  5. Whisk the eggs in a bowl until well combined.
  6. Mix cornstarch and water to create a slurry.
  7. Drain the soaked tofu.
  8. Heat oil in a pot, add diced tomatoes and salt, and sauté for 2 minutes until softened and releasing juices.
  9. Add more water to the pot, then add the tofu and enoki mushrooms. Stir well.
  10. Add soy sauce, mushroom seasoning, and pepper. Stir to combine.
  11. Gradually add the cornstarch slurry while stirring constantly to thicken the soup.
  12. Slowly pour in the egg mixture to create egg ribbons.
  13. Stir gently.
  14. Add chopped scallions and cilantro.
  15. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=BSyzhJ3aKXc

tofu_three_fresh_soup.txt - 豆腐三鲜汤 (Dòufu Sānxian Tāng)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and healthy Tofu Three Fresh Soup.
  • Master simple cooking techniques for a flavorful broth.
  • Prepare this dish easily for family meals.

Ingredients

  • 1 block of fresh tofu (豆腐, dòufu)
  • 1/2 cup of shiitake mushrooms (平菇, pínggū)
  • 1/2 cup of shredded carrots (胡萝卜, húluóbo)
  • 2 eggs (鸡蛋, jīdàn)
  • 1 piece of ginger (生姜, shēngjiāng), minced
  • 2 stalks of cilantro (香菜, xiāngcài), chopped
  • 1 green onion (葱叶, cōngyè), chopped
  • 1 teaspoon salt (盐, yán)
  • A pinch of sugar (白糖, báitáng)
  • A pinch of pepper (胡椒粉, hújiāofěn)
  • 1 teaspoon soy sauce (生抽, shēngchōu)
  • Water (水, shuǐ)
  • 1 tablespoon cornstarch (玉米淀粉, yùmǐ diànfěn)

Instructions

  1. Blanch the tofu in boiling water to remove the beany smell. Drain and set aside.
  2. Tear the shiitake mushrooms into small pieces and rinse. Drain.
  3. Whisk two eggs in a bowl until light and frothy.
  4. Peel and dice the carrots into small pieces. (Tip: cut lengthwise, then into slices, then into thin strips, finally into small dices to prevent slipping).
  5. Mince the ginger and chop the cilantro and green onions.
  6. Cut the tofu into 0.5cm thick slices, then into strips, then into small cubes.
  7. Prepare a sauce: Mix salt, a pinch of sugar, a pinch of pepper, soy sauce, and a little water in a bowl.
  8. Prepare a cornstarch slurry: Mix cornstarch with water until smooth.
  9. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add the minced ginger and cook for 15 seconds.
  10. Add the diced carrots and cook for 15 seconds.
  11. Add the tofu and cook for about 30 seconds.
  12. Add the shiitake mushrooms and cook for 1 minute. Skim off any foam.
  13. Gradually add the cornstarch slurry, stirring constantly, until the desired consistency is reached.
  14. Turn off the heat. Slowly add the egg mixture in two additions, swirling gently to create egg ribbons.
  15. Turn the heat back on high, stir gently.
  16. Pour in the prepared sauce and stir to combine.
  17. Stir in the chopped cilantro and green onions.
  18. Turn off the heat. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=z5lBua_ovDg

tofu_with_tomatoes.txt - 西红柿炖豆腐 (Xīhóngshì dūn dòufu)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple and delicious home-style tofu dish.
  • Master the technique of pan-frying tofu until golden brown and crispy.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to complement the tofu's taste.

Ingredients

  • 2 blocks of firm tofu (老豆腐 - lǎo dòufu)
  • 2 tomatoes (西红柿 - xīhóngshì)
  • Some garlic chives (蒜苗 - suànmiáo)
  • Ginger (姜 - jiāng) - amount unspecified
  • Garlic (蒜 - suàn) - amount unspecified
  • Vegetable oil (菜籽油 - cài zǐyóu) - small amount
  • Salt (食盐 - shíyán) - to taste
  • 1 teaspoon of 松茸鲜 (sōngróng xiān) - a type of mushroom seasoning
  • Some light soy sauce (生抽 - shēng chōu) - to taste
  • Some tomato ketchup (番茄酱 - fānqié jiàng) - to taste
  • 3 tablespoons of water (水 - shuǐ)

Instructions

  1. Score the tomatoes with a cross-shaped cut. Blanch them in boiling water to easily peel the skin.
  2. Cut the tofu into thick slices and set aside.
  3. Chop the garlic chives into small segments.
  4. Peel and dice the tomatoes, removing the core.
  5. Heat a pan with a small amount of vegetable oil. Add a pinch of salt.
  6. Pan-fry the tofu slices over medium-low heat until golden brown and crispy on both sides. Do this in batches if necessary. Don't flip too early; let the tofu release its moisture first. Keep the pan moving to ensure even cooking.
  7. While the tofu is frying, sauté minced ginger and garlic in the same pan until fragrant.
  8. Add the diced tomatoes and stir-fry until they release their juices.
  9. Add 3 tablespoons of water, salt, 松茸鲜 (sōngróng xiān), light soy sauce, and tomato ketchup. Stir well.
  10. Add the fried tofu to the pan and stir to coat it evenly with the sauce.
  11. Cover the pan and simmer over low heat for 2 minutes to allow the flavors to meld.
  12. Remove the lid, increase the heat to high, and reduce the sauce.
  13. Add the chopped garlic chives and stir-fry until wilted.
  14. Turn off the heat, serve, and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Nln54O2FK-w

tomato_braised_tofu.txt - 西红柿烧豆腐

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple and delicious tomato braised tofu dish.
  • Master the technique of pan-frying tofu to achieve a golden-brown crust.
  • Understand how to balance flavors using readily available ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 2 blocks firm tofu (老豆腐)
  • 2 tomatoes (西红柿)
  • Garlic chives (蒜苗), chopped
  • Ginger (姜), minced
  • Garlic (蒜), minced
  • Vegetable oil (菜籽油)
  • Salt (食盐)
  • 1 tsp MSG (味精) (optional)
  • 3 tbsp water (清水)
  • Soy sauce (生抽)
  • Tomato sauce (番茄酱)

Instructions

  1. Score tomatoes with a cross-shaped cut, blanch in boiling water, peel, halve, remove core, and dice.
  2. Cut tofu into thick slices.
  3. Chop garlic chives into small segments.
  4. Heat oil in a pan, add a pinch of salt, and pan-fry tofu slices over medium-low heat until golden brown on both sides. Do this in batches if needed.
  5. While tofu fries, sauté minced ginger and garlic in the same pan until fragrant.
  6. Add diced tomatoes and stir-fry until they release their juices.
  7. Add 3 tablespoons of water, salt, MSG (optional), soy sauce, and tomato sauce. Stir well.
  8. Add the pan-fried tofu to the pan, ensuring it's coated with the sauce.
  9. Cover the pan and simmer over low heat for 2 minutes.
  10. Remove the lid, increase heat to high, and reduce the sauce until thickened.
  11. Add chopped garlic chives, stir-fry until wilted.
  12. Turn off the heat, transfer to a serving dish, and serve hot with rice.

tomato_cabbage_stir_fry.txt - Tomato and Cabbage Stir-fry

Objectives

  • Learn to make a nutritious and delicious tomato and cabbage stir-fry.
  • Master the simple steps to prepare this dish in minutes.
  • Understand the techniques for preparing and cooking the ingredients for optimal flavor.

Ingredients

  • 2 tomatoes
  • 1 head of cabbage
  • Several cloves garlic
  • Small piece of ginger
  • Some green onions
  • 1 tsp salt
  • Several fresh matsutake mushrooms (optional)
  • 1/2 tbsp light soy sauce
  • Small amount oyster sauce
  • Several peppercorns
  • A little pepper
  • 1 tbsp cornstarch
  • Water (amount to thin sauce)
  • 18 black beans
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Prepare the tomatoes: Score the tomatoes in a criss-cross pattern, not too deep. Place in a bowl, add boiling water, and let sit for 2 minutes to make peeling easier. Peel off the skin. Cut the tomatoes in half, remove the core, and dice into small pieces.
  2. Prepare the cabbage: Cut the cabbage in half, then into quarters, then into thicker filaments. Cut into bite-sized pieces, place in a large bowl, and wash twice with clean water to remove any dirt. Drain well.
  3. Prepare the aromatics: Mince several cloves of garlic and a small piece of ginger. Finely chop some green onions.
  4. Make the sauce: In a bowl, combine 1 tsp salt, fresh matsutake mushrooms (optional), 1/2 tbsp light soy sauce, a small amount of oyster sauce, several peppercorns, a little pepper, 1 tbsp cornstarch, and enough water to create a pourable sauce. Mix well and set aside.
  5. Stir-fry: Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan. Add peppercorns and stir-fry until fragrant. Remove peppercorns with a slotted spoon. Add 18 black beans and stir-fry briefly. Add minced garlic, ginger, and green onions, stir-fry until fragrant.
  6. Add tomatoes: Add the diced tomatoes, increase heat, and stir-fry for about a minute until the juices release.
  7. Add cabbage: Add the washed cabbage, stir-fry until the cabbage is slightly softened (about 1 minute).
  8. Add sauce: Add the prepared sauce, stir-fry until the sauce thickens.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=JBoZRg-AYHs

tomato_egg_cake.txt - 西红柿鸡蛋饼 (Xīhóngshì jīdàn bǐng)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a nutritious and delicious tomato and egg cake.
  • Create a simple, low-fat, and low-calorie breakfast or snack.
  • Encourage children to eat vegetables through a fun and tasty recipe.

Ingredients

  • 2 large tomatoes (西红柿 - xīhóngshì)
  • 2 large eggs (鸡蛋 - jīdàn)
  • 1/2 carrot (胡萝卜 - húluóbo), peeled and diced
  • 2-3 RMB worth of lean pork (瘦肉 - shòuròu), minced
  • Several scallions (小葱 - xiǎocōng), chopped
  • 1 tbsp salt (食用盐 - shíyòng yán)
  • A little pepper (胡椒粉 - hújiāofěn)
  • 1 tbsp shrimp paste (optional, 虾皮 - xiāpí)
  • 1 tbsp lettuce (optional, 生菜 - shēngcài)
  • 1 small bowl of all-purpose flour (普通面粉 - pǔtōng miànfěn)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòng yóu)
  • Black sesame seeds (黑芝麻 - hēizhīma), optional

Instructions

  1. Score the tops of two tomatoes with a cross-shaped cut.
  2. Blanch the tomatoes in boiling water to easily remove the skins.
  3. Dice the peeled tomatoes.
  4. Beat two eggs until smooth. Set aside.
  5. Dice the carrot into small pieces.
  6. Mince the lean pork.
  7. Chop the scallions.
  8. Combine the diced tomatoes, beaten eggs, minced pork, diced carrots, and chopped scallions in a large bowl.
  9. Add salt, pepper, optional shrimp paste and lettuce.
  10. Mix well to combine all ingredients.
  11. Add a small bowl of flour and stir until there are no lumps, creating a thick batter.
  12. Heat a little oil in an electric griddle.
  13. Pour spoonfuls of batter onto the hot griddle, shaping them into small round cakes.
  14. Cook for about 3 minutes per side, or until golden brown and cooked through. You may need to cook in batches.
  15. Optionally, sprinkle black sesame seeds on top for added flavor and visual appeal.
  16. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ByPsEQFeGwA

tomato_egg_pancake.txt - Tomato Egg Pancake

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple and nutritious tomato egg pancake.
  • Master a quick breakfast recipe requiring minimal ingredients and time.
  • Understand the technique of cooking the pancake to achieve a golden-brown, crispy texture.

Ingredients

  • A handful of green onions (scallions)
  • 2 tomatoes
  • 2 chicken eggs
  • 1 tsp salt
  • Pepper to taste
  • 2 tbsp plain flour

Instructions

  1. Prepare the tomatoes: Make shallow cross cuts on the tomatoes. Pour boiling water over them. This will help to easily peel off the skin.
  2. Prepare the green onions: Finely chop the white parts of the green onions and set aside.
  3. Prepare the eggs: Crack two eggs into a bowl. Add the chopped green onions.
  4. Prepare the tomatoes: Once the tomatoes are blanched, peel off the skin. Cut the tomatoes in half, remove the core, and dice into small cubes.
  5. Combine ingredients: Add the diced tomatoes to the egg mixture. Mix well with chopsticks.
  6. Season and thicken: Add salt, pepper, and plain flour to the egg and tomato mixture. Stir until well combined and the batter is slightly thick.
  7. Cook the pancakes: Heat a pan and lightly coat it with oil. Pour 3 tablespoons of batter onto the hot pan, spreading it into a thin, round pancake.
  8. Fry the pancakes: Cook over medium-low heat, allowing the bottom to set before flipping. Fry until both sides are golden brown and crispy. Repeat with remaining batter.
  9. Serve: Serve the tomato egg pancakes immediately.

tomato_egg_tofu_soup.txt - 番茄鸡蛋豆腐汤 (Fānqié jīdàn dòufu tāng)

Objectives

  • Prepare a light, nutritious, and delicious tomato, egg, and tofu soup.
  • Learn a simple method for making a flavorful and appetizing summer soup.
  • Master techniques for preparing ingredients and achieving a smooth soup texture.

Ingredients

  • 2 Tomatoes (西红柿 - Xīhóngshì)
  • Mushrooms (蘑菇 - Mógu)
  • 50g Tenderloin (里脊肉 - Lǐjǐròu)
  • 1 block Tofu (豆腐 - Dòufu)
  • 2 Eggs (鸡蛋 - Jīdàn)
  • Green Onions (葱 - Cōng)
  • Ginger (姜 - Jiāng)
  • 1 tbsp Cornstarch (玉米淀粉 - Yùmǐ diànfěn)
  • Water (水 - Shuǐ)
  • Salt (盐 - Yán)
  • Chicken Essence (鸡精 - Jījīng)
  • Pepper (胡椒粉 - Hújiāofěn)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - Shíyòngyóu)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the tomatoes: Score the tomatoes, blanch them in boiling water, peel and dice them.
  2. Prepare the mushrooms: Clean and slice the mushrooms thinly.
  3. Prepare the pork: Wash and slice the tenderloin into thin julienne strips.
  4. Prepare the tofu: Remove the packaging, cut off the corners, and slice the tofu thinly.
  5. Prepare the eggs: Crack the eggs into a bowl, whisk until well combined and light.
  6. Prepare the garnishes: Finely chop the green onions and slice the ginger thinly.
  7. Prepare the cornstarch slurry: Mix cornstarch and water in a bowl until smooth.
  8. Blanch the mushrooms and pork: Bring water to a boil, add mushrooms and blanch for 30 seconds, then add pork and blanch for 10 seconds. Remove and set aside.
  9. Sauté ginger and tomatoes: Heat oil in a pan, sauté ginger until fragrant, add tomatoes, stir, and season with salt.
  10. Simmer the soup: Add water to the pan with the tomatoes, bring to a boil. Add the blanched pork and mushrooms, stir.
  11. Season the soup: Add salt, chicken essence, and pepper. Stir and cook until seasoning is dissolved.
  12. Skim the foam: Use a spoon to remove any foam from the surface of the soup.
  13. Thicken the soup: Add the cornstarch slurry, stir gently until the soup thickens.
  14. Add tofu and eggs: Gently add the tofu slices, then slowly pour in the egg mixture, creating egg flower.
  15. Garnish and serve: Sprinkle with green onions. Turn off the heat, serve in bowls.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=BFj0-bSeJsc

tomato_sauce.txt - Homemade Tomato Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn to make a healthy, additive-free tomato sauce.
  • Understand the benefits of using fresh tomatoes.
  • Learn how to preserve homemade tomato sauce for extended use.

Ingredients

  • 3 jin (approximately 1.5 kg) fresh tomatoes
  • 1 handful of salt
  • 300g white sugar
  • 1 small spoon of salt
  • 1/2 lemon (or white vinegar as substitute)

Instructions

  1. Remove the stems from the tomatoes.
  2. Wash the tomatoes thoroughly in water with salt.
  3. Score a shallow cross at the bottom of each tomato.
  4. Blanch the tomatoes in boiling water for 2 minutes.
  5. Peel off the skins and remove the cores from the tomatoes.
  6. Cut the tomatoes into small pieces.
  7. Blend the tomatoes into a smooth puree using a high-speed blender.
  8. Strain the puree through a sieve (optional, for smoother texture).
  9. Pour the tomato puree into a pot.
  10. Add 300g of white sugar (ratio of tomatoes to sugar is 4:1).
  11. Cook over low heat, stirring frequently, until the sugar dissolves and the sauce thickens and changes color.
  12. Add a small spoon of salt and the juice of half a lemon (or white vinegar).
  13. Continue to cook for about 2 minutes.
  14. Let the sauce cool completely.
  15. Transfer the cooled sauce into clean, dry, and oil-free containers.
  16. Refrigerate for storage (lasts approximately 45 days).

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=VjtRRimf7EE

tomato_yam_balls.txt - 番茄山药小丸子 (Fānqié shānyào xiǎo wánzi)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and nutritious tomato yam balls.
  • Understand how to prepare and cook yam for optimal texture.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to complement the yam balls.

Ingredients

  • 2 鐵棍山藥 (tiěgùn shānyào) - Iron stick yam
  • 5 RMB worth of 瘦肉 (shòuròu) - lean pork
  • 2 pieces 生姜 (shēngjiāng) - ginger
  • Appropriate amount 老抽 (lǎochōu) - dark soy sauce
  • 2 西紅柿 (xīhóngshì) - tomatoes
  • Leftover 青菜 (qīngcài) - green vegetables
  • 2 large scoops 普通面粉 (pǔtōng miànfěn) - all-purpose flour
  • 少量食用油 (shǎoliàng shíyòng yóu) - a small amount of cooking oil
  • 1 scoop 食盐 (shíyán) - salt
  • 1 scoop 胡椒粉 (hújiāofěn) - pepper powder
  • 1 scoop 生抽 (shēngchōu) - light soy sauce

Instructions

  1. Wash and peel two iron stick yams. Cut them into small, long sections.
  2. Steam the yam pieces in a steamer for 15 minutes.
  3. While the yam is steaming, prepare the pork: Cut lean pork into thin slices, then mince into slightly coarse pieces.
  4. Marinate the minced pork with ginger and dark soy sauce for 10 minutes.
  5. Cut two tomatoes into slices and chop leftover green vegetables.
  6. Once the yam is cooked and slightly cooled, mash it into a puree using a rolling pin.
  7. Add two large scoops of all-purpose flour to the yam puree and knead into a smooth dough.
  8. Roll small portions of the dough into smooth balls.
  9. Heat a pan with a small amount of oil. Add the marinated minced pork and stir-fry until cooked. Remove and set aside.
  10. Add the diced tomatoes to the pan and stir-fry until softened and releasing their juices.
  11. Add an appropriate amount of water and bring to a boil.
  12. Add the yam balls to the boiling tomato sauce, gently stirring to prevent sticking.
  13. Once the yam balls are cooked, add the stir-fried pork and chopped green vegetables.
  14. Season with salt, pepper powder, and light soy sauce. Stir well.
  15. Serve immediately.

tonggu_soup.txt - Tonggu Soup (Bone Marrow Soup)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious Tonggu soup.
  • Master the techniques for preparing and cooking the bones for a rich, milky broth.
  • Understand how to achieve a flavorful soup without excessive seasonings.

Ingredients

2 large marrow bones (Tonggu) 1 tablespoon salt 2 potatoes 1 piece of yam 1 piece of ginger Some green onions 1 tablespoon cooking wine Vegetable oil or lard Water

Instructions

  1. Prepare a large basin. Add 1 tablespoon of salt and warm water, mixing until dissolved.
  2. Soak the marrow bones in the salted water for 10 minutes to draw out blood and impurities.
  3. While the bones soak, prepare the potatoes and yam: wash, peel, and cut into bite-sized pieces.
  4. Clean and chop the ginger into thicker slices and prepare the green onions.
  5. Rinse the soaked marrow bones thoroughly until the water runs clear.
  6. In a large pot, add the cleaned bones, 1 tablespoon of cooking wine, chopped ginger, and a bunch of green onions. Add enough water to cover.
  7. Bring to a boil over high heat. Skim off any foam that forms on the surface.
  8. Once boiling, reduce heat and simmer for 2 minutes to reduce purines.
  9. Remove the bones, rinse under warm water (never cold water), and set aside.
  10. Heat a tablespoon of vegetable oil or lard in the pot. Add the bones and brown them lightly on all sides over medium-low heat.
  11. Add enough boiling water to cover the bones. (Never add cold water.)
  12. Add ginger slices and green onions.
  13. Bring to a boil, then reduce heat to low, cover, and simmer for at least one hour.
  14. After one hour, check the bones. If the meat is easily removed, it's ready.
  15. Add the yam, stir, cover, and simmer for 8 minutes.
  16. Season with salt to taste.
  17. Stir in the remaining green onions before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=CagtQVrJSlk

toyo_manok.txt - Toyo Manok (Soy Sauce Chicken)

Objectives

  • Learn to cook delicious and flavorful Toyo Manok using a rice cooker.
  • Master a simple, beginner-friendly recipe perfect for Chinese New Year.
  • Understand the importance of marinating and preparing the chicken properly.

Ingredients

  • 1/2 Soy Sauce Chicken (approx. 500g)
  • 80 grams light soy sauce (薄鹽醬油, bóyán jiàngyóu)
  • 15 grams dark soy sauce (老抽, lǎochōu)
  • 1/2 purple onion (紫洋蔥, zǐ yángcōng), chopped
  • 1 piece old ginger (老薑, lǎo jiāng), sliced
  • Green onions (蔥, cōng), chopped
  • Garlic (大蒜, dàsuàn), minced
  • Toothpicks (牙籤, yáchāi)
  • Cooking oil (食用油, shíyòng yóu)

Instructions

  1. Clean the chicken thoroughly with water, removing any blood, water, and impurities, including cleaning the lungs. Pat dry.
  2. Cut the chicken into pieces. Save the offcuts.
  3. Use toothpicks to make several holes in the chicken to help it absorb the marinade.
  4. Chop green onions into long sections and ginger into slices.
  5. In a large bowl, combine the chicken with light soy sauce, dark soy sauce, chopped green onions, and ginger. Massage the chicken with the marinade for about 3 minutes.
  6. Marinate the chicken for at least 30 minutes, turning occasionally and basting with the sauce.
  7. Chop the purple onion into small pieces.
  8. Prepare the old ginger, slicing it thinly.
  9. Chop the green onions into small pieces.
  10. Heat cooking oil in a pan. Add minced garlic, then the chopped purple onions. Stir-fry until fragrant and slightly browned.
  11. Add the stir-fried garlic and onions to the rice cooker.
  12. Add the sliced ginger and chopped green onions to the rice cooker.
  13. Add the marinated chicken pieces to the rice cooker, placing the legs at the bottom, then the rest of the chicken.
  14. Pour the remaining marinade over the chicken.
  15. Close the rice cooker lid and press the normal cooking button.
  16. After the rice cooker beeps, let it steam for an additional 10 minutes.
  17. Carefully remove the chicken from the rice cooker.
  18. Pour the cooking liquid from the rice cooker over the chicken.
  19. Cut the chicken into bite-sized pieces and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=2itpCr6J6y8

tudou_dun_paigu.txt - 土豆炖排骨 (Potato Braised Pork Ribs)

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare pork ribs without boiling, preserving tenderness and nutrition.
  • Master a method for removing blood and impurities from pork ribs using salt water and flour.
  • Create a flavorful and tender braised pork rib dish with potatoes.

Ingredients

  • 1 large piece of pork ribs (about 101 RMB worth)
  • 1 small spoon of salt
  • Enough water to cover the ribs
  • 2 large spoons of flour
  • Some scallions (葱)
  • Some ginger (姜)
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜)
  • A few pieces of star anise (大料)
  • About 10 peppercorns (花椒)
  • 2 bay leaves (八角)
  • 1 peeled yellow potato (黄心土豆)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)
  • Dark soy sauce (老抽)
  • 1 spoon of braising sauce (红烧酱) or other sauces like Doubanjiang (豆瓣酱) or chili sauce (香辣酱)
  • Water (开水)

Instructions

  1. Chop the pork ribs into small pieces.
  2. Place the ribs in a bowl, add a small spoonful of salt and enough water to cover them. Mix well and let it soak for 20 minutes to draw out the blood.
  3. Remove the ribs from the saltwater and drain.
  4. Add two large spoons of flour to the ribs and mix thoroughly until sticky.
  5. Rinse the ribs with water to remove the flour, blood, and impurities. Repeat until the water runs clear. Drain.
  6. Place the ribs in a bowl. Add chopped scallions and ginger, crushing them slightly to release their juices. Mix well and marinate for 10 minutes.
  7. Prepare the aromatics: slice ginger thinly, chop scallions into rings, chop garlic roughly.
  8. Prepare the spices: crush a few star anise and about 10 peppercorns.
  9. Peel and cut the potato into small pieces. Add water to prevent browning.
  10. Heat the cooking oil in a pot until 60% hot. Add the potatoes and fry until golden brown and crispy. Remove and drain.
  11. Add the marinated ribs (remove the ginger and scallions) to the pot and stir-fry until the surface is slightly browned and the moisture is removed.
  12. Add the prepared aromatics and spices to the pot and stir-fry until fragrant.
  13. Add dark soy sauce for color and stir-fry.
  14. Add braising sauce (or substitute) and stir-fry to blend the flavors.
  15. Pour in boiling water (not cold water). Stir well, cover, and simmer over low heat for 40 minutes.
  16. Add the fried potatoes, a little salt, and stir gently. Cover and simmer for another 10 minutes.
  17. Open the lid; the ribs and potatoes should be tender.
  18. Increase heat, stir-fry to thicken the sauce.
  19. Add chopped scallions, stir-fry briefly to add aroma.
  20. Turn off the heat and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kApu2wsvyJI

tudou_jidan_bing.txt - Potato and Egg Pancakes

Objectives

  • Learn to make crispy potato and egg pancakes.
  • Master a simple, quick recipe suitable for all ages.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients for an economical dish.

Ingredients

  • 1 large potato, peeled and shredded
  • 1/2 carrot, peeled and shredded
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • 4 eggs
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • 1 tablespoon pepper salt
  • Cooking oil
  • Black sesame seeds (optional)

Instructions

  1. Peel and shred one large potato and half a carrot.
  2. Mix the shredded potato and carrot with 1 tablespoon of salt and let it sit for 10 minutes.
  3. In a separate bowl, whisk together 4 eggs, 1 tablespoon of salt, and 1 tablespoon of pepper salt.
  4. After 10 minutes, squeeze out excess water from the shredded vegetables.
  5. Add the vegetables to the egg mixture and stir until well combined and slightly stringy.
  6. Preheat an electric griddle and brush with cooking oil.
  7. Pour the batter onto the hot griddle, spreading it evenly.
  8. Sprinkle with black sesame seeds (optional).
  9. Cook for 3 minutes per side, or until golden brown and crispy.
  10. Cut into smaller pieces for serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=aQGMAhNylNk

vegetable_medley.txt - 孜然蔬菜大杂烩 (Ziran Vegetables Medley)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy vegetable medley.
  • Master a simple technique for perfectly seasoned vegetables.
  • Create a flavorful dish suitable for gatherings or everyday meals.

Ingredients

  • Broccoli (西兰花 xī lán huā)
  • Carrots (胡萝卜 hú luó bo)
  • Onion (洋葱 yáng cōng)
  • Potatoes (土豆 tǔ dòu)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 shí yòng yóu)
  • Cumin seeds (孜然粒 zī rán lì)
  • Salt (食盐 shí yán)
  • Pepper (胡椒粉 hú jiāo fěn)
  • Sugar (白糖 bái táng)
  • Cornstarch or potato starch (玉米淀粉/土豆淀粉 yù mǐ diàn fěn/tǔ dòu diàn fěn)

Instructions

  1. Peel and chop potatoes into irregular small pieces.
  2. Cut carrots into thick slices, then halve them.
  3. Cut onion into small pieces.
  4. Cut broccoli into small florets.
  5. Combine all chopped vegetables in a bowl.
  6. Add cooking oil to the vegetables and toss to coat evenly.
  7. Add cumin seeds, salt, pepper, sugar, and cornstarch/potato starch.
  8. Mix thoroughly until all ingredients are well combined and the starch is no longer visible.
  9. Heat a little oil in a flat pan and spread evenly.
  10. Add the vegetable mixture to the pan, spreading it out evenly.
  11. Cover the pan and cook over low heat for about 8 minutes.
  12. Stir the vegetables every 2 minutes to ensure even cooking.
  13. Cook until vegetables are soft and slightly browned, about 8 minutes total.
  14. Serve and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=HHWV_1NidMc

vegetarian_dumplings.txt - Vegetarian Dumplings (白菜素馅饺子)

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and soft vegetarian dumplings.
  • Master the dumpling dough and filling preparation techniques.
  • Learn a simple cooking method to prevent the dumpling wrappers from breaking.

Ingredients

  • 300 grams all-purpose flour (中筋面粉)
  • 1 teaspoon salt (盐)
  • Hot water (热水)
  • 500 grams Chinese cabbage (大白菜)
  • 1 tablespoon salt (盐)
  • Green onions (葱), chopped
  • Ginger (姜), thinly sliced
  • Carrots (胡萝卜), thinly sliced
  • Cilantro (香菜), chopped
  • 1 star anise (八角)
  • Small piece of cinnamon stick (桂皮)
  • 1 bay leaf (香叶)
  • Cooking oil (油)
  • 2 tablespoons sesame paste (芝麻酱)
  • 1 tablespoon thirteen-spice powder (十三香) or five-spice powder (五香粉)
  • 1 teaspoon pepper (胡椒粉)
  • Salt (盐)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • Sesame oil (麻油)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Dough: Add 300 grams of flour and 1 teaspoon of salt to a bowl. Gradually add hot water while mixing with chopsticks until a soft, firm dough forms. Knead until smooth and elastic. Cover with a damp cloth.

  2. Prepare the Cabbage: Chop 500 grams of Chinese cabbage. Add 1 tablespoon of salt, mix well, and set aside to drain excess moisture. After draining, squeeze out as much water as possible.

  3. Prepare the Aromatics: Finely chop green onions, ginger, and cilantro. Thinly slice carrots.

  4. Prepare the Flavor Base: Heat oil in a pan. Add star anise, cinnamon, and bay leaf. Sauté until fragrant. Add ginger, carrots, and green onions. Stir-fry until moisture evaporates. Add cilantro and continue to stir-fry until slightly browned. Remove from heat.

  5. Combine Filling: Add the stir-fried aromatics, thirteen-spice (or five-spice) powder, pepper, salt, oyster sauce, sesame oil, and sesame paste to the squeezed cabbage. Mix thoroughly.

  6. Prepare the Dumpling Wrappers: Roll out the dough into a long log. Cut into equal pieces. Roll each piece into a thin circle, thicker in the center and thinner at the edges.

  7. Assemble the Dumplings: Place a spoonful of filling in the center of each wrapper. Fold and pleat the edges to seal.

  8. Cook the Dumplings: Bring water to a boil in a pot. Add dumplings one by one. Don't stir immediately; gently shake the pot. Cook for about 30 seconds, then add a little more water. Repeat this process twice.

  9. Serve: Remove the cooked dumplings with a slotted spoon. Garnish with chopped green onions. Serve with a light soy vinegar dipping sauce (optional).

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=xr6qmWXTi4g

white_radish_balls.txt - White Radish Balls

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and nutritious white radish balls.
  • Master the technique of preparing and mixing the ingredients.
  • Understand the steaming process for perfectly cooked radish balls.

Ingredients

  • 1 large white radish
  • 1 tsp salt
  • Fresh mushrooms
  • Lean pork
  • 1 piece ginger
  • Several cloves garlic
  • Some green onions
  • Cooking oil
  • Light soy sauce
  • Oyster sauce
  • Pepper
  • 3 tbsp sweet potato starch
  • 20g water

Instructions

  1. Prepare the white radish: Peel, remove the ends, and cut into 3-4 cm sections. Slice thinly, then dice. Place in a bowl, add salt, and mix thoroughly using disposable gloves. Set aside to drain excess moisture.
  2. Prepare the mushrooms: Clean fresh mushrooms and blanch in boiling water for 2 minutes. Drain and set aside. Chop finely.
  3. Prepare the pork: Cut lean pork into small pieces, then mince finely (or use a meat grinder). Set aside.
  4. Prepare aromatics: Mince ginger and garlic. Chop green onions into small pieces, separating white and green parts.
  5. Squeeze out excess water from the salted radish.
  6. Heat cooking oil in a pan. Add minced pork and stir-fry until white. Add chopped white parts of green onions, ginger, and garlic; stir-fry until fragrant.
  7. Add chopped mushrooms and stir-fry. Add shrimp skin (optional) and stir-fry briefly.
  8. Season with light soy sauce, oyster sauce, and pepper. Stir-fry until the sauce is fragrant.
  9. Transfer the stir-fried mixture to a bowl with the squeezed radish. Add sweet potato starch and water. Mix thoroughly with disposable gloves until slightly sticky.
  10. Form small, round balls (about the size of ping-pong balls).
  11. Place the radish balls in a steamer basket, leaving space between them. Steam over high heat for 15 minutes.
  12. Serve and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Xnuea6Oyqas

white_radish_egg_soup.txt - Puting Labanos at Sabaw ng Itlog

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and warming white radish and egg soup.
  • Master the techniques for preparing the radish and other ingredients.
  • Understand how to achieve a flavorful and visually appealing soup.

Ingredients

  • 1 whole white radish (daikon), peeled, head and tail removed, thinly sliced then cut into thicker strips
  • 1/4 cup cilantro, finely chopped
  • 1/4 cup green onions, white and green parts separated and chopped
  • 1 piece ginger, thinly sliced then minced
  • 2-3 eggs
  • 1 tablespoon rapeseed oil
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • White pepper to taste
  • 1 teaspoon chicken essence (optional)
  • A handful of wolfberries (goji berries)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the white radish: Peel, remove the head and tail, thinly slice, and then cut into thicker strips. Alternatively, grate the radish if preferred. Set aside.
  2. Prepare the garnishes: Finely chop the cilantro and green onions (separate white and green parts). Mince the ginger. Set aside.
  3. Fry the eggs: Heat rapeseed oil in a pot until slightly smoky. Fry the eggs until golden brown on both sides. Set aside.
  4. Sauté aromatics: Add minced ginger and white parts of green onions to the pot. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  5. Stir-fry radish: Add the sliced white radish and stir-fry briefly to release its spiciness.
  6. Add water and simmer: Add boiling water to the pot (enough to cover the ingredients). Add the fried eggs. Bring to a boil, then cover and simmer over high heat for 8 minutes.
  7. Season the soup: After 8 minutes, uncover the pot. Adjust seasoning with salt, white pepper, and chicken essence (optional). Simmer for another 30 seconds. Remove any oil foam from the surface.
  8. Garnish and serve: Gently stir in a handful of wolfberries, chopped cilantro, and green parts of green onions. Turn off the heat. Ladle into bowls and serve warm.
