willow_leaf_pork_liver.txt - Willow Leaf Pork Liver Stir-fry

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare and clean willow leaf pork liver for optimal flavor.
  • Master a stir-fry technique for tender and flavorful pork liver.
  • Create a signature dish with a unique aroma and taste.

Ingredients

  • Willow leaf pork liver (choose pink, not dark or spotted)
  • Water
  • 1 tsp Table salt
  • Pepper
  • 1 tbsp Hunan Long brand soy sauce
  • Garlic cloves, minced
  • Garlic leaves, chopped
  • Millet peppers, chopped (or red chili peppers if you prefer less spice)
  • Ginger, minced
  • Rapeseed oil (or peanut oil)
  • Dried chili peppers
  • Matsutake mushrooms (optional)
  • Light soy sauce

Instructions

  1. Clean the Pork Liver: Cut the pork liver in half, then into willow leaf-shaped slices (or smaller pieces if your knife skills are not great). Ensure even thickness. Place in a large bowl, add water, and gently mix with your hands to remove blood clots. Rinse thoroughly until the water runs clear. Drain well.

  2. Prepare Aromatics: Mince garlic cloves and ginger. Chop garlic leaves and millet peppers (or your chosen chili).

  3. Marinate the Liver: Place the drained liver in a bowl. Add salt, pepper, and soy sauce. Mix well with disposable gloves, ensuring even coating. Marinate for 15 minutes.

  4. Stir-fry: Heat rapeseed oil in a wok or pan until slightly smoking. Add dried chili peppers and stir-fry until fragrant. Remove chilies.

  5. Cook the Liver: Add the marinated liver and stir-fry over high heat for 15 seconds (or 30 seconds if using a smaller burner).

  6. Add Aromatics: Add minced ginger and garlic, followed by millet peppers. Stir-fry until fragrant.

  7. Finish the Dish: Add the stir-fried liver back to the wok. Add matsutake mushrooms (if using) and light soy sauce. Stir-fry over high heat until the sauce thickens and the liver is cooked through and tender.

  8. Garnish and Serve: Add minced garlic leaves and stir-fry until wilted. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=RDgctDNFll8

winter_melon_meat_egg_steamed_cake.txt - Winter Melon and Meat Egg Steamed Cake

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious winter melon and meat steamed cake.
  • Master the techniques of preparing the winter melon and meat filling.
  • Understand the steaming process for optimal texture and flavor.

Ingredients

  • Winter melon (amount as needed, homegrown preferred)
  • 3 grams salt
  • Pre-soaked and washed shiitake mushrooms (amount as needed)
  • Pork fat and lean pork (amount as needed)
  • Ginger (amount as needed)
  • Green onions (amount as needed)
  • A pinch of salt
  • 1 teaspoon five-spice powder
  • Light soy sauce (amount as needed)
  • Sesame oil (amount as needed)
  • 2 tablespoons potato starch
  • Eggs (number as needed, one per cake)
  • Carrots (for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the winter melon: Peel, halve, core, and thinly slice the winter melon. Cut into small, bite-sized pieces. Add 3 grams of salt and mix well. Set aside for 10 minutes to marinate.
  2. Prepare the shiitake mushrooms: Tear and finely chop the soaked shiitake mushrooms. Set aside.
  3. Prepare the pork: Finely chop or mince the pork fat and lean pork. Do not over-process. Set aside.
  4. Prepare the ginger: Peel and finely chop the ginger. Set aside.
  5. Prepare the green onions: Finely chop the green onions. Set aside.
  6. Prepare the meat filling: In a bowl, combine the minced pork, chopped ginger, green onions, salt, five-spice powder, light soy sauce, and sesame oil. Mix well and set aside for 5 minutes to marinate.
  7. Drain the winter melon: Wrap the marinated winter melon in cheesecloth and squeeze out excess moisture.
  8. Combine the filling: Add the drained winter melon to the meat filling. Mix thoroughly. Add potato starch and mix well.
  9. Add mushrooms and winter melon: Add the chopped shiitake mushrooms and remaining winter melon pieces to the filling. Mix well.
  10. Prepare the steaming dishes: Prepare 4 small bowls.
  11. Assemble the cakes: Divide the meat filling evenly among the bowls, shaping it into a nest-like form. Crack an egg into the center of each nest.
  12. Steam the cakes: Place the bowls in a steamer with boiling water. Steam on high heat for 15 minutes.
  13. Garnish and finish steaming: Add sliced carrots for garnish. Continue steaming for another 5 minutes.
  14. Garnish and serve: Sprinkle with chopped green onions. Add a few drops of soy sauce if desired. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=KWHRvfqnywI

winter_melon_pork_rib_soup.txt - 冬瓜排骨汤

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious winter melon pork rib soup.
  • Master the techniques for preparing the pork ribs and winter melon.
  • Understand the importance of using boiling water for a milky white broth.

Ingredients

  • 1 jin 3 liang (approximately 500g) pork ribs (about ¥39)
  • 1 large piece of winter melon (about ¥0.2)
  • Some salt
  • 1 tablespoon plain flour
  • Enough water to cover the ribs
  • Ginger, sliced
  • Spring onions, chopped into segments
  • Corn (optional)
  • Carrot (optional)
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Rinse the pork ribs and remove any visible impurities.
  2. In a bowl, mix the ribs with salt, flour, and enough water to cover them. Soak for 20 minutes to remove blood and impurities.
  3. Rinse the ribs thoroughly under running water until the water runs clear. Drain.
  4. Remove any white fat from the ribs. Set aside.
  5. Prepare the winter melon: remove the seeds and cut into large chunks (about the size of a sesame ball). No need to peel.
  6. Heat some cooking oil in a large clay pot over medium heat. Add the sliced ginger and spring onions and stir-fry until fragrant.
  7. Add the pork ribs to the pot and stir-fry until the moisture is removed.
  8. Pour in plenty of boiling water, bring to a boil, then reduce heat to low, cover, and simmer for 40 minutes.
  9. Remove the ginger and spring onions.
  10. Add the winter melon chunks, corn, and carrot (if using) to the pot. Stir gently.
  11. Cover and simmer for another 18 minutes.
  12. Before serving, add chopped spring onions and salt to taste. Stir well.
  13. Serve hot.

winter_melon_pork_ribs_soup.txt - 冬瓜排骨汤

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious winter melon pork rib soup.
  • Master the techniques for preparing the pork ribs and winter melon.
  • Create a flavorful and healthy soup perfect for summer.

Ingredients

  • 1 jin 3 liang (approximately 500g) pork ribs (about ¥39)
  • Salt
  • 1 tablespoon all-purpose flour
  • Water (to cover the ribs)
  • 1 large piece of winter melon (about ¥0.2)
  • Ginger
  • Scallions
  • Corn (optional)
  • Carrot (optional)
  • Cooking oil
  • Some scallions for garnish

Instructions

  1. Rinse the pork ribs and remove any excess blood.
  2. In a bowl, mix the pork ribs with salt, flour, and enough water to fully submerge them. Let it soak for 20 minutes to remove blood and impurities.
  3. Rinse the soaked pork ribs thoroughly under running water until the water runs clear.
  4. Remove any visible white fat from the ribs.
  5. Prepare the winter melon: remove the seeds and cut into large chunks (similar in size to a sesame ball). No need to peel.
  6. Prepare the ginger and scallions: slice the ginger thickly and cut the scallions into segments.
  7. Heat a small amount of cooking oil in a large sand pot. Add the ginger and scallions and stir-fry until fragrant.
  8. Add the pork ribs to the pot and stir-fry to remove excess moisture.
  9. Pour in plenty of boiling water, bring to a boil, then reduce heat to low, cover, and simmer for 40 minutes.
  10. Remove the ginger and scallions from the pot.
  11. Add the winter melon, corn, and carrots (if using) to the pot. Stir gently.
  12. Cover and simmer for another 18 minutes.
  13. Garnish with chopped scallions and add salt to taste. No other seasonings are needed.
  14. Stir and serve.

winter_melon_shrimp.txt - Winter Melon and Shrimp

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare winter melon and shrimp in a Cantonese-style dish.
  • Master the techniques for cleaning and prepping shrimp for optimal taste and texture.
  • Create a light, flavorful, and visually appealing dish suitable for all ages.

Ingredients

  • 1 piece winter melon
  • 1/2 lb shrimp
  • A handful of green onions (separate white and green parts)
  • Ginger (amount unspecified)
  • 1 tsp salt
  • Pepper (amount unspecified)
  • 1/2 egg white
  • Cooking wine (amount unspecified)
  • 1 tbsp cornstarch
  • Cooking oil
  • Water or broth (amount unspecified)
  • Sesame oil (a few drops)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the winter melon: Remove the seeds, peel, wash, slice, and cut into diamond shapes. Set aside.
  2. Prepare the shrimp: Clean, devein, and peel the shrimp. Rinse and pat dry. Marinate shrimp with salt, pepper, half an egg white, cooking wine, and cornstarch for 5 minutes.
  3. Blanch the winter melon: Boil water, add winter melon slices, and cook for 2 minutes. Continue boiling for another 3 minutes until tender and translucent. Remove with a slotted spoon.
  4. Stir-fry shrimp: Heat oil in a wok or pan. Add shrimp and stir-fry over medium-low heat until cooked through. Remove and set aside.
  5. Prepare the sauce: Add more oil to the pan. Add chopped green onions and ginger, stir-fry until fragrant. Add cooking wine and broth (or water).
  6. Combine ingredients: Add the blanched winter melon to the sauce and stir-fry evenly. Season with salt.
  7. Add shrimp: Add the cooked shrimp to the pan and stir-fry for 1 minute over high heat.
  8. Thicken sauce: Stir until the sauce thickens. Add remaining green onions.
  9. Finish: Drizzle with sesame oil. Stir well.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LIA5NyKLKdI

xianggu_chao.txt - 素炒香菇 (Sù chǎo xiānggū)

Objectives

  • Learn to clean and prepare fresh shiitake mushrooms for optimal flavor.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful stir-fry technique for shiitake mushrooms.
  • Enhance the taste and texture of shiitake mushrooms through specific cooking steps.

Ingredients

  • 1 jin (approximately 500g) fresh shiitake mushrooms (香菇 xiānggū)
  • Salt (盐 yán)
  • Flour (面粉 miànfěn)
  • Water (清水 qīngshuǐ)
  • White sugar (白糖 báitáng)
  • Garlic (蒜 suàn)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 shíyòngyóu)
  • Soy sauce (生抽 shēngchōu)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油 háoyóu)

Instructions

  1. Remove the stems from the shiitake mushrooms using scissors. Select mushrooms with thick flesh.
  2. Clean the mushrooms: Add salt and flour to the mushrooms, add a little water and soak for 1-2 minutes. Rinse thoroughly under running water to remove dirt and impurities.
  3. Blanch the mushrooms: Add a handful of white sugar to the cleaned mushrooms and pour boiling water (101°C) over them. Let them sit for 1-2 minutes to remove any off-flavors. Drain and squeeze out excess water.
  4. Cut the mushrooms: Cut the mushrooms into small pieces.
  5. Prepare the garlic: Mince a generous amount of garlic.
  6. Stir-fry the garlic: Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan. Add the minced garlic and stir-fry over low heat until fragrant.
  7. Season the garlic: Add a small amount of salt, white sugar, soy sauce, and oyster sauce to the garlic. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  8. Stir-fry the mushrooms: Add the prepared shiitake mushrooms to the pan and stir-fry quickly until the mushrooms release their moisture. You can cover the pan to steam for 1-2 minutes.
  9. Add a thickening agent (optional): Add a thickening agent (the transcript mentions "glass芡," likely a starch-based sauce) to coat the mushrooms. Stir-fry for about 30 seconds.
  10. Serve: Turn off the heat and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Y3dKI5ZEH7k

xianggu_dunji.txt - 香菇炖鸡 (Xiānggū dūn jī) - Stewed Chicken with Mushrooms

Objectives

  • Learn to make tender, flavorful stewed chicken without tough or gamey texture.
  • Master a method for cleaning chicken to remove blood and impurities.
  • Create a rich and savory sauce to enhance the chicken's flavor.

Ingredients

  • 1/2 a free-range chicken (丈母娘家养的走地鸡 - zhàngmǔniáng jiā yǎng de zǒudì jī), cut into large pieces
  • 1 tablespoon flour (面粉 - miànfěn)
  • Water (清水 - qīngshuǐ)
  • Several dried shiitake mushrooms (干香菇 - gān xiānggū)
  • Several cloves garlic (大蒜 - dàsuàn), minced
  • 1 small piece ginger (生姜 - shēngjiāng), minced
  • A few peppercorns (花椒 - huājiāo)
  • Several dried chilies (干海椒 - gān háijiāo)
  • 1 large red chili pepper (大红椒 - dà hóngjiāo), seeded and chopped
  • 2 green chili peppers (青椒 - qīngjiāo), seeded and chopped
  • A small handful of scallions (小葱 - xiǎocōng), chopped
  • 1/2 teaspoon salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • A little pepper (胡椒粉 - hújiāofěn)
  • 1 tablespoon soy sauce (生抽 - shēngchōu)
  • A little dark soy sauce (老抽 - lǎochōu)
  • 1 tablespoon cooking wine (料酒 - liàojiǔ)
  • 1 tablespoon yellow soybean paste (黄豆酱 - huángdòujiàng)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòngyóu)

Instructions

  1. Cut the chicken into large pieces.
  2. Place the chicken in a bowl, add flour and a little water. Mix for one minute to remove blood and impurities.
  3. Rinse the chicken thoroughly with water until the water runs clear. Drain.
  4. Soak dried shiitake mushrooms in warm water. Once softened, rinse and squeeze out excess water.
  5. Mince garlic and ginger. Chop chilies and scallions.
  6. In a bowl, mix salt, pepper, soy sauce (light and dark), cooking wine, and yellow soybean paste. Set aside.
  7. Heat oil in a pan or wok. Add ginger, garlic, dried chilies, and peppercorns. Sauté until fragrant.
  8. Add the chicken and stir-fry over high heat until the chicken is browned and most of the moisture is removed.
  9. Add the prepared sauce and stir-fry until the chicken is coated and fragrant.
  10. Add the shiitake mushrooms and stir-fry for about one minute.
  11. Add enough boiling water to cover the chicken. Do not use cold water.
  12. Cover and simmer over low heat for 15 minutes.
  13. Remove the lid and increase heat to high. Reduce the sauce until thickened.
  14. Add the chopped red and green chilies and stir-fry until tender.
  15. Stir in the chopped scallions.
  16. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=N9j8sJ4CsEQ

xianggu_shaorobo.txt - 香菇烧萝卜 (Xiānggū shāo luóbo)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy 香菇烧萝卜 (Xiānggū shāo luóbo) dish.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients for a simple yet flavorful meal.
  • Master basic cooking techniques like blanching, sautéing, and braising.

Ingredients

  • Dried shiitake mushrooms (干香菇 - gānxīanggū): amount unspecified, but enough to complement the amount of radish used.
  • White radish (白萝卜 - báiluóbo): 2 large
  • White sugar (白糖 - báitáng): a small amount for soaking mushrooms
  • Small onion (小葱 - xiǎocōng): amount unspecified, for garnish
  • Ginger (生姜 - shēngjiāng): a piece, for flavoring
  • Garlic (蒜 - suàn): several cloves, for flavoring
  • Salt (盐 - yán): to taste
  • Light soy sauce (生抽 - shēngchōu): 1 tablespoon
  • Dark soy sauce (老抽 - lǎochōu): a small amount, for color
  • MSG (味精 - wèijīng): a small amount (optional)
  • Water (清水 - qīngshuǐ): amount unspecified, for boiling and braising
  • Water starch (水淀粉 - shuǐdiànfěn): a small amount, for thickening the sauce

Instructions

  1. Soak dried shiitake mushrooms in warm water (around 40°C) with a little sugar for about 10 minutes. Reserve the soaking liquid.
  2. Wash and peel two large white radishes. Cut them into large chunks.
  3. Prepare the aromatics: finely chop small onions, ginger, and garlic.
  4. Blanch the radish chunks in boiling water with a spoonful of salt for 2-3 minutes until translucent. Drain well.
  5. Heat oil in a pan or wok over medium-high heat. Sauté the radish until lightly browned.
  6. Add the chopped aromatics (onion, ginger, garlic) and stir-fry until fragrant.
  7. Add the soaked shiitake mushrooms and their soaking liquid to the pan. Stir well to combine.
  8. Season with light soy sauce, a little salt, MSG (optional), and a small amount of dark soy sauce for color.
  9. Cover and simmer for 5-8 minutes.
  10. Increase heat to high and reduce the sauce until thickened.
  11. Thicken the sauce further by adding a little water starch slurry.
  12. Garnish with chopped green onions.
  13. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=m025rxXHQe4

xiang_jian_doufu.txt - 香煎豆腐 (Fragrant Pan-fried Tofu)

Objectives

  • Learn to pan-fry tofu without breaking or sticking.
  • Create flavorful pan-fried tofu with a crispy exterior.
  • Prepare a simple and delicious tofu dish with readily available ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 200g 嫩豆腐 (nèn dòufu) - soft tofu
  • 2 青椒 (qīngjiāo) - green peppers
  • Several 小米椒 (xiǎomǐjiāo) - small chili peppers (optional)
  • Several 蒜 (suàn) - garlic cloves
  • 2-3 slices 五花肉 (wǔhuāròu) - pork belly
  • 2-3 slices 瘦肉 (shòuròu) - lean pork
  • Some 大葱 (dàcōng) - scallions
  • Cooking oil
  • Salt
  • 老抽 (lǎochōu) - dark soy sauce
  • 生抽 (shēngchōu) - light soy sauce
  • 蚝油 (háoyóu) - oyster sauce
  • Water

Instructions

  1. Cut the soft tofu into rectangular pieces.
  2. Cut green peppers into small pieces.
  3. Cut small chili peppers into small rings (optional).
  4. Mince the garlic.
  5. Slice pork belly and lean pork thinly.
  6. Slice scallions into thicker pieces.
  7. Heat a pan and add a small amount of oil. Swirl to coat. Pour out excess oil.
  8. Add a little salt to the hot pan.
  9. Add tofu pieces to the pan, and fry over high heat until golden brown and crispy on both sides (about 2 minutes per side), ensuring they are able to slide freely in the pan.
  10. Remove the tofu and set aside.
  11. Add pork belly to the same pan and fry until crispy.
  12. Add lean pork, garlic, and chili peppers (if using) and stir-fry until fragrant.
  13. Add a little dark soy sauce to color the meat.
  14. Add the fried tofu back to the pan.
  15. Season with light soy sauce and oyster sauce.
  16. Add a small bowl of water, ensuring the tofu is submerged in the liquid.
  17. Simmer for 3 minutes to allow the tofu to absorb the flavors.
  18. Add scallions and stir-fry until wilted.
  19. Serve immediately.

xiang_jian_tudou_bing.txt - 香煎土豆饼 (Xiāngjiān Tǔdòubǐng) - Fragrant Fried Potato Cake

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and visually appealing fragrant fried potato cake.
  • Master the technique of thinly slicing potatoes and removing excess starch.
  • Understand the importance of low and slow cooking for crispy texture.

Ingredients

  • 1 large yellow potato (about 1 jin/500g)
  • 3 eggs
  • 1 small red chili pepper
  • 1 small green chili pepper
  • 1 piece of scallion (葱) (cōng)
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜) (suàn)
  • Cooking oil
  • Salt (盐) (yán)
  • Five-spice powder (五香粉) (wǔxiāngfěn)
  • Sesame oil (小磨香油) (xiǎo mó xiāngyóu)

Instructions

  1. Peel and wash the potato, then thinly slice it. Cut the slices into thin strips. Rinse the potato strips in water to remove excess starch, drain, and set aside for 5 minutes.
  2. Prepare the chili peppers: remove stems, slice in half, then cut into diamond shapes. Mince the scallions and garlic.
  3. Blanch the potato strips in boiling water for 49 seconds until 70% cooked. Immediately remove, rinse with cold water, and drain thoroughly (squeeze out excess water).
  4. In a bowl, whisk 3 eggs until light and frothy.
  5. Add the potato strips to the egg mixture along with a small spoonful of salt and five-spice powder. Mix well to coat the potato strips evenly.
  6. Heat a little oil in a non-stick pan. Add the potato and egg mixture, spreading it into a flat pancake shape.
  7. Cook over medium-low heat for 2 minutes per side, or until golden brown and crispy. Gently move the pan to prevent burning.
  8. Once cooked, transfer the potato cake to a cutting board and cut into smaller pieces.
  9. Heat a little oil in the pan, add minced garlic and scallions, and sauté until fragrant.
  10. Add the chili peppers and sauté until slightly softened. Add a pinch of salt.
  11. Add the cut potato cakes to the pan and toss gently to combine with the chili and garlic mixture.
  12. Drizzle with sesame oil and stir-fry until fragrant.
  13. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=g_ppQBYHweY

xiao_chao_fu_zhu.txt - 小炒腐竹 (Little Stir-fried Dried Tofu)

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare delicious and easy home-style stir-fried dried tofu.
  • Master the techniques for achieving the perfect texture and flavor in this dish.
  • Understand the importance of ingredient selection and preparation.

Ingredients

  • 适量 (sufficient amount) Dried Tofu (腐竹 - fǔ zhú), pre-soaked
  • Several Fresh Shiitake Mushrooms (鲜香菇 - xiān xiānggū)
  • 2 RMB worth of Pork Belly (五花肉 - wǔ huā ròu)
  • 2 Green Bell Peppers (青椒 - qīng jiāo)
  • Several Garlic Cloves (蒜 - suàn)
  • Ginger (姜 - jiāng)
  • Several Small Chili Peppers (小米椒 - xiǎo mǐ jiāo)
  • 2 Scallions (蒜苗 - suàn miáo)
  • 1 tbsp Yellow Soybean Paste (黄豆酱 - huáng dòu jiàng)
  • Salt (食盐 - shí yán)
  • 1 tsp Chopped Green Onions (葱蓉 - cōng róng)
  • Light Soy Sauce (鲜生抽 - xiān shēng chōu)
  • Oyster Sauce (蚝油 - háo yóu)
  • 1 tsp Potato Starch (土豆淀粉 - tǔ dòu diàn fěn)
  • Water (清水 - qīng shuǐ)
  • Cooking Oil (食用油 - shí yòng yóu)

Instructions

  1. Pre-soak dried tofu until fully expanded. Select dry, yellowish dried tofu for best results.
  2. Cut the soaked dried tofu into bite-sized pieces.
  3. Slice shiitake mushrooms into thick pieces.
  4. Cut pork belly into strips.
  5. Remove stems and seeds from green bell peppers; slice into thin strips.
  6. Slice garlic cloves.
  7. Cut ginger into coarse, then fine shreds.
  8. Slice small chili peppers into thin rings.
  9. Slice scallions diagonally.
  10. Prepare the sauce: Combine yellow soybean paste, salt, chopped green onions, light soy sauce, oyster sauce, potato starch, and water; mix well.
  11. Boil water in a pot. Add dried tofu and blanch for 3 minutes.
  12. Add shiitake mushrooms and blanch for 30 seconds. Remove both and drain.
  13. Heat oil in a wok or pan. Add pork belly and stir-fry until golden brown and excess fat is rendered.
  14. Add ginger, garlic, and chili peppers; stir-fry until fragrant.
  15. Add blanched dried tofu and stir-fry over high heat for about 1 minute to remove excess moisture.
  16. Add green bell peppers and stir-fry until combined.
  17. Pour in the prepared sauce and stir-fry until all ingredients are coated.
  18. Add scallions and stir-fry briefly.
  19. Remove from heat and serve.

xiaochao_fuzhu.txt - 小炒腐竹 (Small Stir-fried Dried Tofu)

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare delicious and easy small stir-fried dried tofu.
  • Master the techniques for achieving optimal texture and flavor in this dish.
  • Understand the importance of ingredient selection and preparation.

Ingredients

  • 適量 dried tofu (腐竹), soaked for at least one morning
  • 幾個 fresh shiitake mushrooms (鲜香菇)
  • 2 yuan worth of five-spice pork belly (五花肉)
  • 2 green bell peppers (青椒)
  • several garlic cloves (蒜子)
  • some ginger (姜)
  • several small chili peppers (小米椒)
  • 2 scallions (蒜苗)
  • 1 tbsp yellow soybean paste (黄豆酱)
  • a little salt (食盐)
  • 1 tsp chopped scallions (葱蓉)
  • some fresh light soy sauce (鲜生抽)
  • some oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • 1 tsp potato starch (土豆淀粉)
  • appropriate amount of water (清水)
  • cooking oil (食用油)

Instructions

  1. Soak dried tofu for at least one morning until fully expanded. Select dry, yellowish dried tofu for best results.
  2. Cut soaked dried tofu into bite-sized pieces.
  3. Cut fresh shiitake mushrooms into thick slices.
  4. Cut five-spice pork belly into strips.
  5. Remove stems and seeds from green bell peppers; cut into thin strips.
  6. Slice garlic cloves.
  7. Cut ginger into thick, then thin shreds, and finally mince.
  8. Remove stems from small chili peppers and cut into thin rings.
  9. Cut scallions into diagonal slices.
  10. Prepare sauce: In a bowl, combine yellow soybean paste, salt, chopped scallions, fresh light soy sauce, oyster sauce, potato starch, and water. Mix well until starch is dissolved.
  11. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add dried tofu and blanch for 3 minutes.
  12. Add shiitake mushrooms and blanch for 30 seconds. Remove both and set aside.
  13. Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan. Add five-spice pork belly and stir-fry until golden brown and excess fat is rendered.
  14. Add ginger, garlic, and small chili peppers; stir-fry until fragrant.
  15. Add blanched dried tofu and stir-fry over high heat for about 1 minute to remove excess moisture.
  16. Add green bell peppers and stir-fry until combined.
  17. Pour in prepared sauce and stir-fry until all ingredients are coated and flavors are well combined (about 49 seconds).
  18. Add scallions and stir-fry briefly.
  19. Remove from heat and serve.

xiaochao_niurou.txt - 小炒牛肉 (Small Fried Beef)

Objectives

  • Learn to cut beef against the grain for optimal tenderness.
  • Master a simple yet effective method for marinating beef to remove odor and enhance flavor.
  • Understand the correct order of adding marinating ingredients to ensure a tender and flavorful result.

Ingredients

  • 500g beef (front leg or tenderloin)
  • Several scallions (葱, cōng)
  • 1 piece ginger (姜, jiāng)
  • A small handful of peppercorns (花椒, huājiāo)
  • Appropriate amount of warm water
  • 30g oyster sauce (蚝油, háoyóu)
  • Appropriate amount of dark soy sauce (老抽, lǎochōu)
  • Salt (盐, yán)
  • 1 egg white (蛋清, dànqīng)
  • 1-2 tablespoons potato starch or cornstarch (土豆淀粉/玉米淀粉, tǔdòu diànfěn/yùmǐ diànfěn) or sweet potato starch (红薯淀粉, hóngshǔ diànfěn)
  • Cooking oil (食用油, shíyòng yóu)

Instructions

  1. Cut the beef against the grain into thin slices. The beef should be slightly sticky to the touch, indicating freshness.
  2. Prepare the scallion-ginger water: finely chop scallions and ginger, add peppercorns to a bowl, and pour in warm water. Gently mix to release the juices.
  3. Marinate the beef in the scallion-ginger water for 10 minutes to remove any odor and enhance the flavor.
  4. Add oyster sauce and dark soy sauce to the marinated beef. Do not add yellow wine (黄酒) as it can cause the beef to spoil faster.
  5. Add salt and gently mix the beef clockwise to allow it to absorb the marinade fully.
  6. After about 1-2 minutes, add the egg white and continue mixing until fully incorporated.
  7. Add the starch (potato, corn, or sweet potato) and mix thoroughly.
  8. Add a small amount of cooking oil to lock in moisture.
  9. Refrigerate the marinated beef until ready to cook. It can be steamed, stir-fried, or braised.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=E3T98jPm9N4

xiaochaoniurou.txt - 小炒牛肉 (Small Fried Beef)

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare tender and flavorful beef for stir-fry.
  • Master the correct method for marinating beef to remove odor and enhance taste.
  • Understand the importance of ingredient order and technique in beef preparation.

Ingredients

  • 500g beef (front leg or tenderloin)
  • Several scallions (small pieces)
  • 1 piece ginger (thinly sliced then shredded)
  • A small handful of peppercorns
  • Appropriate amount of warm water
  • Oyster sauce
  • Soy sauce (dark)
  • Salt
  • 1 egg white
  • Potato starch or cornstarch (or sweet potato starch)
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Slice the beef thinly against the grain. The fresher the beef (slightly sticky), the better.
  2. Prepare the scallion-ginger water: Combine chopped scallions, ginger, peppercorns, and warm water in a bowl. Mix well to release the juices.
  3. Marinate the beef in the scallion-ginger water for 10 minutes to remove odor and enhance flavor.
  4. Add oyster sauce and soy sauce to the marinated beef. Do not add yellow rice wine.
  5. Add about 30g of the scallion-ginger water to the beef (for 500g beef).
  6. Gently and patiently mix the beef with the marinade in a clockwise direction, adding salt to help the beef absorb the water.
  7. After about 1-2 minutes, add the egg white (reserve the yolk for other uses) and continue mixing.
  8. Once the egg white is fully incorporated, add the starch (potato, corn, or sweet potato starch). Mix well.
  9. Add cooking oil to seal in moisture.
  10. Refrigerate the marinated beef until ready to use. It can be used for stir-frying, steaming, or braising.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=E3T98jPm9N4

xiaocha_xizhu.txt - Stir-fried Zucchini

Objectives

  • Learn a simple and delicious method for stir-frying zucchini.
  • Achieve a tender-crisp texture in the zucchini.
  • Enhance the flavor of zucchini with complementary ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 2 zucchini (西葫芦 xīhúlú)
  • 1 small handful of enoki mushrooms (平菇 pínggū)
  • 1 small carrot (胡萝卜 húluóbo)
  • 1 small bunch of scallions (葱 cōng)
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜 suàn)
  • 2 eggs (土鸡蛋 tǔjǐdàn)
  • Salt (盐 yán)
  • MSG (味精 wèijīng - optional)
  • Soy sauce (生抽 shēngchōu)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油 háoyóu)
  • Rice vinegar (陈醋 chéncù)
  • Potato starch (土豆淀粉 tǔdòu diànfěn)
  • Water (清水 qīngshuǐ)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 shíyòngyóu)
  • White sugar (白糖 báitáng)

Instructions

  1. Wash and slice two zucchini into coin-sized slices. Marinate with a small spoonful of salt for 10 minutes.
  2. Clean and slice enoki mushrooms into small pieces.
  3. Peel, wash, and cut a small carrot into diamond-shaped pieces.
  4. Chop scallions (separate white and green parts).
  5. Mince garlic.
  6. Whisk two eggs until light and fluffy.
  7. Prepare sauce: Mix a small spoonful of salt, a small spoonful of MSG (optional), a small spoonful of soy sauce, a dash of oyster sauce, a dash of rice vinegar, a little potato starch, and enough water to create a smooth sauce.
  8. Rinse the marinated zucchini to remove excess salt. Drain well.
  9. Blanch the enoki mushrooms in boiling water with a small spoonful of sugar for 30 seconds to remove any odor. Drain.
  10. Heat oil in a wok or pan. Add the egg and scramble until cooked through. Remove and set aside.
  11. Add a little more oil to the pan, add garlic and scallion whites, and sauté until fragrant.
  12. Add the carrots and stir-fry for about 1 minute.
  13. Add the zucchini and stir-fry until slightly softened.
  14. Add the blanched enoki mushrooms and scrambled eggs. Stir-fry until well combined.
  15. Pour in the prepared sauce and stir-fry until the sauce thickens and coats the vegetables.
  16. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=rbiVHzYNEwk

xiaosu_rou.txt - 小酥肉 (Xiǎo sū ròu) - Crispy Pork

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious, crispy pork (小酥肉).
  • Achieve a non-greasy, tender texture.
  • Master the technique of double-frying for optimal crispiness.
  • Understand the importance of marinating the pork.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients.
  • Create a visually appealing dish.
  • Learn to make a flavorful crispy batter.

Ingredients

  • Pork (梅花肉/里脊肉 or 排骨肉 - Meihua rou/Lǐjǐ ròu or Paigǔ ròu - pork shoulder/tenderloin or spareribs): amount unspecified, cut into small, even strips.
  • Ginger (生姜 - shēng jiāng): 1 piece, peeled, thinly sliced then shredded.
  • Garlic (蒜 - suàn): several cloves, smashed and minced.
  • Salt (食盐 - shíyán): amount unspecified.
  • Pepper (胡椒粉 - hújiāo fěn): amount unspecified.
  • Thirteen Spices (十三香 - shísānxīang): amount unspecified.
  • Light Soy Sauce (生抽 - shēng chōu): amount unspecified.
  • Fennel (茴香 - huíxiāng): several stalks, washed and finely chopped.
  • Eggs (鸡蛋 - jīdàn): 2
  • Crispy Pork Powder (小酥肉粉 - xiǎo sū ròu fěn): 50g
  • Water (清水 - qīngshuǐ): a little, added gradually.
  • Vegetable Oil (植物油 - zhíwùyóu): amount unspecified, for batter and frying.
  • Tomato Ketchup (番茄酱 - fānqié jiàng): for dipping (optional).

Instructions

  1. Cut the pork into thin, even strips.
  2. In a large bowl, combine the pork with shredded ginger, minced garlic, salt, pepper, thirteen spices, and light soy sauce. Mix thoroughly to marinate for 10 minutes.
  3. Finely chop the fennel.
  4. Prepare the crispy batter: In a bowl, whisk together eggs, crispy pork powder, and a little water until a yogurt-like consistency is achieved. Add a small amount of vegetable oil and mix well.
  5. Remove the ginger from the marinated pork.
  6. Add the crispy batter and chopped fennel to the marinated pork. Mix until each pork strip is evenly coated.
  7. Heat a generous amount of vegetable oil in a wok or deep pan to medium heat (four to five parts hot).
  8. Add the coated pork strips, spreading them out to prevent sticking. Fry for 30 seconds to set the batter.
  9. Stir the pork frequently to ensure even cooking and prevent sticking.
  10. Continue frying until the pork is golden brown. Remove and drain on a wire rack or paper towels.
  11. Increase the oil temperature to high heat (seven to eight parts hot).
  12. Return the pork to the oil and fry for 40-50 seconds to crisp the exterior and render excess fat.
  13. Remove the pork, drain, and serve. Enjoy with tomato ketchup, if desired.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=-VDrgZ_exJQ

xizhulu_cha.txt - Stir-fried Zucchini

Objectives

  • Learn a simple and delicious way to stir-fry zucchini.
  • Achieve a tender-crisp texture in the zucchini.
  • Maximize the flavor and nutritional value of the dish.

Ingredients

  • 2 fresh zucchini (西葫芦 xīhúlú)
  • 1 small teaspoon of salt (盐 yán)
  • 1 small amount of oyster sauce (蚝油 háoyóu)
  • 1 small amount of rice vinegar (陈醋 chéncù)
  • 1 small amount of potato starch (土豆淀粉 tǔdòu diànfěn)
  • 1 small amount of soy sauce (生抽 shēngchōu)
  • 1 small amount of MSG (味精 wèijīng)
  • Some mushrooms (平菇 pínggū)
  • 1 small carrot (胡萝卜 húluóbo)
  • Small handful of scallions (葱 cōng)
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜 suàn)
  • 2 eggs (土鸡蛋 tǔjǐdàn)
  • Appropriate amount of water (水 shuǐ)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 shíyòngyóu)
  • White sugar (白糖 báitáng)

Instructions

  1. Wash and cut two fresh zucchini into slices about the thickness of a coin. Place in a bowl, add a small spoonful of salt, mix well, and marinate for 10 minutes.
  2. Clean and slice mushrooms into small pieces.
  3. Peel and dice a small carrot into diamond shapes.
  4. Chop scallions (separate white and green parts).
  5. Mince several cloves of garlic.
  6. Whisk two eggs in a bowl until the whites and yolks are fully combined.
  7. Prepare a sauce: In a bowl, mix a small spoonful of salt, a small spoonful of MSG, a small spoonful of soy sauce, a tiny bit of oyster sauce, a tiny bit of rice vinegar, a little potato starch, and enough water to make a smooth sauce. Set aside.
  8. Rinse the marinated zucchini to remove excess salt and drain.
  9. Boil water in a pot. Add a small spoonful of sugar and the mushrooms. Blanch for 30 seconds to remove any peculiar smell, then remove and drain.
  10. Heat oil in a wok or pan. Add the egg mixture and scramble until cooked through, then remove and set aside.
  11. Add a little more oil to the pan, add the garlic and scallion whites, and sauté until fragrant.
  12. Add the carrots and stir-fry for about 1 minute.
  13. Add the zucchini and stir-fry until slightly softened.
  14. Add the blanched mushrooms and the scrambled eggs. Stir-fry until well combined.
  15. Pour in the prepared sauce and stir-fry until the sauce thickens and coats the vegetables.
  16. Turn off the heat and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=rbiVHzYNEwk

yam_balls_sweet_red_date_soup.txt - Yam Balls in Sweet Red Date Soup

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious yam balls in a sweet red date soup.
  • Master the techniques for preparing yam and red dates.
  • Create a comforting and nutritious autumn/winter dessert.

Ingredients

  • Yam (quantity unspecified)
  • Red dates (quantity unspecified)
  • 1 tsp flour
  • 150g glutinous rice flour
  • Brown sugar (quantity unspecified)
  • Mountain spring water (quantity unspecified)
  • Water (quantity unspecified, for boiling and cooking)
  • Optional: Homemade sweet wine

Instructions

  1. Prepare the yams: Clean, peel, and cut into small pieces. Steam for 15 minutes.
  2. Prepare the red dates: Add 1 tsp flour to the red dates, wash thoroughly to remove impurities. Cut and remove pits, set aside.
  3. Mash the steamed yams: Use a meat grinder to create a smooth yam puree.
  4. Make the yam dough: Combine the yam puree with 150g glutinous rice flour. Mix until a smooth, firm dough forms.
  5. Shape the yam balls: Roll small portions of dough into small balls, similar to glutinous rice balls.
  6. Prepare the sweet red date soup: In a pot, combine brown sugar and mountain spring water. Bring to a boil.
  7. Cook the yam balls: In a separate pot, bring water to a boil. Add yam balls gently; do not stir immediately. Cook until they float. Add cold water and cook for 2 more minutes.
  8. Combine and simmer: Add the cooked yam balls to the sweet red date soup. Add sliced red dates and simmer.
  9. Add optional ingredients: Add homemade sweet wine for extra flavor (optional). Simmer for 1 minute.
  10. Serve: Remove the yam balls with a slotted spoon and serve in the sweet red date soup.

yam_balls_sweet_red_dates_soup.txt - Yam Balls with Sweet Red Dates Soup

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious yam balls with a sweet red date soup.
  • Master the technique of preparing yam for a smooth, delicate texture.
  • Create a visually appealing and flavorful dessert suitable for all ages.

Ingredients

  • Yam (quantity not specified)
  • Sweet red dates (quantity not specified)
  • Flour (1 tsp for washing red dates)
  • 150g glutinous rice flour
  • Brown sugar (2 pieces)
  • Mountain spring water (quantity not specified)
  • Milk (quantity not specified)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the yams: Clean, peel, and cut into small pieces. Steam for 15 minutes.
  2. Prepare the sweet red dates: Add 1 tsp flour, water, and scrub to remove dirt. Rinse thoroughly.
  3. Remove the pits from the sweet red dates and chop them. Set aside.
  4. Drain the steamed yams and puree them using a meat grinder.
  5. Mix the yam puree with 150g glutinous rice flour, kneading until smooth and firm.
  6. Form small balls from the yam dough. Set aside.
  7. Prepare the sweet red date soup: In a pot, combine brown sugar and mountain spring water. Bring to a boil.
  8. In a separate pot, boil milk and water.
  9. Once boiling, add the yam balls gently. Do not stir vigorously.
  10. Cover and cook until the yam balls float.
  11. Add cold water and cook for another 2 minutes.
  12. Remove the yam balls with a slotted spoon and add them to the sweet red date soup.
  13. Add the chopped sweet red dates to the soup.
  14. Add homemade sweet wine (optional).
  15. Stir well, cover, and cook for 1 minute.
  16. Serve hot.

yam_pork_soup.txt - Yam and Pork Soup

Objectives

  • Prepare a nutritious and delicious yam and pork soup.
  • Learn to tenderize pork slices for optimal flavor.
  • Master the art of stir-frying yam slices for a crispy texture.

Ingredients

  • Fresh pork (leg or rib preferred), cut into thin slices
  • Yam, peeled and thinly sliced (about 1cm thick)
  • Pickled mustard greens, thinly sliced
  • Ginger, thinly sliced
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Cornstarch
  • Water
  • Peanut oil
  • Chicken bouillon
  • Light soy sauce
  • Chopped green onions

Instructions

  1. Cut the pork into evenly sized pieces, then slice thinly.
  2. Marinate the pork slices: In a bowl, combine the pork with salt, pepper, cornstarch, and a suitable amount of water. Mix well until the slices absorb the water and become slightly sticky (about 30 seconds). Set aside.
  3. Prepare the yam: Peel and slice the yam into thin, even slices (about 1cm thick). It's recommended to wear disposable gloves to prevent skin irritation from yam sap.
  4. Stir-fry the yam: Heat peanut oil in a pan or wok. Stir-fry the yam slices until golden brown and crispy.
  5. Stir-fry aromatics: Add sliced ginger to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant. Add the pickled mustard greens and stir-fry until fragrant. Remove from pan and set aside.
  6. Cook the soup: Add water to the pan or wok, bring to a boil. Add the stir-fried yam and mustard greens.
  7. Add the pork: Add the marinated pork slices to the pot, pressing them down gently with a spoon to submerge them in the soup.
  8. Simmer: Cover and simmer over low heat for 1 minute.
  9. Season: Open the lid, adjust seasoning with salt, pepper, chicken bouillon, and light soy sauce.
  10. Garnish: Garnish with chopped green onions. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=H0skpFcUwvQ

yam_soup.txt - 山药疙瘩汤 (Shānyào Gēdá Tāng)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious yam soup.
  • Master a simple, easy-to-follow recipe suitable for beginners.
  • Prepare a comforting and flavorful soup perfect for any occasion.

Ingredients

  • 2 鐵棍山藥 (tiěgùn shānyào) - Iron stick yams
  • 2 scoops plain flour (普通面粉 - pǔtōng miànfěn)
  • 1 tomato (西红柿 - xīhóngshì), diced
  • Several small oil vegetables (小油菜 - xiǎo yóucài), diced
  • 2 eggs (土鸡蛋 - tǔ jǐdàn)
  • Salt (食用盐 - shíyòng yán)
  • A few drops of white vinegar (白醋 - bái cù)
  • Several scallions (小葱 - xiǎo cōng), chopped
  • Some old ginger (老姜 - lǎo jiāng), minced
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòng yóu)
  • A small spoonful of salt (一小勺毛毛盐 - yī xiǎo sháo máomáo yán)
  • Plenty of mountain spring water (山泉水 - shān quán shuǐ)
  • A little salt (一丢丢盐 - yī diūdiū yán)
  • Some light soy sauce (生抽 - shēng chōu)
  • A little aged vinegar (陈醋 - chén cù)
  • A little sesame oil (小磨香油 - xiǎo mó xiāngyóu)

Instructions

  1. Peel two iron stick yams, wash, and chop into small pieces. Wear disposable gloves to avoid skin irritation from the yam sap.
  2. Add two scoops of plain flour to the yam, and mix well to coat each piece.
  3. Dice one tomato and several small oil vegetables.
  4. Whisk two eggs with a little salt and a few drops of white vinegar until well combined.
  5. Mince some old ginger and chop several scallions.
  6. Heat oil in a pan, add the egg mixture, scramble, and set aside.
  7. Add a little more oil to the pan, sauté the ginger and white parts of the scallions until fragrant.
  8. Add the diced tomatoes and sauté until softened and releasing their juices.
  9. Add a small spoonful of salt and continue sautéing.
  10. Add plenty of mountain spring water, cover, and bring to a boil.
  11. Add the yam pieces, stirring to prevent sticking. Simmer until the yam pieces float. Skim off any foam.
  12. After about 2 minutes, add the diced oil vegetables and the scrambled eggs. Stir well.
  13. Season with a little salt, light soy sauce, and aged vinegar. Stir.
  14. Before serving, drizzle with sesame oil and sprinkle with chopped scallions.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=w4a5jELpuD8

yam_steamed_buns.txt - 山药小馒头 (Shān yào xiǎo mántou)

Objectives

  • Learn to make fluffy and soft yam buns without adding water.
  • Understand the benefits of yam for digestion and health.
  • Create a nutritious and delicious breakfast or snack for family.

Ingredients

  • Several iron sticks of yam (山药 - Shān yào)
  • 1-2 large eggs (鸡蛋 - Jīdàn)
  • 5g yeast (酵母 - Jiàomǔ)
  • 400g flour (面粉 - Miànfěn)
  • 1 peeled carrot (胡萝卜 - Húluóbo), finely diced
  • A little white sugar (白糖 - Báitáng)

Instructions

  1. Prepare several iron stick yams. Wear disposable gloves to prevent skin irritation from the yam sap. Peel and wash the yams, then cut them into even small pieces.
  2. Steam the yam pieces in a steamer for 15 minutes until easily pierced with chopsticks.
  3. While steaming, prepare a peeled carrot. Cut it into thin slices, then into thin strips, and finally into small diced pieces. Set aside.
  4. Once steamed, transfer the yam to a large bowl. Add a little white sugar and mash it into a smooth puree using a spoon.
  5. Add two large eggs to the yam puree and mix well with a spoon.
  6. Add 5g of yeast and 400g of flour gradually, mixing until a large, fluffy dough forms.
  7. Add the diced carrots and continue mixing until a soft dough is formed.
  8. Knead the dough until smooth and elastic. Cover and let it rise in a warm place until doubled in size.
  9. Punch down the dough to release air. Roll it into a long log, divide it into equal-sized pieces, and roll each piece into a small log.
  10. Use a scraper to cut each small log into small bun shapes. Arrange them in a steamer lined with oiled paper.
  11. Let the buns proof for another 10 minutes in the steamer.
  12. Steam over high heat for 12 minutes, then let them sit for 3 minutes before serving to prevent collapsing.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=o4MFc1jblEg

yam_sweet_potato_glutinous_rice_cake.txt - 芋泥紫薯糯米餅

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious yam and sweet potato glutinous rice cakes.
  • Master the techniques of steaming, blending, and pan-frying.
  • Create a visually appealing and flavorful snack or dessert.

Ingredients

  • 1 medium yam (芋頭)
  • 2 medium sweet potatoes (紫薯)
  • 50ml pure milk (純牛奶)
  • 50g white sugar (白糖)
  • 30g corn oil (玉米油)
  • 300g glutinous rice flour (糯米粉) - preferably water-milled (水磨糯米粉)
  • 10g granulated sugar (綿白糖 or 白砂糖)
  • 150ml boiling water (開水)
  • Sesame seeds (芝麻) - for garnish

Instructions

  1. Clean and peel the yam and sweet potatoes. Cut the yam in half, then slice thinly. Do the same with the sweet potatoes.
  2. Steam the yam and sweet potato slices for 20 minutes.
  3. Transfer the steamed yam and sweet potatoes to a food processor. Add 50ml of pure milk and 50g of sugar. Blend until smooth and fine.
  4. Heat 30g of corn oil in a non-stick pan over medium-low heat. Add the yam and sweet potato puree. Stir continuously to prevent sticking for 4-5 minutes, or until thickened. Continue stirring for another 5-6 minutes until a cohesive dough forms.
  5. In a large bowl, mix 300g of glutinous rice flour and 10g of sugar. Gradually add 150ml of boiling water while stirring with chopsticks to form large clumps. Knead into a smooth dough, adding more hot water if too dry or more rice flour if too wet. Let it rest.
  6. Once the yam and sweet potato filling has cooled, form it into small balls (about ping-pong ball size).
  7. Take a portion of the glutinous rice dough, flatten it in your palm, and use your thumb to create a well in the center.
  8. Place a yam and sweet potato ball into the well. Pinch the edges to seal completely, ensuring no filling leaks out. Shape into a small flat cake.
  9. Lightly brush the surface with water and sprinkle with sesame seeds. Gently press to adhere.
  10. Preheat a non-stick pan. Brush with a thin layer of oil. Arrange the cakes leaving space between them. Brush the tops with oil.
  11. Cook over low heat for 2 minutes per side, or until golden brown and springy to the touch.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=oCPFeHvBF8g

yam_xiaowowo.txt - Yam Xiaowowo

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and nutritious yam xiaowowo.
  • Master a unique steaming and mashing technique for yams.
  • Create a flavorful and visually appealing dish suitable for all ages.

Ingredients

  • Yam (amount not specified, but enough to make many small nests)
  • 2x amount of potato starch (relative to the mashed yam)
  • ½ large red chili pepper
  • A handful of green onions
  • Several cloves of garlic
  • Salt (to taste)
  • 1 tbsp red bean paste
  • 1 tbsp water
  • 1 tsp light soy sauce
  • 1 tsp fresh matsutake mushroom (optional)
  • Pepper (to taste)
  • Oil (for stir-frying)
  • Shrimp shells (optional, for added flavor and calcium)
  • Lettuce leaves (optional, for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the yam: Peel and clean a yam (wear gloves if allergic). Cut it into smaller pieces for easier steaming.
  2. Steam the yam: Place the yam pieces in a steamer basket above boiling water. Steam on high heat for 10 minutes, or until tender.
  3. Prepare the aromatics: While steaming, finely chop the red chili pepper, green onions, and garlic. Set aside.
  4. Mash the yam: Once steamed, transfer the yam to a bowl. Add twice the amount of potato starch. Mash thoroughly with a rolling pin until smooth and a paste forms. Season with salt.
  5. Shape the yam nests: Roll the yam mixture into small balls. Use a little finger to create a small dimple in each ball, forming a nest shape. Work quickly to prevent drying.
  6. Cook the yam nests: Bring water to a boil in a pot. Gently place the yam nests in the boiling water. Stir occasionally to prevent sticking. Cook for about 5 minutes, or until they float to the surface.
  7. Cool the yam nests: Remove the cooked yam nests and immediately transfer them to a bowl of cold water to cool. Refrigerate for later use.
  8. Prepare the sauce: Heat oil in a pan. Add green onions and garlic; stir-fry until fragrant. Add red chili pepper and stir-fry. Add shrimp shells (optional) and stir-fry until fragrant. Add red bean paste and stir-fry until it turns red.
  9. Braise the yam nests: Add water, bring to a boil, then add the yam nests. Stir in salt, pepper, matsutake mushroom (optional), and light soy sauce. Simmer until the sauce thickens slightly.
  10. Garnish and serve: Before serving, garnish with chopped green onions.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=r2L3pRNzyb0

yiliangchi.txt - One Fish, Two Dishes

Objectives

  • Learn a recipe for cooking one fish in two ways.
  • Prepare a milky white fish and tofu soup.
  • Make a spicy and flavorful braised fish.
  • Minimize food waste by using all parts of the fish.
  • Learn techniques for frying fish to achieve a crispy texture.
  • Master a flavorful sauce for the braised fish.

Ingredients

  • 1 whole fish (cleaned)
  • Small handful of scallions (cut into segments and some into chopped pieces)
  • 2 purple perilla leaves (chopped)
  • 1 piece ginger (peeled, part sliced thinly, part julienned, part minced)
  • Several cloves garlic (sliced)
  • 3 green chilies (finely sliced and slightly crushed)
  • 3 red chilies (finely sliced and slightly crushed)
  • 1 small piece white radish (thinly sliced into strips)
  • 1 block of soft tofu (cut into 1cm cubes)
  • Small handful of king oyster mushrooms (cleaned and chopped)
  • 2 eggs
  • Cooking oil
  • Water
  • 1 tbsp dry pot sauce (or doubanjiang)
  • 1 tbsp mushroom seasoning
  • 1 tbsp light soy sauce
  • Small amount of oyster sauce
  • Water starch
  • Salt
  • Pepper

Instructions

  1. Clean the fish and pat it dry. Prepare the scallions (segments and chopped), purple perilla, and ginger (sliced, julienned, and minced). Also prepare the garlic and chilies.
  2. Prepare the radish, tofu, and king oyster mushrooms by cutting and cleaning them.
  3. Heat oil in a pan. Fry two eggs until golden brown on both sides. Set aside in a clay pot.
  4. Heat more oil in the same pan. Fry the fish until golden brown and crispy on both sides, ensuring it can easily slide in the pan.
  5. Add plenty of boiling water (not cold water) to the pan with the fish, along with the sliced ginger and scallion knots. Skim off any foam. Simmer for about 5 minutes until the broth turns milky white.
  6. Strain the fish broth into the clay pot, removing any remaining solids. Add the radish, mushrooms, and tofu. Cover and simmer over low heat for 10 minutes.
  7. While the soup simmers, transfer the fried fish to a separate plate.
  8. Heat a little oil in a pan. Stir-fry the ginger, garlic, and chilies until fragrant.
  9. Add the dry pot sauce (or doubanjiang) and stir-fry.
  10. Add a small bowl of water and bring to a boil.
  11. Add mushroom seasoning, light soy sauce, a small amount of oyster sauce, and water starch. Simmer until the sauce thickens slightly.
  12. Add the chopped scallions and purple perilla. Stir and pour the sauce over the fried fish.
  13. For the soup, add purple perilla, salt, mushroom seasoning, and pepper to taste. Garnish with chopped scallions.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=tWqDrcfF4cg

yumi_nmgm_bing.txt - Taro and Sweet Potato Mochi 芋泥糯米餅 - Yùní nuòmǐ bǐng

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious taro and sweet potato mochi.
  • Master the techniques of steaming, blending, and pan-frying.
  • Create a visually appealing and flavorful snack or dessert.

Ingredients

  • 芋頭 (yùtou) - Taro: Amount not specified, but enough to make filling.
  • 紫薯 (zǐshǔ) - Sweet Potato: Amount not specified, but enough to make filling.
  • 純牛奶 (chún niúnǎi) - Pure Milk: 50ml
  • 白糖 (báitáng) - White Sugar: 50g
  • 玉米油 (yùmǐ yóu) - Corn Oil: 30g
  • 糯米粉 (nuòmǐfěn) - Glutinous Rice Flour: 300g
  • 綿白糖/白砂糖 (mián báitáng/báishāntáng) - Cotton White Sugar/White Sugar: 10g
  • 開水 (kāishuǐ) - Boiling Water: 150ml
  • 芝麻 (zhīma) - Sesame Seeds: Amount not specified

Instructions

  1. Clean and peel the taro and sweet potatoes. Cut them into thin slices for easier steaming.
  2. Steam the taro and sweet potato slices for 20 minutes until cooked.
  3. Transfer the steamed taro and sweet potatoes to a food processor.
  4. Add 50ml of pure milk and 50g of white sugar to the food processor.
  5. Blend until a smooth, fine puree is formed. This may take several minutes.
  6. Heat 30g of corn oil in a non-stick pan over medium-low heat.
  7. Add the taro and sweet potato puree to the pan and stir continuously to prevent sticking. This will take 4-5 minutes, or longer until thickened.
  8. In a large bowl, mix 300g of glutinous rice flour and 10g of sugar.
  9. Gradually add 150ml of boiling water while stirring with chopsticks to form a shaggy dough.
  10. Knead the dough until smooth and pliable, adding more hot water if too dry or more rice flour if too wet. Let it rest.
  11. Once the taro and sweet potato filling has cooled, roll it into small balls (about ping pong ball size).
  12. Take a portion of the rested dough, roll it into a ball, and make a well in the center using your thumb.
  13. Place a taro and sweet potato filling ball into the well.
  14. Pinch the edges of the dough to seal, ensuring the filling is completely enclosed. Roll into a small disc.
  15. Lightly brush both sides of the disc with water and sprinkle with sesame seeds.
  16. Preheat a non-stick pan and lightly brush with oil.
  17. Place the mochi discs in the pan, leaving some space between them. Brush the tops with oil.
  18. Cook over low heat for 2 minutes per side, or until golden brown and cooked through. The mochi should spring back when pressed gently.

yun_dou_chao_rou_si.txt - 芸豆炒肉丝 (Yun Dou Chao Rou Si)

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare fresh green beans for cooking.
  • Master a quick and flavorful stir-fry technique.
  • Create a delicious and nutritious side dish.

Ingredients

  • 1 handful of green beans (芸豆 - yún dòu)
  • 1 small piece of lean pork (瘦肉 - shòu ròu)
  • 1 small spoonful of salt (食盐 - shí yán)
  • A dash of pepper (胡椒粉 - hú jiāo fěn)
  • 1 teaspoon of cornstarch (玉米淀粉 - yù mǐ diàn fěn)
  • Some water (清水 - qīng shuǐ)
  • 1 small piece of ginger (生姜 - shēng jiāng)
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜 - suàn)
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒 - xiǎo mǐ jiāo) or a large red pepper (大红椒 - dà hóng jiāo)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shí yòng yóu)
  • A pinch of salt (毛毛盐 - máo mao yán)
  • 1 tablespoon of soy sauce (生抽 - shēng chōu)
  • 1 tablespoon of yellow bean sauce (黄豆酱 - huáng dòu jiàng)
  • 1 tablespoon of chicken juice (鸡汁 - jī zhī)
  • 1 handful of peppercorns (花椒 - huā jiāo)
  • 1 handful of dried chili peppers (干海椒 - gān hǎi jiāo)
  • Some chopped scallions (葱末 - cōng mò)

Instructions

  1. Trim the ends of the green beans and wash them thoroughly with salted water.
  2. Cut the green beans into thin strips diagonally.
  3. Cut the pork into thin slices, then into thin strips.
  4. Marinate the pork strips with salt, pepper, cornstarch, and water.
  5. Mince the ginger, garlic, and chili peppers.
  6. Chop the scallions.
  7. Heat oil in a wok or pan.
  8. Stir-fry the green beans over high heat until they are about 70% cooked. Set aside.
  9. Add oil to the pan, then add ginger, garlic, and chili peppers, stir-frying until fragrant.
  10. Add the pork strips and stir-fry until they change color.
  11. Add peppercorns and yellow bean sauce, stir-fry until fragrant.
  12. Add the green beans, chicken juice, soy sauce, and dried chili peppers. Stir-fry until everything is well combined and cooked through.
  13. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=8yvUOefO3G4

yuxiang_eggs.txt - Fish Fragrant Eggs 鱼香鸡蛋

Objectives

  • Learn to make a flavorful and easy Fish Fragrant Egg dish.
  • Master the technique of quickly cooking eggs to maintain tenderness.
  • Understand how to prepare and balance the fish-fragrant sauce.

Ingredients

  • Eggs (number unspecified, but multiple) 新鲜的鸡蛋 (xīnxiān de jǐdàn)
  • Salt 食盐 (shíyán)
  • Water 清水 (qīngshuǐ)
  • White Vinegar 白醋 (bái cù)
  • 1 Carrot 胡萝卜 (húluóbo)
  • Scallions 小葱 (xiǎocōng)
  • Ginger 生姜 (shēngjiāng)
  • Garlic 蒜 (suàn)
  • 1 tbsp Chéncù 陈醋 (chéncù)
  • 1 tbsp Shēngchōu 生抽 (shēngchōu)
  • Pepper 胡椒粉 (hújiāofěn)
  • Sugar 白糖 (bái táng)
  • Corn Starch 玉米淀粉 (yùmǐ diànfěn)
  • Oyster Sauce 蚝油 (háoyóu)
  • Chili Flakes 细辣椒面 (xì làjiāomiàn)
  • Cooking Oil 食用油 (shíyòng yóu)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the eggs: Wash eggs thoroughly with salt water for 5 minutes to remove any bacteria. Crack eggs into a bowl, add a little white vinegar, and whisk well. Set aside.
  2. Prepare the vegetables: Peel and finely slice a carrot into strips. Finely chop scallions, ginger, and garlic. Set aside.
  3. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, mix together Chéncù, Shēngchōu, pepper, sugar, corn starch, oyster sauce, chili flakes, and a little water. Mix well and set aside.
  4. Cook the eggs: Heat cooking oil in a pan until slightly smoking. Pour in the egg mixture and quickly scramble, ensuring the eggs remain tender.
  5. Sauté aromatics: Add the chopped scallions, ginger, and garlic to the pan and stir-fry until fragrant.
  6. Add carrots: Add the carrot strips and stir-fry until softened.
  7. Add sauce: Pour the prepared sauce into the pan and stir-fry over high heat for about 50 seconds, until the eggs are well coated and the sauce has thickened.
  8. Garnish and serve: Stir in a handful of chopped scallions for garnish. Serve immediately.

zhu_ti.txt - Braised Pig's Trotters

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare tender, flavorful braised pig's trotters.
  • Master a method to remove impurities and enhance the taste.
  • Create a delicious dish suitable for special occasions.

Ingredients

  • 2 jin (approximately 2 pounds) fresh pig's trotters
  • Appropriate amount of salt
  • Appropriate amount of flour
  • Enough water for soaking and braising
  • Several slices of ginger
  • 1 scallion knot
  • 1 tablespoon of cooking wine (料酒)
  • 2 pieces of ginger slices
  • Star anise (八角)
  • Cinnamon (桂皮)
  • Bay leaves (香叶)
  • Half a bottle of 82-year-old beer (啤酒)
  • Dry chili segments (干辣椒段)
  • A little bit of dark soy sauce (老抽)
  • Plenty of garlic cloves (蒜子)
  • A handful of chili powder (辣椒面)
  • A small spoonful of salt (食盐)
  • A small spoonful of MSG (味精) (松茸鲜 - likely a brand of MSG)
  • A little bit of light soy sauce (生抽)
  • Some chopped scallions (葱花)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)

Instructions

  1. Clean the pig's trotters: Mix salt and flour with the pig's trotters, rub thoroughly to remove impurities. Rinse and soak in water for 10 minutes to remove blood. Rinse again until the water runs clear.
  2. Blanch the pig's trotters: Add ginger, scallion knot, and cooking wine to a pot of cold water. Bring to a boil, skim off the foam, and simmer for 2 minutes. Remove and drain, do not rinse with cold water.
  3. Sauté aromatics and pig's trotters: In a separate pot, sauté ginger slices, star anise, cinnamon, and bay leaves until fragrant. Add the pig's trotters and stir-fry until the surface is slightly dry (about 2 minutes).
  4. Braise the pig's trotters: Add beer, dry chili segments, and a little dark soy sauce. Stir-fry until the sauce boils. Transfer to a pressure cooker, pressure cook for 10 minutes.
  5. Prepare the garlic: Mince a large amount of garlic.
  6. Finish the dish: Remove the aromatics from the pressure cooker. Sauté minced garlic and chili powder until fragrant. Add the braised pig's trotters, stir-fry until the sauce boils. Season with salt, MSG, and light soy sauce. Simmer until the sauce thickens. Garnish with scallions before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=d0BC30TywA4

zucchini_vegetarian_dumplings.txt - 西葫芦素菜饺子

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious vegetarian zucchini dumplings.
  • Master the technique of preparing and combining the ingredients.
  • Understand the cooking process for perfectly cooked dumplings.

Ingredients

  • 2 fresh zucchini (西葫芦)
  • 1 carrot (胡萝卜)
  • 1 cup black fungus (黑木耳) - pre-soaked
  • 1 block firm tofu (豆腐)
  • 1 small bunch of scallions (小葱)
  • Salt (盐)
  • Pepper (胡椒粉)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • Sesame oil (香油) - optional
  • Shrimp paste (虾皮) - optional
  • Dumpling wrappers (饺子皮) - store-bought

Instructions

  1. Wash and cut two zucchini into thin slices, then julienne into fine strands. Add salt, mix, and let sit for 5 minutes to draw out moisture.
  2. Prepare other vegetables: Cut the carrot into thin slices, then julienne, then mince. Clean and mince the soaked black fungus. Cut the tofu into small cubes. Mince the scallions.
  3. Squeeze out excess water from the zucchini. Roughly chop the zucchini.
  4. Stir-fry the zucchini in a pan over low heat until moisture evaporates. Set aside.
  5. In a separate pan, add a little oil and stir-fry the tofu until golden brown.
  6. Add the minced carrots and black fungus to the pan with the tofu. Stir-fry until tender.
  7. Season the tofu and vegetable mixture with salt, pepper, oyster sauce, and optional shrimp paste. Stir-fry until flavors combine.
  8. Combine the stir-fried tofu and vegetable mixture with the zucchini in a large bowl. Add the minced scallions and sesame oil. Mix well.
  9. Prepare the dumplings: Place a dumpling wrapper in your palm, brush the edges with water, add a spoonful of filling, and fold to create a dumpling.
  10. Boil a pot of water. Add the dumplings, cover, and cook over high heat for 2-3 minutes until they float. Add cold water, and continue cooking for another 3-4 minutes, or until the dumplings are cooked through and the wrappers are translucent.
  11. Serve the dumplings immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=zasdJB4RZjg

万能蒜蓉酱.txt - Universal Garlic Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn to make a versatile garlic sauce for various dishes.
  • Master the technique of deep-frying garlic for optimal flavor and texture.
  • Understand how to adjust seasonings to achieve the desired taste.

Ingredients

  • 2 jin (approximately 2 pounds) garlic cloves
  • Corn oil (amount not specified, but a generous amount is used)
  • 1 large spoonful of salt
  • A small amount of white sugar
  • 1 large spoonful of soy sauce (生抽 - shēng chōu)
  • An appropriate amount of oyster sauce (蚝油 - háo yóu)
  • Water (for rinsing the garlic)

Instructions

  1. Clean and trim the garlic cloves, removing damaged parts.
  2. Grind the garlic using a meat grinder, pulsing for about 10-15 seconds (3 seconds on, 3 seconds off).
  3. Add water to the minced garlic in the grinder and rinse to remove the sticky residue.
  4. Filter and drain the garlic, squeezing out excess water.
  5. Heat a generous amount of corn oil in a pot over medium heat, stirring to coat the sides.
  6. Once the oil reaches 40% heat, add half of the prepared garlic.
  7. Deep-fry the garlic until golden brown, stirring frequently to prevent burning (approximately 5-10 minutes).
  8. Once the first half is fried and golden, add the remaining garlic and stir-fry over high heat for 1-2 minutes.
  9. Add salt, a little sugar, soy sauce, and oyster sauce; stir-fry until the seasonings are well combined and the garlic is evenly coated.
  10. Turn off the heat and let the garlic sauce cool.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Z6w54p9ST_k

千里香馄饨.txt - Qianlixiang Wonton

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious, juicy wonton filling.
  • Master a restaurant-style wonton recipe.
  • Prepare a flavorful wonton broth.

Ingredients

  • 280g 五花肉 (wǔhuāròu) - pork belly (2 parts lean, 8 parts fat)
  • 1 piece 生姜 (shēngjiāng) - ginger
  • 1 piece 大葱 (dàcōng) - scallion
  • 1 tsp 食盐 (shíyán) - salt
  • 1 tbsp 料酒 (liàojiǔ) - cooking wine
  • 1/2 bowl 清水 (qīngshuǐ) - water
  • A bunch 小葱 (xiǎocōng) - scallions
  • A few stalks 香菜 (xiāngcài) - cilantro
  • 1 tsp 食盐 (shíyán) - salt
  • 1 tbsp 白糖 (báitáng) - sugar
  • 1 tbsp 味精 (wèijīng) - MSG
  • 1 tbsp 虾皮粉 (xiāpípǐnfěn) - dried shrimp powder
  • Some 生抽 (shēngchōu) - light soy sauce
  • Some 蚝油 (háoyóu) - oyster sauce
  • Wonton wrappers (from supermarket)

Instructions

  1. Dice pork belly into thin slices, then mince into a slightly coarse texture. (You can use a food processor if preferred).
  2. Mince ginger and thinly slice scallions.
  3. Combine minced scallions, ginger, 1 tsp salt in a bowl; mix well to release aroma.
  4. Add 1 tbsp cooking wine and 1/2 bowl water; let it sit for 10 minutes to extract flavor.
  5. Mince scallions and cilantro. Set aside.
  6. In a large bowl, combine minced pork with 1 tsp salt, 1 tbsp sugar, 1 tbsp MSG, 1 tbsp shrimp powder, light soy sauce, and oyster sauce. Mix thoroughly in one direction until well combined.
  7. Gradually add the scallion-ginger water in 3 additions, mixing well after each addition until the mixture is sticky and elastic. Do not add starch; the meat should naturally bind together.
  8. Add minced scallions and mix well. Gently beat the mixture for 2 minutes to improve elasticity.
  9. Place a spoonful of filling in the center of each wonton wrapper. Fold diagonally and pinch to seal.
  10. Prepare the wonton broth: In a bowl, combine 1 tbsp soy sauce, 1 tsp salt, a handful of dried shrimp, and a small amount of sesame oil. Add chopped scallions and cilantro.
  11. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add wontons and simmer until they float to the surface.
  12. Ladle 2 spoonfuls of the wonton broth into the prepared broth bowl. Stir well.
  13. Remove wontons with a strainer and serve in bowls with the prepared broth.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Zdtj_sdU-Y0

叉烧肉.txt - Char Siu Pork

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious char siu pork without an oven.
  • Master a simple, cost-effective, and hygienic char siu recipe.
  • Prepare a flavorful marinade and achieve perfectly tender char siu.

Ingredients

  • 3 jin (approximately 1.5 kg) Mei Tou pork (pork shoulder butt)
  • Several cloves garlic, smashed
  • Small piece of ginger, smashed
  • Small handful of scallions, cut into segments
  • Appropriate amount of cooking wine (料酒)
  • 4 small spoons of char siu sauce (叉烧酱)
  • 50g char siu sauce (for 2 jin of pork)
  • 1 spoon of salt (食盐)
  • 1 spoon of soy sauce (生抽)
  • 60g honey (蜂蜜)
  • Appropriate amount of boiled water (白开水)

Instructions

  1. Cut the pork shoulder in half lengthwise, resulting in two pieces approximately 2cm thick.
  2. Place the cut pork in a large bowl.
  3. Smash garlic and ginger to release their juices. Add smashed garlic and ginger, and chopped scallions to the bowl with the pork.
  4. Pour in an appropriate amount of cooking wine and mix well with the garlic, ginger, and scallions to extract their juices.
  5. Add 4 small spoons of char siu sauce, 1 spoon of salt, and 1 spoon of soy sauce to the pork.
  6. Mix everything thoroughly until the pork is evenly coated.
  7. Cover the bowl and refrigerate overnight to marinate.
  8. Prepare the honey water: Mix 60g honey with an appropriate amount of boiled water until the honey is completely dissolved.
  9. Pour the honey water into a rice cooker.
  10. Add the marinated pork pieces to the rice cooker, placing them evenly at the bottom.
  11. Pour the marinade from the bowl into the rice cooker.
  12. Close the lid and press the "cook" button on the rice cooker.
  13. Cook for approximately 20 minutes, stirring two or three times to prevent sticking and ensure even cooking.
  14. Once the sauce has thickened to a desirable consistency (as shown in the video), remove the char siu.
  15. Allow the char siu to cool completely.
  16. Slice the cooled char siu into thick slices.
  17. Serve and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Q0chTnULyrI

四季豆炒肉末.txt - Stir-fried String Beans with Minced Pork

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare fresh string beans for cooking.
  • Master a simple and delicious stir-fry recipe.
  • Understand how to enhance the flavor of string beans and minced pork.

Ingredients

  • String beans (四季豆): A handful (about 200g)
  • Lean pork (瘦肉): 200g
  • Scallions (小葱): 2 stalks
  • Ginger (生姜): 1 piece
  • Garlic (蒜): several cloves
  • Dried chilies (干海椒): a few
  • Salt (食盐): to taste
  • Sugar (白糖): a pinch
  • Light soy sauce (生抽): to taste
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油): to taste
  • Cooking oil (食用油): a generous amount
  • White sesame seeds (白芝麻): a sprinkle

Instructions

  1. Prepare the string beans: Trim the ends of the string beans. Remove the stringy parts. Wash thoroughly in light salt water to remove pesticides and preserve freshness. Break into 3-4 cm pieces. Drain well.
  2. Prepare the pork: Cut lean pork into thin slices, then mince. Do not mince too finely; some texture is desirable. Set aside.
  3. Prepare the aromatics: Finely chop scallions and ginger. Crush and mince garlic. Cut dried chilies into small pieces.
  4. Deep-fry the string beans: Heat a generous amount of oil in a wok or pan until hot (4-5 parts hot). Add the string beans and fry for about 7-9 seconds until slightly blistered. Remove and drain on a wire rack or paper towels.
  5. Stir-fry the aromatics and pork: Add a little oil to the wok. Add ginger, garlic, and dried chilies, stir-frying until fragrant. Add the minced pork and stir-fry over low heat until the color changes.
  6. Combine and season: Add the fried string beans to the wok. Season with salt, sugar, light soy sauce, and oyster sauce. Stir-fry quickly over high heat until well combined and heated through.
  7. Garnish and serve: Sprinkle with white sesame seeds. Stir-fry for another 5-8 seconds. Serve immediately.

土豆丝煎饼.txt - Potato Shredded Pancakes

Objectives

  • Learn a simple method for cooking potatoes.
  • Create crispy and soft potato pancakes without additional ingredients.
  • Utilize readily available kitchen tools for efficient preparation.

Ingredients

2 small potatoes 适量面粉 (shì liàng miànfěn) - appropriate amount of flour 食用油 (shíyòng yóu) - cooking oil 少许盐 (shǎoxǔ yán) - a little salt 细细的辣椒面 (xìxì de làjiāomiàn) - finely ground chili powder 葱花 (cōnghuā) - chopped green onions

Instructions

  1. Wash and peel two small potatoes.
  2. Use a grater to shred the potatoes into thin, even strands. Alternatively, finely slice with a knife.
  3. Gradually add flour to the potato shreds, mixing until they are just sticky enough to hold together. Do not use too much flour.
  4. Heat a non-stick pan or frying pan over medium-low heat. Brush with a thin layer of oil.
  5. Spread the potato mixture into a thin pancake in the pan.
  6. Cook until the bottom is golden brown and crispy.
  7. Flip the pancake and cook the other side until golden brown and crispy. (Use a plate to help flip if needed). This should take about 5-6 minutes total.
  8. Repeat steps 4-7 with the remaining potato mixture.
  9. Remove from heat and transfer to a plate.
  10. Sprinkle with a little salt, chili powder, and chopped green onions (and optionally, pepper or other seasonings).
  11. Serve immediately and enjoy!
