带鱼_香焖.txt - Fragrant Braised Hairtail

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy braised hairtail dish.
  • Master the technique of preparing and seasoning the hairtail.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to complement the hairtail.

Ingredients

  • 2 Hairtail (带鱼 dài yú) - approximately 11 RMB each
  • 1 large Onion (大葱 dà cōng)
  • 1 piece Ginger (生姜 shēng jiāng)
  • 1 tbsp Cooking Wine (料酒 liào jiǔ)
  • 1 tbsp Huadiao Wine (花雕酒 huā diāo jiǔ)
  • 1 tsp Salt (食盐 shí yán)
  • 1/2 tsp Pepper (胡椒粉 hú jiāo fěn)
  • 1 egg (笨鸡蛋 bèn jī dàn)
  • A little bit of salt (毛毛盐 máo mao yán)
  • A little bit of chicken essence (鸡精 jī jīng)
  • A pinch of five-spice powder (五香粉 wǔ xiāng fěn)
  • 1 tsp Sugar (白糖 bái táng)
  • 1 tbsp Soy Sauce (生抽 shēng chōu)
  • 1/2 tbsp Vinegar (陈醋 chén cù)
  • A little bit of oyster sauce (蚝油 háo yóu)
  • Some water (清水 qīng shuǐ)
  • 1 tbsp cornstarch (淀粉 diàn fěn) - approximately 30g
  • Vegetable oil (菜籽油 cài zǐ yóu)

Instructions

  1. Clean the hairtail: Remove fins, gut, and black membrane. Rinse thoroughly until the water runs clear.
  2. Cut the hairtail: Cut off the head (for the cat!), and cut the body into 5-6 cm sections.
  3. Score the hairtail: Use a knife to make shallow cuts along the fish bones on both sides.
  4. Marinate the hairtail: Place the scored hairtail in a bowl. Add onion (cut into diagonal segments), ginger (sliced thinly), cooking wine, Huadiao wine, salt, and pepper. Mix well and marinate for 20 minutes.
  5. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, mix a little salt, chicken essence, five-spice powder, sugar, soy sauce, vinegar, oyster sauce, and water. Stir until well combined.
  6. Prepare the egg: Crack an egg into a bowl and whisk until the egg white and yolk are fully combined.
  7. Coat the hairtail: Add the whisked egg to the marinated hairtail and mix well to coat.
  8. Add cornstarch: Add cornstarch to the hairtail and mix well to coat evenly.
  9. Fry the hairtail: Heat vegetable oil in a pan until slightly smoking. Fry the hairtail over medium-low heat until golden brown on both sides.
  10. Prepare the sauce base: In a clean pan, heat a little oil, add sliced garlic, ginger, and white parts of the onion. Sauté until fragrant.
  11. Combine sauce and hairtail: Add the prepared sauce to the pan. Bring to a boil, then add the fried hairtail. Stir to coat evenly.
  12. Simmer: Optionally cover and simmer for 2 minutes. Uncover and continue to cook over high heat to reduce the sauce.
  13. Serve: Turn off the heat and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_3Zmyco01ys

泡发腐竹肉沫西红柿.txt - Stewed Dried Tofu with Pork and Tomatoes

Objectives

  • Learn how to quickly and effectively soak dried tofu.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful recipe for stewed dried tofu.
  • Understand the importance of controlling cooking time for optimal texture.

Ingredients

  • 高安腐竹 (Gāo'ān fǔzhú) - Dried Tofu from Gao'an (amount unspecified, adjust to your preference)
  • 食盐 (Shíyán) - Salt (a pinch)
  • 白醋 (Bái cù) - White Vinegar (a splash)
  • 清水 (Qīngshuǐ) - Water (a generous amount for soaking)
  • 西红柿 (Xīhóngshì) - Tomatoes (1, large)
  • 瘦肉 (Shòuròu) - Lean Pork (approx. 200g)
  • 小葱 (Xiǎocōng) - Scallions (a few stalks)
  • 生姜 (Shēngjiāng) - Ginger (1 piece)
  • 大蒜 (Dàsuàn) - Garlic (a few cloves)
  • 黄豆酱 (Huángdòujiàng) - Soybean Paste (1 large spoonful)
  • 胡椒粉 (Hújiāofěn) - Black Pepper Powder (a pinch)
  • 生抽 (Shēngchōu) - Light Soy Sauce (a small amount)
  • 蚝油 (Háoyóu) - Oyster Sauce (a small amount)
  • 玻璃芡 (Bōlí qiàn) - Glass Glaze (optional, for thickening)
  • 葱花 (Cōnghuā) - Chopped Scallions (for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Cut dried tofu into small pieces.
  2. Add salt and white vinegar to water, then soak the tofu until fully expanded (approx. 1 hour).
  3. Dice tomatoes, mince pork, and chop scallions, ginger, and garlic.
  4. Bring water to a boil in a pot, add salt, and blanch the soaked tofu for about 1 minute to remove beany smell. Remove and set aside.
  5. Heat oil in a separate pot, add minced pork, and stir-fry until browned and fragrant.
  6. Add minced scallions, ginger, and garlic; stir-fry until fragrant.
  7. Add diced tomatoes and stir-fry briefly, adding a pinch of salt to help release juices. Press tomatoes to release more juices.
  8. Add soybean paste, black pepper powder, light soy sauce, and oyster sauce. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Add water, bring to a boil, then add the blanched tofu. Stir gently and simmer, covered, for 2-3 minutes.
  10. Remove the lid, increase heat, and reduce the sauce, optionally adding glass glaze to thicken.
  11. Garnish with chopped scallions and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZuXrRE-lf4Q

炒花生米.txt - Stir-fried Peanuts

Objectives

  • Learn to make crispy, flavorful stir-fried peanuts.
  • Avoid common mistakes like burning or undercooking peanuts.
  • Master a method for perfectly stir-fried peanuts suitable for any occasion.
  • Understand the importance of properly cleaning and drying peanuts before cooking.
  • Learn how to enhance the flavor and preservation of peanuts using white wine.

Ingredients

500克 (1斤) 花生米 (500g Peanuts) 1汤匙 面粉 (1 tablespoon Flour) 清水 (Water) 少许 白醋 (A little White Vinegar) 少许 食用油 (A little Cooking Oil) 少许 高度白酒 (A little High-proof Liquor) 食盐 or 白糖 (Salt or Sugar, to taste)

Instructions

  1. Clean the peanuts: Pick out any bad, moldy, or sprouted peanuts. Add a tablespoon of flour to the peanuts and mix well. Add plenty of water and rinse thoroughly to remove dust and impurities. Drain and rinse again with clean water, optionally adding a little white vinegar to help prevent the skins from peeling during cooking. Dry the peanuts thoroughly using a colander, paper towels, a hair dryer, or by letting them sit in the sun.

  2. Dry-roast the peanuts: Heat a wok or large pan over low heat. Add the peanuts and stir-fry gently to remove excess moisture. Be patient and stir frequently to prevent burning. Continue until the peanut skins are smooth and shiny.

  3. Add oil and stir-fry: Add a small amount of cooking oil (just enough to lightly coat the peanuts). Continue stir-frying over low heat until you hear a crackling sound.

  4. Add liquor and finish: When the crackling sound subsides and the peanuts are lightly golden, add a little high-proof liquor (e.g., baijiu). Stir well to distribute the aroma.

  5. Season and serve: Remove the peanuts from the heat and transfer to a plate. Use chopsticks to spread them out to cool quickly. Season with salt or sugar to taste. Gently toss to distribute seasoning.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=fRjwguYyBbo

炒面.txt - Fried Noodles

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious, non-clumpy fried noodles.
  • Master techniques to achieve a restaurant-quality taste at home.
  • Understand the importance of proper noodle preparation and ingredient selection.
  • Learn how to create a flavorful sauce for the noodles.

Ingredients

  • 1-2 packs dried noodles (5 kuai)
  • 1 small head of baby bok choy, thinly sliced
  • 1 carrot, peeled and julienned
  • 1 small onion, chopped
  • 1 egg
  • Approximately 100g of lean pork, thinly sliced
  • Salt
  • White vinegar
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽)
  • 1 tsp dark soy sauce (老抽)
  • 1 tsp sugar
  • A pinch of chicken powder (optional)
  • 1 tsp thirteen spice (十三香)
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Boil water in a pot. Add dried noodles and cook for 2 minutes over low heat, then 1 minute over high heat. Stir occasionally to ensure even cooking.
  2. Rinse the cooked noodles under cold water to maintain their texture. Drain and set aside.
  3. Thinly slice the baby bok choy and rinse. Set aside.
  4. Julienne the carrot. Set aside.
  5. Chop the onion. Set aside.
  6. In a bowl, whisk together 1 egg, salt, and a few drops of white vinegar.
  7. Thinly slice the pork. Set aside.
  8. Heat a small amount of oil in a pan. Remove excess oil.
  9. Pour the egg mixture into the pan and cook until golden brown on both sides. Remove, let cool, then slice into strips.
  10. In a bowl, whisk together soy sauce, dark soy sauce, salt, sugar, chicken powder (if using), and thirteen spice. Set aside.
  11. Heat oil in a wok or large pan. Add the carrots and stir-fry until slightly softened.
  12. Add the pork and stir-fry until cooked through.
  13. Add the bok choy and continue stir-frying until wilted. Season with a little salt.
  14. Add the noodles to the pan. Stir-fry over high heat until heated through. If noodles are too long, cut them with scissors.
  15. Pour in the prepared sauce and stir-fry until the noodles are evenly coated and flavorful.
  16. Add the sliced egg and onions. Stir-fry for a short time to combine.
  17. Remove from heat and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=sZw7_z5cG0I

烤土豆.txt - Roasted Potatoes 烤土豆 - Roasted Potatoes

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious roasted potatoes with a simple recipe.
  • Master the technique of achieving crispy exterior and tender interior.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients for a budget-friendly dish.

Ingredients

  • 2 large potatoes (yellow-fleshed preferred)
  • Plenty of spring onions (scallions), chopped
  • Plenty of garlic, minced
  • 1 tbsp cumin powder
  • 1 tbsp chili powder
  • 1/2 tbsp Sichuan peppercorn powder
  • A pinch of salt
  • 2 tbsp white sesame seeds
  • A pinch of black pepper
  • Vegetable oil (preferably canola oil)

Instructions

  1. Peel and thoroughly wash the potatoes.
  2. Cut the potatoes into small, roughly 1-inch cubes.
  3. Rinse the cut potatoes in several changes of water to remove excess starch.
  4. Soak the potatoes in water while preparing other ingredients.
  5. Chop spring onions into small pieces and mince garlic.
  6. Prepare the seasoning: mix cumin powder, chili powder, Sichuan peppercorn powder, salt, white sesame seeds, and black pepper in a bowl.
  7. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add the potatoes and blanch for 4 minutes until translucent.
  8. Drain the potatoes and set aside.
  9. Heat vegetable oil in a flat pan until slightly smoking.
  10. Add the blanched potatoes to the hot pan and stir-fry until the surfaces are golden brown and crispy (approximately 4-5 minutes). Be patient and ensure even cooking.
  11. Add the minced garlic and continue to stir-fry until fragrant.
  12. Sprinkle the prepared seasoning mix over the potatoes and stir-fry until evenly coated.
  13. Add the chopped spring onions and stir-fry briefly.
  14. Serve immediately.

白菜_凉菜.txt - 凉拌白菜

Objectives

  • Learn to make a refreshing and flavorful cold dish using Napa cabbage.
  • Master the technique of preparing and marinating Napa cabbage for optimal texture and taste.
  • Understand how to combine various seasonings to create a balanced and delicious flavor profile.

Ingredients

  • 2 small Napa cabbages
  • Salt (less than usual amount for cooking)
  • A pinch of white sugar
  • 1 bunch of scallions, chopped
  • 1 piece of ginger, minced
  • Several cloves of garlic, minced
  • 1 green chili pepper, sliced
  • 1 red chili pepper, sliced
  • A little chili powder
  • A little white sesame seeds
  • Several peppercorns
  • White vinegar (preferably rice vinegar)
  • A little soy sauce
  • Oyster sauce
  • A little chicken bouillon
  • Hot oil

Instructions

  1. Remove the outer leaves and root end of the Napa cabbages. Wash thoroughly, paying attention to the slippery film on the stems.
  2. Cut the cabbages into thin, even strips lengthwise.
  3. Place the cut cabbage in a bowl, add a small amount of salt and a pinch of sugar. Mix well and let marinate for about 10 minutes.
  4. While the cabbage marinates, prepare the other ingredients: mince the scallions, ginger, and garlic; slice the chili peppers.
  5. After 10 minutes, the cabbage should be softened and slightly translucent. Rinse to remove excess salt. Drain well.
  6. Add the marinated cabbage, sliced chili peppers, minced scallions, ginger, garlic, chili powder, white sesame seeds, and peppercorns to a large bowl.
  7. Add white vinegar, soy sauce, oyster sauce, and chicken bouillon.
  8. Pour hot oil over the mixture.
  9. Toss gently to combine all ingredients.
  10. Serve and enjoy! This dish pairs well with rice, steamed buns, or noodles.

  9. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, mix salt, sugar, yellow soybean paste, soy sauce, and water.

皮蛋瘦肉粥.txt - Pig's Blood and Lean Meat Porridge

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious Pig's Blood and Lean Meat Porridge.
  • Master the techniques for preparing the rice and ingredients.
  • Create a flavorful and fragrant porridge at home economically.

Ingredients

  • Rice (amount depends on serving size)
  • 2-3 Preserved Duck Eggs (松花皮蛋 - sōnghuā pí dàn)
  • Lean pork (瘦肉 - shòuròu), about 200g
  • Spring onion (小葱 - xiǎocōng), a few stalks
  • Ginger (生姜 - shēngjiāng), a small piece
  • Salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • Corn starch (玉米淀粉 - yùmǐ diànfěn)
  • Pepper (胡椒粉 - hújiāo fěn)
  • Water (山泉水 - shānquán shuǐ)

Instructions

  1. Rinse rice thoroughly and soak in water for 10 minutes.
  2. Prepare 2-3 preserved duck eggs, remove shells, and rinse.
  3. While rice soaks, cut lean pork into thin slices, then into fine shreds.
  4. Marinate pork shreds with salt and cornstarch until well combined. Set aside for 10 minutes.
  5. Chop spring onions and ginger into fine pieces.
  6. Drain soaked rice and add to a sand pot.
  7. Add the preserved duck eggs to the rice, then crush the eggs using disposable gloves. Mix well with the rice.
  8. Add sufficient spring water, cover, and simmer over low heat for 40 minutes.
  9. Add marinated pork shreds and ginger to the porridge.
  10. Stir well and cook over high heat for 2-3 minutes.
  11. Season with a little salt and pepper.
  12. Stir in chopped spring onions.
  13. Serve and enjoy!

皮蛋苋菜汤.txt - Pig's Blood and Amaranth Soup

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious Pig's Blood and Amaranth Soup.
  • Understand the importance of preparing the amaranth properly.
  • Master a quick and easy cooking method for this dish.

Ingredients

  • Fresh amaranth (remove old roots)
  • Salt
  • Water
  • Several preserved duck eggs (皮蛋, pí dàn), QQ-textured with a slightly loose yolk
  • Ginger, sliced thinly then into threads
  • Garlic cloves, minced
  • Pork lard (猪油, zhūyóu) - 1 scoop
  • 1 bowl of boiling water
  • 1 scoop of salt
  • Pepper

Instructions

  1. Remove the old roots from the fresh amaranth, leaving only the tender parts.
  2. Wash the amaranth thoroughly and soak in a bowl of salted water for 10 minutes to remove insects and impurities.
  3. Rinse the amaranth several times with clean water and drain.
  4. Peel and crush the preserved duck eggs. Set aside.
  5. Prepare the ginger and garlic.
  6. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add the amaranth and blanch for 1 minute to remove oxalic acid. Remove with a slotted spoon and set aside in a sand pot. (Reserve the blanching water for other uses).
  7. Heat pork lard in a wok. Add the crushed preserved duck eggs and stir-fry until they become slightly browned.
  8. Add the ginger and garlic and stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Pour in a bowl of boiling water, add salt and pepper to taste. Stir well.
  10. Pour the mixture into the sand pot with the blanched amaranth.
  11. Cover and simmer for 2-3 minutes.
  12. Serve immediately.

秋葵鸡蛋饼_qiukui_egg_cake.txt - 秋葵鸡蛋饼 (Qiūkuí jǐdàn bǐng)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious Qiūkuí jǐdàn bǐng (Okra Egg Cake).
  • Master the techniques for preparing and cooking okra.
  • Create a flavorful sauce to complement the okra egg cake.

Ingredients

  • 新鲜秋葵 (xīnxiān qiūkuí) - Fresh Okra (about 200g)
  • 4个母鸡下的蛋 (4 gè mǔjī xià de dàn) - 4 Chicken Eggs
  • 食用盐 (shíyòng yán) - Table Salt (to taste)
  • 胡椒粉 (hújiāo fěn) - Black Pepper (to taste)
  • 瘦肉 (shòu ròu) - Lean Pork (about 100g)
  • 蒜 (suàn) - Garlic (several cloves)
  • 小米椒 (xiǎo mǐjiāo) - Small Chili Peppers (a few)
  • 普宁豆酱 (pǔníng dòujiàng) - Puning Doujiang (fermented soybean paste) (2 tablespoons)
  • 清水 (qīngshuǐ) - Water (about 1/2 bowl)
  • 水淀粉 (shuǐ diànfěn) - Water Starch (small amount)
  • 食用油 (shíyòng yóu) - Cooking Oil (as needed)
  • 葱花 (cōnghuā) - Chopped Green Onions (optional)

Instructions

  1. Wash the okra thoroughly, rubbing it with salt to remove the fuzz. Rinse well.
  2. Blanch the okra in boiling water with salt and oil for 2 minutes. Do not remove the stem and ends.
  3. Immediately transfer the blanched okra to ice water to cool. Drain and set aside.
  4. Slice off a small portion of the okra tops and then slice the okra into thin rounds.
  5. In a bowl, whisk together the eggs, salt, and pepper.
  6. Add the sliced okra to the egg mixture and stir until well coated.
  7. Mince the pork, garlic, and chili peppers.
  8. Heat oil in a pan. Pour in the okra and egg mixture, stir to quickly solidify.
  9. Reduce heat and slowly pan-fry until golden brown on both sides.
  10. Remove the okra egg cake and set aside.
  11. In the same pan, stir-fry the pork until browned.
  12. Add the garlic and chili peppers, stir-frying until fragrant.
  13. Stir in the Puning Doujiang and cook until fragrant.
  14. Add water and bring to a boil. Thicken with water starch.
  15. Pour the sauce over the okra egg cake. Garnish with chopped green onions (optional).

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ujZ6j9JKQWk

糯米卷.txt - Glutinous Rice Rolls

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious glutinous rice rolls for the Dragon Boat Festival.
  • Utilize leftover glutinous rice creatively beyond traditional zongzi.
  • Create a crispy exterior and soft, chewy interior in the glutinous rice rolls.

Ingredients

  • 200g glutinous rice
  • Dried shiitake mushrooms (amount unspecified)
  • 1 carrot, peeled and diced
  • 1 corn cob, kernels removed
  • Sweet peas (amount unspecified)
  • 5 RMB worth of lean pork, minced
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Oyster sauce
  • Light soy sauce
  • 2 RMB worth of dumpling wrappers
  • 2 eggs

Instructions

  1. Rinse glutinous rice gently several times without rubbing, then soak in water for 2 hours.
  2. Soak dried shiitake mushrooms in warm water for 10 minutes until softened. Clean and dice.
  3. Dice the carrot into small pieces.
  4. Cut the corn kernels off the cob.
  5. Rinse sweet peas and drain.
  6. Mince the lean pork.
  7. After 2 hours, drain the soaked glutinous rice and steam for 30 minutes.
  8. Boil corn, peas, carrots, and shiitake mushrooms for 5 minutes. Drain.
  9. Stir-fry minced pork until browned.
  10. Add the boiled vegetables to the pork and stir-fry.
  11. Season with salt, pepper, oyster sauce, and light soy sauce. Stir-fry until flavors combine.
  12. Add the steamed glutinous rice to the vegetable and pork mixture and stir-fry until well combined.
  13. Slightly roll out dumpling wrappers.
  14. Place a spoonful of the glutinous rice mixture onto each wrapper.
  15. Brush the edges of the wrapper with water, fold and roll to seal.
  16. Whisk eggs.
  17. Dip each rice roll into the egg mixture.
  18. Heat oil in a pan to medium-high heat.
  19. Fry the rice rolls until golden brown and crispy, flipping frequently.

素炒萝卜.txt - Stir-fried Radish

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy stir-fried radish dish.
  • Master the technique of blanching radish to remove bitterness and enhance flavor.
  • Understand how to balance flavors and create a visually appealing dish.

Ingredients

  • 2 large white radishes (白萝卜)
  • A small handful of garlic cloves (蒜子)
  • 1 piece of ginger (生姜)
  • Salt (食盐)
  • Soy sauce (酱油)
  • Light soy sauce (生抽)
  • Optional: Chicken bouillon (鸡汁)
  • Water (清水)
  • Water starch (水淀粉)
  • Sesame oil (香油)
  • Leftover chopped celery (芹菜碎, optional)

Instructions

  1. Wash and peel two large white radishes.
  2. Cut the radishes into 3cm thick rounds, then into smaller pieces.
  3. Mince the garlic cloves and julienne the ginger.
  4. Bring a pot of water to a boil, add a pinch of salt, and blanch the radish pieces for 3-5 minutes until translucent.
  5. Drain the blanched radishes well.
  6. Heat oil in a wok or pan over medium heat. Add garlic and ginger and stir-fry until fragrant. Remove from pan.
  7. Add the blanched radishes to the wok and stir-fry for about a minute until slightly softened.
  8. Add a large bowl of water (or broth for a richer flavor).
  9. Season with salt, soy sauce (for color), light soy sauce (for flavor), and optional chicken bouillon. Stir well.
  10. Cover and simmer over high heat for about 8 minutes.
  11. Uncover and add water starch and sesame oil. Stir-fry until the sauce thickens.
  12. Add leftover chopped celery (optional) and stir-fry for a few seconds.
  13. Serve hot.

腌黄瓜.txt - Pickled Cucumber

Objectives

  • Learn to make a restaurant-style pickled cucumber recipe.
  • Master a quick and easy pickling method for crispy cucumbers.
  • Understand the importance of the correct ratio of ingredients for optimal flavor.

Ingredients

  • 6 jin (approximately 3.6 kg) tender yellow cucumbers with thorns
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒)
  • Plenty of garlic cloves (蒜子)
  • 1 lemon (柠檬)
  • 200 grams light soy sauce (生抽)
  • 80 grams Shanxi aged vinegar (山西老陈醋)
  • 50 grams dark soy sauce (老抽)
  • 100 grams ready-made cold dish sauce (凉拌汁)
  • 200 grams white sugar (白糖)
  • Salt (食盐)

Instructions

  1. Wash the cucumbers thoroughly with water and salt to remove thorns.
  2. Cut off both ends of the cucumbers and slice them into 2 cm segments.
  3. Finely slice the chili peppers (add more if you prefer spicier pickles).
  4. Thinly slice the garlic cloves.
  5. Thinly slice the lemon.
  6. In a large bowl, combine the sliced cucumbers, chili peppers, garlic, and lemon slices.
  7. In a separate bowl, whisk together the light soy sauce, aged vinegar, dark soy sauce, cold dish sauce, and white sugar until the sugar dissolves completely.
  8. Pour the sauce over the cucumbers and mix thoroughly to ensure all cucumbers are coated.
  9. Spread the cucumbers evenly in the bowl, ensuring they are submerged in the sauce.
  10. Cover the bowl with plastic wrap to prevent bacterial contamination.
  11. Let the cucumbers marinate at room temperature overnight (approximately 10 hours).
  12. After marinating, the cucumbers will be wrinkled but still crispy.
  13. Serve and enjoy! The pickling sauce can be reused by reheating and adding more soy sauce.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=iy6iwqPvtvE

腐乳炒空心菜.txt - Choy Sum Stir-fried with Fermented Tofu

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and authentic Cantonese-style Choy Sum dish.
  • Master the technique of stir-frying to preserve the crispness of the Choy Sum.
  • Create a flavorful sauce using fermented tofu (Fu Ru) and other simple ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 1 large bunch of choy sum (空心菜 kōngxīncài)
  • 1 green bell pepper (青椒 qīngjiāo)
  • 1 red bell pepper (紅椒 hóngjiāo)
  • 8 cloves garlic (蒜 suàn)
  • 2 pieces fermented tofu (腐乳 fǔrǔ)
  • 1 small spoonful of Matsutake mushroom seasoning (松茸鮮 sōngróng xiān) - Note: This could be substituted with other mushroom seasonings or even chicken bouillon
  • A pinch of white sugar (白糖 báitáng)
  • A dash of light soy sauce (生抽 shēngchōu)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 shíyòngyóu)
  • Pork lard (豬油 zhūyóu) - Optional, for added flavor
  • Salt (食鹽 shíyán)
  • Water (清水 qīngshuǐ)

Instructions

  1. Trim the choy sum, removing the tough bottom parts. Wash thoroughly and drain. Cut into bite-sized pieces.
  2. Cut the green and red bell peppers into small rings.
  3. Mince the garlic cloves after lightly crushing them to release their aroma.
  4. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, mash the fermented tofu with a spoon, adding the Matsutake mushroom seasoning, white sugar, and light soy sauce. Mix well until a thick paste forms.
  5. Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add a pinch of salt and a little cooking oil.
  6. Blanch the choy sum in the boiling water for about 30 seconds. Immediately remove and drain well.
  7. Heat a wok or pan with pork lard (or cooking oil). Add the minced garlic and bell peppers, stir-frying until fragrant.
  8. Add the fermented tofu sauce to the wok and stir-fry until fragrant.
  9. Add the blanched choy sum to the wok. Stir-fry quickly over high heat until everything is well combined and heated through. Do not overcook.
  10. Serve immediately.

茄子_家常烧茄子.txt - Home-Style Braised Eggplant

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy home-style braised eggplant dish.
  • Master the technique of preparing eggplant to prevent oil absorption and discoloration.
  • Create a flavorful sauce that complements the eggplant perfectly.

Ingredients

  • 2 purple eggplants (long eggplants)
  • Salt
  • White vinegar
  • Water
  • 1 green bell pepper
  • 1/4 small onion
  • 100g fatty pork (or substitute with ground pork)
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒)
  • 1 piece ginger
  • Several garlic cloves
  • Some scallions (葱白 and 葱叶)
  • Light soy sauce (生抽)
  • Oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • 1 tbsp.葱蓉鲜 (a type of seasoning sauce)
  • A pinch of sugar (白糖)
  • 1 tbsp. yellow soybean paste (黄豆酱)
  • 1 tbsp. potato starch (土豆淀粉)
  • Peanut oil (花生油)

Instructions

  1. Wash eggplants thoroughly with salt water to remove dirt. Do not peel.
  2. Cut eggplants into small square pieces.
  3. Place eggplant pieces in a bowl, add salt and white vinegar, and soak in plenty of water for 10 minutes to prevent oil absorption and browning.
  4. Cut green pepper, onion, and chili peppers into small pieces.
  5. Mince the pork.
  6. Mince ginger and garlic.
  7. Chop scallions, separating white and green parts.
  8. Prepare sauce: Mix light soy sauce, oyster sauce, 葱蓉鲜, sugar, yellow soybean paste, potato starch, and a little water.
  9. Squeeze out excess water from the eggplant.
  10. Heat oil in a wok or pan. Add minced pork and stir-fry until slightly browned.
  11. Add eggplant and stir-fry over medium heat until softened.
  12. Add ginger, garlic, and chili peppers; stir-fry until fragrant.
  13. Add green pepper and onion; stir-fry for about 20 seconds until slightly softened.
  14. Pour in the prepared sauce and stir well to coat all ingredients.
  15. Stir-fry until the sauce thickens and coats the eggplant.
  16. Drizzle with sesame oil and sprinkle with chopped scallions.
  17. Serve hot. Can be served in a clay pot for added flavor.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=eLwcFSxSQHg

菠菜鸡蛋卷.txt - Spinach and Egg Rolls

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious and nutritious spinach and egg rolls.
  • Master a simple and efficient cooking method for spring spinach.
  • Create a flavorful dipping sauce to enhance the dish.

Ingredients

  • 1 bunch spinach
  • 3 eggs
  • 1 carrot
  • 60g all-purpose flour
  • Several sheets of beancurd skin (千张)
  • A pinch of salt
  • A few drops of white vinegar
  • Sesame oil (for cooking spinach)
  • Vegetable oil (for frying)
  • 葱白 (Scallions, white part), chopped
  • 泡好的小米椒 (Soaked chili peppers), chopped
  • 蒜子 (Garlic), chopped
  • 白芝麻 (White sesame seeds)
  • 1 tsp salt (for dipping sauce)
  • A pinch of sugar (for dipping sauce)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (for dipping sauce)
  • 1/2 tbsp rice vinegar (for dipping sauce)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Spinach: Trim the spinach roots, wash thoroughly with salt water, rinse, drain, and chop into 3-4cm segments.
  2. Prepare the Carrot: Peel and thinly slice a carrot, then julienne into thicker strips. Set aside.
  3. Prepare the Eggs: Crack 3 eggs into a bowl, add a few drops of white vinegar, and whisk until light and frothy.
  4. Blanch Vegetables: Bring a pot of water to a boil, add a pinch of salt. Blanch the carrot strips for 15 seconds, then remove and drain. Blanch the spinach for 10 seconds (add a little oil to the water to preserve the spinach's green color), remove, drain, and immediately plunge into ice water to cool. Squeeze out excess water and place in a large bowl.
  5. Combine Ingredients: Add the blanched carrots and whisked eggs to the spinach. Mix well to combine.
  6. Add Flour: Stir in 60g of all-purpose flour until a thick batter forms. Set aside.
  7. Assemble the Rolls: Lay out a sheet of beancurd skin, spread a thin layer of the spinach mixture evenly over it, and tightly roll it up. Repeat with remaining ingredients.
  8. Steam the Rolls: Place the rolls in a steamer and steam for 15 minutes. Remove and let cool.
  9. Slice and Serve: Once cooled, slice the rolls into 2cm thick pieces.
  10. Prepare the Dipping Sauce: Chop scallions, soaked chili peppers, and garlic. Combine in a bowl with white sesame seeds. Pour hot oil over the mixture to enhance the aroma. Add salt, a pinch of sugar, soy sauce, and rice vinegar. Mix well.
  11. Arrange and Serve: Arrange the sliced spinach and egg rolls on a plate, drizzle with the dipping sauce, and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_nwQH_nRFvE

菠菜鸡蛋汤.txt - Spinach and Egg Drop Soup

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and nutritious spinach and egg drop soup.
  • Master the techniques for preparing the spinach and achieving a smooth, flavorful broth.
  • Understand the importance of using fresh ingredients and proper cooking methods.

Ingredients

  • 1 small bunch of spinach (about 3 RMB worth)
  • 1 small carrot
  • 1 small piece of ginger
  • 1 small bunch of scallions (separate white and green parts)
  • 2 eggs
  • 1 tablespoon cornstarch
  • Appropriate amount of water
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • 1 teaspoon MSG (optional)
  • 1 teaspoon pepper
  • 1 teaspoon soy sauce
  • Cooking oil

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Spinach: Trim the roots of the spinach, rinse thoroughly, and chop into small pieces. Set aside.
  2. Prepare the Carrot: Peel and thinly slice the carrot, then cut into fine strips. Set aside.
  3. Prepare the Scallions and Ginger: Finely chop the white parts of the scallions and julienne the ginger. Set aside. Chop the green parts of the scallions for garnish.
  4. Prepare the Egg Mixture: Crack two eggs into a bowl, whisk until well combined and frothy. Set aside.
  5. Prepare the Cornstarch Slurry: Mix one tablespoon of cornstarch with an appropriate amount of water until smooth. Set aside.
  6. Blanch the Spinach: Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add a small amount of salt and oil, then add the spinach. Blanch for 30 seconds. Remove and immediately plunge into ice water. Squeeze out excess water and set aside. (Blanching prevents the spinach from losing nutrients and keeps its color bright.)
  7. Sauté Aromatics: Heat a small amount of oil in a pot or wok. Add the ginger and white parts of the scallions and sauté until fragrant.
  8. Simmer the Soup: Add a bowl of water (preferably spring water, according to the video), salt, MSG (optional), pepper, and soy sauce. Bring to a boil.
  9. Add Carrot: Add the carrot strips and simmer for 2 minutes.
  10. Thicken the Soup: Stir in the cornstarch slurry and cook until the soup slightly thickens (a glossy consistency).
  11. Add Egg and Spinach: Turn off the heat. Quickly pour in the egg mixture, then gently stir to create egg ribbons. Add the blanched spinach and stir gently for 30 seconds.
  12. Garnish and Serve: Garnish with chopped green scallions. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Y_vPCQsuNKg

萝卜鸡蛋饼.txt - Radish Egg Cake

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy radish egg cake.
  • Master a simple technique to remove bitterness from radishes.
  • Create a flavorful and nutritious breakfast or side dish.

Ingredients

  • 2 large white radishes (白萝卜)
  • 1 tablespoon salt (盐)
  • Chopped scallions (葱花) (amount not specified)
  • 2 dollars worth of lean pork, minced (瘦肉末) (amount not specified)
  • A few eggs (鸡蛋) (amount not specified)
  • A little bit of Song Rong Xian (松茸鲜) (amount not specified)
  • A little bit of pepper powder (胡椒粉) (amount not specified)
  • A little bit of oyster sauce (蚝油) (amount not specified)
  • A small amount of cornstarch (玉米淀粉) (amount not specified)
  • Cooking oil (食用油) (amount not specified)

Instructions

  1. Wash and peel two large radishes.
  2. Cut the radishes into thick slices, then into thin strips. Alternatively, use a shredder.
  3. Place the radish strips in a bowl, add a tablespoon of salt, and mix well. Let it sit for 10 minutes to remove bitterness.
  4. While the radishes marinate, chop scallions and mince lean pork.
  5. After 10 minutes, drain excess water from the marinated radishes.
  6. In a large bowl, combine the drained radishes, minced pork, chopped scallions, and a few eggs.
  7. Season with a little Song Rong Xian, pepper powder, and oyster sauce. Add a small amount of cornstarch. (No additional salt needed due to pre-salting.)
  8. Mix all ingredients thoroughly with chopsticks.
  9. Heat a small amount of cooking oil in a pan.
  10. Pour the radish and egg mixture into the pan and stir quickly to prevent sticking.
  11. Spread the mixture into a pancake shape.
  12. Cover the pan and cook over low heat for 2-3 minutes per side, moving the pan frequently to ensure even cooking.
  13. Flip the pancake carefully using a large plate.
  14. Cook the other side until golden brown and crispy.
  15. Serve and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=73PFnwUxgNI

葱烧豆腐.txt - Scallion-braised Tofu

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and flavorful scallion-braised tofu dish.
  • Master the technique of frying tofu to achieve a golden-brown, crispy exterior.
  • Understand how to prepare a flavorful sauce to enhance the taste of the tofu.

Ingredients

  • 老豆腐 (Lǎo dòufu) - Firm Tofu: Amount not specified, but enough to be broken into irregular pieces.
  • 小葱 (Xiǎo cōng) - Scallions: A few stalks.
  • 生抽 (Shēng chōu) - Light Soy Sauce: 1 large spoonful
  • 老抽 (Lǎo chōu) - Dark Soy Sauce: A tiny amount
  • 白糖 (Bái táng) - White Sugar: Amount not specified.
  • 食盐 (Shí yán) - Salt: Amount not specified.
  • 胡椒粉 (Hú jiāo fěn) - Pepper Powder: Amount not specified.
  • 玉米淀粉 (Yùmǐ diànfěn) - Corn Starch: Amount not specified.
  • 蚝油 (Háo yóu) - Oyster Sauce: 1 small spoonful
  • 清水 (Qīng shuǐ) - Water: 1 small spoonful
  • 食用油 (Shíyòng yóu) - Cooking Oil: Amount not specified

Instructions

  1. Break the firm tofu into irregular pieces. This helps the sauce adhere better.
  2. Cut the scallions into small segments, separating the white and green parts.
  3. Prepare the sauce: Combine light soy sauce, a small amount of dark soy sauce, white sugar, salt, pepper powder, corn starch, oyster sauce, and water in a bowl. Mix well.
  4. Heat cooking oil in a pan over low heat. Add half of the green scallions and slowly sauté until fragrant and slightly browned. Remove the scallions, leaving the infused oil.
  5. Add the tofu pieces to the pan and fry until golden brown on all sides.
  6. Add a pinch of salt to the tofu while frying.
  7. Add the remaining scallions to the pan.
  8. Pour the prepared sauce over the tofu and scallions.
  9. Bring to a boil, then cover and simmer over medium-low heat for 2 minutes.
  10. Remove the lid, increase the heat to high, and cook until the sauce thickens.
  11. Serve hot with rice.

葱花发面小饼.txt - Scallion Flower Leavened Flatbread

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious scallion flatbread without adding water.
  • Master a simple, quick breakfast recipe.
  • Utilize leftover dough efficiently.

Ingredients

  • 400g all-purpose flour (面粉 miànfěn)
  • 4 eggs (鸡蛋 jīdàn)
  • 3g yeast powder (酵母粉 jiàomǔ fěn)
  • 10g white sugar (白糖 báitáng)
  • 20g cooking oil (食用油 shíyòng yóu)
  • Several scallions (小葱 xiǎocōng), chopped
  • Cooking oil for frying

Instructions

  1. Pour 400g flour into a large bowl.
  2. Crack 4 eggs into the bowl.
  3. Add 3g yeast powder and 10g sugar.
  4. Mix thoroughly with chopsticks until a crumbly mixture forms.
  5. Add 20g cooking oil.
  6. Knead the dough until smooth and elastic (no dry flour remains). This will be firm as no water is added.
  7. Place the dough in a warm place to rise until doubled in size.
  8. While the dough is rising, chop several scallions finely.
  9. Once doubled, place the dough on a lightly floured surface and knead to release air.
  10. Roll the dough into a large, thin sheet (about 1cm thick).
  11. Sprinkle chopped scallions evenly over the dough.
  12. Tightly roll the dough into a log.
  13. Pinch the seam to seal.
  14. Gently flatten the log and roll it into a large rectangle.
  15. Cut the rectangle into smaller pieces using a cookie cutter, bottle cap or similar. (The transcript uses a wine glass).
  16. Gather any leftover scraps, knead them together, and roll them out to make more small flatbreads.
  17. Place the flatbread pieces onto a baking sheet.
  18. Heat a non-stick pan over low heat.
  19. Brush the pan with a thin layer of oil.
  20. Arrange the flatbreads in the pan, leaving space between each.
  21. Cover the pan and cook for 2 minutes.
  22. Flip the flatbreads and cook for another 2 minutes.
  23. Continue cooking and flipping until both sides are golden brown and the flatbreads are puffed up. (Approximately 6-7 minutes total cook time).

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=p9q67y9uCLk

葱香鸡蛋饼.txt - Fragrant Scallion Egg Cake

Objectives

  • Learn to make a fluffy and flavorful scallion egg cake.
  • Master the technique of cooking the egg mixture for optimal texture.
  • Create a simple yet delicious dish using readily available ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 5 eggs (母鸡刚刚下的蛋 - mother hen's fresh eggs)
  • 1 bunch scallions (一把小葱 - yī bǎ xiǎo cōng)
  • Salt (食盐 - shíyán)
  • Thirteen spice (十三香 - shísānxīang)
  • Cooking oil (食用油 - shíyòngyóu)

Instructions

  1. Finely chop the scallions into small pieces (葱花 - cōnghuā). Set aside.
  2. Crack 5 eggs into a large bowl.
  3. Add a dash of salt and thirteen spice to the eggs.
  4. Thoroughly whisk the eggs with chopsticks until the egg whites and yolks are fully combined.
  5. Add the chopped scallions to the egg mixture and stir until well combined.
  6. Heat a pan with a moderate amount of cooking oil over medium heat.
  7. Pour half of the egg mixture into the hot pan.
  8. Quickly spread the egg mixture using a spatula to form a thin layer.
  9. Once the egg mixture is set, remove it from the pan and set aside.
  10. Add the remaining egg mixture to the pan and repeat steps 7-8.
  11. Once the second half of the egg mixture is set, place the first half on top.
  12. Using a spatula, gently flatten the combined egg mixture into a cake shape.
  13. Cover the pan with a lid and cook over medium-low heat until both sides are golden brown and cooked through.
  14. Remove the egg cake from the pan and serve.

蒜泥豆角.txt - Garlic Sauce Green Beans

Objectives

  • Learn to make a refreshing and flavorful garlic sauce green bean dish.
  • Master the technique of blanching green beans to preserve their color and texture.
  • Understand how to prepare and season the green beans for optimal taste.

Ingredients

  • 1 bunch green beans (approx. 250g)
  • 1 head garlic
  • 1 large spoonful of salt
  • A few drops of cooking oil
  • 1 small spoonful of salt (for seasoning)
  • 1 small spoonful of mushroom seasoning (松茸鲜)
  • A generous amount of sesame oil (小磨香油)
  • A small amount of sesame paste (芝麻酱)

Instructions

  1. Trim the ends of the green beans and wash them thoroughly.
  2. Cut the green beans into 4-5 cm segments.
  3. Mince the garlic using a garlic press.
  4. Bring a pot of water to a boil over high heat.
  5. Add a large spoonful of salt and a few drops of cooking oil to the boiling water.
  6. Add the green beans to the boiling water and cook for 3-5 minutes until tender-crisp.
  7. Remove the blanched green beans and immediately transfer them to a bowl of ice water to cool.
  8. Drain the cooled green beans thoroughly.
  9. Add the minced garlic, a small spoonful of salt, a small spoonful of mushroom seasoning, a generous amount of sesame oil, and a small amount of sesame paste to the green beans.
  10. Wear disposable gloves and mix thoroughly to coat the green beans evenly with the sauce.
  11. Serve and enjoy.

蒜苔炒肉.txt - Garlic Stems with Pork

Objectives

  • Learn a simple technique to keep garlic stems crisp when stir-frying.
  • Make a flavorful and delicious garlic stems with pork dish.
  • Master a quick and easy stir-fry recipe perfect for a weeknight meal.

Ingredients

  • 1 bunch fresh garlic stems
  • 5 RMB worth of pork (half lean, half fatty)
  • 1 piece ginger
  • Several cloves garlic
  • Plenty of dried chili peppers
  • Salt
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce
  • Appropriate amount of oyster sauce
  • 1 tbsp yellow bean sauce
  • A small handful of fermented black beans
  • A little chicken bouillon
  • Water

Instructions

  1. Trim the tough ends of the garlic stems and cut into 5cm lengths. Discard or save the tips for another use (e.g., scrambled eggs).
  2. Place the cut garlic stems in a large bowl, add salt, and mix well. Let marinate for 10 minutes.
  3. Slice the pork thinly.
  4. Pat the ginger flat and mince it. Mince the garlic cloves as well.
  5. Cut the dried chilies into small pieces and rinse them to remove dust and impurities.
  6. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, combine soy sauce, oyster sauce, yellow bean sauce, fermented black beans, and chicken bouillon. Mix well. (Optional: Substitute yellow bean sauce with doubanjiang for spicier flavor).
  7. After 10 minutes, rinse the marinated garlic stems under running water to remove excess salt. Drain well.
  8. Heat a wok or pan over medium-high heat. Add the fatty pork and slowly render the fat.
  9. Add the lean pork and stir-fry until it changes color.
  10. Add the minced ginger and garlic and stir-fry briefly.
  11. Add the dried chilies and stir-fry until fragrant.
  12. Add the garlic stems and stir-fry until evenly coated with the oil and other ingredients.
  13. Add the prepared sauce and stir-fry quickly over high heat until the ingredients are well-mixed and the sauce has thickened slightly.
  14. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Y7fYlj_ky4c

蒜蓉肉片.txt - Garlic Pork Slices 蒜蓉肉片 - Garlic Pork Slices

Objectives

  • Learn to make tender and flavorful garlic pork slices.
  • Master a quick and easy weeknight dinner recipe.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients for a delicious meal.
  • Learn a simple method for preparing pork slices.
  • Understand the importance of marinating the meat.
  • Learn to blanch the mushrooms properly.
  • Achieve a rich garlic flavor in the dish.
  • Create a visually appealing and appetizing presentation.

Ingredients

  • Fresh pork (leg or loin)
  • 生抽 (Shēngchōu - light soy sauce)
  • 老抽 (Lǎochōu - dark soy sauce)
  • 蚝油 (Háoyóu - oyster sauce)
  • Ginger (姜丝 - jiāng sī)
  • 金针菇 (Jīnzhēngū - golden needle mushroom)
  • 干辣椒段 (Gàn làjiāo duàn - dried chili segments)
  • 花椒 (Huājiāo - Sichuan peppercorn)
  • 自制蒜蓉 (Zìzhì sùnyóng - homemade garlic paste)
  • 水淀粉 (Shuǐdiànfěn - water starch)
  • 小磨香油 (Xiǎo mó xiāngyóu - small grinding sesame oil)
  • 葱花 (Cōnghuā - chopped scallions)
  • Salt (食盐 - shíyán)

Instructions

  1. Cut the pork into evenly sized pieces, then slice thinly.
  2. Place the sliced pork in a bowl.
  3. Add light soy sauce, a little dark soy sauce, oyster sauce, and ginger.
  4. Mix well to marinate for 10 minutes.
  5. Prepare the golden needle mushrooms by trimming the roots. Do not wash.
  6. Boil water in a pot, add salt, and blanch the mushrooms for approximately 7-8 seconds to remove odor.
  7. Drain the mushrooms and set aside.
  8. Heat oil in a wok or pan over medium heat.
  9. Add the marinated pork slices and stir-fry until fully cooked and discolored.
  10. Add dried chili segments, Sichuan peppercorns, and homemade garlic paste.
  11. Stir-fry until fragrant.
  12. Add a little light soy sauce for flavor.
  13. Add water starch and sesame oil.
  14. Stir-fry until the sauce thickens.
  15. Garnish with chopped scallions.
  16. Serve the garlic pork slices over the blanched golden needle mushrooms.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vYFC56YuwV4

蒜香西兰花.txt - Garlic Fragrant Broccoli

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare and clean broccoli effectively.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful garlic broccoli recipe.
  • Create a dish that appeals to children who may be picky eaters.

Ingredients

  • 1 head of broccoli
  • Salt
  • Water
  • Several cloves of garlic
  • Cooking oil
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽 - shēng zhōu)
  • 1 tbsp oyster sauce (蚝油 - háo yóu)
  • 1 tsp sugar (白糖 - bái táng)

Instructions

  1. Select a firm, green broccoli head with tightly packed florets.
  2. Using a knife or scissors, separate the broccoli florets from the stem. Save the stem for another use.
  3. Cut larger florets into smaller, more manageable pieces.
  4. Place the broccoli in a large bowl, add salt and plenty of water, and soak for 10 minutes to remove any insects or impurities.
  5. Rinse the broccoli thoroughly with clean water twice.
  6. Drain the broccoli and set aside.
  7. Peel and mince the garlic cloves.
  8. Bring a pot of water to a boil, add salt, and blanch the broccoli for 1 minute.
  9. Remove the broccoli with a colander and drain well.
  10. Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan.
  11. Add the minced garlic and sauté over medium heat until fragrant.
  12. Add soy sauce, oyster sauce, and sugar; stir well.
  13. Add the blanched broccoli and stir-fry until evenly coated with the garlic sauce (approximately 49 seconds).
  14. Serve and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=o9nVBFMgq3E

西兰花炒口蘑.txt - Stir-fried Broccoli with Mushrooms

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare and cook broccoli for optimal texture and flavor.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful stir-fry recipe using readily available ingredients.
  • Understand the importance of properly preparing ingredients and using a flavorful sauce.

Ingredients

  • 1 head of broccoli
  • 1 package of oyster mushrooms (口蘑)
  • 1 tbsp salt (食盐)
  • Several cloves of garlic (蒜子)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽酱油)
  • Black pepper (黑胡椒粉)
  • 1 tsp oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • 1 tsp cornstarch (淀粉)
  • Water (山泉水)
  • Cooking oil (花生油 or 橄榄油)
  • Sesame oil (小磨香油)

Instructions

  1. Remove broccoli leaves and cut into small florets. Cut larger florets into smaller pieces.
  2. Place broccoli florets in a large bowl, add a tablespoon of salt and plenty of water. Soak for 10 minutes.
  3. Clean and slice oyster mushrooms into thicker slices. Set aside.
  4. Mince garlic finely. Set aside.
  5. Prepare sauce: In a small bowl, combine soy sauce, black pepper, a small amount of salt, oyster sauce, cornstarch, and a small amount of water. Mix well. Set aside.
  6. Rinse broccoli thoroughly after soaking.
  7. Blanch broccoli in boiling water for 30 seconds. Drain and immediately transfer to ice water to cool. Drain again.
  8. Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan over medium-high heat.
  9. Add minced garlic and stir-fry until fragrant.
  10. Add sliced mushrooms and stir-fry for about 2 minutes until slightly browned.
  11. Add a splash of cooking wine (料酒) to remove fishy smell.
  12. Pour in the prepared sauce and stir-fry until everything is well combined and heated through.
  13. Add blanched broccoli and stir-fry until heated through.
  14. Drizzle with sesame oil and stir-fry briefly.
  15. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=3CClsP16hZc

西兰花_素炒西兰花.txt - 素炒西兰花

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and healthy stir-fried broccoli dish.
  • Master the technique of blanching broccoli to maintain its vibrant green color and crisp texture.
  • Create a flavorful sauce that complements the broccoli's natural taste.

Ingredients

  • 1 large head of broccoli (约5元)
  • 1 large tomato
  • 1 handful of shiitake mushrooms (海鲜菇)
  • 1 small piece of ginger
  • Several small chili peppers (小米椒)
  • 1 tbsp soy sauce (生抽)
  • Appropriate amount of oyster sauce (蚝油)
  • A pinch of salt (食盐)
  • A tiny bit of sugar (白糖)
  • 1 tsp Matsutake mushroom seasoning (松茸鲜)
  • A pinch of pepper (胡椒粉)
  • 1 tsp cornstarch (玉米淀粉)
  • Appropriate amount of water (清水)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)

Instructions

  1. Remove broccoli leaves and separate florets, cutting larger ones into smaller, uniform pieces.
  2. Soak broccoli in light salt water for 15 minutes to remove impurities and insects.
  3. Cut the tomato into small pieces.
  4. Cut the shiitake mushrooms into small pieces.
  5. Mince ginger and garlic, finely chop chili peppers.
  6. Prepare the sauce: Combine soy sauce, oyster sauce, salt, sugar, Matsutake seasoning, pepper, cornstarch, and water in a bowl, mixing well.
  7. Rinse the broccoli thoroughly after soaking.
  8. Bring a pot of water to a boil with a spoonful of salt.
  9. Blanch broccoli for 1 minute, then add shiitake mushrooms and blanch for another 20 seconds.
  10. Remove broccoli and mushrooms, drain, and set aside.
  11. Heat oil in a wok or pan, add tomatoes and stir-fry for 2 minutes until softened and releasing their juices.
  12. Add ginger, garlic, and chili peppers, stir-frying for 20 seconds until fragrant.
  13. Add blanched broccoli and mushrooms, stir-frying for 1 minute.
  14. Pour in the prepared sauce, stir-frying until the sauce thickens and coats the vegetables.
  15. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=4Ls82CHIWC4

西兰花蒸蛋.txt - Steamed Broccoli and Egg

Objectives

  • Learn a new way to prepare broccoli that's both delicious and visually appealing.
  • Create a nutritious and satisfying dish perfect for summer meals.
  • Master a simple steaming technique for tender broccoli and eggs.

Ingredients

  • 1 head of broccoli
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • 1 tablespoon all-purpose flour
  • Water
  • 1 tablespoon salt (for boiling water)
  • A little cooking oil (for boiling water)
  • 1 tablespoon salt (for seasoning)
  • 1 tablespoon Songrong Xian (mushroom seasoning)
  • A little pepper
  • 30g cornstarch
  • 4 eggs
  • Vegetable oil (for greasing pan)
  • Optional: Parchment paper
  • High-temperature cling film
  • Toothpick
  • Several dried chili peppers (optional)
  • Several cloves garlic (optional)
  • Some scallions (optional)
  • 1 tablespoon sesame seeds (optional)
  • 1 tablespoon soy sauce (optional)
  • More rice vinegar (optional)
  • Chili oil (optional)

Instructions

  1. Prepare broccoli: Cut the broccoli florets from the stem. Place in a large bowl, add 1 tbsp salt and 1 tbsp flour. Add water and soak for 5 minutes. This helps remove impurities and insects. Rinse thoroughly with water until the water runs clear.
  2. Blanch broccoli: Boil water with 1 tbsp salt and a little cooking oil. Add broccoli and blanch for 36 seconds. Remove with a slotted spoon, rinse with cold water, and drain.
  3. Prepare carrots and broccoli: Dice peeled carrots. Chop the blanched broccoli into small pieces.
  4. Mix ingredients: Combine chopped broccoli and carrots in a bowl. Add 1 tbsp salt, 1 tbsp Songrong Xian, a little pepper, and 30g cornstarch. Mix well.
  5. Add eggs: Add 4 eggs to the mixture and stir until smooth and well combined.
  6. Prepare pan: Grease a small square pan with oil or line it with parchment paper. Pour the broccoli and egg mixture into the pan.
  7. Steam: Cover the pan with high-temperature cling film, piercing several small holes with a toothpick. Steam over boiling water for 12 minutes.
  8. Prepare sauce: While steaming, prepare the sauce. Chop dried chilies, garlic, and scallions. Combine in a bowl with sesame seeds, soy sauce, rice vinegar, and chili oil (optional). Mix well.
  9. Finish: Remove the steamed broccoli and egg from the steamer. Let it cool slightly. Use a spatula to help it release from the pan. Invert onto a plate and remove the cling film and parchment paper. Cut into pieces and serve. Drizzle with prepared sauce before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=T78C96jfjYw

西兰花豆腐.txt - Steamed Tofu with Broccoli

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple, healthy, and delicious dish of steamed tofu with broccoli.
  • Master a quick and easy cooking method suitable for busy individuals.
  • Understand how to enhance the flavor and texture of tofu and broccoli.

Ingredients

  • 2 blocks of firm tofu (老豆腐)
  • 1 small head of broccoli (西兰花)
  • 1 egg (鸡蛋)
  • Salt (食盐)
  • Cooking oil (食用油)
  • 1 tsp Dried mushrooms (松茸鲜)
  • Minced garlic (蒜末)
  • Chopped scallions (葱花)
  • Soy sauce (生抽)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the broccoli: Remove the florets from the stem using a knife. Set aside the florets; save the stem for another meal.
  2. Prepare the tofu: Place the tofu in a bowl and crumble it using your hands until it resembles a coarse mixture. Set aside.
  3. Blanch the broccoli: Bring a pot of water to a boil. Add a pinch of salt and a little cooking oil. Add the broccoli florets and blanch for 30 seconds. Remove with a slotted spoon and add to the bowl with the crumbled tofu.
  4. Mix the ingredients: Add an egg, salt, dried mushrooms, minced garlic, chopped scallions, and soy sauce to the bowl with the tofu and broccoli. Mix thoroughly with chopsticks until well combined.
  5. Cook the dish: Heat cooking oil in a wok or pan over medium-low heat. Add the tofu and broccoli mixture and stir-fry until the tofu is slightly browned and the moisture has evaporated. Stir frequently to ensure even cooking.
  6. Serve: Turn off the heat. Transfer the cooked tofu and broccoli to a serving dish and serve immediately. Enjoy with rice.

酱油萝卜皮_three_ways.txt - Three Ways with Pickled Radish

Objectives

  • Learn three different ways to prepare pickled radish.
  • Understand the importance of proper salting and soaking techniques.
  • Master a simple, cost-effective recipe for a delicious side dish.
  • Learn to prepare a flavorful, restaurant-quality pickled radish dish at home.
  • Discover a versatile radish recipe suitable for various occasions.
  • Learn to store pickled radish for extended periods.
  • Learn how to make pickled radish that is both crispy and flavorful.

Ingredients

For all recipes:

  • 3 large radishes (approximately 8 jin) 白萝卜 (bái luóbo)
  • Salt 食盐 (shíyán)
  • Sugar 白糖 (bái táng)
  • Garlic 大蒜 (dàsuàn)
  • Chili peppers 小米椒 (xiǎomǐjiāo)
  • Rice vinegar/white vinegar 米醋/白醋 (mǐcù/báicù)
  • Soy sauce 酱油 (jiàngyóu)
  • Pickled peppers 泡椒 (pàojiāo) and brine 泡椒水 (pàojiāo shuǐ)
  • Optional: Sprite 雪碧 (xuěbì)

Specific quantities will vary depending on preference and radish size.

Instructions

Recipe 1: 酱油萝卜皮 (Pickled Radish Skin)

  1. Cut off both ends of the radishes. Discard the pointy end.
  2. Cut the radishes in half, then into quarters.
  3. Cut the radish skin into thick pieces.
  4. Place the radish skin in a bowl, add salt, mix well, and let it marinate for 30 minutes.
  5. Rinse the radish skin under cold water to remove excess salt.
  6. Drain the radish skin well.
  7. In a bowl, combine the radish skin with minced garlic, chili peppers, a little sugar, soy sauce, and a small amount of vinegar. Mix thoroughly.
  8. Transfer the mixture to an airtight container. Ensure even distribution of garlic and chilies.
  9. Marinate for at least one day (longer for a stronger flavor). Refrigerate in summer.

Recipe 2: 爽口萝卜条 (Crispy Radish Strips)

  1. Wash and cut the radish into long strips (approximately 1cm thick and wide).
  2. Soak the radish strips in cold water for 2 hours.
  3. Prepare a marinade with garlic, chili peppers, salt, sugar, pickled peppers, pickled pepper brine, optional Sprite, and vinegar.
  4. Drain the soaked radish strips and add them to the marinade. Mix well.
  5. Refrigerate for at least 5 hours (longer for a crispier texture).

Recipe 3: 萝卜因子擦菜 (Radish Residue)

  1. After preparing the radish skin and strips, use the remaining radish.
  2. Cut into small pieces.
  3. Add salt and mix well. Let it marinate for 30 minutes.

Note: The video doesn't provide detailed instructions for the third recipe beyond salting and marinating. More information would be needed to fully explain this preparation.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LT_cHto3buc

酱油萝卜皮.txt - Soy Sauce Radish Skin

Objectives

  • Learn three different ways to prepare radish using simple, inexpensive ingredients.
  • Master a quick and easy method for making delicious soy sauce radish skin.
  • Create flavorful and crunchy radish strips and pickled radish.

Ingredients

For Soy Sauce Radish Skin:

  • 3 large radishes (approximately 8 jin)
  • Salt (amount to taste)
  • Small amount of white sugar
  • Small amount of soy sauce for color
  • Small amount of light soy sauce for flavor
  • Millet pepper (amount to taste)
  • Garlic slices (amount to taste)

For Radish Strips:

  • 3 large radishes (approximately 8 jin)
  • Plenty of cold water for soaking
  • Garlic slices (amount to taste)
  • Ginger slices (amount to taste)
  • Pickled peppers and brine (amount to taste)
  • Salt (amount to taste)
  • White sugar (amount to taste)
  • About half a bottle of Sprite (optional)
  • 50g rice vinegar or white vinegar

For Pickled Radishes:

  • 3 large radishes (approximately 8 jin)
  • Salt (amount to taste)

Instructions

Soy Sauce Radish Skin:

  1. Cut off both ends of the radishes. Discard the pointed end.
  2. Cut the radishes into quarters.
  3. Cut the radish skin into thicker pieces.
  4. Place the radish skin in a bowl, add salt, and mix well.
  5. Let it marinate for 30 minutes.
  6. Rinse the radish skin in cold water to remove excess salt.
  7. Drain the water.
  8. Add millet pepper, garlic slices, a small amount of white sugar, light soy sauce, and soy sauce to the radish skin.
  9. Mix well, ensuring all radish skin is coated. Avoid using oily utensils or gloves to ensure longer preservation.
  10. Transfer to an airtight container. Ensure even distribution of garlic and peppers.
  11. Marinate for at least one day (longer for a stronger flavor). Refrigerate in summer.

Radish Strips:

  1. Wash and cut the radishes into long strips, then into 1cm thick slices, and finally into 1cm wide strips.
  2. Soak the radish strips in plenty of cold water for 2 hours.
  3. While soaking, prepare the marinade: Mince garlic, slice ginger, and prepare pickled peppers.
  4. In a large bowl, combine garlic, ginger, pickled peppers and brine, salt, white sugar, Sprite (optional), and vinegar. Mix well.
  5. Drain the soaked radish strips and add them to the marinade.
  6. Mix well and refrigerate for at least 5 hours (longer for a crispier texture).

Pickled Radishes:

  1. Wash and cut radishes into small pieces.
  2. Add salt, mix well, and let it marinate for 30 minutes.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LT_cHto3buc

香焖带鱼.txt - Fragrant Braised Hairtail

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy braised hairtail dish.
  • Master a simple yet flavorful cooking technique.
  • Utilize readily available ingredients for a quick meal.

Ingredients

  • 2 Hairtail (带鱼 dàiyú), about 11 RMB each
  • 1 large Onion (大葱 dàcōng), cut into diagonal segments
  • 1 piece Ginger (生姜 shēngjiāng), peeled and julienned
  • 1 Egg (鸡蛋 jīdàn)
  • 1 tbsp Cooking Wine (料酒 liàojiǔ)
  • 1 tbsp Huadiao Wine (花雕酒 huādiāojiǔ)
  • 1 tsp Salt (食盐 shíyán)
  • 1/2 tsp Pepper (胡椒粉 hújiāofěn)
  • Garlic (蒜子 suànzi), thinly sliced
  • A pinch of Salt (毛毛盐 máomáoyán)
  • A pinch of Chicken Essence (鸡精 jījīng)
  • A pinch of Five-spice Powder (五香粉 wǔxiāngfěn)
  • 1 tsp Sugar (白糖 báitáng)
  • 1 tbsp Soy Sauce (生抽 shēngchōu)
  • 1/2 tbsp Vinegar (陈醋 chéncù)
  • A little Oyster Sauce (蚝油 háoyóu)
  • Some Water (清水 qīngshuǐ)
  • 1 tbsp Corn Starch (淀粉 diànfěn), about 30g
  • Vegetable Oil (菜籽油 cài zǐyóu) for frying

Instructions

  1. Clean and prepare the hairtail: Remove fins, gut, and black membrane. Rinse thoroughly until the water runs clear. Cut off the head (save for the cat!), and cut the body into 5-6cm segments.
  2. Score the hairtail: Using a knife, make shallow cuts along the fish bones on both sides.
  3. Marinate the hairtail: Place the scored hairtail in a bowl. Add cooking wine, Huadiao wine, salt, and pepper. Mix well and marinate for 20 minutes.
  4. Prepare the garlic and ginger: Slice garlic thinly and julienne the ginger. Set aside.
  5. Prepare the sauce: In a bowl, combine a pinch of salt, chicken essence, five-spice powder, sugar, soy sauce, vinegar, oyster sauce, and water. Stir until well combined. Set aside.
  6. Prepare the egg mixture: Crack an egg into a bowl and whisk until the egg white and yolk are fully blended. Set aside.
  7. Coat the hairtail: Add the egg mixture and cornstarch to the marinated hairtail. Mix well to coat each piece evenly.
  8. Fry the hairtail: Heat vegetable oil in a pan until slightly smoking. Add the hairtail pieces, ensuring not to overcrowd the pan. Fry over medium-low heat until golden brown on both sides, ensuring even cooking.
  9. Prepare the sauce: In a clean pan, heat a little oil. Add the garlic, ginger, and white parts of the onion. Sauté until fragrant.
  10. Combine and simmer: Pour the prepared sauce into the pan. Bring to a boil, then add the fried hairtail. Stir to coat evenly. Optionally cover and simmer for 2 minutes.
  11. Finish and serve: Increase heat to reduce the sauce. Once the sauce has thickened, turn off the heat. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_3Zmyco01ys

香菇炖鸡.txt - Braised Chicken with Mushrooms

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare chicken for tender, flavorful braising.
  • Master a simple yet delicious braising technique for chicken.
  • Create a flavorful dish using readily available ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 半只走地鸡 (Half a free-range chicken)
  • 一勺面粉 (One tablespoon of flour)
  • 少许清水 (A little bit of water)
  • 干香菇 (Dried shiitake mushrooms)
  • 温水 (Warm water)
  • 几瓣大蒜 (Several cloves of garlic)
  • 小块生姜 (A small piece of ginger)
  • 少许花椒 (A pinch of Sichuan peppercorns)
  • 几颗干海椒 (A few dried chili peppers)
  • 一个大红椒 (One large red bell pepper)
  • 2个青椒 (Two green bell peppers)
  • 一小把小葱 (A small handful of scallions)
  • 小半勺食盐 (Half a small spoon of salt)
  • 少许胡椒粉 (A pinch of pepper)
  • 一勺生抽 (One tablespoon of light soy sauce)
  • 少许老抽 (A little bit of dark soy sauce)
  • 一勺料酒 (One tablespoon of cooking wine)
  • 一勺黄豆酱 (One tablespoon of soybean paste)
  • 少许食用油 (A little bit of cooking oil)
  • 适量开水 (Appropriate amount of boiling water)

Instructions

  1. Cut the chicken into bite-sized pieces.
  2. Add flour and a little water to the chicken, mix well for one minute to remove blood and impurities.
  3. Rinse the chicken thoroughly with water until the water runs clear.
  4. Soak dried shiitake mushrooms in warm water.
  5. Mince garlic and ginger.
  6. Chop red and green bell peppers.
  7. Chop scallions.
  8. In a bowl, mix salt, pepper, light soy sauce, dark soy sauce, cooking wine, and soybean paste.
  9. Rinse and squeeze the soaked mushrooms.
  10. Heat oil in a pot, sauté ginger, garlic, chili peppers, and Sichuan peppercorns until fragrant.
  11. Add the chicken and stir-fry until the excess water is evaporated and the chicken skin turns slightly yellow. Use high heat throughout.
  12. Add the prepared sauce and stir-fry until the chicken is coated and fragrant.
  13. Add the mushrooms and stir-fry for about one minute.
  14. Add boiling water (enough to cover the chicken).
  15. Cover and simmer over low heat for 15 minutes.
  16. Increase heat to high, reduce the sauce until thickened.
  17. Add chopped bell peppers and stir-fry until tender.
  18. Add chopped scallions and stir-fry briefly.
  19. Serve and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=N9j8sJ4CsEQ
